 nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam
 devīṃ sarasvatīṃ caiva tato jayam udīrayet
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tato droṇe hate rājan duryodhanamukhā nṛpāḥ
c bhṛśam udvignamanaso droṇaputram upāgaman
d śuklāmbaradharaṃ viṣṇuṃ śaśivarṇaṃ caturbhujam
d prasannavadanaṃ dhyāyet sarvavighnopaśāntaye
a te droṇam upaśocantaḥ kaśmalābhihataujasaḥ
c paryupāsanta śokārtās tataḥ śāradvatīsutam
a muhūrtaṃ te samāśvāsya hetubhiḥ śāstrasaṃmitaiḥ
c rātryāgame mahīpālāḥ svāni veśmāni bhejire
a viśeṣataḥ sūtaputro rājā caiva suyodhanaḥ
c duḥśāsano 'tha śakunir na nidrām upalebhire
a te veśmasv api kauravya pṛthvīśā nāpnuvan sukham
c cintayantaḥ kṣayaṃ tīvraṃ nidrāṃ naivopalebhire
a sahitās te niśāyāṃ tu duryodhananiveśane
c atipracaṇḍād vidveṣāt pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanām
a yat tad dyūtaparikliṣṭāṃ kṛṣṇām āninyire sabhām
c tat smaranto 'nvatapyanta bhṛśam udvignacetasaḥ
a cintayantaś ca pārthānāṃ tān kleśān dyūtakāritān
c kṛcchreṇa kṣaṇadāṃ rājan ninyur abdaśatopamām
a tataḥ prabhāte vimale sthitā diṣṭasya śāsane
c cakrur āvaśyakaṃ sarve vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā
a te kṛtvāvaśyakāryāṇi samāśvasya ca bhārata
c yogam ājñāpayām āsur yuddhāya ca viniryayuḥ
a karṇaṃ senāpatiṃ kṛtvā kṛtakautukamaṅgalāḥ
c vācayitvā dvijaśreṣṭhān dadhipātraghṛtākṣataiḥ
a niṣkair gobhir hiraṇyena vāsobhiś ca mahādhanaiḥ
c vardhyamānā jayāśīrbhiḥ sūtamāgadhabandibhiḥ
a tathaiva pāṇḍavā rājan kṛtasarvāhṇikakriyāḥ
c śibirān niryayū rājan yuddhāya kṛtaniścayāḥ
a tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ romaharṣaṇam
c kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca parasparavadhaiṣiṇām
a tayor dve divase yuddhaṃ kurupāṇḍavasenayoḥ
c karṇe senāpatau rājann abhūd adbhutadarśanam
a tataḥ śatrukṣayaṃ kṛtvā sumahāntaṃ raṇe vṛṣaḥ
c paśyatāṃ dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ phalgunena nipātitaḥ
a tatas tat saṃjayaḥ sarvaṃ gatvā nāgāhvayaṃ puram
c ācakhyau dhṛtarāṣṭrāya yad vṛttaṃ kurujāṅgale
 janamejaya uvāca
a āpageyaṃ hataṃ śrutvā droṇaṃ ca samare paraiḥ
c yo jagāma parām ārtiṃ vṛddho rājāmbikāsutaḥ
a sa śrutvā nihataṃ karṇaṃ duryodhanahitaiṣiṇam
c kathaṃ dvijavara prāṇān adhārayata duḥkhitaḥ
a yasmiñ jayāśāṃ putrāṇām amanyata sa pārthivaḥ
c tasmin hate sa kauravyaḥ kathaṃ prāṇān adhārayat
a durmaraṃ bata manye 'haṃ nṛṇāṃ kṛcchre 'pi vartatām
c yatra karṇaṃ hataṃ śrutvā nātyajaj jīvitaṃ nṛpaḥ
a tathā śāṃtanavaṃ vṛddhaṃ brahman bāhlikam eva ca
c droṇaṃ ca somadattaṃ ca bhūriśravasam eva ca
a tathaiva cānyān suhṛdaḥ putrapautrāṃś ca pātitān
c śrutvā yan nājahāt prāṇāṃs tan manye duṣkaraṃ dvija
a etan me sarvam ācakṣva vistareṇa tapodhana
c na hi tṛpyāmi pūrveṣāṃ śṛṇvānaś caritaṃ mahat
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a hate karṇe mahārāja niśi gāvalgaṇis tadā
c dīno yayau nāgapuram aśvair vātasamair jave
a sa hāstinapuraṃ gatvā bhṛśam udvignamānasaḥ
c jagāma dhṛtarāṣṭrasya kṣayaṃ prakṣīṇabāndhavam
a sa samudvīkṣya rājānaṃ kaśmalābhihataujasam
c vavande prāñjalir bhūtvā mūrdhnā pādau nṛpasya ha
a saṃpūjya ca yathānyāyaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ mahīpatim
c hā kaṣṭam iti coktvā sa tato vacanam ādade
a saṃjayo 'haṃ kṣitipate kaccid āste sukhaṃ bhavān
c svadoṣeṇāpadaṃ prāpya kaccin nādya vimuhyasi
a hitāny uktāni viduradroṇagāṅgeyakeśavaiḥ
c agṛhītāny anusmṛtya kaccin na kuruṣe vyathām
a rāmanāradakaṇvaiś ca hitam uktaṃ sabhātale
c nagṛhītam anusmṛtya kaccin na kuruṣe vyathām
a suhṛdas tvaddhite yuktān bhīṣmadroṇamukhān paraiḥ
c nihatān yudhi saṃsmṛtya kaccin na kuruṣe vyathām
a tam evaṃvādinaṃ rājā sūtaputraṃ kṛtāñjalim
c sudīrgham abhiniḥśvasya duḥkhārta idam abravīt
a gāṅgeye nihate śūre divyāstravati saṃjaya
c droṇe ca parameṣvāse bhṛśaṃ me vyathitaṃ manaḥ
a yo rathānāṃ sahasrāṇi daṃśitānāṃ daśaiva hi
c ahany ahani tejasvī nijaghne vasusaṃbhavaḥ
a sa hato yajñasenasya putreṇeha śikhaṇḍinā
c pāṇḍaveyābhiguptena bhṛśaṃ me vyathitaṃ manaḥ
a bhārgavaḥ pradadau yasmai paramāstraṃ mahātmane
c sākṣād rāmeṇa yo bālye dhanurveda upākṛtaḥ
a yasya prasādāt kaunteyā rājaputrā mahābalāḥ
c mahārathatvaṃ saṃprāptās tathānye vasudhādhipāḥ
a taṃ droṇaṃ nihataṃ śrutvā dhṛṣṭadyumnena saṃyuge
c satyasaṃdhaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ bhṛśaṃ me vyathitaṃ manaḥ
d yayor loke pumān astre na samo 'sti caturvidhe
d tau droṇabhīṣmau śrutvā tu hatau me vyathitaṃ manaḥ
a trailokye yasya śāstreṣu na pumān vidyate samaḥ
c taṃ droṇaṃ nihataṃ śrutvā kim akurvata māmakāḥ
a saṃśaptakānāṃ ca bale pāṇḍavena mahātmanā
c dhanaṃjayena vikramya gamite yamasādanam
a nārāyaṇāstre nihate droṇaputrasya dhīmataḥ
c hataśeṣeṣv anīkeṣu kim akurvata māmakāḥ
a vipradrutān ahaṃ manye nimagnaḥ śokasāgare
c plavamānān hate droṇe sannanaukān ivārṇave
a duryodhanasya karṇasya bhojasya kṛtavarmaṇaḥ
c madrarājasya śalyasya drauṇeś caiva kṛpasya ca
a matputraśeṣasya tathā tathānyeṣāṃ ca saṃjaya
c viprakīrṇeṣv anīkeṣu mukhavarṇo 'bhavat katham
a etat sarvaṃ yathā vṛttaṃ tattvaṃ gāvalgaṇe raṇe
c ācakṣva pāṇḍaveyānāṃ māmakānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a pāṇḍaveyair hi yad vṛttaṃ kauraveyeṣu māriṣa
c tac chrutvā mā vyathāṃ kārṣīd iṣṭe na vyathate manaḥ
a yasmād abhāvī bhāvī vā bhaved artho naraṃ prati
c aprāptau tasya vā prāptau na kaś cid vyathate budhaḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a na vyathā śṛṇvataḥ kā cid vidyate mama saṃjaya
c diṣṭam etat purā manye kathayasva yathecchakam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a hate droṇe maheṣvāse tava putrā mahārathāḥ
c babhūvur āśvastamukhā viṣaṇṇā gatacetasaḥ
a avāṅmukhāḥ śastrabhṛtaḥ sarva eva viśāṃ pate
c aprekṣamāṇāḥ śokārtā nābhyabhāṣan parasparam
a tān dṛṣṭvā vyathitākārān sainyāni tava bhārata
c ūrdhvam evābhyavekṣanta duḥkhatrastāny anekaśaḥ
a śastrāṇy eṣāṃ ca rājendra śoṇitāktāny aśeṣataḥ
c prābhraśyanta karāgrebhyo dṛṣṭvā droṇaṃ nipātitam
a tāni baddhāny aniṣṭāni lambamānāni bhārata
c adṛśyanta mahārāja nakṣatrāṇi yathā divi
a tathārtaṃ stimitaṃ dṛṣṭvā gatasattvam iva sthitam
c svaṃ balaṃ tan mahārāja rājā duryodhano 'bravīt
a bhavatāṃ bāhuvīryaṃ hi samāśritya mayā yudhi
c pāṇḍaveyāḥ samāhūtā yuddhaṃ cedaṃ pravartitam
a tad idaṃ nihate droṇe viṣaṇṇam iva lakṣyate
c yudhyamānāś ca samare yodhā vadhyanti sarvataḥ
a jayo vāpi vadho vāpi yudhyamānasya saṃyuge
c bhavet kim atra citraṃ vai yudhyadhvaṃ sarvatomukhāḥ
a paśyadhvaṃ ca mahātmānaṃ karṇaṃ vaikartanaṃ yudhi
c pracarantaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ divyair astrair mahābalam
a yasya vai yudhi saṃtrāsāt kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥ
c nivartate sadāmarṣāt siṃhāt kṣudramṛgo yathā
a yena nāgāyutaprāṇo bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
c mānuṣeṇaiva yuddhena tām avasthāṃ praveśitaḥ
a yena divyāstravic chūro māyāvī sa ghaṭotkacaḥ
c amoghayā raṇe śaktyā nihato bhairavaṃ nadan
a tasya duṣpāravīryasya satyasaṃdhasya dhīmataḥ
c bāhvor draviṇam akṣayyam adya drakṣyatha saṃyuge
a droṇaputrasya vikrāntaṃ rādheyasyaiva cobhayoḥ
c pāṇḍupāñcālasainyeṣu drakṣyathāpi mahātmanoḥ
d paśyantu pāṇḍuputrās te viṣṇuvāsavayor iva
a sarva eva bhavantaś ca śūrāḥ prājñāḥ kulodgatāḥ
b pāṇḍuputrān raṇe hantuṃ sasainyān kim u saṃhatāḥ
c śīlavantaḥ kṛtāstrāś ca drakṣyathādya parasparam
a evam ukte mahārāja karṇo vaikartano nṛpaḥ
a   cakre senāpatiṃ tadā
a tava putro mahāvīryo bhrātṛbhiḥ sahito 'nagha
a senāpatyam athāsādya
c siṃhanādaṃ vinadyoccaiḥ prāyudhyata mahābalaḥ
a sa sṛñjayānāṃ sarveṣāṃ pāñcālānāṃ ca paśyatām
c kekayānāṃ videhānām akarot kadanaṃ mahat
a tasyeṣudhārāḥ śataśaḥ prādurāsañ śarāsanāt
c agre puṅkhe ca saṃsaktā yathā bhramarapaṅktayaḥ
a sa pīḍayitvā pāñcālān pāṇḍavāṃś ca tarasvinaḥ
c hatvā sahasraśo yodhān arjunena nipātitaḥ
d śibirād dhastinapuraṃ prāpya bhārata saṃjayaḥ
d praviveśa mahāprājño dhṛtarāṣṭraniveśanam
d śokenopahataḥ sūto vihvalo bhṛśaduḥkhitaḥ
d cintayan nidhanaṃ ghoraṃ sūtaputrasya pāṇḍavaiḥ
d antaḥpuraṃ praviśyaiva saṃjayo rājasattama
d aśrukaṇṭho bhṛśaṃ trasto rājānam upajagmivān
d upasthāya ca rājānaṃ viniḥśvasya ca sūtajaḥ
d saṃjayaḥ
d nātihṛṣṭamanā rājann idaṃ vacanam abravīt
d saṃjayo 'haṃ mahārāja namas te bharatarṣabha
d hato vaikartanaḥ karṇaḥ kṛtvā karma suduṣkaram
d cedikāśikarūśānāṃ matsyānāṃ somakaiḥ saha
d kṛtvāsau kadanaṃ śete vātanunna iva drumaḥ
d goṣṭhamadhye ṛṣabha iva govrajaiḥ parivāritaḥ
d vyālena nihato yadvat tathāsau nihataḥ paraiḥ
d nirāśān pāṇḍavān kṛtvā jaye rājan sasātyakān
d pāñcālānāṃ rathāṃś caiva vinihatya sahasraśaḥ
d hatvā śūrān maheṣvāsān vidrāvya ca diśo daśa
d hato vaikartanaḥ karṇaḥ pāṇḍavena kirīṭinā
d vairasya gatam ānṛṇyaṃ durgamasya durātmabhiḥ
d hatvā karṇaṃ mahārāja viśalyaḥ pāṇḍavo 'bhavat
d śoṣaṇaṃ sāgarāṇāṃ vā pātanaṃ śaśisūryayoḥ
d pṛthivyā dāraṇaṃ yādṛk tādṛk karṇasya pātanam
d yodhāś ca bahavo rājan hatās tatra jayaiṣiṇaḥ
d rājāno rājaputrāś ca śūrāḥ parighabāhavaḥ
d rathaughāś ca naraughāś ca hatā rājan sahasraśaḥ
d vāraṇā nihatās tatra vājinaś ca mahāhave
d kṣatriyāś ca mahārāja senayor ubhayor hatāḥ
d parasparam avekṣyātra parasparakṛtāgasaḥ
d kiṃciccheṣān parān kṛtvā tīrtvā pāṇḍavavāhinīm
d pārthavelāṃ samāsādya hato vaikartano vṛṣā
d jayāśā dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ vairasya ca mukhaṃ nṛpa
d tīrṇaṃ tat pāṇḍavai rājan yat purā nāvabudhyase
d procyamānaṃ mahārāja bandhubhir hitabuddhibhiḥ
d tad idaṃ samanuprāptaṃ vyasanaṃ tvāṃ mahābhayam
d putrāṇāṃ rājyakāmena tvayā rājan hitaiṣiṇā
d caritāny ahitāny eva teṣāṃ te phalam āgatam
d hato duḥśāsano rājan yathoktaṃ pāṇḍavena tu
d pratijñā bhīmasenena nistīrṇā sā camūmukhe
d pītaṃ ca kṣatajaṃ tasya dhārtarāṣṭrasya sayuge
d pāṇḍavena mahārāja kṛtvā karma suduṣkaram
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a etac chrutvā mahārāja dhṛtarāṣṭro 'mbikāsutaḥ
c śokasyāntam apaśyan vai hataṃ matvā suyodhanam
e vihvalaḥ patito bhūmau naṣṭacetā iva dvipaḥ
a tasmin nipatite bhūmau vihvale rājasattame
c ārtanādo mahān āsīt strīṇāṃ bharatasattama
a sa śabdaḥ pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ pūrayām āsa sarvaśaḥ
c śokārṇave mahāghore nimagnā bharatastriyaḥ
d rurudur duḥkhaśokārtā bhṛśam udvignacetasaḥ
d netrāṇi vāriṇāpūrya saritaḥ sāgaraṃ yathā
a rājānaṃ ca samāsādya gāndhārī bharatarṣabha
c niḥsaṃjñā patitā bhūmau sarvāṇy antaḥpurāṇi ca
a tatas tāḥ saṃjayo rājan samāśvāsayad āturāḥ
c muhyamānāḥ subahuśo muñcantyo vāri netrajam
a samāśvastāḥ striyas tās tu vepamānā muhur muhuḥ
c kadalya iva vātena dhūyamānāḥ samantataḥ
a rājānaṃ viduraś cāpi prajñācakṣuṣam īśvaram
c āśvāsayām āsa tadā siñcaṃs toyena kauravam
a sa labdhvā śanakaiḥ saṃjñāṃ tāś ca dṛṣṭvā striyo nṛpa
c unmatta iva rājā sa sthitas tūṣṇīṃ viśāṃ pate
a tato dhyātvā ciraṃ kālaṃ niḥśvasaṃś ca punaḥ punaḥ
c svān putrān garhayām āsa bahu mene ca pāṇḍavān
a garhayitvātmano buddhiṃ śakuneḥ saubalasya ca
c dhyātvā ca suciraṃ kālaṃ vepamāno muhur muhuḥ
a saṃstabhya ca mano bhūyo rājā dhairyasamanvitaḥ
c punar gāvalgaṇiṃ sūtaṃ paryapṛcchata saṃjayam
a yat tvayā kathitaṃ vākyaṃ śrutaṃ saṃjaya tan mayā
c kaccid duryodhanaḥ sūta na gato vai yamakṣayam
d jaye nirāśaḥ putro me satataṃ jayakāmukaḥ
d brūyā nirāśaḥ satataṃ putrāṇāṃ śivakāmukaḥ
e brūhi saṃjaya tattvena punar uktāṃ kathām imām
a evam ukto 'bravīt sūto rājānaṃ janamejaya
c hato vaikartano rājan saha putrair mahārathaiḥ
e bhrātṛbhiś ca maheṣvāsaiḥ sūtaputrais tanutyajaiḥ
a duḥśāsanaś ca nihataḥ pāṇḍavena yaśasvinā
c pītaṃ ca rudhiraṃ kopād bhīmasenena saṃyuge
d etac chrutvā mahārāja dhṛtarāṣṭro 'mbikāsutaḥ
d dahyamāno 'bravīt sūtaṃ muhūrtaṃ tiṣṭha saṃjaya
d vyākulaṃ me manas tāta mā tāvat kiṃ cid ucyatām
d rājāpi nābravīt kiṃ cit saṃjayo viduras tathā
d tūṣṇīṃ bhūtas tathā so 'tha babhūva jagatīpatiḥ
 janamejayaḥ
 śrutvā karṇaṃ hataṃ yuddhe putrāṃś caiva palāyinaḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭro nṛpaśreṣṭho dvijaśreṣṭha kim abravīt
 prāptavān paramaṃ duḥkhaṃ putravyasanajaṃ mahat
 kāle yad uktavāṃs tasmiṃs tan mamācakṣva tattvataḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a etac chrutvā mahārāja dhṛtarāṣṭro 'mbikāsutaḥ
c abravīt saṃjayaṃ sūtaṃ śokavyākulacetanaḥ
a duṣpraṇītena me tāta manasābhiplutātmanaḥ
c hataṃ vaikartanaṃ śrutvā śoko marmāṇi kṛntati
a kṛtāstraparamāḥ śalye duḥkhapāraṃ titīrṣavaḥ
c kurūṇāṃ sṛñjayānāṃ ca ke nu jīvanti ke mṛtāḥ
d etan me sarvam ācakṣva kuśalo hy asi saṃjaya
 saṃjaya uvāca
a hataḥ śāṃtanavo rājan durādharṣaḥ pratāpavān
c hatvā pāṇḍavayodhānām arbudaṃ daśabhir dinaiḥ
a tato droṇo maheṣvāsaḥ pāñcālānāṃ rathavrajān
c nihatya yudhi durdharṣaḥ paścād rukmaratho hataḥ
a hataśiṣṭasya bhīṣmeṇa droṇena ca mahātmanā
c ardhaṃ nihatya sainyasya karṇo vaikartano hataḥ
a viviṃśatir mahārāja rājaputro mahābalaḥ
c ānartayodhāñ śataśo nihatya nihato raṇe
a atha putro vikarṇas te kṣatravratam anusmaran
c kṣīṇavāhāyudhaḥ śūraḥ sthito 'bhimukhataḥ parān
a ghorarūpān parikleśān duryodhanakṛtān bahūn
c pratijñāṃ smaratā caiva bhīmasenena pātitaḥ
a vindānuvindāv āvantyau rājaputrau mahābalau
c kṛtvā nasukaraṃ karma gatau vaivasvatakṣayam
a sindhurāṣṭramukhānīha daśa rāṣṭrāṇi yasya vai
c vaśe tiṣṭhanti vīrasya yaḥ sthitas tava śāsane
a akṣauhiṇīr daśaikāṃ ca nirjitya niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c arjunena hato rājan mahāvīryo jayadrathaḥ
a tathā duryodhanasutas tarasvī yuddhadurmadaḥ
c vartamānaḥ pituḥ śāstre saubhadreṇa nipātitaḥ
a tathā dauḥśāsanir vīro bāhuśālī raṇotkaṭaḥ
c draupadeyena vikramya gamito yamasādanam
a kirātānām adhipatiḥ sāgarānūpavāsinām
c devarājasya dharmātmā priyo bahumataḥ sakhā
a bhagadatto mahīpālaḥ kṣatradharmarataḥ sadā
c dhanaṃjayena vikramya gamito yamasādanam
a tathā kauravadāyādaḥ saumadattir mahāyaśāḥ
c hato bhūriśravā rājañ śūraḥ sātyakinā yudhi
a śrutāyur api cāmbaṣṭhaḥ kṣatriyāṇāṃ dhanurdharaḥ
c carann abhītavat saṃkhye nihataḥ savyasācinā
a tava putraḥ sadā saṃkhye kṛtāstro yuddhadurmadaḥ
c duḥśāsano mahārāja bhīmasenena pātitaḥ
a yasya rājan gajānīkaṃ bahusāhasram adbhutam
c sudakṣiṇaḥ sa saṃgrāme nihataḥ savyasācinā
a kosalānām adhipatir hatvā bahuśatān parān
c saubhadreṇa hi vikramya gamito yamasādanam
a bahuśo yodhayitvā ca bhīmasenaṃ mahārathaḥ
c citrasenas tava suto bhīmasenena pātitaḥ
a madrarājātmajaḥ śūraḥ pareṣāṃ bhayavardhanaḥ
c asicarmadharaḥ śrīmān saubhadreṇa nipātitaḥ
a samaḥ karṇasya samare yaḥ sa karṇasya paśyataḥ
c vṛṣaseno mahātejāḥ śīghrāstraḥ kṛtaniścayaḥ
a abhimanyor vadhaṃ smṛtvā pratijñām api cātmanaḥ
c dhanaṃjayena vikramya gamito yamasādanam
a nityaprasaktavairo yaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ
c viśrāvya vairaṃ pārthena śrutāyuḥ sa nipātitaḥ
a śalyaputras tu vikrāntaḥ sahadevena māriṣa
c hato rukmaratho rājan bhrātā mātulajo yudhi
a rājā bhagīratho vṛddho bṛhatkṣatraś ca kekayaḥ
c parākramantau vikrāntau nihatau vīryavattarau
a bhagadattasuto rājan kṛtaprajño mahābalaḥ
c śyenavac caratā saṃkhye nakulena nipātitaḥ
a pitāmahas tava tathā bāhlikaḥ saha bāhlikaiḥ
c bhīmasenena vikramya gamito yamasādanam
a jayatsenas tathā rājañ jārāsaṃdhir mahābalaḥ
c māgadho nihataḥ saṃkhye saubhadreṇa mahātmanā
d asicarmadharaḥ śūraḥ pareṣāṃ bhayavardhanaḥ
d agnicakravad āghūrṇan somadatto nipātitaḥ
a putras te durmukho rājan duḥsahaś ca mahārathaḥ
c gadayā bhīmasenena nihatau śūramāninau
a durmarṣaṇo durviṣaho durjayaś ca mahārathaḥ
c kṛtvā nasukaraṃ karma gatā vaivasvatakṣayam
d ubhau kaliṅgavṛṣabhau bhrātarau yuddhadurmadau
d kṛtvā nasukaraṃ karma gatau vaivasvatakṣayam
a sacivo vṛṣavarmā te sūtaḥ paramavīryavān
c bhīmasenena vikramya gamito yamasādanam
a nāgāyutabalo rājā nāgāyutabalo mahān
c sagaṇaḥ pāṇḍuputreṇa nihataḥ savyasācinā
a vasātayo mahārāja dvisāhasrāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
c śūrasenāś ca vikrāntāḥ sarve yudhi nipātitāḥ
a abhīṣāhāḥ kavacinaḥ praharanto madotkaṭāḥ
c śibayaś ca rathodārāḥ kaliṅgasahitā hatāḥ
a gokule nityasaṃvṛddhā yuddhe paramakovidāḥ
b te 'pāvṛttakavīrāś ca nihatāḥ savyasācinā
c śreṇayo bahusāhasrāḥ saṃśaptakagaṇāś ca ye
e te sarve pārtham āsādya gatā vaivasvatakṣayam
a syālau tava mahārāja rājānau vṛṣakācalau
c tvadarthe saṃparākrāntau nihatau savyasācinā
a ugrakarmā maheṣvāso nāmataḥ karmatas tathā
c śālvarājo mahārāja bhīmasenena pātitaḥ
a oghavāṃś ca mahārāja bṛhantaḥ sahito raṇe
c parākramantau mitrārthe gatau vaivasvatakṣayam
a tathaiva rathināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ kṣemadhūrtir viśāṃ pate
c nihato gadayā rājan bhīmasenena saṃyuge
a tathā rājā maheṣvāso jalasaṃdho mahābalaḥ
c sumahat kadanaṃ kṛtvā hataḥ sātyakinā raṇe
a alāyudho rākṣasendraḥ kharabandhurayānagaḥ
c ghaṭotkacena vikramya gamito yamasādanam
d vikrāntā balavantaś ca bhrātaraḥ saha bhārata
a rādheyāḥ sūtaputrāś ca bhrātaraś ca mahārathāḥ
c kekayāḥ sarvaśaś cāpi nihatāḥ savyasācinā
d ripūṇāṃ kadanaṃ kṛtvā gatā vaivasvatakṣayam
a mālavā madrakāś caiva draviḍāś cogravikramāḥ
c yaudheyāś ca lalitthāś ca kṣudrakāś cāpy uśīnarāḥ
a māvellakās tuṇḍikerāḥ sāvitrīputrakāñcalāḥ
c prācyodīcyāḥ pratīcyāś ca dākṣiṇātyāś ca māriṣa
a pattīnāṃ nihatāḥ saṃghā hayānām ayutāni ca
c rathavrajāś ca nihatā hatāś ca varavāraṇāḥ
a sadhvajāḥ sāyudhāḥ śūrāḥ savarmāmbarabhūṣaṇāḥ
c kālena mahatā yattāḥ kule ye ca vivardhitāḥ
a te hatāḥ samare rājan pārthenākliṣṭakarmaṇā
c anye tathāmitabalāḥ parasparavadhaiṣiṇaḥ
d nihatāḥ samare śūrāḥ parasparasamāgame
a ete cānye ca bahavo rājānaḥ sagaṇā raṇe
c hatāḥ sahasraśo rājan yan māṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi
e evam eṣa kṣayo vṛttaḥ karṇārjunasamāgame
a mahendreṇa yathā vṛtro yathā rāmeṇa rāvaṇaḥ
c yathā kṛṣṇena nihato muro raṇanipātitaḥ
e kārtavīryaś ca rāmeṇa bhārgaveṇa hato yathā
a sajñātibāndhavaḥ śūraḥ samare yuddhadurmadaḥ
c raṇe kṛtvā mahāyuddhaṃ ghoraṃ trailokyaviśrutam
d yathā skandena mahiṣo yathā rudreṇa cāndhakaḥ
a tathārjunena nihato dvairathe yuddhadurmadaḥ
c sāmātyabāndhavo rājan karṇaḥ praharatāṃ varaḥ
a jayāśā dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ vairasya ca mukhaṃ yataḥ
c tīrṇaṃ tat pāṇḍavai rājan yat purā nāvabudhyase
a ucyamāno mahārāja bandhubhir hitakāṅkṣibhiḥ
b na kṛtaṃ ca tvayā pūrvaṃ daivena vidhinā balāt
c tad idaṃ samanuprāptaṃ vyasanaṃ tvāṃ mahātyayam
a putrāṇāṃ rājyakāmānāṃ tvayā rājan hitaiṣiṇā
c ahitānīva cīrṇāni teṣāṃ te phalam āgatam
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a ākhyātā māmakās tāta nihatā yudhi pāṇḍavaiḥ
c nihatān pāṇḍaveyānāṃ māmakair brūhi saṃjaya
 saṃjaya uvāca
a kuntayo yudhi vikrāntā mahāsattvā mahābalāḥ
c sānubandhāḥ sahāmātyā bhīṣmeṇa yudhi pātitāḥ
d naraś cāśvāḥ sanāgāś ca rathāś ca śataśo narāḥ
d nārāyaṇā ballavāś ca rāmāś ca śataśo 'pare
d anuraktāś ca vijaye bhīṣmeṇa nihatā raṇe
a samaḥ kirīṭinā saṃkhye vīryeṇa ca balena ca
c satyajit satyasaṃdhena droṇena nihato raṇe
d pāñcālāś ca maheṣvāsāḥ prāyo rājann amarṣitāḥ
d droṇena saha saṃgamya gatā vaivasvatakṣayam
a tathā virāṭadrupadau vṛddhau sahasutau nṛpau
c parākramantau mitrārthe droṇena nihatau raṇe
a yo bāla eva samare saṃmitaḥ savyasācinā
c keśavena ca durdharṣo baladevena cābhibhūḥ
a sa eṣa kadanaṃ kṛtvā mahad raṇaviśāradaḥ
c parivārya mahāmātraiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ paramakai rathaiḥ
e aśaknuvadbhir bībhatsum abhimanyur nipātitaḥ
a taṃ kṛtaṃ virathaṃ vīraṃ kṣatradharme vyavasthitam
c dauḥśāsanir mahārāja saubhadraṃ hatavān raṇe
d paṭaccaranihantā ca mahatyā senayā vṛtaḥ
d ambaṣṭhasahitaḥ śrīmān mitrahetoḥ parākramī
d āsādya lakṣmaṇaṃ vīraṃ duryodhanasutaṃ raṇe
d sumahat kadanaṃ kṛtvā gato vaivasvatakṣayam
a bṛhantas tu maheṣvāsaḥ kṛtāstro yuddhadurmadaḥ
c duḥśāsanena vikramya gamito yamasādanam
a maṇimān daṇḍadhāraś ca rājānau yuddhadurmadau
c parākramantau mitrārthe droṇena vinipātitau
a aṃśumān bhojarājas tu sahasainyo mahārathaḥ
c bhāradvājena vikramya gamito yamasādanam
d sāmudraś citrasenaś ca saha putreṇa bhārata
d samudrasenena balād gamito yamasādanam
d anūpavāsī nīlaś ca vyāghradattaś ca vīryavān
d aśvatthāmnā mahārāja gamito yamasādanam
a citrāyudhaś citrayodhī kṛtvā tau kadanaṃ mahat
c citramārgeṇa vikramya karṇena nihatau yudhi
a vṛkodarasamo yuddhe dṛḍhaḥ kekayajo yudhi
c kekayenaiva vikramya bhrātrā bhrātā nipātitaḥ
a janamejayo gadāyodhī pārvatīyaḥ pratāpavān
c durmukhena mahārāja tava putreṇa pātitaḥ
a rocamānau naravyāghrau rocamānau grahāv iva
c droṇena yugapad rājan divaṃ saṃpreṣitau śaraiḥ
a nṛpāś ca pratiyudhyantaḥ parākrāntā viśāṃ pate
c kṛtvā nasukaraṃ karma gatā vaivasvatakṣayam
a purujit kuntibhojaś ca mātulaḥ savyasācinaḥ
c saṃgrāmanirjitāṃl lokān gamito droṇasāyakaiḥ
a abhibhūḥ kāśirājaś ca kāśikair bahubhir vṛtaḥ
c vasudānasya putreṇa nyāsito deham āhave
a amitaujā yudhāmanyur uttamaujāś ca vīryavān
b amitaujā jayatseno jayānīkaś ca vīryavān
b amitaujā bṛhatkṣetraḥ kṣatradevaś ca pārthivaḥ
b lakṣmaṇena hatau rājaṃs tava pautreṇa māriṣa
b bṛhatkṣatro maheṣvāsaḥ kṣatradevaś ca pārthivaḥ
c nihatya śataśaḥ śūrān parair vinihatau raṇe
a kṣatradharmā ca pāñcālyaḥ kṣatravarmā ca māriṣa
c droṇena parameṣvāsau gamitau yamasādanam
a śikhaṇḍitanayo yuddhe kṣatradevo yudhāṃ patiḥ
c lakṣmaṇena hato rājaṃs tava pautreṇa bhārata
a sucitraś citradharmā ca pitāputrau mahārathau
c pracarantau mahāvīryau droṇena nihatau raṇe
a vārdhakṣemir mahārāja kṛtvā kadanam āhave
b āyudhakṣayam āsādya praśāntiṃ paramāṃ gataḥ
b purujit paramo rājā kṛtvā kadanam āhave
b senābindur nṛpaśreṣṭhaḥ śātravān pratapan yudhi
c bāhlikena mahārāja kauraveṇa nipātitaḥ
a dhṛṣṭaketur mahārāja cedīnāṃ pravaro rathaḥ
c kṛtvā nasukaraṃ karma gato vaivasvatakṣayam
a tathā satyadhṛtis tāta kṛtvā kadanam āhave
c pāṇḍavārthe parākrānto gamito yamasādanam
d senābinduḥ kuruśreṣṭhaḥ kṛtvā kadanam āhave
a putras tu śiśupālasya suketuḥ pṛthivīpate
c nihatya śātravān saṃkhye droṇena nihato yudhi
d virāṭaputraḥ śaṅkhaś ca uttaraś ca mahārathaḥ
d kurvantau sumahat karma gatau vaivasvatakṣayam
a tathā satyadhṛtir vīro madirāśvaś ca vīryavān
c sūryadattaś ca vikrānto nihato droṇasāyakaiḥ
d matsyād avarajaḥ śrīmāñ śatānīko nipātitaḥ
a śreṇimāṃś ca mahārāja yudhyamānaḥ parākramī
c kṛtvā nasukaraṃ karma gato vaivasvatakṣayam
a tathaiva yudhi vikrānto māgadhaḥ paravīrahā
b māgadhaḥ paramāstrajño gamito yamasādanam
c bhīṣmeṇa nihato rājan yudhyamānaḥ parākramī
a vasudānaś ca kadanaṃ kurvāṇo 'tīva saṃyuge
c bhāradvājena vikramya gamito yamasādanam
d pāṇḍyarājaś ca vikrānto balavān bāhuśālinā
d aśvatthāmnā hatas tatra gamito vai yamakṣayam
a ete cānye ca bahavaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥ
c hatā droṇena vikramya yan māṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a hatapravīre sainye 'smin māmake vadatāṃ vara
c ahatāñ śaṃsa me sūta ye 'tra jīvanti ke cana
a eteṣu nihateṣv adya ye tvayā parikīrtitāḥ
c ahatān manyase yāṃs tvaṃ te 'pi svargajito matāḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a yasmin mahāstrāṇi samarpitāni
citrāṇi śubhrāṇi caturvidhāni
c divyāni rājan nihitāni caiva
droṇena vīradvijasattamena
a mahārathaḥ kṛtimān kṣiprahasto
dṛḍhāyudho dṛḍhamuṣṭir dṛḍheṣuḥ
c sa vīryavān droṇaputras tarasvī
vyavasthito yoddhukāmas tvadarthe
a ānartavāsī hṛdikātmajo 'sau
mahārathaḥ sātvatānāṃ variṣṭhaḥ
c svayaṃ bhojaḥ kṛtavarmā kṛtāstro
vyavasthito yoddhukāmas tvadarthe
a śāradvato gautamaś cāpi rājan
mahābalo bahucitrāstrayodhī
c dhanuś citraṃ sumahad bhārasāhaṃ
vyavasthito yotsyamānaḥ pragṛhya
d mahābalaḥ kekayarājaputraḥ
d sadaśvayuktaṃ ca patākinaṃ ca
d rathāgryam āruhya kurupravīra
d vyavasthito yoddhukāmas tvadarthe
a ārtāyaniḥ samare duṣprakampyaḥ
senāgraṇīḥ prathamas tāvakānām
c svasreyāṃs tān pāṇḍaveyān visṛjya
satyāṃ vācaṃ tāṃ cikīrṣus tarasvī
a tejovadhaṃ sūtaputrasya saṃkhye
pratiśrutvājātaśatroḥ purastāt
c durādharṣaḥ śakrasamānavīryaḥ
śalyaḥ sthito yoddhukāmas tvadarthe
a ājāneyaiḥ saindhavaiḥ pārvatīyair
nadījakāmbojavanāyubāhlikaiḥ
c gāndhārarājaḥ svabalena yukto
vyavasthito yoddhukāmas tvadarthe
d gāndhārarājaḥ sasutaś ca rājan
d durdyūtadevī kalahapriyaś ca
d gāndhāramukhyair yavanaiś ca rājan
d vyavasthito yoddhukāmas tvadarthe
a tathā sutas te jvalanārkavarṇaṃ
rathaṃ samāsthāya kurupravīra
c vyavasthitaḥ kurumitro narendra
vyabhre sūryo bhrājamāno yathā vai
a duryodhano nāgakulasya madhye
mahāvīryaḥ saha sainyapravīraiḥ
c rathena jāmbūnadabhūṣaṇena
vyavasthitaḥ samare yoddhukāmaḥ
a sa rājamadhye puruṣapravīro
rarāja jāmbūnadacitravarmā
c padmaprabho vahnir ivālpadhūmo
meghāntare sūrya iva prakāśaḥ
a tathā suṣeṇo 'py asicarmapāṇis
tavātmajaḥ satyasenaś ca vīraḥ
c vyavasthitau citrasenena sārdhaṃ
hṛṣṭātmānau samare yoddhukāmau
a hrīniṣedhā bharatā rājaputrāś
citrāyudhaḥ śrutakarmā jayaś ca
a   ugrāyudhaḥ kṣaṇabhojī sudarśaḥ
a jārāsaṃdhiḥ prathamaś cādṛḍhaś ca
c śalaś ca satyavrataduḥśalau ca
vyavasthitā balino yoddhukāmāḥ
a kaitavyānām adhipaḥ śūramānī
raṇe raṇe śatruhā rājaputraḥ
c patrī hayī nāgarathaprayāyī
vyavasthito yoddhukāmas tvadarthe
a vīraḥ śrutāyuś ca śrutāyudhaś ca
citrāṅgadaś citravarmā sa vīraḥ
c vyavasthitā ye tu sainye narāgryāḥ
prahāriṇo māninaḥ satyasaṃdhāḥ
a karṇātmajaḥ satyaseno mahātmā
vyavasthitaḥ samare yoddhukāmaḥ
c athāparau karṇasutau varārhau
vyavasthitau laghuhastau narendra
e balaṃ mahad durbhidam alpadhairyaiḥ
samāśritau yotsyamānau tvadarthe
a etaiś ca mukhyair aparaiś ca rājan
yodhapravīrair amitaprabhāvaiḥ
c vyavasthito nāgakulasya madhye
yathā mahendraḥ kururājo jayāya
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a ākhyātā jīvamānā ye parebhyo 'nye yathātatham
c itīdam abhigacchāmi vyaktam arthābhipattitaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evaṃ bruvann eva tadā dhṛtarāṣṭro 'mbikāsutaḥ
c hatapravīraṃ vidhvastaṃ kiṃciccheṣaṃ svakaṃ balam
e śrutvā vyāmoham agamac chokavyākulitendriyaḥ
a muhyamāno 'bravīc cāpi muhūrtaṃ tiṣṭha saṃjaya
c vyākulaṃ me manas tāta śrutvā sumahad apriyam
d mano muhyati cāṅgāni na ca śaknomi dhāritum
d ity evam uktvā vacanaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭro 'mbikāsutaḥ
e naṣṭacittas tataḥ so 'tha babhūva jagatīpatiḥ
 janamejaya uvāca
a śrutvā karṇaṃ hataṃ yuddhe putrāṃś caivāpalāyinaḥ
c narendraḥ kiṃ cid āśvasto dvijaśreṣṭha kim abravīt
a prāptavān paramaṃ duḥkhaṃ putravyasanajaṃ mahat
c tasmin yad uktavān kāle tan mamācakṣva pṛcchataḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a śrutvā karṇasya nidhanam aśraddheyam ivādbhutam
c bhūtasaṃmohanaṃ bhīmaṃ meroḥ paryasanaṃ yathā
a cittamoham ivāyuktaṃ bhārgavasya mahāmateḥ
c parājayam ivendrasya dviṣadbhyo bhīmakarmaṇaḥ
a divaḥ prapatanaṃ bhānor urvyām iva mahādyuteḥ
c saṃśoṣaṇam ivācintyaṃ samudrasyākṣayāmbhasaḥ
a mahīviyaddigīśānāṃ sarvanāśam ivādbhutam
c karmaṇor iva vaiphalyam ubhayoḥ puṇyapāpayoḥ
a saṃcintya nipuṇaṃ buddhyā dhṛtarāṣṭro janeśvaraḥ
c nedam astīti saṃcintya karṇasya nidhanaṃ prati
a prāṇinām etad ātmatvāt syād apīti vināśanam
c śokāgninā dahyamāno dhamyamāna ivāśayaḥ
a vidhvastātmā śvasan dīno hā hety uktvā suduḥkhitaḥ
c vilalāpa mahārāja dhṛtarāṣṭro 'mbikāsutaḥ
d uvāca ca punar vākyaṃ saṃśayaṃ bhṛśavihvalaḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a saṃjayādhiratho vīraḥ siṃhadviradavikramaḥ
c vṛṣam apratimaskandho vṛṣabhākṣagatisvanaḥ
a vṛṣabho vṛṣabhasyeva yo yuddhe na nivartate
c śatror api mahendrasya vajrasaṃhanano yuvā
a yasya jyātalaśabdena śaravṛṣṭiraveṇa ca
c rathāśvanaramātaṅgā nāvatiṣṭhanti saṃyuge
a yam āśritya mahābāhuṃ dviṣatsaṃghaghnam acyutam
c duryodhano 'karod vairaṃ pāṇḍuputrair mahābalaiḥ
a sa kathaṃ rathināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ karṇaḥ pārthena saṃyuge
c nihataḥ puruṣavyāghraḥ prasahyāsahyavikramaḥ
a yo nāmanyata vai nityam acyutaṃ na dhanaṃjayam
c na vṛṣṇīn api tān anyān svabāhubalam āśritaḥ
a śārṅgagāṇḍīvadhanvānau sahitāv aparājitau
c ahaṃ divyād rathād ekaḥ pātayiṣyāmi saṃyuge
a iti yaḥ satataṃ mandam avocal lobhamohitam
c duryodhanam apādīnaṃ rājyakāmukam āturam
a yaś cājaiṣīd atibalān amitrān api durjayān
c gāndhārān madrakān matsyāṃs trigartāṃs taṅgaṇāñ śakān
a pāñcālāṃś ca videhāṃś ca kuṇindān kāśikosalān
c suhmān aṅgāṃś ca puṇḍrāṃś ca niṣādān vaṅgakīcakān
a vatsān kaliṅgāṃs taralān aśmakān ṛṣikāṃs tathā
c yo jitvā samare vīraś cakre balibhṛtaḥ purā
d śabarān parahūṇāṃś ca prāṅmukhān saralān api
d mleccharāṣṭrāṃdhipāṃś caiva durgānāṭavikāṃs tathā
d jitvaitān samare vīraḥ sutīkṣṇaiḥ kaṅkapatribhiḥ
d karam āhārayām āsa jitvā sarvān arīṃs tathā
d śaravrātaiḥ suniśitaiḥ sutīkṣṇaiḥ kaṅkapatribhiḥ
d duryodhanasya vṛddhyarthaṃ vartate yo jayāya ca
d senāgopaś ca sa kathaṃ śatrubhiḥ paramāstravit
d ghātitaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ śūraiḥ samarthair vīryaśālibhiḥ
d vṛṣo mahendro deveṣu vṛṣaḥ karṇo nareṣv api
d tṛtīyam anyaṃ lokeṣu vṛṣaṃ naivānuśuśrumaḥ
d divyāstravin mahātejāḥ karṇo vaikartano vṛṣaḥ
a uccaiḥśravā varo 'śvānāṃ rājñāṃ vaiśravaṇo varaḥ
c varo mahendro devānāṃ karṇaḥ praharatāṃ varaḥ
d yojitaḥ pārthivaiḥ śūraiḥ samarthair vīryaśālibhiḥ
d duryodhanasya vṛddhyarthaṃ kṛtsnām urvīm athājayat
a yaṃ labdhvā māgadho rājā sāntvamānārthagauravaiḥ
c arautsīt pārthivaṃ kṣatram ṛte kauravayādavān
a taṃ śrutvā nihataṃ karṇaṃ dvairathe savyasācinā
b śokārṇave nimagno 'smi samudre bhinnanaur iva
b nṛvṛṣaṃ nihataṃ śrutvā dvairathe rathināṃ varam
c śokārṇave nimagno 'ham aplavaḥ sāgare yathā
a īdṛśair yady ahaṃ duḥkhair na vinaśyāmi saṃjaya
c vajrād dṛḍhataraṃ manye hṛdayaṃ mama durbhidam
a jñātisaṃbandhimitrāṇām imaṃ śrutvā parājayam
c ko mad anyaḥ pumāṃl loke na jahyāt sūta jīvitam
a viṣam agniṃ prapātaṃ vā parvatāgrād ahaṃ vṛṇe
b mahāprasthānagamanaṃ jalaṃ prāyopaveśanam
c na hi śakṣyāmi duḥkhāni soḍhuṃ kaṣṭāni saṃjaya
d cintayann eva sīdāmi mano me 'tīva muhyati
 saṃjaya uvāca
a śriyā kulena yaśasā tapasā ca śrutena ca
c tvām adya santo manyante yayātim iva nāhuṣam
a śrute maharṣipratimaḥ kṛtakṛtyo 'si pārthiva
c paryavasthāpayātmānaṃ mā viṣāde manaḥ kṛthāḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a daivam eva paraṃ manye dhik pauruṣam anarthakam
c yatra rāmapratīkāśaḥ karṇo 'hanyata saṃyuge
a hatvā yudhiṣṭhirānīkaṃ pāñcālānāṃ rathavrajān
c pratāpya śaravarṣeṇa diśaḥ sarvā mahārathaḥ
a mohayitvā raṇe pārthān vajrahasta ivāsurān
c sa kathaṃ nihataḥ śete vātarugṇa iva drumaḥ
a śokasyāntaṃ na paśyāmi samudrasyeva viplukāḥ
c cintā me vardhate tīvrā mumūrṣā cāpi jāyate
a karṇasya nidhanaṃ śrutvā vijayaṃ phalgunasya ca
c aśraddheyam ahaṃ manye vadhaṃ karṇasya saṃjaya
a vajrasāramayaṃ nūnaṃ hṛdayaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ mama
c yac chrutvā puruṣavyāghraṃ hataṃ karṇaṃ na dīryate
a āyur nūnaṃ sudīrghaṃ me vihitaṃ daivataiḥ purā
c yatra karṇaṃ hataṃ śrutvā jīvāmīha suduḥkhitaḥ
a dhig jīvitam idaṃ me 'dya suhṛd dhīnasya saṃjaya
c adya cāhaṃ daśām etāṃ gataḥ saṃjaya garhitām
e kṛpaṇaṃ vartayiṣyāmi śocyaḥ sarvasya mandadhīḥ
a aham eva purā bhūtvā sarvalokasya satkṛtaḥ
c paribhūtaḥ kathaṃ sūta punaḥ śakṣyāmi jīvitum
e duḥkhāt suduḥkhaṃ vyasanaṃ prāptavān asmi saṃjaya
a tasmād bhīṣmavadhe caiva droṇasya ca mahātmanaḥ
c nātra śeṣaṃ prapaśyāmi sūtaputre hate yudhi
a sa hi pāraṃ mahān āsīt putrāṇāṃ mama saṃjaya
c yuddhe vinihataḥ śūro visṛjan sāyakān bahūn
a ko hi me jīvitenārthas tam ṛte puruṣarṣabham
c rathād atiratho nūnam apatat sāyakārditaḥ
a parvatasyeva śikharaṃ vajrapātavidāritam
c śayīta pṛthivīṃ nūnaṃ śobhayan rudhirokṣitaḥ
e mātaṅga iva mattena mātaṅgena nipātitaḥ
a yad balaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ yato bhayam
c so 'rjunena hataḥ karṇaḥ pratimānaṃ dhanuṣmatām
a sa hi vīro maheṣvāsaḥ putrāṇām abhayaṃkaraḥ
c śete vinihato vīraḥ śakreṇeva yathā balaḥ
a paṅgor ivādhvagamanaṃ daridrasyeva kāmitam
c duryodhanasya cākūtaṃ tṛṣitasyeva piplukāḥ
a anyathā cintitaṃ kāryam anyathā tat tu jāyate
c aho nu balavad daivaṃ kālaś ca duratikramaḥ
a palāyamānaḥ kṛpaṇaṃ dīnātmā dīnapauruṣaḥ
c kaccin na nihataḥ sūta putro duḥśāsano mama
a kaccin na nīcācaritaṃ kṛtavāṃs tāta saṃyuge
b putro duryodhanaḥ saṃkhye nihato mama saṃjaya
c kaccin na nihataḥ śūro yathā na kṣatriyā hatāḥ
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d ity evaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭro 'tha vilapya bahu duḥkhitaḥ
d provāca saṃjayaṃ bhūyaḥ śokavyākulalocanaḥ
d yo 'jayat savarkāmbojān ambaṣṭhān kekayaiḥ saha
d gāndhārāṃś ca videhāṃś ca jitvā kāryārtham āhave
a yudhiṣṭhirasya vacanaṃ mā yuddham iti sarvadā
c duryodhano nābhyagṛhṇān mūḍhaḥ pathyam ivauṣadham
a śaratalpe śayānena bhīṣmeṇa sumahātmanā
c pānīyaṃ yācitaḥ pārthaḥ so 'vidhyan medinītalam
a jalasya dhārāṃ vihitāṃ dṛṣṭvā tāṃ pāṇḍavena ha
c abravīt sa mahābāhus tāta saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥ
a praśamād dhi bhavec chāntir madantaṃ yuddham astu ca
c bhrātṛbhāvena pṛthivīṃ bhuṅkṣva pāṇḍusutaiḥ saha
a akurvan vacanaṃ tasya nūnaṃ śocati me sutaḥ
c tad idaṃ samanuprāptaṃ vacanaṃ dīrghadarśinaḥ
a ahaṃ tu nihatāmātyo hataputraś ca saṃjaya
c dyūtataḥ kṛcchram āpanno lūnapakṣa iva dvijaḥ
a yathā hi śakuniṃ gṛhya chittvā pakṣau ca saṃjaya
c visarjayanti saṃhṛṣṭāḥ krīḍamānāḥ kumārakāḥ
a chinnapakṣatayā tasya gamanaṃ nopapadyate
c tathāham api saṃprāpto lūnapakṣa iva dvijaḥ
a kṣīṇaḥ sarvārthahīnaś ca nirbandhur jñātivarjitaḥ
c kāṃ diśaṃ pratipatsyāmi dīnaḥ śatruvaśaṃ gataḥ
a duryodhanasya vṛddhyarthaṃ pṛthivīṃ yo 'jayat prabhuḥ
c sa jitaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ śūraiḥ samarthair vīryaśālibhiḥ
a tasmin hate maheṣvāse karṇe yudhi kirīṭinā
c ke vīrāḥ paryavartanta tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
a kaccin naikaḥ parityaktaḥ pāṇḍavair nihato raṇe
c uktaṃ tvayā purā vīra yathā vīrā nipātitāḥ
a bhīṣmam apratiyudhyantaṃ śikhaṇḍī sāyakottamaiḥ
c pātayām āsa samare sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varam
a tathā draupadinā droṇo nyastasarvāyudho yudhi
b dharmarājavacaḥ śrutvā aśvatthāmā hatas tv iti
c yuktayogo maheṣvāsaḥ śarair bahubhir ācitaḥ
e nihataḥ khaḍgam udyamya dhṛṣṭadyumnena saṃjaya
a antareṇa hatāv etau chalena ca viśeṣataḥ
c aśrauṣam aham etad vai bhīṣmadroṇau nipātitau
a bhīṣmadroṇau hi samare na hanyād vajrabhṛt svayam
c nyāyena yudhyamānau hi tad vai satyaṃ bravīmi te
a karṇaṃ tv asyantam astrāṇi divyāni ca bahūni ca
c katham indropamaṃ vīraṃ mṛtyur yuddhe samaspṛśat
a yasya vidyutprabhāṃ śaktiṃ divyāṃ kanakabhūṣaṇām
c prāyacchad dviṣatāṃ hantrīṃ kuṇḍalābhyāṃ puraṃdaraḥ
a yasya sarpamukho divyaḥ śaraḥ kanakabhūṣaṇaḥ
c aśeta nihataḥ patrī candaneṣv arisūdanaḥ
a bhīṣmadroṇamukhān vīrān yo 'vamanya mahārathān
c jāmadagnyān mahāghoraṃ brāhmam astram aśikṣata
a yaś ca droṇamukhān dṛṣṭvā vimukhān arditāñ śaraiḥ
c saubhadrasya mahābāhur vyadhamat kārmukaṃ śaraiḥ
a yaś ca nāgāyutaprāṇaṃ vātaraṃhasam acyutam
c virathaṃ bhrātaraṃ kṛtvā bhīmasenam upāhasat
a sahadevaṃ ca nirjitya śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c kṛpayā virathaṃ kṛtvā nāhanad dharmavittayā
a yaś ca māyāsahasrāṇi dhvaṃsayitvā raṇotkaṭam
c ghaṭotkacaṃ rākṣasendraṃ śakraśaktyābhijaghnivān
a etāni divasāny asya yuddhe bhīto dhanaṃjayaḥ
c nāgamad dvairathaṃ vīraḥ sa kathaṃ nihato raṇe
d saṃśaptakānāṃ yodhā ye āhvayanta sadānyataḥ
d etān hatvā haniṣyāmi paścād vaikartanaṃ raṇe
d iti vyapadiśan pārtho varjayan sūtajaṃ raṇe
d sa kathaṃ nihato vīraḥ pārthena paramāhave
a rathasaṅgo na cet tasya dhanur vā na vyaśīryata
c na ced astrāṇi nirṇeśuḥ sa kathaṃ nihataḥ paraiḥ
a ko hi śakto raṇe karṇaṃ vidhunvānaṃ mahad dhanuḥ
c vimuñcantaṃ śarān ghorān divyāny astrāṇi cāhave

a dhruvaṃ tasya dhanuś chinnaṃ ratho vāpi gato mahīm

a na hanyām arjunaṃ yāvat tāvat pādau na dhāvaye
c iti yasya mahāghoraṃ vratam āsīn mahātmanaḥ
a yasya bhīto vane nityaṃ dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c trayodaśa samā nidrāṃ na lebhe puruṣarṣabhaḥ
a yasya vīryavato vīryaṃ samāśritya mahātmanaḥ
c mama putraḥ sabhāṃ bhāryāṃ pāṇḍūnāṃ nītavān balāt

c dāsabhāryeti pāñcālīm abravīt kurusaṃsadi
d na santi patayaḥ kṛṣṇe sarve ṣaṇḍhatilaiḥ samāḥ
d upatiṣṭhasva bhartāram anyaṃ vā varavarṇini
d ity evaṃ yaḥ purā vāco rūkṣāḥ saṃśrāvayan ruṣā
d sabhāyāṃ sūtajaḥ kṛṣṇāṃ sa kathaṃ nihataḥ paraiḥ
d yadi bhīṣmo raṇaślāghī droṇo vā yudhi durmadaḥ
d na haniṣyati kaunteyān pakṣapātāt suyodhana

c svabāhubalam āśritya muhūrtam api saṃjaya
a tasya nāhaṃ vadhaṃ manye devair api savāsavaiḥ
c pratīpam upadhāvadbhiḥ kiṃ punas tāta pāṇḍavaiḥ
a na hi jyāṃ spṛśamānasya talatre cāpi gṛhṇataḥ
c pumān ādhiratheḥ kaś cit pramukhe sthātum arhati
a api syān medinī hīnā somasūryaprabhāṃśubhiḥ
c na vadhaḥ puruṣendrasya samareṣv apalāyinaḥ
a yadi mandaḥ sahāyena bhrātrā duḥśāsanena ca

a sa nūnam ṛṣabhaskandhaṃ dṛṣṭvā karṇaṃ nipātitam
c duḥśāsanaṃ ca nihataṃ manye śocati putrakaḥ
a hataṃ vaikartanaṃ śrutvā dvairathe savyasācinā
c jayataḥ pāṇḍavān dṛṣṭvā kiṃ svid duryodhano 'bravīt
a durmarṣaṇaṃ hataṃ śrutvā vṛṣasenaṃ ca saṃyuge
c prabhagnaṃ ca balaṃ dṛṣṭvā vadhyamānaṃ mahārathaiḥ
a parāṅmukhāṃs tathā rājñaḥ palāyanaparāyaṇān
c vidrutān rathino dṛṣṭvā manye śocati putrakaḥ
c   kiṃ cid duryodhano 'bravīt
c viṣame śokaduḥkhābhyāṃ
a aneyaś cābhimānena bālabuddhir amarṣaṇaḥ
c hatotsāhaṃ balaṃ dṛṣṭvā kiṃ svid duryodhano 'bravīt
d svayaṃ vairaṃ mahat kṛtvā vāryamāṇaḥ suhṛdgaṇaiḥ
d pradhānahatabhūyiṣṭhe kiṃ svid duryodhano 'bravīt

c rudhiraṃ pīyamānena kiṃ svid duryodhano 'bravīt
a saha gāndhārarājena sabhāyāṃ yad abhāṣata
c karṇo 'rjunaṃ raṇe hantā hate tasmin kim abravīt
a dyūtaṃ kṛtvā purā hṛṣṭo vañcayitvā ca pāṇḍavān
c śakuniḥ saubalas tāta hate karṇe kim abravīt
a kṛtavarmā maheṣvāsaḥ sātvatānāṃ mahārathaḥ
c karṇaṃ vinihataṃ dṛṣṭvā hārdikyaḥ kim abhāṣata

c dhanurvedaṃ cikīrṣanto droṇaputrasya dhīmataḥ
a yuvā rūpeṇa saṃpanno darśanīyo mahāyaśāḥ
c aśvatthāmā hate karṇe kim abhāṣata saṃjaya
a ācāryatvaṃ dhanurvede gataḥ paramatattvavit
c kṛpaḥ śāradvatas tāta hate karṇe kim abravīt
a madrarājo maheṣvāsaḥ śalyaḥ samitiśobhanaḥ
c diṣṭaṃ tena hi tat sarvaṃ yathā karṇo nipātitaḥ
d kim abhāṣata sauvīro madrāṇām adhipo balī
d dṛṣṭvā vinihataṃ sarve yodhā vāraṇadurjayāḥ
a ye ca ke cana rājānaḥ pṛthivyāṃ yoddhum āgatāḥ
c vaikartanaṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā kim abhāṣanta saṃjaya
a karṇe tu nihate vīre rathavyāghre nararṣabhe
c kiṃ vo mukham anīkānām āsīt saṃjaya bhāgaśaḥ
a madrarājaḥ kathaṃ śalyo niyukto rathināṃ varaḥ
c vaikartanasya sārathye tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
a ke 'rakṣan dakṣiṇaṃ cakraṃ sūtaputrasya saṃyuge
c vāmaṃ cakraṃ rarakṣur vā ke vā vīrasya pṛṣṭhataḥ
a ke karṇaṃ vājahuḥ śūrāḥ ke kṣudrāḥ prādravan bhayāt
c kathaṃ ca vaḥ sametānāṃ hataḥ karṇo mahārathaḥ
a pāṇḍavāś ca kathaṃ śūrāḥ pratyudīyur mahāratham
c sṛjantaṃ śaravarṣāṇi vāridhārā ivāmbudam
a sa ca sarpamukho divyo maheṣupravaras tadā
c vyarthaḥ kathaṃ samabhavat tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
a māmakasyāsya sainyasya hṛtotsedhasya saṃjaya
c avaśeṣaṃ na paśyāmi kakude mṛdite sati

c bhīṣmadroṇau hatau śrutvā ko nv artho jīvitena me
a na mṛṣyāmi ca rādheyaṃ hatam āhavaśobhinam
c yasya bāhvor balaṃ tulyaṃ kuñjarāṇāṃ śataṃ śatam

 saṃjaya uvāca
a hate droṇe maheṣvāse tasminn ahani bhārata
c kṛte ca moghasaṃkalpe droṇaputre mahārathe
a dravamāṇe mahārāja kauravāṇāṃ bale tathā

a tam avasthitam ājñāya putras te bharatarṣabha

a svam anīkam avasthāpya bāhuvīrye vyavasthitaḥ
c yuddhvā ca suciraṃ kālaṃ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha bhārata
a labdhalakṣaiḥ parair hṛṣṭair vyāyacchadbhiś ciraṃ tadā
c saṃdhyākālaṃ samāsādya pratyāhāram akārayat
d niveśya ca balaṃ ghoraṃ kṣutpipāsābhayair yutam
d śrameṇa mahatā yuktaṃ tathā droṇavadhena ca
d dīnarūpā raṇe kṛtvā karma ghorāṃ ca śarvarīm
d niveśaṃ prāpya sā senā viśramya muditābhavat
a kṛtvāvahāraṃ sainyānāṃ praviśya śibiraṃ svakam
c kuravo ''tmahitaṃ mantraṃ mantrayāṃ cakrire tadā
a paryaṅkeṣu parārdhyeṣu spardhyāstaraṇavatsu ca
c varāsaneṣūpaviṣṭāḥ sukhaśayyāsv ivāmarāḥ
d upaviṣṭeṣu teṣv evaṃ rājaputreṣu bhārata
a tato duryodhano rājā sāmnā paramavalgunā
c tān ābhāṣya maheṣvāsān prāptakālam abhāṣata
a matiṃ matimatāṃ śreṣṭhāḥ sarve prabrūta māciram
c evaṃ gate tu yat kāryaṃ bhavet kāryakaraṃ nṛpāḥ
a evam ukte narendreṇa narasiṃhā yuyutsavaḥ
c cakrur nānāvidhāś ceṣṭāḥ siṃhāsanagatās tadā
a teṣāṃ niśamyeṅgitāni yuddhe prāṇāñ juhūṣatām
c samudvīkṣya mukhaṃ rājño bālārkasamavarcasaḥ
e ācāryaputro medhāvī vākyajño vākyam ādade
a rāgo yogas tathā dākṣyaṃ nayaś cety arthasādhakāḥ
c upāyāḥ paṇḍitaiḥ proktāḥ sarve daivasamāśritāḥ
a lokapravīrā ye 'smākaṃ devakalpā mahārathāḥ
c nītimantas tathā yuktā dakṣā raktāś ca te hatāḥ
a na tv eva kāryaṃ nairāśyam asmābhir vijayaṃ prati
c sunītair iha sarvārthair daivam apy anulomyate
a te vayaṃ pravaraṃ nṝṇāṃ sarvair guṇagaṇair yutam
b karṇam evābhiṣekṣyāmaḥ saināpatyena bhārata
c karṇaṃ senāpatiṃ kṛtvā pramathiṣyāmahe ripūn
d eṣa hy atibalaḥ śūraḥ kṛtāstro yuddhadurmadaḥ
d vaivasvata ivāsahyaḥ śakto jetuṃ raṇe ripūn
d etad ācāryatanayāc chrutvā rājaṃs tavātmajaḥ
d duryodhano mahārāja priyaṃ prītamanās tadā
d āśāṃ bahumatīṃ cakre karṇaṃ prati sa vai tadā
d hate bhīṣme ca droṇe ca karṇo jeṣyati pāṇḍavān
d tām āśāṃ hṛdaye kṛtvā samāśvasya ca bhārata
a tato duryodhanaḥ prītaḥ priyaṃ śrutvā vacas tadā
c prītisaṃskārasaṃyuktaṃ tathyam ātmahitaṃ śubham
a svaṃ manaḥ samavasthāpya bāhuvīryam upāśritaḥ
c duryodhano mahārāja rādheyam idam abravīt
a karṇa jānāmi te vīryaṃ sauhṛdaṃ ca paraṃ mayi
c tathāpi tvāṃ mahābāho pravakṣyāmi hitaṃ vacaḥ
a śrutvā yatheṣṭaṃ ca kuru vīra yat tava rocate
c bhavān prājñatamo nityaṃ mama caiva parā gatiḥ
a bhīṣmadroṇāv atirathau hatau senāpatī mama
c senāpatir bhavān astu tābhyāṃ draviṇavattaraḥ
a vṛddhau ca tau maheṣvāsau sāpekṣau ca dhanaṃjaye
c mānitau ca mayā vīrau rādheya vacanāt tava
a pitāmahatvaṃ saṃprekṣya pāṇḍuputrā mahāraṇe
c rakṣitās tāta bhīṣmeṇa divasāni daśaiva ha
a nyastaśastre ca bhavati hato bhīṣmaḥ pitāmahaḥ
c śikhaṇḍinaṃ puraskṛtya phalgunena mahāhave
a hate tasmin mahābhāge śaratalpagate tadā
c tvayokte puruṣavyāghra droṇo hy āsīt puraḥsaraḥ
a tenāpi rakṣitāḥ pārthāḥ śiṣyatvād iha saṃyuge
c sa cāpi nihato vṛddho dhṛṣṭadyumnena satvaram
a nihatābhyāṃ pradhānābhyāṃ tābhyām amitavikrama
c tvatsamaṃ samare yodhaṃ nānyaṃ paśyāmi cintayan
a bhavān eva tu naḥ śakto vijayāya na saṃśayaḥ
c pūrvaṃ madhye ca paścāc ca tavaiva viditaṃ hi tat
a sa bhavān dhuryavat saṃkhye dhuram udvoḍhum arhasi
c abhiṣecaya senānye svayam ātmānam ātmanā
a devatānāṃ yathā skandaḥ senānīḥ prabhur avyayaḥ
c tathā bhavān imāṃ senāṃ dhārtarāṣṭrīṃ bibhartu me
e jahi śatrugaṇān sarvān mahendra iva dānavān
a avasthitaṃ raṇe jñātvā pāṇḍavās tvāṃ mahāratham
c draviṣyanti sapāñcālā viṣṇuṃ dṛṣṭveva dānavāḥ
e tasmāt tvaṃ puruṣavyāghra prakarṣethā mahācamūm
a bhavaty avasthite yat te pāṇḍavā gatacetasaḥ
c bhaviṣyanti sahāmātyāḥ pāñcālaiḥ sṛñjayaiḥ saha
a yathā hy abhyuditaḥ sūryaḥ pratapan svena tejasā
c vyapohati tamas tīvraṃ tathā śatrūn vyapoha naḥ
d saṃjaya uvāca
d āśā balavatī rājan putrasya tava yābhavat
d hate bhīṣme ca droṇe ca karṇo jeṣyati pāṇḍavān
d tām āśāṃ hṛdaye kṛtvā karṇam evaṃ tadābravīt
d sūtaputra na te pārthaḥ sthitvāgre saṃyuyutsati
d saṃjaya uvāca
d evam uktas tu rādheyo rājñā duryodhanena ha
d rājñāṃ madhye mahābāhuḥ prītātmā sa mahābalaḥ
d harṣayann abravīt karṇo duryodhanam idaṃ vacaḥ
 karṇa uvāca
a uktam etan mayā pūrvaṃ gāndhāre tava saṃnidhau
c jeṣyāmi pāṇḍavān rājan saputrān sajanārdanān
a senāpatir bhaviṣyāmi tavāhaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ
c sthiro bhava mahārāja jitān viddhi ca pāṇḍavān
d samaṃ jvaradrojaraddroṇam ahaṃ mahāhave
d bravīmi sarve kuravo nibodhata
d na vā mad anyaḥ prahased raṇe 'rjunaṃ
d kramāgataṃ mṛtyum ivottamāmṛtāt
 saṃjaya uvāca
a evam ukto mahātejās tato duryodhano nṛpaḥ
c uttasthau rājabhiḥ sārdhaṃ devair iva śatakratuḥ
e senāpatyena satkartuṃ karṇaṃ skandam ivāmarāḥ
a tato 'bhiṣiṣicus tūrṇaṃ vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā
c duryodhanamukhā rājan rājāno vijayaiṣiṇaḥ
e śātakaumbhamayaiḥ kumbhair māheyaiś cābhimantritaiḥ
a toyapūrṇair viṣāṇaiś ca dvīpikhaḍgamaharṣabhaiḥ
c maṇimuktāmayaiś cānyaiḥ puṇyagandhais tathauṣadhaiḥ
a audumbare samāsīnam āsane kṣaumasaṃvṛtam
c śāstradṛṣṭena vidhinā saṃbhāraiś ca susaṃbhṛtaiḥ
d brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyās tathā śūdrāś ca saṃmatāḥ
d tuṣṭuvus taṃ mahātmānam abhiṣiktaṃ varāsane
d tato 'bhiṣikto rājendra niṣkair gobhir dhanena ca
d vācayām āsa viprāgryān rādheyaḥ paravīrahā
d pūjayām āsa vastraiś ca viprān vedavidas tataḥ
d sa vyarocata rādheyaḥ sūtamāgadhabandibhiḥ
d stūyamāno yathā bhānur udaye brahmavādibhiḥ
d tataḥ puṇyāhaghoṣeṇa vāditraninadena ca
d jayaśabdena śūrāṇāṃ tumulaḥ sarvato 'bhavat
d jayety ūcur nṛpāḥ sarve rādheyaṃ tatra saṃgatāḥ
a jaya pārthān sagovindān sānugāṃs tvaṃ mahāhave
c iti taṃ bandinaḥ prāhur dvijāś ca bharatarṣabha
a jahi pārthān sapāñcālān rādheya vijayāya naḥ
c udyann iva sadā bhānus tamāṃsy ugrair gabhastibhiḥ
a na hy alaṃ tvad visṛṣṭānāṃ śarāṇāṃ te sakeśavāḥ
c kṛtaghnāḥ sūryaraśmīnāṃ jvalatām iva darśane
a na hi pārthāḥ sapāñcālāḥ sthātuṃ śaktās tavāgrataḥ
c āttaśastrasya samare mahendrasyeva dānavāḥ
d saṃjaya uvāca
d sa satkṛtaḥ stūyamānaḥ suhṛdgaṇavṛto vṛṣā
d karṇo duryodhanaṃ vākyam abravīt prahasan priyam
d duryodhanādya sagaṇaṃ pāṇḍūnāṃ pravaraiḥ saha
d phalgunaṃ sūdayiṣyāmi tvatpriyārthaṃ sabāndhavam
d saparvatārṇavadvīpāṃ śādhi gāṃ gatapāṇḍavām
d putrapautraprapautreṣu pratiṣṭhāṃ gamayiṣyasi
d nāsahyaṃ vidyate mahyaṃ tvatpriyārtham ariṃdama
d satyadharmānuraktasya siddhir ātmavato yathā
a abhiṣiktas tu rādheyaḥ prabhayā so 'mitaprabhaḥ
c vyatyaricyata rūpeṇa divākara ivāparaḥ
a senāpatyena rādheyam abhiṣicya sutas tava
c amanyata tadātmānaṃ kṛtārthaṃ kālacoditaḥ
a karṇo 'pi rājan saṃprāpya senāpatyam ariṃdamaḥ
c yogam ājñāpayām āsa sūryasyodayanaṃ prati
a tava putrair vṛtaḥ karṇaḥ śuśubhe tatra bhārata
c devair iva yathā skandaḥ saṃgrāme tārakāmaye
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a senāpatyaṃ tu saṃprāpya karṇo vaikartanas tadā
c tathoktaś ca svayaṃ rājñā snigdhaṃ bhrātṛsamaṃ vacaḥ
a yogam ājñāpya senāyā āditye 'bhyudite tadā
b hitaś ca priyakāmaś ca mama putrasya nityaśaḥ
c akarot kiṃ mahāprājñas tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
 saṃjaya uvāca
a karṇasya matam ājñāya putras te bharatarṣabha
c yogam ājñāpayām āsa nāndītūryapuraḥsaram
a mahaty apararātre tu tava putrasya māriṣa
c yogo yogeti sahasā prādurāsīn mahāsvanaḥ
a nāgānāṃ kalpamānānāṃ rathānāṃ ca varūthinām
c saṃnahyatāṃ padātīnāṃ vājināṃ ca viśāṃ pate
a krośatāṃ cāpi yodhānāṃ tvaritānāṃ parasparam
c babhūva tumulaḥ śabdo divaspṛk sumahāṃs tadā
a tataḥ śvetapatākena bālārkākāravājinā
c hemapṛṣṭhena dhanuṣā hastikakṣyeṇa ketunā
a tūṇena śarapūrṇena sāṅgadena varūthinā
c śataghnīkiṅkiṇīśaktiśūlatomaradhāriṇā
a kārmukeṇopapannena vimalādityavarcasā
c rathenātipatākena sūtaputro vyadṛśyata
a dhamantaṃ vārijaṃ tāta hemajālavibhūṣitam
c vidhunvānaṃ mahac cāpaṃ kārtasvaravibhūṣitam
a dṛṣṭvā karṇaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ rathasthaṃ rathināṃ varam
c bhānumantam ivodyantaṃ tamo ghnantaṃ sahasraśaḥ
a na bhīṣmavyasanaṃ ke cin nāpi droṇasya māriṣa
c nānyeṣāṃ puruṣavyāghra menire tatra kauravāḥ
a tatas tu tvarayan yodhāñ śaṅkhaśabdena māriṣa
c karṇo niṣkāsayām āsa kauravāṇāṃ varūthinīm
a vyūhaṃ vyūhya maheṣvāso mākaraṃ śatrutāpanaḥ
b makaravyūham āsthāya daṃśito ravinandanaḥ
c pratyudyayau tadā karṇaḥ pāṇḍavān vijigīṣayā
a makarasya tu tuṇḍe vai karṇo rājan vyavasthitaḥ
c netrābhyāṃ śakuniḥ śūra ulūkaś ca mahārathaḥ
a droṇaputras tu śirasi grīvāyāṃ sarvasodarāḥ
c madhye duryodhano rājā balena mahatā vṛtaḥ
a vāme pāde tu rājendra kṛtavarmā vyavasthitaḥ
c nārāyaṇabalair yukto gopālair yuddhadurmadaḥ
a pāde tu dakṣiṇe rājan gautamaḥ satyavikramaḥ
c trigartaiś ca maheṣvāsair dākṣiṇātyaiś ca saṃvṛtaḥ
a anupādas tu yo vāmas tatra śalyo vyavasthitaḥ
c mahatyā senayā sārdhaṃ madradeśasamutthayā
a dakṣiṇe tu mahārāja suṣeṇaḥ satyasaṃgaraḥ
c vṛto rathasahasraiś ca dantināṃ ca śatais tathā
a pucche āstāṃ mahāvīrau bhrātarau pārthivau tadā
c citrasenaś ca citraś ca mahatyā senayā vṛtau
a tataḥ prayāte rājendra karṇe naravarottame
c dhanaṃjayam abhiprekṣya dharmarājo 'bravīd idam
a paśya pārtha mahāsenāṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya saṃyuge
c karṇena nirmitāṃ vīra guptāṃ vīrair mahārathaiḥ
a hatavīratamā hy eṣā dhārtarāṣṭrī mahācamūḥ
c phalguśeṣā mahābāho tṛṇais tulyā matā mama
a eko hy atra maheṣvāsaḥ sūtaputro vyavasthitaḥ
c sadevāsuragandharvaiḥ sakiṃnaramahoragaiḥ
e carācarais tribhir lokair yo 'jayyo rathināṃ varaḥ
a taṃ hatvādya mahābāho vijayas tava phalguna
c uddhṛtaś ca bhavec chalyo mama dvādaśavārṣikaḥ
e evaṃ jñātvā mahābāho vyūhaṃ vyūha yathecchasi
a bhrātus tad vacanaṃ śrutvā pāṇḍavaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ
c ardhacandreṇa vyūhena pratyavyūhata tāṃ camūm
a vāmapārśve 'bhavad rājan bhīmaseno vyavasthitaḥ
c dakṣiṇe ca maheṣvāso dhṛṣṭadyumno mahābalaḥ
a madhye vyūhasya sākṣāt tu pāṇḍavaḥ kṛṣṇasārathiḥ
c nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca dharmarājaś ca pṛṣṭhataḥ
a cakrarakṣau tu pāñcālyau yudhāmanyūttamaujasau
c nārjunaṃ jahatur yuddhe pālyamānau kirīṭinā
a śeṣā nṛpatayo vīrāḥ sthitā vyūhasya daṃśitāḥ
c yathābhāvaṃ yathotsāhaṃ yathāsattvaṃ ca bhārata
a evam etan mahāvyūhaṃ vyūhya bhārata pāṇḍavāḥ
c tāvakāś ca maheṣvāsā yuddhāyaiva mano dadhuḥ
a dṛṣṭvā vyūḍhāṃ tava camūṃ sūtaputreṇa saṃyuge
c nihatān pāṇḍavān mene tava putraḥ sahānvayaḥ
a tathaiva pāṇḍavīṃ senāṃ vyūḍhāṃ dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c dhārtarāṣṭrān hatān mene sakarṇān vai janādhipa
a tataḥ śaṅkhāś ca bheryaś ca paṇavānakagomukhāḥ
c sahasaivābhyahanyanta saśabdāś ca samantataḥ
a senayor ubhayo rājan prāvādyanta mahāsvanāḥ
c siṃhanādaś ca saṃjajñe śūrāṇāṃ jayagṛddhinām
a hayaheṣitaśabdāś ca vāraṇānāṃ ca bṛṃhitam
c rathanemisvanāś cogrāḥ saṃbabhūvur janādhipa
a na droṇavyasanaṃ kaś cij jānīte bharatarṣabha
c dṛṣṭvā karṇaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ mukhe vyūhasya daṃśitam
a ubhe sene mahāsattve prahṛṣṭanarakuñjare
c yoddhukāme sthite rājan hantum anyonyam añjasā
a tatra yattau susaṃrabdhau dṛṣṭvānyonyaṃ vyavasthitau
c anīkamadhye rājendra rejatuḥ karṇapāṇḍavau
a nṛtyamāne tu te sene sameyātāṃ parasparam
c tayoḥ pakṣaiḥ prapakṣaiś ca nirjagmur vai yuyutsavaḥ
a tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ naravāraṇavājinām
c rathināṃ ca mahārāja anyonyaṃ nighnatāṃ dṛḍham
 saṃjaya uvāca
a te sene 'nyonyam āsādya prahṛṣṭāśvanaradvipe
c bṛhatyau saṃprajahrāte devāsuracamūpame
a tato gajā rathāś cāśvāḥ pattayaś ca mahāhave
c saṃprahāraṃ paraṃ cakrur dehapāpmapraṇāśanam
a pūrṇacandrārkapadmānāṃ kāntitviḍgandhataḥ samaiḥ
c uttamāṅgair nṛsiṃhānāṃ nṛsiṃhās tastarur mahīm
a ardhacandrais tathā bhallaiḥ kṣuraprair asipaṭṭiśaiḥ
c paraśvadhaiś cāpy akṛntann uttamāṅgāni yudhyatām
a vyāyatāyatabāhūnāṃ vyāyatāyatabāhubhiḥ
c vyāyatā bāhavaḥ petuś chinnamuṣṭyāyudhāṅgadāḥ
a taiḥ sphuradbhir mahī bhāti raktāṅgulitalais tadā
c garuḍaprahatair ugraiḥ pañcāsyair iva pannagaiḥ
a hayasyandananāgebhyaḥ petur vīrā dviṣaddhatāḥ
c vimānebhyo yathā kṣīṇe puṇye svargasadas tathā
a gadābhir anyair gurvībhiḥ parighair musalair api
c pothitāḥ śataśaḥ petur vīrā vīratarai raṇe
a rathā rathair vinihatā mattā mattair dvipair dvipāḥ
c sādinaḥ sādibhiś caiva tasmin paramasaṃkule
a rathā vararathair nāgair aśvārohāś ca pattibhiḥ
c aśvārohaiḥ padātāś ca nihatā yudhi śerate
a rathāśvapattayo nāgai rathair nāgāś ca pattayaḥ
c rathapattidvipāś cāśvair nṛbhiś cāśvarathadvipāḥ
a rathāśvebhanarāṇāṃ ca narāśvebharathaiḥ kṛtam
b tathāśvanaranāgānām anyonyaṃ saṃkulaṃ babhau
c pāṇipādaiś ca śastraiś ca rathaiś ca kadanaṃ mahat
a tathā tasmin bale śūrair vadhyamāne hate 'pi ca
c asmān abhyāgaman pārthā vṛkodarapurogamāḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca draupadeyāḥ prabhadrakāḥ
c sātyakiś cekitānaś ca draviḍaiḥ sainikaiḥ saha
a bhṛtā vittena mahatā pāṇḍyāś cauḍrāḥ sakeralāḥ
c vyūḍhoraskā dīrghabhujāḥ prāṃśavaḥ priyadarśanāḥ
a āpīḍino raktadantā mattamātaṅgavikramāḥ
c nānāvirāgavasanā gandhacūrṇāvacūrṇitāḥ
a baddhāsayaḥ pāśahastā vāraṇaprativāraṇāḥ
c samānamṛtyavo rājann anīkasthāḥ parasparam
a kalāpinaś cāpahastā dīrghakeśāḥ priyāhavāḥ
c pattayaḥ sātyaker andhrā ghorarūpaparākramāḥ
a athāpare punaḥ śūrāś cedipāñcālakekayāḥ
c karūṣāḥ kosalāḥ kāśyā māgadhāś cāpi dudruvuḥ
a teṣāṃ rathāś ca nāgāś ca pravarāś cāpi pattayaḥ
c nānāvidharavair hṛṣṭā nṛtyanti ca hasanti ca
a tasya sainyasya mahato mahāmātravarair vṛtaḥ
c madhyaṃ vṛkodaro 'bhyāgāt tvadīyaṃ nāgadhūrgataḥ
a sa nāgapravaro 'tyugro vidhivat kalpito babhau
c udayādryagryabhavanaṃ yathābhyuditabhāskaram
a tasyāyasaṃ varmavaraṃ vararatnavibhūṣitam
c tārodbhāsasya nabhasaḥ śāradasya samatviṣam
a sa tomaraprāsakaraś cārumauliḥ svalaṃkṛtaḥ
c caran madhyaṃdinārkābhas tejasā vyadahad ripūn
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā dviradaṃ dūrāt kṣemadhūrtir dvipasthitaḥ
c āhvayāno 'bhidudrāva pramanāḥ pramanastaram
a tayoḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ dvipayor ugrarūpayoḥ
c yadṛcchayā drumavator mahāparvatayor iva
a saṃsaktanāgau tau vīrau tomarair itaretaram
c balavat sūryaraśmyābhair bhittvā bhittvā vinedatuḥ
a vyapasṛtya tu nāgābhyāṃ maṇḍalāni viceratuḥ
c pragṛhya caiva dhanuṣī jaghnatur vai parasparam
a kṣveḍitāsphoṭitaravair bāṇaśabdaiś ca sarvaśaḥ
c tau janān harṣayitvā ca siṃhanādān pracakratuḥ
a samudyatakarābhyāṃ tau dvipābhyāṃ kṛtināv ubhau
c vātoddhūtapatākābhyāṃ yuyudhāte mahābalau
a tāv anyonyasya dhanuṣī chittvānyonyaṃ vinedatuḥ
c śaktitomaravarṣeṇa prāvṛṇmeghāv ivāmbubhiḥ
a kṣemadhūrtis tadā bhīmaṃ tomareṇa stanāntare
c nirbibheda tu vegena ṣaḍbhiś cāpy aparair nadan
a sa bhīmasenaḥ śuśubhe tomarair aṅgamāśritaiḥ
c krodhadīptavapur meghaiḥ saptasaptir ivāṃśumān
a tato bhāskaravarṇābham añjogatimayasmayam
c sasarja tomaraṃ bhīmaḥ pratyamitrāya yatnavān
a tataḥ kulūtādhipatiś cāpam āyamya sāyakaiḥ
c daśabhis tomaraṃ chittvā śaktyā vivyādha pāṇḍavam
a atha kārmukam ādāya mahājaladanisvanam
c ripor abhyardayan nāgam unmadaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ śaraiḥ
a sa śaraughārdito nāgo bhīmasenena saṃyuge
c nigṛhyamāṇo nātiṣṭhad vātadhvasta ivāmbudaḥ
a tām abhyadhāvad dviradaṃ bhīmasenasya nāgarāṭ
c mahāvāteritaṃ meghaṃ vātoddhūta ivāmbudaḥ

c vivyādhābhidrutaṃ bāṇair bhīmasenaṃ sakuñjaram
a tataḥ sādhuvisṛṣṭena kṣureṇa puruṣarṣabhaḥ
c chittvā śarāsanaṃ śatror nāgam āmitram ārdayat
a tataḥ khajākayā bhīmaṃ kṣemadhūrtiḥ parābhinat
c jaghāna cāsya dviradaṃ nārācaiḥ sarvamarmasu
d sa papāta mahānago bhīmasenasya bhārata
a purā nāgasya patanād avaplutya sthito mahīm
c bhīmaseno ripor nāgaṃ gadayā samapothayat
a tasmāt pramathitān nāgāt kṣemadhūrtim avadrutam
b uddhṛtya khaḍgaṃ niśitam abhyadhāvat sa pāṇḍavam
c udyatāsim upāyāntaṃ gadayāhan vṛkodaraḥ
a sa papāta hataḥ sāsir vyasuḥ svam abhito dvipam
c vajraprarugṇam acalaṃ siṃho vajrahato yathā
a nihataṃ nṛpatiṃ dṛṣṭvā kulūtānāṃ yaśaskaram
c prādravad vyathitā senā tvadīyā bharatarṣabha
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tataḥ karṇo maheṣvāsaḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm
c jaghāna samare śūraḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
a tathaiva pāṇḍavā rājaṃs tava putrasya vāhinīm
c karṇasya pramukhe kruddhā vinijaghnur mahārathāḥ
a karṇo rājan mahābāhur nyavadhīt pāṇḍavīṃ camūm
c nārācair arkaraśmyābhaiḥ karmāraparimārjitaiḥ
a tatra bhārata karṇena nārācais tāḍitā gajāḥ
c neduḥ seduś ca mamluś ca babhramuś ca diśo daśa
a vadhyamāne bale tasmin sūtaputreṇa māriṣa
c nakulo 'bhyadravat tūrṇaṃ sūtaputraṃ mahāraṇe
a bhīmasenas tathā drauṇiṃ kurvāṇaṃ karma duṣkaram
c vindānuvindau kaikeyau sātyakiḥ samavārayat
a śrutakarmāṇam āyāntaṃ citraseno mahīpatiḥ
c prativindhyaṃ tathā citraś citraketanakārmukaḥ
a duryodhanas tu rājānaṃ dharmaputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
c saṃśaptakagaṇān kruddho abhyadhāvad dhanaṃjayaḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ kṛpaṃ cātha tasmin vīravarakṣaye
c śikhaṇḍī kṛtavarmāṇaṃ samāsādayad acyutam
a śrutakīrtis tathā śalyaṃ mādrīputraḥ sutaṃ tava
c duḥśāsanaṃ mahārāja sahadevaḥ pratāpavān
a kekayau sātyakiṃ yuddhe śaravarṣeṇa bhāsvatā
c sātyakiḥ kekayau caiva chādayām āsa bhārata
a tāv enaṃ bhrātarau vīraṃ jaghnatur hṛdaye bhṛśam
c viṣāṇābhyāṃ yathā nāgau pratināgaṃ mahāhave
a śarasaṃbhinnavarmāṇau tāv ubhau bhrātarau raṇe
c sātyakiṃ satyakarmāṇaṃ rājan vivyadhatuḥ śaraiḥ
a tau sātyakir mahārāja prahasan sarvatodiśam
c chādayañ śaravarṣeṇa vārayām āsa bhārata
a vāryamāṇau tatas tau tu śaineyaśaravṛṣṭibhiḥ
c śaineyasya rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ chādayām āsatuḥ śaraiḥ
a tayos tu dhanuṣī citre chittvā śaurir mahāhave
c atha tau sāyakais tīkṣṇaiś chādayām āsa duḥsahaiḥ
a athānye dhanuṣī mṛṣṭe pragṛhya ca mahāśarān
c sātyakiṃ pūrayantau tau ceratur laghu suṣṭhu ca
a tābhyāṃ muktā mahābāṇāḥ kaṅkabarhiṇavāsasaḥ
c dyotayanto diśaḥ sarvāḥ saṃpetuḥ svarṇabhūṣaṇāḥ
a bāṇāndhakāram abhavat tayo rājan mahāhave
c anyonyasya dhanuś caiva cicchidus te mahārathāḥ
d sātvatasya dhanus tatra ubhau cicchidatū raṇe
a tataḥ kruddho mahārāja sātvato yuddhadurmadaḥ
c dhanur anyat samādāya sajyaṃ kṛtvā ca saṃyuge
d anumṛjya ca rājendra tad dhanur bhārasādhanam
e kṣurapreṇa sutīkṣṇena anuvindaśiro 'harat
a tacchiro nyapatad bhūmau kuṇḍalotpīḍitaṃ mahat
c śambarasya śiro yadvan nihatasya mahāraṇe
e śoṣayan kekayān sarvāñ jagāmāśu vasuṃdharām
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā nihataṃ śūraṃ bhrātā tasya mahārathaḥ
c sajyam anyad dhanuḥ kṛtvā śaineyaṃ pratyavārayat
a sa śaktyā sātyakiṃ viddhvā svarṇapuṅkhaiḥ śilāśitaiḥ
c nanāda balavan nādaṃ tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt
a sa sātyakiṃ punaḥ kruddhaḥ kekayānāṃ mahārathaḥ
c śarair agniśikhākārair bāhvor urasi cārdayat
a sa śaraiḥ kṣatasarvāṅgaḥ sātvataḥ sattvakovidaḥ
c rarāja samare rājan sapatra iva kiṃśukaḥ
a sātyakiḥ samare viddhaḥ kekayena mahātmanā
c kekayaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā vivyādha prahasann iva
d tāv anyonyasya samare dhanuś chittvā mahārathau
d hatvā ca sārathī tūrṇaṃ hayāṃś ca rathināṃ varau
d virathāv asiyuddhāya samājagmatur āhave
a śatacandracite gṛhya carmaṇī subhujau tu tau
c vyarocetāṃ mahāraṅge nistriṃśavaradhāriṇau

a maṇḍalāni tatas tau ca vicarantau mahāraṇe
c anyonyam asibhis tūrṇaṃ samājaghnatur āhave
d anyonyasya vadhe caiva cakratur yatnam uttamam
a kekayasya tataś carma dvidhā ciccheda sātvataḥ
c sātyakeś ca tathaivāsau carma ciccheda pārthivaḥ
a carma cchittvā tu kaikeyas tārāgaṇaśatair vṛtam
c cacāra maṇḍalāny eva gatapratyāgatāni ca
a taṃ carantaṃ mahāraṅge nistriṃśavaradhāriṇam
c apahastena ciccheda śaineyas tvarayānvitaḥ
a savarmā kekayo rājan dvidhā chinno mahāhave
c nipapāta maheṣvāso vajranunna ivācalaḥ
a taṃ nihatya raṇe śūraḥ śaineyo rathasattamaḥ
c yudhāmanyo rathaṃ tūrṇam āruroha paraṃtapaḥ
a tato 'nyaṃ ratham āsthāya vidhivat kalpitaṃ punaḥ
c kekayānāṃ mahat sainyaṃ vyadhamat sātyakiḥ śaraiḥ
a sā vadhyamānā samare kekayasya mahācamūḥ
c tam utsṛjya rathaṃ śatruṃ pradudrāva diśo daśa
 saṃjaya uvāca
a śrutakarmā mahārāja citrasenaṃ mahīpatim
c ājaghne samare kruddhaḥ pañcāśadbhiḥ śilīmukhaiḥ
a abhisāras tu taṃ rājā navabhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c śrutakarmāṇam āhatya sūtaṃ vivyādha pañcabhiḥ
a śrutakarmā tataḥ kruddhaś citrasenaṃ camūmukhe

d so 'tividdho mahārāja nārācena mahātmanā
d mūrchām abhiyayau vīraḥ kaśmalaṃ cāviveśa ha
a etasminn antare cainaṃ śrutakīrtir mahāyaśāḥ
c navatyā jagatīpālaṃ chādayām āsa patribhiḥ
a pratilabya tataḥ saṃjñāṃ citraseno mahārathaḥ
c dhanuś ciccheda bhallena taṃ ca vivyādha saptabhiḥ
a so 'nyat kārmukam ādāya vegaghnaṃ rukmabhūṣaṇam
c citrarūpataraṃ cakre citrasenaṃ śarormibhiḥ
a sa śaraiś citrito rājaṃś citramālyadharo yuvā
c yuveva samaśobhat sa goṣṭhīmadhye svalaṃkṛtaḥ
a śrutakarmāṇam atha vai nārācena stanāntare
c bibheda samare kruddhas tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt

c susrāva rudhiraṃ bhūri gairikāmbha ivācalaḥ
a tataḥ sa rudhirāktāṅgo rudhireṇa kṛtacchaviḥ
c rarāja samare rājan sapuṣpa iva kiṃśukaḥ

c vivyādha bharataśreṣṭha śrutakarmā mahāyaśāḥ
d navatyā jagatīpālaṃ chādayan nataparvabhiḥ
a tato 'pareṇa bhallena bhṛśaṃ tīkṣṇena satvaraḥ
c jahāra saśirastrāṇaṃ śiras tasya mahātmanaḥ
a tacchiro nyapatad bhūmau sumahac citravarmaṇaḥ
c yadṛcchayā yathā candraś cyutaḥ svargān mahītale
a rājānaṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā abhisāraṃ ca māriṣa
c abhyadravanta vegena citrasenasya sainikāḥ
a tataḥ kruddho maheṣvāsas tat sainyaṃ prādravac charaiḥ
c antakāle yathā kruddhaḥ sarvabhūtāni pretarāṭ
d te vadhyamānāḥ samare tava pautreṇa dhanvinā
d vyadravanta diśas tūrṇaṃ dāvadagdhā iva dvipāḥ
d tāṃs tu vidravato dṛṣṭvā nirutsāhān dviṣajjaye
e drāvayann iṣubhis tūrṇaṃ śrutakarmā vyarocata
a prativindhyas tataś citraṃ bhittvā pañcabhir āśugaiḥ
c sārathiṃ tribhir ānarcchad dhvajam ekeṣuṇā tataḥ
a taṃ citro navabhir bhallair bāhvor urasi cārdayat

a prativindhyo dhanus tasya chittvā bhārata sāyakaiḥ
c pañcabhir niśitair bāṇair athainaṃ saṃprajaghnivān
a tataḥ śaktiṃ mahārāja hemadaṇḍāṃ durāsadām
c prāhiṇot tava putrāya ghorām agniśikhām iva
a tām āpatantīṃ sahasā śaktim ulkām ivāmbarāt
c dvidhā ciccheda samare prativindhyo hasann iva
a sā papāta tadā chinnā prativindhyaśaraiḥ śitaiḥ
c yugānte sarvabhūtāni trāsayantī yathāśaniḥ
a śaktiṃ tāṃ prahatāṃ dṛṣṭvā citro gṛhya mahāgadām
c prativindhyāya cikṣepa rukmajālavibhūṣitām
a sā jaghāna hayāṃs tasya sārathiṃ ca mahāraṇe
c rathaṃ pramṛdya vegena dharaṇīm anvapadyata
a etasminn eva kāle tu rathād āplutya bhārata
c śaktiṃ cikṣepa citrāya svarṇaghaṇṭām alaṃkṛtām
a tām āpatantīṃ jagrāha citro rājan mahāmanāḥ
c tatas tām eva cikṣepa prativindhyāya bhārata
a samāsādya raṇe śūraṃ prativindhyaṃ mahāprabhā
c nirbhidya dakṣiṇaṃ bāhuṃ nipapāta mahītale
e patitābhāsayac caiva taṃ deśam aśanir yathā
a prativindhyas tato rājaṃs tomaraṃ hemabhūṣitam
c preṣayām āsa saṃkruddhaś citrasya vadhakāmyayā
a sa tasya devāvaraṇaṃ bhittvā hṛdayam eva ca
c jagāma dharaṇīṃ tūrṇaṃ mahoraga ivāśayam
a sa papāta tadā rājaṃs tomareṇa samāhataḥ
c prasārya vipulau bāhū pīnau parighasaṃnibhau
a citraṃ saṃprekṣya nihataṃ tāvakā raṇaśobhinaḥ
c abhyadravanta vegena prativindhyaṃ samantataḥ
a sṛjanto vividhān bāṇāñ śataghnīś ca sakiṅkiṇīḥ
c ta enaṃ chādayām āsuḥ sūryam abhragaṇā iva
a tān apāsya mahābāhuḥ śarajālena saṃyuge
c vyadrāvayat tava camūṃ vajrahasta ivāsurīm
a te vadhyamānāḥ samare tāvakāḥ pāṇḍavair nṛpa
c viprakīryanta sahasā vātanunnā ghanā iva
a vipradrute bale tasmin vadhyamāne samantataḥ
c drauṇir eko 'bhyayāt tūrṇaṃ bhīmasenaṃ mahābalam
a tataḥ samāgamo ghoro babhūva sahasā tayoḥ
c yathā devāsure yuddhe vṛtravāsavayor abhūt
 saṃjaya uvāca
a bhīmasenaṃ tato drauṇī rājan vivyādha patriṇā
c tvarayā parayā yukto darśayann astralāghavam
a athainaṃ punar ājaghne navatyā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c sarvamarmāṇi saṃprekṣya marmajño laghuhastavat
a bhīmasenaḥ samākīrṇo drauṇinā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c rarāja samare rājan raśmivān iva bhāskaraḥ
a tataḥ śarasahasreṇa suprayuktena pāṇḍavaḥ
c droṇaputram avacchādya siṃhanādam amuñcata

c lalāṭe 'bhyahanad rājan nārācena smayann iva
a lalāṭasthaṃ tato bāṇaṃ dhārayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ
c yathā śṛṅgaṃ vane dṛptaḥ khaḍgo dhārayate nṛpa
a tato drauṇiṃ raṇe bhīmo yatamānaṃ parākramī
c tribhir vivyādha nārācair lalāṭe vismayann iva
a lalāṭasthais tato bāṇair brāhmaṇaḥ sa vyarocata
c prāvṛṣīva yathā siktas triśṛṅgaḥ parvatottamaḥ
a tataḥ śaraśatair drauṇim ardayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ
c na cainaṃ kampayām āsa mātariśveva parvatam
a tathaiva pāṇḍavaṃ yuddhe drauṇiḥ śaraśataiḥ śitaiḥ
c nākampayata saṃhṛṣṭo vāryogha iva parvatam
a tāv anyonyaṃ śarair ghoraiś chādayānau mahārathau
c rathacaryāgatau śūrau śuśubhāte raṇotkaṭau
a ādityāv iva saṃdīptau lokakṣayakarāv ubhau
c svaraśmibhir ivānyonyaṃ tāpayantau śarottamaiḥ
a kṛtapratikṛte yatnaṃ kurvāṇau ca mahāraṇe
c kṛtapratikṛte yatnaṃ cakrāte tāv abhītavat
a vyāghrāv iva ca saṃgrāme ceratus tau mahārathau
c śaradaṃṣṭrau durādharṣau cāpavyāttau bhayānakau
a abhūtāṃ tāv adṛśyau ca śarajālaiḥ samantataḥ
c meghajālair iva cchannau gagane candrabhāskarau
a prakāśau ca muhūrtena tatraivāstām ariṃdamau
c vimuktau meghajālena śaśisūryau yathā divi
d atha tatraiva saṃgrāme vartamāne sudāruṇe
a apasavyaṃ tataś cakre drauṇis tatra vṛkodaram
c kirañ śaraśatair ugrair dhārābhir iva parvatam
a na tu tan mamṛṣe bhīmaḥ śatror vijayalakṣaṇam
c praticakre ca taṃ rājan pāṇḍavo 'py apasavyataḥ
a maṇḍalānāṃ vibhāgeṣu gatapratyāgateṣu ca

c dyotayanto diśaḥ sarvās tac ca sainyaṃ samantataḥ
a bāṇasaṃghāvṛtaṃ ghoram ākāśaṃ samapadyata
c uklāpātakṛtaṃ yadvat prajānāṃ saṃkṣaye nṛpa
a bāṇābhighātāt saṃjajñe tatra bhārata pāvakaḥ
c savisphuliṅgo dīptārciḥ so 'dahad vāhinīdvayam
a tatra siddhā mahārāja saṃpatanto 'bruvan vacaḥ
c ati yuddhāni sarvāṇi yuddham etat tato 'dhikam
a sarvayuddhāni caitasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm
c naitādṛśaṃ punar yuddhaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati
a aho jñānena saṃyuktāv ubhau cograparākramau
b aho śauryeṇa saṃpannāv ubhau brāhmaṇapāṇḍavau
c aho bhīme balaṃ bhīmam etayoś ca kṛtāstratā
a aho vīryasya sāratvam aho sauṣṭhavam etayoḥ
c sthitāv etau hi samare kālāntakayamopamau
a rudrau dvāv iva saṃbhūtau yathā dvāv iva bhāskarau
c yamau vā puruṣavyāghrau ghorarūpāv imau raṇe

c siṃhanādaś ca saṃjajñe sametānāṃ divaukasām
e adbhutaṃ cāpy acintyaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā karma tayor mṛdhe
f siddhacāraṇasaṃghānāṃ vismayaḥ samapadyata
f praśaṃsanti tadā devāḥ siddhāś ca paramarṣayaḥ
f sādhu drauṇe mahābāho sādhu bhīmeti cābruvan
a tau śūrau samare rājan parasparakṛtāgasau
c parasparam udaikṣetāṃ krodhād udvṛtya cakṣuṣī
a krodharaktekṣaṇau tau tu krodhāt prasphuritādharau
c krodhāt saṃdaṣṭadaśanau saṃdaṣṭadaśanacchadau
a anyonyaṃ chādayantau sma śaravṛṣṭyā mahārathau
c śarāmbudhārau samare śastravidyutprakāśinau
a tāv anyonyaṃ dhvajau viddhvā sārathī ca mahārathau
c anyonyasya hayān viddhvā bibhidāte parasparam
a tataḥ kruddhau mahārāja bāṇau gṛhya mahāhave

a tau parasparavegāc ca śarābhyāṃ ca bhṛśāhatau
c nipetatur mahāvīrau svarathopasthayos tadā
a tatas tu sārathir jñātvā droṇaputram acetanam
c apovāha raṇād rājan sarvakṣatrasya paśyataḥ
a tathaiva pāṇḍavaṃ rājan vihvalantaṃ muhur muhuḥ
