d śrutakīrtim athāyāntaṃ kirantaṃ niśitāñ śarān
d madrarājo mahārāja vārayām āsa hṛṣṭavat
d madrarājaṃ samāsādya śrutakīrtir mahārathaḥ
d vivyādha bhallais triṃśatyā kārtasvaravibhūṣitaiḥ
d prativivyādha taṃ śalyas tribhis tūrṇam ajihmagaiḥ
d sārathiṃ cāsya bhallena bhṛśaṃ vivyādha bhārata
d sa śalyaṃ śaravarṣeṇa chādayām āsa saṃyuge
d mumoca niśitān bāṇān madrarājarathaṃ prati
d tataḥ śalyo mahārāja śrutakīrtibhujacyutān
d ciccheda samare bāṇān bāṇaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
d śrutakīrtis tataḥ śalyaṃ bhittvā navabhir āyasaiḥ
d sārathiṃ tribhir ānarchat punaḥ śalyaṃ ca pañcabhiḥ
d tasya śalyo dhanuś chittvā hastāvāpaṃ nikṛtya ca
d vivyādha samare tūrṇaṃ saptabhis taṃ śarottamaiḥ
d athānyad dhanur ādāya śrutakīrtir mahārathaḥ
d madreśvaraṃ catuḥṣaṣṭyā bāhvor urasi cārpayat
d tatas tu samare rājaṃs tena viddhaḥ śilīmukhaiḥ
d prativivyādha taṃ cāpi navatyā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
d tasya madreśvaraś cāpaṃ punaś ciccheda māriṣa
d saṃchinnadhanvā samare gadāṃ cikṣepa satvaraḥ
d paṭṭair jāmbūnadair baddhāṃ rūpyapaṭṭaiś ca bhārata
d bhrājamānāṃ yathā nārīṃ divyavastravibhūṣitām
d tām āpatantīṃ sahasā dīpyamānāśaniprabhām
d śarair anekasāhasrair vyaṣṭambhayata madrarāṭ
d viṣṭabhya ca gadāṃ vīraḥ pātayitvā ca bhūtale
d śrutakīrtim athāyatto rājan vivyādha pañcabhiḥ
d tasya śaktiṃ raṇe bhūyaś cikṣepa bhujagopamām
d tāṃ dvidhā cācchinac chalyo medinyāṃ sā tv aśīryata
d tasya śalyaḥ kṣurapreṇa yantuḥ kāyāc chiro 'harat
d bālahastād yathā śyena āmiṣaṃ vai narottama
d sa papāta rathopasthāt sārathis tasya bhārata
d tatas te prādravan saṃkhye hayās tasya mahātmanaḥ
d palāyamānais tair aśvaiḥ so 'panīto raṇājirāt
d śrutakīrtir mahārāja paśyatāṃ sarvayodhinām
d tato madreśvaro rājā pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm
d vyagāhata mudā yukto nalinīṃ dvirado yathā
d lolayām āsa sa balaṃ siṃhaḥ paśugaṇān iva
d śalyas tatra mahāraṅge pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanām
d nihatya pāṇḍupāñcālān pṛtanāsu vyavasthitaḥ
d aśobhata raṇe śalyo vidhūmo 'gnir iva jvalan
d senākakṣaṃ mahad dagdhvā kakṣam agnir ivotthitaḥ
d sthito rarāja samare puraṃ dagdhveva śaṃkaraḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a yathā saṃśaptakaiḥ sārdham arjunasyābhavad raṇaḥ
b sūtaputrasya pāñcālaiḥ kathaṃ yuddhaṃ pravartitam
b aśvatthāmnas tu yad yuddham arjunasya ca saṃjaya
c anyeṣāṃ ca madīyānāṃ pāṇḍavais tad bravīhi me
 saṃjaya uvāca
a śṛṇu rājan yathāvṛttaṃ saṃgrāmaṃ bruvato mama
c vīrāṇāṃ śatrubhiḥ sārdhaṃ dehapāpmapraṇāśanam
a pārthaḥ saṃśaptakagaṇaṃ praviśyārṇavasaṃnibham
c vyakṣobhayad amitraghno mahāvāta ivārṇavam
a śirāṃsy unmathya vīrāṇāṃ śitair bhallair dhanaṃjayaḥ
c pūrṇacandrābhavaktrāṇi svakṣibhrūdaśanāni ca
e saṃtastāra kṣitiṃ kṣipraṃ vinālair nalinair iva
a suvṛttān āyatān puṣṭāṃś candanāgurubhūṣitān
c sāyudhān satanutrāṇān pañcāsyoragasaṃnibhān
e bāhūn kṣurair amitrāṇāṃ vicakartārjuno raṇe
a dhuryān dhuryatarān sūtān dhvajāṃś cāpāni sāyakān
c pāṇīn aratnīn asakṛd bhallaiś ciccheda pāṇḍavaḥ
a dvipān hayān rathāṃś caiva sārohān arjuno raṇe
c śarair anekasāhasrai rājan ninye yamakṣayam
a taṃ pravīraṃ pratīyātā nardamānā ivarṣabhāḥ
c vāśitārtham abhikruddhā huṃkṛtvā cābhidudruvuḥ
e nighnantam abhijaghnus te śaraiḥ śṛṅgair ivarṣabhāḥ
a tasya teṣāṃ ca tad yuddham abhaval lomaharṣaṇam
c trailokyavijaye yādṛg daityānāṃ saha vajriṇā
a astrair astrāṇi saṃvārya dviṣatāṃ sarvato 'rjunaḥ
c iṣubhir bahubhis tūrṇaṃ viddhvā prāṇān rarāsa saḥ
a chinnatriveṇucakrākṣān hatayodhāśvasārathīn
c vidhvastāyudhatūṇīrān samunmathitaketanān
a saṃchinnayoktraraśmīkān vitriveṇūn vikūbarān
c vidhvastabandhurayugān viśastāyudhamaṇḍalān
e rathān viśakalīkurvan mahābhrāṇīva mārutaḥ
a vismāpayan prekṣaṇīyaṃ dviṣātāṃ bhayavardhanam
c mahārathasahasrasya samaṃ karmārjuno 'karot
a siddhadevarṣisaṃghāś ca cāraṇāś caiva tuṣṭuvuḥ
c devadundubhayo neduḥ puṣpavarṣāṇi cāpatan
e keśavārjunayor mūrdhni prāha vāk cāśarīriṇī
a candrārkānilavahnīnāṃ kāntidīptibaladyutīḥ
c yau sadā bibhratur vīrau tāv imau keśavārjunau
a brahmeśānāv ivājayyau vīrāv ekarathe sthitau
c sarvabhūtavarau vīrau naranārāyaṇāv ubhau
a ity etan mahad āścaryaṃ dṛṣṭvā śrutvā ca bhārata
c aśvatthāmā susaṃyattaḥ kṛṣṇāv abhyadravad raṇe
a atha pāṇḍavam asyantaṃ yamakālāntakāñ śarān
c seṣuṇā pāṇināhūya hasan drauṇir athābravīt
a yadi māṃ manyase vīra prāptam arham ivātithim
c tataḥ sarvātmanādya tvaṃ yuddhātithyaṃ prayaccha me
a evam ācāryaputreṇa samāhūto yuyutsayā
c bahu mene 'rjuno ''tmānam idaṃ cāha janārdanam
a saṃśaptakāś ca me vadhyā drauṇir āhvayate ca mām
c yad atrānantaraṃ prāptaṃ praśādhi tvaṃ mahābhuja
d ātithyakarmābhyutthāya dīyatāṃ yadi manyase
a evam ukto 'vahat pārthaṃ kṛṣṇo droṇātmajāntikam
c jaitreṇa vidhināhūtaṃ vāyur indram ivādhvare
a tam āmantryaikamanasā keśavo drauṇim abravīt
c aśvatthāman sthiro bhūtvā praharāśu sahasva ca
a nirveṣṭuṃ bhartṛpiṇḍaṃ hi kālo 'yam upajīvinām
c sūkṣmo vivādo viprāṇāṃ sthūlau kṣātrau jayājayau
a yāṃ na saṃkṣamase mohād divyāṃ pārthasya satkriyām
c tām āptum icchan yudhyasva sthiro bhūtvādya pāṇḍavam
a ity ukto vāsudevena tathety uktvā dvijottamaḥ
c vivyādha keśavaṃ ṣaṣṭyā nārācair arjunaṃ tribhiḥ
a tasyārjunaḥ susaṃkruddhas tribhir bhallaiḥ śarāsanam
c cicchedāthānyad ādatta drauṇir ghorataraṃ dhanuḥ
a sajyaṃ kṛtvā nimeṣāt tad vivyādhārjunakeśavau
c tribhiḥ śarair vāsudevaṃ sahasreṇa ca pāṇḍavam
a tataḥ śarasahasrāṇi prayutāny arbudāni ca
c sasṛje drauṇir āyastaḥ saṃstabhya ca raṇe 'rjunam
a iṣudher dhanuṣo jyāyā aṅgulībhyaś ca māriṣa
c bāhvoḥ karābhyām uraso vadanaghrāṇanetrataḥ
a karṇābhyāṃ śiraso 'ṅgebhyo lomavartmabhya eva ca
c rathadhvajebhyaś ca śarā niṣpetur brahmavādinaḥ
a śarajālena mahatā viddhvā keśavapāṇḍavau
c nanāda mudito drauṇir mahāmeghaughanisvanaḥ
a tasya nānadataḥ śrutvā pāṇḍavo 'cyutam abravīt
c paśya mādhava daurātmyaṃ droṇaputrasya māṃ prati
a vadhaprāptau manyate nau praveśya śaraveśmani
c eṣo 'sya hanmi saṃkalpaṃ śikṣayā ca balena ca
d evam uktvāsya ciccheda bhallaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
d dhanuś citraṃ patākāṃ ca rathaṃ śaktiṃ gadāṃ śubhām
a aśvatthāmnaḥ śarān astāṃś chittvaikaikaṃ tridhā tridhā
c vyadhamad bharataśreṣṭho nīhāram iva mārutaḥ
a tataḥ saṃśaptakān bhūyaḥ sāśvasūtarathadvipān
c dhvajapattigaṇān ugrair bāṇair vivyādha pāṇḍavaḥ
a ye ye dadṛśire tatra yad yad rūpaṃ yathā yathā
c te te tat tac charair vyāptaṃ menire ''tmānam eva ca
a te gāṇḍīvapraṇuditā nānārūpāḥ patatriṇaḥ
c krośe sāgre sthitān ghnanti dvipāṃś ca puruṣān raṇe
a bhallaiś chinnāḥ karāḥ petuḥ kariṇāṃ madakarṣiṇām
c chinnā yathā paraśubhiḥ pravṛddhāḥ śaradi drumāḥ
a paścāt tu śailavat petus te gajāḥ saha sādibhiḥ
c vajrivajrapramathitā yathaivādricayās tathā
a gandharvanagarākārān vidhivat kalpitān rathān
c vinītajavanāny uktān āsthitān yuddhadurmadān
a śarair viśakalīkurvann amitrān abhyavīvṛṣat
b te śarāḥ sūryasaṃkāśāḥ patantaḥ sarvatodiśam
c alaṃkṛtān aśvasādīn pattīṃś cāhan dhanaṃjayaḥ
a dhanaṃjayayugāntārkaḥ saṃśaptakamahārṇavam
c vyaśoṣayata duḥśoṣaṃ tīvraiḥ śaragabhastibhiḥ
a punar drauṇimahāśailaṃ nārācaiḥ sūryasaṃnibhaiḥ
c nirbibheda mahāvegais tvaran vajrīva parvatam
a tam ācāryasutaḥ kruddhaḥ sāśvayantāram āśugaiḥ
c yuyutsur nāśakad yoddhuṃ pārthas tān antarācchinat
a tataḥ paramasaṃkruddhaḥ kāṇḍakośān avāsṛjat
c aśvatthāmābhirūpāya gṛhān atithaye yathā
a atha saṃśaptakāṃs tyaktvā pāṇḍavo drauṇim abhyayāt
c apāṅkteyam iva tyaktvā dātā pāṅkteyam arthinam
d sthitāḥ saṃśaptakā rājan dṛṣṭvā yuddhaṃ mahātmanoḥ
a tataḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ śukrāṅgirasavarcasoḥ
c nakṣatram abhito vyomni śukrāṅgirasayor iva
a saṃtāpayantāv anyonyaṃ dīptaiḥ śaragabhastibhiḥ
c lokatrāsakarāv āstāṃ vimārgasthau grahāv iva
a tato 'vidhyad bhruvor madhye nārācenārjuno bhṛśam
c sa tena vibabhau drauṇir ūrdhvaraśmir yathā raviḥ
a atha kṛṣṇau śaraśatair aśvatthāmnārditau bhṛśam
c saraśmijālanikarau yugāntārkāv ivāsatuḥ
a tato 'rjunaḥ sarvatodhāram astram
avāsṛjad vāsudevābhiguptaḥ
c drauṇāyaniṃ cābhyahanat pṛṣatkair
vajrāgnivaivasvatadaṇḍakalpaiḥ
a sa keśavaṃ cārjunaṃ cātitejā
vivyādha marmasv atiraudrakarmā
c bāṇaiḥ sumuktair atitīvravegair
yair āhato mṛtyur api vyatheta
a drauṇer iṣūn arjunaḥ saṃnivārya
vyāyacchatas tad dviguṇaiḥ supuṅkhaiḥ
c taṃ sāśvasūtadhvajam ekavīram
āvṛtya saṃśaptakasainyam ārchat
a dhanūṃṣi bāṇān iṣudhīr dhanurjyāḥ
pāṇīn bhujān pāṇigataṃ ca śastram
c chatrāṇi ketūṃs turagān athaiṣāṃ
vastrāṇi mālyāny atha bhūṣaṇāni
a carmāṇi varmāṇi manorathāṃś ca
priyāṇi sarvāṇi śirāṃsi caiva
c ciccheda pārtho dviṣatāṃ pramuktair
bāṇaiḥ sthitānām aparāṅmukhānām
a sukalpitāḥ syandanavājināgāḥ
samāsthitāḥ kṛtayatnair nṛvīraiḥ
c pārtheritair bāṇagaṇair nirastās
tair eva sārdhaṃ nṛvarair nipetuḥ
a padmārkapūrṇendusamānanāni
kirīṭamālāmukuṭotkaṭāni
c bhallārdhacandrakṣurahiṃsitāni
prapetur urvyāṃ nṛśirāṃsy ajasram
a atha dvipair devapatidvipābhair
devāridarpolbaṇamanyudarpaiḥ
c kaliṅgavaṅgāṅganiṣādavīrā
jighāṃsavaḥ pāṇḍavam abhyadhāvan
a teṣāṃ dvipānāṃ vicakarta pārtho
varmāṇi marmāṇi karān niyantṝn
c dhvajāḥ patākāś ca tataḥ prapetur
vajrāhatānīva gireḥ śirāṃsi
a teṣu prarugṇeṣu guros tanūjaṃ
bāṇaiḥ kirīṭī navasūryavarṇaiḥ
c pracchādayām āsa mahābhrajālair
vāyuḥ samudyuktam ivāṃśumantam
a tato 'rjuneṣūn iṣubhir nirasya
drauṇiḥ śarair arjunavāsudevau
c pracchādayitva divi candrasūryau
nanāda so 'mbhoda ivātapānte
a tam arjunas tāṃś ca punas tvadīyān
abhyarditas tair avikṛttaśastraiḥ
c bāṇāndhakāraṃ sahasaiva kṛtvā
vivyādha sarvān iṣubhiḥ supuṅkhaiḥ
a nāpy ādadat saṃdadhan naiva muñcan
bāṇān raṇe 'dṛśyata savyasācī
c hatāṃś ca nāgāṃs turagān padātīn
saṃsyūtadehān dadṛśū rathāṃś ca
a saṃdhāya nārācavarān daśāśu
drauṇis tvarann ekam ivotsasarja
c teṣāṃ ca pañcārjunam abhyavidhyan
pañcācyutaṃ nirbibhiduḥ sumuktāḥ
a tair āhatau sarvamanuṣyamukhyāv
asṛkkṣarantau dhanadendrakalpau
c samāptavidyena yathābhibhūtau
hatau svid etau kim u menire 'nye
a athārjunaṃ prāha daśārhanāthaḥ
pramādyase kiṃ jahi yodham etam
c kuryād dhi doṣaṃ samupekṣito 'sau
kaṣṭo bhaved vyādhir ivākriyāvān
a tatheti coktvācyutam apramādī
drauṇiṃ prayatnād iṣubhis tatakṣa
b bhujau varau candanasāradigdhau
b vakṣaḥ śiro 'thāpratimau tathorū
b gāṇḍīvamuktaiḥ kupito vikarṇair
b drauṇiṃ śaraiḥ saṃyati nirbibheda
c chittvāśvaraśmīṃs turagān avidhyat
te taṃ raṇād ūhur atīva dūram
d sa tair hṛto vātajavais turaṃgair
d drauṇir dṛḍhaṃ pārthaśarābhibhūtaḥ
a āvṛtya neyeṣa punas tu yuddhaṃ
pārthena sārdhaṃ matimān vimṛśya
c jānañ jayaṃ niyataṃ vṛṣṇivīre
dhanaṃjaye cāṅgirasāṃ variṣṭhaḥ
d viveśa karṇasya balaṃ tarasvī
d bhagnotsāhaḥ kṣīṇabāṇāstrayogaḥ
d niyamya tu hayān drauṇiḥ samāśvasya ca māriṣa
d rathāśvanarasaṃbādhaṃ karṇasya prāviśad balam
a pratīpakāye tu raṇād aśvatthāmni hṛte hayaiḥ
c mantrauṣadhikriyādānair vyādhau dehād ivāhṛte
a saṃśaptakān abhimukhau prayātau keśavārjunau
c vātoddhūtapatākena syandanenaughanādinā
 saṃjaya uvāca
a athottareṇa pāṇḍūnāṃ senāyāṃ dhvanir utthitaḥ
c rathanāgāśvapattīnāṃ daṇḍadhāreṇa vadhyatām
a nivartayitvā tu rathaṃ keśavo 'rjunam abravīt
c vāhayann eva turagān garuḍānilaraṃhasaḥ
a māgadho 'thāpy atikrānto dviradena pramāthinā
c bhagadattād anavaraḥ śikṣayā ca balena ca
a enaṃ hatvā nihantāsi punaḥ saṃśaptakān iti
c vākyānte prāpayat pārthaṃ daṇḍadhārāntikaṃ prati
a sa māgadhānāṃ pravaro 'ṅkuśagraho
graheṣv asahyo vikaco yathā grahaḥ
c sapatnasenāṃ pramamātha dāruṇo
mahīṃ samagrāṃ vikaco yathā grahaḥ
a sukalpitaṃ dānavanāgasaṃnibhaṃ
mahābhrasaṃhrādam amitramardanam
c rathāśvamātaṅgagaṇān sahasraśaḥ
samāsthito hanti śarair dvipān api
a rathān adhiṣṭhāya savājisārathīn
rathāṃś ca padbhis tvarito vyapothayat
c dvipāṃś ca padbhyāṃ caraṇaiḥ kareṇa ca
dvipāsthito hanti sa kālacakravat
d sa nāgayantṝn samare mahārathān
d sapattisaṃghāṃs turagān sasādinaḥ
d dvipāṃś ca bāṇair nijaghāna vīryavān
d samantato ghnann iva kālacakravat
a narāṃś ca kārṣṇāyasavarmabhūṣaṇān
nipātya sāśvān api pattibhiḥ saha
c vyapothayad dantivareṇa śuṣmiṇā
saśabdavat sthūlanaḍān yathā tathā
a athārjuno jyātalaneminisvane
mṛdaṅgabherībahuśaṅkhanādite
c narāśvamātaṅgasahasranāditai
rathottamenābhyapatad dvipottamam
a tato 'rjunaṃ dvādaśabhiḥ śarottamair
janārdanaṃ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ samārdayat
c sa daṇḍadhāras turagāṃs tribhis tribhis
tato nanāda prajahāsa cāsakṛt
a tato 'sya pārthaḥ saguṇeṣukārmukaṃ
cakarta bhallair dhvajam apy alaṃkṛtam
c punar niyantṝn saha pādagoptṛbhis
tatas tu cukrodha girivrajeśvaraḥ
a tato 'rjunaṃ bhinnakaṭena dantinā
ghanāghanenānilatulyaraṃhasā
c atīva cukṣobhayiṣur janārdanaṃ
dhanaṃjayaṃ cābhijaghāna tomaraiḥ
a athāsya bāhū dvipahastasaṃnibhau
śiraś ca pūrṇendunibhānanaṃ tribhiḥ
c kṣuraiḥ praciccheda sahaiva pāṇḍavas
tato dvipaṃ bāṇaśataiḥ samārdayat
a sa pārthabāṇais tapanīyabhūṣaṇaiḥ
samārucat kāñcanavarmabhṛd dvipaḥ
c tathā cakāśe niśi parvato yathā
davāgninā prajvalitauṣadhidrumaḥ
a sa vedanārto 'mbudanisvano nadaṃś
calan bhraman praskhalito ''turo dravan
c papāta rugṇaḥ saniyantṛkas tathā
yathā girir vajranipātacūrṇitaḥ
a himāvadātena suvarṇamālinā
himādrikūṭapratimena dantinā
c hate raṇe bhrātari daṇḍa āvrajaj
jighāṃsur indrāvarajaṃ dhanaṃjayam
a sa tomarair arkakaraprabhais tribhir
janārdanaṃ pañcabhir eva cārjunam
c samarpayitvā vinanāda cārdayaṃs
tato 'sya bāhū vicakarta pāṇḍavaḥ
a kṣuraprakṛttau subhṛśaṃ satomarau
cyutāṅgadau candanarūṣitau bhujau
c gajāt patantau yugapad virejatur
yathādriśṛṅgāt patitau mahoragau
a athārdhacandreṇa hṛtaṃ kirīṭinā
papāta daṇḍasya śiraḥ kṣitiṃ dvipāt
c tac choṇitābhaṃ nipatad vireje
divākaro 'stād iva paścimāṃ diśam
a atha dvipaṃ śvetanagāgrasaṃnibhaṃ
divākarāṃśupratimaiḥ śarottamaiḥ
c bibheda pārthaḥ sa papāta nānadan
himādrikūṭaḥ kuliśāhato yathā
a tato 'pare tatpratimā gajottamā
jigīṣavaḥ saṃyati savyasācinam
c tathā kṛtās tena yathaiva tau dvipau
tataḥ prabhagnaṃ sumahad ripor balam
a gajā rathāśvāḥ puruṣāś ca saṃghaśaḥ
parasparaghnāḥ paripetur āhave
c parasparapraskhalitāḥ samāhatā
bhṛśaṃ ca tat tat kulabhāṣiṇo hatāḥ
a athārjunaṃ sve parivārya sainikāḥ
puraṃdaraṃ devagaṇā ivābruvan
c abhaiṣma yasmān maraṇād iva prajāḥ
sa vīra diṣṭyā nihatas tvayā ripuḥ
a na cet paritrāsya imāñ janān bhayād
dviṣadbhir evaṃ balibhiḥ prapīḍitān
c tathābhaviṣyad dviṣatāṃ pramodanaṃ
yathā hateṣv eṣv iha no 'riṣu tvayā
a itīva bhūyaś ca suhṛdbhir īritā
niśamya vācaḥ sumanās tato 'rjunaḥ
c yathānurūpaṃ pratipūjya taṃ janaṃ
jagāma saṃśaptakasaṃghahā punaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a pratyāgatya punar jiṣṇur ahan saṃśaptakān bahūn
c vakrānuvakragamanād aṅgāraka iva grahaḥ
a pārthabāṇahatā rājan narāśvarathakuñjarāḥ
c vicelur babhramur neduḥ petur mamluś ca māriṣa
a dhuryaṃ dhuryatarān sūtān rathāṃś ca parisaṃkṣipan
c pāṇīn pāṇigataṃ śastraṃ bāhūn api śirāṃsi ca
a bhallaiḥ kṣurair ardhacandrair vatsadantaiś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
c cicchedāmitravīrāṇāṃ samare pratiyudhyatām
d taṃ pravīrās tvadīyānāṃ nardamānābhidudruvuḥ
a vāśitārthe yuyutsanto vṛṣabhā vṛṣabhaṃ yathā
c āpatanty arjunaṃ śūrāḥ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a teṣāṃ tasya ca tad yuddham abhaval lomaharṣaṇam
c trailokyavijaye yādṛg daityānāṃ saha vajriṇā
a tam avidhyat tribhir bāṇair dandaśūkair ivāhibhiḥ
c ugrāyudhas tatas tasya śiraḥ kāyād apāharat
a te 'rjunaṃ sarvataḥ kruddhā nānāśastrair avīvṛṣan
c marudbhiḥ preṣitā meghā himavantam ivoṣṇage
a astrair astrāṇi saṃvārya dviṣatāṃ sarvato 'rjunaḥ
c samyag astaiḥ śaraiḥ sarvān sahitān ahanad bahūn
a chinnatriveṇujaṅgheṣān nihatapārṣṇisārathīn
b vidhvastāyudhatūṇīrān vicakrarathaketanān
c saṃchinnaraśmiyoktrākṣān vyanukarṣayugān rathān
e vidhvastasarvasaṃnāhān bāṇaiś cakre 'rjunas tvaran
a te rathās tatra vidhvastāḥ parārdhyā bhānty anekaśaḥ
c dhaninām iva veśmāni hatāny agnyanilāmbubhiḥ
a dvipāḥ saṃbhinnamarmāṇo vajrāśanisamaiḥ śaraiḥ
c petur giryagraveśmāni vajravātāgnibhir yathā
a sārohās turagāḥ petur bahavo 'rjunatāḍitāḥ
c nirjihvāntrāḥ kṣitau kṣīṇā rudhirārdrāḥ sudurdṛśaḥ
a narāśvanāgā nārācaiḥ saṃsyūtāḥ savyasācinā
c babhramuś caskhaluḥ petur nedur mamluś ca māriṣa
a aṇakaiś ca śilādhautair vajrāśaniviṣopamaiḥ
c śarair nijaghnivān pārtho mahendra iva dānavān
a mahārhavarmābharaṇā nānārūpāmbarāyudhāḥ
c sarathāḥ sadhvajā vīrā hatāḥ pārthena śerate
a vijitāḥ puṇyakarmāṇo viśiṣṭābhijanaśrutāḥ
c gatāḥ śarīrair vasudhām ūrjitaiḥ karmabhir divam
a athārjunarathaṃ vīrās tvadīyāḥ samupādravan
c nānājanapadādhyakṣāḥ sagaṇā jātamanyavaḥ
a uhyamānā rathāśvais te pattayaś ca jighāṃsavaḥ
c samabhyadhāvann asyanto vividhaṃ kṣipram āyudham
a tadāyudhamahāvarṣaṃ kṣiptaṃ yodhamahāmbudaiḥ
c vyadhaman niśitair bāṇaiḥ kṣipram arjunamārutaḥ
a sāśvapattidviparathaṃ mahāśastraugham aplavam
c sahasā saṃtitīrṣantaṃ pārthaṃ śastrāstrasetunā
a athābravīd vāsudevaḥ pārthaṃ kiṃ krīḍase 'nagha
b ete balādhikāḥ prāptāḥ pārtha kiṃ krīḍase 'nagha
c saṃśaptakān pramathyaitāṃs tataḥ karṇavadhe tvara
a tathety uktvārjunaḥ kṣipraṃ śiṣṭān saṃśaptakāṃs tadā
c ākṣipya śastreṇa balād daityān indra ivāvadhīt
a ādadhat saṃdadhan neṣūn dṛṣṭaḥ kaiś cid raṇe 'rjunaḥ
c vimuñcan vā śarāñ śīghraṃ dṛśyate sma hi kair api
a āścaryam iti govindo bruvann aśvān acodayat
c haṃsāṃsagaurās te senāṃ haṃsāḥ sara ivāviśan
d tatas te haṃsasadṛśās turagā vātaraṃhasaḥ
d tāṃ senāṃ viviśur hṛṣṭā haṃsā iva mahat saraḥ
a tataḥ saṃgrāmabhūmiṃ tāṃ vartamāne janakṣaye
c avekṣamāṇo govindaḥ savyasācinam abravīt
a eṣa pārtha mahāraudro vartate bharatakṣayaḥ
c pṛthivyāṃ pārthivānāṃ vai duryodhanakṛte mahān
a paśya bhārata cāpāni rukmapṛṣṭhāni dhanvinām
c mahatām apaviddhāni kalāpān iṣudhīs tathā
a jātarūpamayaiḥ puṅkhaiḥ śarāṃś ca nataparvaṇaḥ
c tailadhautāṃś ca nārācān nirmuktān iva pannagān
a hastidantatsarūn khaḍgāñ jātarūpapariṣkṛtān
c ākīrṇāṃs tomarāṃś cāpāṃś citrān hemavibhūṣitān
d daṇḍān kanakacitrāṃś ca saṃvṛttā raṇabhūmayaḥ
a varmāṇi cāpaviddhāni rukmapṛṣṭhāni bhārata
c suvarṇavikṛtān prāsāñ śaktīḥ kanakabhūṣitāḥ
a jāmbūnadamayaiḥ paṭṭair baddhāś ca vipulā gadāḥ
c jātarūpamayīś carṣṭīḥ paṭṭiśān hemabhūṣitān
a daṇḍaiḥ kanakacitraiś ca vipraviddhān paraśvadhān
b parighān bhiṇḍipālāṃś ca bhuśuṇḍīḥ kuṇapān api
c ayaskuśāntān patitān musalāni gurūṇi ca
a śataghnīḥ paśya citrāś ca vipulān parighāṃs tathā
c cakrāṇi cāpaviddhāni mudgarāṃś ca bahūn raṇe
a nānāvidhāni śastrāṇi pragṛhya jayagṛddhinaḥ
c jīvanta iva lakṣyante gatasattvās tarasvinaḥ
a gadāvimathitair gātrair musalair bhinnamastakān
c gajavājirathakṣuṇṇān paśya yodhān sahasraśaḥ
a manuṣyagajavājīnāṃ śaraśaktyṛṣṭitomaraiḥ
c nistriṃśaiḥ paṭṭiśaiḥ prāsair nakharair laguḍair api
a śarīrair bahudhā bhinnaiḥ śoṇitaughapariplutaiḥ
c gatāsubhir amitraghna saṃvṛtā raṇabhūmayaḥ
a bāhubhiś candanādigdhaiḥ sāṅgadaiḥ śubhabhūṣaṇaiḥ
c satalatraiḥ sakeyūrair bhāti bhārata medinī
a sāṅgulitrair bhujāgraiś ca vipraviddhair alaṃkṛtaiḥ
c hastihastopamaiś chinnair ūrubhiś ca tarasvinām
a baddhacūḍāmaṇivaraiḥ śirobhiś ca sakuṇḍalaiḥ
c nikṛttair vṛṣabhākṣāṇāṃ virājati vasuṃdharā
a kabandhaiḥ śoṇitādigdhaiś chinnagātraśirodharaiḥ
c bhūr bhāti bharataśreṣṭha śāntārcirbhir ivāgnibhiḥ
a rathān bahuvidhān bhagnān hemakiṅkiṇinaḥ śubhān
c aśvāṃś ca bahudhā paśya śoṇitena pariplutān
d anukarṣān upāsaṅgān patākā vividhān dhvajān
a yodhānāṃ ca mahāśaṅkhān pāṇḍurāṃś ca prakīrṇakān
c nirastajihvān mātaṅgāñ śayānān parvatopamān
a vaijayantīvicitrāṃś ca hatāṃś ca gajayodhinaḥ
c vāraṇānāṃ paristomān suyuktāmbarakambalān
a vipāṭitā vicitrāś ca rūpacitrāḥ kuthās tathā
c bhinnāś ca bahudhā ghaṇṭāḥ patadbhiś cūrṇitā gajaiḥ
a vaiḍūryamaṇidaṇḍāṃś ca patitān aṅkuśān bhuvi
b aśvānāṃ ca yugāpīḍān ratnacitrān uraśchadān
c baddhāḥ sādidhvajāgreṣu suvarṇavikṛtāḥ kaśāḥ
a vicitrān maṇicitrāṃś ca jātarūpapariṣkṛtān
c aśvāstaraparistomān rāṅkavān patitān bhuvi
a cūḍāmaṇīn narendrāṇāṃ vicitrāḥ kāñcanasrajaḥ
c chatrāṇi cāpaviddhāni cāmaravyajanāni ca
a candranakṣatrabhāsaiś ca vadanaiś cārukuṇḍalaiḥ
c kḷptaśmaśrubhir atyarthaṃ vīrāṇāṃ samalaṃkṛtaiḥ
e vadanaiḥ paśya saṃchannāṃ mahīṃ śoṇitakardamām
f kumudotpalapatrāṇāṃ ṣaṇḍaiḥ phullair yathā saraḥ
f tathā mahībhṛtāṃ vaktraiḥ kumudotpalasaṃnibhaiḥ
f tārāgaṇavicitrasya nirmalendudyutitviṣaḥ
f paśya gāṃ nabhasas tulyāṃ grahanakṣatramālinaḥ
a sajīvāṃś ca narān paśya kūjamānān samantataḥ
c upāsyamānān bahubhir nyastaśastrair viśāṃ pate
a jñātibhiḥ sahitais tatra rodamānair muhur muhuḥ
c vyutkrāntān aparān yodhāṃś chādayitvā tarasvinaḥ
e punar yuddhāya gacchanti jayagṛddhāḥ pramanyavaḥ
a apare tatra tatraiva paridhāvanti māninaḥ
c jñātibhiḥ patitaiḥ śūrair yācyamānās tathodakam
a jalārthaṃ ca gatāḥ ke cin niṣprāṇā bahavo 'rjuna
c saṃnivṛttāś ca te śūrās tān dṛṣṭvaiva vicetasaḥ
a jalaṃ dṛṣṭvā pradhāvanti krośamānāḥ parasparam
c jalaṃ pītvā mṛtān paśya pibato 'nyāṃś ca bhārata
a parityajya priyān anye bāndhavān bāndhavapriya
c vyutkrāntāḥ samadṛśyanta tatra tatra mahāraṇe
a paśyāparān naraśreṣṭha saṃdaṣṭauṣṭhapuṭān punaḥ
c bhrukuṭīkuṭilair vaktraiḥ prekṣamāṇān samantataḥ
d evaṃ bruvaṃs tadā kṛṣṇo yayau yena yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d arjunaś cāpi nṛpater darśanārthaṃ mahāraṇe
d yāhi yāhīti govindaṃ muhur muhur acodayat
d tāṃ yuddhabhūmiṃ pārthasya darśayitvā ca mādhavaḥ
a etat tavaivānurūpaṃ karmārjuna mahāhave
c divi vā devarājasya tvayā yat kṛtam āhave
a evaṃ tāṃ darśayan kṛṣṇo yuddhabhūmiṃ kirīṭine
c gacchann evāśṛṇoc chabdaṃ duryodhanabale mahat
a śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣān bherīpaṇavamiśritān
c rathāśvagajanādāṃś ca śastraśabdāṃś ca dāruṇān
a praviśya tad balaṃ kṛṣṇas turagair vātavegibhiḥ
c pāṇḍyenābhyarditāṃ senāṃ tvadīyāṃ vīkṣya dhiṣṭhitaḥ
a sa hi nānāvidhair bāṇair iṣvāsapravaro yudhi
c nyahanad dviṣatāṃ vrātān gatāsūn antako yathā
a gajavājimanuṣyāṇāṃ śarīrāṇi śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c bhittvā praharatāṃ śreṣṭho videhāsūṃś cakāra saḥ
a śatrupravīrair astāni nānāśastrāṇi sāyakaiḥ
c bhittvā tān ahanat pāṇḍyaḥ śatrūñ śakra ivāsurān
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a proktas tvayā pūrvam eva pravīro lokaviśrutaḥ
c na tv asya karma saṃgrāme tvayā saṃjaya kīrtitam
a tasya vistarato brūhi pravīrasyādya vikramam
c śikṣāṃ prabhāvaṃ vīryaṃ ca pramāṇaṃ darpam eva ca
 saṃjaya uvāca
a droṇabhīṣmakṛpadrauṇikarṇārjunajanārdanān
c samāptavidyān dhanuṣi śreṣṭhān yān manyase yudhi
d yo hy ākṣipati vīryeṇa sarvān etān mahārathān
d na mene cātmanā tulyaṃ kaṃ cid eva nareśvaram
a tulyatā karṇabhīṣmābhyām ātmano yena dṛśyate
c vāsudevārjunābhyāṃ ca nyūnatāṃ nātmanīcchati
a sa pāṇḍyo nṛpatiśreṣṭhaḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
c karṇasyānīkam avadhīt paribhūta ivāntakaḥ
a tad udīrṇarathāśvaṃ ca pattipravarakuñjaram
c kulālacakravad bhrāntaṃ pāṇḍyenādhiṣṭhitaṃ balam
a vyaśvasūtadhvajarathān vipraviddhāyudhān ripūn
c samyag astaiḥ śaraiḥ pāṇḍyo vāyur meghān ivākṣipat
a dviradān prahataprothān vipatākadhvajāyudhān
c sapādarakṣān avadhīd vajreṇārīn ivārihā
a saśaktiprāsatūṇīrān aśvārohān hayān api
c pulindakhaśabāhlīkān niṣādān dhrakataṅgaṇān
a dākṣiṇātyāṃś ca bhojāṃś ca krūrān saṃgrāmakarkaśān
c viśastrakavacān bāṇaiḥ kṛtvā pāṇḍyo 'karod vyasūn
a caturaṅgaṃ balaṃ bāṇair nighnantaṃ pāṇḍyam āhave
c dṛṣṭvā drauṇir asaṃbhrāntam asaṃbhrāntataro 'bhyayāt
a ābhāṣya cainaṃ madhuram abhi nṛtyann abhītavat
c prāha praharatāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ smitapūrvaṃ samāhvayan
a rājan kamalapatrākṣa pradhānāyudhavāhana
c vajrasaṃhananaprakhya pradhānabalapauruṣa
a muṣṭiśliṣṭāyudhābhyāṃ ca vyāyatābhyāṃ mahad dhanuḥ
c dorbhyāṃ visphārayan bhāsi mahājaladavad bhṛśam
a śaravarṣair mahāvegair amitrān abhivarṣataḥ
c mad anyaṃ nānupaśyāmi prativīraṃ tavāhave
a rathadviradapattyaśvān ekaḥ pramathase bahūn
c mṛgasaṃghān ivāraṇye vibhīr bhīmabalo hariḥ
a mahatā rathaghoṣeṇa divaṃ bhūmiṃ ca nādayan
c varṣānte sasyahā pītho bhābhir āpūrayann iva
a saṃspṛśānaḥ śarāṃs tīkṣṇāṃs tūṇād āśīviṣopamān
c mayaivaikena yudhyasva tryambakeṇāndhako yathā
a evam uktas tathety uktvā prahareti ca tāḍitaḥ
c karṇinā droṇatanayaṃ vivyādha malayadhvajaḥ
a marmabhedibhir atyugrair bāṇair agniśikhopamaiḥ
c smayann abhyahanad drauṇiḥ pāṇḍyam ācāryasattamaḥ
a tato navāparāṃs tīkṣṇān nārācān kaṅkavāsasaḥ
c gatyā daśamyā saṃyuktān aśvatthāmā vyavāsṛjat
a teṣāṃ pañcācchinat pāṇḍyaḥ pañcabhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c catvāro 'bhyāhanan vāhān āśu te vyasavo 'bhavan
a atha droṇasutasyeṣūṃs tāṃś chittvā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c dhanurjyāṃ vitatāṃ pāṇḍyaś cicchedādityavarcasaḥ
a vijyaṃ dhanur athādhijyaṃ kṛtvā drauṇir amitrahā
b prekṣya cāśu rathe yuktān narair anyān hayottamān
c tataḥ śarasahasrāṇi preṣayām āsa pāṇḍyataḥ
e iṣusaṃbādham ākāśam akarod diśa eva ca
a tatas tān asyataḥ sarvān drauṇer bāṇān mahātmanaḥ
c jānāno 'py akṣayān pāṇḍyo 'śātayat puruṣarṣabhaḥ
a prahitāṃs tān prayatnena chittvā drauṇer iṣūn ariḥ
c cakrarakṣau tatas tasya prāṇudan niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a athārer lāghavaṃ dṛṣṭvā maṇḍalīkṛtakārmukaḥ
c prāsyad droṇasuto bāṇān vṛṣṭiṃ pūṣānujo yathā
a aṣṭāv aṣṭagavāny ūhuḥ śakaṭāni yad āyudham
c ahnas tad aṣṭabhāgena drauṇiś cikṣepa māriṣa
a tam antakam iva kruddham antakālāntakopamam
c ye ye dadṛśire tatra visaṃjñāḥ prāyaśo 'bhavan
a parjanya iva gharmānte vṛṣṭyā sādridrumāṃ mahīm
c ācāryaputras tāṃ senāṃ bāṇavṛṣṭyābhyavīvṛṣat
a drauṇiparjanyamuktāṃ tāṃ bāṇavṛṣṭiṃ suduḥsahām
c vāyavyāstreṇa sa kṣipraṃ ruddhvā pāṇḍyānilo 'nadat
a tasya nānadataḥ ketuṃ candanāgurubhūṣitam
c malayapratimaṃ drauṇiś chittvāśvāṃś caturo 'hanat
a sūtam ekeṣuṇā hatvā mahājaladanisvanam
c dhanuś chittvārdhacandreṇa vyadhamat tilaśo ratham
a astrair astrāṇi saṃvārya chittvā sarvāyudhāni ca
c prāptam apy ahitaṃ drauṇir na jaghāna raṇepsayā
d etasminn antare karṇo gajānīkam upādravat
d drāvayām āsa sa tadā pāṇḍavānāṃ mahad balam
d virathān rathinaś cakre gajān aśvāṃś ca bhārata
d gajān bahubhir ānarchac charaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
d atha drauṇir maheṣvāsaḥ pāṇḍyaṃ śatrunibarhaṇam
d virathaṃ rathināṃ śreṣṭhaṃ nāhanad yuddhakāṅkṣayā
a hateśvaro dantivaraḥ sukalpitas
tvarābhisṛṣṭaḥ pratiśarmago balī
b tam ādravad drauṇiśarāhatas tvarañ
b javena kṛtvā pratihastigarjitam
b taṃ vāraṇaṃ vāraṇayuddhakovido
b dvipottamaṃ parvatasānusaṃnibham
c tam adhyatiṣṭhan malayeśvaro mahān
yathādriśṛṅgaṃ harir unnadaṃs tathā
a sa tomaraṃ bhāskararaśmisaṃnibhaṃ
balāstrasargottamayatnamanyubhiḥ
c sasarja śīghraṃ pratipīḍayan gajaṃ
guroḥ sutāyādripatīśvaro nadan
a maṇipratānottamavajrahāṭakair
alaṃkṛtaṃ cāṃśukamālyamauktikaiḥ
c hato 'sy asāv ity asakṛn mudā nadan
parābhinad drauṇivarāṅgabhūṣaṇam
a tad arkacandragrahapāvakatviṣaṃ
bhṛśābhighātāt patitaṃ vicūrṇitam
c mahendravajrābhihataṃ mahāvanaṃ
yathādriśṛṅgaṃ dharaṇītale tathā
a tataḥ prajajvāla pareṇa manyunā
padāhato nāgapatir yathā tathā
c samādadhe cāntakadaṇḍasaṃnibhān
iṣūn amitrāntakarāṃś caturdaśa
a dvipasya pādāgrakarān sa pañcabhir
nṛpasya bāhū ca śiro 'tha ca tribhiḥ
c jaghāna ṣaḍbhiḥ ṣaḍ ṛtūttamatviṣaḥ
sa pāṇḍyarājānucarān mahārathān
a sudīrghavṛttau varacandanokṣitau
suvarṇamuktāmaṇivajrabhūṣitau
c bhujau dharāyāṃ patitau nṛpasya tau
viveṣṭatus tārkṣyahatāv ivoragau
a śiraś ca tat pūrṇaśaśiprabhānanaṃ
saroṣatāmrāyatanetram unnasam
c kṣitau vibabhrāja patat sakuṇḍalaṃ
viśākhayor madhyagataḥ śaśī yathā
d sa tu dvipaḥ pañcabhir uttameṣubhiḥ
d kṛtaḥ ṣaḍaṃśaś caturo nṛpas tribhiḥ
d kṛto daśāṃśaḥ kuśalena yudhyatā
d yathā havis tad daśadaivataṃ tathā
d sa pādaśo rākṣasabhojanān bahūn
d pradāya pāṇḍyo 'śvamanuṣyakuñjarān
d svadhām ivāpya jvalanaḥ pitṛpriyas
d tataḥ praśāntaḥ salilapravāhataḥ
a samāptavidyaṃ tu guroḥ sutaṃ nṛpaḥ
samāptakarmāṇam upetya te sutaḥ
c suhṛdvṛto 'tyartham apūjayan mudā
jite balau viṣṇum ivāmareśvaraḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a pāṇḍye hate kim akarod arjuno yudhi saṃjaya
c ekavīreṇa karṇena drāviteṣu pareṣu ca
a samāptavidyo balavān yukto vīraś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
c sarvabhūteṣv anujñātaḥ śaṃkareṇa mahātmanā
a tasmān mahad bhayaṃ tīvram amitraghnād dhanaṃjayāt
c sa yat tatrākarot pārthas tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
 saṃjaya uvāca
a hate pāṇḍye 'rjunaṃ kṛṣṇas tvarann āha vaco hitam
c paśyātimānyaṃ rājānam apayātāṃś ca pāṇḍavān
a aśvatthāmnaś ca saṃkalpād dhatāḥ karṇena sṛñjayāḥ
c tathāśvanaranāgānāṃ kṛtaṃ ca kadanaṃ mahat
e ity ācaṣṭa sudurdharṣo vāsudevaḥ kirīṭine
a etac chrutvā ca dṛṣṭvā ca bhrātur ghoraṃ mahad bhayam
c vāhayāśvān hṛṣīkeśa kṣipram ity āha pāṇḍavaḥ
a tataḥ prāyād dhṛṣīkeśo rathenāpratiyodhinā
b tadā reṇuḥ samabhavat punas tatra mahāraṇe
c dāruṇaś ca punas tatra prādurāsīt samāgamaḥ
d tataḥ punaḥ samājagmur abhītāḥ kurupāṇḍavāḥ
d bhīmasenamukhāḥ pārthāḥ sūtaputramukhā vayam
a tataḥ pravavṛte bhūyaḥ saṃgrāmo rājasattama
c karṇasya pāṇḍavānāṃ ca yamarāṣṭravivardhanaḥ
a dhanūṃṣi bāṇān parighān asitomarapaṭṭiśān
c musalāni bhuśuṇḍīś ca śaktiṛṣṭiparaśvadhān
a gadāḥ prāsān asīn kuntān bhiṇḍipālān mahāṅkuśān
c pragṛhya kṣipram āpetuḥ parasparajigīṣayā
a bāṇajyātalaśabdena dyāṃ diśaḥ pradiśo viyat
c pṛthivīṃ nemighoṣeṇa nādayanto 'bhyayuḥ parān
a tena śabdena mahatā saṃhṛṣṭāś cakrur āhavam
c vīrā vīrair mahāghoraṃ kalahāntaṃ titīrṣavaḥ
a jyātalatradhanuḥśabdāḥ kuñjarāṇāṃ ca bṛṃhitam
c tāḍitānāṃ ca patatāṃ ninādaḥ sumahān abhūt
a bāṇaśabdāṃś ca vividhāñ śūrāṇām abhigarjatām
c śrutvā śabdaṃ bhṛśaṃ tresur jaghnur mamluś ca bhārata
a teṣāṃ nānadyatāṃ caiva śastravṛṣṭiṃ ca muñcatām
c bahūn ādhirathiḥ karṇaḥ pramamātha raṇeṣubhiḥ
a pañca pāñcālavīrāṇāṃ rathān daśa ca pañca ca
c sāśvasūtadhvajān karṇaḥ śarair ninye yamakṣayam
a yodhamukhyā mahāvīryāḥ pāṇḍūnāṃ karṇam āhave
c śīghrāstrā divam āvṛtya parivavruḥ samantataḥ
a tataḥ karṇo dviṣatsenāṃ śaravarṣair viloḍayan
c vijagāhe 'ṇḍajāpūrṇāṃ padminīm iva yūthapaḥ
a dviṣanmadhyam avaskandya rādheyo dhanur uttamam
c vidhunvānaḥ śitair bāṇaiḥ śirāṃsy unmathya pātayat
d hastinaḥ sumahāmātrān sāśvārohān hayān api
d rathino 'py ekabāṇena bhramataś cāvapātayat
a carmavarmāṇi saṃchindya nirvāpam iva dehinām
c viṣehur nāsya saṃparkaṃ dvitīyasya patatriṇaḥ
a varmadehāsumathanair dhanuṣaḥ pracyutaiḥ śaraiḥ
c maurvyā talatrair nyavadhīt kaśayā vājino yathā
a pāṇḍusṛñjayapāñcālāñ śaragocaram ānayat
c mamarda karṇas tarasā siṃho mṛgagaṇān iva
a tataḥ pāñcālaputrāś ca draupadeyāś ca māriṣa
c yamau ca yuyudhānaś ca sahitāḥ karṇam abhyayuḥ
a vyāyacchamānāḥ subhṛśaṃ kurupāṇḍavasṛñjayāḥ
c priyān asūn raṇe tyaktvā yodhā jagmuḥ parasparam
a susaṃnaddhāḥ kavacinaḥ saśirastrāṇabhūṣaṇāḥ
c gadābhir musalaiś cānye parighaiś ca mahārathāḥ
a samabhyadhāvanta bhṛśaṃ devā daṇḍair ivodyataiḥ
c nadantaś cāhvayantaś ca pravalgantaś ca māriṣa
a tato nijaghnur anyonyaṃ petuś cāhavatāḍitāḥ
c vamanto rudhiraṃ gātrair vimastiṣkekṣaṇā yudhi
a dantapūrṇaiḥ sarudhirair vaktrair dāḍimasaṃnibhaiḥ
c jīvanta iva cāpy ete tasthuḥ śastropabṛṃhitāḥ
a parasparaṃ cāpy apare paṭṭiśair asibhis tathā
c śaktibhir bhiṇḍipālaiś ca nakharaprāsatomaraiḥ
a tatakṣuś cicchiduś cānye bibhiduś cikṣipus tathā
c saṃcakartuś ca jaghnuś ca kruddhā nirbibhiduś ca ha
a petur anyonyanihatā vyasavo rudhirokṣitāḥ
c kṣarantaḥ svarasaṃ raktaṃ prakṛtāś candanā iva
a rathai rathā vinihatā hastinaś cāpi hastibhiḥ
c narā naravaraiḥ petur aśvāś cāśvaiḥ sahasraśaḥ
a dhvajāḥ śirāṃsi cchatrāṇi dvipahastā nṛṇāṃ bhujāḥ
c kṣurair bhallārdhacandraiś ca chinnāḥ śastrāṇi tatyajuḥ
d vadhyatāṃ dāruṇaḥ śabdaḥ patatāṃ stanatām api
d narāśvebharathānāṃ hi narāśvebharathais tadā
a narāṃś ca nāgāṃś ca rathān hayān mamṛdur āhave
b tathā hatā rathāḥ petur aśvārohaiḥ sahasraśaḥ
c aśvārohair hatāḥ śūrāś chinnahastāś ca dantinaḥ
a sapatākā dhvajāḥ petur viśīrṇā iva parvatāḥ
c pattibhiś ca samāplutya dviradāḥ syandanās tathā
a prahatā hanyamānāś ca patitāś caiva sarvaśaḥ
c aśvārohāḥ samāsādya tvaritāḥ pattibhir hatāḥ
e sādibhiḥ pattisaṃghāś ca nihatā yudhi śerate
a mṛditānīva padmāni pramlānā iva ca srajaḥ
c hatānāṃ vadanāny āsan gātrāṇi ca mahāmate
a rūpāṇy atyarthakāmyāni dviradāśvanṛṇāṃ nṛpa
c samunnānīva vastrāṇi prāpur durdarśatāṃ param
d tathaiva mukhavarṇaś ca keṣāṃ cit tatra dṛśyate
d madād iva prasuptānāṃ vikṣiptābharaṇasrajām
 saṃjaya uvāca
a hastibhis tu mahāmātrās tava putreṇa coditāḥ
c dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ jighāṃsantaḥ kruddhāḥ pārṣatam abhyayuḥ
a prācyāś ca dākṣiṇātyāś ca pravīrā gajayodhinaḥ
c aṅgā vaṅgāś ca puṇḍrāś ca māgadhās tāmraliptakāḥ
a mekalāḥ kośalā madrā daśārṇā niṣadhās tathā
c gajayuddheṣu kuśalāḥ kaliṅgaiḥ saha bhārata
a śaratomaranārācair vṛṣṭimanta ivāmbudāḥ
c siṣicus te tataḥ sarve pāñcālācalam āhave
a tān saṃmimardiṣur nāgān pārṣṇyaṅguṣṭhāṅkuśair bhṛśam
c pothitān pārṣato bāṇair nārācaiś cābhyavīvṛṣat
a ekaikaṃ daśabhiḥ ṣaḍbhir aṣṭābhir api bhārata
c dviradān abhivivyādha kṣiptair girinibhāñ śaraiḥ
e pracchādyamāno dviradair meghair iva divākaraḥ
a paryāsuḥ pāṇḍupāñcālā nadanto niśitāyudhāḥ
c tān nāgān abhivarṣanto jyātantrīśaranāditaiḥ
d vīranṛtyaṃ pranṛtyantaḥ śūratālapracoditaiḥ
a nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca draupadeyāḥ prabhadrakāḥ
c sātyakiś ca śikhaṇḍī ca cekitānaś ca vīryavān
d samantāt siṣicur vīrā meghās toyair ivācalān
a te mlecchaiḥ preṣitā nāgā narān aśvān rathān api
c hastair ākṣipya mamṛduḥ padbhiś cāpy atimanyavaḥ
a bibhiduś ca viṣāṇāgraiḥ samākṣipya ca cikṣipuḥ
c viṣāṇalagnaiś cāpy anye paripetur vibhīṣaṇāḥ
a pramukhe vartamānaṃ tu dvipaṃ vaṅgasya sātyakiḥ
c nārācenogravegena bhittvā marmaṇy apātayat
a tasyāvarjitanāgasya dviradād utpatiṣyataḥ
c nārācenābhinad vakṣaḥ so 'patad bhuvi sātyakeḥ
a puṇḍrasyāpatato nāgaṃ calantam iva parvatam
c sahadevaḥ prayatnāt tair nārācair vyahanat tribhiḥ
a vipatākaṃ viyantāraṃ vivarmadhvajajīvitam
c taṃ kṛtvā dviradaṃ bhūyaḥ sahadevo 'ṅgam abhyagāt
a sahadevaṃ tu nakulo vārayitvāṅgam ārdayat
c nārācair yamadaṇḍābhais tribhir nāgaṃ śatena ca
a divākarakaraprakhyān aṅgaś cikṣepa tomarān
c nakulāya śatāny aṣṭau tridhaikaikaṃ tu so 'cchinat
a tathārdhacandreṇa śiras tasya ciccheda pāṇḍavaḥ
c sa papāta hato mlecchas tenaiva saha dantinā
a ācāryaputre nihate hastiśikṣāviśārade
c aṅgāḥ kruddhā mahāmātrā nāgair nakulam abhyayuḥ
a calatpatākaiḥ pramukhair hemakakṣyātanucchadaiḥ
c mimardiśantas tvaritāḥ pradīptair iva parvataiḥ
a mekalotkalakāliṅgā niṣādās tāmraliptakāḥ
c śaratomaravarṣāṇi vimuñcanto jighāṃsavaḥ
a taiś chādyamānaṃ nakulaṃ divākaram ivāmbudaiḥ
c pari petuḥ susaṃrabdhāḥ pāṇḍupāñcālasomakāḥ
a tatas tad abhavad yuddhaṃ rathināṃ hastibhiḥ saha
c sṛjatāṃ śaravarṣāṇi tomarāṃś ca sahasraśaḥ
a nāgānāṃ prasphuṭuḥ kumbhā marmāṇi vividhāni ca
c dantāś caivātividdhānāṃ nārācair bhūṣaṇāni ca
a teṣām aṣṭau mahānāgāṃś catuḥṣaṣṭyā sutejanaiḥ
c sahadevo jaghānāśu te petuḥ saha sādibhiḥ
a añjogatibhir āyamya prayatnād dhanur uttamam
c nārācair ahanan nāgān nakulaḥ kuranandana
a tataḥ śaineyapāñcālyau draupadeyāḥ prabhadrakāḥ
c śikhaṇḍī ca mahānāgān siṣicuḥ śaravṛṣṭibhiḥ
a te pāṇḍuyodhāmbudharaiḥ śatrudviradaparvatāḥ
c bāṇavarṣair hatāḥ petur vajravarṣair ivācalāḥ
a evaṃ hatvā tava gajāṃs te pāṇḍunarakuñjarāḥ
c drutaṃ senām avaikṣanta bhinnakūlām ivāpagām
a te tāṃ senām avālokya pāṇḍuputrasya sainikāḥ
c vikṣobhayitvā ca punaḥ karṇam evābhidudruvuḥ
a sahadevaṃ tataḥ kruddhaṃ dahantaṃ tava vāhinīm
c duḥśāsano mahārāja bhrātā bhrātaram abhyayāt
a tau sametau mahāyuddhe dṛṣṭvā tatra narādhipāḥ
c siṃhanādaravāṃś cakrur vāsāṃsy ādudhuvuś ca ha
a tato bhārata kruddhena tava putreṇa dhanvinā
c pāṇḍuputras tribhir bāṇair vakṣasy abhihato balī
a sahadevas tato rājan nārācena tavātmajam
c viddhvā vivyādha saptatyā sārathiṃ ca tribhis tribhiḥ
a duḥśāsanas tadā rājaṃś chittvā cāpaṃ mahāhave
c sahadevaṃ trisaptatyā bāhvor urasi cārdayat
a sahadevas tataḥ kruddhaḥ khaḍgaṃ gṛhya mahāhave
c vyāvidhyata yudhāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ śrīmāṃs tava sutaṃ prati
a samārgaṇagaṇaṃ cāpaṃ chittvā tasya mahān asiḥ
c nipapāta tato bhūmau cyutaḥ sarpa ivāmbarāt
a athānyad dhanur ādāya sahadevaḥ pratāpavān
c duḥśāsanāya cikṣepa bāṇam antakaraṃ tataḥ
a tam āpatantaṃ viśikhaṃ yamadaṇḍopamatviṣam
c khaḍgena śitadhāreṇa dvidhā ciccheda kauravaḥ
d tatas taṃ niśitaṃ khaḍgam āvidhya yudhi satvaraḥ
d dhanuś cānyat samādāya śaraṃ jagrāha vīryavān
a tam āpatantaṃ sahasā nistriṃśaṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c pātayām āsa samare sahadevo hasann iva
a tato bāṇāṃś catuḥṣaṣṭiṃ tava putro mahāraṇe
c sahadevarathe tūrṇaṃ pātayām āsa bhārata
a tāñ śarān samare rājan vegenāpatato bahūn
c ekaikaṃ pañcabhir bāṇaiḥ sahadevo nyakṛntata
a sa nivārya mahābāṇāṃs tava putreṇa preṣitān
c athāsmai subahūn bāṇān mādrīputraḥ samācinot
c   preṣayām āsa saṃyuge
c tān bāṇāṃs tava putro 'pi chittvaikaikaṃ tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
c nanāda sumahānādaṃ dārayāṇo vasuṃdharām
c tato duḥśāsano rājan viddhvā pāṇḍusutaṃ raṇe
c sārathiṃ navabhir bāṇair
a tataḥ kruddho mahārāja sahadevaḥ pratāpavān
c samādhatta śaraṃ ghoraṃ mṛtyukālāntakopamam
e vikṛṣya balavac cāpaṃ tava putrāya so 'sṛjat
a sa taṃ nirbhidya vegena bhittvā ca kavacaṃ mahat
c prāviśad dharaṇīṃ rājan valmīkam iva pannagaḥ
e tataḥ sa mumuhe rājaṃs tava putro mahārathaḥ
a mūḍhaṃ cainaṃ samālakṣya sārathis tvarito ratham
c apovāha bhṛśaṃ trasto vadhyamānaṃ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
d nādas tu sumahān āsīn nādayan vai vasuṃdharām
a parājitya raṇe taṃ tu pāṇḍavaḥ pāṇḍupūrvaja
c duryodhanabalaṃ hṛṣṭaḥ prāmathad vai samantataḥ
a pipīlikāpuṭaṃ rājan yathāmṛdnān naro ruṣā
c tathā sā kauravī senā mṛditā tena bhārata
a nakulaṃ rabhasaṃ yuddhe dārayantaṃ varūthinīm
c karṇo vaikartano rājan vārayām āsa vai tadā
a nakulaś ca tadā karṇaṃ prahasann idam abravīt
c cirasya bata dṛṣṭo 'haṃ daivataiḥ saumyacakṣuṣā
a yasya me tvaṃ raṇe pāpa cakṣurviṣayam āgataḥ
c tvaṃ hi mūlam anarthānāṃ vairasya kalahasya ca
a tvaddoṣāt kuravaḥ kṣīṇāḥ samāsādya parasparam
c tvām adya samare hatvā kṛtakṛtyo 'smi vijvaraḥ
a evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca nakulaṃ sūtanandanaḥ
c sadṛśaṃ rājaputrasya dhanvinaś ca viśeṣataḥ
a praharasva raṇe bāla paśyāmas tava pauruṣam
c karma kṛtvā raṇe śūra tataḥ katthitum arhasi
a anuktvā samare tāta śūrā yudhyanti śaktitaḥ
c sa yudhyasva mayā śaktyā vineṣye darpam adya te
a ity uktvā prāharat tūrṇaṃ pāṇḍuputrāya sūtajaḥ
c vivyādha cainaṃ samare trisaptatyā śilīmukhaiḥ
a nakulas tu tato viddhaḥ sūtaputreṇa bhārata
c aśītyāśīviṣaprakhyaiḥ sūtaputram avidhyata
a tasya karṇo dhanuś chittvā svarṇapuṅkhaiḥ śilāśitaiḥ
c triṃśatā parameṣvāsaḥ śaraiḥ pāṇḍavam ārdayat
a te tasya kavacaṃ bhittvā papuḥ śoṇitam āhave
c āśīviṣā yathā nāgā bhittvā gāṃ salilaṃ papuḥ
a athānyad dhanur ādāya hemapṛṣṭhaṃ durāsadam
c karṇaṃ vivyādha viṃśatyā sārathiṃ ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
a tataḥ kruddho mahārāja nakulaḥ paravīrahā
c kṣurapreṇa sutīkṣṇena karṇasya dhanur acchinat
a athainaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ sāyakānāṃ śatais tribhiḥ
c ājaghne prahasan vīraḥ sarvalokamahāratham
a karṇam abhyarditaṃ dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍuputreṇa māriṣa
c vismayaṃ paramaṃ jagmū rathinaḥ saha daivataiḥ
a athānyad dhanur ādāya karṇo vaikartanas tadā
c nakulaṃ pañcabhir bāṇair jatrudeśe samārdayat
a uraḥsthair atha tair bāṇair mādrīputro vyarocata
c svaraśmibhir ivādityo bhuvane visṛjan prabhām
a nakulas tu tataḥ karṇaṃ viddhvā saptabhir āyasaiḥ
c athāsya dhanuṣaḥ koṭiṃ punaś ciccheda māriṣa
a so 'nyat kārmukam ādāya samare vegavattaram
c nakulasya tato bāṇaiḥ sarvato 'vārayad diśaḥ
a saṃchādyamānaḥ sahasā karṇacāpacyutaiḥ śaraiḥ
c ciccheda sa śarāṃs tūrṇaṃ śarair eva mahārathaḥ
a tato bāṇamayaṃ jālaṃ vitataṃ vyomny adṛśyata
c khadyotānāṃ gaṇair eva saṃpatadbhir yathā nabhaḥ
a tair vimuktaiḥ śaraśataiś chāditaṃ gaganaṃ tadā
c śalabhānāṃ yathā vrātais tadvad āsīt samākulam
a te śarā hemavikṛtāḥ saṃpatanto muhur muhuḥ
c śreṇīkṛtā abhāsanta haṃsāḥ śreṇīgatā iva
a bāṇajālāvṛte vyomni chādite ca divākare
c samasarpat tato bhūtaṃ kiṃ cid eva viśāṃ pate
a niruddhe tatra mārge tu śarasaṃghaiḥ samantataḥ
c vyarocatāṃ mahābhāgau bālasūryāv ivoditau
a karṇacāpacyutair bāṇair vadhyamānās tu somakāḥ
c avālīyanta rājendra vedanārtāḥ śarārditāḥ
a nakulasya tathā bāṇair vadhyamānā camūs tava
c vyaśīryata diśo rājan vātanunnā ivāmbudāḥ
a te sene vadhyamāne tu tābhyāṃ divyair mahāśaraiḥ
c śarapātam apakramya tataḥ prekṣakavat sthite
a protsārite jane tasmin karṇapāṇḍavayoḥ śaraiḥ
c vivyādhāte mahātmānāv anyonyaṃ śaravṛṣṭibhiḥ
a nidarśayantau tv astrāṇi divyāni raṇamūrdhani
c chādayantau ca sahasā parasparavadhaiṣiṇau
a nakulena śarā muktāḥ kaṅkabarhiṇavāsasaḥ
c te tu karṇam avacchādya vyatiṣṭhanta yathā pare
d tathaiva sūtaputreṇa preṣitāḥ paramāhave
d pāṇḍuputram avacchādya vyatiṣṭhantāmbare śarāḥ
a śaraveśmapraviṣṭau tau dadṛśāte na kaiś cana
c candrasūryau yathā rājaṃś chādyamānau jalāgame
a tataḥ kruddho raṇe karṇaḥ kṛtvā ghorataraṃ vapuḥ
c pāṇḍavaṃ chādayām āsa samantāc charavṛṣṭibhiḥ
a sa cchādyamānaḥ samare sūtaputreṇa pāṇḍavaḥ
c na cakāra vyathāṃ rājan bhāskaro jaladair yathā
a tataḥ prahasyādhirathiḥ śarajālāni māriṣa
c preṣayām āsa samare śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a ekacchāyam abhūt sarvaṃ tasya bāṇair mahātmanaḥ
c abhracchāyeva saṃjajñe saṃpatadbhiḥ śarottamaiḥ
a tataḥ karṇo mahārāja dhanuś chittvā mahātmanaḥ
c sārathiṃ pātayām āsa rathanīḍād dhasann iva
a tathāśvāṃś caturaś cāsya caturbhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c yamasya sadanaṃ tūrṇaṃ preṣayām āsa bhārata
a athāsya taṃ rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ tilaśo vyadhamac charaiḥ
c patākāṃ cakrarakṣau ca dhvajaṃ khaḍgaṃ ca māriṣa
e śatacandraṃ tataś carma sarvopakaraṇāni ca
f suvarṇavikṛtaṃ tac ca dhanuḥ saśaram āhave
a hatāśvo virathaś caiva vivarmā ca viśāṃ pate
c avatīrya rathāt tūrṇaṃ parighaṃ gṛhya viṣṭhitaḥ
a tam udyataṃ mahāghoraṃ parighaṃ tasya sūtajaḥ
c vyahanat sāyakai rājañ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a vyāyudhaṃ cainam ālakṣya śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c ārdayad bahuśaḥ karṇo na cainaṃ samapīḍayat
a sa vadhyamānaḥ samare kṛtāstreṇa balīyasā
c prādravat sahasā rājan nakulo vyākulendriyaḥ
a tam abhidrutya rādheyaḥ prahasan vai punaḥ punaḥ
c sajyam asya dhanuḥ kaṇṭhe so 'vāsṛjata bhārata
a tataḥ sa śuśubhe rājan kaṇṭhāsaktamahādhanuḥ
c pariveṣam anuprāpto yathā syād vyomni candramāḥ
e yathaiva ca sito meghaḥ śakracāpena śobhitaḥ
f aśobhata mahārāja pāṇḍuputras tathā raṇe
a tam abravīt tadā karṇo vyarthaṃ vyāhṛtavān asi
c vadedānīṃ punar hṛṣṭo vadhyaṃ māṃ tvaṃ punaḥ punaḥ
a mā yotsīr gurubhiḥ sārdhaṃ balavadbhiś ca pāṇḍava
c sadṛśais tāta yudhyasva vrīḍāṃ mā kuru pāṇḍava
e gṛhaṃ vā gaccha mādreya yatra vā kṛṣṇaphalgunau
a evam uktvā mahārāja vyasarjayata taṃ tataḥ
c vadhaprāptaṃ tu taṃ rājan nāvadhīt sūtanandanaḥ
e smṛtvā kuntyā vaco rājaṃs tata enaṃ vyasarjayat
a visṛṣṭaḥ pāṇḍavo rājan sūtaputreṇa dhanvinā
c vrīḍann iva jagāmātha yudhiṣṭhirarathaṃ prati
a āruroha rathaṃ cāpi sūtaputrapratāpitaḥ
c niḥśvasan duḥkhasaṃtaptaḥ kumbhe kṣipta ivoragaḥ
a taṃ visṛjya raṇe karṇaḥ pāñcālāṃs tvarito yayau
c rathenātipatākena candravarṇahayena ca
a tatrākrando mahān āsīt pāṇḍavānāṃ viśāṃ pate
c dṛṣṭvā senāpatiṃ yāntaṃ pāñcālānāṃ rathavrajān
a tatrākaron mahārāja kadanaṃ sūtanandanaḥ
c madhyaṃ gate dinakare cakravat pracaran prabhuḥ
a bhagnacakrai rathaiḥ ke cic chinnadhvajapatākibhiḥ
c sasūtair hatasūtaiś ca bhagnākṣaiś caiva māriṣa
e hriyamāṇān apaśyāma pāñcālānāṃ rathavrajān
a tatra tatra ca saṃbhrāntā vicerur mattakuñjarāḥ
c davāgninā parītāṅgā yathaiva syur mahāvane
a bhinnakumbhā virudhirāś chinnahastāś ca vāraṇāḥ
c bhinnagātravarāś caiva cchinnavālāś ca māriṣa
e chinnābhrāṇīva saṃpetur vadhyamānā mahātmanā
a apare trāsitā nāgā nārācaśatatomaraiḥ
c tam evābhimukhā yānti śalabhā iva pāvakam
a apare niṣṭanantaḥ sma vyadṛśyanta mahādvipāḥ
c kṣarantaḥ śoṇitaṃ gātrair nagā iva jalaplavam
a uraśchadair vimuktāś ca vālabandhaiś ca vājinaḥ
c rājataiś ca tathā kāṃsyaiḥ sauvarṇaiś caiva bhūṣaṇaiḥ
a hīnā āstaraṇaiś caiva khalīnaiś ca vivarjitāḥ
c cāmaraiś ca kuthābhiś ca tūṇīraiḥ patitair api
a nihataiḥ sādibhiś caiva śūrair āhavaśobhibhiḥ
b vātāyamānān sahasā prapaśyāma hayottamān
c apaśyāma raṇe tatra bhrāmyamāṇān hayottamān
a prāsaiḥ khaḍgaiś ca saṃsyūtān ṛṣṭibhiś ca narādhipa
c hayayodhān apaśyāma kañcukoṣṇīṣadhāriṇaḥ
d nihatān vadhyamānāṃś ca vepamānāṃś ca bhārata
d nānāṅgāvayavair hīnāṃs tatra tatraiva bhārata
d vihayān sahayāṃś cāpi veṣṭamānāṃs tatas tataḥ
a rathān hemapariṣkārān suyuktāñ javanair hayaiḥ
c bhramamāṇān apaśyāma hateṣu rathiṣu drutam
a bhagnākṣakūbarān kāṃś cic chinnacakrāṃś ca māriṣa
c vipatākādhvajāṃś cānyāñ chinneṣāyugabandhurān
a vihīnān rathinas tatra dhāvamānān samantataḥ
b rathāṃs tu tatra vicchinnāṃs tilaśaḥ karṇavikramaiḥ
c sūryaputraśarais trastān apaśyāma viśāṃ pate
a viśastrāṃś ca tathaivānyān saśastrāṃś ca bahūn hatān
c tāvakāñ jālasaṃchannān uroghaṇṭāvibhūṣitān
a nānāvarṇavicitrābhiḥ patākābhir alaṃkṛtān
c padātīn anvapaśyāma dhāvamānān samantataḥ
a śirāṃsi bāhūn ūrūṃś ca chinnān anyāṃs tathā yudhi
b chinnāñ śarais tathā bāhūn ūrūś cāpāñ janādhipa
b śirobhir bāhubhiś chinnaiś citrair ūrubhir eva ca
c karṇacāpacyutair bāṇair apaśyāma vinākṛtān
a mahān vyatikaro raudro yodhānām anvadṛśyata
c karṇasāyakanunnānāṃ hatānāṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a te vadhyamānāḥ samare sūtaputreṇa sṛñjayāḥ
c tam evābhimukhā yānti pataṃgā iva pāvakam
a taṃ dahantam anīkāni tatra tatra mahāratham
c kṣatriyā varjayām āsur yugāntāgnim ivolbaṇam
a hataśeṣās tu ye vīrāḥ pāñcālānāṃ mahārathāḥ
c tān prabhagnān drutān karṇaḥ pṛṣṭhato vikirañ śaraiḥ
e abhyadhāvata tejasvī viśīrṇakavacadhvajān
a tāpayām āsa tān bāṇaiḥ sūtaputro mahārathaḥ
c madhyaṃdinam anuprāpto bhūtānīva tamonudaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a yuyutsuṃ tava putraṃ tu prādravantaṃ mahad balam
c ulūko 'bhyapatat tūrṇaṃ tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt
a yuyutsus tu tato rājañ śitadhāreṇa patriṇā
c ulūkaṃ tāḍayām āsa vajreṇendra ivācalam
a ulūkas tu tataḥ kruddhas tava putrasya saṃyuge
c kṣurapreṇa dhanuś chittvā tāḍayām āsa karṇinā
a tad apāsya dhanuś chinnaṃ yuyutsur vegavattaram
c anyad ādatta sumahac cāpaṃ saṃraktalocanaḥ
a śākuniṃ ca tataḥ ṣaṣṭyā vivyādha bharatarṣabha
c sārathiṃ tribhir ānarchat taṃ ca bhūyo vyavidhyata
a ulūkas taṃ tu viṃśatyā viddhvā hemavibhūṣitaiḥ
c athāsya samare kruddho dhvajaṃ ciccheda kāñcanam
a sa cchinnayaṣṭiḥ sumahāñ śīryamāṇo mahādhvajaḥ
c papāta pramukhe rājan yuyutsoḥ kāñcanojjvalaḥ
a dhvajam unmathitaṃ dṛṣṭvā yuyutsuḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
c ulūkaṃ pañcabhir bāṇair ājaghāna stanāntare
a ulūkas tasya bhallena tailadhautena māriṣa
c śiraś ciccheda sahasā yantur bharatasattama
d tac chinnam apatad bhūmau yuyutsoḥ sārathes tadā
d tārārūpaṃ yathā citraṃ nipapāta mahītale
d yantuś ciccheda samare śiraḥ krodhasamanvitaḥ
a jaghāna caturo 'śvāṃś ca taṃ ca vivyādha pañcabhiḥ
c so 'tividdho balavatā pratyapāyād rathāntaram
a taṃ nirjitya raṇe rājann ulūkas tvarito yayau
c pāñcālān sṛñjayāṃś caiva vinighnan niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a śatānīkaṃ mahārāja śrutakarmā sutas tava
c vyaśvasūtarathaṃ cakre nimeṣārdhād asaṃbhramam
a hatāśve tu rathe tiṣṭhañ śatānīko mahābalaḥ
c gadāṃ cikṣepa saṃkruddhas tava putrasya māriṣa
a sā kṛtvā syandanaṃ bhasma hayāṃś caiva sasārathīn
c papāta dharaṇīṃ tūrṇaṃ dārayantīva bhārata
a tāv ubhau virathau vīrau kurūṇāṃ kīrtivardhanau
c apākrametāṃ yuddhārtau prekṣamāṇau parasparam
a putras tu tava saṃbhrānto vivitso ratham āviśat
c śatānīko 'pi tvaritaḥ prativindhyarathaṃ gataḥ
a sutasomas tu śakuniṃ vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c nākampayata saṃrabdho vāryogha iva parvatam
a sutasomas tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā pitur atyantavairiṇam
c śarair anekasāhasraiś chādayām āsa bhārata
a tāñ śarāñ śakunis tūrṇaṃ cicchedānyaiḥ patatribhiḥ
c laghvastraś citrayodhī ca jitakāśī ca saṃyuge
a nivārya samare cāpi śarāṃs tān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c ājaghāna susaṃkruddhaḥ sutasomaṃ tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
a tasyāśvān ketanaṃ sūtaṃ tilaśo vyadhamac charaiḥ
c syālas tava mahāvīryas tatas te cukruśur janāḥ
a hatāśvo virathaś caiva chinnadhanvā ca māriṣa
c dhanvī dhanurvaraṃ gṛhya rathād bhūmāv atiṣṭhata
e vyasṛjat sāyakāṃś caiva svarṇapuṅkhāñ śilāśitān
a chādayām āsur atha te tava syālasya taṃ ratham
c pataṃgānām iva vrātāḥ śaravrātā mahāratham
a rathopasthān samīkṣyāpi vivyathe naiva saubalaḥ
c pramṛdnaṃś ca śarāṃs tāṃs tāñ śaravrātair mahāyaśāḥ
a tatrātuṣyanta yodhāś ca siddhāś cāpi divi sthitāḥ
c sutasomasya tat karma dṛṣṭvāśraddheyam adbhutam
e rathasthaṃ nṛpatiṃ taṃ tu padātiḥ sann ayodhayat
a tasya tīkṣṇair mahāvegair bhallaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c vyahanat kārmukaṃ rājā tūṇīraṃ caiva sarvaśaḥ
a sa cchinnadhanvā samare khaḍgam udyamya nānadan
c vaiḍūryotpalavarṇābhaṃ hastidantamayatsarum
a bhrāmyamāṇaṃ tatas taṃ tu vimalāmbbaravarcasam
c kālopamaṃ tato mene sutasomasya dhīmataḥ
a so 'carat sahasā khaḍgī maṇḍalāni sahasraśaḥ
c caturviṃśan mahārāja śikṣābalasamanvitaḥ
d bhrāntam udbhrāntam āviddham āplutaṃ viplutaṃ sṛtam
d saṃpātaṃ samudīryaṃ ca darśayām āsa saṃyuge
a saubalas tu tatas tasya śarāṃś cikṣepa vīryavān
c tān āpatata evāśu ciccheda paramāsinā
a tataḥ kruddho mahārāja saubalaḥ paravīrahā
c prāhiṇot sutasomasya śarān āśīviṣopamān
a ciccheda tāṃś ca khaḍgena śikṣayā ca balena ca
c darśayaṃl lāghavaṃ yuddhe tārkṣyavīryasamadyutiḥ
a tasya saṃcarato rājan maṇḍalāvartane tadā
c kṣurapreṇa sutīkṣṇena khaḍgaṃ ciccheda suprabham
a sa cchinnaḥ sahasā bhūmau nipapāta mahān asiḥ
c avaśasya sthitaṃ haste taṃ khaḍgaṃ satsaruṃ tadā
a chinnam ājñāya nistriṃśam avaplutya padāni ṣaṭ
b so 'nyat kārmukam ādāya sudṛḍhaṃ vegavattaram
c prāvidhyata tataḥ śeṣaṃ sutasomo mahārathaḥ
a sa cchittvā saguṇaṃ cāpaṃ raṇe tasya mahātmanaḥ
c papāta dharaṇīṃ tūrṇaṃ svarṇavajravibhūṣitaḥ
e sutasomas tato 'gacchac chrutakīrter mahāratham
a saubalo 'pi dhanur gṛhya ghoram anyat suduḥsaham
c abhyayāt pāṇḍavānīkaṃ nighnañ śatrugaṇān bahūn
a tatra nādo mahān āsīt pāṇḍavānāṃ viśāṃ pate
c saubalaṃ samare dṛṣṭvā vicarantam abhītavat
a tāny anīkāni dṛptāni śastravanti mahānti ca
c drāvyamāṇāny adṛśyanta saubalena mahātmanā
a yathā daityacamūṃ rājan devarājo mamarda ha
c tathaiva pāṇḍavīṃ senāṃ saubaleyo vyanāśayat
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ kṛpo rājan vārayām āsa saṃyuge
c yathā dṛptaṃ vane nāgaṃ śarabho vārayed yudhi
a niruddhaḥ pārṣatas tena gautamena balīyasā
c padāt padaṃ vicalituṃ nāśaknot tatra bhārata
a gautamasya vapur dṛṣṭvā dhṛṣṭadyumnarathaṃ prati
c vitresuḥ sarvabhūtāni kṣayaṃ prāptaṃ ca menire
a tatrāvocan vimanaso rathinaḥ sādinas tathā
c droṇasya nidhane nūnaṃ saṃkruddho dvipadāṃ varaḥ
a śāradvato mahātejā divyāstravid udāradhīḥ
c api svasti bhaved adya dhṛṣṭadyumnasya gautamāt
a apīyaṃ vāhinī kṛtsnā mucyeta mahato bhayāt
c apy ayaṃ brāhmaṇaḥ sarvān na no hanyāt samāgatān
a yādṛśaṃ dṛśyate rūpam antakapratimaṃ bhṛśam
c gamiṣyaty adya padavīṃ bhāradvājasya saṃyuge
a ācāryaḥ kṣiprahastaś ca vijayī ca sadā yudhi
c astravān vīryasaṃpannaḥ krodhena ca samanvitaḥ
a pārṣataś ca bhṛśaṃ yuddhe vimukho 'dyāpi lakṣyate
c ity evaṃ vividhā vācas tāvakānāṃ paraiḥ saha
d vyaśrūyanta mahārāja tayos tatra samāgame
d vicerus tatra samare gautamād bhayaśaṃsakāḥ
a viniḥśvasya tataḥ kruddhaḥ kṛpaḥ śāradvato nṛpa
c pārṣataṃ chādayām āsa niśceṣṭaṃ sarvamarmasu
a sa vadhyamānaḥ samare gautamena mahātmanā
c kartavyaṃ na prajānāti mohitaḥ paramāhave

c īdṛśaṃ vyasanaṃ yuddhe na te dṛṣṭaṃ kadā cana

c preṣitā dvijamukhyena marmāṇy uddiśya sarvaśaḥ
a vyāvartaye tatra rathaṃ nadīvegam ivārṇavāt

a dhṛṣṭadyumnas tato rājañ śanakair abravīd vacaḥ
c muhyate me manas tāta gātre svedaś ca jāyate
a vepathuṃ ca śarīre me romaharṣaṃ ca paśya vai
c varjayan brāhmaṇaṃ yuddhe śanair yāhi yato 'cyutaḥ
a arjunaṃ bhīmasenaṃ vā samare prāpya sārathe

c kirañ śaraśatāny eva gautamo 'nuyayau tadā

c pārṣataṃ prādravad yantaṃ mahendra iva śambaram

a śikhaṇḍī ca samāsādya hṛdikānāṃ mahāratham
c pañcabhir niśitair bhallair jatrudeśe samārdayat

c dhanur ekena ciccheda hasan rājan mahārathaḥ
a athānyad dhanur ādāya drupadasyātmajo balī

c aśītyā mārgaṇaiḥ kruddho bāhvor urasi cārdayat

b vavāma rudhiraṃ gātraiḥ kumbhavaktrād ivodakam
b rudhireṇa pariklinnaḥ kṛtavarmā tv arājata
b varṣeṇa kledito rājan yathā gairikaparvataḥ
c dhanur anyat samādāya samārgaṇagaṇaṃ prabho

c śākhāpratānair vimalaiḥ sumahān sa yathā drumaḥ

b yathā ca kiṃśukau phullau puṣyamāse 'bhyupāgatau
b rudhirokṣitasarvāṅgau raktacandanarūṣitau
b bhujagāv iva saṃkruddhau rejatus tau narottamau
b tāv ubhau śaranunnāṅgau parasparaśarakṣatau
c anyonyaśṛṅgābhihatau rejatur vṛṣabhāv iva
a anyonyasya vadhe yatnaṃ kurvāṇau tau mahārathau
c rathābhyāṃ ceratus tatra maṇḍalāni sahasraśaḥ
a kṛtavarmā mahārāja pārṣataṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c raṇe vivyādha saptatyā svarṇapuṅkhaiḥ śilāśitaiḥ
a tato 'sya samare bāṇaṃ bhojaḥ praharatāṃ varaḥ
c jīvitāntakaraṃ ghoraṃ vyasṛjat tvarayānvitaḥ
a sa tenābhihato rājan mūrchām āśu samāviśat
c dhvajayaṣṭiṃ ca sahasā śiśriye kaśmalāvṛtaḥ
a apovāha raṇāt taṃ tu sārathī rathināṃ varam
c hārdikyaśarasaṃtaptaṃ niḥśvasantaṃ punaḥ punaḥ
a parājite tataḥ śūre drupadasya sute prabho
c prādravat pāṇḍavī senā vadhyamānā samantataḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a śvetāśvo 'pi mahārāja vyadhamat tāvakaṃ balam
c yathā vāyuḥ samāsādya tūlarāśiṃ samantataḥ
a pratyudyayus trigartās taṃ śibayaḥ kauravaiḥ saha
c śālvāḥ saṃśaptakāś caiva nārāyaṇabalaṃ ca yat

f aparāhṇe mahārāja kāṅkṣatāṃ vijayaṃ yudhi
f kṣayaṃ narāśvanāgānāṃ yamarāṣṭravivardhanam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tataḥ karṇaṃ puraskṛtya tvadīyā yuddhadurmadāḥ
c punar āvṛtya saṃgrāmaṃ cakrur devāsuropamam
a dviradarathanarāśvaśaṅkhaśabdaiḥ
parihṛṣitā vividhaiś ca śastrapātaiḥ
c dviradarathapadātisārthavāhāḥ
paripatitābhimukhāḥ prajahrire te
a śaraparaśuvarāsipaṭṭiśair
iṣubhir anekavidhaiś ca sāditāḥ
c dviradarathahayā mahāhave
varapuruṣaiḥ puruṣāś ca vāhanaiḥ
a kamaladinakarendusaṃnibhaiḥ
sitadaśanaiḥ sumukhākṣināsikaiḥ
c ruciramukuṭakuṇḍalair mahī
puruṣaśirobhir avastṛtā babhau
a parighamusalaśaktitomarair
nakharabhuśuṇḍigadāśatair drutāḥ
c dviradanarahayāḥ sahasraśo
rudhiranadīpravahās tadābhavan
a prahatanararathāśvakuñjaraṃ
pratibhayadarśanam ulbaṇaṃ tadā
c tad ahitanihataṃ babhau balaṃ
pitṛpatirāṣṭram iva prajākṣaye
a atha tava naradeva sainikās
tava ca sutāḥ surasūnusaṃnibhāḥ
c amitabalapuraḥsarā raṇe
kuruvṛṣabhāḥ śiniputram abhyayuḥ
a tad atirucirabhīmam ābabhau
puruṣavarāśvarathadvipākulam
c lavaṇajalasamuddhatasvanaṃ
balam amarāsurasainyasaṃnibham
a surapatisamavikramas tatas
tridaśavarāvarajopamaṃ yudhi
c dinakarakiraṇaprabhaiḥ pṛṣatkai
ravitanayo 'bhyahanac chinipravīram
a tam api sarathavājisārathiṃ
śinivṛṣabho vividhaiḥ śarais tvaran
c bhujagaviṣasamaprabhai raṇe
puruṣavaraṃ samavāstṛṇot tadā
a śinivṛṣabhaśaraprapīḍitaṃ
tava suhṛdo vasuṣeṇam abhyayuḥ
c tvaritam atirathā ratharṣabhaṃ
dviradarathāśvapadātibhiḥ saha
a tam udadhinibham ādravad balī
tvaritataraiḥ samabhidrutaṃ paraiḥ
c drupadasutasakhas tadākarot
puruṣarathāśvagajakṣayaṃ mahat
a atha puruṣavarau kṛtāhnikau
bhavam abhipūjya yathāvidhi prabhum
c arivadhakṛtaniścayau drutaṃ
tava balam arjunakeśavau sṛtau
a jaladaninadanisvanaṃ rathaṃ
pavanavidhūtapatākaketanam
c sitahayam upayāntam antikaṃ
hṛtamanaso dadṛśus tadārayaḥ
d hastena hastipatihastasamānahastas
d tūṇīmukhād atha śarān muhur ādadānaḥ
d vajrīva dānavacamūṃ pragṛhītacāpo
d bhīmānujas tava narendra camūṃ jagāhe
a atha visphārya gāṇḍīvaṃ raṇe nṛtyann ivārjunaḥ
c śarasaṃbādham akarot khaṃ diśaḥ pradiśas tathā
a rathān vimānapratimān sajjayantrāyudhadhvajān
c sasārathīṃs tadā bāṇair abhrāṇīvānilo 'vadhīt
a gajān gajaprayantṝṃś ca vaijayantyāyudhadhvajān
c sādino 'śvāṃś ca pattīṃś ca śarair ninye yamakṣayam
a tam antakam iva kruddham anivāryaṃ mahāratham
c duryodhano 'bhyayād eko nighnan bāṇaiḥ pṛthagvidhaiḥ
a tasyārjuno dhanuḥ sūtaṃ ketum aśvāṃś ca sāyakaiḥ
c hatvā saptabhir ekaikaṃ chatraṃ ciccheda patriṇā
a navamaṃ ca samāsādya vyasṛjat pratighātinam
c duryodhanāyeṣuvaraṃ taṃ drauṇiḥ saptadhācchinat
a tato drauṇer dhanuś chittvā hatvā cāśvavarāñ śaraiḥ
c kṛpasyāpi tathātyugraṃ dhanuś ciccheda pāṇḍavaḥ
a hārdikyasya dhanuś chittvā dhvajaṃ cāśvaṃ tathāvadhīt
c duḥśāsanasyeṣuvaraṃ chittvā rādheyam abhyayāt
a atha sātyakim utsṛjya tvaran karṇo 'rjunaṃ tribhiḥ
c viddhvā vivyādha viṃśatyā kṛṣṇaṃ pārthaṃ punas tribhiḥ
d na glānir āsīt karṇasya kṣipataḥ sāyakān bahūn
d raṇe vinighnataḥ śatrūn kruddhasyeva śatakratoḥ
d karṇasya sphurad atyarthaṃ prāsyataḥ sāyakān dhanuḥ
d nanāda trāsajananaṃ bhūtānām ahitāntakam
a atha sātyakir āgatya karṇaṃ viddhvā śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c navatyā navabhiś cograiḥ śatena punar ārdayat
a tataḥ pravīrāḥ pāṇḍūnāṃ sarve karṇam apīḍayan
c yudhāmanyuḥ śikhaṇḍī ca draupadeyāḥ prabhadrakāḥ
a uttamaujā yuyutsuś ca yamau pārṣata eva ca
c cedikārūṣamatsyānāṃ kekayānāṃ ca yad balam
e cekitānaś ca balavān dharmarājaś ca suvrataḥ
a ete rathāśvadviradaiḥ pattibhiś cogravikramaiḥ
c parivārya raṇe karṇaṃ nānāśastrair avākiran
e bhāṣanto vāgbhir ugrābhiḥ sarve karṇavadhe vṛtāḥ
a tāṃ śastravṛṣṭiṃ bahudhā chittvā karṇaḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c apovāha sma tān sarvān drumān bhaṅktveva mārutaḥ
a rathinaḥ samahāmātrān gajān aśvān sasādinaḥ
c śaravrātāṃś ca saṃkruddho nighnan karṇo vyadṛśyata
a tad vadhyamānaṃ pāṇḍūnāṃ balaṃ karṇāstratejasā
c viśastrakṣatadehaṃ ca prāya āsīt parāṅmukham
a atha karṇāstram astreṇa pratihatyārjunaḥ svayam
c diśaḥ khaṃ caiva bhūmiṃ ca prāvṛṇoc charavṛṣṭibhiḥ
a musalānīva niṣpetuḥ parighā iva ceṣavaḥ
c śataghnya iva cāpy anye vajrāṇy ugrāṇi vāpare
a tair vadhyamānaṃ tat sainyaṃ sapattyaśvarathadvipam
c nimīlitākṣam atyartham udabhrāmyat samantataḥ
a niṣkaivalyaṃ tadā yuddhaṃ prāpur aśvanaradvipāḥ
c vadhyamānāḥ śarair anye tadā bhītāḥ pradudruvuḥ
a evaṃ teṣāṃ tadā yuddhe saṃsaktānāṃ jayaiṣiṇām
c girim astaṃ samāsādya pratyapadyata bhānumān
a tamasā ca mahārāja rajasā ca viśeṣataḥ
c na kiṃ cit pratyapaśyāma śubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubham
a te trasanto maheṣvāsā rātriyuddhasya bhārata
c apayānaṃ tataś cakruḥ sahitāḥ sarvavājibhiḥ
a kauraveṣu ca yāteṣu tadā rājan dinakṣaye
c jayaṃ sumanasaḥ prāpya pārthāḥ svaśibiraṃ yayuḥ
a vāditraśabdair vividhaiḥ siṃhanādaiś ca nartitaiḥ
c parān avahasantaś ca stuvantaś cācyutārjunau
a kṛte 'vahāre tair vīraiḥ sainikāḥ sarva eva te
c āśiṣaḥ pāṇḍaveyeṣu prāyujyanta nareśvarāḥ
a tataḥ kṛte 'vahāre ca prahṛṣṭāḥ kurupāṇḍavāḥ
c niśāyāṃ śibiraṃ gatvā nyaviśanta nareśvarāḥ
d raṇe pravṛttāny ahani kathayantaḥ sukhaṃ tathā
a yakṣarakṣaḥpiśācāś ca śvāpadāni ca saṃghaśaḥ
c jagmur āyodhanaṃ ghoraṃ rudrasyānartanopamam
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a svena cchandena naḥ sarvān nāvadhīd vyaktam arjunaḥ
c na hy asya samare mucyetāntako 'py ātatāyinaḥ
a pārtho hy eko 'harad bhadrām ekaś cāgnim atarpayat
c ekaś cemāṃ mahīṃ jitvā cakre balibhṛto nṛpān
a eko nivātakavacān avadhīd divyakārmukaḥ
b nivātakavacānāṃ ca tisraḥ koṭīr jaghāna ha
c ekaḥ kirātarūpeṇa sthitaṃ śarvam ayodhayat
a eko 'bhyarakṣad bharatān eko bhavam atoṣayat
c tenaikena jitāḥ sarve madīyā ugratejasaḥ
e te na nindyāḥ praśasyāś ca yat te cakrur bravīhi tat
f tato duryodhanaḥ sūta paścāt kim akarot tadā
 saṃjaya uvāca
a hataprahatavidhvastā vivarmāyudhavāhanāḥ
c dīnasvarā dūyamānā māninaḥ śatrubhir jitāḥ
a śibirasthāḥ punar mantraṃ mantrayanti sma kauravāḥ
c bhagnadaṃṣṭrā hataviṣāḥ padākrāntā ivoragāḥ
a tān abravīt tataḥ karṇaḥ kruddhaḥ sarpa iva śvasan
c karaṃ kareṇābhipīḍya prekṣamāṇas tavātmajam
a yatto dṛḍhaś ca dakṣaś ca dhṛtimān arjunaḥ sadā
c sa bodhayati cāpy enaṃ prāptakālam adhokṣajaḥ
a sahasāstravisargeṇa vayaṃ tenādya vañcitāḥ
c śvas tv ahaṃ tasya saṃkalpaṃ sarvaṃ hantā mahīpate
a evam uktas tathety uktvā so 'nujajñe nṛpottamān
b te 'nujñātā nṛpāḥ sarve svāni veśmāni bhejire
c sukhoṣitās te rajanīṃ hṛṣṭā yuddhāya niryayuḥ
a te 'paśyan vihitaṃ vyūhaṃ dharmarājena durjayam
c prayatnāt kurumukhyena bṛhaspatyuśanomatāt
a atha pratīpakartāraṃ satataṃ vijitātmanām
c sasmāra vṛṣabhaskandhaṃ karṇaṃ duryodhanas tadā
a puraṃdarasamaṃ yuddhe marudgaṇasamaṃ bale
c kārtavīryasamaṃ vīrye karṇaṃ rājño 'gaman manaḥ
d sarveṣāṃ caiva sainyānāṃ karṇam evāgaman manaḥ
e sūtaputraṃ maheṣvāsaṃ bandhum ātyayikeṣv iva
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a yad vo 'gaman mano mandāḥ karṇaṃ vaikartanaṃ tadā
c apy adrākṣata taṃ yūyaṃ śītārtā iva bhāskaram
a kṛte 'vahāre sainyānāṃ pravṛtte ca raṇe punaḥ
c kathaṃ vaikartanaḥ karṇas tatrāyudhyata saṃjaya
e kathaṃ ca pāṇḍavāḥ sarve yuyudhus tatra sūtajam
a karṇo hy eko mahābāhur hanyāt pārthān sasomakān
c karṇasya bhujayor vīryaṃ śakraviṣṇusamaṃ matam
e tathāstrāṇi sughorāṇi vikramaś ca mahātmanaḥ
f mama caiva sadā mandaḥ śaṃsate nityam agrataḥ
f karṇaś ca tān maheṣvāsān pāṇḍuputrān mahārathān
a duryodhanaṃ tadā dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavena bhṛśārditam
c parākrāntān pāṇḍusutān dṛṣṭvā cāpi mahāhave
a karṇam āśritya saṃgrāme darpo duryodhane punaḥ
c jetum utsahate pārthān saputrān sahakeśavān
a aho bata mahad duḥkhaṃ yatra pāṇḍusutān raṇe
c nātarad rabhasaḥ karṇo daivaṃ nūnaṃ parāyaṇam
e aho dyūtasya niṣṭheyaṃ ghorā saṃprati vartate
a aho duḥkhāni tīvrāṇi duryodhanakṛtāny aham
c sahiṣyāmi sughorāṇi śalyabhūtāni saṃjaya
a saubalaṃ ca tathā tāta nītimān iti manyate
b karṇaś ca rabhaso nityaṃ rājānaṃ cāpy anuvrataḥ
b karṇaṃ cāpratimaṃ yuddhe devair api durutsaham
b manyate 'bhyadhikaṃ pārthād daivaṃ cāsya hṛdi sthitam
a yuddheṣu nāma divyeṣu vartamāneṣu saṃjaya
c aśrauṣaṃ nihatān putrān nityam eva ca nirjitān
a na pāṇḍavānāṃ samare kaś cid asti nivārakaḥ
c strīmadhyam iva gāhanti daivaṃ hi balavattaram
 saṃjaya uvāca
 rājan pūrvanimittāni dharmiṣṭhāni vicintaya
a atikrāntaṃ hi yat kāryaṃ paścāc cintayatīti ca
c tac cāsya na bhavet kāryaṃ cintayā ca vinaśyati
a tad idaṃ tava kāryaṃ tu dūraprāptaṃ vijānatā
c na kṛtaṃ yat tvayā pūrvaṃ prāptāprāptavicāraṇe
a ukto 'si bahudhā rājan mā yudhyasveti pāṇḍavaiḥ
c gṛhṇīṣe na ca tan mohāt pāṇḍaveṣu viśāṃ pate
a tvayā pāpāni ghorāṇi samācīrṇāni pāṇḍuṣu
c tvatkṛte vartate ghoraḥ pārthivānāṃ janakṣayaḥ
a tat tv idānīm atikramya mā śuco bharatarṣabha
c śṛṇu sarvaṃ yathāvṛttaṃ ghoraṃ vaiśasam acyuta
a prabhātāyāṃ rajanyāṃ tu karṇo rājānam abhyayāt
c sametya ca mahābāhur duryodhanam abhāṣata
a adya rājan sameṣyāmi pāṇḍavena yaśasvinā
c haniṣyāmi ca taṃ vīraṃ sa vā māṃ nihaniṣyati
a bahutvān mama kāryāṇāṃ tathā pārthasya pārthiva
c nābhūt samāgamo rājan mama caivārjunasya ca
a idaṃ tu me yathāprajñaṃ śṛṇu vākyaṃ viśāṃ pate
c anihatya raṇe pārthaṃ nāham eṣyāmi bhārata
a hatapravīre sainye 'smin mayi caiva sthite yudhi
c abhiyāsyati māṃ pārthaḥ śakraśaktyā vinākṛtam
a tataḥ śreyaskaraṃ yat te tan nibodha janeśvara
c āyudhānāṃ ca yad vīryaṃ dravyāṇām arjunasya ca
a kāyasya mahato bhede lāghave dūrapātane
c sauṣṭhave cāstrayoge ca savyasācī na matsamaḥ
d prāṇe śaurye ca vijñāne vikrame cāpi bhārata
d nimittajñānayoge ca savyasācī na matsamaḥ
a sarvāyudhamahāmātraṃ vijayaṃ nāma tad dhanuḥ
c indrārtham abhikāmena nirmitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā
a yena daityagaṇān rājañ jitavān vai śatakratuḥ
c yasya ghoṣeṇa daityānāṃ vimuhyanti diśo daśa
e tad bhārgavāya prāyacchac chakraḥ paramasaṃmatam
a tad divyaṃ bhārgavo mahyam adadād dhanur uttamam
c yena yotsye mahābāhum arjunaṃ jayatāṃ varam
e yathendraḥ samare sarvān daiteyān vai samāgatān
f nijaghāna tathā sarvāñ jeṣyāmi yudhi pāṇḍavān
a dhanur ghoraṃ rāmadattaṃ gāṇḍīvāt tad viśiṣyate
c triḥsaptakṛtvaḥ pṛthivī dhanuṣā tena nirjitā
a dhanuṣo yasya karmāṇi divyāni prāha bhārgavaḥ
c tad rāmo hy adadān mahyaṃ yena yotsyāmi pāṇḍavam
a adya duryodhanāhaṃ tvāṃ nandayiṣye sabāndhavam
c nihatya samare vīram arjunaṃ jayatāṃ varam
a saparvatavanadvīpā hatadviḍ bhūḥ sasāgarā
c putrapautrapratiṣṭhā te bhaviṣyaty adya pārthiva
a nāsādhyaṃ vidyate me 'dya tvatpriyārthaṃ viśeṣataḥ
c samyag dharmānuraktasya siddhir ātmavato yathā
a na hi māṃ samare soḍhuṃ sa śakto 'gniṃ tarur yathā
c avaśyaṃ tu mayā vācyaṃ yena hīno 'smi phalgunāt
a jyā tasya dhanuṣo divyā tathākṣayyau maheṣudhī
b sārathis tasya govindo mama tādṛṅ na vidyate
c tasya divyaṃ dhanuḥ śreṣṭhaṃ gāṇḍīvam ajaraṃ yudhi
a vijayaṃ ca mahad divyaṃ mamāpi dhanur uttamam
c tatrāham adhikaḥ pārthād dhanuṣā tena pārthiva
a mayā cābhyadhiko vīraḥ pāṇḍavas tan nibodha me
c raśmigrāhaś ca dāśārhaḥ sarvalokanamaskṛtaḥ
a agnidattaś ca vai divyo rathaḥ kāñcanabhūṣaṇaḥ
c acchedyaḥ sarvato vīra vājinaś ca manojavāḥ
e dhvajaś ca divyo dyutimān vānaro vismayaṃkaraḥ
a kṛṣṇaś ca sraṣṭā jagato rathaṃ tam abhirakṣati
c ebhir dravyair ahaṃ hīno yoddhum icchāmi pāṇḍavam
a ayaṃ tu sadṛśo vīraḥ śalyaḥ samitiśobhanaḥ
c sārathyaṃ yadi me kuryād dhruvas te vijayo bhavet
a tasya me sārathiḥ śalyo bhavatv asukaraḥ paraiḥ
c nārācān gārdhrapatrāṃś ca śakaṭāni vahantu me
a rathāś ca mukhyā rājendra yuktā vājibhir uttamaiḥ
c āyāntu paścāt satataṃ mām eva bharatarṣabha
a evam abhyadhikaḥ pārthād bhaviṣyāmi guṇair aham
c śalyo hy abhyadhikaḥ kṛṣṇād arjunād adhiko hy aham
a yathāśvahṛdayaṃ veda dāśārhaḥ paravīrahā
c tathā śalyo 'pi jānīte hayānāṃ vai mahārathaḥ
a bāhuvīrye samo nāsti madrarājasya kaś cana
c tathāstrair matsamo nāsti kaś cid eva dhanurdharaḥ
a tathā śalyasamo nāsti hayayāne ha kaś cana
b vīryataḥ sārataś caiva yogataḥ karmato 'rthataḥ
c so 'yam abhyadhikaḥ pārthād bhaviṣyati ratho mama
d samudyātuṃ na śakṣyanti devā api savāsavāḥ
d evaṃ kṛte rathastho 'haṃ guṇair abhyadhiko 'rjunāt
d bhave yudhi jayeyaṃ ca phālgunaṃ kurusattama
d vijayeyam ahaṃ saṃkhye phalgunaṃ kurunandana
a etat kṛtaṃ mahārāja tvayecchāmi paraṃtapa
b kriyatām eṣa kāmo me mā vaḥ kālo 'tyagād ayam
c evaṃ kṛte kṛtaṃ mahyaṃ sarvakāmair bhaviṣyati
a tato draṣṭāsi samare yat kariṣyāmi bhārata
c sarvathā pāṇḍavān sarvāñ jeṣyāmy adya samāgatān
d na hi me samare śaktāḥ samudyātuṃ surāsurāḥ
d saṃjaya uvāca
d kim u pāṇḍusutā rājan raṇe mānuṣayonayaḥ
d evam uktas tava sutaḥ karṇenāhavaśobhinā
d saṃpūjya saṃprahṛṣṭātmā tato rādheyam abravīt
 duryodhana uvāca
a sarvam etat kariṣyāmi yathā tvaṃ karṇa manyase
c sopāsaṅgā rathāḥ sāśvā anuyāsyanti sūtaja
a nārācān gārdhrapakṣāṃś ca śakaṭāni vahantu te
c anuyāsyāma karṇa tvāṃ vayaṃ sarve ca pārthivāḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a evam uktvā mahārāja tava putrāḥ pratāpavān
c abhigamyābravīd rājā madrarājam idaṃ vacaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a putras tava mahārāja madrarājam idaṃ vacaḥ
b evam ukto mahārāja tava putraḥ pratāpavān
b madreśvaraṃ prati raṇe parasainyabhayaṃkaram
b sarvaṃ tathākarot tūrṇaṃ rādheyas tad yad abravīt
b madrarājaṃ ca samare praṇamya ca mahāratham
c vinayenopasaṃgamya praṇayād vākyam abravīt
a satyavrata mahābhāga dviṣatām aghavardhana
c madreśvara raṇe śūra parasainyabhayaṃkara
a śrutavān asi karṇasya bruvato vadatāṃ vara
c yathā nṛpatisiṃhānāṃ madhye tvāṃ varayaty ayam
d tat tvām aprativīryādya śatrupakṣakṣayāvaha
d madreśvara prayāce 'haṃ śirasā vinayena ca
d tvaṃ pāhi sarvataḥ karṇaṃ bhavaṃ brahmeva suvrata
a tasmāt pārthavināśārthaṃ hitārthaṃ mama caiva hi
c sārathyaṃ rathināṃ śreṣṭha sumanāḥ kartum arhasi
d tvayi yantari rādheyo vidviṣo me vijeṣyate
d abhīṣūṇāṃ hi karṇasya grahītānyo na vidyate
a asyābhīśugraho loke nānyo 'sti bhavatā samaḥ
b ṛte hi tvāṃ mahābhāga vāsudevasamaṃ yudhi
c sa pātu sarvataḥ karṇaṃ bhavān brahmeva śaṃkaram
a pārthasya sacivaḥ kṛṣṇo yathābhīśugraho varaḥ
c tathā tvam api rādheyaṃ sarvataḥ paripālaya
d yathā ca sarvathāpatsu vārṣṇeyaḥ pāti pāṇḍavam
d tathā madreśvarādya tvaṃ rādheyaṃ pratipālaya
a bhīṣmo droṇaḥ kṛpaḥ karṇo bhavān bhojaś ca vīryavān
c śakuniḥ saubalo drauṇir aham eva ca no balam
e eṣām eva kṛto bhāgo navadhā pṛtanāpate
a naiva bhāgo 'tra bhīṣmasya droṇasya ca mahātmanaḥ
c tābhyām atītya tau bhāgau nihatā mama śatravaḥ
a vṛddhau hi tau naravyāghrau chalena nihatau ca tau
c kṛtvā nasukaraṃ karma gatau svargam ito 'nagha
a tathānye puruṣavyāghrāḥ parair vinihatā yudhi
c asmadīyāś ca bahavaḥ svargāyopagatā raṇe
e tyaktvā prāṇān yathāśakti ceṣṭāḥ kṛtvā ca puṣkalāḥ
f tad idaṃ hatabhūyiṣṭhaṃ balaṃ mama narādhipa
f pūrvam apy alpakaiḥ pārthair hataṃ kim uta sāṃpratam
f balavanto mahātmānaḥ kaunteyāḥ satyavikramāḥ
f balaṃ śeṣaṃ na hanyur me yathā tat kuru pārthiva
f hatavīram idaṃ sainyaṃ pāṇḍavaiḥ samare vibho
a karṇo hy eko mahābāhur asmatpriyahite rataḥ
c bhavāṃś ca puruṣavyāghra sarvalokamahārathaḥ
d śalya karṇo 'rjunenādya yoddhum icchati saṃyuge
e tasmiñ jayāśā vipulā mama madrajanādhipa
f tasyābhīṣugrahavaro nānyo 'sti bhuvi kaś cana
f tasmāj jayāya me vīra sārathyaṃ kartum arhasi
a pārthasya samare kṛṣṇo yathābhīśuvaragrahaḥ
b tathā karṇarathe rājaṃs tvam abhīṣugraho bhava
c tena yukto raṇe pārtho rakṣyamāṇaś ca pārthiva
e yāni karmāṇi kurute pratyakṣāṇi tathaiva te
a pūrvaṃ na samare hy evam avadhīd arjuno ripūn
b idānīṃ vikramo hy asya kṛṣṇena sahitasya ca
b kṛṣṇena sahitaḥ pārtho dhārtarāṣṭrīṃ mahācamūm
c ahany ahani madreśa drāvayan dṛśyate yudhi
a bhāgo 'vaśiṣṭaḥ karṇasya tava caiva mahādyute
c taṃ bhāgaṃ saha karṇena yugapan nāśayāhave
d aruṇena yathā sārdhaṃ tamaḥ sūryo vyapohati
d tathā karṇena sahito jahi pārthaṃ mahāhave
d udyantau ca yathā sūryau bālasūryasamaprabhau
d karṇaśalyau raṇe dṛṣṭvā vidravantu mahārathāḥ
a sūryāruṇau yathā dṛṣṭvā tamo naśyati māriṣa
c tathā naśyantu kaunteyāḥ sapāñcālāḥ sasṛñjayāḥ
a rathānāṃ pravaraḥ karṇo yantṝṇāṃ pravaro bhavān
b saṃyogo yuvayor loke nābhūn na ca bhaviṣyati
c saṃnipātaḥ samo loke bhavator nāsti kaś cana
a yathā sarvāsv avasthāsu vārṣṇeyaḥ pāti pāṇḍavam
c tathā bhavān paritrātu karṇaṃ vaikartanaṃ raṇe
d sārathyaṃ kriyatāṃ tasya yudhyamānasya saṃyuge
d yathā ca samare kṛṣṇo rakṣate sarvato 'rjunam
d tathā tvam api rādheyaṃ rakṣasva ca mahāraṇe
a tvayā sārathinā hy eṣa apradhṛṣyo bhaviṣyati
c devatānām api raṇe saśakrāṇāṃ mahīpate
e kiṃ punaḥ pāṇḍaveyānāṃ mātiśaṅkīr vaco mama
a duryodhanavacaḥ śrutvā śalyaḥ krodhasamanvitaḥ
b dhārtarāṣṭram athovāca sṛkkiṇī parilelihan
b evam uktas tu sa krodhāt padā spṛṣṭa ivoragaḥ
c triśikhāṃ bhrukuṭīṃ kṛtvā dhunvan hastau punaḥ punaḥ
a krodharakte mahānetre parivartya mahābhujaḥ
c kulaiśvaryaśrutibalair dṛptaḥ śalyo 'bravīd idam
a avamanyase māṃ gāndhāre dhruvaṃ māṃ pariśaṅkase
c yan māṃ bravīṣi visrabdhaṃ sārathyaṃ kriyatām iti
a asmatto 'bhyadhikaṃ karṇaṃ manyamānaḥ praśaṃsasi
c na cāhaṃ yudhi rādheyaṃ gaṇaye tulyam ātmanā
a ādiśyatām abhyadhiko mamāṃśaḥ pṛthivīpate
c tam ahaṃ samare hatvā gamiṣyāmi yathāgatam
a atha vāpy eka evāhaṃ yotsyāmi kurunandana
c paśya vīryaṃ mamādya tvaṃ saṃgrāme dahato ripūn
a na cābhikāmān kauravya vidhāya hṛdaye pumān
c asmadvidhaḥ pravarteta mā mā tvam atiśaṅkithāḥ
a yudhi cāpy avamāno me na kartavyaḥ kathaṃ cana
c paśya hīmau mama bhujau vajrasaṃhananopamau
a dhanuḥ paśya ca me citraṃ śarāṃś cāśīviṣopamān
c rathaṃ paśya ca me kḷptaṃ sadaśvair vātavegitaiḥ
e gadāṃ ca paśya gāndhāre hemapaṭṭavibhūṣitām
a dārayeyaṃ mahīṃ kruddho vikireyaṃ ca parvatān
c śoṣayeyaṃ samudrāṃś ca tejasā svena pārthiva
a tan mām evaṃvidhaṃ jānan samartham arinigrahe
c kasmād yunakṣi sārathye nyūnasyādhirather nṛpa
d na cāpi mama rādheyaḥ kalām arhati ṣoḍaśīm
d sakarṇā ye trayo lokāḥ sārjunāḥ sajanārdanāḥ
d nibaddhāṃs tān raṇe rājan na mucyeyaṃ kathaṃ cana
d tathāpi śaktaṃ kauravya vihāya hṛdayena mām
d na cāhaṃ prākṛtaḥ kaś cin na cāpy adhigataḥ svayam
d ayaṃ cāpy avamāno me na kartavyaḥ kathaṃ cana
a na nāma dhuri rājendra prayoktuṃ tvam ihārhasi
c na hi pāpīyasaḥ śreyān bhūtvā preṣyatvam utsahe
a yo hy abhyupagataṃ prītyā garīyāṃsaṃ vaśe sthitam
c vaśe pāpīyaso dhatte tat pāpam adharottaram
a brāhmaṇā brahmaṇā sṛṣṭā mukhāt kṣatram athorasaḥ
c ūrubhyām asṛjad vaiśyāñ śūdrān padbhyām iti śrutiḥ
e tebhyo varṇaviśeṣāś ca pratilomānulomajāḥ
a athānyonyasya saṃyogāc cāturvarṇyasya bhārata
c goptāraḥ saṃgrahītāro dātāraḥ kṣatriyāḥ smṛtāḥ
a yājanādhyāpanair viprā viśuddhaiś ca pratigrahaiḥ
c lokasyānugrahārthāya sthāpitā brahmaṇā bhuvi
d prajānāṃ rakṣaṇaṃ dānaṃ yuddhaṃ kṣatrasya nirmitam
a kṛṣiś ca pāśupālyaṃ ca viśāṃ dānaṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
c brahmakṣatraviśāṃ śūdrā vihitāḥ paricārakāḥ
a brahmakṣatrasya vihitāḥ sūtā vai paricārakāḥ
c na viṭśūdrasya tatraiva śṛṇu vākyaṃ mamānagha
a so 'haṃ mūrdhāvasiktaḥ san rājarṣikulasaṃbhavaḥ
c mahārathaḥ samākhyātaḥ sevyaḥ stavyaś ca bandinām
a so 'ham etādṛśo bhūtvā nehārikulamardana
c sūtaputrasya saṃgrāme sārathyaṃ kartum utsahe
a avamānam ahaṃ prāpya na yotsyāmi kathaṃ cana
c āpṛcchya tvādya gāndhāre gamiṣyāmi yathāgatam
d na cāhaṃ sūtaputrasya sārathyam upajagmivān
a evam uktvā naravyāghraḥ śalyaḥ samitiśobhanaḥ
c utthāya prayayau tūrṇaṃ rājamadhyād amarṣitaḥ
a praṇayād bahumānāc ca taṃ nigṛhya sutas tava
c abravīn madhuraṃ vākyaṃ sāma sarvārthasādhakam
a yathā śalya tvam ātthedam evam etad asaṃśayam
c abhiprāyas tu me kaś cit taṃ nibodha janeśvara
a na karṇo 'bhyadhikas tvattaḥ śaṅke naiva kathaṃ cana
c na hi madreśvaro rājā kuryād yad anṛtaṃ bhavet
a ṛtam eva hi pūrvās te vahanti puruṣottamāḥ
b jñātam eva hi pūrvaṃ te vartma rājarṣisattama
c tasmād ārtāyaniḥ prokto bhavān iti matir mama
a śalyabhūtaś ca śatrūṇāṃ yasmāt tvaṃ bhuvi mānada
c tasmāc chalyeti te nāma kathyate pṛthivīpate
a yad eva vyāhṛtaṃ pūrvaṃ bhavatā bhūridakṣiṇa
c tad eva kuru dharmajña madarthaṃ yad yad ucyase
a na ca tvatto hi rādheyo na cāham api vīryavān
c vṛṇīmas tvāṃ hayāgryāṇāṃ yantāram iti saṃyuge
a yathā hy abhyadhikaṃ karṇaṃ guṇais tāta dhanaṃjayāt
c vāsudevād api tvāṃ ca loko 'yam iti manyate
a karṇo hy abhyadhikaḥ pārthād astrair eva nararṣabha
c bhavān apy adhikaḥ kṛṣṇād aśvayāne bale tathā
a yathāśvahṛdayaṃ veda vāsudevo mahāmanāḥ
c dviguṇaṃ tvaṃ tathā vettha madrarāja na saṃśayaḥ
 śalya uvāca
a yan mā bravīṣi gāndhāre madhye sainyasya kaurava
c viśiṣṭaṃ devakīputrāt prītimān asmy ahaṃ tvayi
a eṣa sārathyam ātiṣṭhe rādheyasya yaśasvinaḥ
c yudhyataḥ pāṇḍavāgryeṇa yathā tvaṃ vīra manyase
a samayaś ca hi me vīra kaś cid vaikartanaṃ prati
c utsṛjeyaṃ yathāśraddham ahaṃ vāco 'sya saṃnidhau
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tatheti rājan putras te saha karṇena bhārata
c abravīn madrarājasya sutaṃ bharatasattama
 duryodhana uvāca
a bhūya eva tu madreśa yat te vakṣyāmi tac chṛṇu
c yathā purā vṛttam idaṃ yuddhe devāsure vibho
a yad uktavān pitur mahyaṃ mārkaṇḍeyo mahān ṛṣiḥ
c tad aśeṣeṇa bruvato mama rājarṣisattama
e tvaṃ nibodha na cāpy atra kartavyā te vicāraṇā
f samutpannā hi rājānaḥ pramoha iti niścayaḥ
f kṛtvā caiva vyavasyanti sarve dharmārthaniścayān
a devānām asurāṇāṃ ca mahān āsīt samāgamaḥ
b saiṃhikeyās tadodvṛttā vibudhān avasūdayan
b te nirastāḥ kṛtā devair dānavā balagarvitāḥ
c babhūva prathamo rājan saṃgrāmas tārakāmayaḥ
e nirjitāś ca tadā daityā daivatair iti naḥ śrutam
f bhagnadarpā nirutsāhāḥ pātālaṃ viviśus tadā
a nirjiteṣu ca daityeṣu tārakasya sutās trayaḥ
c tārākṣaḥ kamalākṣaś ca vidyunmālī ca pārthiva
d kaś cit prajāpatir ghoras tena sārdhaṃ mahātmanā
d yuddham āsīn mahāghoraṃ daivatair na iti śrutiḥ
d parābabhūvur asurā dānavaiḥ saha saṃyuge
d devair nirastā hy asurā niḥśvasyāmarṣitās tataḥ
a tapa ugraṃ samāsthāya niyame parame sthitāḥ
c tapasā karśayām āsur dehān svāñ śatrutāpana
a damena tapasā caiva niyamena ca pārthiva
c teṣāṃ pitāmahaḥ prīto varadaḥ pradadau varān
a avadhyatvaṃ ca te rājan sarvabhūteṣu sarvadā
c sahitā varayām āsuḥ sarvalokapitāmaham
a tān abravīt tadā devo lokānāṃ prabhur īśvaraḥ
c nāsti sarvāmaratvaṃ hi nivartadhvam ato 'surāḥ
e varam anyaṃ vṛṇīdhvaṃ vai yādṛśaṃ saṃprarocate
a tatas te sahitā rājan saṃpradhāryāsakṛd bahu
c sarvalokeśvaraṃ vākyaṃ praṇamyainam athābruvan
d vayam icchāma nagaraṃ kartuṃ kāmagamaṃ śubham
d sarvakāmasamṛddhārtham avadhyaṃ devadānavaiḥ
d yakṣarakṣoragagaṇair nānājātibhir eva ca
d na kṛtyābhir na śastraiś ca na śāpair brahmavādinām
d vadhyeta tripuraṃ devaṃ prasanne tvayi sādaram
a asmākaṃ tvaṃ varaṃ deva prayacchemaṃ pitāmaha
c vayaṃ purāṇi trīṇy eva samāsthāya mahīm imām
e vicariṣyāma loke 'smiṃs tvatprasādapuraskṛtāḥ
a tato varṣasahasre tu sameṣyāmaḥ parasparam
b brahmovāca
b vilayaḥ samayasyānte maraṇaṃ jīvitasya ca
b iti cintya vadhopāyaṃ kaṃ cid eva niśāmaya
c ekībhāvaṃ gamiṣyanti purāṇy etāni cānagha
a samāgatāni caitāni yo hanyād bhagavaṃs tadā
c ekeṣuṇā devavaraḥ sa no mṛtyur bhaviṣyati
d teṣāṃ tad vacanaṃ śrutvā dānavānāṃ mahāyaśāḥ
e evam astv iti tān devaḥ pratyuktvā prāviśad divam
a te tu labdhavarāḥ prītāḥ saṃpradhārya parasparam
c puratrayavisṛṣṭyarthaṃ mayaṃ vavrur mahāsuram
e viśvakarmāṇam ajaraṃ daityadānavapūjitam
a tato mayaḥ svatapasā cakre dhīmān purāṇi ha
c trīṇi kāñcanam ekaṃ tu raupyaṃ kārṣṇāyasaṃ tathā
a kāñcanaṃ divi tatrāsīd antarikṣe ca rājatam
c āyasaṃ cābhavad bhūmau cakrasthaṃ pṛthivīpate
a ekaikaṃ yojanaśataṃ vistārāyāmasaṃmitam
c gṛhāṭṭāṭṭālakayutaṃ bṛhatprākāratoraṇam
a guṇaprasavasaṃbādham asaṃbādham anāmayam
c prāsādair vividhaiś caiva dvāraiś cāpy upaśobhitam
a pureṣu cābhavan rājan rājāno vai pṛthak pṛthak
b divyamālyāmbaradharā daiteyā rājasattama
c kāñcanaṃ tārakākṣasya citram āsīn mahātmanaḥ
e rājataṃ kamalākṣasya vidyunmālina āyasam
a trayas te daityarājānas trīṃl lokān āśu tejasā
c ākramya tasthur varṣāṇāṃ pūgān nāma prajāpatiḥ
a teṣāṃ dānavamukhyānāṃ prayutāny arbudāni ca
c koṭyaś cāprativīrāṇāṃ samājagmus tatas tataḥ
d māṃsāśanāḥ sudṛptāś ca surair vinikṛtās tathā
e mahad aiśvaryam icchantas tripuraṃ durgam āśritāḥ
a sarveṣāṃ ca punas teṣāṃ sarvayogavaho mayaḥ
c tam āśritya hi te sarve avartantākutobhayāḥ
a yo hi yaṃ manasā kāmaṃ dadhyau tripurasaṃśrayaḥ
c tasmai kāmaṃ mayas taṃ taṃ vidadhe māyayā tadā
a tārakākṣasutaś cāsīd dharir nāma mahābalaḥ
c tapas tepe paramakaṃ yenātuṣyat pitāmahaḥ
a sa tuṣṭam avṛṇod devaṃ vāpī bhavatu naḥ pure
c śastrair vinihatā yatra kṣiptāḥ syur balavattarāḥ
a sa tu labdhvā varaṃ vīras tārakākṣasuto hariḥ
c sasṛje tatra vāpīṃ tāṃ mṛtānāṃ jīvanīṃ prabho
d pūrṇāṃ divyasya toyasya pīyūṣapratimasya vai
a yena rūpeṇa daityas tu yena veṣeṇa caiva ha
c mṛtas tasyāṃ parikṣiptas tādṛśenaiva jajñivān
d saṃpūrṇabalavīryas tu rājañ śauryasamanvitaḥ
d evaṃ vīryeṇa saṃyuktāḥ kṛtās tena mahātmanā
a tāṃ prāpya traipurasthās tu sarvāṃl lokān babādhire
b varaloke 'vasat so 'pi hariḥ paramatejasā
b vidhāya sarvalokānāṃ hitaṃ pathyaṃ vidhāya ca
b tataḥ paramanirvigno hitakārī tāvakātmasu
c mahatā tapasā siddhāḥ surāṇāṃ bhayavardhanāḥ
d ekasmin nihate daitye sṛjanti sma daśāsurān

c nirhrīkāḥ saṃsthitiṃ sarve sthāpitāṃ samalūlupan
a vidrāvya sagaṇān devāṃs tatra tatra tadā tadā
c viceruḥ svena kāmena varadānena darpitāḥ
a devāraṇyāni sarvāṇi priyāṇi ca divaukasām
c ṛṣīṇām āśramān puṇyān yūpāñ janapadāṃs tathā
e vyanāśayanta maryādā dānavā duṣṭacāriṇaḥ
f nisthānāś ca kṛtā devā ṛṣayaḥ pitṛbhiḥ saha
f daityais tribhis trayo lokā hy ākrāntās taiḥ suretaraiḥ
f pīḍyamāneṣu lokeṣu tataḥ śakro marudvṛtaḥ
f purāṇy āyodhayāṃ cakre vajrapātaiḥ samantataḥ
f nāśakat tāny abhedyāni yadā bhettuṃ puraṃdaraḥ
f purāṇi varadattāni dhātrā tena narādhipa
f tadā bhītaḥ surapatir muktvā tāni purāṇy atha
a te devāḥ sahitāḥ sarve pitāmaham ariṃdama
c abhijagmus tadākhyātuṃ viprakāraṃ suretaraiḥ
a te tattvaṃ sarvam ākhyāya śirasābhipraṇamya ca
c vadhopāyam apṛcchanta bhagavantaṃ pitāmaham
a śrutvā tad bhagavān devo devān idam uvāca ha
b mamāpi so 'parādhnoti yo yuṣmākam asaumyakṛt
b śrūyatāṃ tridaśāḥ sarve yathedaṃ vākyagauravam
c asurāś ca durātmānas te cāpi vibudhadviṣaḥ
e aparādhyanti satataṃ ye yuṣmān pīḍayanty uta
f na tvāstu tān ahaṃ manye ye vai yuṣmān apīḍayan
a ahaṃ hi tulyaḥ sarveṣāṃ bhūtānāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ
c adhārmikās tu hantavyā ity ahaṃ prabravīmi vaḥ
d ekeṣuṇā vibhedyāni tāni durgāṇi nānyathā
d na ca sthāṇumṛte śakto bhettum ekeṣuṇā puraḥ
a te yūyaṃ sthāṇum īśānaṃ jiṣṇum akliṣṭakāriṇam
c yoddhāraṃ vṛṇutādityāḥ sa tān hantā suretarān
a iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā devāḥ śakrapurogamāḥ
b te devās tena vākyena coditāḥ praṇatāḥ sthitāḥ
b divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ vai tapas taptvā surarṣabhāḥ
b śubhātmāno mahātmāno jagmur vai vṛṣabhadhvajam
c brahmāṇam agrataḥ kṛtvā vṛṣāṅkaṃ śaraṇaṃ yayuḥ
a tapaḥ paraṃ samātasthur gṛṇanto brahma śāśvatam
c ṛṣibhiḥ saha dharmajñā bhavaṃ sarvātmanā gatāḥ
d devadevaṃ paraṃ sthāṇuṃ varadaṃ tryambakaṃ śivam
d śarvam īḍyam ajaṃ rudraṃ śaśāṅkāṅkitamūrdhajam
a tuṣṭuvur vāgbhir arthyābhir bhayeṣv abhayakṛttamam
c sarvātmānaṃ mahātmānaṃ yenāptaṃ sarvam ātmanā
a tapoviśeṣair bahubhir yogaṃ yo veda cātmanaḥ
c yaḥ sāṃkhyam ātmano veda yasya cātmā vaśe sadā
a te taṃ dadṛśur īśānaṃ tejorāśim umāpatim
