a deva tvayedaṃ kathitaṃ tridaśārinibarhaṇam
c tathā ca kṛtam asmābhiḥ prasanno vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ
a rathaś ca vihito 'smābhir vicitrāyudhasaṃvṛtaḥ
c sārathiṃ tu na jānīmaḥ kaḥ syāt tasmin rathottame
a tasmād vidhīyatāṃ kaś cit sārathir devasattama
c saphalāṃ tāṃ giraṃ deva kartum arhasi no vibho
a evam asmāsu hi purā bhagavann uktavān asi
c hitaṃ kartāsmi bhavatām iti tat kartum arhasi
a sa deva yukto rathasattamo no
durāvaro drāvaṇaḥ śātravāṇām
c pinākapāṇir vihito 'tra yoddhā
vibhīṣayan dānavān udyato 'sau
a tathaiva vedāś caturo hayāgryā
dharā saśailā ca ratho mahātman
c nakṣatravaṃśo 'nugato varūthe
yasmin yoddhā sārathinābhirakṣyaḥ
a tatra sārathir eṣṭavyaḥ sarvair etair viśeṣavān
c tatpratiṣṭho ratho deva hayā yoddhā tathaiva ca
e kavacāni ca śastrāṇi kārmukaṃ ca pitāmaha
a tvām ṛte sārathiṃ tatra nānyaṃ paśyāmahe vayam
c tvaṃ hi sarvair guṇair yukto devatābhyo 'dhikaḥ prabho
d tvaṃ deva śakto loke 'smin niyantuṃ pradrutān imān
d vedāśvān sopaniṣadaḥ sārathir bhava naḥ svayam
d yoddhuṃ balena sattvena vayasā vinayena ca
d adhikaḥ sārathiḥ kāryo nāsti cānyo 'dhiko bhavān
d sa bhavāṃs tārayatv asmān kuru sārathyam avyaya
d bhavān abhyadhikas tvatto nānyo 'sti bhavitā tv iha
d tvaṃ hi deveśa sarvais tu viśiṣṭo vadatāṃ vara
d taṃ rathaṃ tvaṃ samāruhya saṃyaccha paramān hayān
d tava prasādād vadhyeyur deva daivatakaṇṭakāḥ
d sa no rakṣa mahābāho daityebhyo mahato bhayāt
d tvaṃ hi no gatir avyagra tvaṃ no goptā mahāvrata
d tvatprasādāt surāḥ sarve pūjyante tridive prabho
e sārathye tūrṇam āroha saṃyaccha paramān hayān
f jayāya tridiveśānāṃ vadhāya tridaśadviṣām
a iti te śirasā natvā trilokeśaṃ pitāmaham
c devāḥ prasādayām āsuḥ sārathyāyeti naḥ śrutam
 brahmovāca
 evam etat surās tathyaṃ nānyas tv abhyadhiko bhavān
 sārathitvaṃ kariṣyāmi śaṃkarasya mahātmanaḥ
 sarvathā rathinaḥ śreyān kartavyo rathasārathiḥ
 tasmād etad yathātattvaṃ jñātvā yuṣmāṃś ca saṃgatān
 saṃgacchāmi hayān eṣa vibudhāḥ kālamardine
a nātra kiṃ cin mṛṣā vākyaṃ yad uktaṃ vo divaukasaḥ
c saṃyacchāmi hayān eṣa yudhyato vai kapardinaḥ
d duryodhanaḥ
d evam uktvā jaṭābhāraṃ saṃyamya prapitāmahaḥ
d paridhāyājinaṃ gāḍhaṃ saṃnyasya ca kamaṇḍalum
d pratodapāṇir bhagavān āruroha rathaṃ tadā
a tataḥ sa bhagavān devo lokasraṣṭā pitāmahaḥ
c sārathye kalpito devair īśānasya mahātmanaḥ
a tasminn ārohati kṣipraṃ syandanaṃ lokapūjite
c śirobhir agamaṃs tūrṇaṃ te hayā vātaraṃhasaḥ
d āruhya bhagavān devo dīpyamānaḥ svatejasā
d abhīṣūn hi pratodaṃ ca saṃjagrāha pitāmahaḥ
a maheśvare tv āruhati jānubhyām agaman mahīm
b ubhābhyāṃ lokanāthābhyām āsthitaṃ rathasattamam
b voḍhuṃ na śaktā vedāśvā jānubhyām apatan mahīm
a abhīśūn hi trilokeśaḥ saṃgṛhya prapitāmahaḥ
c tān aśvāṃś codayām āsa manomārutaraṃhasaḥ
d abhīśubhis tu bhagavān udyamya ca hayān vibhuḥ
d astu vīryaṃ ca śauryaṃ ca vedāśvānām iti prabhuḥ
d rathaṃ saṃcodayām āsa devānāṃ prabhur avyayaḥ
d tata utthāpya bhagavāṃs tān hayān anilopamān
d babhāṣe ca tadā sthāṇum āroheti surottamaḥ
d tatas tam iṣum ādāya viṣṇusomāgnisaṃbhavam
d āruroha tadā sthāṇur dhanuṣā kampayan parān
d tam ārūḍhaṃ tu deveśaṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ paramarṣayaḥ
d gandharvā devasaṃghāś ca tathaivāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ
d sa śobhamāno varadaḥ khaḍgī bāṇī śarāsanī
d pradīpayan rathe tasthau trīṃl lokān svena tejasā
d tato bhūyo 'bravīd devo devān indrapurogamān
d na hanyād iti kartavyo na śoko vaḥ kathaṃ cana
d hatān ity eva jānīta bāṇenānena cāsurān
d te devāḥ satyam ity āhur nihatā iti cābruvan
d na ca tad vacanaṃ mithyā yad āha bhagavān prabhuḥ
d iti saṃcintya vai devāḥ parāṃ tuṣṭim avāpnuvan
d tataḥ prayāto deveśaḥ sarvair devagaṇair vṛtaḥ
d rathena mahatā rājann upamā nāsti yasya ha
d svaiś ca pāriṣadair devaḥ pūjyamāno mahāyaśāḥ
d nṛtyadbhir aparaiś caiva māṃsabhakṣair durāsadaiḥ
d dhāvamānaiḥ samantāc ca tarjamānaiḥ parasparam
d ṛṣayaś ca mahābhāgās tapoyuktā mahāguṇāḥ
d āśaṃsur vai jayaṃ devā mahādevasya sarvaśaḥ
d evaṃ prayāte deveśe lokānām abhayaṃkare
d tuṣṭam āsīj jagat sarvaṃ devatāś ca narottama
d ṛṣayas tatra deveśaṃ stuvanto bahubhiḥ stavaiḥ
d tejaś cāsmai vardhayanto rājann āsan punaḥ punaḥ
d gandharvāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi prayutāny arbudāni ca
d vādayanti prayāṇe 'sya vādyāni vividhāni ca
a tato 'dhirūḍhe varade prayāte cāsurān prati
c sādhu sādhv iti viśveśaḥ smayamāno 'bhyabhāṣata
a yāhi deva yato daityāś codayāśvān atandritaḥ
c paśya bāhvor balaṃ me 'dya nighnataḥ śātravān raṇe
a tatas tāṃś codayām āsa vāyuvegasamāñ jave
b purāṇy uddiśya khasthāni dānavānāṃ tarasvinām
c yena tat tripuraṃ rājan daityadānavarakṣitam
d tatas te sahasotpatya vedākhyā rathavājinaḥ
d kṣaṇena tāni daityānāṃ purāṇi prāpayan prabhum
d pibadbhir iva cākāśaṃ tair hayair lokapūjitaiḥ
d jagāma bhagavān kṣipraṃ jayāya tridivaukasām
d prayāte ratham āsthāya tripurābhimukhe bhave
d nanāda sumahānādaṃ vṛṣabhaḥ pūrayan diśaḥ
d vṛṣabhasyāsya ninadaṃ śrutvā bhayaṃkaraṃ mahat
d vināśam agamaṃs tatra tārakāḥ suraśatravaḥ
d apare 'vasthitās tatra yuddhāyābhimukhās tadā
d tataḥ sthāṇur mahārāja śūladhṛk krodhamūrchitaḥ
d trastāni sarvabhūtāni trailokyaṃ bhūḥ prakampate
d nimittāni ca ghorāṇi tatra saṃdadhataḥ śaram
d tasmin somāgniviṣṇūnāṃ kṣobheṇa brahmarudrayoḥ
d sa ratho dhanuṣaḥ kṣobhād atīva hy avasīdati
d tato nārāyaṇas tasmāc charabhāgād viniḥsṛtaḥ
d vṛṣarūpaṃ samāsthāya ujjahāra mahāratham
d sīdamāne rathe caiva nardamāneṣu śatruṣu
d sa saṃbhramāt tu bhagavān nādaṃ cakre mahābalaḥ
d vṛṣabhasya sthito mūrdhni hayapṛṣṭhe ca mānada
d tadā sa bhagavān rudro niraikṣad dānavaṃ puram
d vṛṣabhasyāsthito rudro hayasya ca narottama
d stanāṃs tadāśātayata khurāṃś caiva dvidhākarot
d tataḥ prabhṛti bhadraṃ te gavāṃ dvaidhīkṛtāḥ khurāḥ
d hayānāṃ ca stanā rājaṃs tadā prabhṛti nābhavan
d pīḍitānāṃ balavatā rudreṇādbhutakarmaṇā
a athādhijyaṃ dhanuḥ kṛtvā śarvaḥ saṃdhāya taṃ śaram
c yuktvā pāśupatāstreṇa tripuraṃ samacintayat
a tasmin sthite tadā rājan kruddhe vidhṛtakārmuke
c purāṇi tāni kālena jagmur ekatvatāṃ tadā
a ekībhāvaṃ gate caiva tripure samupāgate
c babhūva tumulo harṣo daivatānāṃ mahātmanām
a tato devagaṇāḥ sarve siddhāś ca paramarṣayaḥ
c jayeti vāco mumucuḥ saṃstuvanto mudānvitāḥ
a tato 'grataḥ prādurabhūt tripuraṃ jaghnuṣo 'surān
c anirdeśyogravapuṣo devasyāsahyatejasaḥ
d trīṇi dṛṣṭvaikasaṃsthāni purāṇy atha pinākadhṛk
a sa tad vikṛṣya bhagavān divyaṃ lokeśvaro dhanuḥ
c trailokyasāraṃ tam iṣuṃ mumoca tripuraṃ prati
d utsṛṣṭe vai mahābhāga tasminn iṣuvare tadā
d mahān ārtasvaro hy āsīt purāṇāṃ patatāṃ bhuvi
d ekabāṇena tad devas tripuraṃ parameśvaraḥ
d nijaghne sāsuragaṇaṃ devadevo maheśvaraḥ
d bāṇatejognidagdhe tat praviśīrṇaṃ sahasradhā
d mahad ārtasvaraṃ kṛtvā nāvaśeṣam upāgatam
e tat sāsuragaṇaṃ dagdhvā prākṣipat paścimārṇave
a evaṃ tat tripuraṃ dagdhaṃ dānavāś cāpy aśeṣataḥ
c maheśvareṇa kruddhena trailokyasya hitaiṣiṇā
a sa cātmakrodhajo vahnir hāhety uktvā nivāritaḥ
b trailokyam avaśeṣeṇa punar dagdhuṃ pracakrame
b kālāgnim iva nirdagdhum utthitaṃ taṃ punaḥ punaḥ
c mā kārṣīr bhasmasāl lokān iti tryakṣo 'bravīc ca tam
a tataḥ prakṛtim āpannā devā lokās tatharṣayaḥ
c tuṣṭuvur vāgbhir arthyābhiḥ sthāṇum apratimaujasam
a te 'nujñātā bhagavatā jagmuḥ sarve yathāgatam
c kṛtakāmāḥ prasannena prajāpatimukhāḥ surāḥ
d evaṃ sa bhagavān devo lokasraṣṭā maheśvaraḥ
d devāsuragaṇādhyakṣo lokānāṃ vidadhe śivam
a yathaiva bhagavān brahmā lokadhātā pitāmahaḥ
b sārathyam akarot tatra rudrasya paramo 'vyayaḥ
b tathā bhavān api kṣipraṃ rudrasyeva pitāmahaḥ
b svayaṃ lokatrayaṃ sraṣṭā lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā
c saṃyaccha tvaṃ hayān asya rādheyasya mahātmanaḥ
a tvaṃ hi kṛṣṇāc ca karṇāc ca phalgunāc ca viśeṣataḥ
b balato rūpato yogād astrasaṃpada eva ca
b samāsaktaṃ mahīpāla kuru me hitam īpsitam
c viśiṣṭo rājaśārdūla nāsti tatra vicāraṇā
a yuddhe hy ayaṃ rudrakalpas tvaṃ ca brahmasamo 'nagha
c tasmāc chaktau yuvāṃ jetuṃ macchatrūṃs tāv ivāsurān
a yathā śalyādya karṇo 'yaṃ śvetāśvaṃ kṛṣṇasārathim
c pramathya hanyāt kaunteyaṃ tathā śīghraṃ vidhīyatām
d tvayi madreśa rājyāśā jīvitāśā tathaiva ca
d vijayaś ca tathaivādya karṇasācivyakāritaḥ
d tvayā rājyaṃ sukhaṃ caiva jīvitaṃ jayam eva ca
d samāsaktaṃ mahīpāla kuru me hitam īpsitam
d saṃyacchāsya hayān rājan matpriyārthaṃ paraṃtapa
e tvayi karṇaś ca rājyaṃ ca vayaṃ caiva pratiṣṭhitāḥ
f vijayaś caiva saṃgrāme saṃyacchādya hayottamān
a imaṃ cāpy aparaṃ bhūya itihāsaṃ nibodha me
c pitur mama sakāśe yaṃ brāhmaṇaḥ prāha dharmavit
a śrutvā caitad vacaś citraṃ hetukāryārthasaṃhitam
c kuru śalya viniścitya mā bhūd atra vicāraṇā
a bhārgavāṇāṃ kule jāto jamadagnir mahātapāḥ
c tasya rāmeti vikhyātaḥ putras tejoguṇānvitaḥ
a sa tīvraṃ tapa āsthāya prasādayitavān bhavam
c astrahetoḥ prasannātmā niyataḥ saṃyatendriyaḥ
a tasya tuṣṭo mahādevo bhaktyā ca praśamena ca
c hṛdgataṃ cāsya vijñāya darśayām āsa śaṃkaraḥ
d pratyakṣeṇa mahādevaḥ svāṃ tanuṃ sarvaśaṃkaraḥ
 īśvara uvāca
a rāma tuṣṭo 'smi bhadraṃ te viditaṃ me tavepsitam
c kuruṣva pūtam ātmānaṃ sarvam etad avāpsyasi
a dāsyāmi te tadāstrāṇi yadā pūto bhaviṣyasi
c apātram asamarthaṃ ca dahanty astrāṇi bhārgava
a ity ukto jāmadagnyas tu devadevena śūlinā
c pratyuvāca mahātmānaṃ śirasāvanataḥ prabhum
a yadā jānāsi deveśa pātraṃ mām astradhāraṇe
c tadā śuśrūṣate 'strāṇi bhavān me dātum arhati
 duryodhana uvāca
a tataḥ sa tapasā caiva damena niyamena ca
c pūjopahārabalibhir homamantrapuraskṛtaiḥ
a ārādhayitavāñ śarvaṃ bahūn varṣagaṇāṃs tadā
c prasannaś ca mahādevo bhārgavasya mahātmanaḥ
a abravīt tasya bahuśo guṇān devyāḥ samīpataḥ
c bhaktimān eṣa satataṃ mayi rāmo dṛḍhavrataḥ
a evaṃ tasya guṇān prīto bahuśo 'kathayat prabhuḥ
c devatānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ ca samakṣam arisūdanaḥ
a etasminn eva kāle tu daityā āsan mahābalāḥ
c tais tadā darpamohāndhair abādhyanta divaukasaḥ
a tataḥ saṃbhūya vibudhās tān hantuṃ kṛtaniścayāḥ
c cakruḥ śatruvadhe yatnaṃ na śekur jetum eva te
a abhigamya tato devā maheśvaram athābruvan
c prasādayantas taṃ bhaktyā jahi śatrugaṇān iti
a pratijñāya tato devo devatānāṃ ripukṣayam
c rāmaṃ bhārgavam āhūya so 'bhyabhāṣata śaṃkaraḥ
a ripūn bhārgava devānāṃ jahi sarvān samāgatān
c lokānāṃ hitakāmārthaṃ matprītyarthaṃ tathaiva ca
d evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca tryambakaṃ varadaṃ prabhum
d evam uktas tu devena bhārgavaḥ sumahāyaśāḥ
d pratyuvācātha deveśaṃ śaṃkaraṃ sa kṛtāñjaliḥ
 rāma uvāca
a akṛtāstrasya deveśa kā śaktir me maheśvara
c nihantuṃ dānavān sarvān kṛtāstrān yuddhadurmadān
 īśvara uvāca
a gaccha tvaṃ madanudhyānān nihaniṣyasi dānavān
c vijitya ca ripūn sarvān guṇān prāpsyasi puṣkalān
 duryodhana uvāca
a etac chrutvā ca vacanaṃ pratigṛhya ca sarvaśaḥ
c rāmaḥ kṛtasvastyayanaḥ prayayau dānavān prati
a avadhīd devaśatrūṃs tān madadarpabalānvitān
b mama yuddhaṃ prayacchadhvaṃ daityā yuddhamadotkaṭāḥ
b preṣito devadevena vo vijetuṃ mahāsurāḥ
b ity uktā bhārgaveṇātha daityā yuddhaṃ pracakramuḥ
b sa tān nihatya samare daityān bhārgavanandanaḥ
c vajrāśanisamasparśaiḥ prahārair eva bhārgavaḥ
a sa dānavaiḥ kṣatatanur jāmadagnyo dvijottamaḥ
c saṃspṛṣṭaḥ sthāṇunā sadyo nirvraṇaḥ samajāyata
a prītaś ca bhagavān devaḥ karmaṇā tena tasya vai
c varān prādād brahmavide bhārgavāya mahātmane
a uktaś ca devadevena prītiyuktena śūlinā
c nipātāt tava śastrāṇāṃ śarīre yābhavad rujā
a tayā te mānuṣaṃ karma vyapoḍhaṃ bhṛgunandana
c gṛhāṇāstrāṇi divyāni matsakāśād yathepsitam
a tato 'strāṇi samastāni varāṃś ca manasepsitān
c labdhvā bahuvidhān rāmaḥ praṇamya śirasā śivam
a anujñāṃ prāpya deveśāj jagāma sa mahātapāḥ
c evam etat purāvṛttaṃ tadā kathitavān ṛṣiḥ
a bhārgavo 'py adadāt sarvaṃ dhanurvedaṃ mahātmane
c karṇāya puruṣavyāghra suprītenāntarātmanā
a vṛjinaṃ hi bhavet kiṃ cid yadi karṇasya pārthiva
c nāsmai hy astrāṇi divyāni prādāsyad bhṛgunandanaḥ
d sūtena vardhito nityaṃ na śūdro nṛpa eva saḥ
d viśuddhayoniṃ vijñāya divyāny astrāṇy adāt prabhuḥ
a nāpi sūtakule jātaṃ karṇaṃ manye kathaṃ cana
c devaputram ahaṃ manye kṣatriyāṇāṃ kulodbhavam
d viśiṣṭam avabodhārthaṃ kulasyeti matir mama
d sarvathā na hy ayaṃ śalya karṇaḥ sūtakulodbhavaḥ
a sakuṇḍalaṃ sakavacaṃ dīrghabāhuṃ mahāratham
c katham ādityasadṛśaṃ mṛgī vyāghraṃ janiṣyati
a paśya hy asya bhujau pīnau nāgarājakaropamau
c vakṣaḥ paśya viśālaṃ ca sarvaśatrunibarhaṇam
d na tv eṣa prākṛtaḥ kaś cit karṇo vaikartano vṛṣaḥ
d mahātmā hy eṣa rājendra rāmaśiṣyaḥ pratāpavān
 duryodhana uvāca
a evaṃ sa bhagavān devaḥ sarvalokapitāmahaḥ
c sārathyam akarot tatra yatra rudro 'bhavad rathī
a rathinābhyadhiko vīraḥ kartavyo rathasārathiḥ
c tasmāt tvaṃ puruṣavyāghra niyaccha turagān yudhi
d yathā devagaṇais tatra vṛto yatnāt pitāmahaḥ
d tathāsmābhir bhavān yatnāt karṇād abhyadhiko vṛtaḥ
d yathā devair mahārāja īśvarād adhiko vṛtaḥ
d tathā bhavān api kṣipraṃ rudrasyeva pitāmahaḥ
d śalya uvāca
d niyaccha turagān yuddhe rādheyasya mahādyute
d mayāpy etan naraśreṣṭha bahuśo narasiṃhayoḥ
d kathyamānaṃ śrutaṃ divyam ākhyānam atimānuṣam
d yathā ca cakre sārathyaṃ bhavasya prapitāmahaḥ
d yathāsurāś ca nihatā iṣuṇaikena bhārata
d kṛṣṇasya cāpi viditaṃ sarvam etat purā hy abhūt
d yathā pitāmaho jajñe bhagavān sārathis tadā
d anāgatam atikrāntaṃ veda kṛṣṇo 'pi tattvataḥ
d etadarthaṃ viditvāpi sārathyam upajagmivān
d svayaṃbhūr iva rudrasya kṛṣṇaḥ pārthasya bhārata
d yadi hanyāc ca kaunteyaṃ sūtaputraḥ kathaṃ cana
d dṛṣṭvā pārthaṃ hi nihataṃ svayaṃ yotsyati keśavaḥ
d śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇir dhakṣyate tava vāhinīm
d na cāpi tasya kruddhasya vārṣṇeyasya mahātmanaḥ
d saṃjaya uvāca
d sthāsyate pratyanīkeṣu kaś cid atra nṛpas tava
d taṃ tathā bhāṣamāṇaṃ tu madrarājam ariṃdamaḥ
d pratyuvāca mahābāhur adīnātmā sutas tava
d māvamaṃsthā mahābāho karṇaṃ vaikartanaṃ raṇe
d sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ sarvaśāstrārthapāragam
d yasya jyātalanirghoṣaṃ śrutvā bhayaṃkaraṃ mahat
d pāṇḍaveyāni sainyāni vidravanti diśo daśa
d pratyakṣaṃ te mahābāho yathā rātrau ghaṭotkacaḥ
d māyāśatāni kurvāṇo hato māyāpuraskṛtaḥ
d na cātiṣṭhata bībhatsuḥ pratyanīke kathaṃ cana
d etāṃś ca divasān sarvān bhayena mahatā vṛtaḥ
d bhīmasenaś ca balavān dhanuṣkoṭyābhicoditaḥ
d uktaś ca saṃjñayā rājan mūḍha audariko yathā
d mādrīputrau tathā śūrau yena jitvā mahāraṇe
d kam apy arthaṃ puraskṛtya na hatau yudhi māriṣa
d yena vṛṣṇipravīras tu sātyakiḥ sātvatāṃ varaḥ
d nirjitya samare śūro virathaś ca balātkṛtaḥ
d sṛñjayāś cetare sarve dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamāḥ
d asakṛn nirjitāḥ saṃkhye smayamānena saṃyuge
d taṃ kathaṃ pāṇḍavā yuddhe vijeṣyanti mahāratham
d yo hanyāt samare kruddho vajrahastaṃ puraṃdaram
d tvaṃ ca sarvāstravid vīraḥ sarvavidyāstrapāragaḥ
d bāhuvīryeṇa te tulyaḥ pṛthivyāṃ nāsti kaś cana
d tvaṃ śalyabhūtaḥ śatrūṇām aviṣahyaḥ parākrame
d tatas tvam ucyase rājañ śalya ity arisūdana
d tava bāhubalaṃ prāpya na śekuḥ sarvasātvatāḥ
d tava bāhubalād rājan kiṃ nu kṛṣṇo balādhikaḥ
d yathā hi kṛṣṇena balaṃ dhāryaṃ vai phalgune hate
d tathā karṇātyayībhāve tvayā dhāryaṃ mahad balam
d kimarthaṃ samare sainyaṃ vāsudevo nyavārayat
d kimarthaṃ ca bhavān sainyaṃ na haniṣyati māriṣa
d tvatkṛte padavīṃ gantum iccheyaṃ yudhi māriṣa
d śalya uvāca
d sodarāṇāṃ ca vīrāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ ca mahīkṣitām
d yan māṃ bravīṣi gāndhāre agre sainyasya mānada
d viśiṣṭaṃ devakīputrāt prītimān asmy ahaṃ tvayi
d eṣa sārathyam ātiṣṭhe rādheyasya yaśasvinaḥ
d yudhyataḥ pāṇḍavāgryeṇa yathā tvāṃ vīra manyase
d samayaś ca hi me vīra kaś cid vaikartanaṃ prati
d saṃjaya uvāca
d utsṛjeyaṃ yathāśraddham ahaṃ vāco 'sya saṃnidhau
d tatheti rājan putras te saha karṇena māriṣa
d abravīn madrarājānaṃ sarvakṣatrasya saṃnidhau
d sārathyasyābhyupagamāc chalyenāśvāsitas tadā
d duryodhanas tadā hṛṣṭaḥ karṇaṃ tam abhiṣasvaje
d abravīc ca punaḥ karṇaṃ stūyamānaḥ sutas tava
d jahi pārthān raṇe sarvān mahendro dānavān iva
d sa śalyenābhyupagate hayānāṃ saṃniyacchane
d karṇo hṛṣṭamanā bhūyo duryodhanam abhāṣata
d nātihṛṣṭamanā hy eṣa madrarājo 'bhibhāṣate
d rājan madhurayā vācā punar enaṃ bravīhi vai
d tato rājā mahāprājñaḥ sarvāstrakuśalo balī
d duryodhano 'bravīc chalyaṃ madrarājaṃ mahīpatim
d pūrayann iva ghoṣeṇa meghagambhīrayā girā
d śalya karṇo 'rjunenādya yoddhavyam iti manyate
d tasya tvaṃ puruṣavyāghra niyaccha turagān yudhi
d karṇo hatvetarān sarvān phalgunaṃ hantum icchati
d tasyābhīṣugrahe rājan prayāce tvāṃ punaḥ punaḥ
d pārthasya sacivaḥ kṛṣṇo yathābhīṣugraho varaḥ
d tathā tvam api rādheyaṃ sarvataḥ paripālaya
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tataḥ śalyaḥ pariṣvajya sutaṃ te vākyam abravīt
c duryodhanam amitraghnaḥ prīto madrādhipas tadā
a evaṃ cen manyase rājan gāndhāre priyadarśana
c tasmāt te yat priyaṃ kiṃ cit tat sarvaṃ karavāṇy aham
a yatrāsmi bharataśreṣṭha yogyaḥ karmaṇi karhi cit
c tatra sarvātmanā yukto vakṣye kāryadhuraṃ tava
a yat tu karṇam ahaṃ brūyāṃ hitakāmaḥ priyāpriyam
c mama tatkṣamatāṃ sarvaṃ bhavān karṇaś ca sarvaśaḥ
 karṇa uvāca
a īśānasya yathā brahmā yathā pārthasya keśavaḥ
c tathā nityaṃ hite yukto madrarāja bhajasva naḥ
 śalya uvāca
a ātmanindātmapūjā ca paranindā parastavaḥ
c anācaritam āryāṇāṃ vṛttam etac caturvidham
a yat tu vidvan pravakṣyāmi pratyayārtham ahaṃ tava
c ātmanaḥ stavasaṃyuktaṃ tan nibodha yathātatham
a ahaṃ śakrasya sārathye yogyo mātalivat prabho
c apramādaprayogāc ca jñānavidyācikitsitaiḥ
a tataḥ pārthena saṃgrāme yudhyamānasya te 'nagha
c vāhayiṣyāmi turagān vijvaro bhava sūtaja
 duryodhana uvāca
a ayaṃ te karṇa sārathyaṃ madrarājaḥ kariṣyati
c kṛṣṇād abhyadhiko yantā devendrasyeva mātaliḥ
a yathā harihayair yuktaṃ saṃgṛhṇāti sa mātaliḥ
c śalyas tava tathādyāyaṃ saṃyantā rathavājinām
a yodhe tvayi rathasthe ca madrarāje ca sārathau
c rathaśreṣṭho dhruvaṃ saṃkhye pārtho nābhibhaviṣyati
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tato duryodhano bhūyo madrarājaṃ tarasvinam
c uvāca rājan saṃgrāme saṃyacchantaṃ hayottamān
c   'dhyuṣite paryupasthite
c karṇasya yaccha saṃgrāme
a tvayābhigupto rādheyo vijeṣyati dhanaṃjayam
c ity ukto ratham āsthāya tatheti prāha bhārata
a śalye 'bhyupagate karṇaḥ sārathiṃ sumano 'bravīt
c svaṃ sūta syandanaṃ mahyaṃ kalpayety asakṛt tvaran
a tato jaitraṃ rathavaraṃ gandharvanagaropamam
c vidhivat kalpitaṃ bhartre jayety uktvā nyavedayat
a taṃ rathaṃ rathināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ karṇo 'bhyarcya yathāvidhi
c saṃpāditaṃ brahmavidā pūrvam eva purodhasā
a kṛtvā pradakṣiṇaṃ yatnād upasthāya ca bhāskaram
c samīpasthaṃ madrarājaṃ samāropayad agrataḥ
a tataḥ karṇasya durdharṣaṃ syandanapravaraṃ mahat
c āruroha mahātejāḥ śalyaḥ siṃha ivācalam
a tataḥ śalyāsthitaṃ rājan karṇaḥ svaratham uttamam
c adhyatiṣṭhad yathāmbhodaṃ vidyutvantaṃ divākaraḥ
a tāv ekaratham ārūḍhāv ādityāgnisamatviṣau
c vyabhrājetāṃ yathā meghaṃ sūryāgnī sahitau divi
a saṃstūyamānau tau vīrau tadāstāṃ dyutimattarau
c ṛtvik sadasyair indrāgnī hūyamānāv ivādhvare
a sa śalyasaṃgṛhītāśve rathe karṇaḥ sthito 'bhavat
c dhanur visphārayan ghoraṃ pariveṣīva bhāskaraḥ
a āsthitaḥ sa rathaśreṣṭhaṃ karṇaḥ śaragabhastimān
c prababhau puruṣavyāghro mandarastha ivāṃśumān
a taṃ rathasthaṃ mahāvīraṃ yāntaṃ cāmitatejasam
c duryodhanaḥ sma rādheyam idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a akṛtaṃ droṇabhīṣmābhyāṃ duṣkaraṃ karma saṃyuge
c kuruṣvādhirathe vīra miṣatāṃ sarvadhanvinām
a manogataṃ mama hy āsīd bhīṣmadroṇau mahārathau
c arjunaṃ bhīmasenaṃ ca nihantārāv iti dhruvam
a tābhyāṃ yad akṛtaṃ vīra vīrakarma mahāmṛdhe
c tat karma kuru rādheya vajrapāṇir ivāparaḥ
a gṛhāṇa dharmarājaṃ vā jahi vā tvaṃ dhanaṃjayam
c bhīmasenaṃ ca rādheya mādrīputrau yamāv api
a jayaś ca te 'stu bhadraṃ ca prayāhi puruṣarṣabha
c pāṇḍuputrasya sainyāni kuru sarvāṇi bhasmasāt
a tatas tūryasahasrāṇi bherīṇām ayutāni ca
c vādyamānāny arocanta meghaśabdā yathā divi
a pratigṛhya tu tad vākyaṃ rathastho rathasattamaḥ
c abhyabhāṣata rādheyaḥ śalyaṃ yuddhaviśāradam
a codayāśvān mahābāho yāvad dhanmi dhanaṃjayam
c bhīmasenaṃ yamau cobhau rājānaṃ ca yudhiṣṭhiram
a adya paśyatu me śalya bāhuvīryaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
c asyataḥ kaṅkapatrāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi śatāni ca
a adya kṣepsyāmy ahaṃ śalya śarān paramatejanān
a   pāṇḍavān sajanārdanān
a saṃyokṣyāmi raṇe śalya
c pāṇḍavānāṃ vināśāya duryodhanajayāya ca
d saṃjaya uvāca
d etac chrutvā vacas tasya śalyaḥ karṇaṃ vaco 'bravīt
 śalya uvāca
a sūtaputra kathaṃ nu tvaṃ pāṇḍavān avamanyase
c sarvāstrajñān maheṣvāsān sarvān eva mahārathān
a anivartino mahābhāgān ajeyān satyavikramān
c api saṃjanayeyur ye bhayaṃ sākṣāc chatakratoḥ
a yadā śroṣyasi nirghoṣaṃ visphūrjitam ivāśaneḥ
c rādheya gāṇḍivasyājau tadā naivaṃ vadiṣyasi
d yadā drakṣyasi bhīmena kuñjarānīkam āhave
d viśīrṇadantaṃ nihataṃ tadā naivaṃ vadiṣyasi
d yadā drakṣyasi saṃgrāme dharmaputraṃ yamau tathā
d śitaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ kurvāṇān abhracchāyām ivāmbare
d asyataḥ kṣiṇvataś cārīn laghuhastān durāsadān
d pārthivān api cānyāṃs tvaṃ tadā naivaṃ vadiṣyasi
 saṃjaya uvāca
a anādṛtya tu tad vākyaṃ madrarājena bhāṣitam
c drakṣyasy adyety avocad vai śalyaṃ karṇo nareśvara
a dṛṣṭvā karṇaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ yuyutsuṃ samavasthitam
c cukruśuḥ kuravaḥ sarve hṛṣṭarūpāḥ paraṃtapa
a tato dundubhighoṣeṇa bherīṇāṃ ninadena ca
c bāṇaśabdaiś ca vividhair garjitaiś ca tarasvinām
e niryayus tāvakā yuddhe mṛtyuṃ kṛtvā nivartanam
a prayāte tu tataḥ karṇe yodheṣu muditeṣu ca
c cacāla pṛthivī rājan rarāsa ca suvisvaram
a niścaranto vyadṛśyanta sūryāt sapta mahāgrahāḥ
c ulkāpātaś ca saṃjajñe diśāṃ dāhas tathaiva ca
e tathāśanyaś ca saṃpetur vavur vātāś ca dāruṇāḥ
a mṛgapakṣigaṇāś caiva bahuśaḥ pṛtanāṃ tava
c apasavyaṃ tadā cakrur vedayanto mahad bhayam
a prasthitasya ca karṇasya nipetus turagā bhuvi
c asthivarṣaṃ ca patitam antarikṣād bhayānakam
a jajvaluś caiva śastrāṇi dhvajāś caiva cakampire
c aśrūṇi ca vyamuñcanta vāhanāni viśāṃ pate
a ete cānye ca bahava utpātās tatra māriṣa
c samutpetur vināśāya kauravāṇāṃ sudāruṇāḥ
a na ca tān gaṇayām āsuḥ sarve te daivamohitāḥ
c prasthitaṃ sūtaputraṃ ca jayety ūcur narā bhuvi
d śalyena sahitaṃ dṛṣṭvā karṇam āhavaśobhinam
e nirjitān pāṇḍavāṃś caiva menire tava kauravāḥ
a tato rathasthaḥ paravīrahantā
bhīṣmadroṇāv āttavīryau nirīkṣya
c samajvalad bhārata pāvakābho
vaikartano 'sau rathakuñjaro vṛṣaḥ
a sa śalyam ābhāṣya jagāda vākyaṃ
pārthasya karmāpratimaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā
c mānena darpeṇa ca dahyamānaḥ
krodhena dīpyann iva niḥśvasitvā
a nāhaṃ mahendrād api vajrapāṇeḥ
kruddhād bibhemy āttadhanū rathasthaḥ
c dṛṣṭvā tu bhīṣmapramukhāñ śayānān
na tv eva māṃ sthiratā saṃjahāti
a mahendraviṣṇupratimāv aninditau
rathāśvanāgapravarapramāthinau
c avadhyakalpau nihatau yadā parais
tato mamādyāpi raṇe 'sti sādhvasam
a samīkṣya saṃkhye 'tibalān narādhipair
narāśvamātaṅgarathāñ śarair hatān
c kathaṃ na sarvān ahitān raṇe 'vadhīn
mahāstravid brāhmaṇapuṃgavo guruḥ
a sa saṃsmaran droṇahavaṃ mahāhave
bravīmi satyaṃ kuravo nibodhata
c na vo mad anyaḥ prasahed raṇe 'rjunaṃ
kramāgataṃ mṛtyum ivograrūpiṇam
a śikṣā prasādaś ca balaṃ dhṛtiś ca
droṇe mahāstrāṇi ca saṃnatiś ca
c sa ced agān mṛtyuvaśaṃ mahātmā
sarvān anyān āturān adya manye
a neha dhruvaṃ kiṃ cid api pracintyaṃ
vidur loke karmaṇo 'nityayogāt
c sūryodaye ko hi vimuktasaṃśayo
garvaṃ kurvītādya gurau nipātite
a na nūnam astrāṇi balaṃ parākramaḥ
kriyā sunītaṃ paramāyudhāni vā
c alaṃ manuṣyasya sukhāya vartituṃ
tathā hi yuddhe nihataḥ parair guruḥ
a hutāśanādityasamānatejasaṃ
parākrame viṣṇupuraṃdaropamam
c naye bṛhaspatyuśanaḥsamaṃ sadā
na cainam astraṃ tad apāt suduḥsaham
a saṃprakruṣṭe ruditastrīkumāre
parābhūte pauruṣe dhārtarāṣṭre
c mayā kṛtyam iti jānāmi śalya
prayāhi tasmād dviṣatām anīkam
a yatra rājā pāṇḍavaḥ satyasaṃdho
vyavasthito bhīmasenārjunau ca
c vāsudevaḥ sṛñjayāḥ sātyakiś ca
yamau ca kas tau viṣahen mad anyaḥ
a tasmāt kṣipraṃ madrapate prayāhi
raṇe pāñcālān pāṇḍavān sṛñjayāṃś ca
c tān vā haniṣyāmi sametya saṃkhye
yāsyāmi vā droṇamukhāya manye
a na tv evāhaṃ na gamiṣyāmi madhyaṃ
teṣāṃ śūrāṇām iti mā śalya viddhi
c mitradroho marṣaṇīyo na me 'yaṃ
tyaktvā prāṇān anuyāsyāmi droṇam
a prājñasya mūḍhasya ca jīvitānte
prāṇapramokṣo 'ntakavaktragasya
c ato vidvann abhiyāsyāmi pārthaṃ
diṣṭaṃ na śakyaṃ vyativartituṃ vai
a kalyāṇavṛttaḥ satataṃ hi rājan
vaicitravīryasya suto mamāsīt
c tasyārthasiddhyartham ahaṃ tyajāmi
priyān bhogān dustyajaṃ jīvitaṃ ca
a vaiyāghracarmāṇam akūjanākṣaṃ
haimatrikośaṃ rajatatriveṇum
c rathaprabarhaṃ turagaprabarhair
yuktaṃ prādān mahyam idaṃ hi rāmaḥ
a dhanūṃṣi citrāṇi nirīkṣya śalya
dhvajaṃ gadāṃ sāyakāṃś cograrūpān
c asiṃ ca dīptaṃ paramāyudhaṃ ca
śaṅkhaṃ ca śubhraṃ svanavantam ugram
d astrāṇi divyāny adadān mahātmā
a patākinaṃ vajranipātanisvanaṃ
sitāśvayuktaṃ śubhatūṇaśobhitam
b  rathaprabarhaṃ puruṣaprabarhaḥ
c imaṃ samāsthāya rathaṃ ratharṣabhaṃ
raṇe haniṣyāmy aham arjunaṃ balāt
a taṃ cen mṛtyuḥ sarvaharo 'bhirakṣate
sadāpramattaḥ samare pāṇḍuputram
c taṃ vā haniṣyāmi sametya yuddhe
yāsyāmi vā bhīṣmamukho yamāya
a yamavaruṇakuberavāsavā vā
yadi yugapat sagaṇā mahāhave
c jugupiṣava ihaitya pāṇḍavaṃ
kim u bahunā saha tair jayāmi tam
a iti raṇarabhasasya katthatas
tad upaniśamya vacaḥ sa madrarāṭ
c avahasad avamanya vīryavān
pratiṣiṣidhe ca jagāda cottaram
a virama virama karṇa katthanād
atirabhaso 'syati cāpy ayuktavāk
c kva ca hi naravaro dhanaṃjayaḥ
kva punar iha tvam upāramābudha
a yadusadanam upendrapālitaṃ
tridivam ivāmararājarakṣitam
c prasabham iha vilokya ko haret
puruṣavarāvarajām ṛte 'rjunāt
a tribhuvanasṛjam īśvareśvaraṃ
ka iha pumān bhavam āhvayed yudhi
c mṛgavadhakalahe ṛte 'rjunāt
surapativīryasamaprabhāvataḥ
a asurasuramahoragān narān
garuḍapiśācasayakṣarākṣasān
c iṣubhir ajayad agnigauravāt
svabhilaṣitaṃ ca havir dadau jayaḥ
a smarasi nanu yadā parair hṛtaḥ
sa ca dhṛtarāṣṭrasuto vimokṣitaḥ
c dinakaraja narottamair yadā
maruṣu bahūn vinihatya tān arīn
a prathamam api palāyite tvayi
priyakalahā dhṛtarāṣṭrasūnavaḥ
c smarasi nanu yadā pramocitāḥ
khacaragaṇān avajitya pāṇḍavaiḥ
a samuditabalavāhanāḥ punaḥ
puruṣavareṇa jitāḥ stha gograhe
c sagurugurusutāḥ sabhīṣmakāḥ
kim u na jitaḥ sa tadā tvayārjunaḥ
a idam aparam upasthitaṃ punas
tava nidhanāya suyuddham adya vai
c yadi na ripubhayāt palāyase
samaragato 'dya hato 'si sūtaja
 saṃjaya uvāca
a iti bahuparuṣaṃ prabhāṣati
pramanasi madrapatau ripustavam
c bhṛśam atiruṣitaḥ paraṃ vṛṣaḥ
kurupṛtanāpatir āha madrapam
a bhavatu bhavatu kiṃ vikatthase
nanu mama tasya ca yuddham udyatam
c yadi sa jayati māṃ mahāhave
tata idam astu sukatthitaṃ tava
a evam astv iti madreśa uktvā nottaram uktavān
c yāhi madreśa cāpy enaṃ karṇaḥ prāha yuyutsayā
a sa rathaḥ prayayau śatrūñ śvetāśvaḥ śalyasārathiḥ
c nighnann amitrān samare tamo ghnan savitā yathā
a tataḥ prāyāt prītimān vai rathena
vaiyāghreṇa śvetayujātha karṇaḥ
c sa cālokya dhvajinīṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ
dhanaṃjayaṃ tvarayā paryapṛcchat
 saṃjaya uvāca
a prayān eva tadā karṇo harṣayan vāhinīṃ tava
c ekaikaṃ samare dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavaṃ paryapṛcchata
a yo mamādya mahātmānaṃ darśayec chvetavāhanam
c tasmai dadyām abhipretaṃ varaṃ yaṃ manasecchati
a sa cet tad abhimanyeta tasmai dadyām ahaṃ punaḥ
c śakaṭaṃ ratnasaṃpūrṇaṃ yo me brūyād dhanaṃjayam
d atha vā śakaṭaṃ pūrṇaṃ ratnānāṃ ṣaḍgavāyutam
d dhuri kṣamair bṛhadbhiś ca gobhir yuktam akālikam
a sa cet tad abhimanyeta puruṣo 'rjunadarśivān
b śataṃ dadyāṃ gavāṃ tasmai naityakaṃ kāṃsyadohanam
b śataṃ grāmavarāṃś caiva dadyām arjunadarśine
b tathā tasmai punar dadyāṃ śvetam aśvatarīratham
b yuktam añjanakeśībhir yo me brūyād dhanaṃjayam
b atha vāsmai punar dadyāṃ varam anyad yathepsitam
b yuktaṃ hayavarair jaitraṃ kāmbojair abhiniṣṭhitam
b sa cet tad abhimanyeta puruṣo 'rjunadarśivān
c anyaṃ tasmai punar dadyāṃ sauvarṇaṃ hastiṣaḍgavam
a tathā tasmai punar dadyāṃ strīṇāṃ śatam alaṃkṛtam
c śyāmānāṃ niṣkakaṇṭhīnāṃ gītavādyavipaścitām
d sa cet tad abhimanyeta puruṣo 'rjunadarśivān
d tasmai dadyāṃ śataṃ nāgāñ śataṃ grāmāñ śataṃ rathān
d suvarṇasya ca mukhyasya hayāgryāṇāṃ śataṃ śatān
d ṛddhyā guṇaiḥ sudāntāṃś ca dhuryavāhān suśikṣitān
d tathā suvarṇaśṛṅgīṇāṃ godhenūnāṃ catuḥśatam
d dadyāṃ tasmai savatsānāṃ yo me brūyād dhanaṃjayam
a sa cet tad abhimanyeta puruṣo 'rjunadarśivān
c anyaṃ tasmai varaṃ dadyāṃ śvetān pañcaśatān hayān
a hemabhāṇḍaparicchannān sumṛṣṭamaṇikuṇḍalān
c sudāntān api caivāhaṃ dadyām aṣṭaśatān parān
d atha vāsmai vicitrāṅgān vicitramaṇimaṇḍitān
d rathāñ jātyair hayair yuktān dadyām aṣṭādaśaiva tān
d anyam asmai varaṃ dadyāṃ dhuryān dāntāś catuḥśatam
d rohiṇī rūpasaṃpannā hemaśṛṅgīś catuḥśatam
d dadyām asmai payasvinyo yo me brūyād dhanaṃjayam
a rathaṃ ca śubhraṃ sauvarṇaṃ dadyāṃ tasmai svalaṃkṛtam
c yuktaṃ paramakāmbojair yo me brūyād dhanaṃjayam
d sa cet tad abhimanyeta puruṣo 'rjunadarśivān
a anyaṃ tasmai varaṃ dadyāṃ kuñjarāṇāṃ śatāni ṣaṭ
c kāñcanair vividhair bhāṇḍair ācchannān hemamālinaḥ
e utpannān aparānteṣu vinītān hastiśikṣakaiḥ
a sa cet tad abhimanyeta puruṣo 'rjunadarśivān
b dadyāṃ varṇasya varṇasya hayāgryāṇāṃ śataṃ śatam
b dhuryāṇāṃ sādhudāntānāṃ śikṣitānāṃ narottamaiḥ
b sa cet tad abhimanyeta puruṣo 'rjunadarśivān
b tasmai dadyāṃ grāmaśataṃ śataṃ hastīñ śataṃ hayān
b sa cet tad abhimanyeta puruṣo 'rjunadarśivān
b anyaṃ tasmai varaṃ dadyāṃ vaiśyagrāmāṃś caturdaśa
b susphītān dhanasaṃyuktān pratyāsannavanodakān
b akutobhayān susaṃpannān rājabhojyāṃś caturdaśa
b dāsīnāṃ niṣkakaṇṭhīnāṃ māgadhīnāṃ śataṃ tathā
b pratyagravayasāṃ dadyāṃ yo me brūyād dhanaṃjayam
b sa cet tad abhimanyeta puruṣo 'rjunadarśivān
c anyaṃ tasmai varaṃ dadyāṃ yam asau kāmayet svayam
a putradārān vihārāṃś ca yad anyad vittam asti me
c tac ca tasmai punar dadyāṃ yad yat sa manasecchati
a hatvā ca sahitau kṛṣṇau tayor vittāni sarvaśaḥ
c tasmai dadyām ahaṃ yo me prabrūyāt keśavārjunau
a etā vācaḥ subahuśaḥ karṇa uccārayan yudhi
c dadhmau sāgarasaṃbhūtaṃ susvanaṃ śaṅkham uttamam
a tā vācaḥ sūtaputrasya tathā yuktā niśamya tu
c duryodhano mahārāja prahṛṣṭaḥ sānugo 'bhavat
a tato dundubhinirghoṣo mṛdaṅgānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
c siṃhanādaḥ savāditraḥ kuñjarāṇāṃ ca nisvanaḥ
a prādurāsīt tadā rājaṃs tvatsainye bharatarṣabha
c yodhānāṃ saṃprahṛṣṭānāṃ tathā samabhavat svanaḥ
a tathā prahṛṣṭe sainye tu plavamānaṃ mahāratham
c vikatthamānaṃ samare rādheyam arikarśanam
e madrarājaḥ prahasyedaṃ vacanaṃ pratyabhāṣata
a mā sūtaputra mānena sauvarṇaṃ hastiṣaḍgavam
c prayaccha puruṣāyādya drakṣyasi tvaṃ dhanaṃjayam
a bālyād iva tvaṃ tyajasi vasu vaiśravaṇo yathā
c ayatnenaiva rādheya draṣṭāsy adya dhanaṃjayam
a parāsṛjasi mithyā kiṃ kiṃ ca tvaṃ bahu mūḍhavat
c apātradāne ye doṣās tān mohān nāvabudhyase
a yat pravedayase vittaṃ bahutvena khalu tvayā
c śakyaṃ bahuvidhair yajñair yaṣṭuṃ sūta yajasva taiḥ
a yac ca prārthayase hantuṃ kṛṣṇau mohān mṛṣaiva tat
c na hi śuśruma saṃmarde kroṣṭrā siṃhau nipātitau
a aprārthitaṃ prārthayase suhṛdo na hi santi te
c ye tvāṃ na vārayanty āśu prapatantaṃ hutāśane
a kālakāryaṃ na jānīṣe kālapakvo 'sy asaṃśayam
c bahvabaddham akarṇīyaṃ ko hi brūyāj jijīviṣuḥ
a samudrataraṇaṃ dorbhyāṃ kaṇṭhe baddhvā yathā śilām
c giryagrād vā nipatanaṃ tādṛk tava cikīrṣitam
a sahitaḥ sarvayodhais tvaṃ vyūḍhānīkaiḥ surakṣitaḥ
c dhanaṃjayena yudhyasva śreyaś cet prāptum icchasi
a hitārthaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya bravīmi tvā na hiṃsayā
c śraddhatsvaitan mayā proktaṃ yadi te 'sti jijīviṣā
 karṇa uvāca
a svavīrye 'haṃ parāśvasya prārthayāmy arjunaṃ raṇe
c tvaṃ tu mitramukhaḥ śatrur māṃ bhīṣayitum icchasi
a na mām asmād abhiprāyāt kaś cid adya nivartayet
c apīndro vajram udyamya kiṃ nu martyaḥ kariṣyati
 saṃjaya uvāca
a iti karṇasya vākyānte śalyaḥ prāhottaraṃ vacaḥ
c cukopayiṣur atyarthaṃ karṇaṃ madreśvaraḥ punaḥ
a yadā vai tvāṃ phalgunaveganunnā
jyācoditā hastavatā visṛṣṭāḥ
c anvetāraḥ kaṅkapatrāḥ śitāgrās
tadā tapsyasy arjunasyābhiyogāt
a yadā divyaṃ dhanur ādāya pārthaḥ
prabhāsayan pṛtanāṃ savyasācī
c tvām ardayeta niśitaiḥ pṛṣatkais
tadā paścāt tapsyase sūtaputra
a bālaś candraṃ mātur aṅke śayāno
yathā kaś cit prārthayate 'pahartum
c tadvan mohād yatamāno rathasthas
tvaṃ prārthayasy arjunam adya jetum
d khanyād asiṃ tīkṣṇadhāraṃ yathājñaḥ
d sutejanaṃ nihitaṃ vai pṛthivyām
d tathā khanasy adya śitān pṛṣatkān
d yaḥ prārthayasy arjuneneha yuddham
a triśūlam āśliṣya sutīkṣṇadhāraṃ
sarvāṇi gātrāṇi nigharṣasi tvam
c sutīkṣṇadhāropamakarmaṇā tvaṃ
yuyutsase yo 'rjunenādya karṇa
a siddhaṃ siṃhaṃ kesariṇaṃ bṛhantaṃ
bālo mūḍhaḥ kṣudramṛgas tarasvī
c samāhvayet tadvad etat tavādya
samāhvānaṃ sūtaputrārjunasya
a mā sūtaputrāhvaya rājaputraṃ
mahāvīryaṃ kesariṇaṃ yathaiva
c vane sṛgālaḥ piśitasya tṛpto
mā pārtham āsādya vinaṅkṣyasi tvam
a īṣādantaṃ mahānāgaṃ prabhinnakaraṭāmukham
c śaśakāhvayase yuddhe karṇa pārthaṃ dhanaṃjayam
a bilasthaṃ kṛṣṇasarpaṃ tvaṃ bālyāt kāṣṭhena vidhyasi
c mahāviṣaṃ pūrṇakośaṃ yat pārthaṃ yoddhum icchasi
a siṃhaṃ kesariṇaṃ kruddham atikramyābhinardasi
c sṛgāla iva mūḍhatvān nṛsiṃhaṃ karṇa pāṇḍavam
a suparṇaṃ patagaśreṣṭhaṃ vainateyaṃ tarasvinam
c laṭvevāhvayase pāte karṇa pārthaṃ dhanaṃjayam
a sarvāmbhonilayaṃ bhīmam ūrmimantaṃ jhaṣāyutam
c candrodaye vivartantam aplavaḥ saṃtitīrṣasi
a ṛṣabhaṃ dundubhigrīvaṃ tīkṣṇaśṛṅgaṃ prahāriṇam
c vatsa āhvayase yuddhe karṇa pārthaṃ dhanaṃjayam
d yathā vatsataro bhūtvā jātaskandhena śuṣmiṇā
d yuddham icched gopatinā tathecchasi kirīṭinā
a mahāghoṣaṃ mahāmeghaṃ darduraḥ pratinardasi
c kāmatoyapradaṃ loke naraparjanyam arjunam
a yathā ca svagṛhasthaḥ śvā vyāghraṃ vanagataṃ bhaṣet
c tathā tvaṃ bhaṣase karṇa naravyāghraṃ dhanaṃjayam
a sṛgālo 'pi vane karṇa śaśaiḥ parivṛto vasan
c manyate siṃham ātmānaṃ yāvat siṃhaṃ na paśyati
a tathā tvam api rādheya siṃham ātmānam icchasi
c apaśyañ śatrudamanaṃ naravyāghraṃ dhanaṃjayam
a vyāghraṃ tvaṃ manyase ''tmānaṃ yāvat kṛṣṇau na paśyasi
c samāsthitāv ekarathe sūryācandramasāv iva
a yāvad gāṇḍīvanirghoṣaṃ na śṛṇoṣi mahāhave
c tāvad eva tvayā karṇa śakyaṃ vaktuṃ yathecchasi
a rathaśabdadhanuḥśabdair nādayantaṃ diśo daśa
c nardantam iva śārdūlaṃ dṛṣṭvā kroṣṭā bhaviṣyasi
a nityam eva sṛgālas tvaṃ nityaṃ siṃho dhanaṃjayaḥ
c vīrapradveṣaṇān mūḍha nityaṃ kroṣṭeva lakṣyase
a yathākhuḥ syād biḍālaś ca śvā vyāghraś ca balābale
c yathā sṛgālaḥ siṃhaś ca yathā ca śaśakuñjarau
a yathānṛtaṃ ca satyaṃ ca yathā cāpi viṣāmṛte
c tathā tvam api pārthaś ca prakhyātāv ātmakarmabhiḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a adhikṣiptas tu rādheyaḥ śalyenāmitatejasā
c śalyam āha susaṃkruddho vākśalyam avadhārayan
a guṇān guṇavataḥ śalya guṇavān vetti nāguṇaḥ
c tvaṃ tu nityaṃ guṇair hīnaḥ kiṃ jñāsyasy aguṇo guṇān
a arjunasya mahāstrāṇi krodhaṃ vīryaṃ dhanuḥ śarān
c ahaṃ śalyābhijānāmi na tvaṃ jānāsi tat tathā
c   vikramaṃ ca mahātmanaḥ
c tathā kṛṣṇasya māhātmyam ṛṣabhasya mahīkṣitām
c yathāhaṃ śalya jānāmi
a evam evātmano vīryam ahaṃ vīryaṃ ca pāṇḍave
c jānann evāhvaye yuddhe śalya nāgniṃ pataṃgavat
a asti cāyam iṣuḥ śalya supuṅkho raktabhojanaḥ
c ekatūṇīśayaḥ patrī sudhautaḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ
a śete candanapūrṇena pūjito bahulāḥ samāḥ
c āheyo viṣavān ugro narāśvadvipasaṃghahā
a ekavīro mahāraudras tanutrāsthividāraṇaḥ
c nirbhindyāṃ yena ruṣṭo 'ham api meruṃ mahāgirim
a tam ahaṃ jātu nāsyeyam anyasmin phalgunād ṛte
c kṛṣṇād vā devakīputrāt satyaṃ cātra śṛṇuṣva me
a tenāham iṣuṇā śalya vāsudevadhanaṃjayau
c yotsye paramasaṃkruddhas tat karma sadṛśaṃ mama
a sarveṣāṃ vāsudevānāṃ kṛṣṇe lakṣmīḥ pratiṣṭhitā
c sarveṣāṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ jayaḥ pārthe pratiṣṭhitaḥ
e ubhayaṃ tat samāsādya ko 'tivartitum arhati
a tāv etau puruṣavyāghrau sametau syandane sthitau
c mām ekam abhisaṃyātau sujātaṃ śalya paśya me
a pitṛṣvasāmātulajau bhrātarāv aparājitau
c maṇī sūtra iva protau draṣṭāsi nihatau mayā
a arjune gāṇḍivaṃ kṛṣṇe cakraṃ tārkṣyakapidhvajau
c bhīrūṇāṃ trāsajananau śalya harṣakarau mama
a tvaṃ tu duṣprakṛtir mūḍho mahāyuddheṣv akovidaḥ
c bhayāvatīrṇaḥ saṃtrāsād abaddhaṃ bahu bhāṣase
a saṃstauṣi tvaṃ tu kenāpi hetunā tau kudeśaja
c tau hatvā samare hantā tvām addhā sahabāndhavam
a pāpadeśaja durbuddhe kṣudra kṣatriyapāṃsana
c suhṛd bhūtvā ripuḥ kiṃ māṃ kṛṣṇābhyāṃ bhīṣayann asi
a tau vā mamādya hantārau hantāsmi samare sthitau
c nāhaṃ bibhemi kṛṣṇābhyāṃ vijānann ātmano balam
a vāsudevasahasraṃ vā phalgunānāṃ śatāni ca
c aham eko haniṣyāmi joṣam āssva kudeśaja
a striyo bālāś ca vṛddhāś ca prāyaḥ krīḍāgatā janāḥ
c yā gāthāḥ saṃpragāyanti kurvanto 'dhyayanaṃ yathā
e tā gāthāḥ śṛṇu me śalya madrakeṣu durātmasu
a brāhmaṇaiḥ kathitāḥ pūrvaṃ yathāvad rājasaṃnidhau
c śrutvā caikamanā mūḍha kṣama vā brūhi vottaram
a mitradhruṅ madrako nityaṃ yo no dveṣṭi sa madrakaḥ
c madrake saṃgataṃ nāsti kṣudravākye narādhame
a durātmā madrako nityaṃ nityaṃ cānṛtiko 'nṛjuḥ
c yāvadantaṃ hi daurātmyaṃ madrakeṣv iti naḥ śrutam
a pitā mātā ca putraś ca śvaśrūśvaśuramātulāḥ
c jāmātā duhitā bhrātā naptā te te ca bāndhavāḥ
a vayasyābhyāgatāś cānye dāsīdāsaṃ ca saṃgatam
c puṃbhir vimiśrā nāryaś ca jñātājñātāḥ svayecchayā
a yeṣāṃ gṛheṣu śiṣṭānāṃ saktumanthāśināṃ sadā
c pītvā sīdhuṃ sagomāṃsaṃ nardanti ca hasanti ca
a yāni caivāpy abaddhāni pravartante ca kāmataḥ
c kāmapralāpino 'nyonyaṃ teṣu dharmaḥ kathaṃ bhavet
a madrakeṣu vilupteṣu prakhyātāśubhakarmasu
c nāpi vairaṃ na sauhārdaṃ madrakeṣu samācaret
a madrake saṃgataṃ nāsti madrako hi sacāpalaḥ
c madrakeṣu ca duḥsparśaṃ śaucaṃ gāndhārakeṣu ca
a rājayājakayājyena naṣṭaṃ dattaṃ havir bhavet
a śūdrasaṃskārako vipro yathā yāti parābhavam
c tathā brahmadviṣo nityaṃ gacchantīha parābhavam
d tathaiva saṃgataṃ kṛtvā naraḥ patati madrakaiḥ
d na tathā saṃgataṃ cāpi madrakeṣv iha vidyate
a madrake saṃgataṃ nāsti hataṃ vṛścikato viṣam
c ātharvaṇena mantreṇa sarvā śāntiḥ kṛtā bhavet
a iti vṛścikadaṣṭasya nānāviṣahatasya ca
c kurvanti bheṣajaṃ prājñāḥ satyaṃ tac cāpi dṛśyate
e evaṃ vidvañ joṣam āssva śṛṇu cātrottaraṃ vacaḥ
a vāsāṃsy utsṛjya nṛtyanti striyo yā madyamohitāḥ
c mithune 'saṃyatāś cāpi yathākāmacarāś ca tāḥ
e tāsāṃ putraḥ kathaṃ dharmaṃ madrako vaktum arhati
a yās tiṣṭhantyaḥ pramehanti yathaivoṣṭrīdaśerake
c tāsāṃ vibhraṣṭalajjānāṃ nirlajjānāṃ tatas tataḥ
e tvaṃ putras tādṛśīnāṃ hi dharmaṃ vaktum ihecchasi
a suvīrakaṃ yācyamānā madrakā kaṣati sphijau
c adātukāmā vacanam idaṃ vadati dāruṇam
a mā mā suvīrakaṃ kaś cid yācatāṃ dayito mama
c putraṃ dadyāṃ pratipadaṃ na tu dadyāṃ suvīrakam
a nāryo bṛhatyo nirhrīkā madrakāḥ kambalāvṛtāḥ
c ghasmarā naṣṭaśaucāś ca prāya ity anuśuśruma
d pramehitvā sphijā bhūmiṃ karṣantyo hīnaśodhanāḥ
d spṛṣṭvā vāgbhir na mṛdbhiś ca nityocchiṣṭā bhavanti hi
a evamādi mayānyair vā śakyaṃ vaktuṃ bhaved bahu
c ā keśāgrān nakhāgrāc ca vaktavyeṣu kuvartmasu
a madrakāḥ sindhusauvīrā dharmaṃ vidyuḥ kathaṃ tv iha
c pāpadeśodbhavā mlecchā dharmāṇām avicakṣaṇāḥ
a eṣa mukhyatamo dharmaḥ kṣatriyasyeti naḥ śrutam
c yad ājau nihataḥ śete sadbhiḥ samabhipūjitaḥ
a āyudhānāṃ saṃparāye yan mucyeyam ahaṃ tataḥ
c na me sa prathamaḥ kalpo nidhane svargam icchataḥ
a so 'haṃ priyaḥ sakhā cāsmi dhārtarāṣṭrasya dhīmataḥ
c tadarthe hi mama prāṇā yac ca me vidyate vasu
a vyaktaṃ tvam apy upahitaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ pāpadeśaja
c yathā hy amitravat sarvaṃ tvam asmāsu pravartase
a kāmaṃ na khalu śakyo 'haṃ tvadvidhānāṃ śatair api
c saṃgrāmād vimukhaḥ kartuṃ dharmajña iva nāstikaiḥ
a sāraṅga iva gharmārtaḥ kāmaṃ vilapa śuṣya ca
c nāhaṃ bhīṣayituṃ śakyaḥ kṣatravṛtte vyavasthitaḥ
a tanutyajāṃ nṛsiṃhānām āhaveṣv anivartinām
c yā gatir guruṇā prāṅ me proktā rāmeṇa tāṃ smara
a sveṣāṃ trāṇārtham udyuktaṃ vadhāya dviṣatām api
c viddhi mām āsthitaṃ vṛttaṃ paurūravasam uttamam
a na tad bhūtaṃ prapaśyāmi triṣu lokeṣu madraka
c yo mām asmād abhiprāyād vārayed iti me matiḥ
a evaṃ vidvañ joṣam āssva trāsāt kiṃ bahu bhāṣase
c mā tvā hatvā pradāsyāmi kravyādbhyo madrakādhama
a mitrapratīkṣayā śalya dhārtarāṣṭrasya cobhayoḥ
c apavādatitikṣābhis tribhir etair hi jīvasi
a punaś ced īdṛśaṃ vākyaṃ madrarāja vadiṣyasi
c śiras te pātayiṣyāmi gadayā vajrakalpayā
a śrotāras tv idam adyeha draṣṭāro vā kudeśaja
c karṇaṃ vā jaghnatuḥ kṛṣṇau karṇo vāpi jaghāna tau
a evam uktvā tu rādheyaḥ punar eva viśāṃ pate
c abravīn madrarājānaṃ yāhi yāhīty asaṃbhramam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a māriṣādhiratheḥ śrutvā vaco yuddhābhinandinaḥ
c śalyo 'bravīt punaḥ karṇaṃ nidarśanam udāharan
d jāto 'haṃ yajvanāṃ vaṃśe saṃgrāmeṣv anivartinām
d rājñāṃ mūrdhābhiṣiktānāṃ svayaṃ dharmaparāyaṇaḥ
a yathaiva matto madyena tvaṃ tathā na ca vā tathā
c tathāhaṃ tvāṃ pramādyantaṃ cikitsāmi suhṛttayā
a imāṃ kākopamāṃ karṇa procyamānāṃ nibodha me
c śrutvā yatheṣṭaṃ kuryās tvaṃ vihīna kulapāṃsana
a nāham ātmani kiṃ cid vai kilbiṣaṃ karṇa saṃsmare
c yena tvaṃ māṃ mahābāho hantum icchasy anāgasam
a avaśyaṃ tu mayā vācyaṃ budhyatāṃ yadi te hitam
c viśeṣato rathasthena rājñaś caiva hitaiṣiṇā
a samaṃ ca viṣamaṃ caiva rathinaś ca balābalam
c śramaḥ khedaś ca satataṃ hayānāṃ rathinā saha
a āyudhasya parijñānaṃ rutaṃ ca mṛgapakṣiṇām
c bhāraś cāpy atibhāraś ca śalyānāṃ ca pratikriyā
a astrayogaś ca yuddhaṃ ca nimittāni tathaiva ca
c sarvam etan mayā jñeyaṃ rathasyāsya kuṭumbinā
e atas tvāṃ kathaye karṇa nidarśanam idaṃ punaḥ
a vaiśyaḥ kila samudrānte prabhūtadhanadhānyavān
c yajvā dānapatiḥ kṣāntaḥ svakarmastho 'bhavac chuciḥ
a bahuputraḥ priyāpatyaḥ sarvabhūtānukampakaḥ
c rājño dharmapradhānasya rāṣṭre vasati nirbhayaḥ
a putrāṇāṃ tasya bālānāṃ kumārāṇāṃ yaśasvinām
c kāko bahūnām abhavad ucciṣṭakṛtabhojanaḥ
a tasmai sadā prayacchanti vaiśyaputrāḥ kumārakāḥ
c māṃsodanaṃ dadhi kṣīraṃ pāyasaṃ madhusarpiṣī
a sa cocchiṣṭabhṛtaḥ kāko vaiśyaputraiḥ kumārakaiḥ
c sadṛśān pakṣiṇo dṛptaḥ śreyasaś cāvamanyate
a atha haṃsāḥ samudrānte kadā cid abhipātinaḥ
c garuḍasya gatau tulyāś cakrāṅgā hṛṣṭacetasaḥ
a kumārakās tato haṃsān dṛṣṭvā kākam athābruvan
c bhavān eva viśiṣṭo hi patatribhyo vihaṃgama
d ete nipātinaḥ paśya sahitān viyadāśritān
d ebhis tvam abhiśaknoṣi kasmān na prāpitas tvayā
a pratāryamāṇas tu sa tair alpabuddhibhir aṇḍajaḥ
c tad vacaḥ satyam ity eva maurkhyād darpāc ca manyate
a tān so 'bhipatya jijñāsuḥ ka eṣāṃ śreṣṭhabhāg iti
c ucchiṣṭadarpitaḥ kāko bahūnāṃ dūrapātinām
a teṣāṃ yaṃ pravaraṃ mene haṃsānāṃ dūrapātinām
c tam āhvayata durbuddhiḥ patāma iti pakṣiṇam
a tac chrutvā prāhasan haṃsā ye tatrāsan samāgatāḥ
c bhāṣato bahu kākasya balinaḥ patatāṃ varāḥ
e idam ūcuś ca cakrāṅgā vacaḥ kākaṃ vihaṃgamāḥ
a vayaṃ haṃsāś carāmemāṃ pṛthivīṃ mānasaukasaḥ
c pakṣiṇāṃ ca vayaṃ nityaṃ dūrapātena pūjitāḥ
a kathaṃ nu haṃsaṃ balinaṃ vajrāṅgaṃ dūrapātinam
c kāko bhūtvā nipatane samāhvayasi durmate
e kathaṃ tvaṃ patanaṃ kāka sahāsmābhir bravīṣi tat
a atha haṃsavaco mūḍhaḥ kutsayitvā punaḥ punaḥ
c prajagādottaraṃ kākaḥ katthano jātilāghavāt
a śatam ekaṃ ca pātānāṃ patitāsmi na saṃśayaḥ
c śatayojanam ekaikaṃ vicitraṃ vividhaṃ tathā
a uḍḍīnam avaḍīnaṃ ca praḍīnaṃ ḍīnam eva ca
c niḍīnam atha saṃḍīnaṃ tiryak cātigatāni ca
a viḍīnaṃ pariḍīnaṃ ca parāḍīnaṃ suḍīnakam
c atiḍīnaṃ mahāḍīnaṃ niḍīnaṃ pariḍīnakam
d saṃpātaṃ samudīṣaṃ ca tatonyad vyatiriktakam
d avaḍīnaṃ praḍīnaṃ ca saṃḍīnaṃ ḍīnaḍīnakam
d saṃḍīnoḍḍīnaḍīnaṃ ca punar ḍīnaviḍīnakam
a gatāgatapratigatā bahvīś ca nikuḍīnikāḥ
c kartāsmi miṣatāṃ vo 'dya tato drakṣyatha me balam
d teṣām anyatamenāhaṃ patiṣyāmi vihāyasam
d pradiśadhvaṃ yathānyāyaṃ kena haṃsāḥ patāmy aham
d te vai dhruvaṃ viniścitya patadhvaṃ na mayā saha
d pātair ebhiḥ khalu khagāḥ patituṃ khe nirāśraye
a evam ukte tu kākena prahasyaiko vihaṃgamaḥ
c uvāca haṃsas taṃ kākaṃ vacanaṃ tan nibodha me
a śatam ekaṃ ca pātānāṃ tvaṃ kāka patitā dhruvam
c ekam eva tu ye pātaṃ viduḥ sarve vihaṃgamāḥ
a tam ahaṃ patitā kāka nānyaṃ jānāmi kaṃ cana
c pata tvam api raktākṣa yena vā tena manyase
a atha kākāḥ prajahasur ye tatrāsan samāgatāḥ
c katham ekena pātena haṃsaḥ pātaśataṃ jayet
a ekenaiva śatasyaikaṃ pātenābhibhaviṣyati
b kākaḥ
b aham ekena pātena haṃsa pātaśataṃ jaye
b ekenaiva ca haṃsa tvaṃ pāteneha patiṣyasi
c haṃsasya patitaṃ kāko balavān āśuvikramaḥ
a prapetatuḥ spardhayātha tatas tau haṃsavāyasau
c ekapātī ca cakrāṅgaḥ kākaḥ pātaśatena ca
d spardhinau sahitau tūrṇaṃ kham āsthāya tarasvinau
d pūrvam eva tu vai kākas tūrṇaṃ gantuṃ pracakrame
d kāko 'tha haṃsaṃ cāpalyāc chīghratāṃ pratidarśayan
d vegenātītya tarasā punar eti muhur muhuḥ
d tuṇḍenābhyahanac caitaṃ kurvan nāmāpasavyataḥ
d rorūyann iti cāpy etaṃ samāhvayati vai muhuḥ
a petivān atha cakrāṅgaḥ petivān atha vāyasaḥ
c visismāpayiṣuḥ pātair ācakṣāṇo ''tmanaḥ kriyām
a atha kākasya citrāṇi patitānītarāṇi ca
c dṛṣṭvā pramuditāḥ kākā vinedur atha taiḥ svaraiḥ
a haṃsāṃś cāvahasanti sma prāvadann apriyāṇi ca
c utpatyotpatya ca prāhur muhūrtam iti ceti ca
a vṛkṣāgrebhyaḥ sthalebhyaś ca nipatanty utpatanti ca
c kurvāṇā vividhān rāvān āśaṃsantas tadā jayam
a haṃsas tu mṛdukenaiva vikrāntum upacakrame
c pratyahīyata kākāc ca muhūrtam iva māriṣa
a avamanya rayaṃ haṃsān idaṃ vacanam abravīt
c yo 'sāv utpatito haṃsaḥ so 'sāv eva prahīyate
a atha haṃsaḥ sa tac chrutvā prāpatat paścimāṃ diśam
a   bhāṣitaṃ patatāṃ varaḥ
a vigāhya haṃso vikṣobhya
c upary upari vegena sāgaraṃ varuṇālayam
d bahusattvasamākīrṇaṃ vīcībhir bhīmadarśanam
d athācireṇa rādheya kāko vegād ahīyata
d tato 'tīva pariśrāntaḥ kathaṃ cid dhaṃsam anvagāt
a tato bhīḥ prāviśat kākaṃ tadā tatra vicetasam
c dvīpadrumān apaśyantaṃ nipatantaṃ śramānvitam
d avekṣamāṇas taṃ kākaṃ vihvalaṃ taṃ muhur muhuḥ
e nipateyaṃ kva nu śrānta iti tasmiñ jalārṇave
a aviṣahyaḥ samudro hi bahusattvagaṇālayaḥ
c mahābhūtaśatodbhāsī nabhaso 'pi viśiṣyate
a gāmbhīryād dhi samudrasya na viśeṣaḥ kulādhama
c digambarāmbhasāṃ karṇa samudrasthā hi durjayāḥ
e vidūrapātāt toyasya kiṃ punaḥ karṇa vāyasaḥ
a atha haṃso 'bhyatikramya muhūrtam iti ceti ca
c avekṣamāṇas taṃ kākaṃ nāśaknod vyapasarpitum
e atikramya ca cakrāṅgaḥ kākaṃ taṃ samudaikṣata
f yāvad gatvā pataty eṣa kāko mām iti cintayan
f tataḥ kāko bhṛśaṃ śrānto haṃsam abhyāgamat tadā
f śanakaiḥ parihīyantaṃ pariśrāntam acetasam
f taṃ prahasya ca cakrāṅgaḥ kākaṃ mandagatiṃ tadā
a taṃ tathā hīyamānaṃ ca haṃso dṛṣṭvābravīd idam
c ujjihīrṣur nimajjantaṃ smaran satpuruṣavratam
a bahūni patanāni tvam ācakṣāṇo muhur muhuḥ
c patasy avyāharaṃś cedaṃ na no guhyaṃ prabhāṣase
a kiṃ nāma patanaṃ kāka yat tvaṃ patasi sāṃpratam
c jalaṃ spṛśasi pakṣābhyāṃ tuṇḍena ca punaḥ punaḥ
d prabrūhi katame tatra pāte vartasi vāyasa
d ehy ehi kāka śīghraṃ tvam eṣa tvāṃ pratipālaye
a sa pakṣābhyāṃ spṛśann ārtas tuṇḍena jalam arṇave
b dṛṣṭo haṃsena duṣṭātmann idaṃ haṃsaṃ tato 'bravīt
b apaśyann ambhasaḥ pāraṃ nipataṃś ca śramānvitaḥ
b pātavegapramathito haṃsaṃ kāko 'bravīd idam
b vayaṃ kākāḥ kuto nāma carāmaḥ kākapātikām
b haṃsa prāṇaiḥ prapadye tvāṃ dvīpāntaṃ prāpayasva mām
b sa pakṣābhyāṃ spṛśann ārtas tuṇḍena ca mahārṇavam
c kāko dṛḍhaṃ pariśrāntaḥ sahasā nipapāta ha
d sāgarāmbhasi taṃ dṛṣṭvā patitaṃ dīnacetasam
d mriyamāṇam idaṃ kākaṃ haṃso vākyam uvāca ha
 haṃsa uvāca
a śatam ekaṃ ca pātānāṃ yat prabhāṣasi vāyasa
b ślāghamānas tvam ātmānaṃ kāka bhāṣitavān asi
b sa tvam ekaśataṃ pātaṃ patann abhyadhiko mayā
b katham evaṃ pariśrāntaḥ patito 'si mahārṇave
b pratyuvāca tataḥ kākaḥ sīdamāna idaṃ vacaḥ
b upariṣṭhaṃ tadā haṃsam abhivīkṣya prasādayan
c nānāvidhānīha purā tac cānṛtam ihādya te
 kāka uvāca
a ucchiṣṭadarpito haṃsa manye ''tmānaṃ suparṇavat
c avamanya bahūṃś cāhaṃ kākān anyāṃś ca pakṣiṇaḥ
e prāṇair haṃsa prapadye tvāṃ dvīpāntaṃ prāpayasva mām
f ucchiṣṭānnena puṣṭo 'haṃ darpotsiktaḥ kuvāyasaḥ
f suparṇa iti cātmānaṃ jñātavān buddhilāghavāt
f śaraṇaṃ tvāṃ prapanno 'ham udakāntam avāpnuyām
f haṃsedānīṃ pariśrāntam āpado māṃ samuddhara
a yady ahaṃ svastimān haṃsa svadeśaṃ prāpnuyāṃ punaḥ
c na kaṃ cid avamanyeyam āpado māṃ samuddhara
d yadi nāma punar jīvan gaccheyaṃ svaṃ niveśanam
d naivaṃ punar hīnam api kṣeptāhaṃ khevicāriṇam
a tam evaṃvādinaṃ dīnaṃ vilapantam acetanam
c kāka kāketi vāśantaṃ nimajjantaṃ mahārṇave
d kṛpayābhiparīto vai kṛpāṃ cakre durātmani
a tathaitya vāyasaṃ haṃso jalaklinnaṃ sudurdaśam
c padbhyām utkṣipya vepantaṃ pṛṣṭham āropayac chanaiḥ
a āropya pṛṣṭhaṃ kākaṃ taṃ haṃsaḥ karṇa vicetasam
b avismayaṃs tadā karṇa punar enaṃ samānayat
c ājagāma punar dvīpaṃ spardhayā petatur yataḥ
d utsṛjaṃś cābravīn maivaṃ punaḥ kāryaṃ tvayeti ha
a saṃsthāpya taṃ cāpi punaḥ samāśvāsya ca khecaram
c gato yathepsitaṃ deśaṃ haṃso mana ivāśugaḥ
d evam ucchiṣṭapuṣṭaḥ sa kāko haṃsaparājitaḥ
d balaṃ vīryaṃ mahat karṇa tyaktvā kṣāntim upāgataḥ
a ucchiṣṭabhojanāt kāko yathā vaiśyakule tu saḥ
c evaṃ tvam ucchiṣṭabhṛto dhārtarāṣṭrair na saṃśayaḥ
e sadṛśāñ śreyasaś cāpi sarvān karṇātimanyase
a droṇadrauṇikṛpair gupto bhīṣmeṇānyaiś ca kauravaiḥ
c virāṭanagare pārtham ekaṃ kiṃ nāvadhīs tadā
a yatra vyastāḥ samastāś ca nirjitāḥ stha kirīṭinā
c sṛgālā iva siṃhena kva te vīryam abhūt tadā
a bhrātaraṃ ca hataṃ dṛṣṭvā nirjitaḥ savyasācinā
c paśyatāṃ kuruvīrāṇāṃ prathamaṃ tvaṃ palāyathāḥ
a tathā dvaitavane karṇa gandharvaiḥ samabhidrutaḥ
c kurūn samagrān utsṛjya prathamaṃ tvaṃ palāyathāḥ
a hatvā jitvā ca gandharvāṃś citrasenamukhān raṇe
c karṇa duryodhanaṃ pārthaḥ sabhāryaṃ samamocayat
a punaḥ prabhāvaḥ pārthasya purāṇaḥ keśavasya ca
c kathitaḥ karṇa rāmeṇa sabhāyāṃ rājasaṃsadi
a satataṃ ca tad aśrauṣīr vacanaṃ droṇabhīṣmayoḥ
c avadhyau vadatoḥ kṛṣṇau saṃnidhau vai mahīkṣitām
a kiyantaṃ tatra vakṣyāmi yena yena dhanaṃjayaḥ
c tvatto 'tiriktaḥ sarvebhyo bhūtebhyo brāhmaṇo yathā
a idānīm eva draṣṭāsi pradhane syandane sthitau
c putraṃ ca vasudevasya pāṇḍavaṃ ca dhanaṃjayam
d yathāśrayata cakrāṅgaṃ vāyaso buddhim āsthitaḥ
d tathāśrayasva vārṣṇeyaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ ca dhanaṃjayam
d yadā tvaṃ yudhi vikrāntau vāsudevadhanaṃjayau
d draṣṭāsy ekarathe karṇaṃ tadā naivaṃ vadiṣyasi
d yadā śaraśataiḥ pārtho darpaṃ tava vadhiṣyati
d tadā tvam antaraṃ draṣṭā ātmanaś cārjunasya ca
d tvaṃ śīghram eva vārṣṇeyaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ ca dhanaṃjayam
a devāsuramanuṣyeṣu prakhyātau yau nararṣabhau
b tau māvamaṃsthā maurkhyāt tvaṃ khadyota iva rocanau
b sūryācandramasau yadvat tadvad arjunakeśavau
c prakāśenābhivikhyātau tvaṃ tu khadyotavan nṛṣu
a evaṃ vidvān māvamaṃsthāḥ sūtaputrācyutārjunau
c nṛsiṃhau tau naraśvā tvaṃ joṣam āssva vikatthana
 saṃjaya uvāca
a madrādhipasyādhirathis tadaivaṃ
vaco niśamyāpriyam apratītaḥ
c uvāca śalyaṃ viditaṃ mamaitad
yathāvidhāv arjunavāsudevau
a śaure rathaṃ vāhayato 'rjunasya
balaṃ mahāstrāṇi ca pāṇḍavasya
c ahaṃ vijānāmi yathāvad adya
parokṣabhūtaṃ tava tat tu śalya
a tau cāpradhṛṣyau śastrabhṛtāṃ variṣṭhau
vyapetabhīr yodhayiṣyāmi kṛṣṇau
b purā mahendrādrivare samṛddhe
b tapasvinaṃ rāmam upetya śalya
b astrārthinaṃ mādya śiṣyaṃ gṛhāṇety
b athābruvaṃ brāhmaṇacchadmanā ca
b tatrāvasaṃ brāhmaṇa ity avipro
b brahmāstralobhād anṛtena cāham
b taj jāmadagnyena paraṃ mahāstraṃ
b samantrayuktaṃ vihitaṃ mamāsīt
b astraṃ yadā tad viditaṃ mamāsīt
b tadābravīd brāhmaṇo māṃ maharṣiḥ
b āpadgatenāstram idaṃ prayojyaṃ
b tvayā raṇe gacchatā sādhayeti
c saṃtāpayaty abhyadhikaṃ tu rāmāc
chāpo 'dya māṃ brāhmaṇasattamāc ca
a avātsaṃ vai brāhmaṇacchadmanāhaṃ

c tatrāpi me devarājena vighno
hitārthinā phalgunasyaiva śalya
a kṛto 'vabhedena mamorum etya

d sa dhairyayuktaṃ prasamīkṣya māṃ vai
d na tvaṃ vipraḥ ko 'si satyaṃ vadeti
d tasmai tadātmānam ahaṃ yathāvad

c sūtopadhāv āptam idaṃ tvayāstraṃ

d yo 'yaṃ śalya bharateṣūpapannaḥ

d yena kṣepsye samare śatrupūgān
d pratāpinaṃ balavantaṃ kṛtāstraṃ

d krūraṃ śūraṃ raudram amitrasāhaṃ

d dhruvaṃ kurūṇām ayam antakālo
d mahābhayaḥ śoṇitaughapravāhī

d astraṃ hi me na pratibhām upaiti
d yena kṣayaṃ śatrugaṇān nayiṣye
d tasmāt tam āsādaya madrarāja
d divyaṃ dhanur yasya maheṣavaś ca
d astrāṇi divyāni ca santi yasmiṃs
d tasmin rathaṃ prāpaya śīghram adya
d śroṣyantīmaṃ kathyamānaṃ vicitraṃ
d yāvad bhūmau bhavitāro manuṣyāḥ
d karṇaḥ kṛṣṇau jaghnivān ekavīraḥ

a apāṃ patir vegavān aprameyo

c mahānagaṃ yaḥ kurute samudraṃ
velaiva taṃ vārayaty aprameyam
a pramuñcantaṃ bāṇasaṃghān amoghān
marmacchido vīrahaṇaḥ sapatrān

a evaṃ balenātibalaṃ mahāstraṃ

c śaraughiṇaṃ pārthivān majjayantaṃ

a adyāhave yasya na tulyam anyaṃ
manye manuṣyaṃ dhanur ādadānam
c surāsurān vai yudhi yo jayeta
tenādya me paśya yuddhaṃ sughoram
a atimānī pāṇḍavo yuddhakāmo

c tasyāstram astrair abhihatya saṃkhye
śarottamaiḥ pātayiṣyāmi pārtham
a divākareṇāpi samaṃ tapantaṃ
samāptaraśmiṃ yaśasā jvalantam
b sahasraraśmipratimaṃ jvalantaṃ

c tamonudaṃ megha ivātimātro

d āśīviṣaṃ durdharam aprameyaṃ

d krodhapradīptaṃ tv ahitaṃ mahāntaṃ
d kuntīputraṃ śamayiṣyāmi bhallaiḥ
a pramāthinaṃ balavantaṃ prahāriṇaṃ
