a viśāradaṃ rathamārgeṣv asaktaṃ
dhuryaṃ nityaṃ samareṣu pravīram
c loke varaṃ sarvadhanurdharāṇāṃ
dhanaṃjayaṃ saṃyuge saṃsahiṣye
a adyāhave yasya na tulyam anyaṃ
madhyemanuṣyaṃ dhanur ādadānam
c sarvām imāṃ yaḥ pṛthivīṃ saheta
tathā vidvān yotsyamāno 'smi tena
a yaḥ sarvabhūtāni sadevakāni
prasthe 'jayat khāṇḍave savyasācī
c ko jīvitaṃ rakṣamāṇo hi tena
yuyutsate mām ṛte mānuṣo 'nyaḥ
d mānī kṛtāstraḥ kṛtahastayogo
d divyāstravic chvetahayaḥ pramāthī
d tasyāham adyātirathasya kāyāc
d chiro hariṣyāmi śitaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ
d yotsyāmy enaṃ śalya dhanaṃjayaṃ vai
d mṛtyuṃ puraskṛtya raṇe jayaṃ vā
d anyo hi na hy ekarathena martyo
d yudhyeta yaḥ pāṇḍavam indrakalpam
a ahaṃ tasya pauruṣaṃ pāṇḍavasya
brūyāṃ hṛṣṭaḥ samitau kṣatriyāṇām
c kiṃ tvaṃ mūrkhaḥ prabhaṣan mūḍhacetā
mām avocaḥ pauruṣam arjunasya
a apriyo yaḥ paruṣo niṣṭhuro hi
kṣudraḥ kṣeptā kṣamiṇaś cākṣamāvān
c hanyām ahaṃ tādṛśānāṃ śatāni
kṣamāmi tvāṃ kṣamayā kālayogāt
a avocas tvaṃ pāṇḍavārthe 'priyāṇi
pradharṣayan māṃ mūḍhavat pāpakarman
c mayy ārjave jihmagatir hatas tvaṃ
mitradrohī saptapadaṃ hi mitram
a kālas tv ayaṃ mṛtyumayo 'tidāruṇo
duryodhano yuddham upāgamad yat
c tasyārthasiddhim abhikāṅkṣamāṇas
tam abhyeṣye yatra naikāntyam asti
d tathāpy ahaṃ pāṇḍavavāsudevau
d yotsye raṇe madvidhasyaiva karma
d na prākṛtaḥ sajjate vai kadā cid
d yaḥ pratyudīyāt kṛṣṇadhanaṃjayau tau
a mitraṃ mider nandateḥ prīyater vā
saṃtrāyater mānada modater vā
b pramīyate bhajater yac ca mitraṃ
b tac cāpi sarvaṃ mama duryodhane 'sti
b mitraṃ mitrair nandyate prīyate vā
b saṃtrāyate mānada modate vā
c bravīti tac cāmuta viprapūrvāt
tac cāpi sarvaṃ mama duryodhane 'sti
a śatruḥ śadeḥ śāsateḥ śāyater vā
śṛṇāter vā śvayater vāpi sarge
c upasargād bahudhā sūdateś ca
prāyeṇa sarvaṃ tvayi tac ca mahyam
d śānte śatrau śāsate kauravendro
d bhūmiṃ sarvāṃ sarvasaṃpatsamṛddhām
d prāyeṇa tvaṃ vetsi śalya prabhāvaṃ
d duryodhanārthaṃ yudhyato me narendra
d yaśortham arthārtham athetarārthaṃ
d tasmād ahaṃ pāṇḍavavāsudevau
a duryodhanārthaṃ tava cāpriyārthaṃ
yaśortham ātmārtham apīśvarārtham
c tasmād ahaṃ pāṇḍavavāsudevau
yotsye yatnāt karma tat paśya me 'dya
d yāhi tattvaṃ saṃgataḥ pāṇḍavena
d dhanaṃjayaṃ mṛtyulokaṃ nayiṣye
d tayā cāhaṃ mṛtyulokaṃ gamiṣye
d yasmād upāttaṃ bhārgavād astravṛndam
d tasmād astraṃ śatrusaṃghe pramāmi 
d śalyādyāhaṃ saṃgataḥ pāṇḍavena
d mucyeyaṃ cej jīvamānaḥ kathaṃ cit
d śaśvan mṛtyoḥ syām anādhṛṣyarūpo
d vyaktaṃ tasmāt saṃyugād vipramuktaḥ
a astrāṇi paśyādya mamottamāni
brāhmāṇi divyāny atha mānuṣāṇi
c āsādayiṣyāmy aham ugravīryaṃ
dvipottamaṃ mattam ivābhimattaḥ
a astraṃ brāhmaṃ manasā tad dhy ajayyaṃ
kṣepsye pārthāyāpratimaṃ jayāya
c tenāpi me naiva mucyeta yuddhe
na cet pated viṣame me 'dya cakram
a vaivasvatād daṇḍahastād varuṇād vāpi pāśinaḥ
c sagadād vā dhanapateḥ savajrād vāpi vāsavāt
a nānyasmād api kasmāc cid bibhimo hy ātatāyinaḥ
c iti śalya vijānīhi yathā nāhaṃ bibhemy abhīḥ
a tasmād bhayaṃ na me pārthān nāpi caiva janārdanāt
c adya yuddhaṃ hi tābhyāṃ me saṃparāye bhaviṣyati
d kadā cid vijayasyāham astrahetor aṭan nṛpa
d ajñānād dhi kṣipan bāṇān ghorarūpān bhayānakān
a śvabhre te patatāṃ cakram iti me brāhmaṇo 'vadat
c yudhyamānasya saṃgrāme prāptasyaikāyane bhayam
a tasmād bibhemi balavad brāhmaṇavyāhṛtād aham
c ete hi somarājāna īśvarāḥ sukhaduḥkhayoḥ
d adāṃ tasmai gosahasraṃ balīvardāṃś ca ṣaṭśatān
d prasādaṃ na lebhe śalya brāhmaṇān madrakeśvara
d kadā cid brāhmaṇasyātha homadhenor ahaṃ nṛpa
d ajānann akṣipaṃ bāṇaṃ ghorarūpaṃ bhayānakam
a homadhenvā vatsam asya pramatta iṣuṇāhanam
c carantam ajane śalya brāhmaṇāt tapaso nidheḥ
d yasmāt tvayā pramattena homadhenvā hataḥ sutaḥ
d yasmād vatsa tvayā cātra homadhenvā hataḥ sutaḥ
d tasmāt tvam api rādheya vākśalyaṃ mahad āpnuhi
d śvabhre te patitā cakraṃ
d   yudhyamānasya śatruṇā
d prāpta ekāyane kāle mṛtyusādhāraṇe tvayi
d spardhase yena saṃgrāme yadarthaṃ ghaṭase 'niśam
d tata eva dhruvaṃ mṛtyuṃ sūta prāpsyasi saṃyuge
d ahaṃ prasādayāṃ cakre brāhmaṇaṃ saṃśitavratam
d gavāṃ daśaśataṃ vittaṃ balīvardāṃś ca ṣaṭśatam
d prayacchann ālabhaṃ kāmaṃ brāhmaṇāt tam ahaṃ tadā
d dāsīśataṃ niṣkakaṇṭhaṃ śatam aśvatarīrathān
d kanyānāṃ niṣkakaṇṭhīnāṃ sahasraṃ samalaṃkṛtam
d śalyam uddhartum āyāntaṃ
a īṣādantān saptaśatān dāsīdāsaśatāni ca
a   kuñjarān ṣaṣṭihāyanān
a aśvānāṃ ca sahasre dve
c dadato dvijamukhyāya prasādaṃ na cakāra me
a kṛṣṇānāṃ śvetavatsānāṃ sahasrāṇi caturdaśa
c āharan na labhe tasmāt prasādaṃ dvijasattamāt
a ṛddhaṃ gehaṃ sarvakāmair yac ca me vasu kiṃ cana
c tat sarvam asmai satkṛtya prayacchāmi na cecchati
d yat kiṃ cin māmakaṃ vittaṃ tvadadhīnaṃ karomi tat
d iti māṃ yācamānaṃ vai brāhmaṇaḥ pratyavārayat
d krodhadīptekṣaṇaḥ śalya nirdahānn iva cakṣuṣā
a tato 'bravīn māṃ yācantam aparāddhaṃ prayatnataḥ
c vyāhṛtaṃ yan mayā sūta tat tathā na tad anyathā
a anṛtoktaṃ prajā hanyāt tataḥ pāpam avāpnuyāt
c tasmād dharmābhirakṣārthaṃ nānṛtaṃ vaktum utsahe
a mā tvaṃ brahmagatiṃ hiṃsyāḥ prāyaścittaṃ kṛtaṃ tvayā
b naitad avyāhṛtaṃ kuryāt sarvaloko 'pi sūtaja
b yan mayoktaṃ saroṣeṇa gaccha sūtaja mā ciram
b iti mām asakṛt kruddhaḥ sa uvāca dvijottamaḥ
b ete hi somarājāna īśvarāḥ sukhaduḥkhayoḥ
b nāhaṃ bibhemi bībhatsor na śalya madhusūdanāt
b tasmād bibhemy ahaṃ śāpāt tena satyena te śape
b saha yuddhaṃ sametābhyām adyedaṃ samupasthitam
b yuddhe 'smiñ jīvitaṃ me 'dya śalya saṃśayam āgatam
b śakro 'py amararāṭ tābhyām upagamyāhavaṃ saha
b saṃśayaṃ paramaṃ gacchet kathaṃ vā manyate bhavān
c madvākyaṃ nānṛtaṃ loke kaś cit kuryāt samāpnuhi
a ity etat te mayā proktaṃ kṣiptenāpi suhṛttayā
c jānāmi tvādhikṣipantaṃ joṣam āssvottaraṃ śṛṇu
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tataḥ punar mahārāja madrarājam ariṃdamam
c abhyabhāṣata rādheyaḥ saṃnivāryottaraṃ vacaḥ
a yat tvaṃ nidarśanārthaṃ māṃ śalya jalpitavān asi
c nāhaṃ śakyas tvayā vācā vibhīṣayitum āhave
a yadi māṃ devatāḥ sarvā yodhayeyuḥ savāsavāḥ
b nānyasmād api kasmāc cid amitād ātatāyinaḥ
c tathāpi me bhayaṃ na syāt kim u pārthāt sakeśavāt
a nāhaṃ bhīṣayituṃ śakyo vāṅmātreṇa kathaṃ cana
c anyaṃ jānīhi yaḥ śakyas tvayā bhīṣayituṃ raṇe
d dandahyamānās tīkṣṇena nīcāḥ parayaśogninā
d aśaktās tat padaṃ gantuṃ tato nindāṃ pracakrire
a nīcasya balam etāvat pāruṣyaṃ yat tvam āttha mām
c aśakto 'smadguṇān prāptuṃ valgase bahu durmate
a na hi karṇaḥ samudbhūto bhayārtham iha māriṣa
c vikramārtham ahaṃ jāto yaśorthaṃ ca tathaiva ca
d sakhibhāvena sauhārdān mitrabhāvena caiva hi
d kāraṇais tribhir etais tvaṃ śalya jīvasi sāṃpratam
d rājñaś ca dhārtarāṣṭrasya kāryaṃ sumahad udyatam
d mayi tac cāhitaṃ śalya tena jīvasi me kṣaṇam
d kṛtaś ca samayaḥ pūrvaṃ kṣantavyaṃ vipriyaṃ tava
d samayaḥ paripālyo me tena jīvasi madraka
d ṛte śalyasahasreṇa vijayeyam ahaṃ parān
d mitradrohas tu pāpīyān iti jīvasi sāṃpratam
d śalya uvāca
d nanu pralāpāḥ karṇaite yān bravīṣi parān prati
d saṃjaya uvāca
d ṛte karṇasahasreṇa śakyā jetuṃ pare yudhi
d tathā bruvantaṃ paruṣaṃ karṇo madrādhipaṃ tadā
d paruṣaṃ dviguṇaṃ bhūyaḥ provācāpriyadarśanam
a idaṃ tu me tvam ekāgraḥ śṛṇu madrajanādhipa
c saṃnidhau dhṛtarāṣṭrasya procyamānaṃ mayā śrutam
a deśāṃś ca vividhāṃś citrān pūrvavṛttāṃś ca pārthivān
c brāhmaṇāḥ kathayantaḥ sma dhṛtarāṣṭram upāsate
a tatra vṛddhaḥ purāvṛttāḥ kathāḥ kāś cid dvijottamaḥ
c bāhlīkadeśaṃ madrāṃś ca kutsayan vākyam abravīt
a bahiṣkṛtā himavatā gaṅgayā ca tiraskṛtāḥ
c sarasvatyā yamunayā kurukṣetreṇa cāpi ye
a pañcānāṃ sindhuṣaṣṭhānāṃ nadīnāṃ ye 'ntar āśritāḥ
c tān dharmabāhyān aśucīn bāhlīkān parivarjayet
a govardhano nāma vaṭaḥ subhāṇḍaṃ nāma catvaram
c etad rājakuladvāram ākumāraḥ smarāmy aham
a kāryeṇātyarthagāḍhena bāhlīkeṣūṣitaṃ mayā
c tata eṣāṃ samācāraḥ saṃvāsād vidito mama
a śākalaṃ nāma nagaram āpagā nāma nimnagā
c jartikā nāma bāhlīkās teṣāṃ vṛttaṃ suninditam
a dhānāgauḍāsave pītvā gomāṃsaṃ laśunaiḥ saha
c apūpamāṃsavāṭyānām āśinaḥ śīlavarjitāḥ
a hasanti gānti nṛtyanti strībhir mattā vivāsasaḥ
c nagarāgāravapreṣu bahir mālyānulepanāḥ
a mattāvagītair vividhaiḥ kharoṣṭraninadopamaiḥ
b anāvṛtā maithune tāḥ kāmacārāś ca sarvaśaḥ
c āhur anyonyam uktāni prabruvāṇā madotkaṭāḥ
a hā hate hā hatety eva svāmibhartṛhateti ca
c ākrośantyaḥ pranṛtyanti mandāḥ parvasv asaṃyatāḥ
a teṣāṃ kilāvaliptānāṃ nivasan kurujāṅgale
c kaś cid bāhlīkamukhyānāṃ nātihṛṣṭamanā jagau
a sā nūnaṃ bṛhatī gaurī sūkṣmakambalavāsinī
c mām anusmaratī śete bāhlīkaṃ kuruvāsinam
a śatadrukanadīṃ tīrtvā tāṃ ca ramyām irāvatīm
c gatvā svadeśaṃ drakṣyāmi sthūlaśaṅkhāḥ śubhāḥ striyaḥ
a manaḥśilojjvalāpāṅgā gauryas trikakudāñjanāḥ
c kevalājinasaṃvītāḥ kūrdantyaḥ priyadarśanāḥ
a mṛdaṅgānakaśaṅkhānāṃ mardalānāṃ ca nisvanaiḥ
c kharoṣṭrāśvataraiś caiva mattā yāsyāmahe sukham
a śamīpīlukarīrāṇāṃ vaneṣu sukhavartmasu
c apūpān saktupiṇḍīś ca khādanto mathitānvitāḥ
a pathiṣu prabalā bhūtvā kadāsamṛdite 'dhvani
c khalopahāraṃ kurvāṇās tāḍayiṣyāma bhūyasaḥ
a evaṃ hīneṣu vrātyeṣu bāhlīkeṣu durātmasu
c kaś cetayāno nivasen muhūrtam api mānavaḥ
a īdṛśā brāhmaṇenoktā bāhlīkā moghacāriṇaḥ
c yeṣāṃ ṣaḍbhāgahartā tvam ubhayoḥ śubhapāpayoḥ
a ity uktvā brāhmaṇaḥ sādhur uttaraṃ punar uktavān
c bāhlīkeṣv avinīteṣu procyamānaṃ nibodhata
a tatra sma rākṣasī gāti sadā kṛṣṇacaturdaśīm
c nagare śākale sphīte āhatya niśi dundubhim
a kadā vā ghoṣikā gāthāḥ punar gāsyanti śākale
c gavyasya tṛptā māṃsasya pītvā gauḍaṃ mahāsavam
a gaurībhiḥ saha nārībhir bṛhatībhiḥ svalaṃkṛtāḥ
c palāṇḍugaṇḍūṣayutān khādante caiḍakān bahūn
a vārāhaṃ kaukkuṭaṃ māṃsaṃ gavyaṃ gārdabham auṣṭrakam
c aiḍaṃ ca ye na khādanti teṣāṃ janma nirarthakam
a iti gāyanti ye mattāḥ śīdhunā śākalāvataḥ
c sabālavṛddhāḥ kūrdantas teṣu vṛttaṃ kathaṃ bhavet
d yatra lokeśvaraḥ kṛṣṇo devadevo janārdanaḥ
d vismṛtaḥ puruṣair ugrais teṣāṃ dharmaḥ kathaṃ bhavet
a iti śalya vijānīhi hanta bhūyo bravīmi te
c yad anyo 'py uktavān asmān brāhmaṇaḥ kurusaṃsadi
a pañca nadyo vahanty etā yatra pīluvanāny api
c śatadruś ca vipāśā ca tṛtīyerāvatī tathā
e candrabhāgā vitastā ca sindhuṣaṣṭhā bahir gatāḥ
a āraṭṭā nāma te deśā naṣṭadharmān na tān vrajet
c vrātyānāṃ dāsamīyānāṃ videhānām ayajvanām
a na devāḥ pratigṛhṇanti pitaro brāhmaṇās tathā
b śrāddhatarpaṇakarmeṣu te viprā yatra saṃsthitāḥ
b tat sarvaṃ viphalībhūtam iti satyavatī śrutiḥ
c teṣāṃ pranaṣṭadharmāṇāṃ bāhlīkānām iti śrutiḥ
a brāhmaṇena tathā proktaṃ viduṣā sādhusaṃsadi
c kāṣṭhakuṇḍeṣu bāhlīkā mṛṇmayeṣu ca bhuñjate
e saktuvāṭyāvalipteṣu śvādilīḍheṣu nirghṛṇāḥ
a āvikaṃ cauṣṭrikaṃ caiva kṣīraṃ gārdabham eva ca
c tadvikārāṃś ca bāhlīkāḥ khādanti ca pibanti ca
a putrasaṃkariṇo jālmāḥ sarvānnakṣīrabhojanāḥ
c āraṭṭā nāma bāhlīkā varjanīyā vipaścitā
a uta śalya vijānīhi hanta bhūyo bravīmi te
c yad anyo 'py uktavān sabhyo brāhmaṇaḥ kurusaṃsadi
a yugaṃdhare payaḥ pītvā proṣya cāpy acyutasthale
c tadvad bhūtilaye snātvā kathaṃ svargaṃ gamiṣyati
a pañca nadyo vahanty etā yatra niḥsṛtya parvatāt
c āraṭṭā nāma bāhlīkā na teṣv āryo dvyahaṃ vaset
a bahiś ca nāma hlīkaś ca vipāśāyāṃ piśācakau
c tayor apatyaṃ bāhlīkā naiṣā sṛṣṭiḥ prajāpateḥ
d te kathaṃ vividhān dharmāñ jñāsyante hīnayonayaḥ
a kāraskarān mahiṣakān kaliṅgān kīkaṭāṭavīn
c karkoṭakān vīrakāṃś ca durdharmāṃś ca vivarjayet
a iti tīrthānusartāraṃ rākṣasī kā cid abravīt
c ekarātrā śamīgehe maholūkhalamekhalā
a āraṭṭā nāma te deśā bāhlīkā nāma te janāḥ
b brāhmaṇāpasadā yatra tulyakālāḥ prajāpateḥ
b vedā na teṣāṃ vedyaṃ ca yajñā yajanam eva ca
b vrātyānāṃ dāśamīyānām annaṃ devā na bhuñjate
b prasthalā madragāndhārā āraṭṭā nāmataḥ khaśāḥ
c vasātisindhusauvīrā iti prāyo vikutsitāḥ
a uta śalya vijānīhi hanta bhūyo bravīmi te
c ucyamānaṃ mayā samyak tad ekāgramanāḥ śṛṇu
a brāhmaṇaḥ śilpino geham abhyagacchat purātithiḥ
c ācāraṃ tatra saṃprekṣya prītaḥ śilpinam abravīt
a mayā himavataḥ śṛṅgam ekenādhyuṣitaṃ ciram
c dṛṣṭāś ca bahavo deśā nānādharmasamākulāḥ
a na ca kena ca dharmeṇa virudhyante prajā imāḥ
c sarve hi te 'bruvan dharmaṃ yathoktaṃ vedapāragaiḥ
a aṭatā tu sadā deśān nānādharmasamākulān
c āgacchatā mahārāja bāhlīkeṣu niśāmitam
a tatraiva brāhmaṇo bhūtvā tato bhavati kṣatriyaḥ
c vaiśyaḥ śūdraś ca bāhlīkas tato bhavati nāpitaḥ
a nāpitaś ca tato bhūtvā punar bhavati brāhmaṇaḥ
c dvijo bhūtvā ca tatraiva punar dāso 'pi jāyate
a bhavaty ekaḥ kule vipraḥ śiṣṭānye kāmacāriṇaḥ
c gāndhārā madrakāś caiva bāhlīkāḥ ke 'py acetasaḥ
a etan mayā śrutaṃ tatra dharmasaṃkarakārakam
c kṛtsnām aṭitvā pṛthivīṃ bāhlīkeṣu viparyayaḥ
a uta śalya vijānīhi hanta bhūyo bravīmi te
c yad apy anyo 'bravīd vākyaṃ bāhlīkānāṃ vikutsitam
a satī purā hṛtā kā cid āraṭṭā kila dasyubhiḥ
c adharmataś copayātā sā tān abhyaśapat tataḥ
a bālāṃ bandhumatīṃ yan mām adharmeṇopagacchatha
c tasmān nāryo bhaviṣyanti bandhakyo vai kuleṣu vaḥ
e na caivāsmāt pramokṣyadhvaṃ ghorāt pāpān narādhamāḥ
f tasmāt teṣāṃ bhāgaharā bhāgineyā na sūnavaḥ
a kuravaḥ sahapāñcālāḥ śālvā matsyāḥ sanaimiṣāḥ
c kosalāḥ kāśayo 'ṅgāś ca kaliṅgā magadhās tathā
a cedayaś ca mahābhāgā dharmaṃ jānanti śāśvatam
c nānādeśeṣu santaś ca prāyo bāhyā layād ṛte
a ā matsyebhyaḥ kurupāñcāladeśyā
ā naimiṣāc cedayo ye viśiṣṭāḥ
c dharmaṃ purāṇam upajīvanti santo
madrān ṛte pañcanadāṃś ca jihmān
a evaṃ vidvan dharmakathāṃś ca rājaṃs
tūṣṇīṃbhūto jaḍavac chalya bhūyāḥ
c tvaṃ tasya goptā ca janasya rājā
ṣaḍbhāgahartā śubhaduṣkṛtasya
a atha vā duṣkṛtasya tvaṃ hartā teṣām arakṣitā
c rakṣitā puṇyabhāg rājā prajānāṃ tvaṃ tv apuṇyabhāk
a pūjyamāne purā dharme sarvadeśeṣu śāśvate
c dharmaṃ pāñcanadaṃ dṛṣṭvā dhig ity āha pitāmahaḥ
a vrātyānāṃ dāśamīyānāṃ kṛte 'py aśubhakarmaṇām
b brahmaṇā nindite dharme sa tvaṃ loke kim abravīḥ
c iti pāñcanadaṃ dharmam avamene pitāmahaḥ
e svadharmastheṣu varṇeṣu so 'py etaṃ nābhipūjayet
a uta śalya vijānīhi hanta bhūyo bravīmi te
c kalmāṣapādaḥ sarasi nimajjan rākṣaso 'bravīt
a kṣatriyasya malaṃ bhaikṣaṃ brāhmaṇasyānṛtaṃ malam
c malaṃ pṛthivyā bāhlīkāḥ strīṇāṃ madrastriyo malam
a nimajjamānam uddhṛtya kaś cid rājā niśācaram
c apṛcchat tena cākhyātaṃ proktavān yan nibodha tat
a mānuṣāṇāṃ malaṃ mlecchā mlecchānāṃ mauṣṭikā malam
c mauṣṭikānāṃ malaṃ śaṇḍāḥ śaṇḍānāṃ rājayājakāḥ
a rājayājakayājyānāṃ madrakāṇāṃ ca yan malam
c tad bhaved vai tava malaṃ yady asmān na vimuñcasi
a iti rakṣopasṛṣṭeṣu viṣavīryahateṣu ca
c rākṣasaṃ bheṣajaṃ proktaṃ saṃsiddhaṃ vacanottaram
a brāhmaṃ pāñcālāḥ kauraveyāḥ svadharmaḥ
satyaṃ matsyāḥ śūrasenāś ca yajñaḥ
c prācyā dāsā vṛṣalā dākṣiṇātyāḥ
stenā bāhlīkāḥ saṃkarā vai surāṣṭrāḥ
a kṛtaghnatā paravittāpahāraḥ
surāpānaṃ gurudārāvamarśaḥ
b vākpāruṣyaṃ govadho rātricaryā
b bahirgehaṃ paravastropabhogaḥ
c yeṣāṃ dharmas tān prati nāsty adharma
āraṭṭakān pāñcanadān dhig astu
a ā pāñcālebhyaḥ kuravo naimiṣāś ca
matsyāś caivāpy atha jānanti dharmam
c kaliṅgakāś cāṅgakā māgadhāś ca
śiṣṭān dharmān upajīvanti vṛddhāḥ
a prācīṃ diśaṃ śritā devā jātavedaḥpurogamāḥ
c dakṣiṇāṃ pitaro guptāṃ yamena śubhakarmaṇā
a pratīcīṃ varuṇaḥ pāti pālayann asurān balī
c udīcīṃ bhagavān somo brahmaṇyo brāhmaṇaiḥ saha
a rakṣaḥpiśācān himavān guhyakān gandhamādanaḥ
b tathā rakṣaḥ piśācāś ca himavantaṃ nagottamam
b guhyakāś ca mahārāja parvataṃ gandhamādanam
c dhruvaḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni viṣṇur lokāñ janārdanaḥ
d naiva pāñcanadān pāpān samadān pāti kaś cana
a iṅgitajñāś ca magadhāḥ prekṣitajñāś ca kosalāḥ
c ardhoktāḥ kurupāñcālāḥ śālvāḥ kṛtsnānuśāsanāḥ
e pārvatīyāś ca viṣamā yathaiva girayas tathā
a sarvajñā yavanā rājañ śūrāś caiva viśeṣataḥ
c mlecchāḥ svasaṃjñāniyatā nānukta itaro janaḥ
a pratirabdhās tu bāhlīkā na ca ke cana madrakāḥ
c sa tvam etādṛśaḥ śalya nottaraṃ vaktum arhasi
d pṛthivyāṃ sarvadeśānāṃ madrako malam ucyate
d tathā strīṇāṃ ca sarvāsāṃ madrikā mala ucyate
d sīdhoḥ pānaṃ gurutalpāvamardo
d bhrūṇahatyā paravittāpahāraḥ
a etaj jñātvā joṣam āssva pratīpaṃ mā sma vai kṛthāḥ
c sa tvāṃ pūrvam ahaṃ hatvā haniṣye keśavārjunau
d evaṃ jñātvā joṣam āssva pratīpaṃ
d mā sma krudhyaḥ pāpabhṛtāṃ variṣṭhaḥ
d pūrvaṃ hatvā tvāṃ saputraṃ balaiś ca
d paścād dhaṃsye vāsudevārjunau ca
 śalya uvāca
a āturāṇāṃ parityāgaḥ svadārasutavikrayaḥ
c aṅgeṣu vartate karṇa yeṣām adhipatir bhavān
a rathātirathasaṃkhyāyāṃ yat tvā bhīṣmas tadābravīt
c tān viditvātmano doṣān nirmanyur bhava mā krudhaḥ
a sarvatra brāhmaṇāḥ santi santi sarvatra kṣatriyāḥ
c vaiśyāḥ śūdrās tathā karṇa striyaḥ sādhvyaś ca suvratāḥ
a ramante copahāsena puruṣāḥ puruṣaiḥ saha
c anyonyam avatakṣanto deśe deśe samaithunāḥ
a paravācyeṣu nipuṇaḥ sarvo bhavati sarvadā
c ātmavācyaṃ na jānīte jānann api vimuhyati
d sarvatra santi rājānaḥ svaṃ svaṃ dharmam anuvratāḥ
d durmanuṣyān nigṛhṇanti santi sarvatra dhārmikāḥ
d na karṇa deśasāmānyāt sarvaḥ pāpaṃ niṣevate
d saṃjaya uvāca
d yādṛśāḥ svasvabhāvena devā api na tādṛśāḥ
d tato duryodhano rājā karṇaśalyāv avārayat
d sakhibhāvena rādheyaṃ śalyaṃ svāñjalyakena ca
d tato nivāritaḥ karṇo dhārtarāṣṭreṇa māriṣa
 saṃjaya uvāca
a karṇo 'pi nottaraṃ prāha śalyo 'py abhimukhaḥ parān
c punaḥ prahasya rādheyaḥ punar yāhīty acodayat
d idaṃ tava mayākhyātaṃ kṣiptena na tv asauhṛdāt
d tataḥ prayāntaṃ rādheyaṃ madrarājaḥ smayann iva
d avasphūrjya idaṃ vākyam abravīt kurusaṃnidhau
d camūṃ tavemāṃ vipulāṃ samṛddhām
d asaṃkhyeyām aśvanarākulāṃ ca
d tathā praveṣṭā samare dhanaṃjayaḥ
d kakṣaṃ dahan dīpta ivāśrayāśīḥ
d rathe sthitau vīra raṇe vareṇyau
d siṃhaskandhau lohitapadmanetrau
d draṣṭā bhavān adya vinā prayatnāt
d tathā hi me śakunā vedayanti
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tataḥ parānīkabhidaṃ vyūham apratimaṃ paraiḥ
c samīkṣya karṇaḥ pārthānāṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnābhirakṣitam
a prayayau rathaghoṣeṇa siṃhanādaraveṇa ca
c vāditrāṇāṃ ca ninadaiḥ kampayann iva medinīm
a vepamāna iva krodhād yuddhaśauṇḍaḥ paraṃtapaḥ
c pativyūhya mahātejā yathāvad bharatarṣabha
a vyadhamat pāṇḍavīṃ senām āsurīṃ maghavān iva
c yudhiṣṭhiraṃ cābhibhavann asapavyaṃ cakāra ha
d karṇasya rathaghoṣeṇa maurvīniṣpeṣaṇena ca
d saṃgraheṇa ca raśmīnāṃ samakampanta sṛñjayāḥ
d tāni sarvāṇi sainyāni karṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā viśāṃ pate
d babhūvuḥ saṃprahṛṣṭāni tāvakāni yuyutsayā
d aśrūyanta tato vācas tāvakānāṃ viśāṃ pate
d karṇārjunamahāyuddham etad adya bhaviṣyati
d adya duryodhano rājā hatāmitro bhaviṣyati
d adya karṇaṃ raṇe dṛṣṭvā phalguno vidraviṣyati
d adya tāvad rathaṃ yuddhe karṇasyaivānugāminaḥ
d karṇabāṇamayaṃ yuddhaṃ bhīmaṃ drakṣyāma saṃyuge
d cirakālodyatam idam adyedānīṃ bhaviṣyati
d adya drakṣyāma saṃgrāmaṃ ghoraṃ devāsuropamam
d adyedānīṃ mahad yuddhaṃ bhaviṣyati bhayānakam
d adyedānīṃ jayo nityam ekasyaikasya vā raṇe
d arjunaṃ kila rādheyo vadhiṣyati mahāraṇe
d atha vā kaṃ naraṃ loke na spṛśanti manorathāḥ
d ity uktvā vividhā vācaḥ kuravaḥ kurunandana
d ājaghnuḥ paṭahāṃś caiva tūryāṃś caiva sahasraśaḥ
d bherīśaṅkhāṃś ca vividhān siṃhanādāṃś ca puṣkalān
d murajānāṃ mahāśabdān ānakānāṃ śubhān ravān
d nṛtyamānāś ca bahavas tarjamānāś ca māriṣa
d anyonyam abhyayur yuddhe yuddharaṅgagatā narāḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a kathaṃ saṃjaya rādheyaḥ pratyavyūhata pāṇḍavān
c dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhān vīrān bhīmasenābhirakṣitān
d sarvān eva maheṣvāsān ajayyān amarair api
a ke ca prapakṣau pakṣau vā mama sainyasya saṃjaya
c pravibhajya yathānyāyaṃ kathaṃ vā samavasthitāḥ
a kathaṃ pāṇḍusutāś cāpi pratyavyūhanta māmakān
c kathaṃ caitan mahāyuddhaṃ prāvartata sudāruṇam
a kva ca bībhatsur abhavad yat karṇo 'yād yudhiṣṭhiram
c ko hy arjunasya sāṃnidhye śakto 'bhyetuṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
a sarvabhūtāni yo hy ekaḥ khāṇḍave jitavān purā
c kas tam anyatra rādheyāt pratiyudhyej jijīviṣuḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a śṛṇu vyūhasya racanām arjunaś ca yathā gataḥ
c paridāya nṛpaṃ tebhyaḥ saṃgrāmaś cābhavad yathā
a kṛpaḥ śāradvato rājan māgadhaś ca tarasvinaḥ
c sātvataḥ kṛtavarmā ca dakṣiṇaṃ pakṣam āśritāḥ
a teṣāṃ prapakṣe śakunir ulūkaś ca mahārathaḥ
c sādibhir vimalaprāsais tavānīkam arakṣatām
a gāndhāribhir asaṃbhrāntaiḥ pārvatīyaiś ca durjayaiḥ
c śalabhānām iva vrātaiḥ piśācair iva durdṛśaiḥ
a catustriṃśat sahasrāṇi rathānām anivartinām
c saṃśaptakā yuddhaśauṇḍā vāmaṃ pārśvam apālayan
a samuccitās tava sutaiḥ kṛṣṇārjunajighāṃsavaḥ
c teṣāṃ prapakṣaḥ kāmbojāḥ śakāś ca yavanaiḥ saha
a nideśāt sūtaputrasya sarathāḥ sāśvapattayaḥ
c āhvayanto 'rjunaṃ tasthuḥ keśavaṃ ca mahābalam
a madhyesenāmukhaṃ karṇo vyavātiṣṭhata daṃśitaḥ
c citravarmāṅgadaḥ sragvī pālayan dhvajinīmukham
a rakṣyamāṇaḥ susaṃrabdhaiḥ putraiḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
c vāhinīpramukhaṃ vīraḥ saṃprakarṣann aśobhata
a ayoratnir mahābāhuḥ sūryavaiśvānaradyutiḥ
c mahādvipaskandhagataḥ piṅgalaḥ priyadarśanaḥ
e duḥśāsano vṛtaḥ sainyaiḥ sthito vyūhasya pṛṣṭhataḥ
a tam anvayān mahārāja svayaṃ duryodhano nṛpaḥ
c citrāśvaiś citrasaṃnāhaiḥ sodaryair abhirakṣitaḥ
a rakṣyamāṇo mahāvīryaiḥ sahitair madrakekayaiḥ
c aśobhata mahārāja devair iva śatakratuḥ
a aśvatthāmā kurūṇāṃ ca ye pravīrā mahārathāḥ
c nityamattāś ca mātaṅgāḥ śūrair mlecchair adhiṣṭhitāḥ
d ārohaṇair mahāmātrais tomarāṅkuśapāṇibhiḥ
e anvayus tad rathānīkaṃ kṣaranta iva toyadāḥ
a te dhvajair vaijayantībhir jvaladbhiḥ paramāyudhaiḥ
c sādibhiś cāsthitā rejur drumavanta ivācalāḥ
a teṣāṃ padātināgānāṃ pādarakṣāḥ sahasraśaḥ
c paṭṭiśāsidharāḥ śūrā babhūvur anivartinaḥ
d bhiṇḍipāladharāś caiva śūlahastāḥ sucakriṇaḥ
d teṣāṃ samāgamo ghoro devāsuraraṇopamaḥ
a sādibhiḥ syandanair nāgair adhikaṃ samalaṃkṛtaiḥ
c sa vyūharājo vibabhau devāsuracamūpamaḥ
a bārhaspatyaḥ suvihito nāyakena vipaścitā
c nṛtyatīva mahāvyūhaḥ pareṣām ādadhad bhayam
a tasya pakṣaprapakṣebhyo niṣpatanti yuyutsavaḥ
c pattyaśvarathamātaṅgāḥ prāvṛṣīva balāhakāḥ
a tataḥ senāmukhe karṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c dhanaṃjayam amitraghnam ekavīram uvāca ha
a paśyārjuna mahāvyūhaṃ karṇena vihitaṃ raṇe
c yuktaṃ pakṣaiḥ prapakṣaiś ca senānīkaṃ prakāśate
a tad etad vai samālokya pratyamitraṃ mahad balam
c yathā nābhibhavaty asmāṃs tathā nītir vidhīyatām
a evam ukto 'rjuno rājñā prāñjalir nṛpam abravīt
c yathā bhavān āha tathā tat sarvaṃ na tad anyathā
a yas tv asya vihito ghātas taṃ kariṣyāmi bhārata
c pradhānavadha evāsya vināśas taṃ karomy aham
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a tasmāt tvam eva rādheyaṃ bhīmasenaḥ suyodhanam
c vṛṣasenaṃ ca nakulaḥ sahadevo 'pi saubalam
a duḥśāsanaṃ śatānīko hārdikyaṃ śinipuṃgavaḥ
c dhṛṣṭadyumnas tathā drauṇiṃ svayaṃ yāsyāmy ahaṃ kṛpam
a draupadeyā dhārtarāṣṭrāñ śiṣṭān saha śikhaṇḍinā
c te te ca tāṃs tān ahitān asmākaṃ ghnantu māmakāḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a ity ukto dharmarājena tathety uktvā dhanaṃjayaḥ
c vyādideśa svasainyāni svayaṃ cāgāc camūmukham
d arkavaiśvānaraprakhyaṃ samucchritapatākinam
d agnir vaiśvānaraḥ pūrvo brahmenduḥ saptitāṃ gataḥ
d tasmād yaḥ prathamaṃ jātas taṃ devā brāhmaṇā viduḥ
d tam ādyaṃ prathamaṃ sṛṣṭaṃ brahmaṇā lokakartṛṇā
d brahmeśānendravaruṇān kramaśo yo 'vahat purā
d tam ādyaṃ ratham āsthāya prayātau keśavārjunau
d dhanaṃjayo mahārāja dakṣiṇaṃ pakṣam āsthitaḥ
d bhīmaseno mahābāhur vāmaṃ pakṣam upāśritaḥ
d sātyakir draupadeyāś ca svayaṃ rājā ca pāṇḍavaḥ
d vyūhasya pramukhe tasthuḥ svenānīkena saṃvṛtāḥ
d svabalenārisainyaṃ tat pratyavasthāpya pāṇḍavaḥ
d pratyavyūhat puraskṛtya dhṛṣṭadyumnaśikhaṇḍinau
d tat sādināgakalilaṃ padātirathasaṃkulam
d dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhaṃ vyūham aśobhata mahābalam
a atha taṃ ratham āyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvātyadbhutadarśanam
c uvācādhirathiṃ śalyaḥ punas taṃ yuddhadurmadam
d avasthitam idaṃ vākyaṃ madrarājaḥ smayann iva
a ayaṃ sa ratha āyāti śvetāśvaḥ kṛṣṇasārathiḥ
b durvāraḥ sarvasainyānāṃ vipākaḥ karmaṇām iva
c nighnann amitrān kaunteyo yaṃ yaṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi
a śrūyate tumulaḥ śabdo rathanemisvano mahān
b dhruvam etau mahātmānau vāsudevadhanaṃjayau
c eṣa reṇuḥ samudbhūto divam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati
a cakranemipraṇunnā ca kampate karṇa medinī
b camūṃ tavemāṃ vipulāṃ samṛddhām
b asaṃkhyeyām aśrukulākulāṃ ca
b dhruvaṃ pravekṣaty ajito dhanaṃjayaḥ
b kathaṃ dahan dīpta ivāśrayāśaḥ
b amī hayāś candramarīcivarṇāḥ
b kṛṣṇapratodena pratudyamānāḥ
b vahanti bībhatsum udārasattvāḥ
b sitaprabhāḥ svabhram ivābhrasaṃghāḥ
c pravāty eṣa mahāvāyur abhitas tava vāhinīm
e kravyādā vyāharanty ete mṛgāḥ kurvanti bhairavam
a paśya karṇa mahāghoraṃ bhayadaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
c kabandhaṃ meghasaṃkāśaṃ bhānum āvṛtya saṃsthitam
a paśya yūthair bahuvidhair mṛgāṇāṃ sarvatodiśam
c balibhir dṛptaśārdūlair ādityo 'bhinirīkṣyate
d rarāsa dīptalāṅgūlam ādityam abhitaḥ sthitam
a paśya kaṅkāṃś ca gṛdhrāṃś ca samavetān sahasraśaḥ
b ādityam abhivīkṣante hy aśivāḥ karṇa satvarāḥ
c sthitān abhimukhān ghorān anyonyam abhibhāṣataḥ
a sitāś cāśvāḥ samāyuktās tava karṇa mahārathe
c pradarāḥ prajvalanty ete dhvajaś caiva prakampate
a udīryato hayān paśya mahākāyān mahājavān
c plavamānān darśanīyān ākāśe garuḍān iva
a dhruvam eṣu nimitteṣu bhūmim āvṛtya pārthivāḥ
c svapsyanti nihatāḥ karṇa śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a śaṅkhānāṃ tumulaḥ śabdaḥ śrūyate lomaharṣaṇaḥ
c ānakānāṃ ca rādheya mṛdaṅgānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
a bāṇaśabdān bahuvidhān narāśvarathanisvanān
c jyātalatreṣuśabdāṃś ca śṛṇu karṇa mahātmanām
a hemarūpyapramṛṣṭānāṃ vāsasāṃ śilpinirmitāḥ
c nānāvarṇā rathe bhānti śvasanena prakampitāḥ
a sahemacandratārārkāḥ patākāḥ kiṅkiṇīyutāḥ
c paśya karṇārjunasyaitāḥ saudāminya ivāmbude
a dhvajāḥ kaṇakaṇāyante vātenābhisamīritāḥ
b vibhrājanti raṇe karṇa vimāne devatā yathā
c sapatākā rathāś cāpi pāñcālānāṃ mahātmanām
d paśya kuntīsutaṃ vīraṃ bībhatsum aparājitam
d pradharṣayitum āyāntaṃ kapipravaraketanam
d eṣa dhvajāgre pārthasya prekṣamāṇaḥ samantataḥ
d dṛśyate vānaro bhīmo dviṣatām aghavardhanaḥ
d etac cakraṃ gadā śārṅgaṃ śaṅkhaḥ kṛṣṇasya dhīmataḥ
d atyarthaṃ bhrājate kṛṣṇe kaustubhas tu maṇis tataḥ
d eṣa śārṅgagadāpāṇir vāsudevo 'tivīryavān
d vāhayann eti turagān pāṇḍurān vātaraṃhasaḥ
d etat kūjati gāṇḍīvaṃ vikṛṣṭaṃ savyasācinā
d ete hastavatā muktā ghnanty amitrāñ śitāḥ śarāḥ
d viśālāyatatāmrākṣaiḥ pūrṇacandranibhānanaiḥ
d eṣā bhūḥ kīryate rājñāṃ śirobhir apalāyinām
d ete suparighākārāḥ puṇyagandhānulepanāḥ
d udyatāyudhaśauṇḍānāṃ pātyante sāyudhā bhujāḥ
d nirastanetrajihvāntā vājinaḥ saha sādibhiḥ
d patitāḥ pātyamānāś ca kṣitau kṣīṇāś ca śerate
d ete parvataśṛṅgāṇāṃ tulyarūpā hatā dvipāḥ
d saṃchinnabhinnāḥ pārthena prapanty adrayo yathā
d gandharvanagarākārā rathā hatanareśvarāḥ
d vimānānīva puṇyāni svargiṇāṃ nipatanty amī
d vyākulīkṛtam atyarthaṃ paśya sainyaṃ kirīṭinā
d nānāmṛgasahasrāṇāṃ yūthaṃ kesariṇā yathā
d ghnanty ete pārthivān vīrāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ samabhidrutāḥ
a nāgāśvarathapattyaughāṃs tāvakān samabhighnataḥ
c dhvajāgraṃ dṛśyate tv asya jyāśabdaś cāpi śrūyate
a adya draṣṭāsi taṃ vīraṃ śvetāśvaṃ kṛṣṇasārathim
c nighnantaṃ śātravān saṃkhye yaṃ karṇa paripṛcchasi
a adya tau puruṣavyāghrau lohitākṣau paraṃtapau
c vāsudevārjunau karṇa draṣṭāsy ekarathasthitau
d yatra kṛṣṇo jagannātho yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d yatra gāṇḍīvadhṛk pārtho kathaṃ tvaṃ haṃsi tad balam
a sārathir yasya vārṣṇeyo gāṇḍīvaṃ yasya kārmukam
c taṃ ced dhantāsi rādheya tvaṃ no rājā bhaviṣyasi
d rathanemisvanaḥ saṃkhye meghasyevābhigarjitaḥ
d śrūyate vai yathā vyaktam etau kṛṣṇadhanaṃjayau
a eṣa saṃśaptakāhūtas tān evābhimukho gataḥ
c karoti kadanaṃ caiṣāṃ saṃgrāme dviṣatāṃ balī
e iti bruvāṇaṃ madreśaṃ karṇaḥ prāhātimanyumān
a paśya saṃśaptakaiḥ kruddhaiḥ sarvataḥ samabhidrutaḥ
c eṣa sūrya ivāmbhodaiś channaḥ pārtho na dṛśyate
e etad anto 'rjunaḥ śalya nimagnaḥ śokasāgare
 śalya uvāca
a varuṇaṃ ko 'mbhasā hanyād indhanena ca pāvakam
c ko vānilaṃ nigṛhṇīyāt pibed vā ko mahārṇavam
a īdṛg rūpam ahaṃ manye pārthasya yudhi nigraham
c na hi śakyo 'rjuno jetuṃ sendraiḥ sarvaiḥ surāsuraiḥ
a athaivaṃ paritoṣas te vācoktvā sumanā bhava
c na sa śakyo yudhā jetum anyaṃ kuru manoratham
a bāhubhyām uddhared bhūmiṃ dahet kruddha imāḥ prajāḥ
c pātayet tridivād devān yo 'rjunaṃ samare jayet
a paśya kuntīsutaṃ vīraṃ bhīmam akliṣṭakāriṇam
c prabhāsantaṃ mahābāhuṃ sthitaṃ merum ivācalam
a amarṣī nityasaṃrabdhaś ciraṃ vairam anusmaran
c eṣa bhīmo jayaprepsur yudhi tiṣṭhati vīryavān
a eṣa dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭho dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c tiṣṭhaty asukaraḥ saṃkhye paraiḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ
a etau ca puruṣavyāghrāv aśvināv iva sodarau
c nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca tiṣṭhato yudhi durjayau
a dṛśyanta ete kārṣṇeyāḥ pañca pañcācalā iva
c vyavasthitā yotsyamānāḥ sarve 'rjunasamā yudhi
a ete drupadaputrāś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamāḥ
c hīnāḥ satyajitā vīrās tiṣṭhanti paramaujasaḥ
d asāv indra ivāsahyaḥ sātyakiḥ sātvatāṃ varaḥ
d yuyutsur upayāty asmān kruddhāntakasamaḥ puraḥ
d yatra kṛṣṇārjunau vīrau yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d tatra dharmaś ca satyaṃ ca yato dharmas tato jayaḥ
a iti saṃvadator eva tayoḥ puruṣasiṃhayoḥ
c te sene samasajjetāṃ gaṅgāyamunavad bhṛśam
d tadāsthitam anājñāya pratyamitramahadbalam
d avyūhatārjuno vyūhaṃ putrasya tava durjayam
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a tathā vyūḍheṣv anīkeṣu saṃsakteṣu ca saṃjaya
c saṃśaptakān kathaṃ pārtho gataḥ karṇaś ca pāṇḍavān
a etad vistarato yuddhaṃ prabrūhi kuśalo hy asi
c na hi tṛpyāmi vīrāṇāṃ śṛṇvāno vikramān raṇe
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tat sthāne samavasthāpya pratyamitraṃ mahābalam
c avyūhatārjuno vyūhaṃ putrasya tava durnaye
a tat sādināgakalilaṃ padātirathasaṃkulam
c dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhair vyūḍham aśobhata mahad balam
a pārāvatasavarṇāśvaś candrādityasamadyutiḥ
c pārṣataḥ prababhau dhanvī kālo vigrahavān iva
a pārṣataṃ tv abhi saṃtasthur draupadeyā yuyutsavaḥ
b divyavarmāyudhabhṛtaḥ śārdūlasamavikramāḥ
c sānugā bhīmavapuṣaś candraṃ tārāgaṇā iva
a atha vyūḍheṣv anīkeṣu prekṣya saṃśaptakān raṇe
c kruddho 'rjuno 'bhidudrāva vyākṣipan gāṇḍivaṃ dhanuḥ
a atha saṃśaptakāḥ pārtham abhyadhāvan vadhaiṣiṇaḥ
c vijaye kṛtasaṃkalpā mṛtyuṃ kṛtvā nivartanam
a tad aśvasaṃghabahulaṃ mattanāgarathākulam
b udīryamāṇaṃ saṃrabdhaṃ dhanaṃjayam abhidravat
b tad udyataṃ mahat sainyaṃ sāgaraughasamaṃ jave
b pārthavelāṃ samāsādya viṣṭhitaṃ samadṛśyata
c pattimac chūravīraughair drutam arjunam ādravat
a sa saṃprahāras tumulas teṣām āsīt kirīṭinā
c tasyaiva naḥ śruto yādṛṅ nivātakavacaiḥ saha
a rathān aśvān dhvajān nāgān pattīn rathapatīn api
c iṣūn dhanūṃṣi khaḍgāṃś ca cakrāṇi ca paraśvadhān
a sāyudhān udyatān bāhūn udyatāny āyudhāni ca
c ciccheda dviṣatāṃ pārthaḥ śirāṃsi ca sahasraśaḥ
a tasmin sainye mahāvarte pātālāvartasaṃnibhe
c nimagnaṃ taṃ rathaṃ matvā neduḥ saṃśaptakā mudā
a sa purastād arīn hatvā paścārdhenottareṇa ca
c dakṣiṇena ca bībhatsuḥ kruddho rudraḥ paśūn iva
a atha pāñcālacedīnāṃ sṛñjayānāṃ ca māriṣa
c tvadīyaiḥ saha saṃgrāma āsīt paramadāruṇaḥ
a kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca śakuniś cāpi saubalaḥ
c hṛṣṭasenāḥ susaṃrabdhā rathānīkaiḥ prahāriṇaḥ
a kosalaiḥ kāśimatsyaiś ca kārūṣaiḥ kekayair api
c śūrasenaiḥ śūravīrair yuyudhur yuddhadurmadāḥ
a teṣām antakaraṃ yuddhaṃ dehapāpmapraṇāśanam
c śūdraviṭkṣatravīrāṇāṃ dharmyaṃ svargyaṃ yaśaskaram
a duryodhano 'pi sahito bhrātṛbhir bharatarṣabha
c guptaḥ kurupravīraiś ca madrāṇāṃ ca mahārathaiḥ
a pāṇḍavaiḥ sahapāñcālaiś cedibhiḥ sātyakena ca
c yudhyamānaṃ raṇe karṇaṃ kuruvīro 'bhyapālayat
a karṇo 'pi niśitair bāṇair vinihatya mahācamūm
c pramṛdya ca rathaśreṣṭhān yudhiṣṭhiram apīḍayat
a vipatrāyudhadehāsūn kṛtvā śatrūn sahasraśaḥ
c yuktvā svargayaśobhyāṃ ca svebhyo mudam udāvahat
d evaṃ māriṣa saṃgrāmo naravājigajakṣayaḥ
d kurūṇāṃ sṛñjayānāṃ ca devāsurasamo 'bhavat
d tad vigāhya rathānīkaṃ sūtaputro mahārathaḥ
d nadīṃ pravartayām āsa śoṇitaughataraṅgiṇīm
d śoṇitodāṃ kṣudramatsyāṃ nāganakrāṃ duratyayām
d māṃsamajjākardaminīṃ cakrakūrmāṃ rathoḍupām
d patitair meghasaṃkāśais tatra tatra mahādvipaiḥ
d aśanībhir iva dhvastā mahī rājan virājate
d tāṃ śarormimahāvartāṃ chattrahaṃsasamākulām
d tanutroṣṇīṣasaṃghāṭāṃ hastipāṣāṇasaṃkulām
d apārām anapārāṃ tāṃ śaṅkhadundubhighoṣiṇīm
d raudrāṃ nadīṃ mahārāja rajasā sarvato vṛtām
d atitīkṣṇāṃ nadākīrṇāṃ nadīm antakagāminīm
d samaṃ ca viṣamaṃ caiva samāyāntīṃ mahābhayām
d ā gulphāc cātra sīdantīṃ narāñ śoṇitakardame
d narair abhiparikṣiptā yathā rājan mahādrumāḥ
d tatas te tatra tatraiva prataranto mahānadīm
d viceruḥ sarvato yodhā nauvāraṇamahāsanaiḥ
d śoṇitena samaṃ rājan kṛtam āsīt samantataḥ
d nadīvegair yathā bhūmis tadvad āsīd viśāṃ pate
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a yat tat praviśya pārthānāṃ senāṃ kurvañ janakṣayam
c karṇo rājānam abhyarcchat tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
a ke ca pravīrāḥ pārthānāṃ yudhi karṇam avārayan
c kāṃś ca pramathyādhirathir yudhiṣṭhiram apīḍayat
 saṃjaya uvāca
a dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhān pārthān dṛṣṭvā karṇo vyavasthitān
c samabhyadhāvat tvaritaḥ pāñcālāñ śatrukarśanaḥ
a taṃ tūrṇam abhidhāvantaṃ pāñcālā jitakāśinaḥ
c pratyudyayur mahārāja haṃsā iva mahārṇavam
a tataḥ śaṅkhasahasrāṇāṃ nisvano hṛdayaṃgamaḥ
c prādurāsīd ubhayato bherīśabdaś ca dāruṇaḥ
a nānāvāditranādaś ca dvipāśvarathanisvanaḥ
c siṃhanādaś ca vīrāṇām abhavad dāruṇas tadā
a sādridrumārṇavā bhūmiḥ savātāmbudam ambaram
c sārkendugrahanakṣatrā dyauś ca vyaktaṃ vyaghūrṇata
a ati bhūtāni taṃ śabdaṃ menire 'ti ca vivyathuḥ
c yāni cāplavasattvāni prāyas tāni mṛtāni ca
a atha karṇo bhṛśaṃ kruddhaḥ śīghram astram udīrayan
c jaghāna pāṇḍavīṃ senām āsurīṃ maghavān iva
a sa pāṇḍavarathāṃs tūrṇaṃ praviśya visṛjañ śarān
c prabhadrakāṇāṃ pravarān ahanat saptasaptatim
a tataḥ supuṅkhair niśitai rathaśreṣṭho ratheṣubhiḥ
c avadhīt pañcaviṃśatyā pāñcālān pañcaviṃśatim
a suvarṇapuṅkhair nārācaiḥ parakāyavidāraṇaiḥ
c cedikān avadhīd vīraḥ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a taṃ tathā samare karma kurvāṇam atimānuṣam
c parivavrur mahārāja pāñcālānāṃ rathavrajāḥ
a tataḥ saṃdhāya viśikhān pañca bhārata duḥsahān
c pāñcālān avadhīt pañca karṇo vaikartano vṛṣaḥ
a bhānudevaṃ citrasenaṃ senābinduṃ ca bhārata
c tapanaṃ śūrasenaṃ ca pāñcālān avadhīd raṇe
a pāñcāleṣu ca śūreṣu vadhyamāneṣu sāyakaiḥ
c hāhākāro mahān āsīt pāñcālānāṃ mahāhave
d parivavrur mahārāja pāñcālānāṃ rathā daśa
a teṣāṃ saṃkīryamāṇānāṃ hāhākārakṛtā diśaḥ
c punar eva ca tān karṇo jaghānāśu patatribhiḥ
a cakrarakṣau tu karṇasya putrau māriṣa durjayau
c suṣeṇaḥ satyasenaś ca tyaktvā prāṇān ayudhyatām
a pṛṣṭhagopas tu karṇasya jyeṣṭhaḥ putro mahārathaḥ
c vṛṣasenaḥ svayaṃ karṇaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ paryapālayat
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ sātyakiś ca draupadeyā vṛkodaraḥ
b nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥ
c janamejayaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca pravīrāś ca prabhadrakāḥ
a cedikekayapāñcālā yamau matsyāś ca daṃśitāḥ
c samabhyadhāvan rādheyaṃ jighāṃsantaḥ prahāriṇaḥ
a ta enaṃ vividhaiḥ śastraiḥ śaradhārābhir eva ca
c abhyavarṣan vimṛdnantaḥ prāvṛṣīvāmbudā girim
a pitaraṃ tu parīpsantaḥ karṇaputrāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
c tvadīyāś cāpare rājan vīrā vīrān avārayan
a suṣeṇo bhīmasenasya chittvā bhallena kārmukam
c nārācaiḥ saptabhir viddhvā hṛdi bhīmaṃ nanāda ha
a athānyad dhanur ādāya sudṛḍhaṃ bhīmavikramaḥ
c sajyaṃ vṛkodaraḥ kṛtvā suṣeṇasyācchinad dhanuḥ
a vivyādha cainaṃ navabhiḥ kruddho nṛtyann iveṣubhiḥ
c karṇaṃ ca tūrṇaṃ vivyādha trisaptatyā śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a satyasenaṃ ca daśabhiḥ sāśvasūtadhvajāyudham
c paśyatāṃ suhṛdāṃ madhye karṇaputram apātayat
a kṣurapraṇunnaṃ tat tasya śiraś candranibhānanam
c śubhadarśanam evāsīn nālabhraṣṭam ivāmbujam
a hatvā karṇasutaṃ bhīmas tāvakān punar ārdayat
c kṛpahārdikyayoś chittvā cāpe tāv apy athārdayat
a duḥśāsanaṃ tribhir viddhvā śakuniṃ ṣaḍbhir āyasaiḥ
c ulūkaṃ ca patatriṃ ca cakāra virathāv ubhau
a he suṣeṇa hato 'sīti bruvann ādatta sāyakam
c tam asya karṇaś ciccheda tribhiś cainam atāḍayat
a athānyam api jagrāha suparvāṇaṃ sutejanam
c suṣeṇāyāsṛjad bhīmas tam apy asyācchinad vṛṣaḥ
a punaḥ karṇas trisaptatyā bhīmasenaṃ ratheṣubhiḥ
c putraṃ parīpsan vivyādha krūraṃ krūrair jighāṃsayā
a suṣeṇas tu dhanur gṛhya bhārasādhanam uttamam
c nakulaṃ pañcabhir bāṇair bāhvor urasi cārdayat
a nakulas taṃ tu viṃśatyā viddhvā bhārasahair dṛḍhaiḥ
c nanāda balavan nādaṃ karṇasya bhayam ādadhat
a taṃ suṣeṇo mahārāja viddhvā daśabhir āśugaiḥ
c ciccheda ca dhanuḥ śīghraṃ kṣurapreṇa mahārathaḥ
a athānyad dhanur ādāya nakulaḥ krodhamūrcchitaḥ
c suṣeṇaṃ bahubhir bāṇair vārayām āsa saṃyuge
a sa tu bāṇair diśo rājann ācchādya paravīrahā
c ājaghne sārathiṃ cāsya suṣeṇaṃ ca tatas tribhiḥ
e ciccheda cāsya sudṛḍhaṃ dhanur bhallais tribhis tridhā
a athānyad dhanur ādāya suṣeṇaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
c avidhyan nakulaṃ ṣaṣṭyā sahadevaṃ ca saptabhiḥ
a tad yuddhaṃ sumahad ghoram āsīd devāsuropamam
c nighnatāṃ sāyakais tūrṇam anyonyasya vadhaṃ prati
d sātyakir vṛṣasenaṃ tu viddhvā saptabhir āśugaiḥ
d punar vivyādha saptatyā sārathiṃ ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
d vṛṣasenas tu śaineyaṃ śareṇa nataparvaṇā
d ājaghāna mahārāja śaṅkhadeśe mahāratham
d śaineyo vṛṣasenena patriṇā paripīḍitaḥ
d krodhaṃ cakre mahārāja kruddho vegaṃ ca dāruṇam
d jagrāheṣuvarān vīraḥ śīghraṃ sa daśa pañca ca
a sātyakir vṛṣasenasya hatvā sūtaṃ tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
c dhanuś ciccheda bhallena jaghānāśvāṃś ca saptabhiḥ
e dhvajam ekeṣuṇonmathya tribhis taṃ hṛdy atāḍayat
a athāvasannaḥ svarathe muhūrtāt punar utthitaḥ
b sa raṇe yuyudhānena visūtāśvarathadhvajaḥ
c atho jighāṃsuḥ śaineyaṃ khaḍgacarmabhṛd abhyayāt
a tasya cāplavataḥ śīghraṃ vṛṣasenasya sātyakiḥ
c varāhakarṇair daśabhir avidhyad asicarmaṇī
a duḥśāsanas tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā virathaṃ vyāyudhaṃ kṛtam
c āropya svarathe tūrṇam apovāha rathāntaram
a athānyaṃ ratham āsthāya vṛṣaseno mahārathaḥ
b draupadeyāṃs trisaptatyā yuyudhānaṃ ca pañcabhiḥ
b bhīmasenaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭyā sahadevaṃ ca pañcabhiḥ
b nakulaṃ triṃśatā bāṇaiḥ śatānīkaṃ ca saptabhiḥ
b śikhaṇḍinaṃ ca daśabhir dharmarājaṃ śatena ca
b etāṃś cānyāṃś ca rājendra pravīrāñ jayagṛddhinaḥ
b abhyardayan maheṣvāsaḥ karṇaputro viśāṃ pate
c karṇasya yudhi durdharṣaḥ punaḥ pṛṣṭham apālayat
a duḥśāsanaṃ tu śaineyo navair navabhir āśugaiḥ
c visūtāśvarathaṃ kṛtvā lalāṭe tribhir ārpayat
a sa tv anyaṃ ratham āsthāya vidhivat kalpitaṃ punaḥ
c yuyudhe pāṇḍubhiḥ sārdhaṃ karṇasyāpyāyayan balam
a dhṛṣṭadyumnas tataḥ karṇam avidhyad daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c draupadeyās trisaptatyā yuyudhānas tu saptabhiḥ
a bhīmasenaś catuḥṣaṣṭyā sahadevaś ca pañcabhiḥ
c nakulas triṃśatā bāṇaiḥ śatānīkaś ca saptabhiḥ
e śikhaṇḍī daśabhir vīro dharmarājaḥ śatena tu
a ete cānye ca rājendra pravīrā jayagṛddhinaḥ
c abhyardayan maheṣvāsaṃ sūtaputraṃ mahāmṛdhe
a tān sūtaputro viśikhair daśabhir daśabhiḥ śitaiḥ
c rathe cāru caran vīraḥ pratyavidhyad ariṃdamaḥ
d sātyakiṃ bhīmasenaṃ ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ śikhaṇḍinam
d draupadeyāṃś ca saṃrabdhān yatamānān mahārathān
d paśyatāṃ sarvasainyānām athaitān sūtanandanaḥ
d virathān rathinaḥ śreṣṭhān nimeṣārdhāc cakāra ha
d amoghatvāc ca bāṇānāṃ bhūtasaṃghā visiṣmiyuḥ
a tatrāstravīryaṃ karṇasya lāghavaṃ ca mahātmanaḥ
c apaśyāma mahārāja tad adbhutam ivābhavat
a na hy ādadānaṃ dadṛśuḥ saṃdadhānaṃ ca sāyakān
c vimuñcantaṃ ca saṃrambhād dadṛśus te mahāratham
d pratīcyāṃ diśi taṃ dṛṣṭvā prācyāṃ paśyāma lāghavāt
d na tu paśyāma rājendra kva nu karṇo vyatiṣṭhata
d iṣūn eva sma paśyāmo vikirantaṃ samantataḥ
d chādayanto diśo rājañ śalabhānām iva vrajān
d tasya tair iṣubhis tīkṣṇaiḥ saṃpatadbhiḥ sahasraśaḥ
d marīcibhir ivoṣṇāṃśoḥ śitaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
d vyāptāḥ sarvā diśo rājan yodhāś ca dadṛśus tadā
d śaraiḥ saṃvṛtam ākāśaṃ tatrābhram iva cābhavat
a dyaur viyad bhūr diśaś cāśu praṇunnā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c aruṇābhrāvṛtākāraṃ tasmin deśe babhau viyat
d tataḥ punar ameyātmā karṇo rājan mahārathaḥ
d nyahanat samare yodhān yaudhavratam anuṣṭhitaḥ
a nṛtyann iva hi rādheyaś cāpahastaḥ pratāpavān
c yair viddhaḥ pratyavidhyat tān ekaikaṃ triguṇaiḥ śaraiḥ
a daśabhir daśabhiś cainān punar viddhvā nanāda ha
c sāśvasūtadhvajacchatrās tatas te vivaraṃ daduḥ
d te hanyamānāḥ karṇena palāyante diśo daśa
d nādayanto diśaḥ sarvāḥ karṇatrastā vicetasaḥ
a tān pramṛdnan maheṣvāsān rādheyaḥ śaravṛṣṭibhiḥ
c rājānīkam asaṃbādhaṃ prāviśac chatrukarśanaḥ
a sa rathāṃs triśatān hatvā cedīnām anivartinām
c rādheyo niśitair bāṇais tato 'bhyārcchad yudhiṣṭhiram
d tatas te virathāḥ śūrā rathān anyān samāsthitāḥ
d parivavrur mahārāja dharmaputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
a tatas te pāṇḍavā rājañ śikhaṇḍī ca sasātyakiḥ
c rādheyāt parirakṣanto rājānaṃ paryavārayan
d muñcanto vividhān bāṇān svarṇapuṅkhāñ śilāśitān
a tathaiva tāvakāḥ sarve karṇaṃ durvāraṇaṃ raṇe
c yattāḥ senāmaheṣvāsāḥ paryarakṣanta sarvaśaḥ
a nānāvāditraghoṣāś ca prādurāsan viśāṃ pate
c siṃhanādaś ca saṃjajñe śūrāṇām anivartinām

c yudhiṣṭhiramukhāḥ pārthāḥ sūtaputramukhā vayam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a vidārya karṇas tāṃ senāṃ dharmarājam upādravat
c rathahastyaśvapattīnāṃ sahasraiḥ parivāritaḥ

c chittvā bāṇaśatair ugrais tān avidhyad asaṃbhramaḥ
a nicakarta śirāṃsy eṣāṃ bāhūn ūrūṃś ca sarvaśaḥ
b prahartukāmān aparān saṃdhiteṣūṃs tathāparān

a draviḍāndhraniṣādās tu punaḥ sātyakicoditāḥ
c abhyardayañ jighāṃsantaḥ pattayaḥ karṇam āhave

c petuḥ pṛthivyāṃ yugapac chinnaṃ śālavanaṃ yathā

c hatānīyur mahīṃ dehair yaśasāpūrayan diśaḥ

c vatsadantair maheṣvāsaḥ prahasann iva bhārata
d so 'vajñāya tu nirviddhaḥ sūtaputreṇa māriṣa
d prajajvāla tataḥ krodhād dhaviṣeva hutāśanaḥ

d siṃhanādaś ca saṃjajñe kṣveḍāḥ kilakilās tathā
d pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārāja dṛṣṭvā rājñaḥ parākramam
d pratilabhya tu rādheyaḥ saṃjñāṃ nāticirād iva
d dadhre rājavināśāya manaḥ krūraparākramaḥ
d sa hemavikṛtaṃ cāpaṃ visphārya vijayaṃ mahat
d avākirad ameyātmā pāṇḍavaṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a tataḥ kṣurābhyāṃ pāñcālyau cakrarakṣau mahātmanaḥ
c jaghāna samare śūraḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
a tāv ubhau dharmarājasya pravīrau paripārśvataḥ
c rathābhyāśe cakāśete candrasyeva punarvasū
a yudhiṣṭhiraḥ punaḥ karṇam avidhyat triṃśatā śaraiḥ
c suṣeṇaṃ satyasenaṃ ca tribhis tribhir atāḍayat
a śalyaṃ navatyā vivyādha trisaptatyā ca sūtajam
c tāṃś cāsya goptṝn vivyādha tribhis tribhir ajihmagaiḥ
a tataḥ prahasyādhirathir vidhunvānaḥ sa kārmukam
c bhittvā bhallena rājānaṃ viddhvā ṣaṣṭyānadan mudā
a tataḥ pravīrāḥ pāṇḍūnām abhyadhāvan yudhiṣṭhiram
c sūtaputrāt parīpsantaḥ karṇam abhyardayañ śaraiḥ
a sātyakiś cekitānaś ca yuyutsuḥ pāṇḍya eva ca
b colaṃ ca cerakaṃ caiva siṃhaladvīpavāsinam
b karṇo vivyādha saṃkruddho dākṣiṇātyān samantataḥ
c dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca draupadeyāḥ prabhadrakāḥ
a yamau ca bhīmasenaś ca śiśupālasya cātmajaḥ
c kārūṣā matsyaśeṣāś ca kekayāḥ kāśikosalāḥ
e ete ca tvaritā vīrā vasuṣeṇam avārayan
a janamejayaś ca pāñcālyaḥ karṇaṃ vivyādha sāyakaiḥ
c varāhakarṇair nārācair nālīkair niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
e vatsadantair vipāṭhaiś ca kṣurapraiś caṭakāmukhaiḥ
a nānāpraharaṇaiś cograi rathahastyaśvasādinaḥ

b chādyamānaiḥ śitair bāṇaiḥ svasvanāmāṅkitais tadā
b na cacāla raṇe karṇo mahendro dānavair iva
c udairayad brāhmam astraṃ śaraiḥ saṃpūrayan diśaḥ
d saṃjayaḥ
d nijaghāna maheṣvāsān pāñcālān ekaviṃśatim
d tataḥ punar ameyātmā cedīnāṃ pravarān daśa
d nyahanad bharataśreṣṭha karṇo vaikartanas tadā
d tasya bāṇasahasrāṇi saṃprapannāni māriṣa
d dṛśyante dikṣu sarvāsu śalabhānām iva vrajāḥ
d karṇanāmāṅkitā bāṇāḥ svarṇapuṅkhāḥ sutejanāḥ
d narāśvakāyān nirbhidya petur urvyāṃ samantataḥ
d karṇenaikena samare cedīnāṃ pravarā rathāḥ
d sṛñjayānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ śataśo nihatā raṇe
d karṇasya śarasaṃchannaṃ babhūva vipulaṃ tamaḥ
d nājñāyata tataḥ kiṃ cit pareṣām ātmano 'pi vā

d vicacāra mahābāhur nirdahan kṣatriyān bahūn

c nirdahan pāṇḍavavanaṃ cāru paryacarad raṇe
d tatas teṣāṃ mahārāja pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥ
d sṛñjayānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
d astraiḥ karṇaṃ maheṣvāṃsa samantāt paryavāraya
a sa saṃvārya mahāstrāṇi maheṣvāso mahātmanām
c prahasya puruṣendrasya śaraiś ciccheda kārmukam
a tataḥ saṃdhāya navatiṃ nimeṣān nataparvaṇām
c bibheda kavacaṃ rājño raṇe karṇaḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a tad varma hemavikṛtaṃ rarāja nipatat tadā
c savidyudabhraṃ savituḥ śiṣṭaṃ vātahataṃ yathā
a tad aṅgaṃ puruṣendrasya bhraṣṭavarma vyarocata
c ratnair alaṃkṛtaṃ divyair vyabhraṃ niśi yathā nabhaḥ
a sa vivarmā śaraiḥ pārtho rudhireṇa samukṣitaḥ
b babhāse puruṣaśreṣṭha udyann iva divākaraḥ
b sa śarārpitasarvāṅgaś chinnavarmātha saṃyuge
b kṣatradharmaṃ samāsthāya siṃhanādam athākarot
b naditvā ca ciraṃ kālaṃ pāṇḍavo rabhaso raṇe
c kruddhaḥ sarvāyasīṃ śaktiṃ cikṣepādhirathiṃ prati
a tāṃ jvalantīm ivākāśe śaraiś ciccheda saptabhiḥ
c sā chinnā bhūmim apatan maheṣvāsasya sāyakaiḥ
a tato bāhvor lalāṭe ca hṛdi caiva yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c caturbhis tomaraiḥ karṇaṃ tāḍayitvā mudānadat
a udbhinnarudhiraḥ karṇaḥ kruddhaḥ sarpa iva śvasan
b jaghāna sūtaṃ pārthasya pārṣṇiṃ ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c dhvajaṃ ciccheda bhallena tribhir vivyādha pāṇḍavam
d hatvā sūtaṃ ca pārthasya pṛṣṭhagopaṃ ca sāyakaiḥ
e iṣudhī cāsya ciccheda rathaṃ ca tilaśo 'cchinat
f kālavālās tu ye pārthaṃ dantavarṇāvahan hayāḥ
f tair yuktaṃ ratham āsthāya prāyād rājā parāṅmukhaḥ
f etasminn antare śūrāḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥ
f vavarṣuḥ śaravarṣāṇi rādheyaṃ prati bhārata
f sātyakiḥ pañcaviṃśatyā śikhaṇḍī navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
f avarṣatāṃ mahārāja rādheyaṃ śatrukarśanam
f śaineyaṃ tu tataḥ kruddhaḥ karṇaḥ pañcabhir āyasaiḥ
f vivyādha samare rājaṃs tribhiś cānyaiḥ śilīmukhaiḥ
f dakṣiṇaṃ tu bhujaṃ tasya tribhiḥ karṇo 'py avidhyata
f savyaṃ ṣoḍaśabhir bāṇair yantāraṃ cāsya saptabhiḥ
f athāsya caturo vāhāṃś caturbhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
f sūtaputro 'nayat kṣipraṃ yamasya sadanaṃ prati

f sāratheḥ saśirastrāṇaṃ śiraḥ kāyād apāharat
f hatāśvasūte tu rathe sthitaḥ sa śinipuṃgavaḥ
f śaktiṃ cikṣepa karṇāya vaiḍūryamaṇibhūṣitām
f tām āpatantīṃ sahasā dvidhā ciccheda bhārata
f karṇo vai dhanvināṃ śreṣṭhas tāṃś ca sarvān avārayat
f tatas tān niśitair bāṇaiḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathān
f nyavārayad ameyātmā śikṣayā ca balena ca
f ardayitvā śarais tāṃs tu siṃhaḥ kṣudramṛgān iva
f pīḍayan dharmarājānaṃ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
f abhyadravata rādheyo dharmaputraṃ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a evaṃ pārtho vyapāyāt sa nihataprārṣṭisārathiḥ
c aśaknuvan pramukhataḥ sthātuṃ karṇasya durmanāḥ
a tam abhidrutya rādheyaḥ skandhaṃ saṃspṛśya pāṇinā
b vajracchatrāṅkuśair matsyair dhvajakūrmāmbujādibhiḥ
b lakṣaṇair upapannena pāṇinā pāṇḍunandanam
b pavitrīkartum ātmānaṃ skandhopari samaspṛśat
b grahītum icchan sa balāt kuntīvākyaṃ ca so 'smarat
b taṃ śalyaḥ prāha mā karṇa gṛhṇīthāḥ pārthivottamam
b gṛhītamātro hatvā tvāṃ mā kariṣyati bhasmasāt
c abravīt prahasan rājan kutsayann iva pāṇḍavam
a kathaṃ nāma kule jātaḥ kṣatradharme vyavasthitaḥ
c prajahyāt samare śatrūn prāṇān rakṣan mahāhave
a na bhavān kṣatradharmeṣu kuśalo 'sīti me matiḥ
c brāhme bale bhavān yuktaḥ svādhyāye yajñakarmaṇi
a mā sma yudhyasva kaunteya mā ca vīrān samāsadaḥ
c mā cainān apriyaṃ brūhi mā ca vraja mahāraṇam
d vaktavyā māriṣānye tu na vaktavyās tu mādṛśāḥ
d mādṛśān hi bruvan yuddhe etad anyac ca lapsyase
d svagṛhaṃ gaccha kaunteya yatra vā keśavārjunau

d saṃjayaḥ
d varapradānaṃ kuntyās tu karṇaḥ smṛtvā mahārathaḥ
d vadhaprāptaṃ tu kaunteyaṃ nāvadhīt puruṣottamam

a viśālāyatatāmrākṣaiḥ padmendusadṛśānanaiḥ

c rūpeṇa cātiriktena śabdena ca visarpatā
e viṣādaḥ sumahān āsīt prāyaḥ sainyasya bhārata
a tat tu viprahataṃ sainyaṃ bhīmasenamukhais tava
c bhūyaḥ samādravan vīrāḥ sātyakipramukhā rathāḥ
a teṣām āpatatāṃ vegam aviṣahya mahātmanām
c putrāṇāṃ te mahat sainyam āsīd rājan parāṅmukham

c vidhvastacarmakavacaṃ praviddhāyudhakārmukam
a vyadravat tāvakaṃ sainyaṃ loḍyamānaṃ samantataḥ
c siṃhārditaṃ mahāraṇye yathā gajakulaṃ tathā

a tān abhidravato dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavāṃs tāvakaṃ balam
b duryodhano mahārāja vārayām āsa sarvaśaḥ
b yodhāṃś ca svabalaṃ caiva samantād bharatarṣabha
c krośatas tava putrasya na sma rājan nyavartata
a tataḥ pakṣāt prapakṣāc ca prapakṣaiś cāpi dakṣiṇāt
c udastaśastrāḥ kuravo bhīmam abhyadravan raṇe

b madrarājam uvācedaṃ yāhi bhīmarathaṃ prati

c haṃsavarṇān hayāgryāṃs tān praiṣīd yatra vṛkodaram
a te preṣitā mahārāja śalyenāhavaśobhinā
c bhīmasenarathaṃ prāpya samasajjanta vājinaḥ

c matiṃ dadhre vināśāya karṇasya bharatarṣabha
a so 'bravīt sātyakiṃ vīraṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca pārṣatam
c enaṃ rakṣata rājānaṃ dharmātmānaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram

a agrato me kṛto rājā chinnasarvaparicchadaḥ
c duryodhanasya prītyarthaṃ rādheyena durātmanā
a antam adya kariṣyāmi tasya duḥkhasya pārṣata

c abhyavartata vai karṇaṃ krodhadīpto vṛkodaraḥ
a tathāgataṃ tu saṃprekṣya bhīmaṃ yuddhābhinandinam
c abravīd vacanaṃ śalyaṃ rādheyaḥ prahasann iva
a yad uktaṃ vacanaṃ me 'dya tvayā madrajaneśvara
c bhīmasenaṃ prati vibho tat satyaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ
a eṣa śūraś ca vīraś ca krodhanaś ca vṛkodaraḥ
c nirapekṣaḥ śarīre ca prāṇataś ca balādhikaḥ
a ajñātavāsaṃ vasatā virāṭanagare tadā
c draupadyāḥ priyakāmena kevalaṃ bāhusaṃśrayāt

c kiṃkarodyatadaṇḍena mṛtyunāpi vrajed raṇam
a cirakālābhilaṣito mamāyaṃ tu manorathaḥ
c arjunaṃ samare hanyāṃ māṃ vā hanyād dhanaṃjayaḥ
e sa me kadā cid adyaiva bhaved bhīmasamāgamāt
f saṃśayaḥ sumahāñ śalya prāpya bhīmam ariṃdamam

c abhiyāsyati māṃ pārthas tan me sādhu bhaviṣyati

a abhiyāsi mahābāho bhīmasenaṃ mahābalam

d nirapekṣaś ca yudhyasva śaktiṃ svāṃ saṃpradarśayan

c hantāham arjunaṃ saṃkhye māṃ vā hantā dhanaṃjayaḥ
d evam uktvā tato rājan rādheyo rathināṃ varaḥ

e   nātikṛcchrād dhasann iva

d vacanaṃ hetusaṃpannaṃ śrutvā caitat tathā kuru

d bhīma uvāca

a suduṣkaram idaṃ karma kṛtaṃ bhīmena saṃjaya
c yena karṇo mahābāhū rathopasthe nipātitaḥ

a vibhrāntaṃ prekṣya rādheyaṃ sūtaputraṃ mahāhave
