c prājñāsiṣma vayaṃ tābhyāṃ śarair muktaiḥ sahasraśaḥ
a madhyāhne tapato rājan bhāskarasya mahāprabhāḥ
c hṛtāḥ sarvāḥ śaraughais taiḥ karṇamādhavayos tadā
a saubalaṃ kṛtavarmāṇaṃ drauṇim ādhirathiṃ kṛpam
c saṃsaktān pāṇḍavair dṛṣṭvā nivṛttāḥ kuravaḥ punaḥ
a teṣām āpatatāṃ śabdas tīvra āsīd viśāṃ pate
c uddhūtānāṃ yathā vṛṣṭyā sāgarāṇāṃ bhayāvahaḥ
a te sene bhṛśasaṃvigne dṛṣṭvānyonyaṃ mahāraṇe
c harṣeṇa mahatā yukte parigṛhya parasparam
a tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ madhyaṃ prāpte divākare
c yādṛśaṃ na kadā cid dhi dṛṣṭapūrvaṃ na ca śrutam
a balaughas tu samāsādya balaughaṃ sahasā raṇe
c upāsarpata vegena jalaugha iva sāgaram
a āsīn ninādaḥ sumahān balaughānāṃ parasparam
c garjatāṃ sāgaraughāṇāṃ yathā syān nisvano mahān
a te tu sene samāsādya vegavatyau parasparam
b upāsarpata vegena anyonyena narādhipa
c ekībhāvam anuprāpte nadyāv iva samāgame
a tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ ghorarūpaṃ viśāṃ pate
b harṣeṇa mahatā yuktaiḥ kurupāṇḍavasainikaiḥ
c kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca lipsatāṃ sumahad yaśaḥ
a kurūṇāṃ garjatāṃ tatra avicchedakṛtā giraḥ
c śrūyante vividhā rājan nāmāny uddiśya bhārata
a yasya yad dhi raṇe nyaṅgaṃ pitṛto mātṛto 'pi vā
c karmataḥ śīlato vāpi sa tac chrāvayate yudhi
a tān dṛṣṭvā samare śūrāṃs tarjayānān parasparam
c abhavan me matī rājan naiṣām astīti jīvitam
a teṣāṃ dṛṣṭvā tu kruddhānāṃ vapūṃṣy amitatejasām
c abhavan me bhayaṃ tīvraṃ katham etad bhaviṣyati
a tatas te pāṇḍavā rājan kauravāś ca mahārathāḥ
c tatakṣuḥ sāyakais tīkṣṇair nighnanto hi parasparam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a kṣatriyās te mahārāja parasparavadhaiṣiṇaḥ
c anyonyaṃ samare jaghnuḥ kṛtavairāḥ parasparam
a rathaughāś ca hayaughāś ca naraughāś ca samantataḥ
c gajaughāś ca mahārāja saṃsaktāḥ sma parasparam
a gadānāṃ parighāṇāṃ ca kaṇapānāṃ ca sarpatām
c prāsānāṃ bhiṇḍipālānāṃ bhuśuṇḍīnāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
a saṃpātaṃ cānvapaśyāma saṃgrāme bhṛśadāruṇe
c śalabhā iva saṃpetuḥ samantāc charavṛṣṭayaḥ
a nāgā nāgān samāsādya vyadhamanta parasparam
c hayā hayāṃś ca samare rathino rathinas tathā
e pattayaḥ pattisaṃghaiś ca hayasaṃghair hayās tathā
a pattayo rathamātaṅgān rathā hastyaśvam eva ca
b hastino 'śvān rathāṃś caiva
c nāgāś ca samare tryaṅgaṃ mamṛduḥ śīghragā nṛpa
d   hayās tryaṅgaṃ ca māriṣa
d narāś ca mamṛdus tryaṅgaṃ rathās tryaṅgaṃ ca māriṣa
d śaratomaranārācair gadāśaktiparaśvadhaiḥ
a patatāṃ tatra śūrāṇāṃ krośatāṃ ca parasparam
c ghoram āyodhanaṃ jajñe paśūnāṃ vaiśasaṃ yathā
a rudhireṇa samāstīrṇā bhāti bhārata medinī
c śakragopagaṇākīrṇā prāvṛṣīva yathā dharā
a yathā vā vāsasī śukle mahārajanarañjite
c bibhṛyād yuvatiḥ śyāmā tadvad āsīd vasuṃdharā
d baddhacūḍāmaṇivaraiḥ śirobhiś cārukuṇḍalaiḥ
d ujjhitair vṛṣabhākṣāṇāṃ bhrājate sma vasuṃdharā
e māṃsaśoṇitacitreva śātakaumbhamayīva ca
f bhūr babhau bharataśreṣṭha śāntārcirbhir ivāgnibhiḥ
a chinnānāṃ cottamāṅgānāṃ bāhūnāṃ corubhiḥ saha
c kuṇḍalānāṃ praviddhānāṃ bhūṣaṇānāṃ ca bhārata
a niṣkāṇām adhisūtrāṇāṃ śarīrāṇāṃ ca dhanvinām
c varmaṇāṃ sapatākānāṃ saṃghās tatrāpatan bhuvi
d agamyakalpā pṛthivī sarvato bhṛśadurgamā
a gajān gajāḥ samāsādya viṣāṇāgrair adārayan
c viṣāṇābhihatās te ca bhrājante dviradā yathā
a rudhireṇāvasiktāṅgā gairikaprasravā iva
c yathā bhrājanti syandantaḥ parvatā dhātumaṇḍitāḥ
d tathā rejū raṇe nāgā rudhireṇa samāplutāḥ
a tomarān gajibhir muktān pratīpān āsthitān bahūn
c hastair vicerus te nāgā babhañjuś cāpare tathā
a nārācaiś chinnavarmāṇo bhrājante sma gajottamāḥ
c himāgame mahārāja vyabhrā iva mahīdharāḥ
a śaraiḥ kanakapuṅkhais tu citā rejur gajottamāḥ
c ulkābhiḥ saṃpradīptāgrāḥ parvatā iva māriṣa
a ke cid abhyāhatā nāgā nāgair naganibhā bhuvi
c nipetuḥ samare tasmin pakṣavanta ivādrayaḥ
a apare prādravan nāgāḥ śalyārtā vraṇapīḍitāḥ
c pratimānaiś ca kumbhaiś ca petur urvyāṃ mahāhave
a niṣeduḥ siṃhavac cānye nadanto bhairavān ravān
c mamluś ca bahavo rājaṃś cukūjuś cāpare tathā
a hayāś ca nihatā bāṇaiḥ svarṇabhāṇḍaparicchadāḥ
c niṣeduś caiva mamluś ca babhramuś ca diśo daśa
a apare kṛṣyamāṇāś ca viveṣṭanto mahītale
c bhāvān bahuvidhāṃś cakrus tāḍitāḥ śaratomaraiḥ
a narās tu nihatā bhūmau kūjantas tatra māriṣa
c dṛṣṭvā ca bāndhavān anye pitṝn anye pitāmahān
a dhāvamānān parāṃś caiva dṛṣṭvānye tatra bhārata
c gotranāmāni khyātāni śaśaṃsur itaretaram
a teṣāṃ chinnā mahārāja bhujāḥ kanakabhūṣaṇāḥ
c udveṣṭante viveṣṭante patante cotpatanti ca
a nipatanti tathā bhūmau sphuranti ca sahasraśaḥ
c vegāṃś cānye raṇe cakruḥ sphuranta iva pannagāḥ
a te bhujā bhogibhogābhāś candanāktā viśāṃ pate
c lohitārdrā bhṛśaṃ rejus tapanīyadhvajā iva
a vartamāne tathā ghore saṃkule sarvatodiśam
c avijñātāḥ sma yudhyante vinighnantaḥ parasparam
a bhaumena rajasā kīrṇe śastrasaṃpātasaṃkule
c naiva sve na pare rājan vyajñāyanta tamovṛte
a tathā tad abhavad yuddhaṃ ghorarūpaṃ bhayānakam
c śoṇitodā mahānadyaḥ prasasrus tatra cāsakṛt
a śīrṣapāṣāṇasaṃchannāḥ keśaśaivalaśādvalāḥ
c asthisaṃghātasaṃkīrṇā dhanuḥśaravarottamāḥ
a māṃsakardamapaṅkāś ca śoṇitaughāḥ sudāruṇāḥ
c nadīḥ pravartayām āsur yamarāṣṭravivardhanīḥ
d bhīruvitrāsakāriṇyaḥ śūrāṇāṃ harṣavardhanāḥ
a tā nadyo ghorarūpāś ca nayantyo yamasādanam
c avagāḍhā majjayantyaḥ kṣatrasyājanayan bhayam
a kravyādānāṃ naravyāghra nardatāṃ tatra tatra ha
c ghoram āyodhanaṃ jajñe pretarājapuropamam
a utthitāny agaṇeyāni kabandhāni samantataḥ
c nṛtyanti vai bhūtagaṇāḥ saṃtṛptā māṃsaśoṇitaiḥ
a pītvā ca śoṇitaṃ tatra vasāṃ pītvā ca bhārata
c medomajjāvasātṛptās tṛptā māṃsasya caiva hi
e dhāvamānāś ca dṛśyante kākagṛdhrabalās tathā
a śūrās tu samare rājan bhayaṃ tyaktvā sudustyajam
c yodhavratasamākhyātāś cakruḥ karmāṇy abhītavat
a śaraśaktisamākīrṇe kravyādagaṇasaṃkule
c vyacaranta gaṇaiḥ śūrāḥ khyāpayantaḥ svapauruṣam
a anyonyaṃ śrāvayanti sma nāmagotrāṇi bhārata
c pitṛnāmāni ca raṇe gotranāmāni cābhitaḥ
a śrāvayanto hi bahavas tatra yodhā viśāṃ pate
c anyonyam avamṛdnantaḥ śaktitomarapaṭṭiśaiḥ
a vartamāne tadā yuddhe ghorarūpe sudāruṇe
c vyaṣīdat kauravī senā bhinnā naur iva sāgare
 saṃjaya uvāca
a vartamāne tadā yuddhe kṣatriyāṇāṃ nimajjane
c gāṇḍīvasya mahān ghoṣaḥ śuśruve yudhi māriṣa
a saṃśaptakānāṃ kadanam akarod yatra pāṇḍavaḥ
c kosalānāṃ tathā rājan nārāyaṇabalasya ca
a saṃśaptakās tu samare śaravṛṣṭiṃ samantataḥ
c apātayan pārthamūrdhni jayagṛddhāḥ pramanyavaḥ
a tāṃ vṛṣṭiṃ sahasā rājaṃs tarasā dhārayan prabhuḥ
c vyagāhata raṇe pārtho vinighnan rathināṃ varaḥ
a nigṛhya tu rathānīkaṃ kaṅkapatraiḥ śilāśitaiḥ
c āsasāda raṇe pārthaḥ suśarmāṇaṃ mahāratham
a sa tasya śaravarṣāṇi vavarṣa rathināṃ varaḥ
c tathā saṃśaptakāś caiva pārthasya samare sthitāḥ
a suśarmā tu tataḥ pārthaṃ viddhvā navabhir āśugaiḥ
c janārdanaṃ tribhir bāṇair abhyahan dakṣiṇe bhuje
e tato 'pareṇa bhallena ketuṃ vivyādha māriṣa
f vivyādha samare rājan suśarmā krodhamūrcchitaḥ
a sa vānaravaro rājan viśvakarmakṛto mahān
c nanāda sumahan nādaṃ bhīṣayan vai nanarda ca
a kapes tu ninadaṃ śrutvā saṃtrastā tava vāhinī
c bhayaṃ vipulam ādāya niśceṣṭā samapadyata
a tataḥ sā śuśubhe senā niśceṣṭāvasthitā nṛpa
c nānāpuṣpasamākīrṇaṃ yathā caitrarathaṃ vanam
a pratilabhya tataḥ saṃjñāṃ yodhās te kurusattama
c arjunaṃ siṣicur bāṇaiḥ parvataṃ jaladā iva
e parivavrus tadā sarve pāṇḍavasya mahāratham
f nigṛhya taṃ pracukruśur vadhyamānāḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
f nigrahītum upākrāman krodhāviṣṭāḥ samantataḥ
f nigṛhya taṃ rathaṃ tasya yodhās te tu sahasraśaḥ
f rathabandhaṃ pracakrur hi pāṇḍavasyāmitaujasaḥ
f ratham āruruhuḥ ke cit pārthakṛṣṇau jighṛkṣavaḥ
f saṃśaptakānāṃ yodhās te siṃhanādāṃś ca nedire
f sa rathas tair gṛhītas tu pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ
f syandamāno nāśakat tu tad adbhutam ivābhavat
f tataḥ pārtho mahābāhuḥ saṃvṛtas tair mahārathaiḥ
f nigṛhītaṃ rathaṃ dṛṣṭvā tāṃś cābhidravato bahūn
f rathavadhaṃ pracukṣus te sarve tatra mahāhave
a te hayān rathacakre ca ratheṣāś cāpi bhārata
c nigṛhya balavat tūrṇaṃ siṃhanādam athānadan
a apare jagṛhuś caiva keśavasya mahābhujau
c pārtham anye mahārāja rathasthaṃ jagṛhur mudā
a keśavas tu tadā bāhū vidhunvan raṇamūrdhani
c pātayām āsa tān sarvān duṣṭahastīva hastinaḥ
a tataḥ kruddho raṇe pārthaḥ saṃvṛtas tair mahārathaiḥ
c nigṛhītaṃ rathaṃ dṛṣṭvā keśavaṃ cāpy abhidrutam
e rathārūḍhāṃś ca subahūn padātīṃś cāpy apātayat
a āsannāṃś ca tato yodhāñ śarair āsannayodhibhiḥ
b tāṃs tāpayitvā samare pārthaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ
c cyāvayām āsa samare keśavaṃ cedam abravīt
a paśya kṛṣṇa mahābāho saṃśaptakagaṇān mayā
c kurvāṇān dāruṇaṃ karma vadhyamānān sahasraśaḥ
a rathabandham imaṃ ghoraṃ pṛthivyāṃ nāsti kaś cana
c yaḥ saheta pumāṃl loke mad anyo yadupuṃgava
d paśya tān adya samare matprayuktaiḥ sutejanaiḥ
d patyamānān raṇe kṛṣṇa śarair āśīviṣopamaiḥ
a ity evam uktvā bībhatsur devadattam athādhamat
b vyanādayad ameyātmā devadattaṃ mahāmṛdhe
b devadattasvanaṃ śrutvā keśavo 'pi mahāyaśāḥ
c pāñcajanyaṃ ca kṛṣṇo 'pi pūrayann iva rodasī
a taṃ tu śaṅkhasvanaṃ śrutvā saṃśaptakavarūthinī
c saṃcacāla mahārāja vitrastā cābhavad bhṛśam
a padabandhaṃ tataś cakre pāṇḍavaḥ paravīrahā
c nāgam astraṃ mahārāja saṃprodīrya muhur muhuḥ
d nāgam astraṃ tataḥ pārthaḥ prāduś cakre hasann iva
d pādabandhaṃ sa teṣāṃ vai cakre tena mahāstravit
a yān uddiśya raṇe pārthaḥ padabandhaṃ cakāra ha
c te baddhāḥ padabandhena pāṇḍavena mahātmanā
e niśceṣṭā abhavan rājann aśmasāramayā iva
a niśceṣṭāṃs tu tato yodhān avadhīt pāṇḍunandanaḥ
c yathendraḥ samare daityāṃs tārakasya vadhe purā
a te vadhyamānāḥ samare mumucus taṃ rathottamam
c āyudhāni ca sarvāṇi visraṣṭum upacakramuḥ
d te baddhāḥ pādabandhena na śekuś ceṣṭituṃ nṛpa
d tatas tān avadhīt pārthaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
d sarvayodhā hi samare bhujagair veṣṭitābhavan
a tataḥ suśarmā rājendra gṛhītāṃ vīkṣya vāhinīm
c sauparṇam astraṃ tvaritaḥ prāduścakre mahārathaḥ
a tataḥ suparṇāḥ saṃpetur bhakṣayanto bhujaṃgamān
c te vai vidudruvur nāgā dṛṣṭvā tān khacarān nṛpa
a babhau balaṃ tad vimuktaṃ padabandhād viśāṃ pate
c meghavṛndād yathā mukto bhāskaras tāpayan prajāḥ
a vipramuktās tu te yodhāḥ phalgunasya rathaṃ prati
c sasṛjur bāṇasaṃghāṃś ca śastrasaṃghāṃś ca māriṣa
d vividhāni ca śastrāṇi pratyavidhyanta sarvaśaḥ
a tāṃ mahāstramayīṃ vṛṣṭiṃ saṃchidya śaravṛṣṭibhiḥ
c vyavātiṣṭhat tato yodhān vāsaviḥ paravīrahā
a suśarmā tu tato rājan bāṇenānataparvaṇā
c arjunaṃ hṛdaye viddhvā vivyādhānyais tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
d so 'tividdho maheṣvāsaḥ śarair āśīviṣopamaiḥ
d suśarmāṇaṃ mahārāja krodhāviṣṭo mahārathaḥ
d tataḥ śaraśataiḥ pārthaḥ saṃchādyainaṃ kṣaṇād raṇe
d diśa āvārayām āsa bāṇais tatra mahāstravit
d vimukhīkṛtya samare suśarmāṇaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
e sa gāḍhaviddho vyathito rathopastha upāviśat
f tata uccukruśuḥ sarve hataḥ pārtha iti sma ha
f tataḥ śaṅkhaninādāś ca bherīśabdāś ca puṣkalāḥ
f nānāvāditraninadāḥ siṃhanādāś ca jajñire
a pratilabhya tataḥ saṃjñāṃ śvetāśvaḥ kṛṣṇasārathiḥ
c aindram astram ameyātmā prāduścakre tvarānvitaḥ
e tato bāṇasahasrāṇi samutpannāni māriṣa
a sarvadikṣu vyadṛśyanta sūdayanto nṛpa dvipān
c hayān rathāṃś ca samare śastraiḥ śatasahasraśaḥ
d rarāja samare rājañ śakro nighnann ivāsurān
a vadhyamāne tataḥ sainye vipulā bhīḥ samāviśat
c saṃśaptakagaṇānāṃ ca gopālānāṃ ca bhārata
e na hi kaś cit pumāṃs tatra yo 'rjunaṃ pratyayudhyata
a paśyatāṃ tatra vīrāṇām ahanyata mahad balam
c hanyamānam apaśyaṃś ca niśceṣṭāḥ sma parākrame
a ayutaṃ tatra yodhānāṃ hatvā pāṇḍusuto raṇe
c vyabhrājata raṇe rājan vidhūmo 'gnir iva jvalan
a caturdaśa sahasrāṇi yāni śiṣṭāni bhārata
c rathānām ayutaṃ caiva trisāhasrāś ca dantinaḥ
a tataḥ saṃśaptakā bhūyaḥ parivavrur dhanaṃjayam
c martavyam iti niścitya jayaṃ vāpi nivartanam
a tatra yuddhaṃ mahad dhy āsīt tāvakānāṃ viśāṃ pate
c śūreṇa balinā sārdhaṃ pāṇḍavena kirīṭinā
d jitvā tān nyahanat pārthaḥ śatrūñ śakra ivāsurān
 saṃjaya uvāca
a kṛtavarmā kṛpo drauṇiḥ sūtaputraś ca māriṣa
c ulūkaḥ saubalaś caiva rājā ca saha sodaraiḥ
a sīdamānāṃ camūṃ dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍuputrabhayārditām
c samujjihīrṣur vegena bhinnāṃ nāvam ivārṇave
a tato yuddham atīvāsīn muhūrtam iva bhārata
c bhīrūṇāṃ trāsajananaṃ śūrāṇāṃ harṣavardhanam
d bhīmasenaṃ sapāñcālaṃ cedikaikeyasaṃvṛtam
d vaikartanaḥ svayaṃ yuddhvā vārayām āsa kārmukaiḥ
d tataś cedikarūṣāṃś ca sṛñjayāṃś ca mahārathān
d karṇo jaghāna saṃkruddho bhīmasenasya paśyataḥ
a kṛpeṇa śaravarṣāṇi vipramuktāni saṃyuge
c sṛñjayāḥ śātayām āsuḥ śalabhānāṃ vrajā iva
a śikhaṇḍī tu tataḥ kruddho gautamaṃ tvarito yayau
c vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi samantād eva brāhmaṇe
d mahad āsīt tadā yuddhaṃ muhūrtād iva dāruṇam
d kruddhayoḥ samare rājan rāmarāvaṇayor iva
a kṛpas tu śaravarṣaṃ tad vinihatya mahāstravit
c śikhaṇḍinaṃ raṇe kruddho vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ
a tataḥ śikhaṇḍī kupītaḥ śaraiḥ saptabhir āhave
c kṛpaṃ vivyādha subhṛśaṃ kaṅkapatrair ajihmagaiḥ
a tataḥ kṛpaḥ śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ so 'tividdho mahārathaḥ
b tatas tu niśitais tīkṣṇaiḥ kṣuraprair hemabhūṣaṇaiḥ
c vyaśvasūtarathaṃ cakre pārṣataṃ tu dvijottamaḥ
a hatāśvāt tu tato yānād avaplutya mahārathaḥ
c carmakhaḍge ca saṃgṛhya satvaraṃ brāhmaṇaṃ yayau
a tam āpatantaṃ sahasā śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c chādayām āsa samare tad adbhutam ivābhavat
a tatrādbhutam apaśyāma śilānāṃ plavanaṃ yathā
c niśceṣṭo yad raṇe rājañ śikhaṇḍī samatiṣṭhata
a kṛpeṇa chāditaṃ dṛṣṭvā nṛpottama śikhaṇḍinam
c pratyudyayau kṛpaṃ tūrṇaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārathaḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ tato yāntaṃ śāradvatarathaṃ prati
c pratijagrāha vegena kṛtavarmā mahārathaḥ
a yudhiṣṭhiram athāyāntaṃ śāradvatarathaṃ prati
c saputraṃ sahasenaṃ ca droṇaputro nyavārayat
a nakulaṃ sahadevaṃ ca tvaramāṇau mahārathau
c pratijagrāha te putraḥ śaravarṣeṇa vārayan
a bhīmasenaṃ karūṣāṃś ca kekayān sahasṛñjayān
c karṇo vaikartano yuddhe vārayām āsa bhārata
a śikhaṇḍinas tato bāṇān kṛpaḥ śāradvato yudhi
c prāhiṇot tvarayā yukto didhakṣur iva māriṣa
a tāñ śarān preṣitāṃs tena samantād dhemabhūṣaṇān
c ciccheda khaḍgam āvidhya bhrāmayaṃś ca punaḥ punaḥ
a śatacandraṃ tataś carma gautamaḥ pārṣatasya ha
c vyadhamat sāyakais tūrṇaṃ tata uccukruśur janāḥ
a sa vicarmā mahārāja khaḍgapāṇir upādravat
c kṛpasya vaśam āpanno mṛtyor āsyam ivāturaḥ
a śāradvataśarair grastaṃ kliśyamānaṃ mahābalam
c citraketusuto rājan suketus tvarito yayau
a vikiran brāhmaṇaṃ yuddhe bahubhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c abhyāpatad ameyātmā gautamasya rathaṃ prati
a dṛṣṭvāviṣahyaṃ taṃ yuddhe brāhmaṇaṃ caritavratam
c apayātas tatas tūrṇaṃ śikhaṇḍī rājasattama
a suketus tu tato rājan gautamaṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c viddhvā vivyādha saptatyā punaś cainaṃ tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
a athāsya saśaraṃ cāpaṃ punaś ciccheda māriṣa
c sārathiṃ ca śareṇāsya bhṛśaṃ marmaṇy atāḍayat
a gautamas tu tataḥ kruddho dhanur gṛhya navaṃ dṛḍham
c suketuṃ triṃśatā bāṇaiḥ sarvamarmasv atāḍayat
a sa vihvalitasarvāṅgaḥ pracacāla rathottame
c bhūmicāle yathā vṛkṣaś calaty ākampito bhṛśam
a calatas tasya kāyāt tu śiro jvalitakuṇḍalam
c soṣṇīṣaṃ saśirastrāṇaṃ kṣurapreṇānvapātayat
a tac chiraḥ prāpatad bhūmau śyenāhṛtam ivāmiṣam
c tato 'sya kāyo vasudhāṃ paścāt prāpa tadā cyutaḥ
a tasmin hate mahārāja trastās tasya padānugāḥ
c gautamaṃ samare tyaktvā dudruvus te diśo daśa
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ tu samare saṃnivārya mahābalaḥ
c kṛtavarmābravīd dhṛṣṭas tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti pārṣatam
a tad abhūt tumulaṃ yuddhaṃ vṛṣṇipārṣatayo raṇe
c āmiṣārthe yathā yuddhaṃ śyenayor gṛddhayor nṛpa
a dhṛṣṭadyumnas tu samare hārdikyaṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c ājaghānorasi kruddhaḥ pīḍayan hṛdikātmajam
a kṛtavarmā tu samare pārṣatena dṛḍhāhataḥ
c pārṣataṃ sarathaṃ sāśvaṃ chādayām āsa sāyakaiḥ
a sarathaś chādito rājan dhṛṣṭadyumno na dṛśyate
c meghair iva paricchanno bhāskaro jaladāgame
a vidhūya taṃ bāṇagaṇaṃ śaraiḥ kanakabhūṣaṇaiḥ
c vyarocata raṇe rājan dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ kṛtavraṇaḥ
a tatas tu pārṣataḥ kruddhaḥ śastravṛṣṭiṃ sudāruṇām
c kṛtavarmāṇam āsādya vyasṛjat pṛtanāpatiḥ
a tām āpatantīṃ sahasā śastravṛṣṭiṃ nirantarām
c śarair anekasāhasrair hārdikyo vyadhamad yudhi
d yathā rukmarathenājau vāhān vāhair amiśrayat
d tathaiva sātvato rājan vāhān vāhair amiśrayat
d gṛhītvā carma khaḍgaṃ ca rathaṃ tasyāvapupluve
d miśriteṣv atha vāheṣu pratyāsanne ca pārṣate
d dṛṣṭvāpadānaṃ tasyāśu gadāṃ jagrāha sātvataḥ
d gadāpāṇis tato rājan rathāt tūrṇam avaplutaḥ
d tam adṛṣṭvā rathopasthe sārathiṃ samatāḍayat
d khaḍgena śitadhāreṇa sa hataḥ prāpatad rathāt
d kṛtavarmā tato hṛṣṭas talaśabdaṃ cakāra ha
d pārṣataṃ cābravīd rājann ehy ehīti punaḥ punaḥ
d sa taṃ na mamṛṣe yuddhe talaśabdaṃ samīritam
d yathā nāgaḥ sadā mattas talaśabdaṃ samīritam
d avaplutya rathāt tasmāt svarathaṃ punar āsthitaḥ
d abhyayāt sa tu taṃ tūrṇaṃ tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt
d kṛtavarmā susaṃkruddho didhakṣur iva pāvakaḥ
d dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhān sarvān pāṇḍavān paryavārayat
d tato rājan maheṣvāsaḥ kṛtavarmāṇam āśu vai
d gadāṃ gṛhya punar vegāt kṛtavarmāṇam āhanat
d so 'tividdho balavatā nyapatan mūrchayā hataḥ
d tato rājan maheṣvāsaṃ kṛtavarmāṇam āśu vai
d śrutavān ratham āropya apovāha raṇājirāt
a dṛṣṭvā tu dāritāṃ yuddhe śastravṛṣṭiṃ duruttarām
c kṛtavarmāṇam abhyetya vārayām āsa pārṣataḥ
d hārdikyaṃ chādayām āsa pārṣato niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a sārathiṃ cāsya tarasā prāhiṇod yamasādanam
c bhallena śitadhāreṇa sa hataḥ prāpatad rathāt
a dhṛṣṭadyumnas tu balavāñ jitvā śatruṃ mahāratham
c kauravān samare tūrṇaṃ vārayām āsa sāyakaiḥ
a tatas te tāvakā yodhā dhṛṣṭadyumnam upādravan
c siṃhanādaravaṃ kṛtvā tato yuddham avartata
 saṃjaya uvāca
a drauṇir yudhiṣṭhiraṃ dṛṣṭvā śaineyenābhirakṣitam
c draupadeyais tathā śūrair abhyavartata hṛṣṭavat
a kirann iṣugaṇān ghorān svarṇapuṅkhāñ śilāśitān
c darśayan vividhān mārgāñ śikṣārthaṃ laghuhastavat
a tataḥ khaṃ pūrayām āsa śarair divyāstramantritaiḥ
c yudhiṣṭhiraṃ ca samare paryavārayad astravit
a drauṇāyaniśaracchannaṃ na prājñāyata kiṃ cana
c bāṇabhūtam abhūt sarvam āyodhanaśiro hi tat
a bāṇajālaṃ diviṣṭhaṃ tat svarṇajālavibhūṣitam
c śuśubhe bharataśreṣṭha vitānam iva viṣṭhitam
a tena channe raṇe rājan bāṇajālena bhāsvatā
c abhracchāyeva saṃjajñe bāṇaruddhe nabhastale
a tatrāścaryam apaśyāma bāṇabhūte tathāvidhe
c na sma saṃpatate bhūmau dṛṣṭvā drauṇeḥ parākramam
a lāghavaṃ droṇaputrasya dṛṣṭvā tatra mahārathāḥ
c vyasmayanta mahārāja na cainaṃ prativīkṣitum
e śekus te sarvarājānas tapantam iva bhāskaram
a sātyakir yatamānas tu dharmarājaś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
c tathetarāṇi sainyāni na sma cakruḥ parākramam
a vadhyamāne tataḥ sainye draupadeyā mahārathāḥ
c sātyakir dharmarājaś ca pāñcālāś cāpi saṃgatāḥ
e tyaktvā mṛtyubhayaṃ ghoraṃ drauṇāyanim upādravan
a sātyakiḥ pañcaviṃśatyā drauṇiṃ viddhvā śilāmukhaiḥ
c punar vivyādha nārācaiḥ saptabhiḥ svarṇabhūṣitaiḥ
a yudhiṣṭhiras trisaptatyā prativindhyaś ca saptabhiḥ
c śrutakarmā tribhir bāṇaiḥ śrutakīrtis tu saptabhiḥ
a sutasomaś ca navabhiḥ śatānīkaś ca saptabhiḥ
c anye ca bahavaḥ śūrā vivyadhus taṃ samantataḥ
a so 'tikruddhas tato rājann āśīviṣa iva śvasan
c sātyakiṃ pañcaviṃśatyā prāvidhyata śilāśitaiḥ
a śrutakīrtiṃ ca navabhiḥ sutasomaṃ ca pañcabhiḥ
c aṣṭabhiḥ śrutakarmāṇaṃ prativindhyaṃ tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
e śatānīkaṃ ca navabhir dharmaputraṃ ca saptabhiḥ
a athetarāṃs tataḥ śūrān dvābhyāṃ dvābhyām atāḍayat
c śrutakīrtes tathā cāpaṃ ciccheda niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a athānyad dhanur ādāya śrutakīrtir mahārathaḥ
c drauṇāyaniṃ tribhir viddhvā vivyādhānyaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a tato drauṇir mahārāja śaravarṣeṇa bhārata
c chādayām āsa tat sainyaṃ samantāc ca śarair nṛpān
a tataḥ punar ameyātmā dharmarājasya kārmukam
c drauṇiś ciccheda vihasan vivyādha ca śarais tribhiḥ
a tato dharmasuto rājan pragṛhyānyan mahad dhanuḥ
c drauṇiṃ vivyādha saptatyā bāhvor urasi cārdayat
a sātyakis tu tataḥ kruddho drauṇeḥ praharato raṇe
c ardhacandreṇa tīkṣṇena dhanuś chittvānadad bhṛśam
a chinnadhanvā tato drauṇiḥ śaktyā śaktimatāṃ varaḥ
c sārathiṃ pātayām āsa śaineyasya rathād drutam
a athānyad dhanur ādāya droṇaputraḥ pratāpavān
c śaineyaṃ śaravarṣeṇa chādayām āsa bhārata
a tasyāśvāḥ pradrutāḥ saṃkhye patite rathasārathau
c tatra tatraiva dhāvantaḥ samadṛśyanta bhārata
a yudhiṣṭhirapurogās te drauṇiṃ śastrabhṛtāṃ varam
c abhyavarṣanta vegena visṛjantaḥ śitāñ śarān
a āgacchamānāṃs tān dṛṣṭvā raudrarūpān paraṃtapaḥ
c prahasan pratijagrāha droṇaputro mahāraṇe
a tataḥ śaraśatajvālaḥ senākakṣaṃ mahārathaḥ
c drauṇir dadāha samare kakṣam agnir yathā vane
a tad balaṃ pāṇḍuputrasya droṇaputrapratāpitam
c cukṣubhe bharataśreṣṭha timineva nadīmukham
c   tasminn eva camūmukhe
c tad balaṃ pāṇḍaveyasya droṇaputraśarārciṣā
c tāpayan bharataśreṣṭha gabhastibhir ivāṃśumān
c tat tāpyamānaṃ tīkṣṇāgrair brāhmaṇasya ca sāyakaiḥ
c kṣubhyate pāṇḍavaṃ sainyaṃ
c tad bhajyamānaṃ marṣeṇa brāhmaṇasya śarāhatam
a dṛṣṭvā te ca mahārāja droṇaputraparākramam
c nihatān menire sarvān pāṇḍūn droṇasutena vai
a yudhiṣṭhiras tu tvarito drauṇiṃ śliṣya mahāratham
c abravīd droṇaputraṃ tu roṣāmarṣasamanvitaḥ
d jānāmi tvāṃ yudhi śreṣṭhaṃ vīryavantaṃ balānvitam
d kṛtāstraṃ kṛtinaṃ caiva tathā laghuparākramam
d balam etad bhavān sarvaṃ pārṣate yadi darśayet
d tatas tvāṃ balavantaṃ ca kṛtavīryaṃ ca vidmahe
d sa hi vai pārṣataṃ dṛṣṭvā samare śatrusūdanam
d bhavet tava balaṃ kiṃ cid bravīmi tvāṃ na tu dvija
a naiva nāma tava prītir naiva nāma kṛtajñatā
c yatas tvaṃ puruṣavyāghra mām evādya jighāṃsasi
a brāhmaṇena tapaḥ kāryaṃ dānam adhyayanaṃ tathā
c kṣatriyeṇa dhanur nāmyaṃ sa bhavān brāhmaṇabruvaḥ
a miṣatas te mahābāho jeṣyāmi yudhi kauravān
c kuruṣva samare karma brahmabandhur asi dhruvam
a evam ukto mahārāja droṇaputraḥ smayann iva
c yuktatvaṃ tac ca saṃcintya nottaraṃ kiṃ cid abravīt
a anuktvā ca tataḥ kiṃ cic charavarṣeṇa pāṇḍavam
c chādayām āsa samare kruddho 'ntaka iva prajāḥ
a saṃchādyamānas tu tadā droṇaputreṇa māriṣa
c pārtho 'payātaḥ śīghraṃ vai vihāya mahatīṃ camūm
a apayāte tatas tasmin dharmaputre yudhiṣṭhire
c droṇaputraḥ sthito rājan pratyādeśān mahātmanaḥ
a tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā tyaktvā drauṇiṃ mahāhave
c prayayau tāvakaṃ sainyaṃ yuktaḥ krūrāya karmaṇe
 saṃjaya uvāca
a bhīmasenaṃ sapāñcālyaṃ cedikekayasaṃvṛtam
c vaikartanaḥ svayaṃ ruddhvā vārayām āsa sāyakaiḥ
a tatas tu cedikārūṣān sṛñjayāṃś ca mahārathān
c karṇo jaghāna saṃkruddho bhīmasenasya paśyataḥ
a bhīmasenas tataḥ karṇaṃ vihāya rathasattamam
c prayayau kauravaṃ sainyaṃ kakṣam agnir iva jvalan
a sūtaputro 'pi samare pāñcālān kekayāṃs tathā
c sṛñjayāṃś ca maheṣvāsān nijaghāna sahasraśaḥ
a saṃśaptakeṣu pārthaś ca kauraveṣu vṛkodaraḥ
c pāñcāleṣu tathā karṇaḥ kṣayaṃ cakrūr mahārathāḥ
a te kṣatriyā dahyamānās tribhis taiḥ pāvakopamaiḥ
c jagmur vināśaṃ samare rājan durmantrite tava
a tato duryodhanaḥ kruddho nakulaṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c vivyādha bharataśreṣṭha caturaś cāsya vājinaḥ
a tataḥ punar ameyātmā tava putro janādhipaḥ
c kṣureṇa sahadevasya dhvajaṃ ciccheda kāñcanam
a nakulas tu tataḥ kruddhas tava putraṃ trisaptabhiḥ
c jaghāna samare rājan sahadevaś ca pañcabhiḥ
a tāv ubhau bharataśreṣṭhau śreṣṭhau sarvadhanuṣmatām
c vivyādhorasi saṃkruddhaḥ pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ
a tato 'parābhyāṃ bhallābhyāṃ dhanuṣī samakṛntata
c yamayoḥ prahasan rājan vivyādhaiva ca saptabhiḥ
a tāv anye dhanuṣī śreṣṭhe śakracāpanibhe śubhe
c pragṛhya rejatuḥ śūrau devaputrasamau yudhi
a tatas tau rabhasau yuddhe bhrātarau bhrātaraṃ nṛpa
c śarair vavarṣatur ghorair mahāmeghau yathācalam
a tataḥ kruddho mahārāja tava putro mahārathaḥ
c pāṇḍuputrau maheṣvāsau vārayām āsa patribhiḥ
a dhanurmaṇḍalam evāsya dṛśyate yudhi bhārata
c sāyakāś caiva dṛśyante niścarantaḥ samantataḥ
a tasya sāyakasaṃchannau cakāśetāṃ ca pāṇḍavau
c meghacchannau yathā vyomni candrasūryau hataprabhau
a te tu bāṇā mahārāja hemapuṅkhāḥ śilāśitāḥ
c ācchādayan diśaḥ sarvāḥ sūryasyevāṃśavas tadā
a bāṇabhūte tatas tasmin saṃchanne ca nabhastale
b nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca krodhaṃ tīvraṃ samāsthitau
b tāṃ bāṇavṛṣṭiṃ rājñas tu śaraiḥ śatasahasrabhiḥ sic
b chādayām āsatur ubhau bāṇaughais tanayaṃ tava
b tatas tayor mahārāja sṛjator aniśaṃ śarān
c yamābhyāṃ dadṛśe rūpaṃ kālāntakayamopamam
a parākramaṃ tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā tava sūnor mahārathāḥ
b krodham āsthāya paramaṃ niḥśvasaṃś ca yathoragaḥ
b bāṇāndhakāraṃ sasṛje tava putras tayos tadā
c mṛtyor upāntikaṃ prāptau mādrīputrau sma menire
a tataḥ senāpatī rājan pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ
c pārṣataḥ prayayau tatra yatra rājā suyodhanaḥ
a mādrīputrau tataḥ śūrau vyatikramya mahārathau
c dhṛṣṭadyumnas tava sutaṃ tāḍayām āsa sāyakaiḥ
a tam avidhyad ameyātmā tava putro 'tyamarṣaṇaḥ
c pāñcālyaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā prahasya puruṣarṣabha
a tataḥ punar ameyātmā putras te pṛthivīpate
c viddhvā nanāda pāñcālyaṃ ṣaṣṭyā pañcabhir eva ca
a athāsya saśaraṃ cāpaṃ hastāvāpaṃ ca māriṣa
c kṣurapreṇa sutīkṣṇena rājā ciccheda saṃyuge
a tad apāsya dhanuś chinnaṃ pāñcālyaḥ śatrukarśanaḥ
c anyad ādatta vegena dhanur bhārasahaṃ navam
a prajvalann iva vegena saṃrambhād rudhirekṣaṇaḥ
c aśobhata maheṣvāso dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ kṛtavraṇaḥ
a sa pañcadaśa nārācāñ śvasataḥ pannagān iva
c jighāṃsur bharataśreṣṭhaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumno vyavāsṛjat
a te varma hemavikṛtaṃ bhittvā rājñaḥ śilāśitāḥ
c viviśur vasudhāṃ vegāt kaṅkabarhiṇavāsasaḥ
a so 'tividdho mahārāja putras te 'tivyarājata
c vasante puṣpaśabalaḥ sapuṣpa iva kiṃśukaḥ
a sa chinnavarmā nārācaiḥ prahārair jarjaracchaviḥ
c dhṛṣṭadyumnasya bhallena kruddhaś ciccheda kārmukam
a athainaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ tvaramāṇo mahīpatiḥ
c sāyakair daśabhī rājan bhruvor madhye samārdayat
d vivyādha vividhair bāṇaiḥ kālāntakayamopamaiḥ
a tasya te 'śobhayan vaktraṃ karmāraparimārjitāḥ
c praphullaṃ campakaṃ yadvad bhramarā madhulipsavaḥ
a tad apāsya dhanuś chinnaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumno mahāmanāḥ
c anyad ādatta vegena dhanur bhallāṃś ca ṣoḍaśa
a tato duryodhanasyāśvān hatvā sūtaṃ ca pañcabhiḥ
c dhanuś ciccheda bhallena jātarūpapariṣkṛtam
a rathaṃ sopaskaraṃ chatraṃ śaktiṃ khaḍgaṃ gadāṃ dhvajam
c bhallaiś ciccheda navabhiḥ putrasya tava pārṣataḥ
a tapanīyāṅgadaṃ citraṃ nāgaṃ maṇimayaṃ śubham
c dhvajaṃ kurupateś chinnaṃ dadṛśuḥ sarvapārthivāḥ
a duryodhanaṃ tu virathaṃ chinnasarvāyudhaṃ raṇe
c bhrātaraḥ paryarakṣanta sodaryā bharatarṣabha
a tam āropya rathe rājan daṇḍadhāro janādhipam
c apovāha ca saṃbhrānto dhṛṣṭadyumnasya paśyataḥ
a karṇas tu sātyakiṃ jitvā rājagṛddhī mahābalaḥ
c droṇahantāram ugreṣuṃ sasārābhimukhaṃ raṇe
a taṃ pṛṣṭhato 'bhyayāt tūrṇaṃ śaineyo vitudañ śaraiḥ
c vāraṇaṃ jaghanopānte viṣāṇābhyām iva dvipaḥ
a sa bhārata mahān āsīd yodhānāṃ sumahātmanām
c karṇapārṣatayor madhye tvadīyānāṃ mahāraṇaḥ
a na pāṇḍavānāṃ nāsmākaṃ yodhaḥ kaś cit parāṅmukhaḥ
c pratyadṛśyata yat karṇaḥ pāñcālāṃs tvarito yayau
a tasmin kṣaṇe naraśreṣṭha gajavājinarakṣayaḥ
c prādurāsīd ubhayato rājan madhyaṃgate 'hani
a pāñcālās tu mahārāja tvaritā vijigīṣavaḥ
c sarvato 'bhyadravan karṇaṃ patatriṇa iva drumam
a teṣām ādhirathiḥ kruddho yatamānān manasvinaḥ
c vicinvann eva bāṇāgraiḥ samāsādayad agrataḥ
a vyāghraketuṃ suśarmāṇaṃ śaṅkuṃ cograṃ dhanaṃjayam
c śuklaṃ ca rocamānaṃ ca siṃhasenaṃ ca durjayam
a te vīrā rathavegena parivavrur narottamam
c sṛjantaṃ sāyakān kruddhaṃ karṇam āhavaśobhinam
a yudhyamānāṃs tu tāñ śūrān manujendraḥ pratāpavān
c aṣṭābhir aṣṭau rādheyo nyahanan niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a athāparān mahārāja sūtaputraḥ pratāpavān
c jaghāna bahusāhasrān yodhān yuddhaviśāradaḥ
a viṣṇuṃ ca viṣṇukarmāṇaṃ devāpiṃ bhadram eva ca
c daṇḍaṃ ca samare rājaṃś citraṃ citrāyudhaṃ harim
a siṃhaketuṃ rocamānaṃ śalabhaṃ ca mahāratham
c nijaghāna susaṃkruddhaś cedīnāṃ ca mahārathān
a teṣām ādadataḥ prāṇān āsīd ādhirather vapuḥ
c śoṇitābhyukṣitāṅgasya rudrasyevorjitaṃ mahat
a tatra bhārata karṇena mātaṅgās tāḍitāḥ śaraiḥ
c sarvato 'bhyadravan bhītāḥ kurvanto mahad ākulam
a nipetur urvyāṃ samare karṇasāyakapīḍitāḥ
c kurvanto vividhān nādān vajranunnā ivācalāḥ
a gajavājimanuṣyaiś ca nipatadbhiḥ samantataḥ
c rathaiś cāvagatair mārge paryastīryata medinī
a naiva bhīṣmo na ca droṇo nāpy anye yudhi tāvakāḥ
c cakruḥ sma tādṛśaṃ karma yādṛśaṃ vai kṛtaṃ raṇe
a sūtaputreṇa nāgeṣu ratheṣu ca hayeṣu ca
c nareṣu ca naravyāghra kṛtaṃ sma kadanaṃ mahat
a mṛgamadhye yathā siṃho dṛśyate nirbhayaś caran
c pāñcālānāṃ tathā madhye karṇo 'carad abhītavat
a yathā mṛgagaṇāṃs trastān siṃho drāvayate diśaḥ
c pāñcālānāṃ rathavrātān karṇo drāvayate tathā
a siṃhāsyaṃ ca yathā prāpya na jīvanti mṛgāḥ kva cit
c tathā karṇam anuprāpya na jīvanti mahārathāḥ
a vaiśvānaraṃ yathā dīptaṃ dahyante prāpya vai janāḥ
c karṇāgninā raṇe tadvad dagdhā bhārata sṛñjayāḥ
a karṇena cediṣv ekena pāñcāleṣu ca bhārata
c viśrāvya nāma nihatā bahavaḥ śūrasaṃmatāḥ
a mama cāsīn manuṣyendra dṛṣṭvā karṇasya vikramam
c naiko 'py ādhirather jīvan pāñcālyo mokṣyate yudhi
a pāñcālān vidhaman saṃkhye sūtaputraḥ pratāpavān
b pāñcālān atha nighnantaṃ karṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā mahāraṇe
c abhyadhāvata saṃkruddho dharmaputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca rājānaṃ draupadeyāś ca māriṣa
c parivavrur amitraghnaṃ śataśaś cāpare janāḥ
a śikhaṇḍī sahadevaś ca nakulo nākulis tathā
c janamejayaḥ śiner naptā bahavaś ca prabhadrakāḥ
a ete purogamā bhūtvā dhṛṣṭadyumnasya saṃyuge
c karṇam asyantam iṣvastrair vicerur amitaujasaḥ
a tāṃs tatrādhirathiḥ saṃkhye cedipāñcālapāṇḍavān
b sātyakiṃ ca mahārāja nātyavartata saṃyuge
c eko bahūn abhyapatad garutman pannagān iva
d taiḥ karṇasyābhavad yuddhaṃ ghorarūpaṃ viśāṃ pate
d tādṛg yādṛk purā vṛttaṃ devānāṃ dānavaiḥ saha
d tān sametān maheṣvāsāñ śaravarṣaughavarṣiṇaḥ
d eko 'bhyabhavad avyagras tamāṃsīva divākaraḥ
a bhīmasenas tu saṃkruddhaḥ kurūn madrān sakekayān
b sarvato 'bhyahanat kruddho yamadaṇḍanibhaiḥ śaraiḥ
b bāhlīkān kekayān matsyān vāsātyān madrasaindhavān
c ekaḥ saṃkhye maheṣvāso yodhayan bahv aśobhata
a tatra marmasu bhīmena nārācais tāḍitā gajāḥ
c prapatanto hatārohāḥ kampayanti sma medinīm
a vājinaś ca hatārohāḥ pattayaś ca gatāsavaḥ
c śerate yudhi nirbhinnā vamanto rudhiraṃ bahu
d tāḍitāḥ sahasā nāgā bhīmasenena māriṣa
d nipatanti sma vegena vajrarugṇā ivācalāḥ
d nihatais tair mahārāja vegavadbhir mahāgajaiḥ
d śuśubhe vasudhā rājan vikīrṇair iva parvataiḥ
a sahasraśaś ca rathinaḥ patitāḥ patitāyudhāḥ
c akṣatāḥ samadṛśyanta bhīmād bhītā gatāsavaḥ
a rathibhir vājibhiḥ sūtaiḥ pattibhiś ca tathā gajaiḥ
c bhīmasenaśaracchinnair āstīrṇā vasudhābhavat
a tat stambhitam ivātiṣṭhad bhīmasenabalārditam
c duryodhanabalaṃ rājan nirutsāhaṃ kṛtavraṇam
a niśceṣṭaṃ tumule dīnaṃ babhau tasmin mahāraṇe
c prasannasalilaḥ kāle yathā syāt sāgaro nṛpa
d tadvat tava balaṃ tad vai niścalaṃ samavasthitam
a manyuvīryabalopetaṃ balāt paryavaropitam
c abhavat tava putrasya tat sainyam iṣubhis tadā
d tad balaṃ bharataśreṣṭha vadhyamānaṃ parasparam
e rudhiraughapariklinnaṃ rudhirārdraṃ babhūva ha
f jagāma bharataśreṣṭha vadhyamānaṃ parasparam
a sūtaputro raṇe kruddhaḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm
c bhīmasenaḥ kurūṃś cāpi drāvayan bahv aśobhata
a vartamāne tathā raudre saṃgrāme 'dbhutadarśane
c nihatya pṛtanāmadhye saṃśaptakagaṇān bahūn
a arjuno jayatāṃ śreṣṭho vāsudevam athābravīt
c prabhagnaṃ balam etad dhi yotsyamānaṃ janārdana
a ete dhāvanti sagaṇāḥ saṃśaptakamahārathāḥ
b durjayā hy eva samare devair api savāsavaiḥ
c apārayanto madbāṇān siṃhaśabdān mṛgā iva
d kuravaś cāpi dhāvanti bhīmasenabhayārditāḥ
a dīryate ca mahat sainyaṃ sṛñjayānāṃ mahāraṇe
c hastikakṣyo hy asau kṛṣṇa ketuḥ karṇasya dhīmataḥ
e dṛśyate rājasainyasya madhye vicarato muhuḥ
a na ca karṇaṃ raṇe śaktā jetum anye mahārathāḥ
b durjayā hy eṣa samare devadānavarākṣasaiḥ
c jānīte hi bhavān karṇaṃ vīryavantaṃ parākrame
a tatra yāhi yataḥ karṇo drāvayaty eṣa no balam
a varjayitvā raṇe yāhi sūtaputraṃ mahāratham
c śramo mā bādhate kṛṣṇa yathā vā tava rocate
a etac chrutvā mahārāja govindaḥ prahasann iva
c abravīd arjunaṃ tūrṇaṃ kauravāñ jahi pāṇḍava
a tatas tava mahat sainyaṃ govindapreritā hayāḥ
c haṃsavarṇāḥ praviviśur vahantaḥ kṛṣṇapāṇḍavau
a keśavaprahitair aśvaiḥ śvetaiḥ kāñcanabhūṣaṇaiḥ
c praviśadbhis tava balaṃ caturdiśam abhidyata
d meghastanitanirhrādaḥ sa ratho vānaradhvajaḥ
d calatpatākas tāṃ senāṃ vimānaṃ dyām ivāviśata
a tau vidārya mahāsenāṃ praviṣṭau keśavārjunau
c kruddhau saṃrambharaktākṣau vyabhrājetāṃ mahādyutī
a yuddhaśauṇḍau samāhūtāv aribhis tau raṇādhvaram
c yajvabhir vidhināhūtau makhe devāv ivāśvinau
d krodhatāmrekṣaṇau śūrau śuśubhāte mahābalau
d madotkaṭau yathā nāgau dṛṣṭisaṃcāracāriṇau
a kruddhau tau tu naravyāghrau vegavantau babhūvatuḥ
c talaśabdena ruṣitau yathā nāgau mahāhave
a vigāhan sa rathānīkam aśvasaṃghāṃś ca phalgunaḥ
c vyacarat pṛtanāmadhye pāśahasta ivāntakaḥ
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā yudhi vikrāntaṃ senāyāṃ tava bhārata
c saṃśaptakagaṇān bhūyaḥ putras te samacodayat
a tato rathasahasreṇa dviradānāṃ tribhiḥ śataiḥ
c caturdaśasahasraiś ca turagāṇāṃ mahāhave
a dvābhyāṃ śatasahasrābhyāṃ padātīnāṃ ca dhanvinām
c śūrāṇāṃ nāmalabdhānāṃ viditānāṃ samantataḥ
d duryodhanena te sārdhaṃ jātavegāḥ samantataḥ
e abhyavartanta tau vīrau chādayanto mahārathāḥ
f śaravarṣair mahārāja sarvataḥ pāṇḍunandanam
a sa chādyamānaḥ samare śaraiḥ parabalārdanaḥ
c darśayan raudram ātmānaṃ pāśahasta ivāntakaḥ
e nighnan saṃśaptakān pārthaḥ prekṣaṇīyataro 'bhavat
a tato vidyutprabhair bāṇaiḥ kārtasvaravibhūṣitaiḥ
c nirantaram ivākāśam āsīn nunnaiḥ kirīṭinā
a kirīṭibhujanirmuktaiḥ saṃpatadbhir mahāśaraiḥ
c samācchannaṃ babhau sarvaṃ kādraveyair iva prabho
a rukmapuṅkhān prasannāgrāñ śarān saṃnataparvaṇaḥ
c adarśayad ameyātmā dikṣu sarvāsu pāṇḍavaḥ
d mahī viyad diśaḥ sarvāḥ samudrā girayo 'pi vā
d sphuṭantīti janā jajñuḥ pārthasya talanisvanāt
a hatvā daśa sahasrāṇi pārthivānāṃ mahārathaḥ
c saṃśaptakānāṃ kaunteyaḥ prapakṣaṃ tvarito 'bhyayāt
a prapakṣaṃ sa samāsādya pārthaḥ kāmbojarakṣitam
c pramamātha balād bāṇair dānavān iva vāsavaḥ
a pracicchedāśu bhallaiś ca dviṣatām ātatāyinām
c śastrapāṇīṃs tathā bāhūṃs tathāpi ca śirāṃsy uta
a aṅgāṅgāvayavaiś chinnair vyāyudhās te 'patan kṣitau
c viṣvagvātābhisaṃbhagnā bahuśākhā iva drumāḥ
d kāmbojas tu tataḥ kruddho dṛṣṭvā pārthaṃ mahāratham
a hastyaśvarathapattīnāṃ vrātān nighnantam arjunam
b acodayata yantāram arjunāyaiva māṃ vaha
b tatas taṃ rathināṃ śreṣṭhaṃ bahudakṣiṇam āhave
b arjunasya rathaṃ kṣipraṃ prāpayām āsa sārathiḥ
b tato 'rjunaṃ tribhir bāṇair viddhvā bhārasahair yudhi
b keśavaṃ navabhī rājan bāhvor urasi cāparyat
b tataḥ kruddho mahārāja pāṇḍavaḥ paravīrahā
c sudakṣiṇād avarajaḥ śaravṛṣṭyābhyavīvṛṣat
a asyāsyato 'rdhacandrābhyāṃ sa bāhū parighopamau
c pūrṇacandrābhavaktraṃ ca kṣureṇābhyahanac chiraḥ
a sa papāta tato vāhāt svalohitaparisravaḥ
c manaḥśilāgireḥ śṛṅgaṃ vajreṇevāvadāritam
a sudakṣiṇād avarajaṃ kāmbojaṃ dadṛśur hatam
c prāṃśuṃ kamalapatrākṣam atyarthaṃ priyadarśanam
e kāñcanastambhasaṃkāśaṃ bhinnaṃ hemagiriṃ yathā
a tato 'bhavat punar yuddhaṃ ghoram adbhutadarśanam
c nānāvasthāś ca yodhānāṃ babhūvus tatra yudhyatām
a eteṣv āvarjitair aśvaiḥ kāmbojair yavanaiḥ śakaiḥ
c śoṇitāktais tadā raktaṃ sarvam āsīd viśāṃ pate
a rathai rathāśvasūtaiś ca hatārohaiś ca vājibhiḥ
c dviradaiś ca hatārohair mahāmātrair hatadvipaiḥ
e anyonyena mahārāja kṛto ghoro janakṣayaḥ
a tasmin prapakṣe pakṣe ca vadhyamāne mahātmanā
c arjunaṃ jayatāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ tvarito drauṇir āyayau
a vidhunvāno mahac cāpaṃ kārtasvaravibhūṣitam
c ādadānaḥ śarān ghorān svaraśmīn iva bhāskaraḥ
d krodhāmarṣavivṛttāsyo lohitākṣo babhau balī
d antakāle yathā kruddho mṛtyuḥ kiṃkaradaṇḍabhṛt
d tataḥ prāsṛjad ugrāṇi śaravarṣāṇi saṃghaśaḥ
d tair visṛṣṭair mahārāja vyadravat pāṇḍavī camūḥ
d sa dṛṣṭvaiva tu dāśārhaṃ syandanasthaṃ viśāṃ pate
d punaḥ prāsṛjad ugrāṇi śaravarṣāṇi māriṣa
d tayor āsīn mahad yuddhaṃ dharmabhrātror anaiṣṭhikam
d visiṣmāpayiṣor lokaṃ yaśaś cottamam icchatoḥ
d saṃśaptakāṃs tu kaunteyaḥ kurūṃś cāpi vṛkodaraḥ
d sūtaputras tu pāñcālān bhūyo 'ghnaṃs tvaritāḥ śaraiḥ
d evam eṣa mahārāja vināśaḥ pṛthivīkṣitām
d āsīt kruddhe 'rjune karṇe bhīmasene ca dāruṇe
d yuddhaṃ ghoraṃ tathā tv āsīt tridhābhūte camūmukhe
a taiḥ patadbhir mahārāja drauṇimuktaiḥ samantataḥ
c saṃchāditau rathasthau tāv ubhau kṛṣṇadhanaṃjayau
a tataḥ śaraśatais tīkṣṇair bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān
c niśceṣṭau tāv ubhau cakre yuddhe mādhavapāṇḍavau
a hāhākṛtam abhūt sarvaṃ jaṅgamaṃ sthāvaraṃ tathā
c carācarasya goptārau dṛṣṭvā saṃchāditau śaraiḥ
a siddhacāraṇasaṃghāś ca saṃpetur vai samantataḥ
c cintayanto bhaved adya lokānāṃ svasty apīty aha
a na mayā tādṛśo rājan dṛṣṭapūrvaḥ parākramaḥ
c saṃjajñe yādṛśo drauṇeḥ kṛṣṇau saṃchādayiṣyataḥ
a drauṇes tu dhanuṣaḥ śabdam ahitatrāsanaṃ raṇe
c aśrauṣaṃ bahuśo rājan siṃhasya nadato yathā
a jyā cāsya carato yuddhe savyadakṣiṇam asyataḥ
c vidyud ambudamadhyasthā bhrājamāneva sābhavat
a sa tathā kṣiprakārī ca dṛḍhahastaś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
c saṃmohaṃ paramaṃ gatvā praikṣata droṇajaṃ tataḥ
a sa vikramaṃ hṛtaṃ mene ātmanaḥ sumahātmanā
c tathāsya samare rājan vapur āsīt sudurdṛśam
a drauṇipāṇḍavayor evaṃ vartamāne mahāraṇe
c vardhamāne ca rājendra droṇaputre mahābale
e hīyamāne ca kaunteye kṛṣṇaṃ roṣaḥ samabhyayāt
a sa roṣān niḥśvasan rājan nirdahann iva cakṣuṣā
c drauṇiṃ hy apaśyat saṃgrāme phalgunaṃ ca muhur muhuḥ
a tataḥ kruddho 'bravīt kṛṣṇaḥ pārthaṃ sapraṇayaṃ tadā
c atyadbhutam idaṃ pārtha tava paśyāmi saṃyuge
e atiśete hi yatra tvā droṇaputro 'dya bhārata
f kaccid vīryaṃ yathāpūrvaṃ bhujayor vā balaṃ tava
a kaccit te gāṇḍivaṃ haste rathe tiṣṭhasi cārjuna
c kaccit kuśalinau bāhū kaccid vīryaṃ tad eva te
d udīryamāṇaṃ hi raṇe paśyāmi drauṇim āhave
d guruputra iti hy enaṃ mānayan bharatarṣabha
d upekṣāṃ kuru mā pārtha nāyaṃ kāla upekṣitum
a evam uktas tu kṛṣṇena kṣiptvā bhallāṃś caturdaśa
c tvaramāṇas tvarākāle drauṇer dhanur athācchinat
e dhvajaṃ chatraṃ patākāṃ ca rathaṃ śaktiṃ gadāṃ tathā
a jatrudeśe ca subhṛśaṃ vatsadantair atāḍayat
c sa mūrcchāṃ paramāṃ gatvā dhvajayaṣṭiṃ samāśritaḥ
a taṃ visaṃjñaṃ mahārāja kirīṭibhayapīḍitam
c apovāha raṇāt sūto rakṣamāṇo dhanaṃjayāt
a etasminn eva kāle tu vijayaḥ śatrutāpanaḥ
c nyavadhīt tāvakaṃ sainyaṃ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
e paśyatas tava putrasya tasya vīrasya bhārata
a evam eṣa kṣayo vṛttas tāvakānāṃ paraiḥ saha
c krūro viśasano ghoro rājan durmantrite tava
a saṃśaptakāṃś ca kaunteyaḥ kurūṃś cāpi vṛkodaraḥ
c vasuṣeṇaṃ ca pāñcālaḥ kṛtsnena vyadhamad raṇe
d vartamāne tathā raudre rājan vīravarakṣaye
d utthitāny agaṇeyāni kabandhāni samantataḥ
d yudhiṣṭhiro 'pi saṃgrāme prahārair gāḍhavedanaḥ
d krośamātram apakramya tasthau bharatasattama
d saṃjayaḥ
d duryodhanas tataḥ karṇam upetya bharatarṣabha
d abravīn madrarājaṃ ca tathaivānyān mahārathān
d yadṛcchayopasaṃprāptaṃ svargadvāram apāvṛtam
d sukhinaḥ kṣatriyāḥ karṇa labhante yuddham īdṛśam
d sadṛśaiḥ kṣatriyaiḥ śūraiḥ śūrāṇāṃ yudhyatāṃ yudhi
d iṣṭaṃ bhavati rādheya tad idaṃ samupasthitam
d hatvā vā pāṇḍavān yuddhe sphītām urvīm avāpsyatha
d nihatā vā parair yuddhe vīralokam avāpsyatha
d duryodhanasya tac chrutvā vacanaṃ kṣatriyarṣabhāḥ
d hṛṣṭā nādān udakrośan vāditrāṇi ca sarvaśaḥ
d tataḥ pramudite tasmin duryodhanabale tadā
d harṣayaṃs tāvakān yodhān drauṇir vacanam abravīt
d pratyakṣaṃ sarvasainyānāṃ bhavatāṃ cāpi paśyatām
d nyastaśastro mama pitā dhṛṣṭadyumnena pātitaḥ
d sa tenāham amarṣeṇa mitrārthe cāpi pārthivāḥ
d satyaṃ vaḥ pratijānāmi tad vākyaṃ me nibodhata
d dhṛṣṭadyumnam ahatvāhaṃ na vimokṣyāmi daṃśanam
d anṛtāyāṃ pratijñāyāṃ nāhaṃ svargam avāpnuyām
d arjuno bhīmasenaś ca yaś ca māṃ pratyudeṣyati
d sarvāṃs tān pramathiṣye 'ham iti me nāsti saṃśayaḥ
d evam ukte tataḥ sarvā sahitā bhāratī camūḥ
d abhyadravata kaunteyāṃs tathā te cāpi pāṇḍavāḥ
d sa saṃnipāto rathayūthapānāṃ
d mahātmanāṃ bhārata mohanīyaḥ
d janakṣayaḥ kālayugāntakalpaḥ
d prāvartatāgre kurusṛñjayānām
d tataḥ pravṛtte yudhi saṃprahāre
d bhūtāni sarvāṇi sadaivatāni
d āsan sametāni sahāpsarobhir
d didṛkṣamāṇāni narapravīrān
d divyaiś ca mālyair vividhaiś ca gandhair
d divyaiś ca ratnair vividhair narāgryān
d raṇe svakarmodvahataḥ pravīrān
d avākirann apsarasaḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ
d samīraṇas tāṃś ca niṣevya gandhān
d siṣeva sarvān api yodhamukhyān
d niṣevyamāṇās tv anilena yodhāḥ
d parasparaghnā dharaṇīṃ nipetuḥ
d sā divyapuṣpair avakīryamāṇā
d suvarṇapuṅkhaiś ca śarair vicitraiḥ
d nakṣatrasaṃghair iva citritā dyauḥ
d kṣitair babhau yodhavarair vicitrā
d tato 'ntarikṣād api sādhuvādair
d vāditraghoṣaiḥ samudīryamāṇaḥ
d jyāghoṣanemisvananādacitraḥ
d samākulaḥ so 'bhavat saṃprahāraḥ
d tathā tu tasmiṃs tumule pravṛtte
d duryodhanaḥ krodham amṛṣyamāṇaḥ
d abhyetya bhīmaṃ balinaṃ baliṣṭhaḥ
d samarpayat kṣudrakāṇāṃ śatena
d duḥśāsanaś citrasenaś ca vīras
d tathā caivaṃ kitavaḥ saubalaś ca
d gajānīkaiḥ sarvato bhīmasenaṃ
d tathā viṣaktaṃ sahasaivābhyagacchan
d tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya gajānīkaṃ vṛkodaraḥ
d duryodhanaṃ mahābāhuḥ śaravarṣair avākirat
d duryodhanaṃ tathā bhīmaḥ sāyakaiḥ śataśaḥ śitaiḥ
d pāṇḍavo vimukhīkṛtya gajān abhyadravad balī
d tataḥ pāvakasaṃkāśair bhīmo bāṇair avakragaiḥ
d śalabhair iva nāgāṃs tān ardayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ
d tataḥ kuñjarayūthāni bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
d vyadhaman niśitair bāṇair mahābhrāṇīva mārutaḥ
d anvayus tad rathānīkaṃ maṇijālaiś ca kuñjarāḥ
d rūpyajāmbūnadābhāsāḥ kṣuramālyābhyalaṃkṛtāḥ
d vadhyamānāḥ śarai rājan bhīmasenena te gajāḥ
d vibhinnahṛdayāḥ ke cit tatraivābhyapatan bhuvi
d nipatadbhir mahāvegair hemabhāṇḍavibhūṣitaiḥ
d aśobhata mahārāja dhātucitrair ivācalaiḥ
d dīptābharaṇavadbhiś ca gajapṛṣṭhān nipātitaiḥ
d sa raṇaḥ śuśubhe rājan kṣīṇapuṇyair ivāmaraiḥ
d mahāparighasaṃkāśau candanāgarurūṣitau
d apaśyan bhīmasenasya dhanur vikṣipato bhujau
d tasya jyātalanirghoṣam asyataḥ savyadakṣiṇam
d śrutvā hy abhyadravan nāgā bhīmasenaṃ bhayārditāḥ
d tasya bhīmasya tat karma rājann ekasya dhīmataḥ
d apaśyāma mahārāja tad adbhutam ivābhavat
d saṃjaya uvāca
d evam eṣa mahān āsīt saṃgrāmaḥ pṛthivīkṣitām
d kruddhe 'rjune tathā karṇe bhīmasene ca pāṇḍave
d droṇaputraṃ parājitya jitvā cānyān mahārathān
d abravīd arjuno rājan vāsudevam idaṃ vacaḥ
d paśya kṛṣṇa mahābāho dravantīṃ pāṇḍavīṃ camūm
d karṇaṃ paśya ca saṃgrāme kālayantaṃ mahārathān
d na ca paśyāmi dāśārha dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
d nāpi ketur yudhāṃ śreṣṭha dharmarājasya dṛśyate
d tribhāgaś cāvaśiṣṭo 'yaṃ divasasya janārdana
d na ca māṃ dhārtarāṣṭreṣu kaś cid yudhyati saṃyuge
d tasmāt tvaṃ matpriyaṃ kurvan yāhi yatra yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d dṛṣṭvā kuśalinaṃ yuddhe dharmaputraṃ sahānujam
d punar yoddhāsmi vārṣṇeya śatrubhiḥ saha saṃyuge
d tataḥ prāyād rathenāśu bībhatsor vacanād dhariḥ
d yato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā sṛñjayāś ca mahārathāḥ
d ayudhyaṃs tāvakaiḥ sārdhaṃ mṛtyuṃ kṛtvā nivartanam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tvaramāṇaḥ punaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ pārtham abhyavadac chanaiḥ
c paśya kauravya rājānam apayātāṃś ca pāṇḍavān
a karṇaṃ paśya mahāraṅge jvalantam iva pāvakam
c asau bhīmo maheṣvāsaḥ saṃnivṛtto raṇaṃ prati
a tam ete 'nu nivartante dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamāḥ
c pāñcālānāṃ sṛñjayānāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca yan mukham
e nivṛttaiś ca tathā pārthair bhagnaṃ śatrubalaṃ mahat
a kauravān dravato hy eṣa karṇo dhārayate 'rjuna
c antakapratimo vege śakratulyaparākramaḥ
a asau gacchati kauravya drauṇir astrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
c tam eṣa pradrutaḥ saṃkhye dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārathaḥ
d anuprayāti saṃgrāme hatān paśya ca sṛñjayān
a sarvaṃ vyācaṣṭa durdharṣo vāsudevaḥ kirīṭine
c tato rājan prādurāsīn mahāghoro mahāraṇaḥ
a siṃhanādaravāś cātra prādurāsan samāgame
c ubhayoḥ senayo rājan mṛtyuṃ kṛtvā nivartanam
d evam eṣa kṣayo vṛttaḥ pṛthivyāṃ pṛthivīpate
d tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca rājan durmantrite tava
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tataḥ punaḥ samājagmur abhītāḥ kurusṛñjayāḥ
c yudhiṣṭhiramukhāḥ pārthā vaikartanamukhā vayam
a tataḥ pravavṛte bhīmaḥ saṃgrāmo lomaharṣaṇaḥ
c karṇasya pāṇḍavānāṃ ca yamarāṣṭravivardhanaḥ
a tasmin pravṛtte saṃgrāme tumule śoṇitodake
c saṃśaptakeṣu śūreṣu kiṃcicchiṣṭeṣu bhārata
a dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārāja sahitaḥ sarvarājabhiḥ
c karṇam evābhidudrāva pāṇḍavāś ca mahārathāḥ
a āgacchamānāṃs tān saṃkhye prahṛṣṭān vijayaiṣiṇaḥ
c dadhāraiko raṇe karṇo jalaughān iva parvataḥ
a tam āsādya tu te karṇaṃ vyaśīryanta mahārathāḥ
c yathācalaṃ samāsādya jalaughāḥ sarvatodiśam
e tayor āsīn mahārāja saṃgrāmo lomaharṣaṇaḥ
f prayudhyator mahāraṅge balinor vijigīṣatoḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumnas tu rādheyaṃ śareṇa nataparvaṇā
c tāḍayām āsa saṃkruddhas tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt
a vijayaṃ tu dhanuḥśreṣṭhaṃ vidhunvāno mahārathaḥ
b vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi toyavarṣān ivāmbudaḥ
c pārṣatasya dhanuś chittvā śarān āśīviṣopamān
e tāḍayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ pārṣataṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
a te varma hemavikṛtaṃ bhittvā tasya mahātmanaḥ
c śoṇitāktā vyarājanta śakragopā ivānagha
a tad apāsya dhanuś chinnaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārathaḥ
c anyad dhanur upādāya śarāṃś cāśīviṣopamān
e karṇaṃ vivyādha saptatyā śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
a tathaiva rājan karṇo 'pi pārṣataṃ śatrutāpanam
b chādayām āsa samare śarair āśīviṣopamaiḥ
c droṇaśatruṃ maheṣvāso vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a tasya karṇo mahārāja śaraṃ kanakabhūṣaṇam
c preṣayām āsa saṃkruddho mṛtyudaṇḍam ivāparam
a tam āpatantaṃ sahasā ghorarūpaṃ viśāṃ pate
c ciccheda saptadhā rājañ śaineyaḥ kṛtahastavat
a dṛṣṭvā vinihitaṃ bāṇaṃ śaraiḥ karṇo viśāṃ pate
c sātyakiṃ śaravarṣeṇa samantāt paryavārayat
a vivyādha cainaṃ samare nārācais tatra saptabhiḥ
c taṃ pratyavidhyac chaineyaḥ śarair hemavibhūṣitaiḥ
a tato yuddham atīvāsīc cakṣuḥśrotrabhayāvaham
c rājan ghoraṃ ca citraṃ ca prekṣaṇīyaṃ samantataḥ
a sarveṣāṃ tatra bhūtānāṃ lomaharṣo vyajāyata
c tad dṛṣṭvā samare karma karṇaśaineyayor nṛpa
a etasminn antare drauṇir abhyayāt sumahābalam
c pārṣataṃ śatrudamanaṃ śatruvīryāsunāśanam
d sa dṛṣṭvā samare karṇaṃ pārṣataṃ ca mahāratham
a abhyabhāṣata saṃkruddho drauṇir dūre dhanaṃjaye
b rathaṃ rathena saṃpīḍya śatruvīryapraṇāśanaḥ
c tiṣṭha tiṣṭhādya brahmaghna na me jīvan vimokṣyase
a ity uktvā subhṛśaṃ vīraḥ śīghrakṛn niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c pārṣataṃ chādayām āsa ghorarūpaiḥ sutejanaiḥ
e yatamānaṃ paraṃ śaktyā yatamāno mahārathaḥ
f chādayām āsa samare yatamāno mahārathaḥ
f yatnataḥ parayā śaktyā dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ mahāraṇe
f yodhayām āsa samare kruddharūpo viśāṃ pate
a yathā hi samare drauṇiḥ pārṣataṃ vīkṣya māriṣa
c tathā drauṇiṃ raṇe dṛṣṭvā pārṣataḥ paravīrahā
e nātihṛṣṭamanā bhūtvā manyate mṛtyum ātmanaḥ
f sa jñātvā samare ''tmānaṃ śastreṇāvadhyam eva tu
f javenābhiyayau drauṇiṃ kālaḥ kālam iva kṣaye
a drauṇis tu dṛṣṭvā rājendra dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ raṇe sthitam
c krodhena niḥśvasan vīraḥ pārṣataṃ samupādravat
e tāv anyonyaṃ tu dṛṣṭvaiva saṃrambhaṃ jagmatuḥ param
f tato roṣaparītātmā dhṛṣṭadyumno 'py amarṣaṇaḥ
f provāca cainaṃ saṃrabdho droṇaputraṃ paraṃtapaḥ
f pragṛhya mahatī cāpe śarāsanavirājite
a athābravīn mahārāja droṇaputraḥ pratāpavān
c dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ samīpasthaṃ tvaramāṇo viśāṃ pate
e pāñcālāpasadādya tvāṃ preṣayiṣyāmi mṛtyave
a pāpaṃ hi yat tvayā karma ghnatā droṇaṃ purā kṛtam
c adya tvā patsyate tad vai yathā hy akuśalaṃ tathā
d pataṅgadarśanenādya darśanena vyapohyate
d śaśismaraṇatanmātrān vaṃśān kṛtam apohyate
d mayā mārayitavyas tvaṃ paśumāreṇa pārṣata
d adya śvo vā paraśvo vā satyam etad bhaviṣyati
a arakṣyamāṇaḥ pārthena yadi tiṣṭhasi saṃyuge
c nāpakramasi vā mūḍha satyam etad bravīmi te
a evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ pratāpavān
c prativākyaṃ sa evāsir māmako dāsyate tava
e yenaiva te pitur dattaṃ yatamānasya saṃyuge
f eṣa te prativākyaṃ vai asir dāsyati māmakaḥ
f yena kṛttaṃ tava pitur yatamānasya tac chiraḥ
a yadi tāvan mayā droṇo nihato brāhmaṇabruvaḥ
c tvām idānīṃ kathaṃ yuddhe na haniṣyāmi vikramāt
a evam uktvā mahārāja senāpatir amarṣaṇaḥ
c niśitenātha bāṇena drauṇiṃ vivyādha pārṣataḥ
a tato drauṇiḥ susaṃkruddhaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c prācchādayad diśo rājan dhṛṣṭadyumnasya saṃyuge
a naivāntarikṣaṃ na diśo naiva yodhāḥ samantataḥ
c dṛśyante vai mahārāja śaraiś channāḥ sahasraśaḥ
a tathaiva pārṣato rājan drauṇim āhavaśobhinam
c śaraiḥ saṃchādayām āsa sūtaputrasya paśyataḥ
a rādheyo 'pi mahārāja pāñcālān saha pāṇḍavaiḥ
c draupadeyān yudhāmanyuṃ sātyakiṃ ca mahāratham
e ekaḥ sa vārayām āsa prekṣaṇīyaḥ samantataḥ
f sātyakiṃ ca mahārāja yodhāṃś cānyān sahasraśaḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumno 'pi samare drauṇeś ciccheda kārmukam
b kṣurapreṇa sutīkṣṇena paśyatāṃ sarvayodhinām
c tad apāsya dhanuś chinnam anyad ādatta kārmukam
e vegavat samare ghoraṃ śarāṃś cāśīviṣopamān
a sa pārṣatasya rājendra dhanuḥ śaktiṃ gadāṃ dhvajam
b sa śaktiṃ prāhiṇot tasmai tāṃ drauṇir vyadhamac charaiḥ
b tāṃ nikṛttāṃ raṇe dṛṣṭvā drauṇinā pārṣato balī
b parighaṃ ghoram ādāya kārtasvaravibhūṣitam
b cikṣepa bhujavīryeṇa pārṣato vai purā nadan
b tam āpatantaṃ parighaṃ droṇaputrasya lāghavāt
b ciccheda bahudhā rājañ śarair atiratho raṇe
c hayān sūtaṃ rathaṃ caiva nimeṣād vyadhamac charaiḥ
d pārṣatasya tataḥ kruddho droṇaputraḥ paraṃtapaḥ
a sa chinnadhanvā viratho hatāśvo hatasārathiḥ
c khaḍgam ādatta vipulaṃ śatacandraṃ ca bhānumat
a drauṇis tad api rājendra bhallaiḥ kṣipraṃ mahārathaḥ
c ciccheda samare vīraḥ kṣiprahasto dṛḍhāyudhaḥ
e rathād anavarūḍhasya tad adbhutam ivābhavat
e   dhanvino bāhuśālinaḥ
e paśyatāṃ sarvasainyānāṃ
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ tu virathaṃ hatāśvaṃ chinnakārmukam
c śaraiś ca bahudhā viddham astraiś ca śakalīkṛtam
e nātarad bharataśreṣṭha yatamāno mahārathaḥ
a tasyāntam iṣubhī rājan yadā drauṇir na jagmivān
c atha tyaktvā dhanur vīraḥ pārṣataṃ tvarito 'nvagāt
d pragṛhya vipulaṃ khaḍgaṃ jātarūpapariṣkṛtam
a āsīd ādravato rājan vegas tasya mahātmanaḥ
c garuḍasyeva patato jighṛkṣoḥ pannagottamam
a etasminn eva kāle tu mādhavo 'rjunam abravīt
c paśya pārtha yathā drauṇiḥ pārṣatasya vadhaṃ prati
d etasminn eva kāle tu keśavaḥ paravīrahā
d abravīd bharataśreṣṭham arjunaṃ jayatāṃ varam
d paśya drauṇiṃ pārṣatasya yatamānaṃ vadhaṃ prati
e yatnaṃ karoti vipulaṃ hanyāc cainam asaṃśayam
a taṃ mocaya mahābāho pārṣataṃ śatrutāpanam
c drauṇer āsyam anuprāptaṃ mṛtyor āsyagataṃ yathā
a evam uktvā mahārāja vāsudevaḥ pratāpavān
c praiṣayat tatra turagān yatra drauṇir vyavasthitaḥ
a te hayāś candrasaṃkāśāḥ keśavena pracoditāḥ
c pibanta iva tad vyoma jagmur drauṇirathaṃ prati
a dṛṣṭvāyāntau mahāvīryāv ubhau kṛṣṇadhanaṃjayau
c dhṛṣṭadyumnavadhe rājaṃś cakre yatnaṃ mahābalaḥ
a vikṛṣyamāṇaṃ dṛṣṭvaiva dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ janeśvara
c śarāṃś cikṣepa vai pārtho drauṇiṃ prati mahābalaḥ
a te śarā hemavikṛtā gāṇḍīvapreṣitā bhṛśam
c drauṇim āsādya viviśur valmīkam iva pannagāḥ
a sa vidhvastaiḥ śarair ghorair droṇaputraḥ pratāpavān
b utsṛjya samare rājan pāñcālyam amitaujasam
c ratham āruruhe vīro dhanaṃjayaśarārditaḥ
e pragṛhya ca dhanuḥ śreṣṭhaṃ pārthaṃ vivyādha sāyakaiḥ
a etasminn antare vīraḥ sahadevo janādhipa
c apovāha rathenājau pārṣataṃ śatrutāpanam
a arjuno 'pi mahārāja drauṇiṃ vivyādha patribhiḥ
c taṃ droṇaputraḥ saṃkruddho bāhvor urasi cārdayat
a krodhitas tu raṇe pārtho nārācaṃ kālasaṃmitam
c droṇaputrāya cikṣepa kāladaṇḍam ivāparam
e sa brāhmaṇasyāṃsadeśe nipapāta mahādyutiḥ
a sa vihvalo mahārāja śaravegena saṃyuge
c niṣasāda rathopasthe vaiklavyaṃ ca paraṃ yayau
a tataḥ karṇo mahārāja vyākṣipad vijayaṃ dhanuḥ
c arjunaṃ samare kruddhaḥ prekṣamāṇo muhur muhuḥ
e dvairathaṃ cāpi pārthena kāmayāno mahāraṇe
a taṃ tu hitvā hataṃ vīraṃ sārathiḥ śatrukarśanam
c apovāha rathenājau tvaramāṇo raṇājirāt
a athotkruṣṭaṃ mahārāja pāñcālair jitakāśibhiḥ
c mokṣitaṃ pārṣataṃ dṛṣṭvā droṇaputraṃ ca pīḍitam
a vāditrāṇi ca divyāni prāvādyanta sahasraśaḥ
c siṃhanādaś ca saṃjajñe dṛṣṭvā ghoraṃ mahādbhutam
a evaṃ kṛtvābravīt pārtho vāsudevaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
c yāhi saṃśaptakān kṛṣṇa kāryam etat paraṃ mama
a tataḥ prayāto dāśārhaḥ śrutvā pāṇḍavabhāṣitam
c rathenātipatākena manomārutaraṃhasā
 saṃjaya uvāca
 teṣāṃ pravṛtte saṃgrāme vipule śoṇitodake
 rarāja lohitenorvī saṃraktā bahudhā bhṛśam
 tato rajasi saṃśānte rudhireṇa samantataḥ
 tadā vilokya pārthaṃ ca kṛṣṇo vacanam abravīt
a etasminn antare kṛṣṇaḥ pārthaṃ vacanam abravīt
c darśayann iva kaunteyaṃ dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
a eṣa pāṇḍava te bhrātā dhārtarāṣṭrair mahābalaiḥ
c jighāṃsubhir maheṣvāsair drutaṃ pārthānusaryate
a tathānuyānti saṃrabdhāḥ pāñcālā yuddhadurmadāḥ
c yudhiṣṭhiraṃ mahātmānaṃ parīpsanto mahājavāḥ
a eṣa duryodhanaḥ pārtha rathānīkena daṃśitaḥ
c rājā sarvasya lokasya rājānam anudhāvati
a jighāṃsuḥ puruṣavyāghraṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ sahito balī
c āśīviṣasamasparśaiḥ sarvayuddhaviśāradaiḥ
a ete jighṛkṣavo yānti dvipāśvarathapattayaḥ
c yudhiṣṭhiraṃ dhārtarāṣṭrā ratnottamam ivārthinaḥ
a paśya sātvatabhīmābhyāṃ niruddhādhiṣṭhitaḥ prabhuḥ
c jihīrṣavo 'mṛtaṃ daityāḥ śakrāgnibhyām ivāvaśāḥ
a ete bahutvāt tvaritāḥ punar gacchanti pāṇḍavam
c samudram iva vāryoghāḥ prāvṛṭkāle mahārathāḥ
a nadantaḥ siṃhanādāṃś ca dhamantaś cāpi vārijān
c balavanto maheṣvāsā vidhunvanto dhanūṃṣi ca
a mṛtyor mukhagataṃ manye kuntīputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
c hutam agnau ca bhadraṃ te duryodhanavaśaṃ gatam
a yathāyuktam anīkaṃ hi dhārtarāṣṭrasya pāṇḍava
c nāsya śakro 'pi mucyeta saṃprāpto bāṇagocaram
a duryodhanasya śūrasya drauṇeḥ śāradvatasya ca
c karṇasya ceṣuvego vai parvatān api dārayet
a duryodhanasya śūrasya śaraughāñ śīghram asyataḥ
c saṃkruddhasyāntakasyeva ko vegaṃ saṃsahed raṇe
a karṇena ca kṛto rājā vimukhaḥ śatrutāpanaḥ
c balavāṃl laghuhastaś ca kṛtī yuddhaviśāradaḥ
a rādheyaḥ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭhaṃ śaktaḥ pīḍayituṃ raṇe
c sahito dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putraiḥ śūro mahātmabhiḥ
a tasyaivaṃ yudhyamānasya saṃgrāme saṃyatātmanaḥ
c anyair api ca pārthasya hṛtaṃ varma mahārathaiḥ
a upavāsakṛśo rājā bhṛśaṃ bharatasattama
c brāhme bale sthito hy eṣa na kṣatre 'tibale vibho
d karme sute kṛtaṃ rāṣṭraṃ jīvitaṃ śatrutāpanaḥ
d nityānaśanasaṃgrāme samāptavrataniścayaḥ
d yo vatsodayikaṃ śrāddhe viśeṣeṇa mahībhujā
d karṇena cābhiyukto 'yaṃ bhūpatiḥ śatrutāpanaḥ
d saṃśayaṃ samanuprāptaḥ pāṇḍavo vai yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a na jīvati mahārājo manye pārtha yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c yad bhīmasenaḥ sahate siṃhanādam amarṣaṇaḥ
a nardatāṃ dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ punaḥ punar ariṃdama
c dhamatāṃ ca mahāśaṅkhān saṃgrāme jitakāśinām
a yudhiṣṭhiraṃ pāṇḍaveyaṃ hateti bharatarṣabha
c saṃcodayaty asau karṇo dhārtarāṣṭrān mahābalān
d astrair nānāvidhaiś citraiḥ kauravāḥ pārtha saṃyuge
a sthūṇākarṇendrajālena pārtha pāśupatena ca
c pracchādayanto rājānam anuyānti mahārathāḥ
e āturo me mato rājā saṃniṣevyaś ca bhārata
a yathainam anuvartante pāñcālāḥ saha pāṇḍavaiḥ
c tvaramāṇās tvarākāle sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varāḥ
e majjantam iva pātāle balino 'py ujjihīrṣavaḥ
a na ketur dṛśyate rājñaḥ karṇena nihataḥ śaraiḥ
c paśyator yamayoḥ pārtha sātyakeś ca śikhaṇḍinaḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumnasya bhīmasya śatānīkasya vā vibho
c pāñcālānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ cedīnāṃ caiva bhārata
a eṣa karṇo raṇe pārtha pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm
c śarair vidhvaṃsayati vai nalinīm iva kuñjaraḥ
a ete dravanti rathinas tvadīyāḥ pāṇḍunandana
b drāvyamāṇā raṇe pārtha karṇenāmitatejasā
c paśya paśya yathā pārtha gacchanty ete mahārathāḥ
a ete bhārata mātaṅgāḥ karṇenābhihatā raṇe
c ārtanādān vikurvāṇā vidravanti diśo daśa
a rathānāṃ dravatāṃ vṛndaṃ paśya pārtha samantataḥ
c drāvyamāṇaṃ raṇe caiva karṇenāmitrakarśinā
a hastikakṣyāṃ raṇe paśya carantīṃ tatra tatra ha
c rathasthaṃ sūtaputrasya ketuṃ ketumatāṃ vara
a asau dhāvati rādheyo bhīmasenarathaṃ prati
c kirañ śaraśatānīva vinighnaṃs tava vāhinīm
a etān paśya ca pāñcālān drāvyamāṇān mahātmanā
c śakreṇeva yathā daityān hanyamānān mahāhave
a eṣa karṇo raṇe jitvā pāñcālān pāṇḍusṛñjayān
c diśo viprekṣate sarvās tvadartham iti me matiḥ
a paśya pārtha dhanuḥ śreṣṭhaṃ vikarṣan sādhu śobhate
c śatrūñ jitvā yathā śakro devasaṃghaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ
a ete nadanti kauravyā dṛṣṭvā karṇasya vikramam
c trāsayanto raṇe pārthān sṛñjayāṃś ca sahasraśaḥ
a eṣa sarvātmanā pāṇḍūṃs trāsayitvā mahāraṇe
b trāsayitvā raṇe pārtha rādheyo rathināṃ varaḥ
c abhibhāṣati rādheyaḥ sarvasainyāni mānadaḥ
a abhidravata gacchadhvaṃ drutaṃ dravata kauravāḥ
c yathā jīvan na vaḥ kaś cin mucyate yudhi sṛñjayaḥ
a tathā kuruta saṃyattā vayaṃ yāsyāma pṛṣṭhataḥ
c evam uktvā yayāv eṣa pṛṣṭhato vikirañ śaraiḥ
d rādheyaḥ kauravīṃ senāṃ rakṣamāṇaḥ samantataḥ
a paśya karṇaṃ raṇe pārtha śvetacchavivirājitam
c udayaṃ parvataṃ yadvac chobhayan vai divākaraḥ
a pūrṇacandranikāśena mūrdhni chatreṇa bhārata
c dhriyamāṇena samare tathā śataśalākinā

c uttamaṃ yatnam āsthāya dhruvam eṣyati saṃyuge
a paśya hy enaṃ mahābāho vidhunvānaṃ mahad dhanuḥ

a asau nivṛtto rādheyo dṛśyate vānaradhvaja
b prārthayan samaraṃ pārtha tvayā saha paraṃtapa
c vadhāya cātmano 'bhyeti dīpasya śalabho yathā
d eṣa hy amarṣī śūraś ca dhārtarāṣṭrahite rataḥ
d tvāṃ na marṣayate pārtha nityam eva sumandadhīḥ
d ekākinaṃ ca dṛṣṭvainaṃ dhārtarāṣṭro raṇājire
d tvāṃ ca pārthābhisaṃrabdhaṃ karṇaṃ prati mahāratham
a karṇam ekākinaṃ dṛṣṭvā rathānīkena bhārata
b asau duryodhanaḥ kruddho rathānīkena daṃśitaḥ
c rirakṣiṣuḥ susaṃyatto dhārtarāṣṭro 'bhivartate
a sārvaiḥ sahaibhir duṣṭātmā vadhya eṣa prayatnataḥ
b adīnayor viśrutayor yuvayor yotsyamānayoḥ
b devāsure pārtha mṛdhe devadānavayor iva
b paśyantu kauravāḥ sarve tava pārtha parākramam
b tvāṃ ca dṛṣṭvātisaṃrabdhaṃ karṇaṃ ca bharatarṣabha
b asau duryodhanaḥ kruddho nottaraṃ pratipadyate
c tvayā yaśaś ca rājyaṃ ca sukhaṃ cottamam icchatā
a ātmānaṃ ca kṛtātmānaṃ samīkṣya bharatarṣabha
c kṛtāgasaṃ ca rādheyaṃ dharmātmani yudhiṣṭhire
d sahitaḥ sa tu duṣṭātmā dhārtarāṣṭro 'bhyavartate
d eṣa eva nihantavyo mūlaṃ vairasya bhārata
d mūle chinne yathā nāśaḥ śākhānāṃ jāyate dhruvam
d tathā duryodhane pārtha hate syur akhilā hatāḥ
d dhārtarāṣṭrā mahābāho sabhṛtyāmātyabāndhavāḥ
d paśya sarve yathā yodhā yānti bhīmarathaṃ prati
d bhīmo 'pi śeroṣatāmrākṣo hanti śatrūn aśeṣataḥ
d eṣa dharmasuto rājā yamābhyāṃ paripālitaḥ
d duryodhano 'pi karṇena rakṣyate sasutena ca
d kṛtavarmā kṛpo drauṇī rakṣanto 'nyonyam uttamāḥ
d kulūkaḥ śakuniś caiva kṛtvā rakṣāṃ sthitāv ubhau
a pratipadyasva rādheyaṃ prāptakālam anantaram
c āryāṃ yuddhe matiṃ kṛtvā pratyehi rathayūthapam
a pañca hy etāni mukhyānāṃ rathānāṃ rathasattama
c śatāny āyānti vegena balināṃ bhīmatejasām
a pañca nāgasahasrāṇi dviguṇā vājinas tathā
c abhisaṃhatya kaunteya padātiprayutāni ca
e anyonyarakṣitaṃ vīra balaṃ tvām abhivartate
f droṇaputraṃ puraskṛtya tataḥ śīghraṃ ca sūdaya
f nikṛtyaitad rathānīkaṃ balinaṃ lokaviśrutam
a sūtaputre maheṣvāse darśayātmānam ātmanā
c uttamaṃ yatnam āsthāya pratyehi bharatarṣabha
d bhūtāni caiva sarvāṇi kurupāñcālasṛñjayāḥ
a asau karṇaḥ susaṃrabdhaḥ pāñcālān abhidhāvati
c ketum asya hi paśyāmi dhṛṣṭadyumnarathaṃ prati
e samucchetsyati pāñcālān iti manye paraṃtapa
a ācakṣe te priyaṃ pārtha tad evaṃ bharatarṣabha
c rājā jīvati kauravyo dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a asau bhimo mahābāhuḥ saṃnivṛttaś camūmukhe
c vṛtaḥ sṛñjayasainyena sātyakena ca bhārata
a vadhyanta ete samare kauravā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c bhīmasenena kaunteya pāñcālaiś ca mahātmabhiḥ
a senā hi dhārtarāṣṭrasya vimukhā cābhavad raṇāt
c vipradhāvati vegena bhīmasya nihatā śaraiḥ
a vipannasasyeva mahī rudhireṇa samukṣitā
c bhāratī bharataśreṣṭha senā kṛpaṇadarśanā
a nivṛttaṃ paśya kaunteya bhīmasenaṃ yudhāṃ patim
c āśīviṣam iva kruddhaṃ tasmād dravati vāhinī
a pītaraktāsitasitās tārācandrārkamaṇḍitāḥ
c patākā viprakīryante chatrāṇy etāni cārjuna
a sauvarṇā rājatāś caiva taijasāś ca pṛthagvidhāḥ
c ketavo vinipātyante hastyaśvaṃ viprakīryate
a rathebhyaḥ prapatanty ete rathino vigatāsavaḥ
c nānāvarṇair hatā bāṇaiḥ pāñcālair apalāyibhiḥ
a nirmanuṣyān gajān aśvān rathāṃś caiva dhanaṃjaya
c samādravanti pāñcālā dhārtarāṣṭrāṃs tarasvinaḥ
a mṛdnanti ca naravyāghrā bhīmasenavyapāśrayāt
c balaṃ pareṣāṃ durdharṣaṃ tyaktvā prāṇān ariṃdama
a ete nadanti pāñcālā dhamanty api ca vārijān
c abhidravanti ca raṇe nighnantaḥ sāyakaiḥ parān
a paśya svargasya māhātmyaṃ pāñcālā hi paraṃtapa
c dhārtarāṣṭrān vinighnanti kruddhāḥ siṃhā iva dvipān
d śastram ācchidya śatrūṇāṃ sāyudhānāṃ nirāyudhāḥ
d tenaivaitān amoghāstrā nighnanti ca nadanti ca
d śirāṃsy etāni pātyante śatrūṇāṃ bāhavo 'pi ca
d rathanāgahayā vīrā yaśasyāḥ sarva eva ca
a sarvataś cābhipannaiṣā dhārtarāṣṭrī mahācamūḥ
b pāñcālair māgadhaiś caiva yodhā nītā yamakṣayam
b tyaktvā prāṇān maheṣvāsaiḥ pāñcālaiḥ paripātyate
c pāñcālair mānasād etya haṃsair gaṅgeva vegitaiḥ
a subhṛśaṃ ca parākrāntāḥ pāñcālānāṃ nivāraṇe
c kṛpakarṇādayo vīrā ṛṣabhāṇām ivarṣabhāḥ
d suhṛdaś ca parākrāntāḥ kṛpakarṇādayo vibho
d nivāraṇe maheṣvāsāḥ pāñcālānāṃ paraṃtapa
a sunimagnāṃś ca bhīmāstrair dhārtarāṣṭrān mahārathān
c dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhā vīrā ghnanti śatrūn sahasraśaḥ
d pāñcāleṣv abhibhūteṣu dviṣadbhir apabhīr nadan
d śatrupakṣam avaskandya śarān asyati mārutiḥ
d rathāś ca vimukhāḥ sarve nivṛtte bharatarṣabhe
e viṣaṇṇabhūyiṣṭharathā dhārtarāṣṭrī mahācamūḥ
f rathāś caite suvitrastā bhīmasenabhayārditāḥ
a paśya bhīmena nārācaiś chinnā nāgāḥ patanty amī
b nānā nāgā hatā bāṇair bhīmena prapatanty amī
c vajrivajrāhatānīva śikharāṇi mahībhṛtām
d bhīmasenena mātaṅgāḥ prāpitā yamasādanam
d girīṇāṃ śikharāṇīva nipatanti nararṣabha
a bhīmasenasya nirviddhā bāṇaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c svāny anīkāni mṛdnanto dravanty ete mahāgajāḥ
d ete dravanti kuravo bhīmasenabhayārditāḥ
d tyaktvā rathān gajāṃś caiva hayāṃś caiva sahasraśaḥ
d hastyaśvarathapattīnaṃ dravatāṃ nisvanaṃ śṛṇu
d bhīmasenasya ninadaṃ drāvayāṇasya kauravān
a nābhijānāsi bhīmasya siṃhanādaṃ durutsaham
c nadato 'rjuna saṃgrāme vīrasya jitakāśinaḥ
a eṣa naiṣādir abhyeti dvipamukhyena pāṇḍavam
c jighāṃsus tomaraiḥ kruddho daṇḍapāṇir ivāntakaḥ
a satomarāv asya bhujau chinnau bhīmena garjataḥ
c tīkṣṇair agniśikhāprakhyair nārācair daśabhir hataḥ
a hatvainaṃ punar āyāti nāgān anyān prahāriṇaḥ
c paśya nīlāmbudanibhān mahāmātrair adhiṣṭhitān
e śaktitomarasaṃkāśair vinighnantaṃ vṛkodaram
a sapta sapta ca nāgāṃs tān vaijayantīś ca sadhvajāḥ
c nihatya niśitair bāṇaiś chinnāḥ pārthāgrajena te
e daśabhir daśabhiś caiko nārācair nihato gajaḥ
a na cāsau dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ śrūyate ninadas tathā
c puraṃdarasame kruddhe nivṛtte bharatarṣabhe
a akṣauhiṇyas tathā tisro dhārtarāṣṭrasya saṃhatāḥ
c kruddhena narasiṃhena bhīmasenena vāritāḥ
d na śaknuvanti vai pārthaṃ pārthivāḥ samudīkṣitum
d madhyaṃdinagataṃ sūryaṃ yathā durbalacakṣuṣaḥ
d ete bhīmasya saṃtrastāḥ siṃhasyevetare mṛgāḥ
d śaraiḥ saṃtrāsitāḥ saṃkhye na labhante sukhaṃ kva cit
d rājānaṃ ca mahābāhuṃ pīḍayanty āttamanyavaḥ
d rādheyo bahubhiḥ sārdham asau gacchati vegitaḥ
d varjayitvā tu bhīruṃ taṃ pārśvato hy ānayad dhanuḥ
d taṃ pālayan mahārājaṃ dhārtarāṣṭro balānvitaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
 etac chrutvā mahābāhur vāsudevād dhanaṃjayaḥ
a bhīmasenena tat karma kṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā suduṣkaram
c arjuno vyadhamac chiṣṭān ahitān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a te vadhyamānāḥ samare saṃśaptakagaṇāḥ prabho
b prabhagnāḥ samare bhītāḥ diśo daśa mahābalāḥ
c śakrasyātithitāṃ gatvā viśokā hy abhavan mudā
d śakrasyātithitāṃ prāptāḥ samapadyanta vijvarāḥ
d viśokāḥ samapadyanta śakrasyāntikatāṃ gatāḥ
d nārāyaṇāṃs tu gopālān vyadhamat pāṇḍunandanaḥ
d uttamaṃ vegam āsthāya caṇḍavāyur ghanān iva
d anvakīryanta bhītās te tatra tatraiva bhārata
d lulitāṃś ca tataḥ śūrān ahanat puruṣottamaḥ
a pārthaś ca puruṣavyāghraḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c jaghāna dhārtarāṣṭrasya caturvidhabalāṃ camūm
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a nivṛtte bhīmasene ca pāṇḍave ca yudhiṣṭhire
c vadhyamāne bale cāpi māmake pāṇḍusṛñjayaiḥ
a dravamāṇe balaughe ca nirākrande muhur muhuḥ
b avaśeṣaṃ na paśyāmi mama sainyeṣu saṃjaya
b aho bata daśāṃ prāpto na hi śakṣyāmi jīvitum
b jayakāṅkṣī kathaṃ sūta putrāṇām anivartinām
b kathaṃ jīvāmi nihatāñ śrutvā ca mama sainikān
b bahunādya kim uktena daivaṃ teṣāṃ parāyaṇam
c kim akurvanta kuravas tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
 saṃjaya uvāca
 kṣayas teṣāṃ mahāñ jāto rājan durmantrite tava
a dṛṣṭvā bhīmaṃ mahābāhuṃ sūtaputraḥ pratāpavān
c krodharaktekṣaṇo rājan bhīmasenam upādravat
d tiṣṭha tiṣṭha pṛthāputra paśya me 'dya parākramam
d adya tvāṃ preṣayiṣyāmi yamasya sadanaṃ prati
d ity uktvā prayayau tūrṇaṃ yatra bhīmo vyavasthitaḥ
a tāvakaṃ ca balaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenāt parāṅmukham
c yatnena mahatā rājan paryavasthāpayad balī
a vyavasthāpya mahābāhus tava putrasya vāhinīm
c pratyudyayau tadā karṇaḥ pāṇḍavān yuddhadurmadān
a pratyudyayus tu rādheyaṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥ
c dhunvānāḥ kārmukāṇy ājau vikṣipantaś ca sāyakān
a bhīmasenaḥ śiner naptā śikhaṇḍī janamejayaḥ
c dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca balavān sarve cāpi prabhadrakāḥ
a pāñcālāś ca naravyāghrāḥ samantāt tava vāhinīm
c abhyadravanta saṃkruddhāḥ samare jitakāśinaḥ
a tathaiva tāvakā rājan pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm
c abhyadravanta tvaritā jighāṃsanto mahārathāḥ
a rathanāgāśvakalilaṃ pattidhvajasamākulam
c babhūva puruṣavyāghra sainyam adbhutadarśanam
a śikhaṇḍī ca yayau karṇaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ sutaṃ tava
c duḥśāsanaṃ mahārāja mahatyā senayā vṛtam
a nakulo vṛṣasenaṃ ca citrasenaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c ulūkaṃ samare rājan sahadevaḥ samabhyayāt
a sātyakiḥ śakuniṃ cāpi bhīmasenaś ca kauravān
c arjunaṃ ca raṇe yattaṃ droṇaputro mahārathaḥ
a yudhāmanyuṃ maheṣvāsaṃ gautamo 'bhyapatad raṇe
c kṛtavarmā ca balavān uttamaujasam ādravat
d yudhāmanyuṃ kṛpo rājann uttamaujasam āhave
d kṛtavarmā maheṣvāsaḥ paryavārayad āhave
a bhīmasenaḥ kurūn sarvān putrāṃś ca tava māriṣa
c sahānīkān mahābāhur eka evābhyavārayat
a śikhaṇḍī ca tataḥ karṇaṃ vicarantam abhītavat
c bhīṣmahantā mahārāja vārayām āsa patribhiḥ
a pratirabdhas tataḥ karṇo roṣāt prasphuritādharaḥ
c śikhaṇḍinaṃ tribhir bāṇair bhruvor madhye vyatāḍayat
a dhārayaṃs tu sa tān bāṇāñ śikhaṇḍī bahv aśobhata
c rājataḥ parvato yadvat tribhiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ samanvitaḥ
a so 'tividdho maheṣvāsaḥ sūtaputreṇa saṃyuge
c karṇaṃ vivyādha samare navatyā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a tasya karṇo hayān hatvā sārathiṃ ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
c unmamātha dhvajaṃ cāsya kṣurapreṇa mahārathaḥ
a hatāśvāt tu tato yānād avaplutya mahārathaḥ
b saṃchinnakārmuko rājan sūtaputreṇa saṃyuge
c śaktiṃ cikṣepa karṇāya saṃkruddhaḥ śatrutāpanaḥ
a tāṃ chittvā samare karṇas tribhir bhārata sāyakaiḥ
c śikhaṇḍinam athāvidhyan navabhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a karṇacāpacyutān bāṇān varjayaṃs tu narottamaḥ
c apayātas tatas tūrṇaṃ śikhaṇḍī jayatāṃ varaḥ
a tataḥ karṇo mahārāja pāṇḍusainyāny aśātayat
c tūlarāśiṃ samāsādya yathā vāyur mahājavaḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārāja tava putreṇa pīḍitaḥ
c duḥśāsanaṃ tribhir bāṇair abhyavidhyat stanāntare
a tasya duḥśāsano bāhuṃ savyaṃ vivyādha māriṣa
c śitena rukmapuṅkhena bhallena nataparvaṇā
a dhṛṣṭadyumnas tu nirviddhaḥ śaraṃ ghoram amarṣaṇaḥ
c duḥśāsanāya saṃkruddhaḥ preṣayām āsa bhārata
d āśīviṣasamaṃ bāṇam āśu mārutaraṃhasam
a āpatantaṃ mahāvegaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnasamīritam
c śaraiś ciccheda putras te tribhir eva viśāṃ pate
a athāparaiḥ saptadaśair bhallaiḥ kanakabhūṣaṇaiḥ
c dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ samāsādya bāhvor urasi cārdayat
a tataḥ sa pārṣataḥ kruddho dhanuś ciccheda māriṣa
c kṣurapreṇa sutīkṣṇena tata uccukruśur janāḥ
a athānyad dhanur ādāya putras te bharatarṣabha
c dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ śaravrātaiḥ samantāt paryavārayat
a tava putrasya te dṛṣṭvā vikramaṃ taṃ mahātmanaḥ
c vyahasanta raṇe yodhāḥ siddhāś cāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ
d dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ na paśyāma ghaṭamānaṃ mahābalam
d duḥśāsanena saṃruddhaṃ siṃheneva mahāgajam
d tataḥ sarathanāgāśvāḥ pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍupūrvaja
d senāpatiṃ parīpsanto rurudhus tanayaṃ tava
a tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ tāvakānāṃ paraiḥ saha
c ghoraṃ prāṇabhṛtāṃ kāle ghorarūpaṃ paraṃtapa
a nakulaṃ vṛṣasenas tu viddhvā pañcabhir āyasaiḥ
c pituḥ samīpe tiṣṭhantaṃ tribhir anyair avidhyata
a nakulas tu tataḥ kruddho vṛṣasenaṃ smayann iva
c nārācena sutīkṣṇena vivyādha hṛdaye dṛḍham
a so 'tividdho balavatā śatruṇā śatrukarśanaḥ
c śatruṃ vivyādha viṃśatyā sa ca taṃ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ
a tataḥ śarasahasreṇa tāv ubhau puruṣarṣabhau
c anyonyam ācchādayatām athābhajyata vāhinī
a dṛṣṭvā tu pradrutāṃ senāṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya sūtajaḥ
c nivārayām āsa balād anupatya viśāṃ pate
d etasminn antare kaṣṭaṃ yuddham āsīd viśāṃ pate
e nivṛtte tu tataḥ karṇe nakulaḥ kauravān yayau
f vṛṣasenas tu pāñcālān pitrā sārdhaṃ viśāṃ pate
a karṇaputras tu samare hitvā nakulam eva tu
c jugopa cakraṃ tvaritaṃ rādheyasyaiva māriṣa
a ulūkas tu raṇe kruddhaḥ sahadevena vāritaḥ
b nivāritaḥ śaraśataiḥ kruddhena raṇamūrdhani
c tasyāśvāṃś caturo hatvā sahadevaḥ pratāpavān
e sārathiṃ preṣayām āsa yamasya sadanaṃ prati
a ulūkas tu tato yānād avaplutya viśāṃ pate
b apayātas tatas tūrṇam ulūko raṇamūrdhani
c trigartānāṃ balaṃ pūrṇaṃ jagāma pitṛnandanaḥ
d ratham anyaṃ samāsthāya jagāma pitur antikam
a sātyakiḥ śakuniṃ viddhvā viṃśatyā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c dhvajaṃ ciccheda bhallena saubalasya hasann iva
a saubalas tasya samare kruddho rājan pratāpavān
b sārathiṃ preṣayām āsa yamasya sadanaṃ prati
c vidārya kavacaṃ bhūyo dhvajaṃ ciccheda kāñcanam
a athainaṃ niśitair bāṇaiḥ sātyakiḥ pratyavidhyata
c sārathiṃ ca mahārāja tribhir eva samārdayat
e athāsya vāhāṃs tvaritaḥ śarair ninye yamakṣayam
a tato 'vaplutya sahasā śakunir bharatarṣabha
c āruroha rathaṃ tūrṇam ulūkasya mahārathaḥ
e apovāhātha śīghraṃ sa śaineyād yuddhaśālinaḥ
f apovāha rathasthaṃ taṃ sātyakasyājisāgarāt
a sātyakis tu raṇe rājaṃs tāvakānām anīkinīm
c abhidudrāva vegena tato 'nīkam abhidyata
a śaineyaśaranunnaṃ tu tataḥ sainyaṃ viśāṃ pate
c bheje daśa diśas tūrṇaṃ nyapatac ca gatāsuvat
a bhīmasenaṃ tava suto vārayām āsa saṃyuge
c taṃ tu bhīmo muhūrtena vyaśvasūtarathadhvajam
e cakre lokeśvaraṃ tatra tenātuṣyanta cāraṇāḥ
f śatruṇā vijitaṃ jñātvā bhayāt supuruṣarṣabha
a tato 'pāyān nṛpas tatra bhīmasenasya gocarāt
c kurusainyaṃ tataḥ sarvaṃ bhīmasenam upādravat
e tatra rāvo mahān āsīd bhīmam ekaṃ jighāṃsatām
a yudhāmanyuḥ kṛpaṃ viddhvā dhanur asyāśu cicchide
c athānyad dhanur ādāya kṛpaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
a yudhāmanyor dhvajaṃ sūtaṃ chatraṃ cāpātayat kṣitau
c tato 'pāyād rathenaiva yudhāmanyur mahārathaḥ
a uttamaujās tu hārdikyaṃ śarair bhīmaparākramam
c chādayām āsa sahasā megho vṛṣṭyā yathācalam
a tad yuddhaṃ sumahac cāsīd ghorarūpaṃ paraṃtapa
c yādṛśaṃ na mayā yuddhaṃ dṛṣṭapūrvaṃ viśāṃ pate
a kṛtavarmā tato rājann uttamaujasam āhave
c hṛdi vivyādha sa tadā rathopastha upāviśat
a sārathis tam apovāha rathena rathināṃ varam
c tatas tu satvaraṃ rājan pāṇḍusainyam upādravat
d kurusainyaṃ tataḥ sarvaṃ bhīmasenam upādravat
d yudhiṣṭhiraś citrasenaṃ śaravarṣair avākirat
d citraseno 'pi kaunteyaṃ saṃkruddhaḥ samavārayat
d muhūrtād vimukhīkṛtya citrasenaṃ sa dharmarāṭ
d tāvakaṃ sainyam abhyaghnat samantān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
d tasmin pravṛtte tumule naravīrajanakṣaye
d duryodhanaḥ krodham upetya tīvraṃ
d krodhāgnināsau paridahyamānaḥ
d anyaṃ rathaṃ samupetyāśu caiva
d bhīmaṃ pravivyādha sucitrapuṅkhaiḥ
d duḥśāsano 'dyāpi ca citraseno
d durdyūtasevī kitavaḥ saubalaś ca
d gajānīkaiḥ sarvato bhīmasenaṃ
d tathābhyarditaṃ sahasābhyadhāvat
d tāvakāś ca mahābāho duryodhanapurogamāḥ
d yudhiṣṭhiraṃ jighṛkṣantaḥ sarvasainyam avākṣipan
d duḥśāsanaḥ saubalaś ca gajānīkena pāṇḍavam
d mahatā parivāryaiva kṣudrakair abhyatāḍayat
d tato bhīmaḥ śaraśatair duryodhanam amarṣaṇam
d vimukhīkṛtya tarasā gajānīkam upādravat
d tam āpatantaṃ sahasā gajānīkaṃ vṛkodaraḥ
d dṛṣṭvaiva subhṛśaṃ kruddho divyam astram udairayat
d gajair gajān abhyahanad vajreṇendra ivāsurān
d tato 'ntarikṣaṃ bāṇaughaiḥ śalabhair iva pādapam
d chādayām āsa samare gajān nighnan vṛkodaraḥ
d tataḥ kuñjarayūthāni sametāni sahasraśaḥ
d vyadhamat tarasā bhīmo meghasaṃghān ivānilaḥ
d suvarṇajālāpihitā maṇijālaiś ca kuñjarāḥ
d rejur abhyadhikaṃ saṃkhye vidyutvanta ivāmbudāḥ
d te vadhyamānā bhīmena gajā rājan vidudruvuḥ
d ke cid vibhinnahṛdayāḥ kuñjarā nyapatan bhuvi
d patitair nipatadbhiś ca gajair hemavibhūṣitaiḥ
d aśobhata mahī tatra viśīrṇair iva parvataiḥ
d dīptābhai ratnavadbhiś ca patitair gajayodhibhiḥ
d rarāja bhūmiḥ patitaiḥ kṣīṇapuṇyair iva grahaiḥ
d tato bhinnakaṭā nāgā bhinnakumbhakarās tathā
d dudruvuḥ śataśaḥ saṃkhye bhīmasenaśarāhatāḥ
d ke cid vamanto rudhiraṃ bhayārtāḥ parvatopamāḥ
d vyadravañ śaraviddhāṅgā dhātucitrā ivācalāḥ
d mahābhujagasaṃkāśau candanāgarurūṣitau
d apaśyaṃ bhīmasenasya dhanur vikṣipato bhujau
d tasya jyātalanirghoṣaṃ śrutvāśanisamasvanam
d vimuñcantaḥ śakṛnmūtraṃ gajāḥ prādudruvur bhṛśam
d bhīmasenasya tat karma rājann ekasya dhīmataḥ
d nighnataḥ sarvabhūtāni rudrasyeva ca nirbabhau
d saṃjaya uvāca
d tataḥ śvetāśvasaṃyukte nārāyaṇasamāhite
d tiṣṭhan rathavare śrīmān arjunaḥ samapadyata
d tad balaṃ nṛpatiśreṣṭha tāvakaṃ vijayo raṇe
d vyakṣobhayad udīrṇāśvaṃ mahodadhim ivānalaḥ
d duryodhanas tava sutaḥ pramatte śvetavāhane
d abhyetya sahasā kruddhaḥ sainyārdhenābhisaṃvṛtaḥ
d paryavārayad āyāntaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram amarṣaṇam
d kṣuraprāṇāṃ trisaptatyā tato 'vidhyata pāṇḍavam
d akrudhyata bhṛśaṃ tatra kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d sa bhallāṃs triṃśatas tūrṇaṃ tava putre nyaveśayat
d tato 'dhāvanta kauravyā jighṛkṣanto yudhiṣṭhiram
d duṣṭabhāvān parāñ jñātvā samavetā mahārathāḥ
d ājagmus taṃ parīpsaṃtaḥ kuntīputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
d nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥ
d akṣauhiṇyā parivṛtās te 'bhyadhāvan yudhiṣṭhiram
d bhīmasenaś ca samare mṛdnaṃs tava mahārathān
d abhyadhāvad abhiprepsū rājānaṃ śatrubhir vṛtam
d tāṃs tu sarvān maheṣvāsān karṇo vaikartano nṛpa
d śaravarṣeṇa mahatā pratyavārayad āgatān
d śaraughān visṛjantas te prerayantaś ca tomarān
d na śekur yatnavanto 'pi rādheyaṃ prativīkṣitum
d tāṃś ca sarvān maheṣvāsān sarvaśastrāstrapāragaḥ
d mahatā śaravarṣeṇa rādheyaḥ pratyavārayat
d duryodhanaṃ tu viṃśatyā śīghram astram udīrayan
d avidhyat tūrṇam abhyetya sahadevo mahāmanāḥ
d sa viddhaḥ sahadevena rarājācalasaṃnibhaḥ
d prabhinna iva mātaṅgo rudhireṇa pariplutaḥ
d dṛṣṭvā tava sutaṃ tatra gāḍhaviddhaṃ sutejanaiḥ
d abhyadhāvad dṛḍhaṃ kruddho rādheyo rathināṃ varaḥ
d duryodhanaṃ tathā dṛṣṭvā śīghram astram udīrya saḥ
d tena yaudhiṣṭhiraṃ sainyam avadhīt pārṣataṃ tathā
d tato yaudhiṣṭhiraṃ sainyaṃ vadhyamānaṃ mahātmanā
d sahasā prādravad rājan sūtaputraśarārditam
d vividhā viśikhās tatra saṃpatantaḥ parasparam
d phalaiḥ puṅkhān samājaghnuḥ sūtaputradhanuścyutāḥ
d antarikṣe śaraughāṇāṃ patatāṃ ca parasparam
d saṃgharṣeṇa mahārāja pāvakaḥ samajāyata
d tato daśa diśaḥ karṇaḥ śalabhair iva yāyibhiḥ
d abhyaghnaṃs tarasā rājañ śaraiḥ paraśarīragaiḥ
d raktacandanasaṃdigdhau maṇihemavibhūṣitau
d bāhū vyatyakṣipat karṇaḥ paramāstraṃ vidarśayan
d tataḥ sarvā diśo rājan sāyakair vipramohayan
d apīḍayad bhṛśaṃ karṇo dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
d tataḥ kruddho mahārāja dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d niśitair iṣubhiḥ karṇaṃ pañcāśadbhiḥ samārpayat
d bāṇāndhakāram abhavat tad yuddhaṃ ghoradarśanam
d hāhākāro mahān āsīt tāvakānāṃ viśāṃ pate
d vadhyamāne tadā sainye dharmaputreṇa māriṣa
d sāyakair vividhais tīkṣṇaiḥ kaṅkapatraiḥ śilāśitaiḥ
d bhallair anekair vividhaiḥ śaktyṛṣṭimusalair api
d yatra yatra sa dharmātmā duṣṭāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ vyasarjayat
d tatra tatra vyaśīryanta tāvakā bharatarṣabha
d karṇo 'pi bhṛśasaṃkruddho dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
d nārācair ardhacandraiś ca vatsadantaiś ca saṃyuge
d amarṣī krodhanaś caiva roṣaprasphuritānanaḥ
d sāyakair aprameyātmā yudhiṣṭhiram abhidravat
d yudhiṣṭhiraś cāpi śataṃ svarṇapuṅkhaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
d prahasann iva taṃ karṇaḥ kaṅkapatraiḥ śilāśitaiḥ
d urasy avidhyad rājānaṃ tribhir bhallaiś ca pāṇḍavam
d sa pīḍito bhṛśaṃ tena dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d upaviśya rathopasthe sūtaṃ yāhīty acodayat
d prākrośanta tataḥ sarve dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ sarājakāḥ
d gṛhīdhvam iti rājānam abhyadhāvanta sarvaśaḥ
d tataḥ śatāḥ saptadaśa kekayānāṃ prahāriṇām
d pāñcālaiḥ sahitā rājan dhārtarāṣṭrān nyavārayan
d tasmin sutumule yuddhe vartamāne janakṣaye
d duryodhanaś ca bhīmaś ca sameyātāṃ mahābalau
d karṇo 'tha śarajālena kekayānāṃ mahārathān
d vyadhamat parameṣvāsān agrataḥ paryavasthitān
d teṣāṃ prayatamānānāṃ rādheyasya nivāraṇe
d rathān pañcaśatān karṇaḥ prāhiṇod yamasādanam
d aviṣahyaṃ tato dṛṣṭvā rādheyaṃ yudhi yodhinaḥ
d bhīmasenam upāgacchan karṇabāṇaprapīḍitāḥ
d rathānīkaṃ vidāryaiva śarajālair anekadhā
d karṇa ekarathenaiva yudhiṣṭhiram upādravat
d senāniveśam ārchantaṃ mārgaṇaiḥ kṣatavikṣatam
d yamayor madhyagaṃ vīraṃ śanair yāntaṃ vicetasam
d samāsādya tu rājānaṃ duryodhanahitepsayā
d sūtaputras tribhis tīkṣṇair vivyādha parameṣubhiḥ
d tathaiva rājā rādheyaṃ pratyavidhyat stanāntare
d śarais tribhiś ca yantāraṃ caturbhiś caturo hayān
d cakrarakṣau tu pārthasya mādrīputrau paraṃtapau
d tāv apy adhāvatāṃ karṇaṃ rājānaṃ mā vadhīr iti
d tau pṛthak śaravarṣābhyāṃ rādheyam abhyavarṣatām
d nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca paramaṃ yatnam āsthitau
d tathaiva tau pratyavidhyat sūtaputraḥ pratāpavān
d bhallābhyāṃ śitadhārābhyāṃ mahātmānāv ariṃdamau
d dantavarṇāṃs tu rādheyo nijaghāna manojavān
d yudhiṣṭhirasya saṃgrāme kālavālān hayottamān
d tato 'pareṇa bhallena śirastrāṇam apātayat
d kaunteyasya maheṣvāsaḥ prahasann iva sūtajaḥ
d tathaiva nakulasyāpi hayān hatvā pratāpavān
d īṣāṃ dhanuś ca ciccheda mādrīputrasya dhīmataḥ
d tau hatāśvau hatarathau pāṇḍavau bhṛśavikṣatau
d bhrātarāv āruruhatuḥ sahadevarathaṃ tadā
d tau dṛṣṭvā mātulas tatra virathau paravīrahā
d abhyabhāṣata rādheyaṃ madrarājo 'nukampayā
d yoddhavyam adya pārthena phalgunena tvayā saha
d kimarthaṃ dharmarājena yudhayse bhṛśaroṣitaḥ
d kṣīṇaśastrāstrakavacaḥ kṣīṇabāṇo vibāṇadhiḥ
d śrāntasārathivāhaś ca channo 'strair aribhis tathā
d pārtham āsādya rādheya upahāsyo bhaviṣyasi
d evam ukto 'pi karṇas tu madrarājena saṃyuge
d tathaiva karṇaḥ saṃrabdho yudhiṣṭhiram atāḍayat
d śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ parāvidhya mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavau
d prahasya samare karṇaś cakāra vimukhaṃ śaraiḥ
d tataḥ śalyaḥ prahasyedaṃ karṇaṃ punar uvāca ha
d rathastham atisaṃrabdhaṃ yudhiṣṭhiravadhe dhṛtam
d yadarthaṃ dhārtarāṣṭreṇa satataṃ mānito bhavān
d taṃ pārthaṃ jahi rādheya kiṃ te hatvā yudhiṣṭhiram
d śaṅkhayor dhmāyatoḥ śabdaḥ sumahān eṣa kṛṣṇayoḥ
d śrūyate cāpaghoṣo 'yaṃ prāvṛṣīvāmbudasya ha
d asau nighnan rathodārān arjunaḥ śaravṛṣṭibhiḥ
d sarvāṃ grasati naḥ senāṃ karṇa paśyainam āhave
d pṛṣṭharakṣau ca śūrasya yudhāmanyūttamaujasau
d uttaraṃ cāsya vai śūraś cakraṃ rakṣati sātyakiḥ
d dhṛṣṭadyumnas tathā cāsya cakraṃ rakṣati dakṣiṇam
d bhīmasenaś ca vai rājñā dhārtarāṣṭreṇa yudhyate
d yathā na hanyāt taṃ bhīmaḥ sarveṣāṃ no 'dya paśyatām
d tathā rādheya kriyatāṃ rājā mucyeta no yathā
d paśyainaṃ bhīmasenena grastam āhavaśobhinam
d yadi tv āsādya mucyeta vismayaḥ sumahān bhavet
d paritrāhy enam abhyetya saṃśayaṃ paramaṃ gatam
d kiṃ nu mādrīsutau hatvā rājānaṃ ca yudhiṣṭhiram
d iti śalyavacaḥ śrutvā rādheyaḥ pṛthivīpate
d dṛṣṭvā duryodhanaṃ caiva bhīmagrastaṃ mahāhave
d rājagṛddhī bhṛśaṃ caiva śalyavākyapracoditaḥ
d ajātaśatrum utsṛjya mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavau
d tava putraṃ paritrātum abhyadhāvata vīryavān
d madrarājapraṇuditair aśvair ākāśagair iva
d gate karṇe tu kaunteyaḥ pāṇḍuputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d apāyāj javanair aśvaiḥ sahadevasya māriṣa
d tābhyāṃ sa sahitas tūrṇaṃ vrīḍann iva nareśvaraḥ
d prāpya senāniveśaṃ ca mārgaṇaiḥ kṣatavikṣataḥ
d avatīrṇo rathāt tūrṇam āviśac chayanaṃ śubham
d apanītaśalyaḥ subhṛśaṃ hṛcchalyābhinipīḍitaḥ
d so 'bravīd bhrātarau rājā mādrīputrau mahārathau
d anīkaṃ bhīmasenasya pāṇḍavāv āśu gacchatām
d jīmūta iva nardaṃs tu yudhyate sa vṛkodaraḥ
d tato 'nyaṃ ratham āsthāya nakulo rathapuṃgavaḥ
d sahadevaś ca tejasvī bhrātarau śatrukarśanau
d turagair agryaraṃhobhir yātvā bhīmasya śuṣmiṇau
d anīkaṃ sahitau tatra bhrātarau paryavasthitau
 saṃjaya uvāca
a drauṇis tu rathavaṃśena mahatā parivāritaḥ
c āpatat sahasā rājan yatra rājā vyavasthitaḥ
a tam āpatantaṃ sahasā śūraḥ śaurisahāyavān
c dadhāra sahasā pārtho veleva makarālayam
a tataḥ kruddho mahārāja droṇaputraḥ pratāpavān
c arjunaṃ vāsudevaṃ ca chādayām āsa patribhiḥ
a avacchannau tataḥ kṛṣṇau dṛṣṭvā tatra mahārathāḥ
c vismayaṃ paramaṃ gatvā praikṣanta kuravas tadā
a arjunas tu tato divyam astraṃ cakre hasann iva
c tad astraṃ brāhmaṇo yuddhe vārayām āsa bhārata
a yad yad dhi vyākṣipad yuddhe pāṇḍavo 'straṃ jighāṃsayā
c tat tad astraṃ maheṣvāso droṇaputro vyaśātayat
a astrayuddhe tato rājan vartamāne bhayāvahe
c apaśyāma raṇe drauṇiṃ vyāttānanam ivāntakam
a sa diśo vidiśaś caiva chādayitvā vijihmagaiḥ
c vāsudevaṃ tribhir bāṇair avidhyad dakṣiṇe bhuje
a tato 'rjuno hayān hatvā sarvāṃs tasya mahātmanaḥ
c cakāra samare bhūmiṃ śoṇitaughataraṅgiṇīm
d sarvalokavahāṃ raudrāṃ paralokavahāṃ nadīm
d sarathān rathinaḥ sarvān pārthacāpacyutaiḥ śaraiḥ
d drauṇer apahatān saṃkhye dadṛśuḥ sa ca tāṃ tathā
d prāvartayan mahāghorāṃ nadīṃ paravahāṃ tathā
d tayos tu vyākule yuddhe drauṇeḥ pārthasya dāruṇe
d amaryādaṃ yodhayantaḥ paryadhāvann itas tataḥ
d rathair hatāśvasūtaiś ca hatārohaiś ca vājibhiḥ
d dviradaiś ca hatārohair mahāmātrair hatadvipaiḥ
d pārthena samare rājan kṛto ghoro janakṣayaḥ
a nihatā rathinaḥ petuḥ pārthacāpacyutaiḥ śaraiḥ
c hayāś ca paryadhāvanta muktayoktrās tatas tataḥ
a tad dṛṣṭvā karma pārthasya drauṇir āhavaśobhinaḥ
b arjunaṃ jayatāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ tvarito 'bhyetya vīryavān
b vidhunvāno mahac cāpaṃ kārtasvaravibhūṣitam
c avākirad raṇe kṛṣṇaṃ samantān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a tato 'rjunaṃ mahārāja drauṇir āyamya patriṇā
c vakṣodeśe samāsādya tāḍayām āsa saṃyuge
a so 'tividdho raṇe tena droṇaputreṇa bhārata
b gāṇḍīvadhanvā prasabhaṃ śaravarṣair udāradhīḥ
b saṃchādya samare drauṇiṃ cicchedāsya ca cārmukam
b sa chinnadhanvā parighaṃ vajrasparśasamaṃ yudhi
c ādatta parighaṃ ghoraṃ drauṇeś cainam avākṣipat
d ādāya cikṣepa tadā droṇaputraḥ kirīṭine
a tam āpatantaṃ parighaṃ kārtasvaravibhūṣitam
a   jāmbūnadapariṣkṛtam
a ciccheda sahasā rājan prahasann iva pāṇḍavaḥ
c drauṇiś ciccheda sahasā tata uccukruśur janāḥ
a so 'nekadhāpatad bhūmau bhāradvājasya sāyakaiḥ
c viśīrṇaḥ parvato rājan yathā syān mātariśvanā
d tataḥ kruddho mahārāja droṇaputro mahārathaḥ
d aindreṇa cāstravegena bībhatsuṃ samavākirat
d tasyendrajālāvatataṃ samīkṣya
d pārtho rājan gāṇḍivam ādade saḥ
d aindraṃ jālaṃ pratyahanat tarasvī
d varāstram ādāya mahendrasṛṣṭam
d vidārya taj jālam athendramuktaṃ
d pārthas tato drauṇirathaṃ kṣaṇena
d pracchādayām āsa tathābhyupetya
d drauṇis tadā pārthaśarābhibhūtaḥ
d vigāhya tāṃ pāṇḍavabāṇavṛṣṭiṃ
d śaraiḥ paraṃ nāma tataḥ prakāśya
d śatena kṛṣṇaṃ sahasābhyavidhyat
d tribhiḥ śatair arjunaṃ kṣudrakāṇām
d tato 'rjunaḥ sāyakānāṃ śatena
d guroḥ sutaṃ marmasu nirbibheda
d aśvāṃś ca sūtaṃ ca tathā dhanur jyām
d avākirat paśyatāṃ tāvakānām
a tato 'rjuno raṇe drauṇiṃ vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ
b sa viddhvā marmasu drauṇiṃ pāṇḍavaḥ paravīrahā
c sārathiṃ cāsya bhallena rathanīḍād apāharat
a sa saṃgṛhya svayaṃ vāhān kṛṣṇau prācchādayac charaiḥ
c tatrādbhutam apaśyāma drauṇer āśu parākramam
a ayacchat turagān yac ca phalgunaṃ cāpy ayodhayat
c tad asya samare rājan sarve yodhā apūjayan
d tenāsya samare rājaṃs tuṣṭuvuḥ sarvasainikāḥ
