d tataḥ prahasya bībhatsur droṇaputrasya saṃyuge
a yadā tv agrasyata raṇe droṇaputreṇa phalgunaḥ
c tato raśmīn rathāśvānāṃ kṣurapraiś cicchide jayaḥ
a prādravaṃs turagās te tu śaravegaprabādhitāḥ
c tato 'bhūn ninado bhūyas tava sainyasya bhārata
a pāṇḍavās tu jayaṃ labdhvā tava sainyam upādravan
c samantān niśitān bāṇān vimuñcanto jayaiṣiṇaḥ
a pāṇḍavais tu mahārāja dhārtarāṣṭrī mahācamūḥ
c punaḥ punar atho vīrair abhajyata jayoddhataiḥ
a paśyatāṃ te mahārāja putrāṇāṃ citrayodhinām
c śakuneḥ saubaleyasya karṇasya ca mahātmanaḥ
a vāryamāṇā mahāsenā putrais tava janeśvara
c nāvatiṣṭhata saṃgrāme tāḍyamānā samantataḥ
a tato yodhair mahārāja palāyadbhis tatas tataḥ
c abhavad vyākulaṃ bhītaiḥ putrāṇāṃ te mahad balam
a tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti satataṃ sūtaputrasya jalpataḥ
c nāvatiṣṭhata sā senā vadhyamānā mahātmabhiḥ
a athotkruṣṭaṃ mahārāja pāṇḍavair jitakāśibhiḥ
c dhārtarāṣṭrabalaṃ dṛṣṭvā dravamāṇaṃ samantataḥ
a tato duryodhanaḥ karṇam abravīt praṇayād iva
c paśya karṇa yathā senā pāṇḍavair arditā bhṛśam
a tvayi tiṣṭhati saṃtrāsāt palāyati samantataḥ
c etaj jñātvā mahābāho kuru prāptam ariṃdama
a sahasrāṇi ca yodhānāṃ tvām eva puruṣarṣabha
c krośanti samare vīra drāvyamāṇāni pāṇḍavaiḥ
a etac chrutvā tu rādheyo duryodhanavaco mahat
c madrarājam idaṃ vākyam abravīt sūtanandanaḥ
a paśya me bhujayor vīryam astrāṇāṃ ca janeśvara
c adya hanmi raṇe sarvān pāñcālān pāṇḍubhiḥ saha
e vāhayāśvān naravyāghra bhadreṇaiva janeśvara
a evam uktvā mahārāja sūtaputraḥ pratāpavān
c pragṛhya vijayaṃ vīro dhanuḥśreṣṭhaṃ purātanam
e sajyaṃ kṛtvā mahārāja saṃmṛjya ca punaḥ punaḥ
a saṃnivārya ca yodhān svān satyena śapathena ca
c prāyojayad ameyātmā bhārgavāstraṃ mahābalaḥ
a tato rājan sahasrāṇi prayutāny arbudāni ca
c koṭiśaś ca śarās tīkṣṇā niragacchan mahāmṛdhe
a jvalitais tair mahāghoraiḥ kaṅkabarhiṇavājitaiḥ
c saṃchannā pāṇḍavī senā na prājñāyata kiṃ cana
a hāhākāro mahān āsīt pāñcālānāṃ viśāṃ pate
c pīḍitānāṃ balavatā bhārgavāstreṇa saṃyuge
a nipatadbhir gajai rājan naraiś cāpi sahasraśaḥ
c rathaiś cāpi naravyāghra hayaiś cāpi samantataḥ
a prākampata mahī rājan nihatais tais tatas tataḥ
c vyākulaṃ sarvam abhavat pāṇḍavānāṃ mahad balam
a karṇas tv eko yudhāṃ śreṣṭho vidhūma iva pāvakaḥ
c dahañ śatrūn naravyāghra śuśubhe sa paraṃtapaḥ
a te vadhyamānāḥ karṇena pāñcālāś cedibhiḥ saha
c tatra tatra vyamuhyanta vanadāhe yathā dvipāḥ
e cukruśus te naravyāghra yathāprāg vā narottamāḥ
a teṣāṃ tu krośatāṃ śrutvā bhītānāṃ raṇamūrdhani
c dhāvatāṃ ca diśo rājan vitrastānāṃ samantataḥ
e ārtanādo mahāṃs tatra pretānām iva saṃplave
a vadhyamānāṃs tu tān dṛṣṭvā sūtaputreṇa māriṣa
c vitresuḥ sarvabhūtāni tiryagyonigatāny api
a te vadhyamānāḥ samare sūtaputreṇa sṛñjayāḥ
c arjunaṃ vāsudevaṃ ca vyākrośanta muhur muhuḥ
d śrutvā tu ninadaṃ teṣāṃ vadhyatāṃ karṇasāyakaiḥ
e pretarājapure yadvat pretarājaṃ vicetasaḥ
f athārjuno mahābāhuḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
f duḥsaho vajriṇāpy ājau parājitya guroḥ sutam
a athābravīd vāsudevaṃ kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥ
c bhārgavāstraṃ mahāghoraṃ dṛṣṭvā tatra sabhīritam
a paśya kṛṣṇa mahābāho bhārgavāstrasya vikramam
c naitad astraṃ hi samare śakyaṃ hantuṃ kathaṃ cana
a sūtaputraṃ ca saṃrabdhaṃ paśya kṛṣṇa mahāraṇe
c antakapratimaṃ vīraṃ kurvāṇaṃ karma dāruṇam
a sutīkṣṇaṃ codayann aśvān prekṣate māṃ muhur muhuḥ
c na ca paśyāmi samare karṇasya prapalāyitam
a jīvan prāpnoti puruṣaḥ saṃkhye jayaparājayau
c jitasya tu hṛṣīkeśa vadha eva kuto jayaḥ
d evam uktas tu pārthena kṛṣṇo matimatāṃ varam
d dhanaṃjayam uvācedaṃ prāptakālam ariṃdamam
d karṇena hi dṛḍhaṃ rājā kuntīputraḥ parikṣataḥ
d taṃ dṛṣṭvāśvāsya ca punaḥ karṇaṃ pārtha vadhiṣyasi
d pratipadyasva kaunteya prāptakālam anantaram
d karṇam ekākinaṃ hatvā rathānīkena bhārata
d eṣa karṇo raṇe bhāti madhyāhna iva bhāskaraḥ
d nivartaya rathaṃ kṛṣṇa jīvan bhadrāṇi paśyati
a tato janārdanaḥ prāyād draṣṭum icchan yudhiṣṭhiram
b saṃjaya uvāca
b tato janārdanaḥ śrutvā tasya vākyaṃ viśāṃ pate
b rathenāpayayau kṣipraṃ saṃgrāmād iti bhārata
b pratyanīkam avasthāpya bhīmaṃ bhīmaparākramam
b alaṃ viṣahituṃ hy eṣa kurūṇāṃ saṃprapadyatām
c śrameṇa grāhayiṣyaṃś ca karṇaṃ yuddhena māriṣa
d karṇaṃ ca samare rājan grāhayiṣyañ śramaṃ prati
d viśramārthaṃ ca kauravya pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ
d apayāto raṇād vīro rājānaṃ draṣṭum eva ca
a arjunaṃ cābravīt kṛṣṇo bhṛśaṃ rājā parikṣataḥ
c tam āśvāsya kuruśreṣṭha tataḥ karṇaṃ haniṣyasi
a tato dhanaṃjayo draṣṭuṃ rājānaṃ bāṇapīḍitam
b yāhi yāhīti bahuśo vāsudevam acodayat
b rājānaṃ prati vārṣṇeya dūyate me dṛḍhaṃ manaḥ
b sa codyamānaḥ pārthena keśighno vṛṣṇinandanaḥ
c rathena prayayau kṣipraṃ saṃgrāme keśavājñayā
a gacchann eva tu kaunteyo dharmarājadidṛkṣayā
c sainyam ālokayām āsa nāpaśyat tatra cāgrajam
a yuddhaṃ kṛtvā tu kaunteyo droṇaputreṇa bhārata
c duḥsahaṃ vajriṇā saṃkhye parājigye bhṛgoḥ sutam
a drauṇiṃ parājitya tatogradhanvā
kṛtvā mahad duṣkaram āryakarma
c ālokayām āsa tataḥ svasainyaṃ
dhanaṃjayaḥ śatrubhir apradhṛṣyaḥ
a sa yudhyamānaḥ pṛtanāmukhasthāñ
śūrāñ śūro harṣayan savyasācī
c pūrvāpadānaiḥ prathitaiḥ praśaṃsan
sthirāṃś cakārātmarathān anīke
a apaśyamānas tu kirīṭamālī
yudhi jyeṣṭhaṃ bhrātaram ājamīḍham
c uvāca bhīmaṃ tarasābhyupetya
rājñaḥ pravṛttis tv iha keti rājan
 bhīma uvāca
a apayāta ito rājā dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c karṇabāṇavibhugnāṅgo yadi jīvet kathaṃ cana
 arjuna uvāca
a tasmād bhavāñ śīghram itaḥ prayātu
rājñaḥ pravṛttyai kurusattamasya
c nūnaṃ hi viddho 'tibhṛśaṃ pṛṣatkaiḥ
karṇena rājā śibiraṃ gato 'sau
a yaḥ saṃprahāre niśi saṃpravṛtte
droṇena viddho 'tibhṛśaṃ tarasvī
c tasthau ca tatrāpi jayapratīkṣo
droṇena yāvan na hataḥ kilāsīt
a sa saṃśayaṃ gamitaḥ pāṇḍavāgryaḥ
saṃkhye 'dya karṇena mahānubhāvaḥ
c jñātuṃ prayāhy āśu tam adya bhīma
sthāsyāmy ahaṃ śatrugaṇān nirudhya
 bhīma uvāca
a tvam eva jānīhi mahānubhāva
rājñaḥ pravṛttiṃ bharatarṣabhasya
c ahaṃ hi yady arjuna yāmi tatra
vakṣyanti māṃ bhīta iti pravīrāḥ
a tato 'bravīd arjuno bhīmasenaṃ
saṃśaptakāḥ pratyanīkaṃ sthitā me
c etān ahatvā na mayā tu śakyam
ito 'payātuṃ ripusaṃghagoṣṭhāt
a athābravīd arjunaṃ bhīmasenaḥ
svavīryam āśritya kurupravīra
c saṃśaptakān pratiyotsyāmi saṃkhye
sarvān ahaṃ yāhi dhanaṃjayeti
a tad bhīmasenasya vaco niśamya
sudurvacaṃ bhrātur amitramadhye
b saṃśaptakānīkam asahyam ekaḥ
b suduṣkaraṃ dhārayāmīti pārthaḥ
b uvāca nārāyaṇam aprameyaṃ
b kapidhvajaḥ satyaparākramasya
b śrutvā vaco bhrātur adīnasattvas
b tadāhave satyavaco mahātmā
c draṣṭuṃ kuruśreṣṭham abhiprayātuṃ
provāca vṛṣṇipravaraṃ tadānīm
d rājānaṃ prati vārṣṇeya dūyate me dṛḍhaṃ manaḥ
a codayāśvān hṛṣīkeśa vigāhyaitaṃ rathārṇavam
c ajātaśatruṃ rājānaṃ draṣṭum icchāmi keśava
d taṃ rathaṃ codayām āsa bībhatsor vacanād dhariḥ
a tato hayān sarvadāśārhamukhyaḥ
prācodayad bhīmam uvāca cedam
c naitac citraṃ tava karmādya vīra
yāsyāmahe jahi bhīmārisaṃghān
a tato yayau hṛṣīkeśo yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c śīghrāc chīghrataraṃ rājan vājibhir garuḍopamaiḥ
a pratyanīke vyavasthāpya bhīmasenam ariṃdamam
c saṃdiśya caiva rājendra yuddhaṃ prati vṛkodaram
d kṣaṇenaiva tu rājānam āsedatur ariṃdamau
a tatas tu gatvā puruṣapravīrau
rājānam āsādya śayānam ekam
c rathād ubhau pratyavaruhya tasmād
vavandatur dharmarājasya pādau
d javena gatvā tu dāśārhamukhyaḥ
d śayānam ekaṃ kururājaṃ dadarśa
d praharṣavegeritamānasāv ubhau
d rājānam āsādya parisravad vraṇam
d ity evam abhisaṃgṛhya ubhau tu prāñjalī sthitau
d śastrakṣatau mahārāja rudhireṇa samukṣitau
d nihatya vāhinīṃ tubhyam apayātau raṇājirāt
a tau dṛṣṭvā puruṣavyāghrau kṣemiṇau puruṣarṣabha
c mudābhyupagatau kṛṣṇāv aśvināv iva vāsavam
a tāv abhyanandad rājā hi vivasvān aśvināv iva
c hate mahāsure jambhe śakraviṣṇū yathā guruḥ
a manyamāno hataṃ karṇaṃ dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a   prītaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ
a sa bhūtvā puruṣavyāghrau
c harṣagadgadayā vācā prītaḥ prāha paraṃtapau
 saṃjaya uvāca
 athopayātau pṛthulohitākṣau
 śarācitāṅgau rudhirapradigdhau
 yudhiṣṭhirasya prativedayantau
 priyaṃ tadānīṃ puruṣapravīrau
 tāv āgatau prekṣya mahendrakalpau
 yudhiṣṭhiro duḥkhaparītacetāḥ
 kṛcchreṇa rājā pratilabhya saṃjñāṃ
 tataḥ punaḥ prītamanā babhūva
 samīkṣya senāgranarapravīrau
 yudhiṣṭhiro vākyam idaṃ babhāṣe
a mahāsattvau tu tau dṛṣṭvā sahitau keśavārjunau
c hatam ādhirathiṃ mene saṃkhye gāṇḍīvadhanvanā
a tāv abhyanandat kaunteyaḥ sāmnā paramavalgunā
c smitapūrvam amitraghnaḥ pūjayan bharatarṣabha
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a svāgataṃ devakīputra svāgataṃ te dhanaṃjaya
c priyaṃ me darśanaṃ bāḍhaṃ yuvayor acyutārjunau
a akṣatābhyām ariṣṭābhyāṃ kathaṃ yudhya mahāratham
c āśīviṣasamaṃ yuddhe sarvaśastraviśāradam
a agragaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ śarma varma ca
c rakṣitaṃ vṛṣasenena suṣeṇena ca dhanvinā
a anujñātaṃ mahāvīryaṃ rameṇāstreṣu durjayam
b rāmeṇa jāmadagnyena anujñātaṃ yaśasvinā
b mukhyaṃ sarvasya lokasya rathinaṃ lokaviśrutam
c trātāraṃ dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ gantāraṃ vāhinīmukhe
a hantāram arisainyānām amitragaṇamardanam
c duryodhanahite yuktam asmadyuddhāya codyatam
a apradhṛṣyaṃ mahāyuddhe devair api savāsavaiḥ
c analānilayos tulyaṃ tejasā ca balena ca
a pātālam iva gambhīraṃ suhṛdānandavardhanam
c antakābham amitrāṇāṃ karṇaṃ hatvā mahāhave
e diṣṭyā yuvām anuprāptau jitvāsuram ivāmarau
a tena yuddham adīnena mayā hy adyācyutārjunau
b kṛtaṃ ghoraṃ mahābāho dhṛṣṭadyumnasya paśyataḥ
c kupitenāntakeneva prajāḥ sarvā jighāṃsatā
a tena ketuś ca me chinno hatau ca pārṣṇisārathī
c hatavāhaḥ kṛtaś cāsmi yuyudhānasya paśyataḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumnasya yamayor vīrasya ca śikhaṇḍinaḥ
c paśyatāṃ draupadeyānāṃ pāñcālānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
a etāñ jitvā mahāvīryān karṇaḥ śatrugaṇān bahūn
c jitavān māṃ mahābāho yatamānaṃ mahāraṇe
a anusṛtya ca māṃ yuddhe paruṣāṇy uktavān bahu
c tatra tatra yudhāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ paribhūya na saṃśayaḥ
a bhīmasenaprabhāvāt tu yaj jīvāmi dhanaṃjaya
c bahunātra kim uktena nāhaṃ tat soḍhum utsahe
a trayodaśāhaṃ varṣāṇi yasmād bhīto dhanaṃjaya
c na sma nidrāṃ labhe rātrau na cāhani sukhaṃ kva cit
a tasya dveṣeṇa saṃyuktaḥ paridahye dhanaṃjaya
c ātmano maraṇaṃ jānan vādhrīṇasa iva dvipaḥ
d kṛṣṇagrīvo raktaśirāḥ śvetapakṣo vihaṃgamaḥ
d sa vai vādhrīṇasaḥ prokto yājñikaiḥ pitṛkarmasu
a yasyāyam agamat kālaś cintayānasya me vibho
c kathaṃ śakyo mayā karṇo yuddhe kṣapayituṃ bhavet
a jāgrat svapaṃś ca kaunteya karṇam eva sadā hy aham
c paśyāmi tatra tatraiva karṇabhūtam idaṃ jagat
a yatra yatra hi gacchāmi karṇād bhīto dhanaṃjaya
c tatra tatra hi paśyāmi karṇam evāgrataḥ sthitam
a so 'haṃ tenaiva vīreṇa samareṣv apalāyinā
c sahayaḥ sarathaḥ pārtha jitvā jīvan visarjitaḥ
a ko nu me jīvitenārtho rājyenārtho 'tha vā punaḥ
c mamaivaṃ dhikkṛtasyeha karṇenāhavaśobhinā
a na prāptapūrvaṃ yad bhīṣmāt kṛpād droṇāc ca saṃyuge
c tat prāptam adya me yuddhe sūtaputrān mahārathāt
a tat tvā pṛcchāmi kaunteya yathā hy akuśalas tathā
c tan mamācakṣva kārtsnyena yathā karṇas tvayā hataḥ
a śakravīryasamo yuddhe yamatulyaparākramaḥ
c rāmatulyas tathāstre yaḥ sa kathaṃ vai niṣūditaḥ
a mahārathaḥ samākhyātaḥ sarvayuddhaviśāradaḥ
c dhanurdharāṇāṃ pravaraḥ sarveṣām ekapūruṣaḥ
a pūjito dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa saputreṇa viśāṃ pate
c sadā tvadarthaṃ rādheyaḥ sa kathaṃ nihatas tvayā
a dhṛtarāṣṭro hi yodheṣu sarveṣv eva sadārjuna
c tava mṛtyuṃ raṇe karṇaṃ manyate puruṣarṣabhaḥ
a sa tvayā puruṣavyāghra kathaṃ yuddhe niṣūditaḥ
c taṃ mamācakṣva bībhatso yathā karṇo hatas tvayā
a sotsedham asya ca śiraḥ paśyatāṃ suhṛdāṃ hṛtam
c tvayā puruṣaśārdūla śārdūlena yathā ruroḥ
a yaḥ paryupāsīt pradiśo diśaś ca
tvāṃ sūtaputraḥ samare parīpsan
c ditsuḥ karṇaḥ samare hastipūgaṃ
sa hīdānīṃ kaṅkapatraiḥ sutīkṣṇaiḥ
d ditsan nṛṇāṃ śakaṭaṃ ratnapūrṇaṃ
d kathaṃ tvayāsau nihato 'dya karṇaḥ
a tvayā raṇe nihataḥ sūtaputraḥ
kaccic chete bhūmitale durātmā
c kaccit priyaṃ me paramaṃ tvayādya
kṛtaṃ raṇe sūtaputraṃ nihatya
a yaḥ sarvataḥ paryapatat tvadarthe
madānvito garvitaḥ sūtaputraḥ
c sa śūramānī samare sametya
kaccit tvayā nihataḥ saṃyuge 'dya
a raukmaṃ rathaṃ hastivaraiś ca yuktaṃ
rathaṃ ditsur yaḥ parebhyas tvadarthe
c sadā raṇe spardhate yaḥ sa pāpaḥ
kaccit tvayā nihatas tāta yuddhe
a yo 'sau nityaṃ śūramadena matto
vikatthate saṃsadi kauravāṇām
c priyo 'tyarthaṃ tasya suyodhanasya
kaccit sa pāpo nihatas tvayādya
a kaccit samāgamya dhanuḥpramuktais
tvatpreṣitair lohitārthair vihaṃgaiḥ
c śete 'dya pāpaḥ sa vibhinnagātraḥ
kaccid bhagno dhārtarāṣṭrasya bāhuḥ
a yo 'sau sadā ślāghate rājamadhye
duryodhanaṃ harṣayan darpapūrṇaḥ
c ahaṃ hantā phalgunasyeti mohāt
kaccid dhatas tasya na vai tathā rathaḥ
d kaccid vaco 'sya vitathaṃ tvayā kṛtaṃ
d yat tat priyām avadat tāta karṇaḥ
d sabhāmadhye rūkṣam anekarūpaṃ
d dhik pāṇḍavān apatis tvaṃ hi kṛṣṇe
d kaccid dhruvaṃ śatrur ayaṃ mahātmā
d hy adhārayad dvādaśa yaḥ samāstu
d karṇo vrataṃ ghoram amitrasāho
d duryodhanasyārthaniviṣṭabuddhiḥ
a nāhaṃ pādau dhāvayiṣye kadā cid
yāvat sthitaḥ pārtha ity alpabuddhiḥ
c vrataṃ tasyaitat sarvadā śakrasūno
kaccit tvayā nihataḥ so 'dya karṇaḥ
d pādau na dhāve yāvad ahaṃ na hanmi
d dhanaṃjayaṃ samareṣūgravegam
d kaccid raṇe phalguna taṃ nihatya
d kaccid vrataṃ tasya bhagnaṃ tvayādya
a yo 'sau kṛṣṇām abravīd duṣṭabuddhiḥ
karṇaḥ sabhāyāṃ kuruvīramadhye
c kiṃ pāṇḍavāṃs tvaṃ na jahāsi kṛṣṇe
sudurbalān patitān hīnasattvān
a yat tat karṇaḥ pratyajānāt tvadarthe
nāhatvāhaṃ saha kṛṣṇena pārtham
a mahābalaḥ saṃyuge śatruhantā
c ihopayāteti sa pāpabuddhiḥ
kaccic chete śarasaṃbhinnagātraḥ
a kaccit saṃgrāme vidito vā tadāyaṃ
samāgamaḥ sṛñjayakauravāṇām
c yatrāvasthām īdṛśīṃ prāpito 'haṃ
kaccit tvayā so 'dya hataḥ sametya
a kaccit tvayā tasya sumandabuddher
gāṇḍīvamuktair viśikhair jvaladbhiḥ
c sakuṇḍalaṃ bhānumad uttamāṅgaṃ
kāyāt prakṛttaṃ yudhi savyasācin
a yat tan mayā bāṇasamarpitena
dhyāto 'si karṇasya vadhāya vīra
c tan me tvayā kaccid amogham adya
dhyātaṃ kṛtaṃ karṇanipātanena
a yad darpapūrṇaḥ sa suyodhano 'smān
avekṣate karṇasamāśrayeṇa
c kaccit tvayā so 'dya samāśrayo 'sya
bhagnaḥ parākramya suyodhanasya
a yo naḥ purā ṣaṇḍhatilān avocat
sabhāmadhye pārthivānāṃ samakṣam
c sa durmatiḥ kaccid upetya saṃkhye
tvayā hataḥ sūtaputro 'tyamarṣī
a yaḥ sūtaputraḥ prahasan durātmā
purābravīn nirjitāṃ saubalena
c svayaṃ prasahyānaya yājñasenīm
apīha kaccit sa hatas tvayādya
d yaḥ prāhiṇot sūtaputro durātmā
d kṛṣṇāṃ jitāṃ saubalenānayeti
d sa mandabuddhir nihataḥ prasahya
d vaikartanas tv adya kaccin mahātman
d anavāpyāṃ prāptum icchann acintyaṃ
d śiśur yathā candramasaṃ grahītum
d sa pāpātmā sa tu no vidviṣāṇaḥ
d kaccit karṇo nihato vā tvayā dhik
d asmin saṃgrāme bhīmarūpe tvayādya
d vrataṃ tu bhagnaṃ sūtaputrasya pārtha
d kaccit pāpaṃ vacanaṃ dyūtakāle
d yac cāpy asau samitau vāsudevam
d tadoktavān paruṣaṃ so 'tikāmam
d hitaṃ caran yaḥ satataṃ kurūṇām
d kaccit sa karṇo nihato 'dya saṃkhe
d yo dhārtarāṣṭraṃ paripālayan raṇe
d ekaḥ sadā śoṣayan māmakaṃ balaṃ
d sa pāñcālān kekayāṃś caiva sarvān
d śriyaṃ diditsan dhārtarāṣṭrīṃ sa karṇaḥ
d kaccin mahyaṃ pratyavadhīs tvam adya
d atho bhāsāś ca sṛgālāś ca gṛdhrā
d hatasya māṃsāny uddharanti sma kāyāt
a yaḥ śastrabhṛc chreṣṭhatamaṃ pṛthivyāṃ
pitāmahaṃ vyākṣipad alpacetāḥ
c saṃkhyāyamāno 'rdharathaḥ sa kaccit
tvayā hato 'dyādhirathir durātmā
d yat tat tvayā saṃśrutaṃ me kirīṭin
d sabhāmadhye dvairatheneha bhūyaḥ
d ahaṃ karṇaṃ sūdayiṣye saputraṃ
d tat karma kṛtvā hy anṛṇo 'si kaccit
a amarṣaṇaṃ nikṛtisamīraṇeritaṃ
hṛdi śritaṃ jvalanam imaṃ sadā mama
c hato mayā so 'dya sametya pāpadhīr
iti bruvan praśamaya me 'dya phalguna
d bravīhi me durlabham etad adya
d kathaṃ tvayā nihataḥ sūtaputraḥ
d anudhyāye tvāṃ satataṃ pravīra
d vṛtre hate 'sau bhagavān ivendraḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tad dharmaśīlasya vaco niśamya
rājñaḥ kruddhasyādhirathau mahātmā
c uvāca durdharṣam adīnasattvaṃ
yudhiṣṭhiraṃ jiṣṇur anantavīryaḥ
d droṇaṃ hataṃ pārtha karṇo viditvā
d bhinnāṃ nāvam ivātyagādhe kurūṇām
d saṃmuhyamānān dhārtarāṣṭrān viditvā
d nirutsāhāṃś ca vijaye pareṣām
d sodaryavat tvarito 'mitaujā
d uttārayiṣyan dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putrān
d raṇe rathenādhirathir mahātmā
d tato hi māṃ tvaritaḥ so 'bhyadhāvat
a saṃśaptakair yudhyamānasya me 'dya
senāgrayāyī kurusainyasya rājan
c āśīviṣābhān khagamān pramuñcan
drauṇiḥ purastāt sahasā vyatiṣṭhat
a dṛṣṭvā rathaṃ meghanibhaṃ mamemam
ambaṣṭhasenā maraṇe vyatiṣṭhat
c teṣām ahaṃ pañca śatāni hatvā
tato drauṇim agamaṃ pārthivāgrya
d sa me dṛṣṭvā śūratamo dhvajāgraṃ
d samādiśad rathasaṃghān anekān
d teṣām ahaṃ pañcaśatān nihatya
d āsādayaṃ droṇaputraṃ nadantam
d sa droṇaputraḥ sadṛśaṃ mahātmā
d mām apy arautsīt tadanīkamadhye
d kirañ śaraughān bahurūpān vicitrāṃś
d citrāṃ gataḥ śukra ivātivarṣan
d sa me śarān sarvataḥ kaṅkapatrān
d avāsṛjad vai pṛthivīprakāśān
d nivārya tūrṇaṃ paramājimadhye
d tato hi māṃ bāṇagaṇaiḥ samarpayat
d ākarṣaṇaṃ vāpi vikṛṣya muktaṃ
d na dṛśyate tasya mahārathasya
d sa māṃ samāsādya narendra yattaḥ
d samabhyayāt siṃha iva dvipendraḥ
d akārṣīc ca rathinām ujjihīrṣāṃ
d mahārāja vadhyatāṃ kauravāṇām
d tato raṇe bhārata duṣprakampya
d ācāryaputraḥ pravaraḥ kurūṇām
d mām ardayām āsa śitaiḥ pṛṣatkair
d janārdanaṃ caiva viṣāgnikalpaiḥ
d aṣṭau gavām aṣṭaśatāni bāṇān
d mayā prayuddhasya vahanti tasya
d tāṃs tena muktān aham asya bāṇair
d vyanāśayaṃ vāyur ivābhrajālam
a tato 'parān bāṇasaṃghān anekān
ākarṇapūrṇāyatavipramuktān
c sasarja śikṣāstrabalaprayatnais
tathā yathā prāvṛṣi kālameghaḥ
a naivādadānaṃ na ca saṃdadhānaṃ
jānīmahe katareṇāsyatīti
c vāmena vā yadi vā dakṣiṇena
sa droṇaputraḥ samare paryavartat
d na saṃdadhānaḥ kuta ādadhāno
d na vyākṣipann āvikarṣan vimuñcan
d savyena vā yadi vā dakṣiṇena
d na jñāyate katareṇāsyatīti
d ācāryavat samare paryavartan
d mahac citraṃ dṛśyate sarvataḥ sma
d dṛṣṭir viṣaṃ cāsukaraṃ pareṣāṃ
d sarvā diśaḥ pūrayānaṃ śaraughaiḥ
d alātacakrapratimaṃ mahātmanaḥ
d sadā nataṃ kārmukaṃ brahmabandhoḥ
d tasyātataṃ maṇḍalam eva sajyaṃ
d pradṛśyate kārmukaṃ droṇasūnoḥ
a avidhyan māṃ pañcabhir droṇaputraḥ
śitaiḥ śaraiḥ pañcabhir vāsudevam
c ahaṃ tu taṃ triṃśatā vajrakalpaiḥ
samārdayaṃ nimiṣasyāntareṇa
d abhyaghnaṃ bāṇais tam ahaṃ sudhārair
d nimeṣamātreṇa suvarṇapuṅkhaiḥ
d kṣaṇāc chvāvitsamarūpo babhūva
d samārdito madvisṛṣṭaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ
a sa vikṣaran rudhiraṃ sarvagātrai
rathānīkaṃ sūtasūnor viveśa
c mayābhibhūtaḥ sainikānāṃ prabarhān
asāv apaśyan rudhireṇa pradigdhān
d sa nirviddho vikṣaran droṇaputro
d rathānīkaṃ cātirather viveśa
d mayābhibhūtān svarathaprabarhān
d astraṃ ca paśyan rudhirapradigdham
a tato 'bhibhūtaṃ yudhi vīkṣya sainyaṃ
vidhvastayodhaṃ drutavājināgam
c pañcāśatā rathamukhyaiḥ sametaḥ
karṇas tvaran mām upāyāt pramāthī
a tān sūdayitvāham apāsya karṇaṃ
draṣṭuṃ bhavantaṃ tvarayābhiyātaḥ
c sarve pāñcālā hy udvijante sma karṇād
gandhād gāvaḥ kesariṇo yathaiva
a mahājhaṣasyeva mukhaṃ prapannāḥ
prabhadrakāḥ karṇam abhi dravanti
c mṛtyor āsyaṃ vyāttam ivānvapadyan
prabhadrakāḥ karṇam āsādya rājan
d yāsyāmi tāṃs tārayiṣyan balaughān
d diṣṭyā bhavān svastimān pārtha dṛṣṭaḥ
d rathāṃs tu tān saptaśatān nimagnāṃs
d tadā karṇaḥ prāhiṇon mṛtyusadma
d na cāpy abhūt klāntamanāḥ sa rājan
d yāvan nāsmān dṛṣṭavān sūtaputraḥ
d śrutvā tu tvāṃ tena dṛṣṭaṃ sametam
d aśvatthāmnā pūrvataraṃ kṣataṃ ca
d manye kālam apayānasya rājan
d krūrāt karṇāt te 'ham acintyakarman
d na me karṇasyāstram idaṃ purastād
d yuddhe dṛṣṭaṃ pāṇḍava citrarūpam
d na hy anyayoddhā vidyate sṛñjayānāṃ
d mahārathaṃ yo 'dya saheta karṇam
d śaineyo me sātyakiś cakrarakṣau
d dhṛṣṭadyumnaś cāpi tathaiva rājan
d yudhāmanyuś cottamaujāś ca śūrau
d pṛṣṭhato māṃ rakṣatāṃ rājaputrau
d rathapravīreṇa mahānubhāva
d dviṣatsainye vartatā dustareṇa
a āyāhi paśyādya yuyutsamānaṃ
māṃ sūtaputraṃ ca vṛtau jayāya
c ṣaṭsāhasrā bhārata rājaputrāḥ
svargāya lokāya rathā nimagnāḥ
d tān adya yāsyāmi raṇād vimoktuṃ
d sarvātmanā sūtaputraṃ ca hantum
d rathapravīreṇa mahānubhāva
d dviṣat sainyaṃ nirdahan vistareṇa
a sametyāhaṃ sūtaputreṇa saṃkhye
vṛtreṇa vajrīva narendramukhya
b evaṃ gate kiṃ ca mayādya śakyaṃ
b kāryaṃ kartuṃ nigrahe sūtajasya
b tathaiva rājñaś ca suyodhanasya
b ye cāpi māṃ yoddhukāmāḥ sametāḥ
c yotsye bhṛśaṃ bhārata sūtaputram
asmin saṃgrāme yadi vai dṛśyate 'dya
a karṇaṃ na ced adya nihanmi rājan
sabāndhavaṃ yudhyamānaṃ prasahya
c pratiśrutyākurvatāṃ vai gatir yā
kaṣṭāṃ gaccheyaṃ tām ahaṃ rājasiṃha
a āmantraye tvāṃ brūhi jayaṃ raṇe me
purā bhīmaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrā grasante
c sautiṃ haniṣyāmi narendrasiṃha
sainyaṃ tathā śatrugaṇāṃś ca sarvān
 saṃjaya uvāca
a śrutvā karṇaṃ kalyam udāravīryaṃ
kruddhaḥ pārthaḥ phalgunasyāmitaujāḥ
c dhanaṃjayaṃ vākyam uvāca cedaṃ
yudhiṣṭhiraḥ karṇaśarābhitaptaḥ
d vipradrutā tāta camūs tvadīyā
d tiraskṛtā cādya yathā na sādhu
d bhīto bhīmaṃ tyajya cāyās tathā tvaṃ
d yan nāśakaḥ karṇam atho nihantum
d steyaṃ tvayā pārtha kṛtaṃ pṛthāyā
d garbhaṃ samāviśya yathā na sādhu
d raudraṃ raṇe duṣprativāryavīryaḥ
d sautis tvayā nādya śakyo nihantum
d tyaktvā raṇe yad apāyāḥ sa bhīmaṃ
d yan nāśakaḥ sūtaputraṃ nihantum
d yat tad vākyaṃ dvaitavane tvayoktaṃ
d hantā karṇam ekarathena satyam
d tyaktvā taṃ vai katham adyāpayātaḥ
d karṇād bhīto bhīmasenaṃ vihāya
d imāṃ ca vasatiṃ prāpto bhayāt karṇena bādhitaḥ
d ahaṃ tvaṃ bhīmasenaś ca mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavau
d vāsudevena sahitā vayaṃ karṇena nirjitāḥ
d punar eva vanaṃ prāpya tapaścaryāṃ carāmahe
d atha vā dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ paricaryāṃ carāmahe
d ity evam uktvā bībhatsuṃ roṣāt saṃraktalocanaḥ
d abravīt punar evātra dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a idaṃ yadi dvaitavane hy avakṣyaḥ
karṇaṃ yoddhuṃ na prasahe nṛpeti
c vayaṃ tadā prāptakālāni sarve
vṛttāny upaiṣyāma tadaiva pārtha
a mayi pratiśrutya vadhaṃ hi tasya
balasya cāptasya tathaiva vīra
c ānīya naḥ śatrumadhyaṃ sa kasmāt
samutkṣipya sthaṇḍile pratyapiṃṣṭhāḥ
a anvāśiṣma vayam arjuna tvayi
yiyāsavo bahu kalyāṇam iṣṭam
c tan naḥ sarvaṃ viphalaṃ rājaputra
phalārthināṃ nicula ivātipuṣpaḥ
d anvāsya satyena yad āttha pārtha
d satyaṃ śapan vāsudevena sārdham
d taṃ naḥ satyam aphalam akārṣīs tvaṃ
d phalakāle puṣpavṛkṣaṃ nikṛntaḥ
a pracchāditaṃ baḍiśam ivāmiṣeṇa
pracchādito gavaya ivāpavācā
c anarthakaṃ me darśitavān asi tvaṃ
rājyārthino rājyarūpaṃ vināśam
d pracchāditas tvaṃ bāliśa duryaśenā
d narthavākyo 'syarjuna naiva sādhuḥ
d tyaktvā bhīmaṃ sarvabhīmeṣu bhīmaṃ
d saṃyojitas tvaṃ sūtaputraṃ nihantum
d trayodaśemā hi samāḥ sadā vayaṃ
d tvām anvajīviṣma dhanaṃjayāśayā
d kāle varṣaṃ devam ivoptabījaṃ
d tan naḥ sarvān narake tvaṃ nyamajjayaḥ
a yat tat pṛthāṃ vāg uvācāntarikṣe
saptāhajāte tvayi mandabuddhau
c jātaḥ putro vāsavavikramo 'yaṃ
sarvāñ śūrāñ śātravāñ jeṣyatīti
d apāpīyān vāsavāt kuntijāto
d bahūn saṃgrāmān ayam eva jetā
a ayaṃ jetā khāṇḍave devasaṃghān
sarvāṇi bhūtāny api cottamaujāḥ
c ayaṃ jetā madrakaliṅgakekayān
ayaṃ kurūn hanti ca rājamadhye
c daityāṃś ca rakṣāṃsi samāgatāni
c bhūmiṃ ca sarvān nikhilena jetā
a asmāt paro na bhavitā dhanurdharo
na vai bhūtaḥ kaś cana jātu jetā
c icchann āryaḥ sarvabhūtāni kuryād
vaśe vaśī sarvasamāptavidyaḥ
a kāntyā śaśāṅkasya javena vāyoḥ
sthairyeṇa meroḥ kṣamayā pṛthivyāḥ
c sūryasya bhāsā dhanadasya lakṣmyā
śauryeṇa śakrasya balena viṣṇoḥ
a tulyo mahātmā tava kunti putro
jāto 'diter viṣṇur ivārihantā
c sveṣāṃ jayāya dviṣatāṃ vadhāya
khyāto 'mitaujāḥ kulatantukartā
a ity antarikṣe śataśṛṅgamūrdhni
tapasvināṃ śṛṇvatāṃ vāg uvāca
c evaṃvidhaṃ tvāṃ tac ca nābhūt tavādya
devā hi nūnam anṛtaṃ vadanti
a tathāpareṣām ṛṣisattamānāṃ
śrutvā giraṃ pūjayatāṃ sadaiva
c na saṃnatiṃ praimi suyodhanasya
na tvā jānāmy ādhirather bhayārtam
a tvaṣṭrā kṛtaṃ vāham akūjanākṣaṃ
śubhaṃ samāsthāya kapidhvajaṃ tvam
c khaḍgaṃ gṛhītvā hemacitraṃ samiddhaṃ
dhanuś cedaṃ gāṇḍivaṃ tālamātram
e sa keśavenohyamānaḥ kathaṃ nu
karṇād bhīto vyapayāto 'si pārtha
f pūrvaṃ yad uktaṃ hi suyodhanena
f na phalgunaḥ pramukhe sthāsyatīti
f karṇasya yuddhe hi mahābalasya
f maurkhyāt tu tan nāvabuddhaṃ mayāsīt
f tenādya tapsye bhṛśam aprameyaṃ
f yan mitravargo narakaṃ praviṣṭaḥ
f tadaiva vācyo 'smi nanu tvayāhaṃ
f na yotsye 'haṃ sūtaputraṃ kathaṃ cit
f tato nāhaṃ sṛñjayān kekayāṃś ca
f samānayeyaṃ suhṛdo raṇāya
f evaṃ gate kiṃ ca mayādya śakyaṃ
f kāryaṃ kartuṃ nigrahe sūtajasya
f tathaiva rājñaś ca suyodhanasya
f ye cāpi māṃ yoddhukāmāḥ sametāḥ
f dhig astu majjīvitam adya kṛṣṇa
f yo 'haṃ vaśaṃ sūtaputrasya yātaḥ
f madhye kurūṇāṃ sasuyodhanānāṃ
f ye cāpy anye yoddhukāmāḥ sametāḥ
f ekas tu me bhīmaseno 'dya nātho
f yenābhipanno 'smi raṇe mahābhaye
f vimocya māṃ cāpi ruṣānvitas tataḥ
f śareṇa tīkṣṇena bibheda karṇam
f tyaktvā prāṇān samare bhīmasenaś
f cakre yuddhaṃ kurumukhyaiḥ sametaiḥ
f gadāgrahasto rudhirokṣitāṅgaś
f caran raṇe kāla ivāntakāle
f asau hi bhīmasya mahān ninādo
f muhur muhuḥ śrūyate dhārtarāṣṭraiḥ
f yadi sma jīvet samare nihantā
f mahārathānāṃ pravaro narottamaḥ
f tavābhimanyus tanayo 'dya pārtha
f na cāsmi gantā samare parābhavam
f athāpi jīvet samare ghaṭotkacas
f tathāpi nāhaṃ samare parāṅmukhaḥ
f bhīmasya putraḥ samarāgrayāyī
f mahāstravic cāpi tavānurūpaḥ
f yatnaṃ samāsādya ripor balaṃ no
f nimīlitākṣaṃ bhayaviplutaṃ bhavet
f cakāra yo 'sau niśi yuddham ekas
f tyaktvā raṇaṃ yasya bhayād dravante
f sa cet samāsādya mahānubhāvaḥ
f karṇaṃ raṇe bāṇagaṇaiḥ pramohya
f dhairye sthitenāpi ca sūtajena
f śaktyā hato vāsavadattayā tayā
f mamaiva bhāgyāni purā kṛtāni
f pāpāni nūnaṃ phalavanti yuddhe
f tṛṇaṃ ca kṛtvā samare bhavantaṃ
f tato 'ham evaṃ nikṛto durātmanā
f vaikartaneneha tathā kṛto 'haṃ
f yathā hy aśaktaḥ kriyate hy abāndhavaḥ
f āpadgataṃ yaś ca naraṃ vimokṣayet
f sa bāndhavaḥ snehayutaḥ suhṛd vai
f evaṃ purāṇā ṛṣayo vadanti
f dharmaḥ sadā sadbhir anuṣṭhitaś ca
a dhanuś caitat keśavāya pradāya
yantābhaviṣyas tvaṃ raṇe ced durātman
c tato 'haniṣyat keśavaḥ karṇam ugraṃ
marutpatir vṛtram ivāttavajraḥ
d rādheyam evaṃ yadi cāpy aśaktaś
d carantam ugraṃ pratibodhanāya
d yacchānyasmai gāṇḍivam etad adya
d tvatto yo 'strair abhyadhiko narendraḥ
d tasmān naivaṃ putradārair vihīnān
d sukhād bhraṣṭān rājyanāśāc ca bhūyaḥ
d draṣṭā lokaḥ patitān apy agādhe
d pāpair juṣṭe narake pāṇḍaveya
d rathe sthitaḥ phālguna keśavas te
d raśmī samādāya raṇe prayātu
d jahi tvam adyaiva sametya karṇaṃ
d caidyaṃ yathā keśavo rājamadhye
a māse 'patiṣyaḥ pañcame tvaṃ prakṛcchre
na vā garbho 'py abhaviṣyaḥ pṛthāyāḥ
c tat te śramo rājaputrābhaviṣyan
na saṃgrāmād apayātuṃ durātman
d dhig gāṇḍivaṃ dhik ca te bāhuvīryam
d asaṃkhyeyān bāṇagaṇāṃś ca dhik te
d dhik te ketuḥ kesariṇaḥ sutasya
d kṛśānudattaṃ ca rathaṃ ca te dhik
 saṃjaya uvāca
a yudhiṣṭhireṇaivam uktaḥ kaunteyaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ
c asiṃ jagrāha saṃkruddho jighāṃsur bharatarṣabham
a tasya kopaṃ samudvīkṣya cittajñaḥ keśavas tadā
c uvāca kim idaṃ pārtha gṛhītaḥ khaḍga ity uta
a neha paśyāmi yoddhavyaṃ tava kiṃ cid dhanaṃjaya
c te dhvastā dhārtarāṣṭrā hi sarve bhīmena dhīmatā
a apayāto 'si kaunteya rājā draṣṭavya ity api
c sa rājā bhavatā dṛṣṭaḥ kuśalī ca yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā nṛpaśārdūlaṃ śārdūlasamavikramam
c harṣakāle tu saṃprāpte kasmāt tvā manyur āviśat
a na taṃ paśyāmi kaunteya yas te vadhyo bhaved iha
b prahartum icchase kasmāt kiṃ vā te cittavibhramaḥ
c kasmād bhavān mahākhaḍgaṃ parigṛhṇāti satvaram
a tat tvā pṛcchāmi kaunteya kim idaṃ te cikīrṣitam
c parāmṛśasi yat kruddhaḥ khaḍgam adbhutavikrama
a evam uktas tu kṛṣṇena prekṣamāṇo yudhiṣṭhiram
c arjunaḥ prāha govindaṃ kruddhaḥ sarpa iva śvasan
a dada gāṇḍīvam anyasmā iti māṃ yo 'bhicodayet
c chindyām ahaṃ śiras tasya ity upāṃśuvrataṃ mama
d yudhiṣṭhireṇa tenāham uktaś cāsmi janārdana
a tad ukto 'ham adīnātman rājñāmitaparākrama
c samakṣaṃ tava govinda na tat kṣantum ihotsahe
a tasmād enaṃ vadhiṣyāmi rājānaṃ dharmabhīrukam
c pratijñāṃ pālayiṣyāmi hatvemaṃ narasattamam
e etadarthaṃ mayā khaḍgo gṛhīto yadunandana
a so 'haṃ yudhiṣṭhiraṃ hatvā satye 'py ānṛṇyatāṃ gataḥ
c viśoko vijvaraś cāpi bhaviṣyāmi janārdana
a kiṃ vā tvaṃ manyase prāptam asmin kāle samutthite
c tvam asya jagatas tāta vettha sarvaṃ gatāgatam
d jātas tvatto hi dharmaś cādharmaś ceti parā śrutiḥ
e tat tathā prakariṣyāmi yathā māṃ vakṣyate bhavān
f saṃjaya uvāca
f dhig dhig ity eva govindaḥ pārtham uktvābravīt punaḥ
 kṛṣṇa uvāca
a idānīṃ pārtha jānāmi na vṛddhāḥ sevitās tvayā
c akāle puruṣavyāghra saṃrambhakriyayānayā
e na hi dharmavibhāgajñaḥ kuryād evaṃ dhanaṃjaya
f yathā tvaṃ pāṇḍavādyeha dharmabhīrur apaṇḍitaḥ
a akāryāṇāṃ ca kāryāṇāṃ saṃyogaṃ yaḥ karoti vai
c kāryāṇām akriyāṇāṃ ca sa pārtha puruṣādhamaḥ
a anusṛtya tu ye dharmaṃ kavayaḥ samupasthitāḥ
c samāsavistaravidāṃ na teṣāṃ vettha niścayam
a aniścayajño hi naraḥ kāryākāryaviniścaye
c avaśo muhyate pārtha yathā tvaṃ mūḍha eva tu
a na hi kāryam akāryaṃ vā sukhaṃ jñātuṃ kathaṃ cana
c śrutena jñāyate sarvaṃ tac ca tvaṃ nāvabudhyase
a avijñānād bhavān yac ca dharmaṃ rakṣati dharmavit
c prāṇināṃ hi vadhaṃ pārtha dhārmiko nāvabudhyate
a prāṇinām avadhas tāta sarvajyāyān mato mama
c anṛtaṃ tu bhaved vācyaṃ na ca hiṃsyāt kathaṃ cana
a sa kathaṃ bhrātaraṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ rājānaṃ dharmakovidam
c hanyād bhavān naraśreṣṭha prākṛto 'nyaḥ pumān iva
a ayudhyamānasya vadhas tathāśastrasya bhārata
c parāṅmukhasya dravataḥ śaraṇaṃ vābhigacchataḥ
e kṛtāñjaleḥ prapannasya na vadhaḥ pūjyate budhaiḥ
e   pramattasya tathaiva ca
e na vadhaḥ pūjyate sadbhis tac ca sarvaṃ gurau tava
a tvayā caiva vrataṃ pārtha bālenaiva kṛtaṃ purā
c tasmād adharmasaṃyuktaṃ mauḍhyāt karma vyavasyasi
a sa guruṃ pārtha kasmāt tvaṃ hanyā dharmam anusmaran
c asaṃpradhārya dharmāṇāṃ gatiṃ sūkṣmāṃ duranvayām
a idaṃ dharmarahasyaṃ ca vakṣyāmi bharatarṣabha
c yad brūyāt tava bhīṣmo vā dharmajño vā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a viduro vā tathā kṣattā kuntī vāpi yaśasvinī
b kuntī vā bharataśreṣṭha draupadī vā yaśasvinī
c tat te vakṣyāmi tattvena tan nibodha dhanaṃjaya
a satyasya vacanaṃ sādhu na satyād vidyate param
c tattvenaitat sudurjñeyaṃ yasya satyam anuṣṭhitam
a bhavet satyam avaktavyaṃ vaktavyam anṛtaṃ bhavet
c sarvasvasyāpahāre tu vaktavyam anṛtaṃ bhavet
a prāṇātyaye vivāhe ca vaktavyam anṛtaṃ bhavet
c yatrānṛtaṃ bhavet satyaṃ satyaṃ cāpy anṛtaṃ bhavet
d vivāhakāle ratisaṃprayoge
d prāṇātyaye sarvadhanāpahāre
d viprasya cārthe hy anṛtaṃ vadeta
d pañcānṛtāny āhur apātakāni
a tādṛśaṃ paśyate bālo yasya satyam anuṣṭhitam
b bhavet satyam avaktavyaṃ na vaktavyam anuṣṭhitam
c satyānṛte viniścitya tato bhavati dharmavit
a kim āścaryaṃ kṛtaprajñaḥ puruṣo 'pi sudāruṇaḥ
c sumahat prāpnuyāt puṇyaṃ balāko 'ndhavadhād iva
a kim āścaryaṃ punar mūḍho dharmakāmo 'py apaṇḍitaḥ
c sumahat prāpnuyāt pāpam āpagām iva kauśikaḥ
 arjuna uvāca
a ācakṣva bhagavann etad yathā vidyām ahaṃ tathā
c balākāndhābhisaṃbaddhaṃ nadīnāṃ kauśikasya ca
 kṛṣṇa uvāca
a mṛgavyādho 'bhavat kaś cid balāko nāma bhārata
c yātrārthaṃ putradārasya mṛgān hanti na kāmataḥ
a so 'ndhau ca mātāpitarau bibharty anyāṃś ca saṃśritān
c svadharmanirato nityaṃ satyavāg anasūyakaḥ
a sa kadā cin mṛgāṃl lipsur nānvavindat prayatnavān
c athāpaśyat sa pītodaṃ śvāpadaṃ ghrāṇacakṣuṣam
a adṛṣṭapūrvam api tat sattvaṃ tena hataṃ tadā
c anv eva ca tato vyomnaḥ puṣpavarṣam avāpatat
a apsarogītavāditrair nāditaṃ ca manoramam
c vimānam āgamat svargān mṛgavyādhaninīṣayā
a tad bhūtaṃ sarvabhūtānām abhāvāya kilārjuna
c tapas taptvā varaṃ prāptaṃ kṛtam andhaṃ svayaṃbhuvā
a tad dhatvā sarvabhūtānām abhāvakṛtaniścayam
c tato balākaḥ svaragād evaṃ dharmaḥ sudurvidaḥ
a kauśiko 'py abhavad vipras tapasvī na bahuśrutaḥ
c nadīnāṃ saṃgame grāmād adūre sa kilāvasat
a satyaṃ mayā sadā vācyam iti tasyābhavad vratam
c satyavādīti vikhyātaḥ sa tadāsīd dhanaṃjaya
a atha dasyubhayāt ke cit tadā tad vanam āviśan
c dasyavo 'pi gatāḥ krūrā vyamārganta prayatnataḥ
a atha kauśikam abhyetya prāhus taṃ satyavādinam
c katamena pathā yātā bhagavan bahavo janāḥ
e satyena pṛṣṭaḥ prabrūhi yadi tān vettha śaṃsa naḥ
a sa pṛṣṭaḥ kauśikaḥ satyaṃ vacanaṃ tān uvāca ha
b satyasya tv avibhāgajñaḥ satyaṃ tebhyaḥ śaśaṃsa saḥ
c bahuvṛkṣalatāgulmam etad vanam upāśritāḥ
d iti tān khyāpayām āsa sa tebhyaḥ pārtha kauśikaḥ
e tatas te tān samāsādya krūrā jaghnur iti śrutiḥ
a tenādharmeṇa mahatā vāgduruktena kauśikaḥ
c gataḥ sukaṣṭaṃ narakaṃ sūkṣmadharmeṣv akovidaḥ
e aprabhūtaśruto mūḍho dharmāṇām avibhāgavit
a vṛddhān apṛṣṭvā saṃdehaṃ mahac chvabhram ito 'rhati
c tatra te lakṣaṇoddeśaḥ kaś cid eva bhaviṣyati
a duṣkaraṃ paramajñānaṃ tarkeṇātra vyavasyati
c śrutir dharma iti hy eke vadanti bahavo janāḥ
a na tv etat pratisūyāmi na hi sarvaṃ vidhīyate
b śrutir dhāryeyam ity eke vadanti bahavo janāḥ
b na tān pārthābhyasūyāmi na ca sarvatra śiṣyati
b smṛtir dhāryā iti tv eke vadanti bahavo janāḥ
b na tu tān pratyasūyāmi nātra sarvaṃ vidhīyate
c prabhavārthāya bhūtānāṃ dharmapravacanaṃ kṛtam
d evaṃvidhā gatir vīra dharmasyātīva durdṛśā
d vidyāśīlavayovṛddhān anupāsyānadhītya vā
d manvādīnāṃ tu kṛtsnaṃ vai ko dharmaṃ vaktum arhati
d adharmād eva bhavati dharme 'pi ca mahān yathā
d vyādhakauśikayor yadvad dharmādharmaviruddhayoḥ
d vedo mūlaṃ hi dharmāṇām iti santo yad abruvan
d jijñāsate hi vidyānāṃ sādhanāny eva tattvavit
d vedaṃ brāhmaṇam āsādya puṇyapāpe paraṃtapa
d sa tu vetti paraṃ dharmam ahiṃsāṃ vetti bhārata
d yat syād ahiṃsāsaṃyuktaṃ sa dharma iti niścayaḥ
d ahiṃsārthāya bhūtānāṃ dharmapravacanaṃ kṛtam
a dhāraṇād dharmam ity āhur dharmo dhārayati prajāḥ
c yaḥ syād dhāraṇasaṃyuktaḥ sa dharma iti niścayaḥ
a ye 'nyāyena jihīrṣanto janā icchanti karhi cit
c akūjanena cen mokṣo nātra kūjet kathaṃ cana
a avaśyaṃ kūjitavyaṃ vā śaṅkeran vāpy akūjataḥ
c śreyas tatrānṛtaṃ vaktuṃ satyād iti vicāritam
d yaḥ kāryebhyo vrataṃ kṛtvā karmaṇā nopapādayet
d na tat phalam avāpnoti evam āhur manīṣiṇaḥ
d satye sati na pāpebhyo dhanaṃ deyaṃ kadā cana
a prāṇātyaye vivāhe vā sarvajñātidhanakṣaye
c narmaṇy abhipravṛtte vā pravaktavyaṃ mṛṣā bhavet
e adharmaṃ nātra paśyanti dharmatattvārthadarśinaḥ
f sarvadā hi vadet tat tu nānṛtaḥ syād vicakṣaṇaḥ
a yaḥ stenaiḥ saha saṃbandhān mucyate śapathair api
c śreyas tatrānṛtaṃ vaktuṃ tat satyam avicāritam
a na ca tebhyo dhanaṃ deyaṃ śakye sati kathaṃ cana
c pāpebhyo hi dhanaṃ dattaṃ dātāram api pīḍayet
e tasmād dharmārtham anṛtam uktvā nānṛtavāg bhavet
a eṣa te lakṣaṇoddeśaḥ samuddiṣṭo yathāvidhi
b yathādharmaṃ yathābuddhi mayā pārthārthitas tava
c etac chrutvā brūhi pārtha yadi vadhyo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
 arjuna uvāca
a yathā brūyān mahāprājño yathā brūyān mahāmatiḥ
c hitaṃ caiva yathāsmākaṃ tathaitad vacanaṃ tava
a bhavān mātṛsamo 'smākaṃ tathā pitṛsamo 'pi ca
c gatiś ca paramā kṛṣṇa tena te vākyam adbhutam
a na hi te triṣu lokeṣu vidyate 'viditaṃ kva cit
c tasmād bhavān paraṃ dharmaṃ veda sarvaṃ yathātatham
a avadhyaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ manye dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
c tasmin samayasaṃyoge brūhi kiṃ cid anugraham
e idaṃ cāparam atraiva śṛṇu hṛtsthaṃ vivakṣitam
a jānāsi dāśārha mama vrataṃ tvaṃ
yo māṃ brūyāt kaś cana mānuṣeṣu
c anyasmai tvaṃ gāṇḍivaṃ dehi pārtha
yas tvatto 'strair bhavitā vā viśiṣṭaḥ
a hanyām ahaṃ keśava taṃ prasahya
bhīmo hanyāt tūbaraketi coktaḥ
c tan me rājā proktavāṃs te samakṣaṃ
dhanur dehīty asakṛd vṛṣṇisiṃha
a taṃ hatvā cet keśava jīvaloke
sthātā kālaṃ nāham apy alpamātram
b evaṃ tvaṃ māṃ kṛṣṇa jānāsi sarvaṃ
b kālaṃ loke hīnadharmo hi jīvan
b satyāc cyuto lokam imaṃ tyajeyaṃ
b tasmāt krodhāt pratikṣapeyaṃ dharmaputram
b dhyātvā nūnaṃ hy enasā cāpi mukto
b vadhaṃ rājño bhraṣṭavīryo vicetāḥ
c sā ca pratijñā mama lokaprabuddhā
bhavet satyā dharmabhṛtāṃ variṣṭha
e yathā jīvet pāṇḍavo 'haṃ ca kṛṣṇa
tathā buddhiṃ dātum adyārhasi tvam
f evaṃ jñātvā yad dhitaṃ me sadaiva
f tathārhasi tvaṃ tu nibodhituṃ ca
 vāsudeva uvāca
a rājā śrānto jagato vikṣataś ca
karṇena saṃkhye niśitair bāṇasaṃghaiḥ
a śarārditaḥ sūtaputreṇa caiva
b yaś cāniśaṃ sūtaputreṇa vīra
b śarair bhṛśaṃ tāḍito yudhyamānaḥ
b atas tvam etena saroṣamukto
b duḥkhānvite nedam ayuktarūpam
b akopito hy eṣa yadi sma saṃkhye
b karṇaṃ na hanyād iti cābravīc ca
b jānāti taṃ pāṇḍava eṣa cāpi
b pāpaṃ loke karṇam asahyam anyaiḥ
b tatas tvam ukto bhṛśaroṣitena
b rājñā samakṣaṃ paruṣāṇi pārtha
b bhṛśārditaś cāpi mahāmanasvī
c tasmāt pārtha tvāṃ paruṣāṇy avocat
karṇe dyūtaṃ hy adya raṇe nibaddham
a tasmin hate kuravo nirjitāḥ syur
evaṃbuddhiḥ pārthivo dharmaputraḥ
b tato vadhaṃ nārhati dharmaputras
b tvayā pratijñārjuna pālanīyā
b jīvann ayaṃ yena mṛto bhaved dhi
b tan me nibodheha tavānurūpam
b yadā mānaṃ labhate mānanārhas
b tadā sa vai jīvati jīvaloke
c yadāvamānaṃ labhate mahāntaṃ
tadā jīvan mṛta ity ucyate saḥ
a tan mānitaḥ pārthivo 'yaṃ sadaiva
tvayā sabhīmena tathā yamābhyām
c vṛddhaiś ca loke puruṣapravīrais
tasyāvamānaṃ kalayā tvaṃ prayuṅkṣva
d yad idaṃ dharmaśāstrārthaṃ vedeṣu ca nidarśanam
d śṛṇu pārtha yathā nityo hataḥ syād bhavatā guruḥ
d hato bhavety evam ukto guruḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
a tvam ity atrabhavantaṃ tvaṃ brūhi pārtha yudhiṣṭhiram
c tvam ity ukto hi nihato gurur bhavati bhārata
a evam ācara kaunteya dharmarāje yudhiṣṭhire
c adharmayuktaṃ saṃyogaṃ kuruṣvaivaṃ kurūdvaha
a atharvāṅgirasī hy eṣā śrutīnām uttamā śrutiḥ
c avicāryaiva kāryaiṣā śreyaḥkāmair naraiḥ sadā
d avadhena vadhaḥ prokto yad gurus tvam iti prabhuḥ
d tad brūhi tvaṃ yan mayoktaṃ dharmarājasya dharmavit
a vadho hy ayaṃ pāṇḍava dharmarājñas
tvatto yukto vetsyate caivam eṣaḥ
c tato 'sya pādāv abhivādya paścāc
chamaṃ brūyāḥ sāntvapūrvaṃ ca pārtham
a bhrātā prājñas tava kopaṃ na jātu
kuryād rājā kaṃ cana pāṇḍaveyaḥ
c mukto 'nṛtād bhrātṛvadhāc ca pārtha
hṛṣṭaḥ karṇaṃ tvaṃ jahi sūtaputram
 saṃjaya uvāca
a ity evam uktas tu janārdanena
pārthaḥ praśasyātha suhṛdvadhaṃ tam
c tato 'bravīd arjuno dharmarājam
anuktapūrvaṃ paruṣaṃ prasahya
a mā tvaṃ rājan vyāhara vyāharatsu
na tiṣṭhase krośamātre raṇārdhe
b mā vocas tvaṃ kiṃ cid ihādya rājaṃs
b tyaktvā yuddhaṃ ya iha vyavasthitas tvam
c bhīmas tu mām arhati garhaṇāya
yo yudhyate sarvayodhapravīraḥ
a kāle hi śatrūn pratipīḍya saṃkhye
hatvā ca śūrān pṛthivīpatīṃs tān
b rathapradhānottamanāgamukhyān
b sādipravekān amitāṃś ca śūrān
c yaḥ kuñjarāṇām adhikaṃ sahasraṃ
hatvānadat tumulaṃ siṃhanādam
d kāmbojānām ayuta pārvatīyān
d mṛgān siṃho vinihatyeva cājau
a suduṣkaraṃ karma karoti vīraḥ
kartuṃ yathā nārhasi tvaṃ kadā cit
c rathād avaplutya gadāṃ parāmṛśaṃs
tayā nihanty aśvanaradvipān raṇe
a varāsinā vājirathāśvakuñjarāṃs
tathā rathāṅgair dhanuṣā ca hanty arīn
c pramṛdya padbhyām ahitān nihanti yaḥ
punaś ca dorbhyāṃ śatamanyuvikramaḥ
a mahābalo vaiśravaṇāntakopamaḥ
prasahya hantā dviṣatāṃ yathārham
c sa bhīmaseno 'rhati garhaṇāṃ me
na tvaṃ nityaṃ rakṣyase yaḥ suhṛdbhiḥ
a mahārathān nāgavarān hayāṃś ca
padātimukhyān api ca pramathya
c eko bhīmo dhārtarāṣṭreṣu magnaḥ
sa mām upālabdhum ariṃdamo 'rhati
a kaliṅgavaṅgāṅganiṣādamāgadhān
sadāmadān nīlabalāhakopamān
c nihanti yaḥ śatrugaṇān anekaśaḥ
sa mābhivaktuṃ prabhavaty anāgasam
a suyuktam āsthāya rathaṃ hi kāle
dhanur vikarṣañ śarapūrṇamuṣṭiḥ
c sṛjaty asau śaravarṣāṇi vīro
mahāhave megha ivāmbudhārāḥ
d śatāny aṣṭau vāraṇānām apaśyaṃ
d viśātitaiḥ kumbhakarāgrahastaiḥ
d bhīmenājau nihatāny adya bāṇaiḥ
d sa māṃ krūraṃ vaktum arhaty arighnaḥ
d mahārathānām ayutaṃ supūrṇam
d athāśvānām ayutāni ṣaṭ ca
d padātisaṃghān bahuśo vimṛdya
d vīrān hatvā śataśo 'thāpramādī
d prāṇāṃs tyaktvā dustyajān ājimadhye
d saṃyuddhe yo vairibhir bhīmasenaḥ
d yo bhīmaseno nihatārisaṃghaḥ
d sa mām upālabdhum ariṃdamo 'rhati
d rathāś ca nāgāś ca hayāś ca rājan
d bhīmenājau nihatāḥ saṃghaśo 'dya
d rājānaś ca bahavo mahābalāḥ
d sa mām upālabdhum ariṃdamo 'rhati
d dhṛtarāṣṭraputrā balinaś ca yena
d mahābalā nihatāḥ prāyaśo vai
d śūro yuddheṣv aprativāryavīryaḥ
d sa mām upālabdhum ariṃdamo 'rhati
d pratāpayaṃs tad balam ugrarūpaṃ
d yo 'sau raṇe dhārtarāṣṭrasya vīraḥ
d ekaḥ sahetāpratisahyapauruṣas
d tenāsmi vācyo na tvayā vai kadā cit
d mahārathā yatra yatraiva yuddhe
d bhindanti sainyaṃ tava kāmato 'dya
d tatraiva tatraiva raṇe mahātmā
d dṛḍhaṃ bhīmaḥ parasaṃghān amṛdnāt
d tenāsmi vācyo na tvayāhaṃ kadā cit
d mā mā vocaḥ krūram ihādya pārtha
d nāsmadvidho vai bhavatā tu vācyo
d yathā bhavān sarvalokasya vācyaḥ
d evaṃ hi mā te bruvato narendra
d kathaṃ na dīryec chatadhādya jihvā
d aho batedaṃ sunṛśaṃsarūpaṃ
d bhavān api hy atra karṇād bibheti
a balaṃ tu vāci dvijasattamānāṃ
kṣātraṃ budhā bāhubalaṃ vadanti
c tvaṃ vāgbalo bhārata niṣṭhuraś ca
tvam eva māṃ vetsi yathāvidho 'ham
d nakulena rājan gajavājiyodhā
d hatāś ca śūrāḥ sahasā sametya
d tyaktvā prāṇān samare yuddhakāṅkṣī
d sa mām upālabdhum ariṃdamo 'rhati
d kṛtaṃ karma sahadevena duṣkaraṃ
d yo yudhyate parasainyāvamardī
d na cābravīt kiṃ cid ihāgato balī
d paśyāntaraṃ tasya caivātmanaś ca
d dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ sātyakir draupadeyā
d yudhāmanyuś cottamaujāḥ śikhaṇḍī
d ete 'dya sarve yudhi saṃprapīḍitās
d te mām upālabdhum arhanti na tvam
d tvanmūlam asmābhir idaṃ hi vairaṃ
d prāptaṃ tathā vyasanaṃ cātighoram
d dyūte pramattena kṛtaṃ tvayāsakṛt
d kasmād upālabdhum ihārhasi tvam
d tvam eva rājan satataṃ pramattas
d tvam eva mūḍho bhāratānām asādhuḥ
d tvāṃ prāpya rājyaṃ ca vinaṣṭam etat
d prāptā mahat pāṇḍavāś caiva dāsyam
d tvattaḥ kṛte syād vanavāsaduḥkhaṃ
d rājyasya nāśo hy abhimanyoś ca ghoraḥ
d ātmānam evaṃ sunṛśaṃsarūpaṃ
d jñātvā kimarthaṃ garhase mādya vīra
d lajjasva rājan yadi te 'sti lajjā
d tūṣṇīṃ bhūtaḥ paśya sarvaṃ kṛtaṃ naḥ
d bhīmo nityaṃ samarasya kartā
d darpasya bhettā punar eva nityam
d svayaṃ hy aśaktena narendra yuddhe
d nareṇa kāryā satataṃ kṣamaiva
a yatāmi nityaṃ tava kartum iṣṭaṃ
dāraiḥ sutair jīvitenātmanā ca
c evaṃ ca māṃ vāgviśikhair nihaṃsi
tvattaḥ sukhaṃ na vayaṃ vidma kiṃ cit
a avāmaṃsthā māṃ draupadītalpasaṃstho
mahārathān pratihanmi tvadarthe
c tenātiśaṅkī bhārata niṣṭhuro 'si
tvattaḥ sukhaṃ nābhijānāmi kiṃ cit
a proktaḥ svayaṃ satyasaṃdhena mṛtyus
tava priyārthaṃ naradeva yuddhe
c vīraḥ śikhaṇḍī draupado 'sau mahātmā
mayābhiguptena hataś ca tena
d droṇo hato yaḥ satatopakārī
d dhṛṣṭadyumnena syandanād viprakṛṣya
d drauṇiś ca kruddho sagaṇo mahātmā
d tathāpi te vai vacanaṃ nṛśaṃsavat
d duḥkhaṃ priyaṃ te naradeva kartuṃ
d yasya priyaṃ te na karomy ahaṃ vai
d na mucyate vai divi ceha vā pumān
d yas te mad anyo 'priyam ārabheta
a na cābhinandāmi tavādhirājyaṃ
yatas tvam akṣeṣv ahitāya saktaḥ
c svayaṃ kṛtvā pāpam anāryajuṣṭam
ebhir yuddhe tartum icchasy arīṃs tu
a akṣeṣu doṣā bahavo vidharmāḥ
śrutās tvayā sahadevo 'bravīd yān
c tān naiṣi saṃtartum asādhujuṣṭān
yena sma sarve nirayaṃ prapannāḥ
d sukhaṃ tvatto nābhijānīma kiṃ cid
d yatas tvam akṣair devituṃ saṃpravṛttaḥ
d svayaṃ kṛtvā paruṣaṃ pāṇḍava tvaṃ
d bhūyas tīkṣṇāḥ śrāvayasy adya vācaḥ
d śete 'smābhir nihatā śatrusenā
d chinnair gātrair bhūmitale nadantī
d tvayā hi tat karma kṛtaṃ nṛśaṃsaṃ
d yasmād doṣaḥ kauravāṇāṃ vadhaś ca
d hatā udīcyā nihatāḥ pratīcyā
d naṣṭāḥ prācyā dākṣiṇātyā viśastāḥ
d kṛtaṃ karmāpratirūpaṃ mahadbhis
d teṣāṃ yodhair asmadīyaiś ca yuddhe
a tvaṃ devitā tvatkṛte rājyanāśas
tvat saṃbhavaṃ vyasanaṃ no narendra
c māsmān krūrair vākpratodais tuda tvaṃ
bhūyo rājan kopayann alpabhāgyān
a etā vācaḥ paruṣāḥ savyasācī
sthiraprajñaṃ śrāvayitvā tatakṣa
b babhūvāsau vimanā dharmabhīruḥ
b kṛtvā prājñaḥ pātakaṃ kiṃ cid evam
b viniśvasañ jyeṣṭham aniṣṭam uktvā
b tatas tu kośād asim udbabarha
b samuddadhārāsim udārakarmā
b nihantum ātmānam amitrasāham
c tadānutepe surarājaputro
viniḥśvasaṃś cāpy asim udbabarha
a tam āha kṛṣṇaḥ kim idaṃ punar bhavān
vikośam ākāśanibhaṃ karoty asim
c prabrūhi satyaṃ punar uttaraṃ vidher
vacaḥ pravakṣyāmy aham arthasiddhaye
a ity eva pṛṣṭaḥ puruṣottamena
suduḥkhitaḥ keśavam āha vākyam
c ahaṃ haniṣye svaśarīram eva
prasahya yenāhitam ācaraṃ vai
a niśamya tat pārthavaco 'bravīd idaṃ
dhanaṃjayaṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ variṣṭhaḥ
b rājānam enaṃ tvam itīdam uktvā
b kiṃ kaśmalaṃ prāviśaḥ pārtha ghoram
b tvaṃ cātmānaṃ hantum icchasy arighna
b nedaṃ sadbhiḥ sevitaṃ vai kirīṭin
b dharmātmānaṃ bhrātaraṃ jyeṣṭham adya
b khaḍgena cainaṃ yadi hanyā nṛvīra
b dharmād bhītas tat kathaṃ nāma te syāt
b kiṃ cottaraṃ vākariṣyas tvam eva
b sūkṣmo dharmo durvidaś cāpi pārtha
b viśeṣato 'jñaiḥ procyamānaṃ nibodha
b hatvātmānam ātmanā prāpnuyās tvaṃ
b vadhād bhrātur narakaṃ cātighoram
c prabrūhi pārtha svaguṇān ihātmanas
tathā svahārdaṃ bhavatīha sadyaḥ
a tathāstu kṛṣṇety abhinandya vākyaṃ
dhanaṃjayaḥ prāha dhanur vināmya
c yudhiṣṭhiraṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ variṣṭhaṃ
śṛṇuṣva rājann iti śakrasūnuḥ
a na mādṛśo 'nyo naradeva vidyate
dhanurdharo devam ṛte pinākinam
c ahaṃ hi tenānumato mahātmanā
kṣaṇena hanyāṃ sacarācaraṃ jagat
a mayā hi rājan sadigīśvarā diśo
vijitya sarvā bhavataḥ kṛtā vaśe
c sa rājasūyaś ca samāptadakṣiṇaḥ
sabhā ca divyā bhavato mamaujasā
a pāṇau pṛṣatkā likhitā mameme
dhanuś ca saṃkhye vitataṃ sabāṇam
c pādau ca me saśarau sahadhvajau
na mādṛśaṃ yuddhagataṃ jayanti
a hatā udīcyā nihatāḥ pratīcyāḥ
prācyā nirastā dākṣiṇātyā viśastāḥ
c saṃśaptakānāṃ kiṃ cid evāvaśiṣṭaṃ
sarvasya sainyasya hataṃ mayārdham
a śete mayā nihatā bhāratī ca
camū rājan devacamūprakāśā
c ye nāstrajñās tān ahaṃ hanmi śastrais
tasmāl lokaṃ neha karomi bhasmasāt
d jaitraṃ rathaṃ bhīmam āsthāya kṛṣṇa
d prayāva śīghraṃ sūtaputraṃ nihantum
d rājā bhavatv adya sunirvṛto 'yaṃ
d karṇaṃ raṇe nāśayitāsmi bāṇaiḥ
a ity evam uktvā punar āha pārtho
yudhiṣṭhiraṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ variṣṭham
b vimuktaśastrāstradhanur visṛjya
b kośe ca khaḍgaṃ vinidhāya tūrṇam
b sa vrīḍayā namraśirāḥ kirīṭī
b yudhiṣṭhiraṃ prāñjalir abhyuvāca
c apy aputrā tena rādhā bhavitrī
kuntī mayā vā tad ṛtaṃ viddhi rājan
d satyaṃ vadāmy adya na karṇam ājau
d śarair ahatvā kavacaṃ vimokṣye
e prasīda rājan kṣama yan mayoktaṃ
kāle bhavān vetsyati tan namas te
a prasādya rājānam amitrasāhaṃ
sthito 'bravīc cainam abhiprapannaḥ
c yāmy eṣa bhīmaṃ samarāt pramoktuṃ
sarvātmanā sūtaputraṃ ca hantum
a tava priyārthaṃ mama jīvitaṃ hi
bravīmi satyaṃ tad avehi rājan
c iti prāyād upasaṃgṛhya pādau
samutthito dīptatejāḥ kirīṭī
e nedaṃ cirāt kṣipram idaṃ bhaviṣyaty
āvartate 'sāv abhiyāmi cainam
a etac chrutvā pāṇḍavo dharmarājo
bhrātur vākyaṃ paruṣaṃ phalgunasya
c utthāya tasmāc chayanād uvāca
pārthaṃ tato duḥkhaparītacetāḥ
a kṛtaṃ mayā pārtha yathā na sādhu
yena prāptaṃ vyasanaṃ vaḥ sughoram
c tasmāc chiraś chinddhi mamedam adya
kulāntakasyādhamapūruṣasya
a pāpasya pāpavyasanānvitasya
vimūḍhabuddher alasasya bhīroḥ
c vṛddhāvamantuḥ paruṣasya caiva
kiṃ te ciraṃ mām anuvṛtya rūkṣam
a gacchāmy ahaṃ vanam evādya pāpaḥ
sukhaṃ bhavān vartatāṃ madvihīnaḥ
c yogyo rājā bhīmaseno mahātmā
klībasya vā mama kiṃ rājyakṛtyam
a na cāsmi śaktaḥ paruṣāṇi soḍhuṃ
punas tavemāni ruṣānvitasya
c bhīmo 'stu rājā mama jīvitena
kiṃ kāryam adyāvamatasya vīra
a ity evam uktvā sahasotpapāta
rājā tatas tac chayanaṃ vihāya
c iyeṣa nirgantum atho vanāya
taṃ vāsudevaḥ praṇato 'bhyuvāca
a rājan viditam etat te yathā gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ
c pratijñā satyasaṃdhasya gāṇḍīvaṃ prati viśrutā
a brūyād ya evaṃ gāṇḍīvaṃ dehy anyasmai tvam ity uta
c sa vadhyo 'sya pumāṃl loke tvayā cokto 'yam īdṛśam
a ataḥ satyāṃ pratijñāṃ tāṃ pārthena parirakṣatā
c macchandād avamāno 'yaṃ kṛtas tava mahīpate
e gurūṇām avamāno hi vadha ity abhidhīyate
a tasmāt tvaṃ vai mahābāho mama pārthasya cobhayoḥ
c vyatikramam imaṃ rājan saṃkṣamasvārjunaṃ prati
a śaraṇaṃ tvāṃ mahārāja prapannau sva ubhāv api
c kṣantum arhasi me rājan praṇatasyābhiyācataḥ
a rādheyasyādya pāpasya bhūmiḥ pāsyati śoṇitam
c satyaṃ te pratijānāmi hataṃ viddhy adya sūtajam
e yasyecchasi vadhaṃ tasya gatam evādya jīvitam
a iti kṛṣṇavacaḥ śrutvā dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c sasaṃbhramaṃ hṛṣīkeśam utthāpya praṇataṃ tadā
e kṛtāñjalim idaṃ vākyam uvācānantaraṃ vacaḥ
a evam etad yathāttha tvam asty eṣo 'tikramo mama
c anunīto 'smi govinda tāritaś cādya mādhava
e mokṣitā vyasanād ghorād vayam adya tvayācyuta
a bhavantaṃ nātham āsādya āvāṃ vyasanasāgarāt
c ghorād adya samuttīrṇāv ubhāv ajñānamohitau
a tvadbuddhiplavam āsādya duḥkhaśokārṇavād vayam
c samuttīrṇāḥ sahāmātyāḥ sanāthāḥ sma tvayācyuta
 saṃjaya uvāca
 dharmarājasya tac chrutvā prītiyuktaṃ vacas tataḥ
 pārthaṃ provāca dharmātmā govindo yadunandanaḥ
a iti sma kṛṣṇavacanāt pratyuccārya yudhiṣṭhiram
c babhūva vimanāḥ pārthaḥ kiṃ cit kṛtveva pātakam
a tato 'bravīd vāsudevaḥ prahasann iva pāṇḍavam
c kathaṃ nāma bhaved etad yadi tvaṃ pārtha dharmajam
e asinā tīkṣṇadhāreṇa hanyā dharme vyavasthitam
a tvam ity uktvaiva rājānam evaṃ kaśmalam āviśaḥ
c hatvā tu nṛpatiṃ pārtha akariṣyaḥ kim uttaram
e evaṃ sudurvido dharmo mandaprajñair viśeṣataḥ
a sa bhavān dharmabhīrutvād dhruvam aiṣyan mahattamaḥ
c narakaṃ ghorarūpaṃ ca bhrātur jyeṣṭhasya vai vadhāt
a sa tvaṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ rājānaṃ dharmasaṃhitam
c prasādaya kuruśreṣṭham etad atra mataṃ mama
a prasādya bhaktyā rājānaṃ prītaṃ caiva yudhiṣṭhiram
c prayāmas tvaritā yoddhuṃ sūtaputrarathaṃ prati
a hatvā sudurjayaṃ karṇaṃ tvam adya niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c vipulāṃ prītim ādhatsva dharmaputrasya mānada
a etad atra mahābāho prāptakālaṃ mataṃ mama
c evaṃ kṛte kṛtaṃ caiva tava kāryaṃ bhaviṣyati
a tato 'rjuno mahārāja lajjayā vai samanvitaḥ
c dharmarājasya caraṇau prapede śirasānagha
a uvāca bharataśreṣṭha prasīdeti punaḥ punaḥ
c kṣamasva rājan yat proktaṃ dharmakāmena bhīruṇā
a pādayoḥ patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c dhanaṃjayam amitraghnaṃ rudantaṃ bharatarṣabha
a utthāpya bhrātaraṃ rājā dharmarājo dhanaṃjayam
c samāśliṣya ca sasnehaṃ praruroda mahīpatiḥ
a ruditvā tu ciraṃ kālaṃ bhrātarau sumahādyutī
c kṛtaśaucau naravyāghrau prītimantau babhūvatuḥ
a tata āśliṣya sa premṇā mūrdhni cāghrāya pāṇḍavam
c prītyā paramayā yuktaḥ prasmayaṃś cābravīj jayam
d abravīt taṃ maheṣvāsaṃ dharmarājo dhanaṃjayam
a karṇena me mahābāho sarvasainyasya paśyataḥ
c kavacaṃ ca dhvajaś caiva dhanuḥ śaktir hayā gadā
d hataḥ sūto dhanuś caiva rathaḥ śaktir dhvajaḥ śarāḥ
e śaraiḥ kṛttā maheṣvāsa yatamānasya saṃyuge
a so 'haṃ jñātvā raṇe tasya karma dṛṣṭvā ca phalguna
c vyavasīdāmi duḥkhena na ca me jīvitaṃ priyam
a tam adya yadi vai vīra na haniṣyasi sūtajam
c prāṇān eva parityakṣye jīvitārtho hi ko mama
a evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca vijayo bharatarṣabha
c satyena te śape rājan prasādena tavaiva ca
e bhīmena ca naraśreṣṭha yamābhyāṃ ca mahīpate
f aham enaṃ naraśreṣṭha sāmātyaṃ ca mahīpate
a yathādya samare karṇaṃ haniṣyāmi hato 'tha vā
c mahītale patiṣyāmi satyenāyudham ālabhe
a evam ābhāṣya rājānam abravīn mādhavaṃ vacaḥ
c adya karṇaṃ raṇe kṛṣṇa sūdayiṣye na saṃśayaḥ
e tad anudhyāhi bhadraṃ te vadhaṃ tasya durātmanaḥ
a evam ukto 'bravīt pārthaṃ keśavo rājasattama
c śakto 'smi bharataśreṣṭha yatnaṃ kartuṃ yathābalam
a evaṃ cāpi hi me kāmo nityam eva mahāratha
c kathaṃ bhavān raṇe karṇaṃ nihanyād iti me matiḥ
d evam uktas tato rājan pārtho vacanam abravīt
a bhūyaś covāca matimān mādhavo dharmanandanam
c yudhiṣṭhiremaṃ bībhatsuṃ tvaṃ sāntvayitum arhasi
e anujñātuṃ ca karṇasya vadhāyādya durātmanaḥ
a śrutvā hy ayam ahaṃ caiva tvāṃ karṇaśarapīḍitam
c pravṛttiṃ jñātum āyātāv iha pāṇḍavanandana
a diṣṭyāsi rājan nirujo diṣṭyā na grahaṇaṃ gataḥ
c parisāntvaya bībhatsuṃ jayam āśādhi cānagha
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a ehy ehi pārtha bībhatso māṃ pariṣvaja pāṇḍava
c vaktavyam ukto 'smy ahitaṃ tvayā kṣāntaṃ ca tan mayā
a ahaṃ tvām anujānāmi jahi karṇaṃ dhanaṃjaya
c manyuṃ ca mā kṛthāḥ pārtha yan mayokto 'si dāruṇam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tato dhanaṃjayo rājañ śirasā praṇatas tadā
c pādau jagrāha pāṇibhyāṃ bhrātur jyeṣṭhasya māriṣa
a samutthāpya tato rājā pariṣvajya ca pīḍitam
c mūrdhny upāghrāya caivainam idaṃ punar uvāca ha
a dhanaṃjaya mahābāho mānito 'smi dṛḍhaṃ tvayā
c māhātmyaṃ vijayaṃ caiva bhūyaḥ prāpnuhi śāśvatam
 arjuna uvāca
a adya taṃ pāpakarmāṇaṃ sānubandhaṃ raṇe śaraiḥ
c nayāmy antaṃ samāsādya rādheyaṃ balagarvitam
a yena tvaṃ pīḍito bāṇair dṛḍham āyamya kārmukam
c tasyādya karmaṇaḥ karṇaḥ phalaṃ prāpsyati dāruṇam
a adya tvām aham eṣyāmi karṇaṃ hatvā mahīpate
c sabhājayitum ākrandād iti satyaṃ bravīmi te
a nāhatvā vinivarte 'haṃ karṇam adya raṇājirāt
c iti satyena te pādau spṛśāmi jagatīpate
d saṃjaya uvāca
d iti bruvāṇaṃ sumanāḥ kirīṭinaṃ
d yudhiṣṭhiraḥ prāha vaco bṛhattaram
d yaśo 'kṣayaṃ jīvitam īpsitaṃ te
d jayaṃ sadā vīryam arikṣayaṃ tadā
d prayāhi vṛddhiṃ ca diśantu devatā
d yathāham icchāmi tavāstu tat tathā
d prayāhi śīghraṃ jahi karṇam āhave
d puraṃdaro vṛtra ivātmavṛddhaye
d rathe sthitaḥ phālguna keśavas te
d raśmīn samādāya raṇe prayātu
d jahi tvam adyaiva sametya karṇaṃ
d daityaṃ yathā keśavo rājamadhye
 saṃjaya uvāca
a prasādya dharmarājānaṃ prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā
c pārthaḥ provāca govindaṃ sūtaputravadhodyataḥ
a kalpyatāṃ ca ratho bhūyo yujyantāṃ ca hayottamāḥ
c āyudhāni ca sarvāṇi sajjyantāṃ vai mahārathe
a upāvṛttāś ca turagāḥ śikṣitāś cāśvasādinaḥ
c rathopakaraṇaiḥ sarvair upāyāntu tvarānvitāḥ
d prayātau svo 'dya govinda sūtaputrajighāṃsayā
a evam ukte mahārāja phalgunena mahātmanā
c uvāca dārukaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ kuru sarvaṃ yathābravīt
e arjuno bharataśreṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sarvadhanuṣmatām
a ājñaptas tv atha kṛṣṇena dāruko rājasattama
c yojayām āsa sa rathaṃ vaiyāghraṃ śatrutāpanam
d sajjaṃ nivedayām āsa pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ
a yuktaṃ tu ratham āsthāya dārukeṇa mahātmanā
b upasthitaṃ rathaṃ dṛṣṭvā padmanābho raṇāntakṛt
c āpṛcchya dharmarājānaṃ brāhmaṇān svasti vācya ca
e samaṅgalasvastyayanam āruroha rathottamam
a tasya rājā mahāprājño dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c āśiṣo 'yuṅkta paramā yuktāḥ karṇavadhaṃ prati
a taṃ prayāntaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhūtāni bhārata
c nihataṃ menire karṇaṃ pāṇḍavena mahātmanā
a babhūvur vimalāḥ sarvā diśo rājan samantataḥ
c cāṣāś ca śatapatrāś ca krauñcāś caiva janeśvara
e pradakṣiṇam akurvanta tadā vai pāṇḍunandanam
a bahavaḥ pakṣiṇo rājan puṃnāmānaḥ śubhāḥ śivāḥ
c tvarayanto 'rjunaṃ yuddhe hṛṣṭarūpā vavāśire
a kaṅkā gṛdhrā vaḍāś caiva vāyasāś ca viśāṃ pate
c agratas tasya gacchanti bhakṣyahetor bhayānakāḥ
a nimittāni ca dhanyāni pārthasya praśaśaṃsire
c vināśam arisainyānāṃ karṇasya ca vadhaṃ tathā
d nimittāni ca śubhrāṇi rutaṃ ca mṛgapakṣiṇām
a prayātasyātha pārthasya mahān svedo vyajāyata
c cintā ca vipulā jajñe kathaṃ nv etad bhaviṣyati
d viṣaṇṇaṃ tu tato jñātvā savyasācinam acyutaḥ
d saṃcodayati tejasvī madhuhā vānaradhvajam
a tato gāṇḍīvadhanvānam abravīn madhusūdanaḥ
c dṛṣṭvā pārthaṃ tadāyastaṃ cintāparigataṃ tadā
a gāṇḍīvadhanvan saṃgrāme ye tvayā dhanuṣā jitāḥ
c na teṣāṃ mānuṣo jetā tvad anya iha vidyate
a dṛṣṭā hi bahavaḥ śūrāḥ śakratulyaparākramāḥ
c tvāṃ prāpya samare vīraṃ ye gatāḥ paramāṃ gatim
a ko hi droṇaṃ ca bhīṣmaṃ ca bhagadattaṃ ca māriṣa
c vindānuvindāv āvantyau kāmbojaṃ ca sudakṣiṇam
a śrutāyuṣaṃ mahāvīryam acyutāyuṣam eva ca
c pratyudgamya bhavet kṣemī yo na syāt tvam iva kṣamī
a tava hy astrāṇi divyāni lāghavaṃ balam eva ca
c vedhaḥ pātaś ca lakṣaś ca yogaś caiva tavārjuna
e asaṃmohaś ca yuddheṣu vijñānasya ca saṃnatiḥ
a bhavān devāsurān sarvān hanyāt sahacarācarān
c pṛthivyāṃ hi raṇe pārtha na yoddhā tvatsamaḥ pumān
d na cābhimukhato vācyo bhavān etad vaco mayā
d mānitasya mahādarpo bhaviṣyati raṇe 'rjuna
d avaśyam eva vaktavyam atas tvāṃ prabravīmy aham
d atimānāc ca tenātmā mantavyo vai kathaṃ cana
d jīvamāne raṇe karṇe sūtaputre mahārathe
d bahunātra kim uktena saṃkṣepāc chṛṇu pāṇḍava
d tvatsamaṃ tvadviśiṣṭaṃ vā karṇaṃ manye mahāratham
d paramaṃ yatnam āsthāya tvayā vadhyo mahāhave
d na hi karṇaṃ raṇe prāpya śakto hi syāt puraṃdaraḥ
d kṣemī pratyāgamet pārtha tādṛśo 'sya parākramaḥ
d tvāṃ tu prāpya mahāraṅge yatnavān api bhārata
d nivarteta raṇāt karṇa iti me dhīyate matiḥ
a dhanurgrahā hi ye ke cit kṣatriyā yuddhadurmadāḥ
c ā devāt tvatsamaṃ teṣāṃ na paśyāmi śṛṇomi vā
a brahmaṇā ca prajāḥ sṛṣṭā gāṇḍīvaṃ ca mahādbhutam
c yena tvaṃ yudhyase pārtha tasmān nāsti tvayā samaḥ
a avaśyaṃ tu mayā vācyaṃ yat pathyaṃ tava pāṇḍava
c māvamaṃsthā mahābāho karṇam āhavaśobhinam
a karṇo hi balavān dhṛṣṭaḥ kṛtāstraś ca mahārathaḥ
c kṛtī ca citrayodhī ca deśe kāle ca kovidaḥ
a tejasā vahnisadṛśo vāyuvegasamo jave
c antakapratimaḥ krodhe siṃhasaṃhanano balī
a ayoratnir mahābāhur vyūḍhoraskaḥ sudurjayaḥ
c atimānī ca śūraś ca pravīraḥ priyadarśanaḥ
a sarvair yodhaguṇair yukto mitrāṇām abhayaṃkaraḥ
c satataṃ pāṇḍavadveṣī dhārtarāṣṭrahite rataḥ
d na bhīṣaye tvāṃ pārthāhaṃ harṣaṃ saṃjanayāmi te
a sarvair avadhyo rādheyo devair api savāsavaiḥ
c ṛte tvām iti me buddhis tvam adya jahi sūtajam
a devair api hi saṃyattair bibhradbhir māṃsaśoṇitam
c aśakyaḥ samare jetuṃ sarvair api yuyutsubhiḥ
d devair api hi saṃrabdhaiḥ sarvalokeśvarair api
d aśakyaṃ taṃ raṇe manye sarvair api yuyutsubhiḥ
a durātmānaṃ pāpamatiṃ nṛśaṃsaṃ
duṣṭaprajñaṃ pāṇḍaveyeṣu nityam
c hīnasvārthaṃ pāṇḍaveyair virodhe
hatvā karṇaṃ dhiṣṭhitārtho bhavādya
d taṃ sūtaputraṃ rathināṃ variṣṭhaṃ
d niṣkālikaṃ kālavaśaṃ nayādya
d taṃ sūtaputraṃ rathināṃ variṣṭhaṃ
d hatvā prītiṃ dharmarāje kuruṣva
d jānāmi te pārtha vīryaṃ yathāvad
d durvāraṇīyaṃ ca surāsuraiś ca
d sadāvajānāti hi pāṇḍuputrān
d asau darpāt sūtaputro durātmā
a vīraṃ manyata ātmānaṃ yena pāpaḥ suyodhanaḥ
c tam adya mūlaṃ pāpānāṃ jaya sautiṃ dhanaṃjaya
d khaḍgajihvaṃ dhanurāsyaṃ śaradaṃṣṭraṃ tarasvinam
d dṛptaṃ puruṣaśārdūlaṃ jahi karṇaṃ dhanaṃjaya
d ahaṃ tvām anujānāmi vīryeṇa ca balena ca
d jahi karṇaṃ raṇe śūraṃ mātaṅgam iva kesarī
d yasya vīryeṇa vīryaṃ te dhārtarāṣṭro 'vamanyate
d tam adya pārtha saṃgrāme karṇaṃ vaikartanaṃ jahi
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tataḥ punar ameyātmā keśavo 'rjunam abravīt
c kṛtasaṃkalpam āyastaṃ vadhe karṇasya sarvaśaḥ
a adya saptadaśāhāni vartamānasya bhārata
c vināśasyātighorasya naravāraṇavājinām
a bhūtvā hi vipulā senā tāvakānāṃ paraiḥ saha
c anyonyaṃ samare prāpya kiṃciccheṣā viśāṃ pate
a bhūtvā hi kauravāḥ pārtha prabhūtagajavājinaḥ
c tvāṃ vai śatruṃ samāsādya vinaṣṭā raṇamūrdhani
a ete ca sarve pāñcālāḥ sṛñjayāś ca sahānvayāḥ
c tvāṃ samāsādya durdharṣaṃ pāṇḍavāś ca vyavasthitāḥ
a pāñcālaiḥ pāṇḍavair matsyaiḥ kārūṣaiś cedikekayaiḥ
b māgadhaiḥ pārijātaiś ca dākṣiṇātyaiś ca keralaiḥ
c tvayā guptair amitraghna kṛtaḥ śatrugaṇakṣayaḥ
a ko hi śakto raṇe jetuṃ kauravāṃs tāta saṃgatān
c anyatra pāṇḍavān yuddhe tvayā guptān mahārathān
a tvaṃ hi śakto raṇe jetuṃ sasurāsuramānuṣān
c trīṃl lokān samam udyuktān kiṃ punaḥ kauravaṃ balam
a bhagadattaṃ hi rājānaṃ ko 'nyaḥ śaktas tvayā vinā
c jetuṃ puruṣaśārdūla yo 'pi syād vāsavopamaḥ
a tathemāṃ vipulāṃ senāṃ guptāṃ pārtha tvayānagha
c na śekuḥ pārthivāḥ sarve cakṣurbhir abhivīkṣitum
a tathaiva satataṃ pārtha rakṣitābhyāṃ tvayā raṇe
b hatvā tu balaniṣpiṣṭau bhīṣmadroṇau mahāraṇe
c dhṛṣṭadyumnaśikhaṇḍibhyāṃ bhīṣmadroṇau nipātitau
a ko hi śakto raṇe pārtha pāñcālānāṃ mahārathau
c bhīṣmadroṇau yudhā jetuṃ śakratulyaparākramau
a ko hi śāṃtanavaṃ saṃkhye droṇaṃ vaikartanaṃ kṛpam
c drauṇiṃ ca saumadattiṃ ca kṛtavarmāṇam eva ca
e saindhavaṃ madrarājaṃ ca rājānaṃ ca suyodhanam
a vīrān kṛtāstrān samare sarvān evānuvartinaḥ
c akṣauhiṇīpatīn ugrān saṃrabdhān yuddhadurmadān
d tvām ṛte puruṣavyāghra jetuṃ śaktaḥ pumān iha
a śreṇyaś ca bahulāḥ kṣīṇāḥ pradīrṇāśvarathadvipāḥ
c nānājanapadāś cogrāḥ kṣatriyāṇām amarṣiṇām
a govāsadāsamīyānāṃ vasātīnāṃ ca bhārata
b nānādeśasamutthāś ca nānādeśasamudbhavāḥ
b tvāṃ samāsādya bībhatso hatā nāgāś ca saṃyuge
c vrātyānāṃ vāṭadhānānāṃ bhojānāṃ cāpi māninām
a udīrṇāś ca mahāsenā brahmakṣatrasya bhārata
c tvāṃ samāsādya nidhanaṃ gatāḥ sāśvarathadvipāḥ
a ugrāś ca krūrakarmāṇas tukhārā yavanāḥ khaśāḥ
c dārvābhisārā daradāḥ śakā ramaṭhataṅgaṇāḥ
a andhrakāś ca pulindāś ca kirātāś cogravikramāḥ
c mlecchāś ca pārvatīyāś ca sāgarānūpavāsinaḥ
e saṃrambhiṇo yuddhaśauṇḍā balino dṛbdhapāṇayaḥ
a ete suyodhanasyārthe saṃrabdhāḥ kurubhiḥ saha
c na śakyā yudhi nirjetuṃ tvad anyena paraṃtapa
a dhārtarāṣṭram udagraṃ hi vyūḍhaṃ dṛṣṭvā mahābalam
c yasya tvaṃ na bhaves trātā pratīyāt ko nu mānavaḥ
a tat sāgaram ivoddhūtaṃ rajasā saṃvṛtaṃ balam
c vidārya pāṇḍavaiḥ kruddhais tvayā guptair hataṃ vibho
a māgadhānām adhipatir jayatseno mahābalaḥ
c adya saptaiva cāhāni hataḥ saṃkhye 'bhimanyunā
a tato daśa sahasrāṇi gajānāṃ bhīmakarmaṇām
c jaghāna gadayā bhīmas tasya rājñaḥ paricchadam
e tato 'nye 'pi hatā nāgā rathāś ca śataśo balāt
a tad evaṃ samare tāta vartamāne mahābhaye
c bhīmasenaṃ samāsādya tvāṃ ca pāṇḍava kauravāḥ
e savājirathanāgāś ca mṛtyulokam ito gatāḥ
a tathā senāmukhe tatra nihate pārtha pāṇḍavaiḥ
c bhīṣmaḥ prāsṛjad ugrāṇi śaravarṣāṇi māriṣa
a sa cedikāśipāñcālān karūṣān matsyakekayān
c śaraiḥ pracchādya nidhanam anayat paruṣāstravit
a tasya cāpacyutair bāṇaiḥ paradehavidāraṇaiḥ
c pūrṇam ākāśam abhavad rukmapuṅkhair ajihmagaiḥ
d hanyād rathasahasrāṇi ekenaiva tu muṣṭinā
d lakṣaṃ naradvipān hatvā sametān sa mahābalān
d hatvā daśasahasrāṇi saṃnāhaṃ svaśarīrataḥ
d protsārayati gāṃgeya iti tasyābhavad vratam
d nihatya nānānṛpatīn āyudhāny āhave tyajet
d tena śūreṇa balinā muktās tv ayutaśaḥ śarāḥ
a gatyā daśamyā te gatvā jaghnur vājirathadvipān
c hitvā nava gatīr duṣṭāḥ sa bāṇān vyāyato 'mucat
a dināni daśa bhīṣmeṇa nighnatā tāvakaṃ balam
c śūnyāḥ kṛtā rathopasthā hatāś ca gajavājinaḥ
dA daśame 'hani saṃprāpte kṛtvā ghoraṃ parākramam
a darśayitvātmano rūpaṃ rudropendrasamaṃ yudhi
c pāṇḍavānām anīkāni pravigāhya vyaśātayat
a vinighnan pṛthivīpālāṃś cedipāñcālakekayān
c vyadahat pāṇḍavīṃ senāṃ narāśvagajasaṃkulām
a majjantam aplave mandam ujjihīrṣuḥ suyodhanam
c tathā carantaṃ samare tapantam iva bhāskaram
d padātikoṭisāhasrāḥ pravarāyudhapāṇayaḥ
e na śekuḥ sṛñjayā draṣṭuṃ tathaivānye mahīkṣitaḥ
a vicarantaṃ tathā taṃ tu saṃgrāme jitakāśinam
c sarvodyogena sahasā pāṇḍavāḥ samupādravan
a sa tu vidrāvya samare pāṇḍavān sṛñjayān api
c eka eva raṇe bhīṣma ekavīratvam āgataḥ
a taṃ śikhaṇḍī samāsādya tvayā gupto mahāratham
c jaghāna puruṣavyāghraṃ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
d mṛtyur jāto 'vadhīd bhīṣmaṃ śaraughaiḥ pātayan rathāt
a sa eṣa patitaḥ śete śaratalpe pitāmahaḥ
c tvāṃ prāpya puruṣavyāghra gṛdhraḥ prāpyeva vāyasam
a droṇaḥ pañca dināny ugro vidhamya ripuvāhinīḥ
c kṛtvā vyūhaṃ mahāyuddhe pātayitvā mahārathān
a jayadrathasya samare kṛtvā rakṣāṃ mahārathaḥ
c antakapratimaś cogrāṃ rātriṃ yuddhvādahat prajāḥ
a adyeti dve dine vīro bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān
c dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ samāsādya sa gataḥ paramāṃ gatim
a yadi caiva parān yuddhe sūtaputramukhān rathān
c nāvārayiṣyaḥ saṃgrāme na sma droṇo vyanaṅkṣyata
a bhavatā tu balaṃ sarvaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya vāritam
c tato droṇo hato yuddhe pārṣatena dhanaṃjaya
a ka ivānyo raṇe kuryāt tvad anyaḥ kṣatriyo yudhi
b kaś ca śakto raṇe kartuṃ tvad anyaḥ puruṣabruvaḥ
c yādṛśaṃ te kṛtaṃ pārtha jayadrathavadhaṃ prati
a nivārya senāṃ mahatīṃ hatvā śūrāṃś ca pārthivān
c nihataḥ saindhavo rājā tvayāstrabalatejasā
a āścaryaṃ sindhurājasya vadhaṃ jānanti pārthivāḥ
c anāścaryaṃ hi tat tvattas tvaṃ hi pārtha mahārathaḥ
a tvāṃ hi prāpya raṇe kṣatram ekāhād iti bhārata
c tapyamānam asaṃyuktaṃ na bhaved iti me matiḥ
a seyaṃ pārtha camūr ghorā dhārtarāṣṭrasya saṃyuge
c hatā sasarvavīrā hi bhīṣmadroṇau yadā hatau
a śīrṇapravarayodhādya hatavājinaradvipā
c hīnā sūryendunakṣatrair dyaur ivābhāti bhāratī
a vidhvastā hi raṇe pārtha seneyaṃ bhīmavikramāt
c āsurīva purā senā śakrasyeva parākramaiḥ
a teṣāṃ hatāvaśiṣṭās tu pañca santi mahārathāḥ
c aśvatthāmā kṛtavarmā karṇo madrādhipaḥ kṛpaḥ
a tāṃs tvam adya naravyāghra hatvā pañca mahārathān
c hatāmitraḥ prayacchorvīṃ rājñaḥ sadvīpapattanām
d droṇaputraṃ kṛpaṃ śalyaṃ bhojam ādhirathiṃ tathā
d etāṃs tu vai naravyāghra hatvā vīrān mahārathān
a sākāśajalapātālāṃ saparvatamahāvanām
c prāpnotv amitavīryaśrīr adya pārtho vasuṃdharām
a etāṃ purā viṣṇur iva hatvā daiteyadānavān
c prayaccha medinīṃ rājñe śakrāyeva yathā hariḥ
a adya modantu pāñcālā nihateṣv ariṣu tvayā
c viṣṇunā nihateṣv eva dānaveyeṣu devatāḥ
a yadi vā dvipadāṃ śreṣṭha droṇaṃ mānayato gurum
c aśvatthāmni kṛpā te 'sti kṛpe cācāryagauravāt
a atyantopacitān vā tvaṃ mānayan bhrātṛbāndhavān
c kṛtavarmāṇam āsādya na neṣyasi yamakṣayam
d yuddhvā yāmy adya tau pārtha saṃrabdhāv ātatāyinau
a bhrātaraṃ mātur āsādya śalyaṃ madrajanādhipam
c yadi tvam aravindākṣa dayāvān na jighāṃsasi
a imaṃ pāpamatiṃ kṣudram atyantaṃ pāṇḍavān prati
c karṇam adya naraśreṣṭha jahy āśu niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a etat te sukṛtaṃ karma nātra kiṃ cin na yujyate
c vayam apy atra jānīmo nātra doṣo 'sti kaś cana
a dahane yat saputrāyā niśi mātus tavānagha
c dyūtārthe yac ca yuṣmāsu prāvartata suyodhanaḥ
e tatra sarvatra duṣṭātmā karṇo mūlam ihārjuna
a karṇād dhi manyate trāṇaṃ nityam eva suyodhanaḥ
c tato mām api saṃrabdho nigrahītuṃ pracakrame
d vyanāśeya ca yuṣmāsu acarmitaḥ suyodhanaḥ sic
a sthirā buddhir narendrasya dhārtarāṣṭrasya mānada
c karṇaḥ pārthān raṇe sarvān vijeṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
a karṇam āśritya kaunteya dhārtarāṣṭreṇa vigrahaḥ
c rocito bhavatā sārdhaṃ jānatāpi balaṃ tava
a karṇo hi bhāṣate nityam ahaṃ pārthān samāgatān
c vāsudevaṃ sarājānaṃ vijeṣyāmi mahāraṇe
a protsāhayan durātmānaṃ dhārtarāṣṭraṃ sudurmatiḥ
c samitau garjate karṇas tam adya jahi bhārata
a yac ca yuṣmāsu pāpaṃ vai dhārtarāṣṭraḥ prayuktavān
b sarvatrānṛjur aprājñaḥ karṇam āśritya vai purā
c tatra sarvatra duṣṭātmā karṇaḥ pāpamatir mukham
a yac ca tad dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ krūraiḥ ṣaḍbhir mahārathaiḥ
c apaśyaṃ nihataṃ vīraṃ saubhadram ṛṣabhekṣaṇam
a droṇadrauṇikṛpān vīrān kampayanto mahārathān
c nirmanuṣyāṃś ca mātaṅgān virathāṃś ca mahārathān
d prādravanti sma samare diśo bhītābhimanyave
a vyaśvārohāṃś ca turagān pattīn vyāyudhajīvitān
c kurvantam ṛṣabhaskandhaṃ kuruvṛṣṇiyaśaskaram
a vidhamantam anīkāni vyathayantaṃ mahārathān
c manuṣyavājimātaṅgān prahiṇvantaṃ yamakṣayam
a śaraiḥ saubhadram āyastaṃ dahantam iva vāhinīm
c tan me dahati gātrāṇi sakhe satyena te śape
a yat tatrāpi ca duṣṭātmā karṇo 'bhyadruhyata prabho
c aśaknuvaṃś cābhimanyoḥ karṇaḥ sthātuṃ raṇe 'grataḥ
a saubhadraśaranirbhinno visaṃjñaḥ śoṇitokṣitaḥ
c niḥśvasan krodhasaṃdīpto vimukhaḥ sāyakārditaḥ
a apayānakṛtotsāho nirāśaś cāpi jīvite
b duryodhanaṃ raṇe dṛṣṭvā lajjamāno muhur muhuḥ
b nāpayāsīt tataḥ pārthaḥ so 'bhimanyor mahāraṇe
b dṛṣṭvā droṇaṃ vadhopāyam abhimanyos tu pṛṣṭavān
c tasthau suvihvalaḥ saṃkhye prahārajanitaśramaḥ
a atha droṇasya samare tat kālasadṛśaṃ tadā
c śrutvā karṇo vacaḥ krūraṃ tataś ciccheda kārmukam
a tataś chinnāyudhaṃ tena raṇe pañca mahārathāḥ
c sa caiva nikṛtiprajñaḥ prāvadhīc charavṛṣṭibhiḥ
d tasmin vinihate vīre sarveṣāṃ duḥkham āviśat
d prāhasat sa tu duṣṭātmā karṇaḥ sa ca suyodhanaḥ
a yac ca karṇo 'bravīt kṛṣṇāṃ sabhāyāṃ paruṣaṃ vacaḥ
c pramukhe pāṇḍaveyānāṃ kurūṇāṃ ca nṛśaṃsavat
a vinaṣṭāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kṛṣṇe śāśvataṃ narakaṃ gatāḥ
c patim anyaṃ pṛthuśroṇi vṛṇīṣva mitabhāṣiṇi
a lekhābhru dhṛtarāṣṭrasya dāsī bhūtvā niveśanam
c praviśārālapakṣmākṣi na santi patayas tava
d na pāṇḍavāḥ prabhavanti tava kṛṣṇe kathaṃ cana
d dāsabhāryāsi pāñcāli svayaṃ dāsī ca śobhane
d adya duryodhano hy ekaḥ pṛthivyāṃ nṛpatiḥ smṛtaḥ
d sarve cāsya mahīpālā yogakṣemam upāsate
d paśyedānīṃ yathā bhadre vinaṣṭāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ samam
d anyonyaṃ samudīkṣante dhārtarāṣṭrasya tejasā
d vyaktaṃ ṣaṇḍhatilā hy ete narake ca nimajjitāḥ
d preṣyavac cāpi rājānam upasthāsyanti kauravam
a ity uktavān adharmajñas tadā paramadurmatiḥ
c pāpaḥ pāpaṃ vacaḥ karṇaḥ śṛṇvatas tava bhārata
a tasya pāpasya tad vākyaṃ suvarṇavikṛtāḥ śarāḥ
c śamayantu śilādhautās tvayāstā jīvitacchidaḥ
d adya karṇaṃ raṇe grastaṃ paśyantu kuravas tvayā
d pratapantam ivādityaṃ svargadvāragataṃ yathā
d adya te samare vīryaṃ paśyantu kuruyodhinaḥ
d sūtaputre hate pārtha jānantu tvāṃ mahāratham
d adya kaṅkā valā gṛdhrā vāyasā jambukās tathā
d viprakarṣantu gātrāṇi sūtaputrasya bhārata
d adyātirathir ākṣipto nihataś ca tvayā raṇe
d kurūṇāṃ śokam ādhattāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mudaṃ tathā
d adya tvāṃ pratinandantu pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
d yathā vṛtravadhe vṛtte devāḥ sarve śatakratum
d adya karṇaṃ raṇe hatvā prāpya caivottamaṃ yaśaḥ
d viśoko vijvaraḥ pārtha bhava bandhupuraskṛtaḥ
d nārasiṃhavapuḥ kṛtvā yathā śasto mahāsuraḥ
d hiraṇyakaśipur daityo viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā
d tathā tvam api rādheyaṃ ghoraṃ kṛtvā mahad vapuḥ
d jahi yuddhe mahābāho trāyasva ca bhayāt svakān
a yāni cānyāni duṣṭātmā pāpāni kṛtavāṃs tvayi
c tāny adya jīvitaṃ cāsya śamayantu śarās tava
d śāntaṃ kuru parikleśaṃ kṛṣṇāyāḥ śatrutāpana
d hatvā śatruṃ raṇe 'ślāghyaṃ garjantam atipauruṣam
d adya cādhirathir viddhas tava bāṇaiḥ samantataḥ
d manyatāṃ tvāṃ naravyāghra pravaraṃ sarvadhanvinām
d gāṇḍīvaprasṛtān ghorān adya gātraiḥ spṛśañ śarān
d etu karṇo raṇe pārthaḥ śvāvicchalalito yathā
a gāṇḍīvaprahitān ghorān adya gātraiḥ spṛśañ śarān
c karṇaḥ smaratu duṣṭātmā vacanaṃ droṇabhīṣmayoḥ
a suvarṇapuṅkhā nārācāḥ śatrughnā vaidyutaprabhāḥ
c tvayāstās tasya marmāṇi bhittvā pāsyanti śoṇitam
a ugrās tvadbhujanirmuktā marma bhittvā śitāḥ śarāḥ
c adya karṇaṃ mahāvegāḥ preṣayantu yamakṣayam
d gāṇḍīvapreṣitair bhallaiḥ śitaiś chinnatanucchadaḥ
d na cet smarati rādheyo vacanaṃ droṇabhīṣmayoḥ
d suvarṇapuṅkhāḥ śatrughnā nārācā vaidyutaprabhāḥ
d na ced ādhirather varma bhittvā pāsyanti śoṇitam
d ugrās tvadbāhunirmuktā na cen marmacchidaḥ śarāḥ
d adya karṇaṃ mahāvegāḥ prahiṇvanti yamakṣayam
a adya hāhākṛtā dīnā viṣaṇṇās tvaccharārditāḥ
b taṃ ca hāhākṛtaṃ dīnaṃ viṣaṇṇaṃ śarapīḍitam
c prapatantaṃ rathāt karṇaṃ paśyantu vasudhādhipāḥ
a adya svaśoṇite magnaṃ śayānaṃ patitaṃ bhuvi
c apaviddhāyudhaṃ karṇaṃ paśyantu suhṛdo nijāḥ
d tac caivādya mahad varma gāṇḍīvapreṣitaiḥ śaraiḥ
d rathopasthe viśīryeta tārājālam ivāmbarāt
d āśu cādya śarās tasya saṃpatanto mahāhave
d tvaccharaiḥ saṃnikṛttāgrā viśīryantāṃ mahītale
d tvayā cādya hate tasya vikrame bharatarṣabha
d vimukhāḥ sarvarājāno bhavantu gatajīvitāḥ
d tathā cādhirathau yāte prayāntu kuravo diśaḥ
d manvānās tvāṃ rathaśreṣṭhaṃ sarvalokeṣu dhanvinam
d sa caivādya bhayāt tyaktvā dhārtarāṣṭro mahācamūm
d duryodhano bhayodvigno dravatu svapuraṃ prati
d tathādya taṃ hataṃ śrutvā dhārtarāṣṭro janeśvaraḥ
d mohena nipated bhūmau niḥsaṃjño vai mahīpatiḥ
d adya jānantu te pārtha vikramaṃ sarvadhanvinaḥ
d yān avocat sabhāmadhye paruṣān bhārata tvayi
a hastikakṣyo mahān asya bhallenonmathitas tvayā
c prakampamānaḥ patatu bhūmāv ādhirather dhvajaḥ
a tvayā śaraśataiś chinnaṃ rathaṃ hemavibhūṣitam
c hatayodhaṃ samutsṛjya bhītaḥ śalyaḥ palāyatām
d na cet karṇasutaṃ pārtha sūtaputrasya paśyataḥ
d pratijñāpālanārthāya nihaniṣyasi sāyakaiḥ
d hataṃ karṇaḥ sutaṃ dṛṣṭvā priyaṃ putraṃ durātmavān
d smaratāṃ droṇabhīṣmābhyāṃ vacaḥ kṣattuś ca mānada
a tataḥ suyodhano dṛṣṭvā hatam ādhirathiṃ tvayā
c nirāśo jīvite tv adya rājye caiva dhanaṃjaya
d asau hi tāvakān pārtha karṇo nighnati saṃyuge
d śakratulyabalo vīryāc chaṃkarapratimo 'pi vā
a ete dravanti pāñcālā vadhyamānāḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c karṇena bharataśreṣṭha pāṇḍavān ujjihīrṣavaḥ
a pāñcālān draupadeyāṃś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaśikhaṇḍinau
c dhṛṣṭadyumnatanūjāṃś ca śatānīkaṃ ca nākulim
a nakulaṃ sahadevaṃ ca durmukhaṃ janamejayam
c suvarmāṇaṃ sātyakiṃ ca viddhi karṇavaśaṃ gatān
a abhyāhatānāṃ karṇena pāñcālānāṃ mahāraṇe
c śrūyate ninado ghoras tvadbandhūnāṃ paraṃtapa
a na tv eva bhītāḥ pāñcālāḥ kathaṃ cit syuḥ parāṅmukhāḥ
c na hi mṛtyuṃ maheṣvāsā gaṇayanti mahārathāḥ
a ya ekaḥ pāṇḍavīṃ senāṃ śaraughaiḥ samaveṣṭayat
c taṃ samāsādya pāñcālā bhīṣmaṃ nāsan parāṅmukhāḥ
d te kathaṃ karṇam āsādya vidraveyur mahābalāḥ
d yas tv ekaḥ sarvapāñcālān ahany ahani nāśayan
d kālavac carate vīraḥ pāñcālānāṃ rathavraje
d tam apy āsādya samare mitrārthe mitravatsalāḥ
a tathā jvalantam astrāgniṃ guruṃ sarvadhanuṣmatām
c nirdahantaṃ samārohan durdharṣaṃ droṇam ojasā
a te nityam uditā jetuṃ yuddhe śatrūn ariṃdamāḥ
c na jātv ādhirather bhītāḥ pāñcālāḥ syuḥ parāṅmukhāḥ
a teṣām āpatatāṃ śūraḥ pāñcālānāṃ tarasvinām
c ādatte 'sūñ śaraiḥ karṇaḥ pataṃgānām ivānalaḥ
d ete dravanti pāñcālā drāvyante yodhibhir drutam
d karṇena bharataśreṣṭha paśya paśya tathākṛtān
a tāṃs tathābhimukhān vīrān mitrārthe tyaktajīvitān
c kṣayaṃ nayati rādheyaḥ pāñcālāñ śataśo raṇe
d nistāraya mahābāho karṇāstrāt pāvakopamāt
d tad bhārata maheṣvāsān agādhe majjato 'plave
d karṇārṇave plavo bhūtvā pāñcālāṃs trātum arhasi
a astraṃ hi rāmāt karṇena bhārgavād ṛṣisattamāt
c yad upāttaṃ purā ghoraṃ tasya rūpam udīryate
a tāpanaṃ sarvasainyānāṃ ghorarūpaṃ sudāruṇam
c samāvṛtya mahāsenāṃ jvalati svena tejasā
a ete caranti saṃgrāme karṇacāpacyutāḥ śarāḥ
c bhramarāṇām iva vrātās tāpayantaḥ sma tāvakān
d bhramarā iva śatrūṇāṃ pātayānā janān prabho
a ete caranti pāñcālā dikṣu sarvāsu bhārata
c karṇāstraṃ samare prāpya durnivāram anātmabhiḥ
a eṣa bhīmo dṛḍhakrodho vṛtaḥ pārtha samantataḥ
c sṛñjayair yodhayan karṇaṃ pīḍyate sma śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a pāṇḍavān sṛñjayāṃś caiva pāñcālāṃś caiva bhārata
c hanyād upekṣitaḥ karṇo rogo deham ivātataḥ
a nānyaṃ tvatto 'bhipaśyāmi yodhaṃ yaudhiṣṭhire bale
c yaḥ samāsādya rādheyaṃ svastimān āvrajed gṛham
a tam adya niśitair bāṇair nihatya bharatarṣabha
c yathāpratijñaṃ pārtha tvaṃ kṛtvā kīrtim avāpnuhi
a tvaṃ hi śakto raṇe jetuṃ sakarṇān api kauravān
c nānyo yudhi yudhāṃ śreṣṭha satyam etad bravīmi te
a etat kṛtvā mahat karma hatvā karṇaṃ mahāratham
c kṛtārthaḥ saphalaḥ pārtha sukhī bhava narottama
 saṃjaya uvāca
a sa keśavasya bībhatsuḥ śrutvā bhārata bhāṣitam
c viśokaḥ saṃprahṛṣṭaś ca kṣaṇena samapadyata
a tato jyām anumṛjyāśu vyākṣipad gāṇḍivaṃ dhanuḥ
c dadhre karṇavināśāya keśavaṃ cābhyabhāṣata
a tvayā nāthena govinda dhruva eṣa jayo mama
c prasanno yasya me 'dya tvaṃ bhūtabhavyabhavatprabhuḥ
a tvatsahāyo hy ahaṃ kṛṣṇa trīṃl lokān vai samāgatān
c prāpayeyaṃ paraṃ lokaṃ kim u karṇaṃ mahāraṇe
a paśyāmi dravatīṃ senāṃ pāñcālānāṃ janārdana
c paśyāmi karṇaṃ samare vicarantam abhītavat
a bhārgavāstraṃ ca paśyāmi vicarantaṃ samantataḥ
c sṛṣṭaṃ karṇena vārṣṇeya śakreṇeva mahāśanim
a ayaṃ khalu sa saṃgrāmo yatra kṛṣṇa mayā kṛtam
b nirjitā bahuśo yodhāḥ palāyanaparāyaṇāḥ
c kathayiṣyanti bhūtāni yāvad bhūmir dhariṣyati
a adya kṛṣṇa vikarṇā me karṇaṃ neṣyanti mṛtyave
c gāṇḍīvamuktāḥ kṣiṇvanto mama hastapracoditāḥ
a adya rājā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ svāṃ buddhim avamaṃsyate
c duryodhanam arājyārhaṃ yayā rājye 'bhyaṣecayat
d guṇavantaṃ hi yo hitvā nirguṇaṃ kurute prabhum
d sa śocati nṛpaḥ kṛṣṇa kṣipram evāgate kṣaye
d yathā hi puruṣaḥ kaś cic chittvā cāmravaṇaṃ mahat
d palāśasecane buddhiṃ kṛtvā śocati mandadhīḥ
d dṛṣṭvā puṣpaṃ phale gṛdhnuḥ phalaṃ dṛṣṭvānuśocati
d tathedaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya puṣpalubdhasya mānada
d phalaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhṛśaṃ duḥkhaṃ bhaviṣyati janārdana
d sūtaputre hate tv adya nirāśo bhavitā prabhuḥ
a adya rājyāt sukhāc caiva śriyo rāṣṭrāt tathā purāt
c putrebhyaś ca mahābāho dhṛtarāṣṭro viyokṣyate
d adya rājyāc ca putrāc ca śriyaś caiva nirāśavān
d sukhāc ca vipulāt kṛṣṇa dhṛtarāṣṭro viyokṣyati
a adya duryodhano rājā jīvitāc ca nirāśakaḥ
c bhaviṣyati hate karṇe kṛṣṇa satyaṃ bravīmi te
a adya dṛṣṭvā mayā karṇaṃ śarair viśakalīkṛtam
b purā devāsure yuddhe vṛtraṃ balabhidā yathā
c smaratāṃ tava vākyāni śamaṃ prati janeśvaraḥ
a adyāsau saubalaḥ kṛṣṇa glahaṃ jānātu vai śarān
c durodaraṃ ca gāṇḍīvaṃ maṇḍalaṃ ca rathaṃ mama
d adya kuntīsutasyāhaṃ dṛḍhaṃ rājñaḥ prajāgaram
d vyapaneṣyāmi govinda hatvā karṇaṃ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
d adya kuntīsuto rājā hate sūtasute mayā
d suprahṛṣṭamanāḥ prītaś ciraṃ sukham avāpsyati
d adya cāham anādhṛṣyaṃ keśavāpratimaṃ śaram
d utsrakṣyāmīha yaḥ karṇaṃ jīvitād bhraṃśayiṣyati
d yasya caitad vrataṃ mahyaṃ vadhe kila durātmanaḥ
d pādau na dhāvaye tāvad yāvad dhanyāṃ na phalgunam
d mṛṣā kṛtvā vrataṃ tasya pāpasya madhusūdana
d pātayiṣye rathāt kāyaṃ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
a yo 'sau raṇe naraṃ nānyaṃ pṛthivyām abhimanyate
c tasyādya sūtaputrasya bhūmiḥ pāsyati śoṇitam
d apatir hy asi kṛṣṇeti sūtaputro yad abravīt
d dhṛtarāṣṭramate karṇaḥ ślāghamānaḥ svakān guṇān
d anṛtaṃ tat kariṣyanti māmakā niśitāḥ śarāḥ
d āśīviṣā iva kruddhās tasya pāsyanti śoṇitam
d mayā hastavatā muktā nārācā vaidyutatviṣaḥ
e gāṇḍīvasṛṣṭā dāsyanti karṇasya paramāṃ gatim
a adya tapsyati rādheyaḥ pāñcālīṃ yat tadābravīt
c sabhāmadhye vacaḥ krūraṃ kutsayan pāṇḍavān prati
a ye vai ṣaṇḍhatilās tatra bhavitāro 'dya te tilāḥ
c hate vaikartane karṇe sūtaputre durātmani
a ahaṃ vaḥ pāṇḍuputrebhyas trāsyāmīti yad abravīt
b dhṛtarāṣṭrasutān karṇaḥ ślāghamāno ''tmano guṇān
c anṛtaṃ tat kariṣyanti māmakā niśitāḥ śarāḥ
d adyāgaḥ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ samāptim upayāsyati
a hantāhaṃ pāṇḍavān sarvān saputrān iti yo 'bravīt
c tam adya karṇaṃ hantāsmi miṣatāṃ sarvadhanvinām
a yasya vīrye samāśvasya dhārtarāṣṭro bṛhanmanāḥ
c avāmanyata durbuddhir nityam asmān durātmavān
d hatvāhaṃ karṇam ājau hi toṣayiṣyāmi bhrātaram
d śarān nānāvidhān muktvā trāsayiṣyāmi śātravān
d ākarṇamuktair iṣubhir yamarāṣṭravivardhanaiḥ
d bhūmiśobhāṃ kariṣyāmi pātitai rathakuñjaraiḥ
d tatrāhave mahatsaṃkhye saṃyate yuddhadurmade
d haniṣye tasya sainyaṃ tu rathebhāśvapadātimat
e tam adya karṇaṃ rādheyaṃ hantāsmi madhusūdana
a adya karṇe hate kṛṣṇa dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ sarājakāḥ
c vidravantu diśo bhītāḥ siṃhatrastā mṛgā iva
a adya duryodhano rājā pṛthivīm anvavekṣatām
c hate karṇe mayā saṃkhye saputre sasuhṛjjane
a adya karṇaṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā dhārtarāṣṭro 'tyamarṣaṇaḥ
c jānātu māṃ raṇe kṛṣṇa pravaraṃ sarvadhanvinām
d saputraputrau sāmātyaṃ sabhṛtyaṃ ca nirāśiṣam
d pitrye rājye nirāśaś ca dhārtarāṣṭro janādhipaḥ
d adya rājye kariṣyāmi dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ janeśvaram
d adya karṇasya cakrāṅgāḥ kravyādāś ca pṛthagvidhāḥ
d śaraiś chinnāni gātrāṇi vicariṣyanti keśava
d adya rādhāsutasyāhaṃ saṃgrāme madhusūdana
d śiraś chetsyāmi karṇasya miṣatāṃ sarvadhanvinām
d adya tīkṣṇair vipāṭhaiś ca kṣuraiś ca madhusūdana
d raṇe chetsyāmi gātrāṇi rādheyasya durātmanaḥ
d adya rājā mahat kṛcchraṃ saṃtyakṣyati yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d saṃtāpaṃ mānasaṃ vīraś cirasaṃbhṛtam ātmanaḥ
d adya keśava rādheyam ahaṃ hatvā sabāndhavam
d nandayiṣyāmi rājānaṃ dharmaputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
d adyāham anugān kṛṣṇa karṇasya kṛpaṇān yudhi
d hantā jvalanasaṃkāśaiḥ śaraiḥ sarpaviṣopamaiḥ
d adyāhaṃ hemakavacair ābaddhamaṇikuṇḍalaiḥ
d saṃstariṣyāmi govinda vasudhāṃ vasudhādhipaiḥ
d adyābhimanyoḥ śatrūṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ madhusūdana
d pramathiṣyāmi gātrāṇi śirāṃsi ca śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
d adya nirdhārtarāṣṭrāṃ ca bhrātre dāsyāmi medinīm
d nirarjunāṃ vā pṛthivīṃ keśavānucariṣyasi
d adya rājā dharmaputro hatāmitro bhaviṣyati
d adya duryodhano dīptāṃ śriyaṃ rājyaṃ ca hāsyati
d hate vaikartane karṇe bhīṣme droṇe ca saṃyuge
d katarat tad balaṃ kṛṣṇa praviṣṭaṃ mokṣyate tu yat
d adyaprabhṛti rājānaṃ dharmaśīlaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
d anumodantu suhṛdo jñātapūrvāś ca brāhmaṇāḥ
d adya taṃ nihataṃ śrutvā karṇaṃ vaikartanaṃ mayā
d karotu paṭahonmiśraṃ devatāsthānapūjanam
d adya kṛṣṇa hate karṇe kurutāṃ cirasaṃbhṛtam
d yājanaṃ vai mahābāho devatānāṃ yathāvidhi
d adya tv ambā ca kṛṣṇā ca tvaramāṇe parasparam
d sasvajetāṃ hṛṣīkeśa saṃpūrṇe 'smin manorathe
d adya tvāṃ pāṇḍavo jyeṣṭhas tathāryaś ca vṛkodaraḥ
d udīkṣetāṃ hate karṇe kṛṣṇa saumyena cakṣuṣā
d abhivādya gurūn adya kaniṣṭhaiś cābhivāditaḥ
d sasvajāno hy ahaṃ dorbhyāṃ prāpsyāmi vipulaṃ yaśaḥ
d adya karṇe hate kṛṣṇa praśaṃsanto 'rjunaṃ surāḥ
d tridivaṃ yāntu saṃhṛṣṭāḥ saṃgatāś ca tapodhanāḥ
d adya lokās trayaḥ kṛṣṇa jānantu mama pauruṣam
d dṛṣṭvā karṇaṃ hataṃ yuddhe dvairathe savyasācinā
a adyāham anṛṇaḥ kṛṣṇa bhaviṣyāmi dhanurbhṛtām
c krodhasya ca kurūṇāṃ ca śarāṇāṃ gāṇḍivasya ca
a adya duḥkham ahaṃ mokṣye trayodaśasamārjitam
c hatvā karṇaṃ raṇe kṛṣṇa śambaraṃ maghavān iva
a adya karṇe hate yuddhe somakānāṃ mahārathāḥ
c kṛtaṃ kāryaṃ ca manyantāṃ mitrakāryepsavo yudhi
a na jāne ca kathaṃ prītiḥ śaineyasyādya mādhava
c bhaviṣyati hate karṇe mayi cāpi jayādhike
a ahaṃ hatvā raṇe karṇaṃ putraṃ cāsya mahāratham
c prītiṃ dāsyāmi bhīmasya yamayoḥ sātyaker api
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaśikhaṇḍibhyāṃ pāñcālānāṃ ca mādhava
b dhṛṣṭadyumnasya vīrasya tathaiva ca śikhaṇḍinaḥ
c adhyānṛṇyaṃ gamiṣyāmi hatvā karṇaṃ mahāraṇe
d dharmarājasya vārṣṇeya saṃśrutya śapathaṃ mithaḥ
a adya paśyantu saṃgrāme dhanaṃjayam amarṣaṇam
c yudhyantaṃ kauravān saṃkhye pātayantaṃ ca sūtajam
e bhavatsakāśe vakṣye ca punar evātmasaṃstavam
f ity apy amitrapravaram adyāhaṃ hanmi sūtajam
a dhanurvede matsamo nāsti loke
parākrame vā mama ko 'sti tulyaḥ
c ko vāpy anyo matsamo 'sti kṣamāyāṃ
tathā krodhe sadṛśo 'nyo na me 'sti
a ahaṃ dhanuṣmān asurān surāṃś ca
sarvāṇi bhūtāni ca saṃgatāni
c svabāhuvīryād gamaye parābhavaṃ
matpauruṣaṃ viddhi paraḥ parebhyaḥ
a śarārciṣā gāṇḍivenāham ekaḥ
sarvān kurūn bāhlikāṃś cābhipatya
c himātyaye kakṣagato yathāgnis
tahā daheyaṃ sagaṇān prasahya
a pāṇau pṛṣatkā likhitā mamaite
dhanuś ca savye nihitaṃ sabāṇam
c pādau ca me sarathau sadhvajau ca
na mādṛśaṃ yuddhagataṃ jayanti
d ity evam uktvācyutam ekavīraḥ
d kṣipraṃ ripukṣit kṣatajopamākṣaḥ
d bhīmaṃ mumukṣuḥ samare prayātaḥ
d karṇasya kāyāc ca śiro jihīrṣuḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
 mahābhaye pāṇḍavasṛñjayānāṃ
 mahābhaye māmakānām agādhe
 dhanaṃjaye tāta raṇāya yāte
 babhūva tad yuddham atho nu kīdṛk
 saṃjaya uvāca
a teṣām anīkāni bṛhaddhvajāni
raṇe samṛddhāni samāgatāni
c garjanti bherīninadonmukhāni
meghair yathā meghagaṇās tapānte
d bherīninādair mukharāṇy agarjan
d meghā yathā prāvṛṣi mārutās tāḥ
a mahāgajābhrākulam astratoyaṃ
vāditranemītalaśabdavac ca
c hiraṇyacitrāyudhavaidyutaṃ ca
mahārathair āvṛtaśabdavac ca
a tad bhīmavegaṃ rudhiraughavāhi
khaḍgākulaṃ kṣatriyajīvavāhi
c anārtavaṃ krūram aniṣṭavarṣaṃ
babhūva tat saṃharaṇaṃ prajānām
d ekaṃ rathaṃ saṃparivārya mṛtyuṃ
d nayanty aneke ca rathāḥ sametāḥ
d ekas tathaikaṃ rathinaṃ rathāgryāṃs
d tathā rathaś cāpi rathān anekān
d rathaṃ sasūtaṃ sahayaṃ ca kaṃ cit
d kaś cid rathī mṛtyuvaśaṃ nināya
d nināya cāpy ekagajena kaś cid
d rathān bahūn mṛtyuvaśe tathāśvān
a rathān sasūtān sahayān gajāṃś ca
sarvān arīn mṛtyuvaśaṃ śaraughaiḥ
c ninye hayāṃś caiva tathā sasādīn
padātisaṃghāṃś ca tathaiva pārthaḥ
d nināya pārtho balagarvitākṣo
d yathāntakaḥ sarvaharo mahaujāḥ
a kṛpaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca raṇe sametau
duryodhanaṃ sātyakir abhyagacchata
c śrutaśravā droṇasutena sārdhaṃ
yudhāmanyuś citrasenena cāpi
a karṇasya putras tu rathī suṣeṇaṃ
samāgataḥ sṛñjayāṃś cottamaujāḥ
c gāndhārarājaṃ sahadevaḥ kṣudhārto
maharṣabhaṃ siṃha ivābhyadhāvat
a śatānīko nākuliḥ karṇaputraṃ
yuvā yuvānaṃ vṛṣasenaṃ śaraughaiḥ
c samārdayat karṇasutaś ca vīraḥ
pāñcāleyaṃ śaravarṣair anekaiḥ
a ratharṣabhaḥ kṛtavarmāṇam ārcchan
mādrīputro nakulaś citrayodhī
