c pāñcālānām adhipo yājñaseniḥ
senāpatiṃ karṇam ārcchat sasainyam
a duḥśāsano bhārata bhāratī ca
saṃśaptakānāṃ pṛtanā samṛddhā
c bhīmaṃ raṇe śastrabhṛtāṃ variṣṭhaṃ
tadā samārcchat tam asahyavegam
d vyāttānanaḥ krūra ivāntakābhaḥ
d samāsadad bhārata bhīmasenam
a karṇātmajaṃ tatra jaghāna śūras
tathācchinac cottamaujāḥ prasahya
c tasyottamāṅgaṃ nipapāta bhūmau
ninādayad gāṃ ninadena khaṃ ca
a suṣeṇaśīrṣaṃ patitaṃ pṛthivyāṃ
vilokya karṇo 'tha tadārtarūpaḥ
c krodhād dhayāṃs tasya rathaṃ dhvajaṃ ca
bāṇaiḥ sudhārair niśitair nyakṛntat
a sa tūttamaujā niśitaiḥ pṛṣatkair
vivyādha khaḍgena ca bhāsvareṇa
c pārṣṇiṃ hayāṃś caiva kṛpasya hatvā
śikhaṇḍivāhaṃ sa tato 'bhyarohat
d pāñcālarājasya sutas tarasvī
d cakre śikhaṇḍī virathaṃ kṛpaṃ vai
a kṛpaṃ tu dṛṣṭvā virathaṃ rathastho
naicchac charais tāḍayituṃ śikhaṇḍī
c taṃ drauṇir āvārya rathaṃ kṛpaṃ sma
samujjahre paṅkagatāṃ yathā gām
a hiraṇyavarmā niśitaiḥ pṛṣatkais
tavātmajānām anilātmajo vai
c atāpayat sainyam atīva bhīmaḥ
kāle śucau madhyagato yathārkaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a atha tv idānīṃ tumule vimarde
dviṣadbhir eko bahubhiḥ samāvṛtaḥ
c mahābhaye sārathim ity uvāca
bhīmaś camūṃ vārayan dhārtarāṣṭrīm
e tvaṃ sārathe yāhi javena vāhair
nayāmy etān dhārtarāṣṭrān yamāya
a saṃcodito bhīmasenena caivaṃ
sa sārathiḥ putrabalaṃ tvadīyam
c prāyāt tataḥ sārathir ugravego
yato bhīmas tad balaṃ gantum aicchat
a tato 'pare nāgarathāśvapattibhiḥ
pratyudyayuḥ kuravas taṃ samantāt
c bhīmasya vāhāgryam udāravegaṃ
samantato bāṇagaṇair nijaghnuḥ
a tataḥ śarān āpatato mahātmā
ciccheda bāṇais tapanīyapuṅkhaiḥ
c te vai nipetus tapanīyapuṅkhā
dvidhā tridhā bhīmaśarair nikṛttāḥ
a tato rājan nāgarathāśvayūnāṃ
bhīmāhatānāṃ tava rājamadhye
c ghoro ninādaḥ prababhau narendra
vajrāhatānām iva parvatānām
a te vadhyamānāś ca narendramukhyā
nirbhinnā vai bhīmasenapravekaiḥ
c bhīmaṃ samantāt samare 'dhyarohan
vṛkṣaṃ śakuntā iva puṣpahetoḥ
a tato 'bhipātaṃ tava sainyamadhye
prāduścakre vegam ivāttavegaḥ
c yathāntakāle kṣapayan didhakṣur
bhūtāntakṛtkāla ivāttadaṇḍaḥ
a tasyātivegasya raṇe 'tivegaṃ
nāśaknuvan dhārayituṃ tvadīyāḥ
c vyāttānanasyāpatato yathaiva
kālasya kāle harataḥ prajā vai
a tato balaṃ bhārata bhāratānāṃ
pradahyamānaṃ samare mahātman
c bhītaṃ diśo 'kīryata bhīmanunnaṃ
mahānilenābhragaṇo yathaiva
d tad viprakīrṇaṃ tv atha bhārataṃ balaṃ
d punaś ca bhīmaṃ parivārayad raṇe
a tato dhīmān sārathim abravīd balī
sa bhīmasenaḥ punar eva hṛṣṭaḥ
b tvara tvara hy adya viśoka śīghram
b etān dhvajāgrāṃś ca rathāṃś ca paśya
c sūtābhijānīhi parān svakān vā
rathān dhvajāṃś cāpatataḥ sametān
e yudhyann ahaṃ nābhijānāmi kiṃ cin
mā sainyaṃ svaṃ chādayiṣye pṛṣatkaiḥ
a arīn viśokābhinirīkṣya sarvato
manas tu cintā pradunoti me bhṛśam
c rājāturo nāgamad yat kirīṭī
bahūni duḥkhāny abhijāto 'smi sūta
a etad duḥkhaṃ sārathe dharmarājo
yan māṃ hitvā yātavāñ śatrumadhye
c nainaṃ jīvan nāpi jānāmy ajīvan
bībhatsuṃ vā tan mamādyātiduḥkham
a so 'haṃ dviṣatsainyam udagrakalpaṃ
vināśayiṣye paramapratītaḥ
c etān nihatyājimadhye sametān
prīto bhaviṣyāmi saha tvayādya
a sarvāṃs tūṇīrān mārgaṇān vānvavekṣya
kiṃ śiṣṭaṃ syāt sāyakānāṃ rathe me
b kiyanto me iṣavaḥ sadya eva
b avekṣasva me iṣudhī viśoka
b kiyanto vā iṣavo me 'vaśiṣṭāḥ
c kā vā jātiḥ kiṃ pramāṇaṃ ca teṣāṃ
jñātvā vyaktaṃ tan mamācakṣva sūta
d kati vā sahasrāṇi kati vā śatāni
d viśoka uvāca
d hy ācakṣva me sārathe kṣipram eva
d sarvaṃ viditvaivam ahaṃ vadāmi
d tavārthasiddhipradam adya vīra
d kaikeyakāmbhojasurāṣṭrabāhlikā
d mlecchāś ca suhmāḥ parataṅkaṇāś ca
d madrāś ca vaṅgā magadhāḥ kuṇindā
d ānartakāvartakāḥ pārvatīyāḥ
d sarve gṛhītapravarāyudhās tvāṃ
d saṃveṣṭya saṃveṣṭya tato vineduḥ
d rathe tavāsmin niśitāḥ supītās
d tato bhallā dvādaśa vai sahasrāḥ
 viśoka uvāca
a ṣaṇmārgaṇānām ayutāni vīra
kṣurāś ca bhallāś ca tathāyutākhyāḥ
c nārācānāṃ dve sahasre tu vīra
trīṇy eva ca pradarāṇāṃ ca pārtha
c vatsadantānāṃ daśa karṇināṃ ca
c ardhacandrā dvādaśa ṣaṭśataṃ ca
c vipāṭhānāṃ pravarāṇāṃ ca sapta
c śilīmukhānāṃ daśa ca triṃśataṃ ca
c ayomukhānāṃ kṣudrakāṇāṃ ca triṃśat
a asty āyudhaṃ pāṇḍaveyāvaśiṣṭaṃ
na yad vahec chakaṭaṃ ṣaḍgavīyam
b astrāyutaṃ pāṇḍava te 'vaśiṣṭam
b etad vahec chakaṭaṃ ṣaḍgavaṃ yat
b prāsāś ca mudgarāḥ śaktayas tomarāś ca
b mā bhaiṣīs tvaṃ saṃkṣayād āyudhānām
c etad vidvan muñca sahasraśo 'pi
gadāsibāhudraviṇaṃ ca te 'sti
c śatrūñ jayasvāśusahasravīra
 bhīma uvāca
 adyaiva nūnaṃ kathayantu siddhāṃ
 mama pratijñāṃ sarvaloke viśoka
 na mokṣyate vā samare bhīmasena
 ekaḥ śatrūn samare vāpy ajaiṣīt
 āśaṃsitānām idam ekam astu
 tan me devāḥ sakalaṃ sādhayantu
a sūtādyemaṃ paśya bhīmapramuktaiḥ
saṃbhindadbhiḥ pārthivān āśuvegaiḥ
c ugrair bāṇair āhavaṃ ghorarūpaṃ
naṣṭādityaṃ mṛtyulokena tulyam
a adyaiva tad viditaṃ pārthivānāṃ
bhaviṣyati ākumāraṃ ca sūta
c nimagno vā samare bhīmasena
ekaḥ kurūn vā samare vijetā
a sarve saṃkhye kuravo niṣpatantu
māṃ vā lokāḥ kīrtayantv ākumāram
c sarvān ekas tān ahaṃ pātayiṣye
te vā sarve bhīmasenaṃ tudantu
a āśāstāraḥ karma cāpy uttamaṃ vā
tan me devāḥ kevalaṃ sādhayantu
c āyātv ihādyārjunaḥ śatrughātī
śakras tūrṇaṃ yajña ivopahūtaḥ
d āyātīha keśavasārathī ratha
d indro yajñe sahasaivopahūtaḥ
d paśyasva paśyasva viśoka me balaṃ
d balaṃ pareṣām abhitaś ca bhinnam
d nānāsvarān paśya vimucya sarve
d tathā dravante balino dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ
a īkṣasvaitāṃ bhāratīṃ dīryamāṇām
ete kasmād vidravante narendrāḥ
c vyaktaṃ dhīmān savyasācī narāgryaḥ
sainyaṃ hy etac chādayaty āśu bāṇaiḥ
d dhanaṃjayo nūnam āyāti sūta
d tasmād eṣā dīryate bhāratī camūḥ
a paśya dhvajāṃś ca dravato viśoka
nāgān hayān pattisaṃghāṃś ca saṃkhye
c rathān viśīrṇāñ śaraśaktitāḍitān
paśyasvaitān rathinaś caiva sūta
a āpūryate kauravī cāpy abhīkṣṇaṃ
senā hy asau subhṛśaṃ hanyamānā
c dhanaṃjayasyāśanitulyavegair
grastā śarair barhisuvarṇavājaiḥ
a ete dravanti sma rathāśvanāgāḥ
padātisaṃghān avamardayantaḥ
c saṃmuhyamānāḥ kauravāḥ sarva eva
dravanti nāgā iva dāvabhītāḥ
e hāhākṛtāś caiva raṇe viśoka
muñcanti nādān vipulān gajendrāḥ
 viśoka uvāca
 kiṃ bhīma nainaṃ tvam ihāśṛṇoṣi
 visphāritaṃ gāṇḍivasyātighoram
 kruddhena pārthena vikṛṣyato 'dya
 kaccin nemau tava karṇau vinaṣṭau
a sarve kāmāḥ pāṇḍava te samṛddhāḥ
kapidhvajo dṛśyate hastisainye
c nīlād dhanād vidyutam uccarantīṃ
tathāpaśyaṃ visphurad vai dhanus tat
d dodhūyamānasya dhanaṃjayena
a kapir hy asau vīkṣyate sarvato vai
dhvajāgram āruhya dhanaṃjayasya
b vitrāsayan dvipasaṃghān vimarde
b bibhemy asmād ātmanaivābhivīkṣya
b vibhrājate cātimātraṃ kirīṭaṃ
b vicitram etac ca dhanaṃjayasya
c divākarābho maṇir eṣa divyo
vibhrājate caiva kirīṭasaṃsthaḥ
a pārśve bhīmaṃ pāṇḍurābhraprakāśaṃ
paśyemaṃ tvaṃ devadattaṃ sughoṣam
b mahābalaṃ bhīma virājamānaṃ
b paśyasva saṃkhye dviṣatāṃ nihantuḥ
b pārśve sthitaṃ pārtha dhanaṃjayasya
b divyaṃ śaṅkhaṃ pāñcajanyaṃ ca paśya
c abhīśuhastasya janārdanasya
vigāhamānasya camūṃ pareṣām
a raviprabhaṃ vajranābhaṃ kṣurāntaṃ
pārśve sthitaṃ paśya janārdanasya
b cakraṃ ca paśya jvalanaprakāśaṃ
b pārśve sthitaṃ pārtha dhanaṃjayasya
c cakraṃ yaśo vardhayat keśavasya
sadārcitaṃ yadubhiḥ paśya vīra
d tathaiva kṛṣṇasya ca pāñcajanyaṃ
d mahārham etad vijamājavarṇam 
d kaunteya paśyorasi kaustubhaṃ ca
d jājvalyamānāṃ vijayasrajaṃ ca
d kṛṣṇasyemāṃ paśya ca bhīmasena
d savidyutaś caiva ghanasya śabdaṃ
d viṣphāryato dhanuṣo gāṇḍivasya
d dhanaṃjayenābhipannasya kāle
d śabdo ghoraḥ śrūyate tasya nāsmin
d kaccic chrotāho badhiro 'si pārtha
d mahādvipānāṃ saraladrumopamāḥ
d karā nikṛttāḥ prapatanty amī kṣuraiḥ
d kirīṭinā tena punaḥ sasādinaḥ
d śarair nikṛttāḥ kuliśair ivādrayaḥ
d tathaiva kṛṣṇasya ca pāñcajanyaṃ
d mahārham etad dvijarājavarṇam
d kaunteya paśyorasi kaustubhaṃ ca
d jājvalyamānaṃ vijayāṃ srajaṃ ca
d dhruvaṃ rathāgryaḥ samupaiti pārtho
d vidrāvayan sainyam idaṃ pareṣām
d sitābhravarṇair asitaprayuktaiḥ
d hayair mahārhai rathināṃ variṣṭhaḥ
d rathān hayān pattigaṇāṃś ca sāyakair
d vidāritān paśya patanty amī yathā
d tavānujenāmararājatejasā
d mahāvanānīva suparṇavāyunā
d catuḥśatān paśya rathān imān hatān
d savājisūtān samare kirīṭinā
d maheṣubhiḥ sapta śatāni dantināṃ
d padātisādīṃś ca rathān anekaśaḥ
d ayaṃ samabhyeti tavāntikaṃ balī
d nighnan kurūṃś citra iva graho 'rjunaḥ
d samṛddhakāmo 'si hatās tavāhitā
d balaṃ tavāyuś ca cirāya vardhatām
 bhīma uvāca
a dadāmi te grāmavarāṃś caturdaśa
priyākhyāne sārathe suprasannaḥ
c dasīśataṃ cāpi rathāṃś ca viṃśatiṃ
yad arjunaṃ vedayase viśoka
 saṃjaya uvāca
a śrutvā ca rathanirghoṣaṃ siṃhanādaṃ ca saṃyuge
c arjunaḥ prāha govindaṃ śīghraṃ codaya vājinaḥ
d jayatu bhuvanabhartā dharmavid dharmarājo
d diśatu śivam idānīṃ keśavaḥ pāṇḍavebhyaḥ
d vipulavijayavājī jṛmbhatāṃ vai kirīṭī
d ripukulavanadāhau mādriputrau bhavetām
a arjunasya vacaḥ śrutvā govindo 'rjunam abravīt
c eṣa gacchāmi sukṣipraṃ yatra bhīmo vyavasthitaḥ
a āyāntam aśvair himaśaṅkhavarṇaiḥ
suvarṇamuktāmaṇijālanaddhaiḥ
c jambhaṃ jighāṃsuṃ pragṛhītavajraṃ
jayāya devendram ivogramanyum
a rathāśvamātaṅgapadātisaṃghā
bāṇasvanair nemikhurasvanaiś ca
c saṃnādayanto vasudhāṃ diśaś ca
kruddhā nṛsiṃhā jayam abhyudīyuḥ
a teṣāṃ ca pārthasya mahat tadāsīd
dehāsupāpmakṣapaṇaṃ suyuddham
c trailokyahetor asurair yathāsīd
devasya viṣṇor jayatāṃ varasya
d trailokanāthasya ca cakrapāṇeḥ
a tair astam uccāvacam āyudhaugham
ekaḥ praciccheda kirīṭamālī
c kṣurārdhacandrair niśitaiś ca bāṇaiḥ
śirāṃsi teṣāṃ bahudhā ca bāhūn
a chatrāṇi vālavyajanāni ketūn
aśvān rathān pattigaṇān dvipāṃś ca
c te petur urvyāṃ bahudhā virūpā
vātaprabhagnāni yathā vanāni
a suvarṇajālāvatatā mahāgajāḥ
savaijayantīdhvajayodhakalpitāḥ
c suvarṇapuṅkhair iṣubhiḥ samācitāś
cakāśire prajvalitā yathācalāḥ
d vidīryamāṇā valinātra nāgāḥ
d davāgnidagdhair iva vaṃśadagdhaiḥ
a vidārya nāgāṃś ca rathāṃś ca vājinaḥ
śarottamair vāsavavajrasaṃnibhaiḥ
c drutaṃ yayau karṇajighāṃsayā tathā
yathā marutvān balabhedane purā
a tataḥ sa puruṣavyāghraḥ sūtasainyam ariṃdama
c praviveśa mahābāhur makaraḥ sāgaraṃ yathā
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā tāvakā rājan rathapattisamanvitāḥ
c gajāśvasādibahulāḥ pāṇḍavaṃ samupādravan
a tatrābhidravatāṃ pārtham ārāvaḥ sumahān abhūt
c sāgarasyeva mattasya yathā syāt salilasvanaḥ
a te tu taṃ puruṣavyāghraṃ vyāghrā iva mahārathāḥ
c abhyadravanta saṃgrāme tyaktvā prāṇakṛtaṃ bhayam
a teṣām āpatatāṃ tatra śaravarṣāṇi muñcatām
c arjuno vyadhamat sainyaṃ mahāvāto ghanān iva
a te 'rjunaṃ sahitā bhūtvā rathavaṃśaiḥ prahāriṇaḥ
c abhiyāya maheṣvāsā vivyadhur niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
d śaktibhis tomarair bāṇaiḥ kuṇapaiḥ kuramudgaraiḥ
d śūlais trimūlaiḥ parighair bhiṇḍipālaiḥ paraśvadhaiḥ
d karanālair gaḍaiḥ khaḍgair iṣṭibhir muśalais tathā
d parighaiḥ paṭṭiśaiś caiva gadābhiś ca paraśvadhaiḥ
d mahāyodhanaraiḥ kṣiptaiḥ saśarkarajapāṃśubhiḥ
d saśakrāśanisaṃpātaṃ jālaiḥ pāśaiḥ kaḍaṃgaraiḥ
d pradīptaśikharāvarṣaiḥ śilābhiḥ kāṣṭhaśaṃkubhiḥ
d mahārṣṭikābhiḥ kāntābhir ayaskāntair vināśinaiḥ
d praduṣṭacakrebhahayaiḥ sasaṃghair gūḍham āyudhaiḥ
d śibirād ekam āyāntam arjunaṃ sahakeśavam
d nānādeśyā nṛpavarā mlecchāś cāyutaśo 'bhyayuḥ
a tato 'rjunaḥ sahasrāṇi rathavāraṇavājinām
c preṣayām āsa viśikhair yamasya sadanaṃ prati
a te vadhyamānāḥ samare pārthacāpacyutaiḥ śaraiḥ
c tatra tatra sma līyante bhaye jāte mahārathāḥ
a teṣāṃ catuḥśatān vīrān yatamānān mahārathān
c arjuno niśitair bāṇair anayad yamasādanam
a te vadhyamānāḥ samare nānāliṅgaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c arjunaṃ samabhityajya dudruvur vai diśo bhayāt
a teṣāṃ śabdo mahān āsīd dravatāṃ vāhinīmukhe
c mahaughasyeva bhadraṃ te girim āsādya dīryataḥ
a tāṃ tu senāṃ bhṛśaṃ viddhvā drāvayitvārjunaḥ śaraiḥ
c prāyād abhimukhaḥ pārthaḥ sūtānīkāni māriṣa
a tasya śabdo mahān āsīt parān abhimukhasya vai
b tasyābhidravataḥ karṇaṃ rathaghoṣo mahān abhūt
c garuḍasyeva patataḥ pannagārthe yathā purā
a taṃ tu śabdam abhiśrutya bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
c babhūva paramaprītaḥ pārthadarśanalālasaḥ
a śrutvaiva pārtham āyāntaṃ bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān
c tyaktvā prāṇān mahārāja senāṃ tava mamarda ha
a sa vāyuvegapratimo vāyuvegasamo jave
c vāyuvad vyacarad bhīmo vāyuputraḥ pratāpavān
a tenārdyamānā rājendra senā tava viśāṃ pate
c vyabhrāmyata mahārāja bhinnā naur iva sāgare
a tāṃ tu senāṃ tadā bhīmo darśayan pāṇilāghavam
b rathaṃ rathenābhyahanat turagāṃs turagais tathā
b gajān gajair naravarān narair evānayat kṣayam
b kaṃ cid gajaṃ samutkṣipya gajaṃ bhīmo 'bhyadhāvata
b mahauṣadhisamāyuktaṃ hanumān iva parvatam
b sa tu tenāhanat kruddho giriṇeva mahāgirim
b kasya cid dantam utpāṭya dantenaivāhanad gajam
b yathairāvatam āsādya kumbhakarṇaḥ purā raṇe
b gajau saṃgṛhya pāṇibhyāṃ saṃnipātair amārayat
b rathān hayān nṛpavarān āviṣṭa iva pāṇḍavaḥ
c śarair avacakartograiḥ preṣayiṣyan yamakṣayam
a tatra bhārata bhīmasya balaṃ dṛṣṭvātimānuṣam
c vyatrasyanta raṇe yodhāḥ kālasyeva yugakṣaye
a tathārditān bhīmabalān bhīmasenena bhārata
c dṛṣṭvā duryodhano rājā idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a sainikān sa maheṣvāso yodhāṃś ca bharatarṣabha
c samādiśad raṇe sarvān hata bhīmam iti sma ha
e tasmin hate hataṃ manye sarvasainyam aśeṣataḥ
a pratigṛhya ca tām ājñāṃ tava putrasya pārthivāḥ
c bhīmaṃ pracchādayām āsuḥ śaravarṣaiḥ samantataḥ
d tasmin raṇe mahārāja maheṣvāsā narās tathā
a gajāś ca bahulā rājan narāś ca jayagṛddhinaḥ
c rathā hayāś ca rājendra parivavrur vṛkodaram
a sa taiḥ parivṛtaḥ śūraiḥ śūro rājan samantataḥ
c śuśubhe bharataśreṣṭha nakṣatrair iva candramāḥ
d pariveṣī yathā somaḥ paripūrṇo virājate
a sa rarāja tathā saṃkhye darśanīyo narottamaḥ
c nirviśeṣaṃ mahārāja yathā hi vijayas tathā
a tatra te pārthivāḥ sarve śaravṛṣṭīḥ samāsṛjan
c krodharaktekṣaṇāḥ krūrā hantukāmā vṛkodaram
a sa vidārya mahāsenāṃ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c niścakrāma raṇād bhīmo matsyo jālād ivāmbhasi
a hatvā daśa sahasrāṇi gajānām anivartinām
c nṛṇāṃ śatasahasre dve dve śate caiva bhārata
a pañca cāśvasahasrāṇi rathānāṃ śatam eva ca
c hatvā prāsyandayad bhīmo nadīṃ śoṇitakardamām
a śoṇitodāṃ rathāvartāṃ hastigrāhasamākulām
c naramīnām aśvanakrāṃ keśaśaivalaśādvalām
a saṃchinnabhujanāgendrāṃ bahuratnāpahāriṇīm
c ūrugrāhāṃ majjapaṅkāṃ śīrṣopalasamākulām
a dhanuṣkāśāṃ śarāvāpāṃ gadāparighaketanām
b haṃsacchatradhvajopetām uṣṇīṣavaraphenilām
b hārapadmākarāṃ caiva bhūmireṇūrmimālinīm
b āryavṛttavatīṃ saṃkhye sutarāṃ bhīrudustarām
c yodhavrātavatīṃ saṃkhye vahantīṃ yamasādanam
a kṣaṇena puruṣavyāghraḥ prāvartayata nimnagām
c yathā vaitaraṇīm ugrāṃ dustarām akṛtātmabhiḥ
d tathā dustaraṇīṃ ghorāṃ bhīrūṇāṃ bhayavardhanīm
d tathā prāvartayad bhīmo vīrayodhāpahāriṇīm
a yato yataḥ pāṇḍaveyaḥ pravṛtto rathasattamaḥ
c tatas tato 'pātayata yodhāñ śatasahasraśaḥ
a evaṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛtaṃ karma bhīmasenena saṃyuge
c duryodhano mahārāja śakuniṃ vākyam abravīt
a jaya mātula saṃgrāme bhīmasenaṃ mahābalam
c asmiñ jite jitaṃ manye pāṇḍaveyaṃ mahābalam
a tataḥ prāyān mahārāja saubaleyaḥ pratāpavān
c raṇāya mahate yukto bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritaḥ
a sa samāsādya saṃgrāme bhīmaṃ bhīmaparākramam
c vārayām āsa taṃ vīro veleva makarālayam
e sa nyavartata taṃ bhīmo vāryamāṇaḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
f bhāgineyavacaḥ śrutvā śakuniḥ śaṭhakṛttamaḥ
a śakunis tasya rājendra vāme pārśve stanāntare
c preṣayām āsa nārācān rukmapuṅkhāñ śilāśitān
a varma bhittvā tu sauvarṇaṃ bāṇās tasya mahātmanaḥ
c nyamajjanta mahārāja kaṅkabarhiṇavāsasaḥ
a so 'tividdho raṇe bhīmaḥ śaraṃ hemavibhūṣitam
c preṣayām āsa sahasā saubalaṃ prati bhārata
a tam āyāntaṃ śaraṃ ghoraṃ śakuniḥ śatrutāpanaḥ
c ciccheda śatadhā rājan kṛtahasto mahābalaḥ
a tasmin nipatite bhūmau bhīmaḥ kruddho viśāṃ pate
c dhanuś ciccheda bhallena saubalasya hasann iva
a tad apāsya dhanuś chinnaṃ saubaleyaḥ pratāpavān
c anyad ādatta vegena dhanur bhallāṃś ca ṣoḍaśa
a tais tasya tu mahārāja bhallaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c caturbhiḥ sārathiṃ hy ārcchad bhīmaṃ pañcabhir eva ca
a dhvajam ekena ciccheda chatraṃ dvābhyāṃ viśāṃ pate
c caturbhiś caturo vāhān vivyādha subalātmajaḥ
d tato hṛṣṭo mahārāja tava putro mahīpatiḥ
d sādhu sādhu mahābāho jahi bhīmaṃ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
d ayam eva suduṣṭātmā sarvadāsmān prabādhate
d mardayainaṃ mahābāho vinihatya sukhī bhava
a tataḥ kruddho mahārāja bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān
c śaktiṃ cikṣepa samare rukmadaṇḍām ayasmayīm
a sā bhīmabhujanirmuktā nāgajihveva cañcalā
c nipapāta rathe tūrṇaṃ saubalasya mahātmanaḥ
a tatas tām eva saṃgṛhya śaktiṃ kanakabhūṣaṇām
c bhīmasenāya cikṣepa kruddharūpo viśāṃ pate
d bhīmo 'pi paramāmarṣī tāṃ śaktiṃ saṃnivārya ca
d mumoca śaravarṣāṇi śakuneḥ sarvamarmasu
d saubalaḥ so 'pi duṣṭātmā bhīmasenaśarārditaḥ
d papāta ca rathopasthe paśyatāṃ sarvabhūbhṛtām
a sā nirbhidya bhujaṃ savyaṃ pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ
c papāta ca tato bhūmau yathā vidyun nabhaścyutā
a athotkruṣṭaṃ mahārāja dhārtarāṣṭraiḥ samantataḥ
c na tu taṃ mamṛṣe bhīmaḥ siṃhanādaṃ tarasvinām
a sa saṃgṛhya dhanuḥ sajyaṃ tvaramāṇo mahārathaḥ
c muhūrtād iva rājendra chādayām āsa sāyakaiḥ
e saubalasya balaṃ saṃkhye tyaktvātmānaṃ mahābalaḥ
a tasyāśvāṃś caturo hatvā sūtaṃ caiva viśāṃ pate
c dhvajaṃ ciccheda bhallena tvaramāṇaḥ parākramī
a hatāśvaṃ ratham utsṛjya tvaramāṇo narottamaḥ
c tasthau visphārayaṃś cāpaṃ krodharaktekṣaṇaḥ śvasan
e śaraiś ca bahudhā rājan bhīmam ārcchat samantataḥ
a pratihatya tu vegena bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān
c dhanuś ciccheda saṃkruddho vivyādha ca śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a so 'tividdho balavatā śatruṇā śatrukarśanaḥ
c nipapāta tato bhūmau kiṃ cit prāṇo narādhipa
a tatas taṃ vihvalaṃ jñātvā putras tava viśāṃ pate
c apovāha rathenājau bhīmasenasya paśyataḥ
a rathasthe tu naravyāghre dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ parāṅmukhāḥ
c pradudruvur diśo bhītā bhīmāj jāte mahābhaye
a saubale nirjite rājan bhīmasenena dhanvinā
c bhayena mahatā bhagnaḥ putro duryodhanas tava
e apāyāj javanair aśvaiḥ sāpekṣo mātulaṃ prati
a parāṅmukhaṃ tu rājānaṃ dṛṣṭvā sainyāni bhārata
c viprajagmuḥ samutsṛjya dvairathāni samantataḥ
a tān dṛṣṭvātirathān sarvān dhārtarāṣṭrān parāṅmukhān
c javenābhyapatad bhīmaḥ kirañ śaraśatān bahūn
a te vadhyamānā bhīmena dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ parāṅmukhāḥ
c karṇam āsādya samare sthitā rājan samantataḥ
e sa hi teṣāṃ mahāvīryo dvīpo 'bhūt sumahābalaḥ
a bhinnanaukā yathā rājan dvīpam āsādya nirvṛtāḥ
c bhavanti puruṣavyāghra nāvikāḥ kālaparyaye
a tathā karṇaṃ samāsādya tāvakā bharatarṣabha
b agādhe majjatāṃ teṣāṃ karṇo dvīpo 'bhavat tadā
c samāśvastāḥ sthitā rājan saṃprahṛṣṭāḥ parasparam
e samājagmuś ca yuddhāya mṛtyuṃ kṛtvā nivartanam
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a tato bhagneṣu sainyeṣu bhīmasenena saṃyuge
c duryodhano 'bravīt kiṃ nu saubalo vāpi saṃjaya
a karṇo vā jayatāṃ śreṣṭho yodhā vā māmakā yudhi
c kṛpo vā kṛtavarmā ca drauṇir duḥśāsano 'pi vā
a atyadbhutam idaṃ manye pāṇḍaveyasya vikramam
b yad ekaḥ samare sarvān yodhamāyāsa māmakān
c yathāpratijñaṃ yodhānāṃ rādheyaḥ kṛtavān api
a kurūṇām api sarveṣāṃ karṇaḥ śatruniṣūdanaḥ
b sarveṣāṃ kuruyaudhānāṃ karṇo vai śatrusūdanaḥ
c śarma varma pratiṣṭhā ca jīvitāśā ca saṃjaya
a tat prabhagnaṃ balaṃ dṛṣṭvā kaunteyenāmitaujasā
c rādheyānām adhirathaḥ karṇaḥ kim akarod yudhi
a putrā vā mama durdharṣā rājāno vā mahārathāḥ
c etan me sarvam ācakṣva kuśalo hy asi saṃjaya
 saṃjaya uvāca
a aparāhṇe mahārāja sūtaputraḥ pratāpavān
c jaghāna somakān sarvān bhīmasenasya paśyataḥ
e bhīmo 'py atibalaḥ sainyaṃ dhārtarāṣṭraṃ vyapothayat
f atha karṇo 'bravīc chalyaṃ pāñcālān prāpayasva mām
a drāvyamāṇaṃ balaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenena dhīmatā
c yantāram abravīt karṇaḥ pāñcālān eva mā vaha
a madrarājas tataḥ śalyaḥ śvetān aśvān mahājavān
c prāhiṇoc cedipāñcālān karūṣāṃś ca mahābalaḥ
a praviśya ca sa tāṃ senāṃ śalyaḥ parabalārdanaḥ
c nyayacchat turagān hṛṣṭo yatra yatraicchad agraṇīḥ
a taṃ rathaṃ meghasaṃkāśaṃ vaiyāghraparivāraṇam
c saṃdṛśya pāṇḍupāñcālās trastā āsan viśāṃ pate
a tato rathasya ninadaḥ prādurāsīn mahāraṇe
c parjanyasamanirghoṣaḥ parvatasyeva dīryataḥ
a tataḥ śaraśatais tīkṣṇaiḥ karṇo 'py ākarṇaniḥsṛtaiḥ
c jaghāna pāṇḍavabalaṃ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a taṃ tathā samare karma kurvāṇam atimānuṣam
c parivavrur maheṣvāsāḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥ
a taṃ śikhaṇḍī ca bhīmaś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥ
c nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca draupadeyāḥ sasātyakāḥ
e parivavrur jighāṃsanto rādheyaṃ śaravṛṣṭibhiḥ
a sātyakis tu tataḥ karṇaṃ viṃśatyā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c atāḍayad raṇe śūro jatrudeśe narottamaḥ
a śikhaṇḍī pañcaviṃśatyā dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pañcabhiḥ
c draupadeyāś catuḥṣaṣṭyā sahadevaś ca saptabhiḥ
e nakulaś ca śatenājau karṇaṃ vivyādha sāyakaiḥ
a bhīmasenas tu rādheyaṃ navatyā nataparvaṇām
c vivyādha samare kruddho jatrudeśe mahābalaḥ
a tataḥ prahasyādhirathir vikṣipan dhanur uttamam
c mumoca niśitān bāṇān pīḍayan sumahābalaḥ
e tān pratyavidhyad rādheyaḥ pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ
a sātyakes tu dhanuś chittvā dhvajaṃ ca puruṣarṣabhaḥ
c athainaṃ navabhir bāṇair ājaghāna stanāntare
a bhīmasenas tu taṃ kruddho vivyādha triṃśatā śaraiḥ
b sahadevasya bhallena dhvajaṃ ciccheda māriṣa
c sārathiṃ ca tribhir bāṇair ājaghāna paraṃtapaḥ
a virathān draupadeyāṃś ca cakāra puruṣarṣabhaḥ
c akṣṇor nimeṣamātreṇa tad adbhutam ivābhavat
a vimukhīkṛtya tān sarvāñ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c pāñcālān ahanac chūraś cedīnāṃ ca mahārathān
a te vadhyamānāḥ samare cedimatsyā viśāṃ pate
c karṇam ekam abhidrutya śarasaṃghaiḥ samārdayan
e tāñ jaghāna śitair bāṇaiḥ sūtaputro mahārathaḥ
f prādravanta raṇe bhītāḥ siṃhatrastā mṛgā iva
f tatas tān prahasan vīro vijigye pāṇḍavān raṇe
a etad atyadbhutaṃ karṇe dṛṣṭavān asmi bhārata
c yad ekaḥ samare śūrān sūtaputraḥ pratāpavān
c   yatamānān mahārathān
c yodhayām āsa samare
a yatamānān paraṃ śaktyāyodhayat tāṃś ca dhanvinaḥ
c pāṇḍaveyān mahārāja śarair vāritavān raṇe
a tatra bhārata karṇasya lāghavena mahātmanaḥ
c tutuṣur devatāḥ sarvāḥ siddhāś ca paramarṣayaḥ
a apūjayan maheṣvāsā dhārtarāṣṭrā narottamam
c karṇaṃ rathavaraśreṣṭhaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ sarvadhanuṣmatām
a tataḥ karṇo mahārāja dadāha ripuvāhinīm
b ekavīro maheṣvāso vighnastāparivāhiṇam sic
b samardayañ charais tīkṣṇaiḥ pāñcālānāṃ pravāhinīm
c kakṣam iddho yathā vahnir nidāghe jvalito mahān
a te vadhyamānāḥ karṇena pāṇḍaveyās tatas tataḥ
c prādravanta raṇe bhītāḥ karṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā mahābalam
a tatrākrando mahān āsīt pāñcālānāṃ mahāraṇe
c vadhyatāṃ sāyakais tīkṣṇaiḥ karṇacāpavaracyutaiḥ
a tena śabdena vitrastā pāṇḍavānāṃ mahācamūḥ
c karṇam ekaṃ raṇe yodhaṃ menire tatra śātravāḥ
a tatrādbhutaṃ paraṃ cakre rādheyaḥ śatrukarśanaḥ
c yad ekaṃ pāṇḍavāḥ sarve na śekur abhivīkṣitum
a yathaughaḥ parvataśreṣṭham āsādyābhipradīryate
c tathā tat pāṇḍavaṃ sainyaṃ karṇam āsādya dīryate
a karṇo 'pi samare rājan vidhūmo 'gnir iva jvalan
c dahaṃs tasthau mahābāhuḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahācamūm
a śirāṃsi ca mahārāja karṇāṃś cañcalakuṇḍalān
c bāhūṃś ca vīro vīrāṇāṃ ciccheda laghu ceṣubhiḥ
a hastidantān tsarūn khaḍgān dhvajāñ śaktīr hayān gajān
c rathāṃś ca vividhān rājan patākā vyajanāni ca
a akṣeṣāyugayoktrāṇi cakrāṇi vividhāni ca
c ciccheda śatadhā karṇo yodhavratam anuṣṭhitaḥ
a tatra bhārata karṇena nihatair gajavājibhiḥ
c agamyarūpā pṛthivī māṃsaśoṇitakardamā
a viṣamaṃ ca samaṃ caiva hatair aśvapadātibhiḥ
c rathaiś ca kuñjaraiś caiva na prājñāyata kiṃ cana
a nāpi sve na pare yodhāḥ prājñāyanta parasparam
c ghore śarāndhakāre tu karṇāstre ca vijṛmbhite
a rādheyacāpanirmuktaiḥ śaraiḥ kāñcanabhūṣitaiḥ
c saṃchāditā mahārāja yatamānā mahārathāḥ
a te pāṇḍaveyāḥ samare karṇena sma punaḥ punaḥ
c abhajyanta mahārāja yatamānā mahārathāḥ
a mṛgasaṃghān yathā kruddhaḥ siṃho drāvayate vane
b pāñcālānāṃ rathaśreṣṭhān drāvayañ chātravāṃs tathā
c karṇas tu samare yodhāṃs tatra tatra mahāyaśāḥ
e kālayām āsa tat sainyaṃ yathā paśugaṇān vṛkaḥ
a dṛṣṭvā tu pāṇḍavīṃ senāṃ dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ parāṅmukhīm
c abhijagmur maheṣvāsā ruvanto bhairavān ravān
a duryodhano hi rājendra mudā paramayā yutaḥ
c vādayām āsa saṃhṛṣṭo nānāvādyāni sarvaśaḥ
a pāñcālāpi maheṣvāsā bhagnā bhagnā narottamāḥ
c nyavartanta yathā śūrā mṛtyuṃ kṛtvā nivartanam
a tān nivṛttān raṇe śūrān rādheyaḥ śatrutāpanaḥ
c anekaśo mahārāja babhañja puruṣarṣabhaḥ
a tatra bhārata karṇena pāñcālā viṃśatī rathāḥ
c nihatāḥ sādayaḥ krodhāc cedayaś ca paraḥśatāḥ
a kṛtvā śūnyān rathopasthān vājipṛṣṭhāṃś ca bhārata
c nirmanuṣyān gajaskandhān pādātāṃś caiva vidrutān
a āditya iva madhyāhne durnirīkṣyaḥ paraṃtapaḥ
c kālāntakavapuḥ krūraḥ sūtaputraś cacāra ha
a evam etān mahārāja naravājirathadvipān
c hatvā tasthau maheṣvāsaḥ karṇo 'rigaṇasūdanaḥ
a yathā bhūtagaṇān hatvā kālas tiṣṭhen mahābalaḥ
c tathā sa somakān hatvā tasthāv eko mahārathaḥ
a tatrādbhutam apaśyāma pāñcālānāṃ parākramam
c vadhyamānāpi karṇena nājahū raṇamūrdhani
a rājā duḥśāsanaś caiva kṛpaḥ śāradvatas tathā
c aśvatthāmā kṛtavarmā śakuniś cāpi saubalaḥ
e nyahanan pāṇḍavīṃ senāṃ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a karṇaputrau ca rājendra bhrātarau satyavikramau
c anāśayetāṃ balinaḥ pāñcālān vai tatas tataḥ
e tatra yuddhaṃ tadā hy āsīt krūraṃ viśasanaṃ mahat
a tathaiva pāṇḍavāḥ śūrā dhṛṣṭadyumnaśikhaṇḍinau
c draupadeyāś ca saṃkruddhā abhyaghnaṃs tāvakaṃ balam
a evam eṣa kṣayo vṛttaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ tatas tataḥ
c tāvakānām api raṇe bhīmaṃ prāpya mahābalam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a arjunas tu mahārāja kṛtvā sainyaṃ pṛthagvidham
c sūtaputraṃ susaṃrabdhaṃ dṛṣṭvā caiva mahāraṇe
d hatvā tu phalgunaḥ sainyaṃ kauravāṇāṃ pṛthak pṛthak
d sūtaputrasya saṃrambhaṃ dṛṣṭvā cāpi mahāhave
a śoṇitodāṃ mahīṃ kṛtvā māṃsamajjāsthivāhinīm
b manuṣyaśīrṣapāṣāṇāṃ hastyaśvakṛtarodhasam
b śūrāsthicayasaṃkīrṇāṃ kākagṛdhrānunāditām
b chatrahaṃsaplavopetāṃ vīravṛkṣāpahāriṇīm
b hārapadmākaravatīm uṣṇīṣavaraphenilām
b dhanuḥśaradhvajopetāṃ narakṣudrakapālinīm
b carmavarmabhramopetāṃ rathoḍupasamākulām
b jayaiṣiṇāṃ ca sutarāṃ bhīrūṇāṃ ca sudustarām
b tāṃ nadīṃ prāpayitvā tu bībhatsuḥ paravīrahā
c vāsudevam idaṃ vākyam abravīt puruṣarṣabha
a eṣa ketū raṇe kṛṣṇa sūtaputrasya dṛśyate
c bhīmasenādayaś caite yodhayanti mahārathān
e ete dravanti pāñcālāḥ karṇāt trastā janārdana
a eṣa duryodhano rājā śvetacchatreṇa bhāsvatā
c karṇena bhagnān pāñcālān drāvayan bahu śobhate
a kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca drauṇiś caiva mahābalaḥ
c ete rakṣanti rājānaṃ sūtaputreṇa rakṣitāḥ
e avadhyamānās te 'smābhir ghātayiṣyanti somakān
a eṣa śalyo rathopasthe raśmisaṃcārakovidaḥ
c sūtaputrarathaṃ kṛṣṇa vāhayan bahu śobhate
a tatra me buddhir utpannā vāhayātra mahāratham
c nāhatvā samare karṇaṃ nivartiṣye kathaṃ cana
a rādheyo 'py anyathā pārthān sṛñjayāṃś ca mahārathān
c niḥśeṣān samare kuryāt paśyator nau janārdana
d evam uktas tu pārthena kṛṣṇo rājaṃs tvarānvitaḥ
a tataḥ prāyād rathenāśu keśavas tava vāhinīm
c karṇaṃ prati maheṣvāsaṃ dvairathe savyasācinā
a prayātaś ca mahābāhuḥ pāṇḍavānujñayā hariḥ
b sa prayāto rathenāśu kṛṣṇo rājan mahāhave
c āśvāsayan rathenaiva pāṇḍusainyāni sarvaśaḥ
a rathaghoṣaḥ sa saṃgrāme pāṇḍaveyasya saṃbabhau
c vāsavāśanitulyasya mahaughasyeva māriṣa
d rathaghoṣas tatas tasya pāṇḍavasya babhūva ha
d vāsavāstranipātena parvateṣv iva māriṣa
a mahatā rathaghoṣeṇa pāṇḍavaḥ satyavikramaḥ
c abhyayād aprameyātmā vijayas tava vāhinīm
a tam āyāntaṃ samīkṣyaiva śvetāśvaṃ kṛṣṇasārathim
c madrarājo 'bravīt karṇaṃ ketuṃ dṛṣṭvā mahātmanaḥ
a ayaṃ sa ratha āyāti śvetāśvaḥ kṛṣṇasārathiḥ
c nighnann amitrān samare yaṃ karṇa paripṛcchasi
a eṣa tiṣṭhati kaunteyaḥ saṃspṛśan gāṇḍivaṃ dhanuḥ
c taṃ haniṣyasi ced adya tan naḥ śreyo bhaviṣyati
d tvām abhiprepsur āyāti karṇa nighnan varān rathān
d asajjamāno rādheya taṃ yāhi prati bhāratam
d ghṛṇāṃ tyaktvā prasādaṃ ca bhṛgor astraṃ ca saṃsmaran
d dṛṣṭiṃ muṣṭiṃ ca saṃdhānaṃ smṛtvā rāmopadeśajam
d dhanaṃjayaṃ jaye prepsuḥ pratyudgamya mahārathān
d vājividyāparijñāne na me yuddhe bale hariḥ
d na māṃ vijeṣyate karṇa gadāyuddhe viśeṣataḥ
d dhanurjyā candratārārkapatākā kiṅkiṇīyutā
d paśya karṇārjunasyaiṣā saudāminy ambare yathā
d eṣa dhvajāgre pārthasya prekṣamāṇaḥ samantataḥ
d dṛśyate vānaro bhīmo vīkṣatāṃ bhayavardhanaḥ
d etac cakraṃ gadā śaṅkhaḥ śārṅgaṃ kṛṣṇasya ca prabho
d dṛśyate pāṇḍavarathe vāhayānasya vājinaḥ
d etat kūjati gāṇḍīvaṃ vikṛṣṭaṃ savyasācinā
d ete hastavatā muktā ghnanty amitrāñ śitāḥ śarāḥ
d viśālāyatatāmrākṣaiḥ pūrṇacandranibhānanaiḥ
d eṣā bhūḥ kīryate rājñāṃ śirobhir apalāyinām
d ete parighasaṃkāśāḥ puṇyagandhānulepanāḥ
d udyatā raṇaśauṇḍānāṃ pātyante sāyudhā bhujāḥ
d nirastajihvānetrāntā vājinaḥ sahasādibhiḥ
d patitāḥ pātyamānāś ca kṣitau kṣīṇā viśerate
d ete parvataśṛṅgāṇāṃ tulyā haimavatā gajāḥ
d saṃchinnahastāḥ pārthena prapatanty adrayo yathā
d gandharvanagarākārā rathā hatanareśvarāḥ
d vimānānīva puṇyānte svargiṇāṃ nipatanty amī
d vyākulīkṛtam atyarthaṃ paśya sainyaṃ kirīṭinā
d nānāmṛgasahasrāṇāṃ yūthaṃ kesariṇā yathā
a eṣā vidīryate senā dhārtarāṣṭrī samantataḥ
c arjunasya bhayāt tūrṇaṃ nighnataḥ śātravān bahūn
a varjayan sarvasainyāni tvarate hi dhanaṃjayaḥ
c tvadartham iti manye 'haṃ yathāsyodīryate vapuḥ
a na hy avasthāpyate pārtho yuyutsuḥ kena cit saha
c tvām ṛte krodhadīpto hi pīḍyamāne vṛkodare
a virathaṃ dharmarājaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā sudṛḍhavikṣatam
c śikhaṇḍinaṃ sātyakiṃ ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca pārṣatam
a draupadeyān yudhāmanyum uttamaujasam eva ca
c nakulaṃ sahadevaṃ ca bhrātarau dvau samīkṣya ca
a sahasaikarathaḥ pārthas tvām abhyeti paraṃtapa
c krodharaktekṣaṇaḥ kruddho jighāṃsuḥ sarvadhanvinām
a tvarito 'bhipataty asmāṃs tyaktvā sainyāny asaṃśayam
c tvaṃ karṇa pratiyāhy enaṃ nāsty anyo hi dhanurdharaḥ
a na taṃ paśyāmi loke 'smiṃs tvatto 'py anyaṃ dhanurdharam
c arjunaṃ samare kruddhaṃ yo velām iva dhārayet
d yo 'rjunaṃ sāgaraughābhaṃ kruddhaṃ veleva vārayet
a na cāsya rakṣāṃ paśyāmi pṛṣṭhato na ca pārśvataḥ
c eka evābhiyāti tvāṃ paśya sāphalyam ātmanaḥ
a tvaṃ hi kṛṣṇau raṇe śaktaḥ saṃsādhayitum āhave
c tavaiṣa bhāro rādheya pratyudyāhi dhanaṃjayam
a tvaṃ kṛto hy eva bhīṣmeṇa droṇadrauṇikṛpair api
c savyasācipratirathas taṃ nivartaya pāṇḍavam
d savyasācinam āyāntaṃ nivāraya mahāraṇe
a lelihānaṃ yathā sarpaṃ garjantam ṛṣabhaṃ yathā
c layasthitaṃ yathā vyāghraṃ jahi karṇa dhanaṃjayam
a ete dravanti samare dhārtarāṣṭrā mahārathāḥ
c arjunasya bhayāt tūrṇaṃ nirapekṣā janādhipāḥ
a dravatām atha teṣāṃ tu yudhi nānyo 'sti mānavaḥ
c bhayahā yo bhaved vīra tvām ṛte sūtanandana
a ete tvāṃ kuravaḥ sarve dvīpam āsādya saṃyuge
c viṣṭhitāḥ puruṣavyāghra tvattaḥ śaraṇakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
a vaidehāmbaṣṭhakāmbojās tathā nagnajitas tvayā
c gāndhārāś ca yayā dhṛtyā jitāḥ saṃkhye sudurjayāḥ
a tāṃ dhṛtiṃ kuru rādheya tataḥ pratyehi pāṇḍavam
c vāsudevaṃ ca vārṣṇeyaṃ prīyamāṇaṃ kirīṭinā
d pratyudyāhi mahābāho pauruṣe mahati sthitaḥ
d yathaikena tvayā pūrvaṃ kṛto digvijayo mahān

d duryodhanasya mahiṣī jarāsaṃdhaṃ vijitya ca
d tad eva sattvam ālambya jahi pārthaṃ dhanaṃjayam
 karṇa uvāca
a prakṛtistho hi me śalya idānīṃ saṃmatas tathā
c pratibhāsi mahābāho vibhīś caiva dhanaṃjayāt
a paśya bāhvor balaṃ me 'dya śikṣitasya ca paśya me
c eko 'dya nihaniṣyāmi pāṇḍavānāṃ mahācamūm
a kṛṣṇau ca puruṣavyāghrau tac ca satyaṃ bravīmi te
c nāhatvā yudhi tau vīrāv apayāsye kathaṃ cana

c kṛtārtho vā bhaviṣyāmi hatvā tāv atha vā hataḥ

d kṛtārtho vā gamiṣyāmi hato vā svagam āpnuyām

d ajayyam enaṃ pravadanti yuddhe

d ekākinaṃ kim u kṛṣṇābhiguptaṃ
d vijetum enaṃ ka ihotsaheta
a naitādṛśo jātu babhūva loke

b adyāhaṃ taṃ nihaniṣyāmi saṃkhye
b dhanaṃjayaṃ paśyatas te samṛddham
c tam īdṛśaṃ pratiyotsyāmi pārthaṃ
mahāhave paśya ca pauruṣaṃ me
a rathe caraty eṣa rathapravīraḥ

c sa vādya māṃ neṣyati kṛcchram etat

d rathān varān eti rathapravīraḥ
d śīghrair hayaiḥ kauravarājaputraḥ

d karṇo 'syānte 'py atra bhavet samarthaḥ
a asvedinau rājaputrasya hastāv
avepinau jātakiṇau bṛhantau
c dṛḍhāyudhaḥ kṛtimān kṣiprahasto

a gṛhṇāty anekān api kaṅkapatrān
ekaṃ yathā tān kṣitipān pramathya
c te krośamātraṃ nipatanty amoghāḥ
kas tena yodho 'sti samaḥ pṛthivyām
d gṛhṇan vimuñcan sa nimeṣamātrāt
d puraṃdarasyeva ca tulyavīryaḥ
d te krośamātre nipatanty amoghā
d na pāṇḍavasya sadṛśo 'sti kaś cit
d atīvānyān dhanuṣā rājaputras
d tv atīvānyān keśavaś cakrayuddhe
a atoṣayat pāṇḍaveyo hutāśaṃ
kṛṣṇadvitīyo 'tirathas tarasvī
c lebhe cakraṃ yatra kṛṣṇo mahātmā
dhanur gāṇḍīvaṃ pāṇḍavaḥ savyasācī
a śvetāśvayuktaṃ ca sughoṣam agryaṃ
rathaṃ mahābāhur adīnasattvaḥ
c maheṣudhī cākṣayau divyarūpau
śastrāṇi divyāni ca havyavāhāt
a tathendraloke nijaghāna daityān
asaṃkhyeyān kālakeyāṃś ca sarvān
c lebhe śaṅkhaṃ devadattaṃ sma tatra
ko nāma tenābhyadhikaḥ pṛthivyām
a mahādevaṃ toṣayām āsa caiva
sākṣāt suyuddhena mahānubhāvaḥ
c lebhe tataḥ pāśupataṃ sughoraṃ

a pṛthak pṛthag lokapālāḥ sametā
dadur hy astrāṇy aprameyāṇi yasya
c yais tāñ jaghānāśu raṇe nṛsiṃhān
sa kālakhañjān asurān sametān
a tathā virāṭasya pure sametān
sarvān asmān ekarathena jitvā
c jahāra tad godhanam ājimadhye
vastrāṇi cādatta mahārathebhyaḥ
a tam īdṛśaṃ vīryaguṇopapannaṃ
kṛṣṇadvitīyaṃ varaye raṇāya
b tam āhvayan sāhasam uttamaṃ vai
b jāne svayaṃ sarvalokasya śalya
c anantavīryeṇa ca keśavena
nārāyaṇenāpratimena guptam
a varṣāyutair yasya guṇā na śakyā
vaktuṃ sametair api sarvalokaiḥ
c mahātmanaḥ śaṅkhacakrāsipāṇer
viṣṇor jiṣṇor vasudevātmajasya
e bhayaṃ me vai jāyate sādhvasaṃ ca
dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇāv ekarathe sametau
f atīva pārtho yudhi kārmukibhyo
f nārāyaṇaś cāprati cakrayuddhe
f evaṃvidhau pāṇḍavavāsudevau
f calet svadeśād dhi bhavān na kṛṣṇau
f karṇaḥ
f kiṃ madrarājārjunavarṇanena
f māṃ bhīṣayasy adya raṇe 'pramattam
f nāhaṃ tvayā bhīṣayituṃ hi śakyo
f bandīva tasyaiva guṇāṃś ca stauṣi
f vīryeṇa yukto yudhi phalguno 'sau
f gupto yathā keśavenādya saṃkhye
f tathāpi te paśyatas taṃ nihanmi
f tūṣṇīṃ sthitaś codaya tāvad aśvān
f dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇāv ekarathe sametāv
f atīva harṣo mama jāyate 'dya
a ubhau hi śūrau kṛtinau dṛḍhāstrau
mahārathau saṃhananopapannau
b etādṛśau naravīrau sametau
b sthānāc cyutau devakumārarūpau
b agnyanilāv indrabṛhaspatī vā
b yamāntakau vā śaśipūṣaṇau vā
b bhagāṃśamitrāvaruṇāśvinau vā
b marudgaṇā vā vasavaḥ sahendrāḥ
b vyastāḥ samastāś ca yudhā na śaktā
b jetuṃ prasahyārjunam acyutaṃ ca
c etādṛśau phalgunavāsudevau
ko 'nyaḥ pratīyān mad ṛte nu śalya
d manoratho yas tu mamādya śalya
d madreśa yuddhaṃ prati pāṇḍavasya
d nedaṃ cirād āśu bhaviṣyatīdam
d atyadbhutaṃ citram atulyarūpam
d sarveṣāṃ vṛṣṇivīrāṇāṃ kṛṣṇe lakṣmīḥ pratiṣṭhitā
d sarveṣāṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ jayaḥ pārthe pratiṣṭhitaḥ
d tāv ubhau puruṣavyāghrau samāne syandane sthitau
d mām ekam abhiyoddhārau sujātaṃ bata śalya me
d naitac cirāt kṣipram imaṃ rathaṃ me
d pravartayaitāv abhiyāmi caiva
d asmin muhūrte nihatau paśya kṛṣṇau
d tābhyāṃ hataṃ vā yudhi māṃ ripubhyām
a etāv ahaṃ yudhi vā pātayiṣye
māṃ vā kṛṣṇau nihaniṣyato 'dya
c iti bruvañ śalyam amitrahantā
karṇo raṇe megha ivonnanāda
d asmin muhūrte nihatau paśya kṛṣṇau
d mayā hataṃ vā yudhi mām aribhyām
d evaṃ bruvāṇaḥ sahasā mahārathas
d tv abhyadravat pāṇḍavaṃ sūtaputraḥ
a abhyetya putreṇa tavābhinanditaḥ
sametya covāca kurupravīrān
c kṛpaṃ ca bhojaṃ ca mahābhujāv ubhau
tathaiva gāndhāranṛpaṃ sahānujam
e guroḥ sutaṃ cāvarajaṃ tathātmanaḥ
padātino 'tha dvipasādino 'nyān
f guroḥ sutas tatra tavātmajas tathā
f padātisādidviradā rathās tathā
a nirundhatābhidravatācyutārjunau
śrameṇa saṃyojayatāśu sarvataḥ
c yathā bhavadbhir bhṛśavikṣatāv ubhau
sukhena hanyām aham adya bhūmipāḥ
a tatheti coktvā tvaritāḥ sma te 'rjunaṃ
jighāṃsavo vīratamāḥ samabhyayuḥ
b śaraiś ca jaghnur yudhi taṃ mahārathā
b dhanaṃjayaṃ karṇanideśakāriṇaḥ
c nadīnadān bhūrijalo mahārṇavo
yathā tathā tān samare 'rjuno 'grasat
a na saṃdadhāno na tathā śarottamān
pramuñcamāno ripubhiḥ pradṛśyate
b na saṃdadhan naiva samuddharañ śarān
b na cābhimuñcann aribhiḥ sa dṛśyate
c dhanaṃjayas tasya śaraiś ca dāritā
hatāś ca petur naravājikuñjarāḥ
a śarārciṣaṃ gāṇḍivacārumaṇḍalaṃ
yugāntasūryapratimānatejasam
c na kauravāḥ śekur udīkṣituṃ jayaṃ
yathā raviṃ vyādhitacakṣuṣo janāḥ
d śarottamān sa prahitān mahārathaiś
d ciccheda pārthaḥ prahasañ śaraughaiḥ
d bhūyaś ca tān ahanad bāṇasaṃghān
d gāṇḍīvadhanvāyatapūrṇamaṇḍalam
d yathograraśmiḥ śuciśukramadhyagaḥ
d sukhaṃ vivasvān harate jalaughān
d tathārjuno bāṇagaṇān nirasya
d dadāha senāṃ tava pārthivendra
a tam abhyadhāvad visṛjañ śarān kṛpas
tathaiva bhojas tava cātmajaḥ svayam
b mahāratho droṇasutaś ca sāyakair
b avākiraṃs toyadharā yathācalam
b jighāṃsavaḥ pātham asahyavikramaṃ
b yathaiva vahniṃ śalabhā mahārciṣam
c jighāṃsubhis tān kuśalaiḥ śarottamān
mahāhave saṃjavitān prayatnataḥ
e śaraiḥ praciccheda ca pāṇḍavas tvaran
parābhinad vakṣasi ca tribhis tribhiḥ
a sa gāṇḍivābhyāyatapūrṇamaṇḍalas
tapan ripūn arjunabhāskaro babhau
c śarograraśmiḥ śuciśukramadhyago
yathaiva sūryaḥ pariveṣagas tathā
a athāgryabāṇair daśabhir dhanaṃjayaṃ
parābhinad droṇasuto 'cyutaṃ tribhiḥ
c caturbhir aśvāṃś caturaḥ kapiṃ tathā
śaraiḥ sa nārācavarair avākirat
a tathā tu tat tat sphurad āttakārmukaṃ
tribhiḥ śarair yantṛśiraḥ kṣureṇa
c hayāṃś caturbhiś caturas tribhir dhvajaṃ
dhanaṃjayo drauṇirathān nyapātayat
d sa droṇaputrasya śarāsanaṃ balī
d bhallena saṃchidya ca tad vyapātayat
a sa roṣapūrṇo 'śanivajrahāṭakair
alaṃkṛtaṃ takṣakabhogavarcasam
c subandhanaṃ kārmukam anyad ādade
yathā mahāhipravaraṃ gires tathā
a svam āyudhaṃ copavikīrya bhūtale
dhanuś ca kṛtvā saguṇaṃ guṇādhikaḥ
c samānayānāv ajitau narottamau
śarottamair drauṇir avidhyad antikāt
a kṛpaś ca bhojaś ca tathātmajaś ca te
tamonudaṃ vāridharā ivāpatan
b śarair anekair yudhi pāṇḍavarṣabham
b mahārathāḥ saṃyugamūrdhani sthitāḥ
b mahābalā vītabhayā raṇājire
c kṛpasya pārthaḥ saśaraṃ śarāsanaṃ
hayān dhvajaṃ sārathim eva patribhiḥ
d samārpayad bāhusahasravikramas
d tathā yathā vajradharaḥ purā baleḥ
d sa pārthabāṇair vinipātitāyudho
d dhvajāvamarde ca kṛte mahāhave
d kṛtaḥ kṛpo bāṇasahasrayantrito
d yathāpageyaḥ prathamaṃ kirīṭinā
a śaraiḥ praciccheda tavātmajasya
dhvajaṃ dhanuś ca pracakarta nardataḥ
c jaghāna cāśvān kṛtavarmaṇaḥ śubhān
dhvajaṃ ca ciccheda tataḥ pratāpavān
a savājisūteṣv asanān saketanāñ
jaghāna nāgāśvarathāṃs tvaraṃś ca saḥ
c tataḥ prakīrṇaṃ sumahad balaṃ tava
pradāritaṃ setur ivāmbhasā yathā
e tato 'rjunasyāśu rathena keśavaś
cakāra śatrūn apasavyam āturān
a tataḥ prayāntaṃ tvaritaṃ dhanaṃjayaṃ
śatakratuṃ vṛtranijaghnuṣaṃ yathā
c samanvadhāvan punar ucchritair dhvajai
rathaiḥ suyuktair apare yuyutsavaḥ
a athābhisṛtya prativārya tān arīn
dhanaṃjayasyābhi rathaṃ mahārathāḥ
c śikhaṇḍiśaineyayamāḥ śitaiḥ śarair
vidārayanto vyanadan subhairavam
a tato 'bhijaghnuḥ kupitāḥ parasparaṃ
śarais tadāñjogatibhiḥ sutejanaiḥ
c kurupravīrāḥ saha sṛñjayair yathā
surāḥ purā devavarair ayodhayan
a jayepsavaḥ svargamanāya cotsukāḥ
patanti nāgāśvarathāḥ paraṃtapa
c jagarjur uccair balavac ca vivyadhuḥ
śaraiḥ sumuktair itaretaraṃ pṛthak
a śarāndhakāre tu mahātmabhiḥ kṛte
mahāmṛdhe yodhavaraiḥ parasparam
c babhur daśāśā na divaṃ ca pārthiva
prabhā ca sūryasya tamovṛtābhavat
d śarāndhakāraṃ ca kṛtaṃ mahātmabhis
d tadā diśo na prababhuḥ śarārditāḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a rājan kurūṇāṃ pravarair balair bhīmam abhidrutam
c majjantam iva kaunteyam ujjihīrṣur dhanaṃjayaḥ
a vimṛdya sūtaputrasya senāṃ bhārata sāyakaiḥ
c prāhiṇon mṛtyulokāya paravīrān dhanaṃjayaḥ
a tato 'syāmbaram āvṛtya śarajālāni bhāgaśaḥ
c adṛśyanta tathānye ca nighnantas tava vāhinīm
a sa pakṣisaṃghācaritam ākāśaṃ pūrayañ śaraiḥ
c dhanaṃjayo mahārāja kurūṇām antako 'bhavat
a tato bhallaiḥ kṣurapraiś ca nārācair nirmalair api
c gātrāṇi prākṣiṇot pārthaḥ śirāṃsi ca cakarta ha
a chinnagātrair vikavacair viśiraskaiḥ samantataḥ
c patitaiś ca patadbhiś ca yodhair āsīt samāvṛtam
a dhanaṃjayaśarābhyastaiḥ syandanāśvanaradvipaiḥ
b saṃchinnabhinnavidhvastair vyaṅgāṅgāvayavaiḥ stṛtā
b sudurgamā suviṣamā ghorātyarthaṃ sudurdṛśā
c raṇabhūmir abhūd rājan mahāvaitaraṇī yathā
f gatasattvaiḥ sasattvaiś ca saṃvṛtāsīd vasuṃdharā
a īṣācakrākṣabhaṅgaiś ca vyaśvaiḥ sāśvaiś ca yudhyatām
c sasūtair hatasūtaiś ca rathaiḥ stīrṇābhavan mahī
d sasūtair hatasūtaiś ca sādihīnaiś ca vājibhiḥ
d īṣācakrākṣabhagnaiś ca rathaiḥ stīrṇā vasuṃdharā
a suvarṇavarmasaṃnāhair yodhaiḥ kanakabhūṣaṇaiḥ
c āsthitāḥ kṛtavarmāṇo bhadrā nityamadā dvipāḥ
e kruddhāḥ kruddhair mahāmātraiḥ preṣitārjunam abhyayuḥ
a catuḥśatāḥ śaravarṣair hatāḥ petuḥ kirīṭinā
c paryastānīva śṛṅgāṇi sasattvāni mahāgireḥ
a dhanaṃjayaśarābhyastaiḥ stīrṇā bhūr varavāraṇaiḥ
b samantāj jaladaprakhyān vāraṇān madavarṣiṇaḥ
c abhipede 'rjunaratho ghanān bhindann ivāṃśumān
a hatair gajamanuṣyāśvair bhagnaiś ca bahudhā rathaiḥ
c viśastrapatrakavacair yuddhaśauṇḍair gatāsubhiḥ
e apaviddhāyudhair mārgaḥ stīrṇo 'bhūt phalgunena vai
a vyasphūrjayac ca gāṇḍīvaṃ sumahad bhairavasvanam
c ghoro vajraviniṣpeṣaḥ stanayitnor ivāmbare
a tataḥ prādīryata camūr dhanaṃjayaśarāhatā
c mahāvātasamāviddhā mahānaur iva sāgare
a nānārūpāḥ praharaṇāḥ śarā gāṇḍīvacoditāḥ
c alātolkāśaniprakhyās tava sainyaṃ vinirdahan
a mahāgirau veṇuvanaṃ niśi prajvalitaṃ yathā
c tathā tava mahat sainyaṃ prāsphurac charapīḍitam
a saṃpiṣṭadagdhavidhvastaṃ tava sainyaṃ kirīṭinā
c hataṃ pravihataṃ bāṇaiḥ sarvataḥ pradrutaṃ diśaḥ
a mahāvane mṛgagaṇā dāvāgnigrasitā yathā
c kuravaḥ paryavartanta nirdagdhāḥ savyasācinā
a utsṛjya hi mahābāhuṃ bhīmasenaṃ tadā raṇe
c balaṃ kurūṇām udvignaṃ sarvam āsīt parāṅmukham
a tataḥ kuruṣu bhagneṣu bībhatsur aparājitaḥ
c bhīmasenaṃ samāsādya muhūrtaṃ so 'bhyavartata
a samāgamya sa bhīmena mantrayitvā ca phalgunaḥ
c viśalyam arujaṃ cāsmai kathayitvā yudhiṣṭhiram
a bhīmasenābhyanujñātas tataḥ prāyād dhanaṃjayaḥ
c nādayan rathaghoṣeṇa pṛthivīṃ dyāṃ ca bhārata
a tataḥ parivṛto bhīmair daśabhiḥ śatrupuṃgavaiḥ
c duḥśāsanād avarajais tava putrair dhanaṃjayaḥ
a te tam abhyardayan bāṇair ulkābhir iva kuñjaram
c ātateṣv asanāḥ krūrā nṛtyanta iva bhārata
a apasavyāṃs tu tāṃś cakre rathena madhusūdanaḥ
b niyuktān hi sa tān mene yamāyāśu kirīṭinā
c tatas te prādravañ śūrāḥ parāṅmukharathe 'rjune
a teṣām āpatatāṃ ketūn rathāṃś cāpāni sāyakān
c nārācair ardhacandraiś ca kṣipraṃ pārtho nyapātayat
a athānyair daśabhir bhallaiḥ śirāṃsy eṣāṃ nyapātayat
c roṣasaṃraktanetrāṇi saṃdaṣṭauṣṭhāni bhūtale
e tāni vaktrāṇi vibabhur vyomni tārāgaṇā iva
a tāṃs tu bhallair mahāvegair daśabhir daśa kauravān
c rukmāṅgadān rukmapuṅkhair viddhvā prāyād amitrahā
 saṃjaya uvāca
a taṃ tu yāntaṃ mahāvegair aśvaiḥ kapivaradhvajam
c yuddhāyābhyadravan vīrāḥ kurūṇāṃ navatī rathāḥ
d kṛtvā saṃśaptakā ghorāñ śapathān brāhmalaukikān
e parivavrur naravyāghrā naravyāghraṃ raṇe 'rjunam
a kṛṣṇaḥ śvetān mahāvegān aśvān kanakabhūṣaṇān
c muktājālapraticchannān praiṣīt karṇarathaṃ prati
a tataḥ karṇarathaṃ yāntam arīn ghnantaṃ dhanaṃjayam
c bāṇavarṣair abhighnantaḥ saṃśaptakarathā yayuḥ
a tvaramāṇāṃs tu tān sarvān sasūteṣvasanadhvajān
c jaghāna navatiṃ vīrān arjuno niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a te 'patanta hatā bāṇair nānārūpaiḥ kirīṭinā
c savimānā yathā siddhāḥ svargāt puṇyakṣaye tathā
a tataḥ sarathanāgāśvāḥ kuravaḥ kurusattama
b kṣipram evābhisaṃkruddhāḥ samare 'rijighāṃsayā
c nirbhayā bharataśreṣṭham abhyavartanta phalgunam
a tad āyastam amuktāstram udīrṇavaravāraṇam
c putrāṇāṃ te mahat sainyaṃ samarautsīd dhanaṃjayaḥ
a śaktyṛṣṭitomaraprāsair gadānistriṃśasāyakaiḥ
c prācchādayan maheṣvāsāḥ kuravaḥ kurunandanam
a tāṃ kurūṇāṃ pravitatāṃ śastravṛṣṭiṃ samudyatām
c vyadhamat pāṇḍavo bāṇais tamaḥ sūrya ivāṃśubhiḥ
a tato mlecchāḥ sthitair mattais trayodaśaśatair gajaiḥ
c pārśvato 'bhyahanan pārthaṃ tava putrasya śāsanāt
a karṇinālīkanārācais tomaraiḥ prāsaśaktibhiḥ
c kampanair bhiṇḍipālaiś ca rathasthaṃ pārtham ārdayan
a tām astravṛṣṭiṃ prahitāṃ dvipasthair yavanaiḥ smayan
c ciccheda niśitair bhallair ardhacandraiś ca phalgunaḥ
a atha tān dviradān sarvān nānāliṅgair mahāśaraiḥ
c sapatākān sahārohān girīn vajrair ivābhinat
a te hemapuṅkhair iṣubhir ācitā hemamālinaḥ
c hatāḥ petur mahānāgāḥ sāgnijvālā ivādrayaḥ
a tato gāṇḍīvanirghoṣo mahān āsīd viśāṃ pate
c stanatāṃ kūjatāṃ caiva manuṣyagajavājinām
a kuñjarāś ca hatā rājan prādravaṃs te samantataḥ
c aśvāś ca paryadhāvanta hatārohā diśo daśa
a rathā hīnā mahārāja rathibhir vājibhis tathā
c gandharvanagarākārā dṛśyante sma sahasraśaḥ
a aśvārohā mahārāja dhāvamānās tatas tataḥ
b nardantaḥ kūjamānāś ca manuṣyagajavājinaḥ
c tatra tatraiva dṛśyante patitāḥ pārthasāyakaiḥ
a tasmin kṣaṇe pāṇḍavasya bāhvor balam adṛśyata
c yat sādino vāraṇāṃś ca rathāṃś caiko 'jayad yudhi
d asaṃyuktāś ca te rājan parivṛttā raṇaṃ prati
d narā nāgā rathāś caiva nadanto 'rjunam abhyayuḥ
a tatas tryaṅgeṇa mahatā balena bharatarṣabha
c dṛṣṭvā parivṛtaṃ rājan bhīmasenaḥ kirīṭinam
a hatāvaśeṣān utsṛjya tvadīyān kati cid rathān
c javenābhyadravad rājan dhanaṃjayarathaṃ prati
a tatas tat prādravat sainyaṃ hatabhūyiṣṭham āturam
c dṛṣṭvā yad arjunaṃ bhīmo jagāma bhrātaraṃ prati
a hatāvaśiṣṭāṃs turagān arjunena mahājavān
c bhīmo vyadhamad abhrānto gadāpāṇir mahāhave
d gadāpāṇiṃ tadā bhīmaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhārata bhāratāḥ
d menire tam anuprāptaṃ daṇḍahastam ivāntakam
a kālarātrim ivātyugrāṃ naranāgāśvabhojanām
c prākārāṭṭapuradvāradāraṇīm atidāruṇām
a tato gadāṃ nṛnāgāśveṣv āśu bhīmo vyavāsṛjat
b gajān aśvān hayārohān uddiśyoddiśya bhārata
c sā jaghāna bahūn aśvān aśvārohāṃś ca māriṣa
a kāṃsyāyasatanutrāṃs tān narān aśvāṃś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
c pothayām āsa gadayā saśabdaṃ te 'patan hatāḥ
d kṣaṇena bhīmaḥ saṃkruddhas tān ninye vai yamakṣayam
f tataḥ sa samaraślāghī gajānīkam apātayat
f gadayā vyadhamat saṃkhye daṇḍapāṇir ivāntakaḥ
f gajān sakaṅkaṭān mattān sārohān sapatākinaḥ
f nyahanal līlayā rājañ śikṣayā ca balena ca
f te gajā bahvaśobhanta hanyamānā mahāraṇe
f vinadanto yathā tūrṇaṃ pakṣavanta ivādrayaḥ
f nipetur urvyāṃ samare bhīmasenena pīḍitāḥ
f chinnapakṣā yathā kāle vajrarugṇā ivādrayaḥ
f dantair daśanto vasudhāṃ śerate kṣatajokṣitāḥ
f bhagnamūrdhāsthicaraṇāḥ kravyādagaṇabhojanāḥ
f asṛṅmāṃsavasābhiś ca tṛptā māṃsavasāśanāḥ
f asthīny apy aśnatī tasthau kālarātrīva durdṛśā
f sahasrāṇi daśāśvānāṃ hatvā pattīṃś ca bhūyasā
f bhīmo 'bhyadhāvat saṃkruddho gadāpāṇir itas tataḥ
f gadāpāṇiṃ tato bhīmaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhārata tāvakāḥ
f menire samanuprāptaṃ kālaṃ daṇḍodyataṃ yathā
f sa matta iva mātaṅgaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ pāṇḍunandanaḥ
f praviveśa gajānīkaṃ makaraḥ sāgaraṃ yathā
f vigāhya ca gajānīkaṃ pragṛhya mahatīṃ gadām
f kṣaṇena bhīmaḥ saṃkruddhas tān ninye yamasādanam
f gajān sakaṅkaṭān mattān sarohān sapatākinaḥ
f patataḥ samapaśyāma sapakṣān parvatān iva
a hatvā tu tad gajānīkaṃ bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
c punaḥ svaratham āsthāya pṛṣṭhato 'rjunam anvagāt
a hataṃ parāṅmukhaprāyaṃ nirutsāhaṃ paraṃ balam
c vyālambata mahārāja prāyaśaḥ śastraveṣṭitam
a vilambamānaṃ tat sainyam apragalbham avasthitam
c dṛṣṭvā prācchādayad bāṇair arjunaḥ prāṇatāpanaiḥ
d narāśvarathamātaṅgā yudhi gāṇḍīvadhanvanā
d śaravrātaiś citā rejuḥ kadambā iva kesaraiḥ
a tataḥ kurūṇām abhavad ārtanādo mahāmṛdhe
b śataśo vadhyamānānāṃ niśitair arjuneṣubhiḥ
c rathāśvanāgāsuharair vadhyatām arjuneṣubhiḥ
d kurūṇāṃ tu mahārāja āsīd ārtasvaro mahān
d narāśvanāgāsuharān dṛṣṭvā bāṇān kirīṭinaḥ
a hāhākṛtaṃ bhṛśaṃ tasthau līyamānaṃ parasparam
c alātacakravat sainyaṃ tadābhramata tāvakam
d tatas tad yuddham abhavat kurūṇāṃ sumahad balam
d na hy atrāsīd anirbhinno rathaḥ sādī hayo gajaḥ
d tataḥ śaradhvastam abhūt kurūṇāṃ sumahad balam
d na tatrāsīd anirbhinno ratho vājī naro gajaḥ
a ādīptaṃ tava tat sainyaṃ śaraiś chinnatanucchadam
c āsīt svaśoṇitaklinnaṃ phullāśokavanaṃ yathā
d tat sainyaṃ bharataśreṣṭha vadhyamānaṃ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
d na jahau samaraṃ prāpya phalgunaṃ śatrutāpanam
d tatrādbhutam apaśyāma kauravāṇāṃ parākramam
d vadhyamānāpi yat pārthaṃ na jahuḥ samare prabho
a tad dṛṣṭvā kuravas tatra vikrāntaṃ savyasācinaḥ
c nirāśāḥ samapadyanta sarve karṇasya jīvite
a aviṣahyaṃ tu pārthasya śarasaṃpātam āhave
c matvā nyavartan kuravo jitā gāṇḍīvadhanvanā
a te hitvā samare pārthaṃ vadhyamānāś ca sāyakaiḥ
c pradudruvur diśo bhītāś cukruśuś cāpi sūtajam
a abhyadravata tān pārthaḥ kirañ śaraśatān bahūn
c harṣayan pāṇḍavān yodhān bhīmasenapurogamān
a putrās tu te mahārāja jagmuḥ karṇarathaṃ prati
c agādhe majjatāṃ teṣāṃ dvīpaḥ karṇo 'bhavat tadā
a kuravo hi mahārāja nirviṣāḥ pannagā iva
c karṇam evopalīyanta bhayād gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ
a yathā sarvāṇi bhūtāni mṛtyor bhītāni bhārata
c dharmam evopalīyante karmavanti hi yāni ca
a tathā karṇaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ putrās tava narādhipa
c upālīyanta saṃtrāsāt pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ
a tāñ śoṇitapariklinnān viṣamasthāñ śarāturān
c mā bhaiṣṭety abravīt karṇo hy abhito mām iteti ca
a saṃbhagnaṃ hi balaṃ dṛṣṭvā balāt pārthena tāvakam
c dhanur visphārayan karṇas tasthau śatrujighāṃsayā
d viṣphārayitvā durdharṣaś cāpam ādhirathir mahat
d tān vidrutān kurūn dṛṣṭvā karṇaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
d saṃcintayitvā pārthasya vadhe dadhre manaḥ śvasan
d visphārya sumahac cāpaṃ tataś cādhirathir vṛṣaḥ
e pāñcālān punar ādhāvat paśyataḥ savyasācinaḥ
a tataḥ kṣaṇena kṣitipāḥ kṣatajapratimekṣaṇāḥ
c karṇaṃ vavarṣur bāṇaughair yathā meghā mahīdharam
d śaraughaiś chādayām āsa mahāmegha ivācalam
a tataḥ śarasahasrāṇi karṇamuktāni māriṣa
c vyayojayanta pāñcālān prāṇaiḥ prāṇabhṛtāṃ vara
d pāñcālānāṃ harat prāṇāṃs tamāṃsīva tamonudaḥ
a tato raṇo mahān āsīt pāñcālānāṃ viśāṃ pate
c vadhyatāṃ sūtaputreṇa mitrārthe 'mitraghātinām
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tataḥ karṇaḥ kuruṣu pradruteṣu
varūthinā śvetahayena rājan
c pāñcālaputrān vyadhamat sūtaputro
maheṣubhir vāta ivābhrasaṃghān
a sūtaṃ rathād añjalikena pātya
jaghāna cāśvāñ janamejayasya
c śatānīkaṃ sutasomaṃ ca bhallair
avākirad dhanuṣī cāpy akṛntat
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ nirbibhedātha ṣaḍbhir
jaghāna cāśvaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ tasya saṃkhye
c hatvā cāśvān sātyakeḥ sūtaputraḥ
kaikeyaputraṃ nyavadhīd viśokam
a tam abhyadhāvan nihate kumāre
kaikeyasenāpatir ugradhanvā
c śarair vibhinnaṃ bhṛśam ugravegaiḥ
karṇātmajaṃ so 'bhyahanat suṣeṇam
a tasyārdhacandrais tribhir uccakarta
prasahya bāhū ca śiraś ca karṇaḥ
c sa syandanād gām apatad gatāsuḥ
paraśvadhaiḥ śāla ivāvarugṇaḥ
a hatāśvam añjogatibhiḥ suṣeṇaḥ
śinipravīraṃ niśitaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ
c pracchādya nṛtyann iva sautiputraḥ
śaineyabāṇābhihataḥ papāta
a putre hate krodhaparītacetāḥ
karṇaḥ śinīnām ṛṣabhaṃ jighāṃsuḥ
c hato 'si śaineya iti bruvan sa
vyavāsṛjad bāṇam amitrasāham
a sa tasya ciccheda śaraṃ śikhaṇḍī
tribhis tribhiś ca pratutoda karṇam
c śikhaṇḍinaḥ kārmukaṃ sa dhvajaṃ ca
cchittvā śarābhyām ahanat sujātam
a śikhaṇḍinaṃ ṣaḍbhir avidhyad ugro
dānto dhārṣṭadyumnaśiraś cakarta
c athābhinat sutasomaṃ śareṇa
sa saṃśitenādhirathir mahātmā
d tato 'pare bhārata duṣprakampyāḥ
d pāñcālānāṃ rathasaṃghāḥ sametāḥ
d pratiśrutā hy antarikṣe gatābhā
d dhanuḥpravīrās tu rathapravīrāḥ
a athākrande tumule vartamāne
dhārṣṭadyumne nihate tatra kṛṣṇaḥ
c apāñcālyaṃ kriyate yāhi pārtha
karṇaṃ jahīty abravīd rājasiṃha
a tataḥ prahasyāśu narapravīro
rathaṃ rathenādhirather jagāma
c bhaye teṣāṃ trāṇam icchan subāhur
abhyāhatānāṃ rathayūthapena
a visphārya gāṇḍīvam athograghoṣaṃ
jyayā samāhatya tale bhṛśaṃ ca
c bāṇāndhakāraṃ sahasaiva kṛtvā
jaghāna nāgāśvarathān narāṃś ca
d prītāḥ śukāḥ prādravann antarikṣe
d guhā girīṇām apatan vayāṃsi
d yan maṇḍalajyena vijṛmbhamāṇo
d raudre muhūrte 'bhyapatat kirīṭī
a taṃ bhīmaseno 'nu yayau rathena
pṛṣṭhe rakṣan pāṇḍavam ekavīram
c tau rājaputrau tvaritau rathābhyāṃ
karṇāya yātāv aribhir vimuktau
a atrāntare sumahat sūtaputraś
cakre yuddhaṃ somakān saṃpramṛdnan
c rathāśvamātaṅgagaṇāñ jaghāna
pracchādayām āsa diśaḥ śaraiś ca
a tam uttamaujā janamejayaś ca
kruddhau yudhāmanyuśikhaṇḍinau ca
c karṇaṃ vineduḥ sahitāḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ
saṃmardamānāḥ saha pārṣatena
a te pañca pāñcālarathāḥ surūpair
vaikartanaṃ karṇam abhidravantaḥ
c tasmād rathāc cyāvayituṃ na śekur
dhairyāt kṛtātmānam ivendriyāṇi
a teṣāṃ dhanūṃṣi dhvajavājisūtāṃs
tūṇaṃ patākāś ca nikṛtya bāṇaiḥ
b teṣāṃ dhvajān vājisūtān patākās
b tūṇīr dhanūṃṣi pracakarta bāṇaiḥ
c tān pañcabhiḥ sa tv ahanat pṛṣatkaiḥ
karṇas tataḥ siṃha ivonnanāda
a tasyāsyatas tān abhinighnataś ca
jyābāṇahastasya dhanuḥsvanena
c sādridrumā syāt pṛthivī viśīrṇā
ity eva matvā janatā vyaṣīdat
a sa śakracāpapratimena dhanvanā
bhṛśātatenādhirathiḥ śarān sṛjan
c babhau raṇe dīptamarīcimaṇḍalo
yathāṃśumālī pariveṣavāṃs tathā
a śikhaṇḍinaṃ dvādaśabhiḥ parābhinac
chitaiḥ śaraiḥ ṣaḍbhir athottamaujasam
c tribhir yudhāmanyum avidhyad āśugais
tribhis tribhiḥ somakapārṣatātmajau
a parājitāḥ pañca mahārathās tu te
mahāhave sūtasutena māriṣa
c nirudyamās tasthur amitramardanā
yathendriyārthātmavatā parājitāḥ
a nimajjatas tān atha karṇasāgare
vipannanāvo vaṇijo yathārṇave
c uddadhrire naubhir ivārṇavād rathaiḥ
sukalpitair draupadijāḥ svamātulān
a tataḥ śinīnām ṛṣabhaḥ śitaiḥ śarair
nikṛtya karṇaprahitān iṣūn bahūn
c vidārya karṇaṃ niśitair ayasmayais
tavātmajaṃ jyeṣṭham avidhyad aṣṭabhiḥ
a kṛpo 'tha bhojaś ca tavātmajas tathā
svayaṃ ca karṇo niśitair atāḍayat
c sa taiś caturbhir yuyudhe yadūttamo
digīśvarair daityapatir yathā tathā
a samānateneṣvasanena kūjatā
bhṛśātatenāmitabāṇavarṣiṇā
c babhūva durdharṣataraḥ sa sātyakiḥ
śaran nabhomadhyagato yathā raviḥ
a punaḥ samāsādya rathān sudaṃśitāḥ
śinipravīraṃ jugupuḥ paraṃtapāḥ
c sametya pāñcālarathā mahāraṇe
marudgaṇāḥ śakram ivārinigrahe
a tato 'bhavad yuddham atīva dāruṇaṃ
tavāhitānāṃ tava sainikaiḥ saha
c rathāśvamātaṅgavināśanaṃ tathā
yathā surāṇām asuraiḥ purābhavat
a rathadvipā vājipadātayo 'pi vā
bhramanti nānāvidhaśastraveṣṭitāḥ
c paraspareṇābhihatāś ca caskhalur
vinedur ārtā vyasavo 'patanta ca
a tathā gate bhīmam abhīs tavātmajaḥ
sasāra rājāvarajaḥ kirañ śaraiḥ
c tam abhyadhāvat tvarito vṛkodaro
mahāruruṃ siṃha ivābhipetivān
a tatas tayor yuddham atītamānuṣaṃ
pradīvyatoḥ prāṇadurodare 'bhavat
c paraspareṇābhiniviṣṭaroṣayor
udagrayoḥ śambaraśakrayor yathā
a śaraiḥ śarīrāntakaraiḥ sutejanair
nijaghnatus tāv itaretaraṃ bhṛśam
c sakṛtprabhinnāv iva vāśitāntare
mahāgajau manmathasaktacetasau
d ālokya tau caiva parasparaṃ tataḥ
d samaṃ ca śūrau ca sasārathī tadā
d bhīmo 'bravīd yāhi duḥśāsanāya
d duḥśāsano yāhi vṛkodarāya
d tayo rathau sārathibhyāṃ pracoditau
d samaṃ rathau tau sahasā samīyatuḥ
d nānāyudhau citrapatākinadhvajau
d bhīmaḥ
d divīva pūrvaṃ balaśakrayo raṇe
d diṣṭyāsi duḥśāsana adya dṛṣṭa
d ṛṇaṃ pratīccheḥ sahavṛddhimūlam
d ciroditaṃ taṃ yan mayā te sabhāyāṃ
d kṛṣṇābhimarśena gṛhāṇa mattaḥ
d sa evam uktas tu tato mahātmā
d duḥśāsano vākyam uvāca vīraḥ
d sarvaṃ smare naiva ca vismarāmi
d udīryamāṇaṃ śṛṇu bhīmasena
d smarāmi cātmaprabhavaṃ cirāya
d yaj jātuṣe veśmani rātry ahāni
d viśvāsahīnā mṛgayāṃ caranto
d vasanti sarvatra nirākṛtās tu
d mahad bhayād rātry ahani smarantas
d tathopabhogāc ca sukhāc ca hīnāḥ
d vaneṣv aṭanto girigahvarāṇi
d pāñcālarājasya puraṃ praviṣṭāḥ
d māyāṃ yūyaṃ kām api saṃpraviṣṭā
d yato vṛtaḥ kṛṣṇayā phalguno vaḥ
d saṃbhūya pāpais tad anāryavṛttaṃ
d kṛtaṃ tadā mātṛkṛtānurūpam
d eko vṛtaḥ pañcabhiḥ sābhipannā
d hy alajjamānaiś ca parasparasya
d smare sabhāyāṃ subalātmajena
d saṃjayaḥ
d dāsīkṛtāḥ stha saha kṛṣṇayā tu
d tenaivam uktas tu tavātmajena
d subālacittena vṛkodaro 'pi
d pragṛhya cāpaṃ bhṛkuṭīṃ lalāṭe
d kṛtvā tu roṣojjvalatāmranetraḥ
a tavātmajasyātha vṛkodaras tvaran
dhanuḥ kṣurābhyāṃ dhvajam eva cācchinat
c lalāṭam apy asya bibheda patriṇā
śiraś ca kāyāt prajahāra sāratheḥ
a sa rājaputro 'nyad avāpya kārmukaṃ
vṛkodaraṃ dvādaśabhiḥ parābhinat
c svayaṃ niyacchaṃs turagān ajihmagaiḥ
śaraiś ca bhīmaṃ punar abhyavīvṛṣat
d tataḥ śaraṃ sūryamarīcisaprabhaṃ
d suvarṇavajrottamaratnabhūṣitam
d mahendravajrāśanipātaduḥsahaṃ
d mumoca bhīmāṅgavidāraṇakṣamam
d sa tena nirbhinnatanur vṛkodaro
d nipātitaḥ srastatanur gatāsuvat
d prasārya bāhū rathavaryam āśritaḥ
d punaś ca saṃjñām upalabhya cānadat
 saṃjaya uvāca
 sa rājaputreṇa samārcchad ugraṃ
 duḥśāsanena nikṛto nikṛtyā
a tatrākarod duṣkaraṃ rājaputro
duḥśāsanas tumule yudhyamānaḥ
b yad bhīmasenaṃ pratiyodhayad raṇe
b jambho yathā śakram udāravīryam
c ciccheda bhīmasya dhanuḥ kṣureṇa
ṣaḍbhiḥ śaraiḥ sārathim apy avidhyat
d sa tat kṛtvā rājaputras tarasvī
d vivyādha bhīmaṃ navabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ
a tato 'bhinad bahubhiḥ kṣipram eva
vareṣubhir bhīmasenaṃ mahātmā
b tataḥ kruddho bhīmasenas tarasvī
b śaktiṃ cogrāṃ prāhiṇot te sutāya
b tām āpatantīṃ sahasātighorāṃ
b dṛṣṭvā sutas te jvalitām ivolkām
b ākarṇapūrṇair iṣubhir mahātmā
b ciccheda putro daśabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ
b dṛṣṭvā tu tat karma kṛtaṃ suduṣkaraṃ
b prāpūjayan sarvayodhāḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ
b athāśu bhīmaṃ ca śareṇa bhūyo
b gāḍhaṃ sa vivyādha sutas tvadīyaḥ
b cukrodha bhīmaḥ punar āśu tasmai
b bhṛśaṃ prajajvāla ruṣābhivīkṣya
b viddho 'smi vīrāśu bhṛśaṃ tvayādya
b sahasva bhūyo 'pi gadāprahāram
b uktvaivam uccaiḥ kupito 'tha bhīmo
b jagrāha tāṃ bhīmagadāṃ vadhāya
b uvāca cādyāham ahaṃ durātman
b pāsyāmi te śoṇitam ājimadhye
b athaivam uktas tanayas tavogrāṃ
b śaktiṃ vegāt prāhiṇon mṛtyurūpām
b āvidhya bhīmo 'pi gadāṃ sughorāṃ
b vicikṣipe roṣaparītamūrtiḥ
b sā tasya śaktiṃ sahasā virujya
b putraṃ tavājau tāḍayām āsa mūrdhni
b sa kārmukaṃ gṛhya tu bhārasādhanaṃ
b bhīmas tadā rājaputraṃ hy avidhyat
b pañcāśatā bāṇagaṇaiḥ stanāntare
b tottrair yathātīva bhinad dvipendram
b tato 'tividdho virathaṃ mahātmā
b duḥśāsano bhīmasenaṃ cakāra
b nihatya saṃkhye caturo 'sya vāhāñ
b chittvā ratheṣāṃ punar eva cākṣipat
b tataḥ kṣitistho hy avaruhya yānād
b vṛkodaro gadayā tasya vāhān
b yamakṣayaṃ preṣayitvā mahātmā
b rathaṃ samākarṣata rājasūnoḥ
b tasmād avaplutya rathāt sasarja
b duḥśāsanas tomaram ugravegam
b sa tena viddho hy urasi hy aprameyo
b gadāṃ tasmai visasarjāprameyām
b tataḥ krodhād bhīmasenaḥ kṛtāni
b sarvāṇi duḥkhāny anusaṃsmaran vai
b saṃsmṛtya saṃsmṛtya tathā pratijñām
b ugrām atho rājaputro nyaṣīdat
b saṃcintayan roṣam atīva kopāt
b trayodaśābdaṃ puruṣapravīraḥ
b pragṛhya vajrāśanitulyavegāṃ
b gadāṃ kareṇātha vṛkodaro ruṣā
b nipātayitvā pṛthivītale bhṛśaṃ
b saṃtāḍayām āsa balī vṛkodaraḥ
b atīva saṃtāḍitabhinnagātro
b duḥśāsano vai nipapāta bhūmau
b ākramya kaṇṭhe yudhi rājaputraṃ
b saṃraktanetro hy abravīd dhārtarāṣṭram
b tad brūhi kiṃ tvaṃ parimārgamāṇo
b hy asmān parābhūya ihāgatān punaḥ
b tad idam adya bhṛśasaṃbhṛtaṃ me
b cirārjitaṃ roṣam atipradīptam
b madhu prapāsye tava koṣṭhabhājanād
b ity abravīd bhīmasenas tarasvī
b duḥśāsanaṃ kaṇṭhadeśe pramṛdnaṃs
b tataḥ krūraṃ bhīmasenaś cakāra
b taṃ vyaṃsayitvā sahasā sasāra
b balād asau dhārtarāṣṭras tarasvī
b sapatnatāṃ darśayan dhārtarāṣṭre
b bhīmo 'bhidudrāva sutaṃ tvadīyam
b mṛgaṃ muhuḥ siṃhaśiśur yathā vane
b tathāśv abhidrutya mahābalaṃ balī
b nigṛhya cainaṃ parameṇa karmaṇā
b utkṣipya cotkṣipya ca tūrṇam enam
b bhūmau tadā niṣpipeṣātha vīraḥ
b asiṃ vikośaṃ vimalaṃ cakāra
b kaṇṭhe samākrāmya ca vepamānaṃ
b kṛtvā tu rūpaṃ paramaṃ sughoram
b kālāntakābhyāṃ pratimaṃ tadānīṃ
b vidārya vakṣaḥ sa mahārathasya
b duḥśāsanasya ripuśāsanasya
c sa vikṣaran nāga iva prabhinno
gadām asmai tumule prāhiṇod vai
a tayāharad daśa dhanvantarāṇi
duḥśāsanaṃ bhīmasenaḥ prasahya
c tayā hataḥ patito vepamāno
duḥśāsano gadayā vegavatyā
a hayāḥ sasūtāś ca hatā narendra
cūrṇīkṛtaś cāsya rathaḥ patantyā
c vidhvastavarmābharaṇāmbarasrag
viceṣṭamāno bhṛśavedanārtaḥ
d duḥśāsanaṃ pāṇḍavāḥ prekṣya sarve
d hṛṣṭāḥ pāñcālāḥ siṃhanādān amuñcan
d taṃ pātayitvātha vṛkodaro 'yaṃ
d jagarja harṣeṇa vinādayan diśaḥ
d nādena tenākhilapārśvavartino
d mūrchākulāḥ patitās tv ājamīḍha
d sa samīpasthito bhīmo visajñaṃ vīkṣya te sutam
d cakāra khedaṃ manasā cintāṃ ca paramāṃ yayau
d acetanasya rudhiraṃ kathaṃ pāsyāmy ahaṃ ripoḥ
d ajānato 'sya pāpasya durmater mitraghātinaḥ
d evaṃ vicintayad bhīmo dadarśātha vicetanam
d vastreṇāvījayac cainaṃ tena saṃjñām avāpa ha
d dṛṣṭvā sasaṃjñaṃ sāvajñaṃ pādenākramya vakṣasi
d prahṛṣṭarūpo bhīmas tu sāsīḥ provāca taṃ tadā
d bhīmo 'pi vegād avatīrya yānād
d duḥśāsanaṃ vegavān abhyadhāvat
a tataḥ smṛtvā bhīmasenas tarasvī
sāpatnakaṃ yat prayuktaṃ sutais te
b tasmin sughore tumule vartamāne
b pradhānabhūyiṣṭhataraiḥ samantāt
b duḥśāsanaṃ tatra samīkṣya rājan
b bhīmo mahābāhur acintyakarmā
b smṛtvātha keśagrahaṇaṃ ca devyā
b vastrāpahāraṃ ca rajasvalāyāḥ
b anāgaso bhartṛparāṅmukhāyā
b duḥkhāni dattāny api vipracintya
b jajvāla krodhāmarṣeṇa bhīma
b ājyaprasikto hi yathā hutāśaḥ
b tatrāha karṇaṃ ca suyodhanaṃ ca
b kṛpaṃ drauṇiṃ kṛtavarmāṇam eva
b nihanmi duḥśāsanam adya pāpaṃ
b saṃrakṣyatām adya samastayodhāḥ
b ity evam uktvā sahasābhyadhāvan
b nihantukāmo 'tibalas tarasvī
b tathā tu vikramya raṇe vṛkodaro
b mahāgajaṃ kesariṇo yathaiva
b nigṛhya duḥśāsanam ekavīraḥ
b suyodhanasyādhiratheḥ samakṣam
c rathād avaplutya gataḥ sa bhūmau
yatnena tasmin praṇidhāya cakṣuḥ
d tato bhīmas tam abravīn mahātmā
d kathaṃ draupadīṃ keśapakṣe pradharṣīḥ
d vadāśu yad gaur iti tad bruvāṇo
d hṛṣṭaḥ samaṃ karṇasuyodhanābhyām
d teṣāṃ samīkṣyāpavite sic durātman
d gacchāmi yenādya kulapradhānaḥ
d śrutvā tu tad bhīmavacaḥ sughoraṃ
d duḥśāsano bhīmam idaṃ nirīkṣya
d uvāca bhīmaṃ sa tadā smitena
d saṃpaśyatāṃ kauravasomakānām
d sa eṣa me bāhuvaro 'stu bhūya
d eṣa tvayā rājyaharaḥ samīkṣya
d dyūtacchalād vañcayitā sametāṃ
d kliṣṭām āryāṃ paśyatas te tv anena
d asau karo godhanavān samartho
d viṣasya dātā bhujagendrakalpaḥ
d bhikṣābhujo yena kṛtāḥ samastā
d aṣṭādaśa dvā ca kuruṣva yatnam
d bhīmaḥ
d draupadyās tu kacagrāhe yaḥ prayuktas tvayā karaḥ
d duḥśāsanaḥ
d diśyatāṃ ca sa me pāpin kaṃ tam utpāṭayāmy aham
d ayaṃ karikarākāraḥ kāminīkucamardanaḥ
d saṃjayaḥ
d gosahasrapradātā ca kṣatriyāntakaraḥ karaḥ
d etac chrutvā tu vacanaṃ bhīmaseno 'tyamarṣaṇaḥ
d utpāṭayām āsa bhujaṃ vāmetaram ariṃdama
a asiṃ samuddhṛtya śitaṃ sudhāraṃ
kaṇṭhe samākramya ca vepamānam
b ye rājasūyāvabhṛthe pavitrā
b jātāḥ kacā yājñasenyā durātman
b te pāṇinā katareṇāvakṛṣṭāḥ
b prabrūhi tvāṃ pṛcchate bhīmasenaḥ
b uktas tathājau sa tadā saroṣaṃ
b jagāda bhīmaṃ parivṛtya netre
b ayaṃ karikarākāraḥ pīnastanavimardanaḥ
b gosahasrapradātā ca kṣatriyāntakaraḥ karaḥ
b anena yājñasenyā me bhīma keśā vikarṣitāḥ
b paśyatāṃ kurumukhyānāṃ yuṣmākaṃ ca sabhāsadām
b evaṃ tv asau rājasutaṃ niśamya
b bruvantam ājau vinipīḍya vakṣaḥ
b bhīmo balād bāhum udhṛtya dorbhyām
b uccair nanādātha samastayodhān
b uvāca yasyāsti balaṃ kulaṃ ca
b rakṣatv asau me 'dya nirastabāhuḥ
b duḥśāsanaṃ jīvitam utsṛjantam
b ākṣipya yodhās tarasā mahābalam
b kruddho raṇe 'tīva karaṃ kareṇa
b utpāṭya vīraḥ sahasaiva rājan
b duḥśāsanaṃ tena tu vīramadhye
b jaghāna vajrāśanisaṃnibhena
c utkṛtya vakṣaḥ patitasya bhūmāv
athāpibac choṇitam asya koṣṇam
d tato nipātyāsya śiro 'pahṛtya
d tenāsinā tava putrasya rājan
d satyāṃ cikīrṣur matiman pratijñāṃ
d bhīmo 'pibac choṇitam asya koṣṇam
e āsvādya cāsvādya ca vīkṣamāṇaḥ
kruddho 'tivelaṃ prajagāda vākyam
a stanyasya mātur madhusarpiṣo vā
mādhvīkapānasya ca satkṛtasya
c divyasya vā toyarasasya pānāt
payodadhibhyāṃ mathitāc ca mukhyāt
d anyāni pānāni ca yāni loke
d sudhāmṛtasvādurasāni tebhyaḥ
d tathekṣusārasya manoharasya
e sarvebhya evābhyadhiko raso 'yaṃ
mato mamādyāhitalohitasya
f athāha bhīmaḥ punar ugrakarmā
f duḥśāsanaṃ krodhaparītacetāḥ
f gatāsum ālokya vihasya susvaraṃ
f kiṃ vā kuryāṃ mṛtyunā rakṣito 'si
a evaṃ bruvāṇaṃ punar ādravantam
āsvādya valgantam atiprahṛṣṭam
c ye bhīmasenaṃ dadṛśus tadānīṃ
bhayena te 'pi vyathitā nipetuḥ
a ye cāpi tatrāpatitā manuṣyās
teṣāṃ karebhyaḥ patitaṃ ca śastram
c bhayāc ca saṃcukruśur uccakais te
nimīlitākṣā dadṛśuś ca tan na
a ye tatra bhīmaṃ dadṛśuḥ samantād
dauḥśāsanaṃ tadrudhiraṃ pibantam
c sarve palāyanta bhayābhipannā
nāyaṃ manuṣya iti bhāṣamāṇāḥ
d saṃjayaḥ
d sa pītvā rudhiraṃ tasya caraṇau gṛhya bhārata
d tasmin kṛte bhīmasenena rūpe
d dṛṣṭvā ca tac cchoṇitaṃ pīyamānam
d saṃprādravaṃś citrasenena sārdhaṃ
d bhīmaṃ rakṣo bhāṣamāṇā bhayārtāḥ
d yudhāmanyuḥ pradrutaṃ citrasenaṃ
d mahānīkaṃ smābhyayād rājaputraḥ
d vivyādha cainaṃ niśitaiḥ pṛṣatkair
d vyapetabhīḥ saptabhir āśumuktaiḥ
d padākrāntaḥ sarpaval lelihāno
d mahoragaḥ krodhaviṣaṃ sisṛkṣuḥ
d nivṛtya pāñcālajam abhyavidhyat
d tribhiḥ śaraiḥ sārathiṃ cāpy avidhyat
d tataḥ supuṅkhena supatritena
d susaṃśitāgreṇa śareṇa śūraḥ
d ākarṇamuktena samāhitena
d yudhāmanyus tasya śiro jahāra
d tasmin hate bhrātari citrasene
d kruddhaḥ karṇaḥ pauruṣaṃ darśayānaḥ
d dudrāva tat pāṇḍavānām anīkaṃ
d pratyudyāto nakulenāmitaujāḥ
d bhīmo 'pi hatvā tatraiva duḥśāsanam amarṣaṇam
d pūrayitvāñjaliṃ bhūyo rudhirasyogranisvanaḥ
a śṛṇvatāṃ lokavīrāṇām idaṃ vacanam abravīt
b ity uccair vacanaṃ prāha pratinṛtya vṛkodaraḥ
c eṣa te rudhiraṃ kaṇṭhāt pibāmi puruṣādhama
e brūhīdānīṃ susaṃrabdhaḥ punar gaur iti gaur iti
f ye tadāsmān pranṛtyanti punar gaur iti gaur iti
f tān vayaṃ pratinṛtyāmaḥ punar gaur iti gaur iti
a pramāṇakoṭyāṃ śayanaṃ kālakūṭasya bhojanam
c daśanaṃ cāhibhiḥ kaṣṭaṃ dāhaṃ ca jatuveśmani
a dyūtena rājyaharaṇam araṇye vasatiś ca yā
b draupadyāḥ keśapakṣasya grahaṇaṃ ca sudāruṇam
c iṣvastrāṇi ca saṃgrāmeṣv asukhāni ca veśmani
d virāṭabhavane yaś ca kleśo 'smākaṃ pṛthagvidhaḥ
d śakuner dhārtarāṣṭrasya rādheyasya ca mantrite
d anubhūtāni duḥkhāni teṣāṃ hetus tvam eva hi
a duḥkhāny etāni jānīmo na sukhāni kadā cana
c dhṛtarāṣṭrasya daurātmyāt saputrasya sadā vayam
d sukhāny etāni jānīmo labdhavanto na saṃśayaḥ
a ity uktvā vacanaṃ rājañ jayaṃ prāpya vṛkodaraḥ
c punar āha mahārāja smayaṃs tau keśavārjunau
d asṛgdigdho visravallohitāsyaḥ
d kruddho 'tyarthaṃ bhīmasenas tarasvī
d raktārdragātras tu tato mahātmā
d gadāpāṇiḥ kāla ivāntakāle
d vibhīṣayānas tava putrasainyam
d itas tato dhāvati vāhinīṃ te
d tataḥ kṣaṇād bhārata śūnyam āsīd
d āyodhanaṃ ghorataraṃ kurūṇām
d yatrājimadhye prāpibad bhīmaseno
d duḥśāsanasya rudhiraṃ krodhadīptaḥ
d sa hatvā samare rājan rājaputraṃ mahābalam
d pūrṇakāmo madodagraḥ siṃho rurum ivotkaṭam
d rudhirārdro mahārāja hy aśobhata paraṃtapaḥ
d sapuṣpaḥ kiṃśuka iva raktād raktataro babhau
d rudhirārdravapur ghoraḥ kruddho rājan vaco 'bravīt
d brūhīdānīṃ pāpamate nṛśaṃsa patito hy asi
d brūhīdānīṃ pāpamate nṛśaṃsa
d apatir hy asi drupadasyātmajā tvam
a duḥśāsane yad raṇe saṃśrutaṃ me
tad vai sarvaṃ kṛtam adyeha vīrau
c adyaiva dāsyāmy aparaṃ dvitīyaṃ
duryodhanaṃ yajñapaśuṃ viśasya
e śiro mṛditvā ca padā durātmanaḥ
śāntiṃ lapsye kauravāṇāṃ samakṣam
f yā cāpatiḥ sā sapatir hi jātā
f yās tāḥ sapatayo 'patayas tu jātāḥ
f paśyantu citraṃ vividhaṃ hi loke
f ye vai tilāḥ ṣaṇḍatilā babhūvuḥ
f te cet siddhā nidhanaṃ gatāḥ pare
f kiṃ citrarūpaṃ bata jīvaloke
a etāvad uktvā vacanaṃ prahṛṣṭo
nanāda coccai rudhirārdragātraḥ
c nanarta caivātibalo mahātmā
vṛtraṃ nihatyeva sahasranetraḥ
d dṛṣṭvā tu nṛtyantam udagrarūpaṃ
d kālaṃ yathā tv antakāle prajānām
d mahad bhayaṃ cādhirathiṃ viveśa
d jaye nirāśāś ca sutās tvadīyāḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a duḥśāsane tu nihate putrās tava mahārathāḥ
c mahākrodhaviṣā vīrāḥ samareṣv apalāyinaḥ
e daśa rājan mahāvīryo bhīmaṃ prācchādayañ śaraiḥ
a kavacī niṣaṅgī pāśī daṇḍadhāro dhanurdharaḥ
c alolupaḥ śalaḥ saṃdho vātavegasuvarcasau
a ete sametya sahitā bhrātṛvyasanakarśitāḥ
c bhīmasenaṃ mahābāhuṃ mārgaṇaiḥ samavārayan
a sa vāryamāṇo viśikhaiḥ samantāt tair mahārathaiḥ
c bhīmaḥ krodhābhiraktākṣaḥ kruddhaḥ kāla ivābabhau
d tataḥ parivṛto rājan navabhiḥ śatrutāpanaiḥ
d duḥśāsanād avarajaiḥ putrais tava vṛkodaraḥ
a tāṃs tu bhallair mahāvegair daśabhir daśabhiḥ śitaiḥ
c rukmāṅgado rukmapuṅkhaiḥ pārtho ninye yamakṣayam
a hateṣu teṣu vīreṣu pradudrāva balaṃ tava
c paśyataḥ sūtaputrasya pāṇḍavasya bhayārditam
a tataḥ karṇo mahārāja praviveśa mahāraṇam
c dṛṣṭvā bhīmasya vikrāntam antakasya prajāsv iva
a tasya tv ākārabhāvajñaḥ śalyaḥ samitiśobhanaḥ
c uvāca vacanaṃ karṇaṃ prāptakālam ariṃdama
e mā vyathāṃ kuru rādheya naitat tvayy upapadyate
a ete dravanti rājāno bhīmasenabhayārditāḥ
c duryodhanaś ca saṃmūḍho bhrātṛvyasanaduḥkhitaḥ
a duḥśāsanasya rudhire pīyamāne mahātmanā
c vyāpannacetasaś caiva śokopahatamanyavaḥ
a duryodhanam upāsante parivārya samantataḥ
c kṛpaprabhṛtayaḥ karṇa hataśeṣāś ca sodarāḥ
a pāṇḍavā labdhalakṣāś ca dhanaṃjayapurogamāḥ
c tvām evābhimukhāḥ śūrā yuddhāya samupāsthitāḥ
a sa tvaṃ puruṣaśārdūla pauruṣe mahati sthitaḥ
c kṣatradharmaṃ puraskṛtya pratyudyāhi dhanaṃjayam
a bhāro hi dhārtarāṣṭreṇa tvayi sarvaḥ samarpitaḥ
c tam udvaha mahābāho yathāśakti yathābalam
e jaye syād vipulā kīrtir dhruvaḥ svargaḥ parājaye
a vṛṣasenaś ca rādheya saṃkruddhas tanayas tava
c tvayi mohasamāpanne pāṇḍavān abhidhāvati
a etac chrutvā tu vacanaṃ śalyasyāmitatejasaḥ
c hṛdi mānuṣyakaṃ bhāvaṃ cakre yuddhāya susthiram
a tataḥ kruddho vṛṣaseno 'bhyadhāvad
ātasthivāṃsaṃ svarathaṃ hatārim
c vṛkodaraṃ kālam ivāttadaṇḍaṃ
gadāhastaṃ pothamānaṃ tvadīyān
d bhīmaṃ samāyāntam amitrasāham
d bāṇaiḥ kirantaṃ pratiyātya cograṃ
d vyāttānanaṃ kālam ivāpatantam
a tam abhyadhāvan nakulaḥ pravīro
roṣād amitraṃ pratudan pṛṣatkaiḥ
c karṇasya putraṃ samare prahṛṣṭaṃ
jiṣṇur jighāṃsur maghaveva jambham
a tato dhvajaṃ sphāṭikacitrakambuṃ
ciccheda vīro nakulaḥ kṣureṇa
c karṇātmajasyeṣvasanaṃ ca citraṃ
bhallena jāmbūnadapaṭṭanaddham
a athānyad ādāya dhanuḥ suśīghraṃ
karṇātmajaḥ pāṇḍavam abhyavidhyat
c divyair mahāstrair nakulaṃ mahāstro
duḥśāsanasyāpacitiṃ yiyāsuḥ
a tataḥ kruddho nakulas taṃ mahātmā
śarair maholkāpratimair avidhyat
c divyair astrair abhyavidhyac ca so 'pi
karṇasya putro nakulaṃ kṛtāstraḥ
d śarābhighātāc ca ruṣā ca rājan
d svayaṃ ca bhāsāstrasamīraṇāc ca
d jajvāla karṇasya suto 'timātram
d iddho yathā jyāhutibhir hutāśaḥ
a karṇasya putro nakulasya rājan
sarvān aśvān akṣiṇod uttamāstraiḥ
b āsīt sughoraṃ bharatapravīra
b yuddhaṃ tadā karṇajapāṇḍavābhyām
c vanāyujān sukumārasya śubhrān
alaṃkṛtāñ jātarūpeṇa śīghrān
d jaghāna cāśvān nakulasya vīro
d raṇājire sūtaputrasya putraḥ
a tato hatāśvād avaruhya yānād
ādāya carma ruciraṃ cāṣṭacandram
c ākāśasaṃkāśam asiṃ gṛhītvā
poplūyamānaḥ khagavac cacāra
a tato 'ntarikṣe nṛvarāśvanāgāṃś
ciccheda mārgān vicaran vicitrān
b tato 'sya pakṣān anayad yamāya
b dvisāhasrān nakulaḥ kṣiprakārī
c te prāpatann asinā gāṃ viśastā
yathāśvamedhe paśavaḥ śamitrā
a dvisāhasrā viditā yuddhaśauṇḍā
nānādeśyāḥ subhṛtāḥ satyasaṃdhāḥ
c ekena śīghraṃ nakulena kṛttāḥ
sārepsunevottamacandanās te
a tam āpatantaṃ nakulaṃ so 'bhipatya
samantataḥ sāyakair abhyavidhyat
a karṇasya putraḥ sahasābhipatya ca
a raṇe jighāṃsuṃ niśitair anekaiḥ
b bhūmau carantaṃ nakulaṃ rathasthāḥ
b samantataḥ sāyakaiḥ pratyagṛhṇan
c sa tudyamāno nakulaḥ pṛṣatkair
vivyādha vīraṃ sa cukopa viddhaḥ
d mahābhaye rakṣyamāṇo mahātmā
d bhrātrā bhīmenākarot tatra bhīmam
a taṃ karṇaputro vidhamantam ekaṃ
narāśvamātaṅgarathapravekān
c krīḍantam aṣṭādaśabhiḥ pṛṣatkair
vivyādha vīraṃ sa cukopa viddhaḥ
d sa tena viddho 'tibhṛśaṃ tarasvī
d mahāhave vṛṣasenena rājan
a tato 'bhyadhāvat samare jighāṃsuḥ
karṇātmajaṃ pāṇḍusuto nṛvīraḥ
b vitatya pakṣau sahasā patantaṃ
b śyenaṃ yathaivāmiṣalubdham ājau
b avākirad vṛṣasenas tatas taṃ
b śitaiḥ śarair nakulam udāravīryam
b sa tān moghāṃs tasya kurvañ śaraughāṃś
b cacāra mārgān nakulaś citrarūpān
b athāsya tūrṇaṃ carato narendra
b khaḍgena citraṃ nakulasya tasya
c tasyeṣubhir vyadhamat karṇaputro
mahāraṇe carma sahasratāram
a tasyāyasaṃ niśitaṃ tīkṣṇadhāram
asiṃ vikośaṃ gurubhārasāham
c dviṣaccharīrāpaharaṃ sughoram
ādhunvataḥ sarpam ivograrūpam
a kṣipraṃ śaraiḥ ṣaḍbhir amitrasāhaś
cakarta khaḍgaṃ niśitaiḥ sudhāraiḥ
c punaś ca pītair niśitaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ
stanāntare gāḍham athābhyavidhyat
d kṛtvā tu tad duṣkaram āryajuṣṭaṃ
d narair anyaiḥ karma raṇe mahātmā
d yayau rathaṃ bhīmasenasya rājañ
d śarābhitapto nakulo mahātmā
a sa bhīmasenasya rathaṃ hatāśvo
mādrīsutaḥ karṇasutābhitaptaḥ
c āpupluve siṃha ivācalāgraṃ
saṃprekṣamāṇasya dhanaṃjayasya
d sa bhīmasenasya rathaṃ ca hatvā
d vavarṣa vai śaravarṣaṃ sughoram
d tataḥ kruddho vṛṣaseno mahātmā
d vavarṣa tāv iṣujālena vīraḥ
d mahārathāv ekarathe sametau
d śaraiḥ prabhindann iva pāṇḍaveyau
d tasmin rathe nihate pāṇḍavasya
d kṣipraṃ ca khaḍge viśikhair nikṛtte
d bhīmārjunau vṛṣasenāya kruddhau
d vavarṣatuḥ śaravarṣaṃ sughoram
d athābravīn mārutiḥ phalgunaṃ tu
d paśyasvainaṃ nakulaṃ pīḍayantam
d ayaṃ ca no bādhate karṇaputras
d tasmād bhavān pratyupayātu kārṇim
d sa tan niśamyaiva vacaḥ kirīṭī
d rathaṃ samāsādya vṛkodarasya
d kapidhvajaṃ keśavasaṃgṛhītaṃ
d praiṣīd ugro vṛṣasenāya vāham
a nakulam atha viditvā chinnabāṇāsanāsiṃ
viratham ariśarārtaṃ karṇaputrāstrabhagnam
c pavanadhutapatākā hrādino valgitāśvā
varapuruṣaniyattās te rathāḥ śīghram īyuḥ
a drupadasutavariṣṭhāḥ pañca śaineyaṣaṣṭhā
drupadaduhitṛputrāḥ pañca cāmitrasāhāḥ
c dviradarathanarāśvān sūdayantas tvadīyān
bhujagapatinikāśair mārgaṇair āttaśastrāḥ
a atha tava rathamukhyās tān pratīyus tvaranto
hṛdikasutakṛpau ca drauṇiduryodhanau ca
c śakuniśukavṛkāś ca krāthadevāvṛdhau ca
dviradajaladaghoṣaiḥ syandanaiḥ kārmukaiś ca
a tava naravaravaryās tān daśaikaṃ ca vīrān
pravaraśaravarāgryais tāḍayanto 'bhyarundhan
c navajaladasavarṇair hastibhis tān udīyur
giriśikharanikāśair bhīmavegaiḥ kuṇindāḥ
a sukalpitā haimavatā madotkaṭā
raṇābhikāmaiḥ kṛtibhiḥ samāsthitāḥ
c suvarṇajālāvatatā babhur gajās
tathā yathā vai jaladāḥ savidyutaḥ
a kuṇindaputro daśabhir mahāyasaiḥ
kṛpaṃ sasūtāśvam apīḍayad bhṛśam
c tataḥ śaradvatsutasāyakair hataḥ
sahaiva nāgena papāta bhūtale
a kuṇindaputrāvarajas tu tomarair
divākarāṃśupratimair ayasmayaiḥ
c rathaṃ ca vikṣobhya nanāda nardatas
tato 'sya gāndhārapatiḥ śiro 'harat
a tataḥ kuṇindeṣu hateṣu teṣv atha
prahṛṣṭarūpās tava te mahārathāḥ
c bhṛśaṃ pradadhmur lavaṇāmbusaṃbhavān
parāṃś ca bāṇāsanapāṇayo 'bhyayuḥ
a athābhavad yuddham atīva dāruṇaṃ
punaḥ kurūṇāṃ saha pāṇḍusṛñjayaiḥ
c śarāsiśaktyṛṣṭigadāparaśvadhair
narāśvanāgāsuharaṃ bhṛśākulam
a rathāśvamātaṅgapadātibhis tataḥ
parasparaṃ viprahatāpatan kṣitau
c yathā savidyutstanitā balāhakāḥ
samāsthitā digbhya ivogramārutaiḥ
a tataḥ śatānīkahatān mahāgajāṃs
tathā rathān pattigaṇāṃś ca tāvakān
c jaghāna bhojaś ca hayān athāpatan
viśastrakṛttāḥ kṛtavarmaṇā dvipāḥ
a athāpare drauṇiśarāhatā dvipās
trayaḥ sasarvāyudhayodhaketavaḥ
c nipetur urvyāṃ vyasavaḥ prapātitās
tathā yathā vajrahatā mahācalāḥ
a kuṇindarājāvarajād anantaraḥ
stanāntare patrivarair atāḍayat
c tavātmajaṃ tasya tavātmajaḥ śaraiḥ
śitaiḥ śarīraṃ bibhide dvipaṃ ca tam
a sa nāgarājaḥ saha rājasūnunā
papāta raktaṃ bahu sarvataḥ kṣaran
c śacīśavajraprahato 'mbudāgame
yathā jalaṃ gairikaparvatas tathā
a kuṇindaputraprahito 'paradvipaḥ
śukaṃ sasūtāśvarathaṃ vyapothayat
c tato 'patat krāthaśarābhidāritaḥ
saheśvaro vajrahato yathā giriḥ
a rathī dvipasthena hato 'patac charaiḥ
krāthādhipaḥ parvatajena durjayaḥ
c savājisūteṣvasanas tathāpatad
yathā mahāvātahato mahādrumaḥ
a vṛko dvipasthaṃ girirājavāsinaṃ
bhṛśaṃ śarair dvādaśabhiḥ parābhinat
c tato vṛkaṃ sāśvarathaṃ mahājavaṃ
tvaraṃś caturbhiś caraṇe vyapothayat
a sa nāgarājaḥ saniyantṛko 'patat
parāhato babhrusuteṣubhir bhṛśam
a samāgato yatra vṛko mahābalaḥ
b sa pothito nāgavareṇa vīryavān
b parābhinad dvādaśabhiḥ śilīmukhaiḥ
b vṛkeṇa bāṇābhihato 'patat kṣitau
b sa vāraṇo babhrusutena sārdham
b kuṇindarājasya suto 'paras tadā
b dvipena devāpṛthudaivāvṛdha
m abhyapīḍayat
c sa cāpi devāvṛdhasūnur arditaḥ
papāta nunnaḥ sahadevasūnunā
a viṣāṇapotrāparagātraghātinā
gajena hantuṃ śakuneḥ kuṇindajaḥ
b nināya vaivasvatamandiraṃ raṇe
c jagāma vegena bhṛśārdayaṃś ca taṃ
tato 'sya gāndhārapatiḥ śiro 'harat
a tataḥ śatānīkahatā mahāgajā
hayā rathāḥ pattigaṇāś ca tāvakāḥ
c suparṇavātaprahatā yathā nagās
tathā gatā gām avaśā vicūrṇitāḥ
a tato 'bhyavidhyad bahubhiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
kuṇindaputro nakulātmajaṃ smayan
c tato 'sya kāyān nicakarta nākuliḥ
śiraḥ kṣureṇāmbujasaṃnibhānanam
a tataḥ śatānīkam avidhyad āśugais
tribhiḥ śitaiḥ karṇasuto 'rjunaṃ tribhiḥ
c tribhiś ca bhīmaṃ nakulaṃ ca saptabhir
janārdanaṃ dvādaśabhiś ca sāyakaiḥ
a tad asya karmātimanuṣyakarmaṇaḥ
samīkṣya hṛṣṭāḥ kuravo 'bhyapūjayan
c parākramajñās tu dhanaṃjayasya te
huto 'yam agnāv iti taṃ tu menire
a tataḥ kirīṭī paravīraghātī
hatāśvam ālokya narapravīram
b mādrīsutaṃ nakulaṃ lokamadhye
b samīkṣya kṛṣṇaṃ bhṛśavikṣataṃ ca
c tam abhyadhāvad vṛṣasenam āhave
sa sūtajasya pramukhe sthitaṃ tadā
a tam āpatantaṃ naravīram ugraṃ
mahāhave bāṇasahasradhāriṇam
b tam āpatantaṃ tarasograrūpaṃ
b kurūttamaṃ bāṇasahasradhāram
c abhyāpatat karṇasuto mahāratho
yathaiva cendraṃ namuciḥ purātane
d tau tatra śūrau rathakuñjarau raṇe
d parasparasyābhimukhau mahārathau
d sasarjatuḥ śarasaṃghān anekān
d saṃbhrāntarūpau subhṛśaṃ tadānīm
a tato 'dbhutenaikaśatena pārthaṃ
śarair viddhvā sūtaputrasya putraḥ
c nanāda nādaṃ sumahānubhāvo
viddhveva śakraṃ namuciḥ purā vai
a punaḥ sa pārthaṃ vṛṣasena ugrair
bāṇair avidhyad bhujamūlamadhye
c tathaiva kṛṣṇaṃ navabhiḥ samārdayat
punaś ca pārthaṃ daśabhiḥ śitāgraiḥ
d pūrvaṃ tathā vṛṣasenena viddho
d mahājavaiḥ śvetahayaḥ śarais taiḥ
d saṃrambham īṣad gamito vadhāya
d karṇātmajasyātha manaḥ pradadhre
a tataḥ kirīṭī raṇamūrdhni kopāt
kṛtvā triśākhāṃ bhrukuṭiṃ lalāṭe
b mumoca tūrṇaṃ viśikhān mahātmā
b vadhe dhṛtaḥ karṇasutasya saṃkhye
b āraktanetro 'ntakaśatruhantā
b uvāca karṇaṃ bhṛśam utsmayaṃs tadā
b duryodhanaṃ drauṇimukhāṃś ca sarvān
b ahaṃ raṇe vṛṣasenaṃ tam ugram
b saṃpaśyataḥ karṇa tavādya saṃkhye
b nayāmi lokaṃ niśitaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ
b yamasya yāvad dhi janā vadanti
b bhavadbhiḥ sarvair mama sūnur hato 'sau
b eko ratho madvihīnas tarasvī
b ahaṃ haniṣye bhavatāṃ samakṣam
b saṃrakṣyatāṃ rathasaṃsthāḥ suto 'yam
b ahaṃ haniṣye vṛṣasenam enam
b paścād vadhiṣye tvām api saṃpramūḍham
b ahaṃ haniṣye 'rjuna ājimadhye
b tam adya mūlaṃ kalahasya saṃkhye
b duryodhanāpāśrayajātadarpam
b tvām adya hantāsmi raṇe prasahya
b asyaiva hantā yudhi bhīmasenaḥ
b duryodhanasyādhamapūruṣasya
b yasyānayād eṣa mahān kṣayo 'bhavat
b sa evam uktvā vinimṛjya cāpaṃ
b lakṣyaṃ hi kṛtvā vṛṣasenam ājau
c mumoca bāṇān viśikhān mahātmā
vadhāya rājan sūtaputrasya saṃkhye
a vivyādha cainaṃ daśabhiḥ pṛṣatkair
marmasv asaktaṃ prasabhaṃ kirīṭī
c ciccheda cāsyeṣvasanaṃ bhujau ca
kṣuraiś caturbhiḥ śira eva cograiḥ
a sa pārthabāṇābhihataḥ papāta
rathād vibāhur viśirā dharāyām
c supuṣpitaḥ parṇadharo 'tikāyo
vāteritaḥ śāla ivādriśṛṅgāt
a taṃ prekṣya bāṇābhihataṃ patantaṃ
rathāt sutaṃ sūtajaḥ kṣiprakārī
c rathaṃ rathenāśu jagāma vegāt
kirīṭinaḥ putravadhābhitaptaḥ
d saṃjayaḥ
d tam āyāntam abhiprekṣya velodvṛttam ivārṇavam
d garjantaṃ sumahākāyaṃ durnivāraṃ surair api
d arjunaṃ prāha dāśārhaḥ prahasya puruṣarṣabhaḥ
d ayaṃ sa ratha āyāti śvetāśvaḥ śalyasārathiḥ
d yena te saha yoddhavyaṃ sthiro bhava dhanaṃjaya
d paśya cainaṃ samāyuktaṃ rathaṃ karṇasya pāṇḍava
d śvetavājisamāyuktaṃ yuktaṃ rādhāsutena ca
d nānāpatākākalilaṃ kiṅkiṇījālamālinam
d uhyamānam ivākāśe vimānaṃ pāṇḍurair hayaiḥ
d dhvajaṃ ca paśya karṇasya nāgakakṣaṃ mahātmanaḥ
d ākhaṇḍaladhanuḥprakhyam ullikhantam ivāmbaram
d paśya karṇaṃ samāyāntaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrapriyaiṣiṇam
d śaradhārā vimuñcantaṃ dhārāsāram ivāmbudam
d eṣa madreśvaro rājā rathāgre paryavasthitaḥ
d niyacchati hayān asya rādheyasyāmitaujasaḥ
d śṛṇu dundubhinirghoṣaṃ śaṅkhaśabdaṃ ca dāruṇam
d siṃhanādāṃś ca vividhāñ śṛṇu pāṇḍava sarvaśaḥ
d antardhāya mahāśabdān karṇenāmitatejasā
d dodhūyamānasya bhṛśaṃ dhanuṣaḥ śṛṇu nisvanam
d ete dīryanti sagaṇāḥ pāñcālānāṃ mahārathāḥ
d dṛṣṭvā kesariṇaṃ kruddhaṃ mṛgā iva mahāvane
d sarvayatnena kaunteya hantum arhasi sūtajam
d na hi karṇaśarān anyaḥ soḍhum utsahate 'nagha
d sadevāsuragandharvāṃs trīṃl lokān sacarācarān
d tvaṃ hi jetuṃ raṇe śaktas tathaiva viditaṃ mama
d bhīmam ugraṃ mahādevaṃ tryakṣaṃ śarvaṃ kapardinam
d na śaktā draṣṭum īśānaṃ kiṃ punar yodhituṃ prabhum
d tvayā sākṣān mahādevaḥ sarvabhūtaśivaḥ śivaḥ
d yuddhenārādhitaḥ sthāṇur devāś ca varadās tava
d tasya pārtha prasādena devadevasya śūlinaḥ
d jahi karṇaṃ mahābāho namuciṃ vṛtrahā yathā
d arjuna uvāca
d śreyas te 'stu sadā pārtha yuddhe jayam avāpnuhi
d dhruva eva jayaḥ kṛṣṇa mama nāsty atra saṃśayaḥ
d sarvalokagurur yas tvaṃ tuṣṭo 'si madhusūdana
d codayāśvān hṛṣīkeśa rathaṃ mama mahāratha
d nāhatvā samare śatruṃ nivartiṣyati phalgunaḥ
d adya karṇaṃ hataṃ paśya maccharaiḥ śakalīkṛtam
d māṃ vā drakṣyasi govinda karṇena nihataṃ śaraiḥ
d upasthitam idaṃ ghoraṃ yuddhaṃ trailokyamohanam
d yaj janāḥ kathayiṣyanti yāvad bhūmir dhariṣyati
d evaṃ bruvaṃs tadā pārthaḥ kṛṣṇam akliṣṭakāriṇam
d pratyudyayau rathenāśu gajaṃ pratigajo yathā
d punaś cāha mahātejāḥ pārthaḥ kṛṣṇam ariṃdamam
d codayāśvān hṛṣīkeśa kālo 'yam ativartate
d evam uktas tadā tena pāṇḍavena mahātmanā
d jayena saṃpūjya sa pāṇḍavaṃ tadā
d pracodayām āsa hayān manojavān
d sa pāṇḍuputrasya ratho manojavaḥ
d kṣaṇena karṇasya rathāgrato 'bhavat
d tataḥ samakṣaṃ svasutaṃ vilokya
d karṇo hataṃ śvetahayena saṃkhye
d saṃrambham āgamya paraṃ mahātmā
d kṛṣṇārjunau sahasaivābhyadhāvat
d śiraḥ karau caiva dhanuś ca pārtha
d ekeṣuṇā vṛṣasenasya saṃkhye
d ciccheda pārtho hy aṅgarājasya sainyaṃ
d kopāgninā caturaṅgaṃ dadāha
 saṃjaya uvāca
a vṛṣasenaṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā śokāmarṣasamanvitaḥ
c muktvā śokodbhavaṃ vāri netrābhyāṃ sahasā vṛṣaḥ
a rathena karṇas tejasvī jagāmābhimukho ripūn
c yuddhāyāmarṣatāmrākṣaḥ samāhūya dhanaṃjayam
a tau rathau sūryasaṃkāśau vaiyāghraparivāraṇau
c sametau dadṛśus tatra dvāv ivārkau samāgatau
a śvetāśvau puruṣādityāv āsthitāv arimardanau
b rathau caturbhir jaladair bhagamitrāv ivāmbare
c śuśubhāte mahātmānau candrādityau yathā divi
a tau dṛṣṭvā vismayaṃ jagmuḥ sarvabhūtāni māriṣa
c trailokyavijaye yattāv indravairocanāv iva
a rathajyātalanirhrādair bāṇaśaṅkharavair api
c tau rathāv abhidhāvantau samālokya mahīkṣitām
a dhvajau ca dṛṣṭvā saṃsaktau vismayaḥ samapadyata
c hastikakṣyāṃ ca karṇasya vānaraṃ ca kirīṭinaḥ
a tau rathau saṃprasaktau ca dṛṣṭvā bhārata pārthivāḥ
c siṃhanādaravāṃś cakruḥ sādhuvādāṃś ca puṣkalān
a śrutvā tu dvairathaṃ tābhyāṃ tatra yodhāḥ samantataḥ
c cakrur bāhuvalaṃ caiva tathā celavalaṃ mahat
a ājagmuḥ kuravas tatra vāditrānugatās tadā
c karṇaṃ praharṣayantaś ca śaṅkhān dadhmuś ca puṣkalān
d rādheyam abhito dadhmuḥ śaṅkhāñ śatasahasraśaḥ
a tathaiva pāṇḍavāḥ sarve harṣayanto dhanaṃjayam
c tūryaśaṅkhaninādena diśaḥ sarvā vyanādayan
a kṣveḍitāsphoṭitotkruṣṭais tumulaṃ sarvato 'bhavat
c bāhughoṣāś ca vīrāṇāṃ karṇārjunasamāgame
a tau dṛṣṭvā puruṣavyāghrau rathasthau rathināṃ varau
c pragṛhītamahācāpau śaraśaktigadāyudhau
a varmiṇau baddhanistriṃśau śvetāśvau śaṅkhaśobhinau
b kṛṣṇaśalyarathopetau tulyarūpau mahārathau
b siṃhaskandhau siṃhabhujau raktākṣau hemamālinau
