b cāpavidyuddhvajopetau śastrasaṃpattiśobhinau
b camaravyajanopetau śvetacchattrābhiśobhinau
c tūṇīravarasaṃpannau dvāv api sma sudarśanau
a raktacandanadigdhāṅgau samadau vṛṣabhāv iva
b siṃhaskandhapratīkāśau vyūḍhoraskau mahābalau
b anyonyaspardhinau rājann anyonyasya vadhaiṣiṇau
b anyonyam abhidhāvantau goṣṭheṣv iva maharṣabhau
b prabhinnāv iva mātaṅgau saṃrabdhāv iva cācalau
c āśīviṣasamaprakhyau yamakālāntakopamau
a indravṛtrāv iva kruddhau sūryācandramasaprabhau
c mahāgrahāv iva krūrau yugānte samupasthitau
a devagarbhau devasamau devatulyau ca rūpataḥ
b yadṛcchayā sameyātāṃ sūryācandramasāv iva
b balinau samare dṛptau nānāśastradharau yudhi
b tau dṛṣṭvā puruṣavyāghrau śārdūlāv iva vegitau
b babhūva paramo harṣas tāvakānāṃ viśāṃ pate
b saṃśayaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ vijaye samapadyata
c sametau puruṣavyāghrau prekṣya karṇadhanaṃjayau
a ubhau varāyudhadharāv ubhau raṇakṛtaśramau
b ubhāv astrabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭhāv ubhau siṃhaparākramau
c ubhau ca bāhuśabdena nādayantau nabhastalam
a ubhau viśrutakarmāṇau pauruṣeṇa balena ca
c ubhau ca sadṛśau yuddhe śambarāmararājayoḥ
a kārtavīryasamau yuddhe tathā dāśaratheḥ samau
c viṣṇuvīryasamau vīrye tathā bhavasamau yudhi
a ubhau śvetahayau rājan rathapravaravāhinau
c sārathī pravarau caiva tayor āstāṃ mahābalau
a tau tu dṛṣṭvā mahārāja rājamānau mahārathau
c siddhacāraṇasaṃghānāṃ vismayaḥ samapadyata
a dhārtarāṣṭrās tataḥ karṇaṃ sabalā bharatarṣabha
c parivavrur mahātmānaṃ kṣipram āhavaśobhinam
a tathaiva pāṇḍavā hṛṣṭā dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamāḥ
b yamau ca cekitānaś ca prahṛṣṭāś ca prabhadrakāḥ
b nānādeśyāś ca ye śūrāḥ śiṣṭā yuddhābhinandinaḥ
b te sarve sahitā hṛṣṭāḥ parivavrur dhanaṃjayam
b rirakṣiṣantaḥ śatrughnāḥ patyaśvarathakuñjaraiḥ
b dhanaṃjayasya vijaye dhṛtāḥ karṇavadhe 'pi ca
b tathaiva tāvakāḥ sarve yattāḥ senāprahāriṇaḥ
b duryodhanamukhā rājan karṇaṃ jugupur āhave
c parivavrur mahātmānaṃ pārtham apratimaṃ yudhi
a tāvakānāṃ raṇe karṇo glaha āsīd viśāṃ pate
c tathaiva pāṇḍaveyānāṃ glahaḥ pārtho 'bhavad yudhi
a ta eva sabhyās tatrāsan prekṣakāś cābhavan sma te
c tatraiṣāṃ glahamānānāṃ dhruvau jayaparājayau
a tābhyāṃ dyūtaṃ samāyattaṃ vijayāyetarāya vā
c asmākaṃ paṇḍavānāṃ ca sthitānāṃ raṇamūrdhani
a tau tu sthitau mahārāja samare yuddhaśālinau
c anyonyaṃ pratisaṃrabdhāv anyonyasya jayaiṣiṇau
a tāv ubhau prajihīrṣetām indravṛtrāv ivābhitaḥ
c bhīmarūpadharāv āstāṃ mahādhūmāv iva grahau
a tato 'ntarikṣe sākṣepā vivādā bharatarṣabha
c mitho bhedāś ca bhūtānām āsan karṇārjunāntare
e vyāśrayanta diśo bhinnāḥ sarvalokāś ca māriṣa
a devadānavagandharvāḥ piśācoragarākṣasāḥ
c pratipakṣagrahaṃ cakruḥ karṇārjunasamāgame
a dyaur āsīt karṇato vyagrā sanakṣatrā viśāṃ pate
c bhūmir viśālā pārthasya mātā putrasya bhārata
a saritaḥ sāgarāś caiva girayaś ca narottama
c vṛkṣāś cauṣadhayas tatra vyāśrayanta kirīṭinam
a asurā yātudhānāś ca guhyakāś ca paraṃtapa
c karṇataḥ samapadyanta khecarāṇi vayāṃsi ca
c   hṛṣṭarūpāḥ samantataḥ
c munayaś cāraṇāḥ siddhāḥ
a ratnāni nidhayaḥ sarve vedāś cākhyānapañcamāḥ
c sopavedopaniṣadaḥ sarahasyāḥ sasaṃgrahāḥ
a vāsukiś citrasenaś ca takṣakaś copatakṣakaḥ
c parvatāś ca tathā sarve kādraveyāś ca sānvayāḥ
e viṣavanto mahāroṣā nāgāś cārjunato 'bhavan
a airāvatāḥ saurabheyā vaiśāleyāś ca bhoginaḥ
c ete 'bhavann arjunataḥ kṣudrasarpās tu karṇataḥ
a īhāmṛgā vyāḍamṛgā maṅgalyāś ca mṛgadvijāḥ
b maṅgaḷyāḥ paśavaś caiva siṃhavyāghrās tathaiva ca
c pārthasya vijayaṃ rājan sarva evābhisaṃśritāḥ
a vasavo marutaḥ sādhyā rudrā viśve 'śvinau tathā
b arjunasya jaye cāstām aśvināv api sapriyau
c agnir indraś ca somaś ca pavanaś ca diśo daśa
d karṇataḥ samapadyanta śvasṛgālavayāṃsi ca
d mṛgāś ca paśavaś caiva siṃhavyāghrās tathaiva ca
d vasavaś ca mahendreṇa marutaś ca sahāgninā
d agnignī  rudraś ca somaś ca yamo vaiśravaṇas tadā
e dhanaṃjayam upājagmur ādityāḥ karṇato 'bhavan
f viśaḥ śūdrāś ca sūtāś ca varṇasaṃkarajāś ca ye
f sarvasattveṣu te rājan rādheyam abhajaṃs tadā
a devās tu pitṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ sagaṇārjunato 'bhavan
c yamo vaiśravaṇaś caiva varuṇaś ca yato 'rjunaḥ
d brahma kṣatraṃ ca yajñāś ca dakṣiṇāś cārjunaṃ śritāḥ
d asurā yātudhānāś ca kravyādāś ca mṛgāṇḍajāḥ
d rākṣasāḥ saha yādobhiḥ śvasṛgālāś ca karṇataḥ
a devabrahmanṛparṣīṇāṃ gaṇāḥ pāṇḍavato 'bhavan
b devarṣibrahmarṣigaṇāḥ sarve ca khacarāś ca ye
c tumburupramukhā rājan gandharvāś ca yato 'rjunaḥ
a prāveyāḥ saha mauneyair gandharvāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ
b sahāpsarobhiḥ śubhrābhir devadūtāś ca guhyakāḥ
b kirīṭinaṃ saṃśritāḥ sma puṇyagandhā manoramāḥ
b amanojñāś ca ye gandhās te sarve karṇam āśritāḥ
b viparītāny aniṣṭāni bhavanti vinaśiṣyatām
b yāny antakāle puruṣaṃ viparītam upadrutam
b praviśanti naraṃ kṣipraṃ mṛtyukāle 'bhyupāgate
b te bhāvāḥ sahitāḥ karṇaṃ praviṣṭāḥ sūtanandanam
b ojas tejaś ca siddhiś ca praharṣaḥ satyavikramau
b manastuṣṭir jayaś cāpi tathānando nṛpottama
b īdṛśāś ca naravyāghra tasmin saṃgrāmasāgare
b nimittāni ca śubhrāṇi viviśur jiṣṇum āhave
b ṛṣayo brāhmaṇaiḥ sārdham abhajanta kirīṭinam
b tato devagaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ siddhāś ca saha cāraṇaiḥ
b dvidhā bhūtā mahārāja vyāśrayanta narottamau
b vimānāni vicitrāṇi guṇavanti ca sarvataḥ
b samāruhya samājagmur dvairathaṃ karṇapārthayoḥ
b didṛkṣavaḥ samājagmuḥ karṇārjunasamāgamam
b antarikṣe mahārāja devagandharvarākṣasāḥ
b evaṃ sarveṣu bhūteṣu dvidhābhūteṣu bhārata
b āśaṃsamāneṣu jayaṃ rādheyasyārjunasya ca
b vimānāyutasaṃbādham ākāśam abhavat tadā
c īhāmṛgavyāḍamṛgair dvipāś ca rathapattibhiḥ
a uhyamānās tathā meghair vāyunā ca manīṣiṇaḥ
c didṛkṣavaḥ samājagmuḥ karṇārjunasamāgamam
a devadānavagandharvā nāgā yakṣāḥ patatriṇaḥ
c maharṣayo vedavidaḥ pitaraś ca svadhābhujaḥ
a tapo vidyās tathauṣadhyo nānārūpāmbaratviṣaḥ
c antarikṣe mahārāja vinadanto 'vatasthire
a brahmā brahmarṣibhiḥ sārdhaṃ prajāpatibhir eva ca
c bhavenāvasthito yānaṃ divyaṃ taṃ deśam abhyayāt
d sametau tau mahātmānau dṛṣṭvā karṇadhanaṃjayau
d arjuno jayatāṃ karṇam iti śakro 'bravīt svayam
d jayatām arjunaṃ karṇa iti sūryo 'bhyabhāṣata
d hatvārjunaṃ mama sutaḥ karṇo jayatu saṃyuge
d hatvā karṇaṃ jayatv adya mama putro dhanaṃjayaḥ
d iti sūryasya caivāsīd vivādo vāsavasya ca
d pakṣasaṃsthitayos tatra tayoḥ puruṣasiṃhayoḥ
d dvaipakṣam āsīd devānām asurāṇāṃ tathaiva ca
d sametau tau mahātmānau dṛṣṭvā karṇadhanaṃjayau
d akampanta trayo lokāḥ sahadevarṣicāraṇāḥ
d sarve devagaṇāś caiva sarvabhūtāni yāni ca
d yataḥ pārthas tato devā yataḥ karṇas tato 'surāḥ
d rathayūthapayoḥ pakṣau kurupāṇḍavavīrayoḥ
d tataḥ prajāpatis tūrṇam ājagāma mahīpate
d dvairathaṃ yudhi taṃ draṣṭuṃ karṇapāṇḍavayos tadā
d vijitya karṇaḥ svid imāṃ vasuṃdharām
d athārjunaḥ svit pratipadyate 'khilām
d itīśvarasyāpi babhūva saṃśayaḥ
d saṃjayaḥ
d prajāpateḥ prekṣya tayor mahad balam
d prajāpatis tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā devabhāgaṃ samāgatam
d abravīt tu tato rājan paśyato vai svayaṃbhuvaḥ
d ubhāv atirathau śūrāv ubhau dṛḍhaparākramau
d ubhau sadṛśakarmāṇau vajricakrāyudhopamau
d aho bata mahad yuddhaṃ karṇārjunasamāgame
d bhaviṣyati mahāghoraṃ vṛtravāsavayor iva
a dṛṣṭvā prajāpatiṃ devāḥ svayaṃbhuvam upāgaman
b ko 'nayor vijayī deva kurupāṇḍavayodhayoḥ
c samo 'stu deva vijaya etayor narasiṃhayoḥ
a tad upaśrutya maghavā praṇipatya pitāmaham
c karṇārjunavināśena mā naśyatv akhilaṃ jagat
d svayaṃbho brūhi nas tathyam etayor vijayaṃ prabho
a svayaṃbho brūhi tad vākyaṃ samo 'stu vijayo 'nayoḥ
b vyajñāpayata deveśam idaṃ matimatāṃ varaḥ
b pūrvaṃ bhagavatā proktaṃ kṛṣṇayor vijayo dhruvaḥ
b evam uktas tu bhagavāñ jaye tābhyām aniścite
b ity abravīn mahārāja mahān brahmā prajāpatiḥ
b dvāv apy etau hi kṛtinau dvāv apy atibalotkaṭau
b bhaviṣyaty anayor yuddhaṃ trailokyasya bhayāvaham
b tataḥ prajāpatiṃ tatra sahasrākṣo 'bhyacodayat
c tat tathāstu namas te 'stu prasīda bhagavan mama
a brahmeśānāv atho vākyam ūcatus tridaśeśvaram
c vijayo dhruva evāstu vijayasya mahātmanaḥ
d khāṇḍave yena hutabhuktoṣitaḥ savyasācinā
d svargaṃ ca samanuprāpya sāhāyyaṃ śakra te kṛtam
d karṇaś ca dānavaḥ pakṣa ataḥ kāryaḥ parājayaḥ
d evaṃ kṛte bhavet kāryaṃ devānām eva niścitam
d ātmakāryaṃ ca sarveṣāṃ garīyas tridaśeśvara
d mahātmā phalgunaś cāpi satyadharmarataḥ sadā
d vijayas tasya niyataṃ jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
d toṣito bhagavān yena mahātmā vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ
d kathaṃ vā tasya na jayo jāyate śatalocana
d yasya cakre svayaṃ viṣṇuḥ sārathyaṃ jagataḥ prabhuḥ
a manasvī balavāñ śūraḥ kṛtāstraś ca tapodhanaḥ
c bibharti ca mahātejā dhanurvedam aśeṣataḥ
d pārthaḥ sarvaguṇopeto devakāryam idaṃ yataḥ
d kliśyante pāṇḍavā nityaṃ vanavāsādibhir bhṛśam
d saṃpannas tapasā caiva paryāptaḥ puruṣarṣabhaḥ
a atikramec ca māhātmyād diṣṭam etasya paryayāt
c atikrānte ca lokānām abhāvo niyato bhavet
a na vidyate vyavasthānaṃ kṛṣṇayoḥ kruddhayoḥ kva cit
c sraṣṭārau hy asataś cobhau sataś ca puruṣarṣabhau
a naranārāyaṇāv etau purāṇāv ṛṣisattamau
c aniyattau niyantārāv abhītau sma paraṃtapau
d naitayos tu samaḥ kaś cid divi vā mānuṣeṣu vā
d anugamya trayo lokāḥ saha devarṣicāraṇaiḥ
d sarvadevagaṇāś cāpi sarvabhūtāni yāni ca
d anayos tu prabhāvena vartate nikhilaṃ jagat
a karṇo lokān ayaṃ mukhyān prāpnotu puruṣarṣabhaḥ
c vīro vaikartanaḥ śūro vijayas tv astu kṛṣṇayoḥ
a vasūnāṃ ca salokatvaṃ marutāṃ vā samāpnuyāt
c sahito droṇabhīṣmābhyāṃ nākaloke mahīyatām
d kleśito hi vane pārtho dīrghakālaṃ pitāmaha
d tasmād eṣa jayed yuddhe tapasābhyadhiko 'rjunaḥ
d pūrvaṃ bhagavatā proktaḥ kṛṣṇayor vijayo dhruvaḥ
d tat tathāstu namaste 'stu prabho brūhi pitāmaha
d tat sahasrākṣavacanaṃ niśamya bhagavān prabhuḥ
d novāca taj jayaṃ tulyaṃ tayoḥ karṇakirīṭinoḥ
d tasmād āśāṃ gataḥ śakras tūṣṇīṃbhūte pitāmahe
d vijayaṃ pāṇḍaveyasya vadhaṃ karṇasya cāhave
a ity ukto devadevābhyāṃ sahasrākṣo 'bravīd vacaḥ
c āmantrya sarvabhūtāni brahmeśānānuśāsanāt
a śrutaṃ bhavadbhir yat proktaṃ bhagavadbhyāṃ jagaddhitam
c tat tathā nānyathā tad dhi tiṣṭhadhvaṃ gatamanyavaḥ
a iti śrutvendravacanaṃ sarvabhūtāni māriṣa
c vismitāny abhavan rājan pūjayāṃ cakrire ca tat
d nocus tadā jayaṃ tulyaṃ tayoḥ puruṣasiṃhayoḥ
a vyasṛjaṃś ca sugandhīni nānārūpāṇi khāt tathā
c puṣpavarṣāṇi vibudhā devatūryāṇy avādayan
a didṛkṣavaś cāpratimaṃ dvairathaṃ narasiṃhayoḥ
c devadānavagandharvāḥ sarva evāvatasthire
d vismayotphullanayanā nānyā bubudhire kriyāḥ
e rathau ca tau śvetahayau yuktaketū mahāsvanau
f yau tau karṇārjunau rājan prahṛṣṭāv abhyatiṣṭhatām
a samāgatā lokavīrāḥ śaṅkhān dadhmuḥ pṛthak pṛthak
c vāsudevārjunau vīrau karṇaśalyau ca bhārata
a tad bhīrusaṃtrāsakaraṃ yuddhaṃ samabhavat tadā
c anyonyaspardhinor vīrye śakraśambarayor iva
a tayor dhvajau vītamālau śuśubhāte rathasthitau
b rāhuketū yathākāśe uditau jagataḥ kṣaye
c pṛthagrūpau samārchantau krodhaṃ yuddhe parasparam
a karṇasyāśīviṣanibhā ratnasāravatī dṛḍhā
c puraṃdaradhanuḥprakhyā hastikakṣyā vyarājata
a kapiśreṣṭhas tu pārthasya vyāditāsyo bhayaṃkaraḥ
c bhīṣayann eva daṃṣṭrābhir durnirīkṣyo ravir yathā
a yuddhābhilāṣuko bhūtvā dhvajo gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ
c karṇadhvajam upātiṣṭhat so 'vadīd abhinardayan
a utpatya ca mahāvegaḥ kakṣyām abhyahanat kapiḥ
c nakhaiś ca daśanaiś caiva garuḍaḥ pannagaṃ yathā
a sukiṅkiṇīkābharaṇā kālapāśopamāyasī
c abhyadravat susaṃkruddhā nāgakakṣyā mahākapim
a ubhayor uttame yuddhe dvairathe dyūta āhṛte
c prakurvāte dhvajau yuddhaṃ pratyaheṣan hayān hayāḥ
d hayā hayān abhyaheṣan spardhamānāḥ parasparam
a avidhyat puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ śalyaṃ nayanasāyakaiḥ
c sa cāpi puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ tathaivābhisamaikṣata
a tatrājayad vāsudevaḥ śalyaṃ nayanasāyakaiḥ
c karṇaṃ cāpy ajayad dṛṣṭyā kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥ
a athābravīt sūtaputraḥ śalyam ābhāṣya sasmitam
b uvāca praṇayād rājan sāmapūrvam idaṃ vacaḥ
c yadi pārtho raṇe hanyād adya mām iha karhi cit
e kim uttaraṃ tadā te syāt sakhe satyaṃ bravīhi me
 śalya uvāca
 hate tvayi hy ahaṃ hanyām ubhau kṛṣṇadhanaṃjayau
a yadi karṇa raṇe hanyād adya tvāṃ śvetavāhanaḥ
c ubhāv ekarathenāhaṃ hanyāṃ mādhavapāṇḍavau
 saṃjaya uvāca
a evam eva tu goviṃdam arjunaḥ pratyabhāṣata
c taṃ prahasyābravīt kṛṣṇaḥ pārthaṃ param idaṃ vacaḥ
a pated divākaraḥ sthānāc chīryetānekadhā kṣitiḥ
c śaityam agnir iyān na tvā karṇo hanyād dhanaṃjayam
a yadi tv evaṃ kathaṃ cit syāl lokaparyasanaṃ yathā
c hanyāṃ karṇaṃ tathā śalyaṃ bāhubhyām eva saṃyuge
a iti kṛṣṇavacaḥ śrutvā prahasan kapiketanaḥ
c arjunaḥ pratyuvācedaṃ kṛṣṇam akliṣṭakāriṇam
e mamāpy etāv aparyāptau karṇaśalyau janārdana
a sapatākādhvajaṃ karṇaṃ saśalyarathavājinam
c sacchatrakavacaṃ caiva saśaktiśarakārmukam
a draṣṭāsy adya śaraiḥ karṇaṃ raṇe kṛttam anekadhā
c adyainaṃ sarathaṃ sāśvaṃ saśaktikavacāyudham
d saṃcūrṇitam ivāmarde pādapaṃ paśya dantinā
d adya rādheyabhāryāṇāṃ vaidhavyaṃ samupasthitam
d dhruvaṃ svapneṣv aniṣṭāni tābhir dṛṣṭāni mādhava
d dhruvam adyaiva draṣṭāsi vidhavāḥ karṇayoṣitaḥ
e na hi me śāmyate vairaṃ kṛṣṇāṃ yat prāhasat purā
f kṛṣṇāṃ sabhāgatāṃ dṛṣṭvā mūḍhenādīrghadarśinā
f asmāṃs tathāvahasatā kṣipatā ca punaḥ punaḥ
a adya draṣṭāsi govinda karṇam unmathitaṃ mayā
c vāraṇeneva mattena puṣpitaṃ jagatīruham
a adya tā madhurā vācaḥ śrotāsi madhusūdana
b diṣṭyā jayasi vārṣṇeya iti karṇe nipātite
c adyābhimanyujananīm anṛṇaḥ sāntvayiṣyasi
e kuntīṃ pitṛṣvasāraṃ ca saṃprahṛṣṭo janārdana
a adya bāṣpamukhīṃ kṛṣṇāṃ sāntvayiṣyasi mādhava
c vāgbhiś cāmṛtakalpābhir dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tad devanāgāsurasiddhasaṃghair
gandharvayakṣāpsarasāṃ ca saṃghaiḥ
c brahmarṣirājarṣisuparṇajuṣṭaṃ
babhau viyad vismayanīyarūpam
a nānadyamānaṃ ninadair manojñair
vāditragītastutibhiś ca nṛttaiḥ
c sarve 'ntarikṣe dadṛśur manuṣyāḥ
khasthāṃś ca tān vismayanīyarūpān
a tataḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ kurupāṇḍuyodhā
vāditrapatrāyudhasiṃhanādaiḥ
c ninādayanto vasudhāṃ diśaś ca
svanena sarve dviṣato nijaghnuḥ
a nānāśvamātaṅgarathāyutākulaṃ
varāsiśaktyṛṣṭinipātaduḥsaham
c abhīrujuṣṭaṃ hatadehasaṃkulaṃ
raṇājiraṃ lohitaraktam ābabhau
d babhūva yuddhaṃ kurupāṇḍavānāṃ
d yathā surāṇām asuraiḥ sahābhavat
a tathā pravṛtte 'strabhṛtāṃ parābhave
dhanaṃjayaś cādhirathiś ca sāyakaiḥ
c diśaś ca sainyaṃ ca śitair ajihmagaiḥ
parasparaṃ prorṇuvatuḥ sma daṃśitau
a tatas tvadīyāś ca pare ca sāyakaiḥ
kṛte 'ndhakāre vividur na kiṃ cana
c bhayāt tu tāv eva rathau samāśrayaṃs
tamonudau khe prasṛtā ivāṃśavaḥ
a tato 'stram astreṇa parasparasya tau
vidhūya vātāv iva pūrvapaścimau
c ghanāndhakāre vitate tamonudau
yathoditau tadvad atīva rejatuḥ
a na cābhimantavyam iti pracoditāḥ
pare tvadīyāś ca tadāvatasthire
c mahārathau tau parivārya sarvataḥ
surāsurā vāsavaśambarāv iva
a mṛdaṅgabherīpaṇavānakasvanair
ninādite bhārata śaṅkhanisvanaiḥ
c sasiṃhanādau babhatur narottamau
śaśāṅkasūryāv iva meghasaṃplave
d virejatus tau puruṣarṣabhau tadā
a mahādhanurmaṇḍalamadhyagāv ubhau
suvarcasau bāṇasahasraraśminau
c didhakṣamāṇau sacarācaraṃ jagad
yugāstasūryāv iva duḥsahau raṇe
a ubhāv ajeyāv ahitāntakāv ubhau
jighāṃsatus tau kṛtinau parasparam
c mahāhave vīravarau samīyatur
yathendrajambhāv iva karṇapāṇḍavau
a tato mahāstrāṇi mahādhanurdharau
vimuñcamānāv iṣubhir bhayānakaiḥ
c narāśvanāgān amitau nijaghnatuḥ
parasparaṃ jaghnatur uttameṣubhiḥ
a tato visasruḥ punar arditāḥ śarair
narottamābhyāṃ kurupāṇḍavāśrayāḥ
c sanāgapattyaśvarathā diśo gatās
tathā yathā siṃhabhayād vanaukasaḥ
a tatas tu duryodhanabhojasaubalāḥ
kṛpaś ca śāradvatasūnunā saha
c mahārathāḥ pañca dhanaṃjayācyutau
śaraiḥ śarīrāntakarair atāḍayan
a dhanūṃṣi teṣām iṣudhīn hayān dhvajān
rathāṃś ca sūtāṃś ca dhanaṃjayaḥ śaraiḥ
c samaṃ ca ciccheda parābhinac ca tāñ
śarottamair dvādaśabhiś ca sūtajam
d te pañca vīrāḥ satataṃ hatāyārathāḥ
d nikṛttadehārjunabāṇavegaiḥ
d pradudruvus tatra padātayo bhṛśaṃ
d ruruhahū rathānyeṣu punar yayuś ca tam
a athābhyadhāvaṃs tvaritāḥ śataṃ rathāḥ
śataṃ ca nāgārjunam ātatāyinaḥ
c śakās tukhārā yavanāś ca sādinaḥ
sahaiva kāmbojavarair jighāṃsavaḥ
a varāyudhān pāṇigatān karaiḥ saha
kṣurair nyakṛntaṃs tvaritāḥ śirāṃsi ca
c hayāṃś ca nāgāṃś ca rathāṃś ca yudhyatāṃ
dhanaṃjayaḥ śatrugaṇaṃ tam akṣiṇot
d tadā sa teṣāṃ yudhi savyasācī
d kṣuraiḥ praciccheda dhanaṃjayaś ca
d nāgān hayān rathasūtāṃś ca tatra
d śirāṃsi teṣām iṣubhiḥ kirīṭī
d dhanaṃjaye yudhyamāne ca tatra
d kṣaṇena sarvaṃ kṣayam āviveśa
a tato 'ntarikṣe suratūryanisvanāḥ
sasādhuvādā hṛṣitaiḥ samīritāḥ
c nipetur apy uttamapuṣpavṛṣṭayaḥ
surūpagandhāḥ pavaneritāḥ śivāḥ
a tad adbhutaṃ devamanuṣyasākṣikaṃ
samīkṣya bhūtāni visiṣmiyur nṛpa
b aho 'rjunenaiva kṛtaṃ mahattaraṃ
b yad ekavīro yuyudhe mahārathān
b samīkṣya devāś ca nṛrājamukhyāḥ
b śaśaṃsuḥ kṛṣṇārjunayor mahad yaśaḥ
c tavātmajaḥ sūtasutaś ca na vyathāṃ
na vismayaṃ jagmatur ekaniścayau
a athābravīd droṇasutas tavātmajaṃ
karaṃ kareṇa pratipīḍya sāntvayan
c prasīda duryodhana śāmya pāṇḍavair
alaṃ virodhena dhig astu vigraham
a hato gurur brahmasamo mahāstravit
tathaiva bhīṣmapramukhā nararṣabhāḥ
c ahaṃ tv avadhyo mama cāpi mātulaḥ
praśādhi rājyaṃ saha pāṇḍavaiś ciram
a dhanaṃjayaḥ sthāsyati vārito mayā
janārdano naiva virodham icchati
c yudhiṣṭhiro bhūtahite sadā rato
vṛkodaras tadvaśagas tathā yamau
a tvayā ca pārthaiś ca paraspareṇa
prajāḥ śivaṃ prāpnuyur icchati tvayi
c vrajantu śeṣāḥ svapurāṇi pārthivā
nivṛttavairāś ca bhavantu sainikāḥ
d na ced dhataṃ śroṣyasi caiva karṇaṃ
d mahābalaṃ pārthiva sūtaputram
d vihāya rājyaṃ tv akhilaṃ samastaṃ
d gantāsi karṇasya pathaṃ vicitram
a na ced vacaḥ śroṣyasi me narādhipa
dhruvaṃ prataptāsi hato 'ribhir yudhi
c idaṃ ca dṛṣṭaṃ jagatā saha tvayā
kṛtaṃ yad ekena kirīṭamālinā
e yathā na kuryād balabhinna cāntako
na ca pracetā bhagavān na yakṣarāṭ
f vṛddhaṃ pitaram ālokya gāndhārīṃ ca yaśasvinīm
f kṛpālur dharmarājo hi yācitaḥ śamam eṣyati
f yathocitaṃ ca vai rājyam anujñāsyati te prabhuḥ
f vipaścit sumatir vīraḥ sarvaśāstrārthatattvavit
f vairaṃ neṣyati dharmātmā svajane nāsty atikramaḥ
f na vigrahamatiḥ kṛṣṇaḥ svajane pratinandati
f bhīmasenārjunau cobhau mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavau
f vāsudevamate caiva pāṇḍavasya ca dhīmataḥ
f sthāsyanti puruṣavyāghrās tayor vacanagauravāt
f rakṣa duryodhanātmānam ātmā sarvasya bhājanam
f jīvite yatnam ātiṣṭha jīvan bhadrāṇi paśyati
f rājyaṃ śrīś caiva bhadraṃ te jīvamāne tu kalpyate
f mṛtasya khalu kauravya naiva rājyaṃ kutaḥ sukham
f lokavṛttam idaṃ vṛttaṃ pravṛttaṃ paśya bhārata
f śāmya tvaṃ pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdhaṃ rakṣa śeṣaṃ kulasya ca
f mā bhūt sa kālaḥ kauravya yadāham ahitaṃ vacaḥ
f brūyāṃ kāmaṃ mahābāho māvamaṃsthā vaco mama
f dharmiṣṭhaṃ hitam atyantaṃ rājñaś caiva kulasya ca
f etad dhi paramaṃ śreyaḥ kuruvaṃśasya vṛddhaye
f prajāhitaṃ ca gāndhāre kulasya ca sukhāvaham
f pathyam āyatisaṃyuktaṃ karṇo hy arjunam āhave
f na jeṣyati naravyāghram iti me dhīyate matiḥ
f rocatāṃ te naraśreṣṭha mamaitad vacanaṃ śubham
f ato 'nyathā hi rājendra vināśaḥ sumahān bhavet
a ato 'pi bhūyāṃś ca guṇair dhanaṃjayaḥ
sa cābhipatsyaty akhilaṃ vaco mama
c tavānuyātrāṃ ca tathā kariṣyati
prasīda rājañ jagataḥ śamāya vai
d na cātitīvraṃ pitṛvairam udyataṃ
d nihantum ugre ripum ulbaṇaṃ yudhi
d tathāpi tat pathyahitaṃ na cecchataḥ
d prakāśitaṃ sādhur ihādya pāṇḍavaiḥ
a mamāpi mānaḥ paramaḥ sadā tvayi
bravīmy atas tvāṃ paramāc ca sauhṛdāt
c nivārayiṣyāmi hi karṇam apy ahaṃ
yadā bhavān sapraṇayo bhaviṣyati
a vadanti mitraṃ sahajaṃ vicakṣaṇās
tathaiva sāmnā ca dhanena cārjitam
b mayā hi pūrvaṃ kathitaṃ kṛpādibhis
b tathā hi rājā tava dehadehajaḥ
b anyaiś ca sarvair guṇabhāvavistaraiḥ
b dhanaṃjayān nāsti samo dhanurdharaḥ
b babhūva loke paramāstrasaṃgrahī
b viṣṇuḥ sakhā yasya sakhā na vigrahaḥ
b karmāṇi yasyākhilāny adbhutāni
b sarvāṇi vaḥ saṃsmara tāni pūrvam
b yuddhāntam ācchādya suyodhanādya
b karṇasya putrāvadhi mā vyanīnaśaḥ
b na śroṣyasi tvaṃ yadi me mahāratha
b tathā hataṃ drakṣyasi pāṇḍavair balam
b athārjunaṃ kālasamaprabhāvaṃ
b kathaṃ na draṣṭāsi raṇe carantam
b tejasvinām adya raviṃ mahāprabhaṃ
b kathaṃ varāstraṃ samare na paśyasi
b tvayi pranaṣṭe naravīrasatkṛto
b bhoktā hi rājyaṃ bhuvi dharmasūnuḥ
b ity evam ukto gurusūnunā kathaṃ
b sa me sthitaś caiva tathaiva durmanāḥ
b sakhe tvam evādya kathaṃ pravaktā
b pārthasya pakṣād yudhi jātaharṣāt
b vimuktabāhuḥ prahasan sudurbalo
b duryodhano durgatikālacoditaḥ
b vṛkodaraṃ hanmi sabāndhavaṃ raṇe
b kathaṃ bibhemi prayato mahāmṛdhe
c pratāpataś copanataṃ caturvidhaṃ
tad asti sarvaṃ tvayi pāṇḍaveṣu ca
a nisargatas te tava vīra bāndhavāḥ
punaś ca sāmnā ca samāpnuhi sthiram
c tvayi prasanne yadi mitratām iyur
dhruvaṃ narendrendra tathā tvam ācara
a sa evam uktaḥ suhṛdā vaco hitaṃ
vicintya niḥśvasya ca durmanābravīt
c yathā bhavān āha sakhe tathaiva tan
mamāpi ca jñāpayato vacaḥ śṛṇu
d ko 'nyo 'sti me duḥkhasakhaḥ sadaiva
d muktvā bhavantaṃ mama caikavīram
a nihatya duḥśāsanam uktavān bahu
prasahya śārdūlavad eṣa durmatiḥ
c vṛkodaras tad dhṛdaye mama sthitaṃ
na tatparokṣaṃ bhavataḥ kutaḥ śamaḥ
d na cāpi karṇaṃ prasahed raṇe 'rjuno
d mahāgiriṃ merum ivogramārutaḥ
d na cāśvasiṣyanti pṛthātmajā mayi
d prasahya vairaṃ bahuśo vicintya
a na cāpi karṇaṃ guruputra saṃstavād
upāramety arhasi vaktum acyuta
c śrameṇa yukto mahatādya phalgunas
tam eṣa karṇaḥ prasabhaṃ haniṣyati
d vasuṃdharāyāḥ parivartanaṃ bhaved
d vrajec ca śoṣaṃ makarālayo 'rṇavaḥ
d plaveyur apy adrivarā mahāmbudhau
d na cārjuno jeṣyati karṇam āhave
d apāṃ pṛthivyā nabhaso nabhasvataḥ
d sutigmadīpteś ca hiraṇyaretasaḥ
d abhāva eṣām api sarvato bhaven
d na cārjuno jeṣyati karṇam āhave
a tam evam uktvābhyanunīya cāsakṛt
tavātmajaḥ svān anuśāsti sainikān
c samāghnatābhidravatāhitān imān
sabāṇaśabdān kim u joṣam āsyate
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tau śaṅkhabherīninade samṛddhe
samīyatuḥ śvetahayau narāgryau
c vaikartanaḥ sūtaputro 'rjunaś ca
durmantrite tava putrasya rājan
d āśīviṣāv agnim ivotsṛjantau
d vairaṃ mukhābhyām abhiniśvasantau
d yaśasvinau jajvalatur mṛdhe tadā
d ghṛtāvasiktāv iva havyavāhau
a yathā gajau haimavatau prabhinnau
pragṛhya dantāv iva vāśitārthe
c tathā samājagmatur ugravegau
dhanaṃjayaś cādhirathiś ca vīrau
a balāhakeneva yathā balāhako
yadṛcchayā vā giriṇā girir yathā
c tathā dhanurjyātalaneminisvanau
samīyatus tāv iṣuvarṣavarṣiṇau
d śarāstraśaktyṛṣṭigadāsisarpau
d roṣānilodbhūtamahormimālau
d yathācalau cācalatas tathā tau
d yathārṇavau cāyayatur yugānte
a pravṛddhaśṛṅgadrumavīrudoṣadhī
pravṛddhanānāvidhaparvataukasau
b mahāmahīdhrāv iva pakṣavantau
c yathācalau vā galitau mahābalau
tathā mahāstrair itaretaraṃ ghnataḥ
a sa saṃnipātas tu tayor mahān abhūt
sureśavairocanayor yathā purā
c śarair vibhugnāṅganiyantṛvāhanaḥ
suduḥsaho 'nyaiḥ paṭuśoṇitodakaḥ
a prabhūtapadmotpalamatsyakacchapau
mahāhradau pakṣigaṇānunāditau
c susaṃnikṛṣṭāv aniloddhatau yathā
tathā rathau tau dhvajinau samīyatuḥ
a ubhau mahendrasya samānavikramāv
ubhau mahendrapratimau mahārathau
c mahendravajrapratimaiś ca sāyakair
mahendravṛtrāv iva saṃprajahratuḥ
a sanāgapattyaśvarathe ubhe bale
vicitravarṇābharaṇāmbarasraje
c cakampatuś connamataḥ sma vismayād
viyadgatāś cārjunakarṇasaṃyuge
a bhujāḥ savajrāṅgulayaḥ samucchritāḥ
sasiṃhanādā hṛṣitair didṛkṣubhiḥ
c yadārjunaṃ mattam iva dvipo dvipaṃ
samabhyayād ādhirathir jighāṃsayā
d tataḥ kurūṇām atha somakānāṃ
d śabdo mahān prādurabhūt samantāt
d yadārjunaṃ sūtaputro 'parāhṇe
d mahāhave śailam ivāmbudo 'rchat
d tathaiva cāsīd rathayoḥ samāgamo
d mahāraṇe śoṇitamāṃsakardame
a abhyakrośan somakās tatra pārthaṃ
tvarasva yāhy arjuna vidhya karṇam
c chindhy asya mūrdhānam alaṃ cireṇa
śraddhāṃ ca rājyād dhṛtarāṣṭrasūnoḥ
a tathāsmākaṃ bahavas tatra yodhāḥ
karṇaṃ tadā yāhi yāhīty avocan
c jahy arjunaṃ karṇa tataḥ sacīrāḥ
punar vanaṃ yāntu cirāya pārthāḥ
a tataḥ karṇaḥ prathamaṃ tatra pārthaṃ
maheṣubhir daśabhiḥ paryavidhyat
c tam arjunaḥ pratyavidhyac chitāgraiḥ
kakṣāntare daśabhir atīva kruddhaḥ
d karṇo 'tha pūrvaṃ daśabhiḥ pṛṣatkair
d gāṇḍīvadhanvānam avidhyad āśu
d jaghāna taṃ cāpi tataḥ kirīṭī
d śarais tathāṣṭādaśabhiḥ sumuktaiḥ
d punaś ca karṇas tvarito 'tha pārthaṃ
d ratheṣubhis taṃ daśabhir jaghāna
d taṃ cāpi pārtho daśabhiḥ śitāgraiḥ
d kakṣyāntare tīkṣṇamukhair avidhyat
d karṇas tato bhārata sāṃparāye
d ghore 'tivelaṃ raṇasaṃvimardī
d jaghāna pārthaṃ navabhiḥ śitāgraiḥ
d kakṣyāntare nāgam iva prabhinnam
d tato 'parābhyāṃ yudhi sūtaputro
d dvābhyāṃ kṣurābhyāṃ harim āśukārī
d samājaghāna tvarayā mahātmā
d yathā surendraṃ namuciḥ prasahya
d taṃ pāṇḍavaḥ pañcabhir āyasāgrair
d ākarṇapūrṇair nijaghāna karṇam
d te śoṇitaṃ tasya papus tadānīṃ
d kālasya dūtā iva pārthabāṇāḥ
d karṇo 'pi pārthaṃ sahavāsudevaṃ
d samācinod bhārata vatsadantaiḥ
a parasparaṃ tau viśikhaiḥ sutīkṣṇais
tatakṣatuḥ sūtaputro 'rjunaś ca
c parasparasyāntarepsū vimarde
subhīmam abhyāyayatuḥ prahṛṣṭau
d tato 'rjunaḥ prāsṛjad ugradhanvā
d bhujāv ubhau gāṇḍivaṃ cānumṛjya
d nārācanālīkavarāhakarṇān
d kṣurāṃs tathā sāñjalikārdhacandrān
d te sarvataḥ samakīryanta rājan
d pārtheṣavaḥ karṇarathaṃ viśantaḥ
d avāṅmukhāḥ pakṣigaṇā dinānte
d viśanti ketārtham ivāśu vṛkṣam
d yān arjunaḥ sabhrukuṭīkaṭākṣaḥ
d karṇāya rājann asṛjaj jitāriḥ
d tān sāyakair grasate sūtaputraḥ
d kṣiptān kṣiptān pāṇḍavasyeṣusaṃghān
d tataḥ karṇo bhārgaveṇābhisṛṣṭaṃ
d prāduścakre brāhmam astraṃ mahātmā
d tataḥ prajajvāla tad astram ugraṃ
d yugāntasūryajvalanaprakāśam
d pātālam astreṇa nihatya tena
d jaghāna karṇo naranāgasaṃghān
d tato 'stram āgneyam amitratāpanaṃ
d mumoca karṇāya sureśvarātmajaḥ
d dhanaṃjayaḥ saṃyugamūrdhani jvalann
d atha prajajvāla tad astram uttamam
d jvālābhir atyarthaviniḥsṛtābhir
d astrasya sūrasya mahendrasūnoḥ
d bhūmy antarikṣe ca diśo 'rkamārgaṃ
d prāvṛtya deho 'sya babhūva dīptaḥ
d yodhāś ca sarve jvalitāntarārtāḥ
d pradudruvus tatra vidagdhavastrāḥ
d śabdaś ca ghoro 'ti babhūva tatra
d yathā vane veṇuvanasya dahyataḥ
d samīkṣya karṇo jvalanāstram udyataṃ
d sa vāruṇaṃ tat praśamārtham āhave
d samutsṛjan sūtasutaḥ pratāpavān
d sa tena vahniṃ śamayāṃ babhūva
d balāhakāstreṇa diśas tarasvī
d cakāra sarvāṃs timireṇa saṃvṛtāḥ
d tato dharitrīdharatulyarodhasaḥ
d samantato vai parivārya vāriṇā
d taiś cātivegāt sa tathāvidho 'pi
d nītaḥ śamaṃ vahnir atipracaṇḍaḥ
d balāhakaiś caiva digantarāṇi
d vyāptāni sarvāṇi yathā nabhaś ca
d tathā ca sarvās timireṇa vai diśo
d meghair vṛtā na pradṛśyeta kiṃ cit
d apāvahan meghagaṇāṃs tatas tān
d samīraṇāstreṇa samīritena saḥ
d tataḥ so 'straṃ dayitaṃ devarājñaḥ
d prāduścakre vajram amitratāpanaḥ
d gāṇḍīvajyāṃ vimṛśaṃś cātimanyur
d dhanaṃjayaḥ śatrusaṃghapramāthī
d tataḥ kṣuraprāñjalikārdhacandrā
d nārācanāḷīkavarāhakarṇāḥ
d gāṇḍīvataḥ prādurāsan sutīkṣṇāḥ
d sahasraśo vajrasamānavegāḥ
d te sarvataḥ paryadhāvanta ghorāḥ
d pārtheṣavaḥ karṇarathaṃ vihaṃgāḥ
d adhomukhāḥ pakṣigaṇā dinānte
d niśāniketārtham ivāśu vṛkṣam
d jagrāha tān sūtaputraḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ
d kṣiptāṃs tathā pāṇḍavabāṇasaṃghān
d amṛṣyamāṇasya dhanaṃjayasya
d raṇājire tv antakatulyakarmā
d vaikartano roṣaparītacetā
d jyotiṣprabhāṃ yadvad udāgataḥ san
d divākaro nāśayate kṣaṇena
d pārthasya tān bāṇagaṇān samagrān
d vyanāśayad yudhyata eva karṇaḥ
d te karṇam āsādya mahāprabhāvāḥ
d sutejanā gārdhrapatrāḥ suvegāḥ
d gātreṣu sarveṣu hayeṣu cāpi
d śarāsane yugacakre dhvaje ca
d nirbhidya tūrṇaṃ viviśuḥ sutīkṣṇās
d tārkṣyatrastā bhūmim ivoragās te
d śarācitāṅgo rudhirārdragātraḥ
d karṇas tadā roṣavivṛttanetraḥ
d dṛḍhajyamānāmya samudraghoṣaṃ
d prāduścakre bhārgavāstraṃ mahātmā
d mahendraśastrābhimukhān vimuktāṃś
d chittvā karṇaḥ pāṇḍavasyeṣusaṃghān
d pārthāstram astreṇa nihatya tena
d jaghāna karṇo nṛgajāśvasaṃghān
d amṛṣyamāṇas tu mahāvimarde
d mahāratho bhārgavāstraprabhāvāt
d pāñcālānāṃ pravarāṃś cāpi yodhān
d krodhāviṣṭaḥ sūtaputras tarasvī
d bāṇair vivyādhāhave supramuktaiḥ
d prahasya kṛṣṇau tu narapravīraḥ
d tataḥ pāñcālāḥ somakāś cāpi rājan
d karṇenājau pīḍyamānāḥ śaraughaiḥ
d krodhāviṣṭā vivyadhus taṃ samantāt
d tīkṣṇair bāṇaiḥ sūtaputraṃ sametāḥ
d tān astāṃs taiḥ sa nikṛtyāśu bāṇān
d pāñcālānāṃ rathanāgāśvasaṃghān
d abhyardayad bāṇagaṇaiḥ prasahya
d vikṣobhayan samare sūtaputraḥ
d te bhinnadehā vyasavo nipetuḥ
d karṇeṣubhir bhūmitale svanantaḥ
d kruddhena siṃhena yathaiva nāgā
d mahābalā bhīmabalena tadvat
d pāñcālānāṃ pravarān saṃnihatya
d praspardhamānān balino yodhamukhyān
d tataḥ sa rājan virarāja karṇaḥ
d śarān vaman megha ivāmbudhārāḥ
d karṇasya matvā tu jayaṃ tvadīyāḥ
d parāṃ mudaṃ siṃhanādāṃś ca cakruḥ
d sarve hy amanyanta vaśe kṛtau tau
d karṇena kṛṣṇāv iti kauravendra
d tat tādṛśaṃ prekṣya mahārathasya
d karṇasya vīryaṃ ca parair asahyam
d dṛṣṭvā tu karṇena dhanaṃjayasya
d saṃgrāmamadhye nihataṃ tad astram
a amṛṣyamāṇaś ca mahāvimarde
tatrākrudhyad bhīmaseno mahātmā
c athābravīt pāṇinā pāṇim āghnan
saṃdaṣṭauṣṭho nṛtyati vādayann iva
d tatas tv amarṣī krodhasaṃdīptanetro
d vātātmajaḥ pāṇinā pāṇim ārchat
d bhīmo 'bravīd arjunaṃ satyasaṃdham
d amarṣito niḥśvasañ jātamanyuḥ
d roṣāt pradīptaḥ sumahān vimarde
d bhīmas tato 'krudhyad adīnasattvaḥ
d pāṇiṃ sa pāṇau vinipiṣya roṣād
d amarṣito vākyam uvāca pārtham
d kathaṃ nu pāpo 'yam apetadharmaḥ
d sūtātmajaḥ samare 'dya prasahya
d pāñcālānāṃ yodhamukhyān anekān
d nijaghnivāṃs tava jiṣṇo samakṣam
d pūrvaṃ daityair ajitaṃ kālakeyaiḥ
d sākṣāt sthāṇor bāhusaṃsparśam etya
e kathaṃ nu tvāṃ sūtaputraḥ kirīṭin
maheṣubhir daśabhir avidhyad agre
f tvayā kṣiptāṃś cāgrasadbāṇasaṃghānn
f āścaryam etat pratibhāti me 'dya
f kṛṣṇāparikleśam anusmara tvaṃ
f yathābravīt ṣaṇḍhatilān sma vācaḥ
f vācaḥ sutīkṣṇāsthibhido 'manojñāḥ
f sūtātmajo 'yaṃ gatabhīr durātmā
f saṃsmṛtya sarvaṃ tad ihādya pāpaṃ
f jahy āśu karṇaṃ yudhi savyasācin
f kasmād upekṣāṃ kuruṣe kirīṭinn
f upekṣituṃ nāyam ihādya kālaḥ
a yayā dhṛtyā sarvabhūtāny ajaiṣīr
grāsaṃ dadad vahnaye khāṇḍave tvam
c tayā dhṛtyā sūtaputraṃ jahi tvam
ahaṃ vainaṃ gadayā pothayiṣye
d sametya pārthaṃ sa nṛśaṃsavādī
d jīvan nāyaṃ yāsyati kālapakvaḥ
a athābravīd vāsudevo 'pi pārthaṃ
dṛṣṭvā ratheṣūn pratihanyamānān
c amīmṛdat sarvathā te 'dya karṇo
hy astrair astrāṇi kim idaṃ kirīṭin
a sa vīra kiṃ muhyasi nāvadhīyase
nadanty ete kuravaḥ saṃprahṛṣṭāḥ
c karṇaṃ puraskṛtya vidur hi sarve
tvadastram astrair vinipātyamānam
a yayā dhṛtyā nihataṃ tāmasāstraṃ
yuge yuge rākṣasāś cāpi ghorāḥ
c dambhodbhavāś cāsurāś cāhaveṣu
tayā dhṛtyā tvaṃ jahi sūtaputram
c darpotsiktaṃ vīryamantaṃ kirīṭin
d karṇaṃ samāsādya ripupramāthin
d pārthāhave vyaktam astraṃ samartham
a anena vāsya kṣuraneminādya
saṃchinddhi mūrdhānam areḥ prasahya
c mayā nisṛṣṭena sudarśanena
vajreṇa śakro namucer ivāreḥ
a kirātarūpī bhagavān yayā ca
tvayā mahatyā paritoṣito 'bhūt
c tāṃ tvaṃ dhṛtiṃ vīra punar gṛhītvā
sahānubandhaṃ jahi sūtaputram
a tato mahīṃ sāgaramekhalāṃ tvaṃ
sapattanāṃ grāmavatīṃ samṛddhām
c prayaccha rājñe nihatārisaṃghāṃ
yaśaś ca pārthātulam āpnuhi tvam
d sa evam ukto 'tibalo mahātmā
d cakāra buddhiṃ hi vadhāya sauteḥ
d karṇaṃ puraskṛtya nadanti sarve
d tavāstram urvyāṃ pratihatya vīrāḥ
d kuru prayatnaṃ bharatapravīra
d dravanty amī sṛñjayasomakāś ca
d dṛṣṭvā ca karṇaṃ samare prahṛṣṭaṃ
d tvāṃ cāpi dṛṣṭvā parihīyamānam
a saṃcodito bhīmajanārdanābhyāṃ
smṛtvā tadātmānam avekṣya sattvam
c mahātmanaś cāgamane viditvā
prayojanaṃ keśavam ity uvāca
a prāduṣkaromy eṣa mahāstram ugraṃ
śivāya lokasya vadhāya sauteḥ
c tan me 'nujānātu bhavān surāś ca
brahmā bhavo brahmavidaś ca sarve
d iti smoktvā pāṇḍavaḥ savyasācī
d namaskṛtvā brahmaṇe so 'mitātmā
a ity ūcivān brāhmam asahyam astraṃ
prāduścakre manasā saṃvidheyam
b tad asya hatvā virarāja karṇo
b muktvā śarān megha ivāmbudhārāḥ
b samīkṣya karṇena kirīṭinas tu
b tathājimadhye vihitaṃ tad astram
b tato 'marṣī balavān krodhadīpto
b bhīmo 'bravīd arjunaṃ satyasaṃdham
b nanu tv āhur veditāraṃ mahāstraṃ
b brāhmaṃ vidheyaṃ paramaṃ janās tat
b punar yuktāstram abhitaḥ kirīṭinn
b iti smokto 'yojayat savyasācī
c tato diśaś ca pradiśaś ca sarvāḥ
samāvṛṇot sāyakair bhūritejāḥ
d gāṇḍīvamuktair bhujagair ivograir
d divākarāṃśupratimair jvaladbhiḥ
e sasarja bāṇān bharatarṣabho 'pi
śataṃśatān ekavad āśuvegān
f prācchādayan karṇarathaṃ kṣaṇena
f yugāntavahnyarkakaraprakāśāḥ
f tataś ca śūlāni parasvadhāni
f cakrāṇi nārācaśatāni caiva
f niścakramur ghoratarāṇi yodhās
f tato nyahanyanta samantato 'pi
f chinnaṃ śiraḥ kasya cid ājimadhye
f papāta yodhasya parasya kāyāt
f bhayena so 'py āśu papāta bhūmāv
f anyaḥ pranaṣṭaḥ patitaṃ vilokya
f anyasya sāsir nipapāta kṛtto
f yodhasya bāhuḥ karihastatulyaḥ
f anyasya savyaḥ saha carmaṇā ca
f kṣuraprakṛttaḥ patito dharaṇyām
f evaṃ samastān api yodhamukhyān
f vidhvaṃsayām āsa kirīṭamālī
f śaraiḥ śarīrāntakaraiḥ sughorair
f dauryodhanaṃ sainyam aśeṣam eva
a vaikartanenāpi tathājimadhye
sahasraśo bāṇagaṇā visṛṣṭāḥ
c te ghoṣiṇaḥ pāṇḍavam abhyupeyuḥ
parjanyamuktā iva vāridhārāḥ
a sa bhīmasenaṃ ca janārdanaṃ ca
kirīṭinaṃ cāpy amanuṣyakarmā
c tribhis tribhir bhīmabalo nihatya
nanāda ghoraṃ mahatā svareṇa
a sa karṇabāṇābhihataḥ kirīṭī
bhīmaṃ tathā prekṣya janārdanaṃ ca
c amṛṣyamāṇaḥ punar eva pārthaḥ
śarān daśāṣṭau ca samudbabarha
a suṣeṇam ekena śareṇa viddhvā
śalyaṃ caturbhis tribhir eva karṇam
c tataḥ sumuktair daśabhir jaghāna
sabhāpatiṃ kāñcanavarmanaddham
a sa rājaputro viśirā vibāhur
vivājisūto vidhanur viketuḥ
c tato rathāgrād apatat prabhagnaḥ
paraśvadhaiḥ śāla ivābhikṛttaḥ
a punaś ca karṇaṃ tribhir aṣṭabhiś ca
dvābhyāṃ caturbhir daśabhiś ca viddhvā
c catuḥśatān dviradān sāyudhīyān
hatvā rathān aṣṭaśataṃ jaghāna
e sahasram aśvāṃś ca punaś ca sādīn
aṣṭau sahasrāṇi ca pattivīrān
f karṇaṃ sasūtaṃ sarathāśvaketum
f adṛśyam añjogatibhiś ca cakre
f tato 'krośan kuravo vadhyamānā
f dhanaṃjayenādhirathiṃ samantāt
f muñcābhividdhyārjunam āśu karṇa
f bāṇaiḥ purā hanti kurūn samagrān
f sa coditaḥ sarvayatnena karṇo
f mumoca bāṇān subahūn abhīkṣṇam
f te pāṇḍupāñcālagaṇān nijaghnur
f marmacchidaḥ śoṇitamāṃsadigdhāḥ
f tāv uttamau sarvadhanurdharāṇāṃ
f mahābalau sarvasapatnasāhau
f nijaghnatuś cāhitasainyam ugrāv
f anyonyam apy astravidau mahāstraiḥ
f athopayātas tvarito didṛkṣur
f mantrauṣadhābhyāṃ virujo viśalyaḥ
f kṛtaḥ suhṛdbhir bhiṣajāṃ variṣṭhair
f yudhiṣṭhiras tatra suvarṇavarmā
f tatropayātaṃ yudhi dharmarājaṃ
f dṛṣṭvā mudā sarvabhūtāny anandan
f rāhor vimuktaṃ vimalaṃ samagraṃ
f candraṃ yathaivābhyuditaṃ tathaiva
f nāsatyadasrātrisutodbhavādyair
f aṣṭāṅgavidyāśramam udvahadbhiḥ
f ābaddhapaṭṭo vraṇalāghavena
f yathā sureśo ditijaiḥ kṣatāṅgaḥ
a dṛṣṭvājimukhyāv atha yudhyamānau
didṛkṣavaḥ śūravarāv arighnau
c karṇaṃ ca pārthaṃ ca niyamya vāhān
khasthā mahīsthāś ca janāvatasthuḥ
d sa kārmukajyātalasaṃnipātaḥ
d sumuktabāṇas tumulo babhūva
d ghnatos tathānyonyam iṣupravaikair
d dhanaṃjayasyādhiratheś ca rājan
a tato dhanurjyā sahasātikṛṣṭā
sughoṣam ācchidyata pāṇḍavasya
c tasmin kṣaṇe sūtaputras tu pārthaṃ
samācinot kṣudrakāṇāṃ śatena
a nirmuktasarpapratimaiś ca tīkṣṇais
tailapradhautaiḥ khagapatravājaiḥ
c ṣaṣṭyā nārācair vāsudevaṃ bibheda
tadantaraṃ somakāḥ prādravanta
d pūṣātmajo marmasu nirbibheda
d marutsutaṃ cāyutaśaḥ śarāgraiḥ
d kṛṣṇaṃ ca pārthaṃ ca tathā dhvajaṃ ca
d pārthānujān somakān pātayaṃś ca
d prācchādayaṃs te niśitaiḥ pṛṣatkair
d jīmūtasaṃghā nabhasīva sūryam
d āgacchatas tān viśikhair anekair
d vyaṣṭambhayat sūtaputraḥ kṛtāstraḥ
d tair astam astraṃ vinihatya sarvaṃ
d jaghāna teṣāṃ rathavājināgān
d tathā tu sainyapravarāṃś ca rājann
d abhyardayan mārgaṇaiḥ sūtaputraḥ
d te bhinnadehā vyasavo nipetuḥ
d karṇeṣubhir bhūmitale stanantaḥ
d kruddhena siṃhena yathāśvayūthyā
d mahābalā bhīmabalena tadvat
d punaś ca pāñcālavarās tathānye
d tadantaraṃ karṇadhanaṃjayābhyām
d praskandanto balinaḥ sādhumuktaiḥ
d karṇena bāṇair nihatāḥ prasahya
d jayaṃ tu matvā vipulaṃ tvadīyās
d talān nijaghnuḥ siṃhanādāṃś ca neduḥ
d sarve hy amanyanta vaśe kṛtau tau
d karṇena kṛṣṇāv iti te vineduḥ
d tato navajyāṃ sudṛḍhāṃ kirīṭī
d svabāhuvikṣepaṇajāṃ pragṛhya
d samādade gāṇḍive kṣiprakārī
d nimeṣamātreṇa mahādhanuṣmān
d jyācchedanaṃ jyāvidhānaṃ ca tasya
d naivāvabudhyat sūtaputro laghutvāt
d pārthasya saṃkhye dviṣatāṃ nihantus
d tad adbhūtaṃ tatra babhūva rājan
a tato dhanurjyām avadhamya śīghraṃ
śarān astān ādhirather vidhamya
b pārtho 'pi tāṃ jyām avadhāya tūrṇaṃ
b śarāsanajyām ādhirather vidhamya
c susaṃrabdhaḥ karṇaśarakṣatāṅgo
raṇe pārthaḥ somakān pratyagṛhṇāt
d jyāṃ cānumṛjyābhyahanat talatre
d bāṇāndhakāraṃ tv akarot kṣaṇena
d śalyaṃ ca karṇaṃ ca kurūṃś ca sarvān
d bāṇair avidhyad yugapat kirīṭī
e na pakṣiṇaḥ saṃpatanty antarikṣe
kṣepīyasāstreṇa kṛte 'ndhakāre
f vāyur viyatsthair amaraiḥ sametya
f vyuvāha bāṇān avalokayadbhiḥ
a śalyaṃ ca pārtho daśabhiḥ pṛṣatkair
bhṛśaṃ tanutre prahasann avidhyat
c tataḥ karṇaṃ dvādaśabhiḥ sumuktair
viddhvā punaḥ saptabhir abhyavidhyat
a sa pārthabāṇāsanaveganunnair
dṛḍhāhataḥ patribhir ugravegaiḥ
c vibhinnagātraḥ kṣatajokṣitāṅgaḥ
karṇo babhau rudra ivātateṣuḥ
d prakrīḍamāno 'tha śmaśānamadhye
d raudre muhūrte rudhirārdragātraḥ
a tatas tribhiś ca tridaśādhipopamaṃ
śarair bibhedādhirathir dhanaṃjayam
c śarāṃs tu pañca jvalitān ivoragān
pravīrayām āsa jighāṃsur acyute
a te varma bhittvā puruṣottamasya
suvarṇacitraṃ nyapatan sumuktāḥ
c vegena gām āviviśuḥ suvegāḥ
snātvā ca karṇābhimukhāḥ pratīyuḥ
a tān pañcabhallais tvaritaiḥ sumuktais
tridhā tridhaikaikam athoccakarta
c dhanaṃjayas te nyapatan pṛthivyāṃ
mahāhayas takṣakaputrapakṣāḥ
a tataḥ prajajvāla kirīṭamālī
krodhena kakṣaṃ pradahann ivāgniḥ
b tathā vinunnāṅgam avekṣya kṛṣṇaṃ
b sarpeṣubhiḥ karṇabhujaprasṛṣṭaiḥ
c sa karṇam ākarṇavikṛṣṭasṛṣṭaiḥ
śaraiḥ śarīrāntakarair jvaladbhiḥ
e marmasv avidhyat sa cacāla duḥkhād
dhairyāt tu tasthāv atimātradhairyaḥ
f prāduścakārātha śarān mahātmā
f dehaṃ vicinvann iva sūtajasya
f śarās tu te kāñcanacitrapuṅkhāḥ
f saṃpetur urvyāṃ śataśo mahāntaḥ
a tataḥ śaraughaiḥ pradiśo diśaś ca
raviprabhā karṇarathaś ca rājan
c adṛśya āsīt kupite dhanaṃjaye
tuṣāranīhāravṛtaṃ yathā nabhaḥ
a sa cakrarakṣān atha pādarakṣān
puraḥsarān pṛṣṭhagopāṃś ca sarvān
b bhītā dravanti sma nihanyamānā
b maheṣubhiḥ pārthakarapraṇunnaiḥ
b tato 'rjuno vai bharatapravīro
b mahānubhāvaḥ samare nihantā
c duryodhanenānumatān arighnān
samuccitān surathān sārabhūtān
a dvisāhasrān samare savyasācī
kurupravīrān ṛṣabhaḥ kurūṇām
c kṣaṇena sarvān sarathāśvasūtān
nināya rājan kṣayam ekavīraḥ
a athāpalāyanta vihāya karṇaṃ
tavātmajāḥ kuravaś cāvaśiṣṭāḥ
c hatān avākīrya śarakṣatāṃś ca
lālapyamānāṃs tanayān pitṝṃś ca
d sarve praṇeśuḥ kuravo vihīnāḥ
d pārtheṣubhiḥ saṃparitapyamānāḥ
d suyodhanenātha punar variṣṭhāḥ
d pracoditāḥ karṇarathānuyāne
d bhoḥ kṣatriyāḥ śūratamāś ca sarve
d kṣātre ca dharme niratāḥ stha yūyam
d na yuktarūpaṃ bhavatāṃ samīpāt
d palāyanaṃ karṇam abhiprahāya
d tavātmajenāpi tathocyamānāḥ
d pārtheṣubhiḥ saṃparitapyamānāḥ
d naivāvatiṣṭhanta bhayād vivarṇāḥ
d kṣaṇena naṣṭāḥ pradiśo diśaś ca
a sa sarvataḥ prekṣya diśo viśūnyā
bhayāvadīrṇaiḥ kurubhir vihīnaḥ
c na vivyathe bhārata tatra karṇaḥ
pratīpam evārjunam abhyadhāvat
c mahārathaḥ sūtaputras tathāpi
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tato 'payātāḥ śarapātamātram
avasthitāḥ kuravo bhinnasenāḥ
c vidyutprakāśaṃ dadṛśuḥ samantād
dhanaṃjayāstraṃ samudīryamāṇam
a tad arjunāstraṃ grasate sma vīrān
viyat tathākāśam anantaghoṣam
c kruddhena pārthena tadāśu sṛṣṭaṃ
vadhāya karṇasya mahāvimarde
d karṇaḥ sughoreṣvasanaṃ dṛḍhajyaṃ
d visphārayitvā visṛjañ charaughān
d udīryamāṇaṃ sma kurūn dahantaṃ
d suvarṇapuṅkhair iṣubhir mahātmā
a rāmād upāttena mahāmahimnā
ātharvaṇenārivināśanena
c tad arjunāstraṃ vyadhamad dahantaṃ
pārthaṃ ca bāṇair niśitair nijaghne
a tato vimardaḥ sumahān babhūva
tasyārjunasyādhiratheś ca rājan
c anyonyam āsādayatoḥ pṛṣatkair
viṣāṇaghātair dvipayor ivograiḥ
d tato 'strasaṃghātasamāvṛtaṃ tadā
d babhūva rājaṃs tumulaṃ raṇājiram
d tat karṇapārthau śaravṛṣṭisaṃghair
d nirantaraṃ cakratur ambaraṃ tadā
d tad bāṇajālaikamayaṃ mahāstraṃ
d sarve 'drākṣuḥ kuravaḥ somakāś ca
d nānyaṃ ca bhūtaṃ dadṛśus tadā te
d bāṇāndhakāre tumule ca tasmin
d tatas tu tau vai puruṣapravīrau
d rājan varau sarvadhanurdharāṇām
d tyaktvātmadehau samare 'tighore
d prāptaśramau śatrudurāsadau hi
d dṛṣṭvā tu tau saṃprati saṃprayuktau
d parasparaṃ chidraniviṣṭadṛṣṭī
d devarṣigandharvagaṇāḥ sayakṣāḥ
d saṃtuṣṭuvus tau pitaraś ca hṛṣṭāḥ
d tau saṃdadhānāv aniśaṃ sma rājan
d samasyantau cāpi śarān anekān
d saṃdarśayantau yudhi mārgān vicitrān
d dhanurdharāṇāṃ pravarau kṛtāstrau
d tayor evaṃ yudhyator ājimadhye
d sūtātmajo 'bhūd adhikaḥ kadā cit
d pārthaḥ kadā cit tv adhikaḥ kirīṭī
d vīryāstrasamyagbalalāghavais tu
d dṛṣṭvā tatas taṃ yudhi saṃprahāraṃ
d parasparasyāntaraprekṣiṇo ye
d ghoraṃ tadā durviṣahaṃ raṇe 'nyair
d yodhāḥ sarve vismayam abhyagacchan
d tato 'tha bhūtāny antarikṣe sthitāni
d karṇārjunau tau praśaśaṃsur narendra
d bhoḥ karṇa sādhv arjuna sādhu ceti
d hṛṣṭāḥ procuḥ saṃghaśaḥ prītimantaḥ
d tasmin vimarde rathavājināgāḥ
d padātisaṃghā vasudhāṃ vyakampayan
d tatas tu pātālatale śayāno
d nāgo 'śvasenaḥ kṛtavairo 'rjunena
d rājaṃs tadā khāṇḍavadāhamukto
d kṛtvā suvegaṃ vasudhātalasthaḥ
d athotpapātordhvagatir javena
d saṃdṛśya karṇārjunayor vimardam
d ayaṃ hi kālo 'sya durātmano vai
d pārthasya vairapratiyātanāya
d saṃcintya tūṇaṃ praviveśa caiva
d karṇasya rājañ śararūpadhārī
d tato 'strasaṃghātasamākulaṃ tadā
d babhūva jālaṃ vitatāṃśujālam
d tat karṇapārthau śarasaṃghavṛṣṭibhir
d nirantaraṃ cakratur ambaraṃ tadā
d tadbāṇajālaikamayaṃ mahāntaṃ
d sarve 'trasan kuravaḥ somakāś ca
d nānyat kiṃ cid dadṛśuḥ saṃpatad vai
d bāṇāndhakāre tumule 'timātram
d tatas tau puruṣavyāghrau sarvalokadhanurdharau
d tyaktaprāṇau raṇe vīrau yuddhaśramam upāgatau
d samutkṣepair vīkṣamāṇau siktau candanavāriṇā
d satālavyajanair divyair divisthair apsarogaṇaiḥ
d śakrasūryakarābjābhyāṃ pramārjitamukhāv ubhau
d karṇas tu pārthaṃ na viśeṣayad yadā
d dṛḍhaṃ ca pārthena śarair nipīḍitaḥ
d tataḥ sa karṇaḥ śaravikṣatāṅgo
d mano dadhe hy ekaśayasya tasya
a tato ripughnaṃ samadhatta karṇaḥ
susaṃśitaṃ sarpamukhaṃ jvalantam
c raudraṃ śaraṃ saṃyati supradhautaṃ
pārthārtham atyarthacirāya guptam
a sadārcitaṃ candanacūrṇaśāyinaṃ
suvarṇanālīśayanaṃ mahāviṣam
b ākarṇapūrṇaṃ pravikṛṣya karṇaḥ
b pārthonmukhaṃ saṃdadhe tigmamanyum
c pradīptam airāvatavaṃśasaṃbhavaṃ
śiro jihīrṣur yudhi phalgunasya
c mumoca śīghraṃ sa ripupramāthī
d tataḥ prajajvāla diśo nabhaś ca
d ulkāś ca ghorāḥ sahasā nipetuḥ
d tasmiṃs tu nāge dhanuṣi prayukte
d hāhākṛtāḥ sarvalokāḥ saśakrāḥ
d na cāpi taṃ bubudhe sūtaputro
d bāṇe praviṣṭaṃ yogabalena nāgam
d daśaśatanayano 'hiṃ dṛśya bāṇe praviṣṭaṃ
d nihata iti suto me srastagātro babhūva
d jalajakusumayoniḥ śreṣṭhabhāvo 'jitātmā
d tridaśapatim avocan mā vyadhiṣṭhā jaye śrīḥ
d sa sūtaputras tam apāṅgadeśe
d avāṅmukhaṃ saṃdhayati sma roṣāt
d na taṃ sma jānāti mahānubhāvam
d apāṅgadeśābhiniviṣṭam ājau
a tam abravīn madrarājo mahātmā
vaikartanaṃ prekṣya hi saṃhiteṣum
c na karṇa grīvām iṣur eṣa prāpsyate
saṃlakṣya saṃdhatsva śaraṃ śiroghnam
a athābravīt krodhasaṃraktanetraḥ
karṇaḥ śalyaṃ saṃdhiteṣuḥ prasahya
c na saṃdhatte dviḥ śaraṃ śalya karṇo
na mādṛśāḥ śāṭhyayuktā bhavanti
d prāptasya pārthaḥ praṇatāḥ sva svāhāḥ
d saṃsthāpya kṛṣṇena punas tadīyam sic
a tathaivam uktvā visasarja taṃ śaraṃ
balāhakaṃ varṣaghanābhipūjitam
c hato 'si vai phalguna ity avocat
tatas tvarann ūrjitam utsasarja
a saṃdhīyamānaṃ bhujagaṃ dṛṣṭvā karṇena mādhavaḥ
c ākramya syandanaṃ padbhyāṃ balena balināṃ varaḥ
a avagāḍhe rathe bhūmau jānubhyām agaman hayāḥ
c tataḥ śaraḥ so 'bhyahanat kirīṭaṃ tasya dhīmataḥ
d sa sāyakaḥ karṇabhujābhisṛṣṭo
d hutāśanārkapratimaḥ sughoraḥ
d guṇacyutaḥ prājvalad antarikṣe
d kurvan sīmantaṃ nabhaso bhīmarūpaḥ
d taṃ prekṣya dīptaṃ yudhi mādhavas tu
d tvarānvitaḥ kaṃsaripuḥ salīlam
d padā viniṣpiṣya rathottamaṃ taṃ
d prāveśayaj jagatīṃ kiṣkumātram
d kṣitiṃ gatā jānubhis te tu vāhās
d tataḥ śaraḥ so 'bhyahanat kirīṭam
d tam āpatantaṃ jvalitaṃ nirīkṣya
d viyadgataṃ vṛṣṇikulapravīraḥ
d rathasya cakraṃ sahasā nipīḍya
d pañcāṅgulaṃ majjayati sma vīraḥ
d tato 'ntarikṣe sumahān ninādaḥ
d saṃpūjanārthaṃ madhusūdanasya
d divyāś ca vācaḥ sahasā babhūvur
d divyāni puṣpāṇy atha siṃhanādāḥ
d tasmiṃs tathā vai dharaṇīṃ nimagne
d rathe prayogān madhusūdanasya
dA tataḥ śaraḥ so 'bhyahanat kirīṭaṃ
dA tasyendradattaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ ca dhīmataḥ
a athārjunasyottamagātrabhūṣaṇaṃ
dharāviyaddyosalileṣu viśrutam
c balāstrasargottamayatnamanyubhiḥ
śareṇa mūrdhnaḥ sa jahāra sūtajaḥ
a divākarendujvalanagrahatviṣaṃ
suvarṇamuktāmaṇijālabhūṣitam
c puraṃdarārthaṃ tapasā prayatnataḥ
svayaṃ kṛtaṃ yad bhuvanasya sūnunā
a mahārharūpaṃ dviṣatāṃ bhayaṃkaraṃ
vibhāti cātyarthasukhaṃ sugandhi tat
c nijaghnuṣe devaripūn sureśvaraḥ
svayaṃ dadau yat sumanāḥ kirīṭine
a harāmbupākhaṇḍalavittagoptṛbhiḥ
pinākapāśāśanisāyakottamaiḥ
b kṣataṃ nayad rudragaṇaiḥ pinākinā
b sahāyavān pāvakasaṃnibhaiḥ śaraiḥ
c surottamair apy aviṣahyam ardituṃ
prasahya nāgena jahāra yad vṛṣaḥ
c ciraṃ dhṛtenāditineha rājan
d sa duṣṭabhāvo vitathapratijñaḥ
d kirīṭam abhyāhanad arjunasya
d viśuddhajāmbūnadaratnabhūṣitaṃ
d pārthottamāṅgād aharat tarasvī
d tad dhemajālāvatataṃ sughoṣaṃ
d jājvalyamānaṃ nipapāta bhūmau
a tad uttameṣūn mathitaṃ viṣāgninā
pradīptam arciṣmad abhikṣiti priyam
c papāta pārthasya kirīṭam uttamaṃ
divākaro 'stād iva parvatāj jvalan
a tataḥ kirīṭaṃ bahuratnamaṇḍitaṃ
jahāra nāgo 'rjunamūrdhato balāt
c gireḥ sujātāṅkurapuṣpitadrumaṃ
mahendravajraḥ śikharaṃ yathottamam
a mahī viyad dyauḥ salilāni vāyunā
yathā vibhinnāni vibhānti bhārata
c tathaiva śabdo bhuvaneṣv abhūt tadā
janā vyavasyan vyathitāś ca caskhaluḥ
a tataḥ samudgrathya sitena vāsasā
svamūrdhajānavyathitaḥ sthito 'rjunaḥ
b vinā kirīṭaṃ śuśubhe sa pārthaḥ
b śyāmo yuvā śaila ivāstaśṛṅgaḥ
c vibhāti saṃpūrṇamarīcibhāsvatā
śirogatenodayaparvato yathā
d tato 'rjunaḥ karṇam avakragair navaiḥ
d suvarṇapuṅkhaiḥ sudṛḍhair ayasmayaiḥ
d yamāgnidaṇḍapratimaiḥ stanāntare
d parābhinat krauñcam ivādrim agnijaḥ
d tataḥ śarāvāpam apāsya sūtajo
d dhanuś ca tac chakraśarāsanopamam
d tatāpa tasthau na mumoha caskhale
d dṛḍhāhataḥ saṃś ca punas tatas tataḥ
d na hy arjunas taṃ vyasane tadeyivān
d nihantum āryaḥ puruṣavrate sthitaḥ
d tatas tam indrāvarajo 'pi saṃbhramād
d uvāca kiṃ pāṇḍava he pramādyasi
d naivāhitānāṃ satataṃ vipaścitaḥ
d kṣaṇaṃ pratīkṣanty api durbalīyasām
d viśeṣato 'rīn vyasaneṣu paṇḍito
d nihatya dharmaṃ ca yaśaś ca vindati
d tam ekavīraṃ tava cāhitaṃ sadā
d tvarasva karṇaṃ sahasābhimarditum
d purā samarthaḥ samupaiti sūtajo
d vidhya tvam enaṃ namuciṃ yathā hariḥ
d tathāstu devety abhipūjya satvaraṃ
d janārdanaṃ karṇam avidhyad arjunaḥ
d śarottamaiḥ sarvakurūttamas tvaraṃs
d tathā yathā śambaram ambarādhipaḥ
d gokarṇā sumukhī kṛtena iṣuṇā goputrasaṃpreṣitā
d gośabdātmajabhūṣaṇaṃ suvihitaṃ suvyaktago 'suprabham
d dṛṣṭvā gogatakaṃ jahāra mukuṭaṃ gośabdagopūri vai
d gokarṇāsanamardanaś ca na yayāv aprāpya mṛtyor vaśam
a balāhakaḥ karṇabhujeritas tato
hutāśanārkapratimadyutir mahān
c mahoragaḥ kṛtavairo 'rjunena
kirīṭam āsādya samutpapāta
d kirīṭam ākṛṣya tathārjunasya
d mahoragaḥ kṛtavairaḥ sa tūrṇam
d yathāsṛjat pārthavadhāya karṇaḥ
d samīkṣya sarpaḥ punar eti karṇam
d vyāvṛtya tasmāc ca tataḥ kirīṭāt
d tam utpatantaṃ sa kirīṭam īkṣya
d pārtho 'bravīd vāsudevaṃ mahātmā
d taṃ cāpi dagdhvā tapanīyacitraṃ
d kirīṭam ākṛṣya tad arjunasya
d punaḥ sa matvā praviveśa tūṇaṃ
d pṛṣṭaś ca karṇena tato 'bravīd idam
d muktas tvayāhaṃ na samīkṣya karṇa
d śiro hṛtaṃ yan na mayārjunasya
d samīkṣya māṃ muñca raṇe tvam āśu
d hantāsmi śatruṃ tava cātmanaś ca
d ity evam ukto yudhi sūtaputras
d tam abravīt ko bhavān ugrarūpaḥ
d tataḥ sa nāgaḥ prahasann ivāhitaṃ
d papāta cāvekṣya tam arjunas tvaran
a tam abravīd viddhi kṛtāgasaṃ me
kṛṣṇādya mātur vadhajātavairam
b nāgaḥ
b nāgo 'smi śvetaḥ kṛtavairo 'rjunena
b mātā purā hy utpatitā nabhastaḥ
b yadi svayaṃ vajradharo 'sya goptā
b tathāpi yātā pitṛrājaveśmani
b karṇaḥ
b na nāga karṇo 'dya raṇe parasya
b balaṃ samāsthāya jayaṃ bubhūṣet
b na saṃdadhe dviḥ śaram eva nāga
b yady arjunānāṃ śatam eva hanyāt
b tam āha karṇaḥ punar eva nāgaṃ
b tadājimadhye ravisūnusattamaḥ
b vyālāstrasargottamayatnamanyubhir
b hantāsmi pārthaṃ susukhī vraja tvam
b sa evam ukto yudhi nāgarājaḥ
b karṇena dīno hy asahaṃs tu vākyam
b svayaṃ prāyāt pārthavadhāya rājan
b kṛtveṣurūpaṃ vijighāṃsur arjunam
b tato 'bravīd vāsudevaṃ sa pārthaḥ
b dāśārha ko hy eṣa mahān hi nāgaḥ
b tvaṃ māvamaṃsthāḥ kuru me vaco 'dya
b nihanmi śatruṃ tava muñca māṃ tvam
b tvayā na saṃdhānavatāhaṃ muktas
b tenāpi kṛṣṇena ca vañcito 'si
b mamaiva bāhvos tu balena śakto
b yuddhe 'rjunānāṃ śatam eva hantum
b vrataṃ yad atrāpi na vetsi me bhavān
b vadāmi kṛṣṇasya samakṣam eva
b eṣo 'dya hatvā yudhi pāṇḍavānāṃ
b hantāsmi yuddhe hi svativikrameṇa
b etad vrataṃ jānamānaḥ prayātu
b nāgaḥ
b kiṃ vai kṛtā pāṇḍave te pratijñā
b jitvā ahaṃ yuddhagataṃ yamāya
b karṇaḥ
b pravartituṃ śvo bhavanaṃ prayātum
b mitrārtham etan mama jānato 'pi
b yatnaḥ śarīre yad apāti vīra
b hantā yadi tvaṃ raṇamūrdhni pārthaṃ
b nāgaḥ
b kiṃ vābhiśakto 'smi ha kauraveyaiḥ
b sakṛd eva hi vai karṇa vāsudevaṃ mahābalam
b aham eva haniṣyāmi pārthaṃ caiva na saṃśayaḥ
c tataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ pārtham uvāca saṃkhye
mahoragaṃ kṛtavairaṃ jahi tvam
c tavājimadhye ravisūnusattamo
c nāgāstram aṅge sudṛḍhaṃ vimuktam
d tam utpatantaṃ dvipadāṃ variṣṭho
d dṛṣṭvā vacaḥ pārtham uvāca kṛṣṇaḥ
d mahoragaṃ pāṇḍava paśya paśya
d prayojitaṃ tvan nidhanārtham ugram
a sa evam ukto madhusūdanena
gāṇḍīvadhanvā ripuṣūgradhanvā
c uvāca ko nv eṣa mamādya nāgaḥ
svayaṃ ya āgād garuḍasya vaktram
d tato 'bravīd vāsudevaṃ mahātmā
d dāśārha ko nv eṣa mamādya nāgaḥ
d dhanuścyutaḥ śara iva śīghravegaḥ
d svayaṃ ya āyād garuḍasyeva vaktram
 kṛṣṇa uvāca
a yo 'sau tvayā khāṇḍave citrabhānuṃ
saṃtarpayānena dhanurdhareṇa
c viyadgato bāṇanikṛttadeho
hy anekarūpo nihatāsya mātā
d sa eṣa te vairam anusmaran vai
d tvām adya cāyāti vadhāya pārtha
d nabhaścyutāṃ prajvalitāṃ maholkāṃ
d paśyainam āyāntam amitrasāha
a tatas tu jiṣṇuḥ parihṛtya śeṣāṃś
ciccheda ṣaḍbhir niśitaiḥ sudhāraiḥ
c nāgaṃ viyat tiryag ivotpatantaṃ
sa chinnagātro nipapāta bhūmau
d hate tu tasmin bhujage kirīṭinā
d svayaṃ vibhuḥ pārthivabhūtalād atha
d samujjahārāśu mahābhujaḥ sa taṃ
d rathaṃ bhujābhyāṃ puruṣottamaḥ punaḥ
a tasmin muhūrte daśabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ
śilāśitair barhiṇavājitaiś ca
c vivyādha karṇaḥ puruṣapravīraṃ
dhanaṃjayaṃ tiryag avekṣamāṇam
a tato 'rjuno dvādaśabhir vimuktair
ākarṇamuktair niśitaiḥ samarpya
c nārācam āśīviṣatulyavegam
ākarṇapūrṇāyatam utsasarja
a sa citravarmeṣuvaro vidārya
prāṇān nirasyann iva sādhu muktaḥ
c karṇasya pītvā rudhiraṃ viveśa
vasuṃdharāṃ śoṇitavājadigdhaḥ
a tato vṛṣo bāṇanipātakopito
mahorago daṇḍavighaṭṭito yathā
c tathāśukārī vyasṛjac charottamān
mahāviṣaḥ sarpa ivottamaṃ viṣam
a janārdanaṃ dvādaśabhiḥ parābhinan
navair navatyā ca śarais tathārjunam
b saṃchādya bāṇaiḥ sa tu gārdhrapatraiḥ
c śareṇa ghoreṇa punaś ca pāṇḍavaṃ
vibhidya karṇo 'bhyanadaj jahāsa ca
d jagarja cājīvarhi 
harṣayan kurun
a tam asya harṣaṃ mamṛṣe na pāṇḍavo
bibheda marmāṇi tato 'sya marmavit
c paraṃ śaraiḥ patribhir indravikramas
tathā yathendro balam ojasāhanat
a tataḥ śarāṇāṃ navatīr navārjunaḥ
sasarja karṇe 'ntakadaṇḍasaṃnibhāḥ
c śarair bhṛśāyastatanuḥ pravivyathe
tathā yathā vajravidārito 'calaḥ
c purā ruṣā gotrasamūhabhidyatā
a maṇipravekottamavajrahāṭakair
alaṃkṛtaṃ cāsya varāṅgabhūṣaṇam
c praviddham urvyāṃ nipapāta patribhir
dhanaṃjayenottamakuṇḍale 'pi ca
a mahādhanaṃ śilpivaraiḥ prayatnataḥ
kṛtaṃ yad asyottamavarma bhāsvaram
c sudīrghakālena tad asya pāṇḍavaḥ
kṣaṇena bāṇair bahudhā vyaśātayat
d tasyeṣubhiḥ khaṇḍitakuṇḍalāntaḥ
d parikṣataś cābhyadhikaṃ tadānīm
d sa lohitāṅgaśravaṇaś cakāśe
d salohitāṅgaśravaṇo yathā divi
a sa taṃ vivarmāṇam athottameṣubhiḥ
śaraiś caturbhiḥ kupitaḥ parābhinat
c sa vivyathe 'tyartham ariprahārito
yathāturaḥ pittakaphānilavraṇaiḥ
a mahādhanurmaṇḍalaniḥsṛtaiḥ śitaiḥ
kriyāprayatnaprahitair balena ca
c tatakṣa karṇaṃ bahubhiḥ śarottamair
bibheda marmasv api cārjunas tvaran
a dṛḍhāhataḥ patribhir ugravegaiḥ
pārthena karṇo vividhaiḥ śitāgraiḥ
c babhau girir gairikadhāturaktaḥ
kṣaran prapātair iva raktam ambhaḥ
a sāśvaṃ tu karṇaṃ sarathaṃ kirīṭī
samācinod bhārata vatsadantaiḥ
c pracchādayām āsa diśaś ca bāṇaiḥ
sarvaprayatnāt tapanīyapuṅkhaiḥ
a sa vatsadantaiḥ pṛthupīnavakṣāḥ
samācitaḥ smādhirathir vibhāti
c supuṣpitāśokapalāśaśālmalir
yathācalaḥ spandanacandanāyutaḥ
a śaraiḥ śarīre bahudhā samarpitair
vibhāti karṇaḥ samare viśāṃ pate
c mahīruhair ācitasānukandaro
yathā mahendraḥ śubhakarṇikāravān
a sa bāṇasaṃghān dhanuṣā vyavāsṛjan
vibhāti karṇaḥ śarajālaraśmivān
c salohito raktagabhastimaṇḍalo
divākaro 'stābhimukho yathā tathā
a bāhvantarād ādhirather vimuktān
bāṇān mahāhīn iva dīpyamānān
c vyadhvaṃsayann arjunabāhumuktāḥ
śarāḥ samāsādya diśaḥ śitāgrāḥ
d tataḥ sa karṇaḥ samavāpya dhairyaṃ
d bāṇān vimuñcan kupitāhikalpān
d vivyādha pārthaṃ daśabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ
d kṛṣṇaṃ ca ṣaḍbhiḥ kupitāhikalpaiḥ
d tato mahendrāśanitulyanisvanaṃ
d mahāśaraṃ sarpaviṣānalopamam
d ayasmayaṃ raudramahāstrasaṃmitaṃ
d mahāhave kṣeptumanā dhanaṃjayaḥ
d kālo hy adṛśyo nṛpa vipraśāpān
d nidarśayan karṇavadhaṃ bruvāṇaḥ
d bhūmis tu cakraṃ grasatīty avocat
d karṇasya tasmin vadhakāle 'bhyupete
d brāhmaṃ mahāstraṃ manasi pranaṣṭaṃ
d yad bhārgavo 'py asya dadau mahātmā
d vāmaṃ cakraṃ grasate medinī sma
d prāpte tasmin vadhakāle nṛvīra
d tato ratho ghūrṇitavān narendra
d śāpāt tadā brāhmaṇasattamasya
d na cāsya ghoraṃ pratibhāti cāstraṃ
d yad bhārgavo hy abhyavadan mahātmā
d cakraṃ tu vāmaṃ grasate 'sya bhūmir
d yathāsya kālo mṛtyupatir vyatiṣṭhat
d tato ratho bhārata ghūrṇate sma
d śāpāt tadā brāhmaṇasattamasya
d prāptaṃ vadhaṃ śaṃsati cāpy athāstraṃ
d praṇaśyamānaṃ dvijamukhyaśāpāt
a tataś cakramapatat tasya bhūmau
sa vihvalaḥ samare sūtaputraḥ
b savedikaś caitya ivātimātraḥ
b supuṣpito bhūmitale nimagnaḥ
c ghūrṇe rathe brāhmaṇasyābhiśāpād
rāmād upātte 'pratibhāti cāstre
d chinne śare sarpamukhe ca ghore
d pārthena tasmin viṣasāda karṇaḥ
a amṛṣyamāṇo vyasanāni tāni
hastau vidhunvan sa vigarhamāṇaḥ
c dharmapradhānān abhipāti dharma
ity abruvan dharmavidaḥ sadaiva
d vayaṃ ca nityaṃ prayatāma dharmaṃ
d cartuṃ yathāśakti yathāśrutaṃ ca
e mamāpi nimno 'dya na pāti bhaktān
manye na nityaṃ paripāti dharmaḥ
a evaṃ bruvan praskhalitāśvasūto
vicālyamāno 'rjunaśastrapātaiḥ
c marmābhighātāc calitaḥ kriyāsu
punaḥ punar dharmam agarhad ājau
a tataḥ śarair bhīmatarair avidhyat tribhir āhave
c haste karṇas tadā pārtham abhyavidhyac ca saptabhiḥ
d tataḥ śarair bhīmatarair avidhyat
d stanāntare kṛṣṇadhanaṃjayau saḥ
a tato 'rjunaḥ saptadaśa tigmatejān ajihmagān
c indrāśanisamān ghorān asṛjat pāvakopamān
a nirbhidya te bhīmavegā nyapatan pṛthivītale
c kampitātmā tathā karṇaḥ śaktyā ceṣṭām adarśayat
a balenātha sa saṃstabhya brahmāstraṃ samudairayat
c aindrāstram arjunaś cāpi tad dṛṣṭvābhinyamantrayat
a gāṇḍīvaṃ jyāṃ ca bāṇāṃś ca anumantrya dhanaṃjayaḥ
c asṛjac charavarṣāṇi varṣāṇīva puraṃdaraḥ
a tatas tejomayā bāṇā rathāt pārthasya niḥsṛtāḥ
c prādurāsan mahāvīryāḥ karṇasya ratham antikāt
a tān karṇas tv agrato 'bhyastān moghāṃś cakre mahārathaḥ
c tato 'bravīd vṛṣṇivīras tasminn astre vināśite
a visṛjāstraṃ paraṃ pārtha rādheyo grasate śarān
c brahmāstram arjunaś cāpi saṃmantryātha prayojayat
a chādayitvā tato bāṇaiḥ karṇaṃ prabhrāmya cārjunaḥ
c tasya karṇaḥ śaraiḥ kruddhaś ciccheda jyāṃ sutejanaiḥ
d dvitīyāṃ ca tṛtīyāṃ ca caturthīṃ pañcamīṃ tathā
d ṣaṣṭhīm athāsya ciccheda saptamīṃ ca tathāṣṭamīm
d navamīṃ daśamīṃ cāsya tathā caikādaśīṃ vṛṣaḥ
d jyāśataṃ śatasaṃdhānaḥ sa karṇo nāvabudhyate
a tato jyām avadhāyānyām anumṛjya ca pāṇḍavaḥ
c śarair avākirat karṇaṃ dīpyamānaiḥ sahasraśaḥ
a tasya jyācchedanaṃ karṇo jyāvadhānaṃ ca saṃyuge
c nānvabudhyata śīghratvāt tad adbhutam ivābhavat
a astrair astrāṇi rādheyaḥ pratyahan savyasācinaḥ
c cakre cābhyadhikaṃ pārthāt svavīryaṃ pratidarśayan
a tataḥ kṛṣṇo 'rjunaṃ dṛṣṭvā karṇāstreṇābhipīḍitam
c abhyasyety abravīt pārtham ātiṣṭhāstram anuttamam
a tato 'nyam agnisadṛśaṃ śaraṃ sarpaviṣopamam
c aśmasāramayaṃ divyam anumantrya dhanaṃjayaḥ
a raudram astraṃ samādāya kṣeptukāmaḥ kirīṭavān
c tato 'grasan mahī cakraṃ rādheyasya mahāmṛdhe
d tato 'vatīrya rādheyo rathād āśu samudyataḥ
d cakraṃ bhujābhyām ālambya samutkṣeptum iyeṣa saḥ
d saptadvīpā vasumatī saśailavanakānanā
d gīrṇacakrā samutkṣiptā karṇena caturaṅgulam
a grastacakras tu rādheyaḥ kopād aśrūṇy avartayat
b arjunaṃ vīkṣya saṃrabdham idaṃ vacanam abravīt
b bho bho pārtha maheṣvāsa muhūrtaṃ paripālaya
c so 'bravīd arjunaṃ cāpi muhūrtaṃ kṣama pāṇḍava
d yāvac cakram idaṃ grastam uddharāmi mahītalāt
d kṣatradharmam avekṣasva kartum arhasi pāṇḍava
a madhye cakram avagrastaṃ dṛṣṭvā daivād idaṃ mama
c pārtha kāpuruṣācīrṇam abhisaṃdhiṃ vivarjaya
d na tvaṃ kāpuruṣācīrṇaṃ mārgam āsthātum arhasi
d khyātas tvam asi kaunteya viśiṣṭo raṇakarmasu
d viśiṣṭataram eva tvaṃ kartum arhasi pāṇḍava
a prakīrṇakeśe vimukhe brāhmaṇe ca kṛtāñjalau
c śaraṇāgate nyastaśastre tathā vyasanage 'rjuna
a abāṇe bhraṣṭakavace bhraṣṭabhagnāyudhe tathā
c na śūrāḥ praharanty ājau na rājñe pārthivās tathā
e tvaṃ ca śūro 'si kaunteya tasmāt kṣama muhūrtakam
f na vimuñcanti śastrāṇi śūrāḥ sādhuvrate sthitāḥ
f tvaṃ ca śūratamo loke sādhuvṛttaś ca pāṇḍava
f abhijño yuddhadharmāṇāṃ tasmāt kṣama mama kṣaṇam
f divyāstravid ameyātmā kārtavīryasamo yudhi
a yāvac cakram idaṃ bhūmer uddharāmi dhanaṃjaya
c na māṃ rathastho bhūmiṣṭham asajjaṃ hantum arhasi
e na vāsudevāt tvatto vā pāṇḍaveya bibhemy aham
f smṛtvā tu dharmaṃ śūrāṇāṃ muhūrtaṃ pratipālaya
a tvaṃ hi kṣatriyadāyādo mahākulavivardhanaḥ
c smṛtvā dharmopadeśaṃ tvaṃ muhūrtaṃ kṣama pāṇḍava
d yāvat karomi dhanuṣaṃ sajjaṃ matimatāṃ vara
 saṃjaya uvāca
a athābravīd vāsudevo rathastho
rādheya diṣṭyā smarasīha dharmam
b dharme hi gṛddhāḥ satataṃ hi pārthās
b tebhyas tato vṛddhim asau dadāti
b dharmād apetāḥ paribaddhalobhās
b tasmād gatā vai kuravo vināśam
c prāyeṇa nīcā vyasaneṣu magnā
nindanti daivaṃ kukṛtaṃ na tat tat
a yad draupadīm ekavastrāṃ sabhāyām
ānāyya tvaṃ caiva suyodhanaś ca
c duḥśāsanaḥ śakuniḥ saubalaś ca
na te karṇa pratyabhāt tatra dharmaḥ
a yadā sabhāyāṃ kaunteyam anakṣajñaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
b kaitavāt sauvalo 'jaiṣīd dayāluṃ sarvajantuṣu
c akṣajñaḥ śakunir jetā tadā dharmaḥ kva te gataḥ
d yad bhīmasenaṃ sarpaiś ca viṣayuktaiś ca bhojanaiḥ
d ācarat tvanmate rājā kva te dharmas tadā gataḥ
d yad vāraṇāvate pārthān suptāñ jatugṛhe tadā
d ādīpayas tvaṃ rādheya kva te dharmas tadā gataḥ
d vanavāse vyatīte ca karṇa varṣe trayodaśe
d na prayacchasi yad rājyaṃ kva te dharmas tadā gataḥ
a yadā rajasvalāṃ kṛṣṇāṃ duḥśāsanavaśe sthitām
c sabhāyāṃ prāhasaḥ karṇa kva te dharmas tadā gataḥ
d yad anāryaiḥ purā kṛṣṇāṃ kliśyamānām anāgasam
d vinaṣṭāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kṛṣṇe śāśvataṃ narakaṃ gatāḥ
d patim anyaṃ vṛṇīṣveti vadaṃs tvaṃ gajagāminīm
d upaprekṣasi rādheya kva te dharmas tadā gataḥ
a rājyalubdhaḥ punaḥ karṇa samāhvayasi pāṇḍavam
c gāndhārarājam āśritya kva te dharmas tadā gataḥ
d yadābhimanyuṃ bahavo yuddhe jaghnur mahārathāḥ
d parivārya raṇe bālaṃ kva te dharmas tadā gataḥ
d yady eṣa dharmas tatra na vidyate hi
d kiṃ sarvathā tāluviśoṣaṇena
d adyaiva dharmāṇi vidhatsva sūta
d tathāpi naivādya vimokṣyase tvam
d nalo hy akṣair nirjitaḥ puṣkareṇa
d punar yathā rājyam avāpa vīryāt
d prāptās tathā pāṇḍavā bāhuvīryāt
d sarve samastāḥ parivṛttalobhāḥ
d nihatya śatrūn samare pravṛddhān
d sasomakā rājyam avāpnuyus te
d tathā gatā dhārtarāṣṭrā vināśaṃ
d dharmābhiguptaiḥ satataṃ nṛsiṃhaiḥ
d saṃjaya uvāca
d evam uktas tadā karṇo vāsudevena bhārata
d lajjayāvanato bhūtvā nottaraṃ kiṃ cid uktavān
d krodhāt prasphuramāṇauṣṭho dhanur udyamya bhārata
d yodhayām āsa vai pārthaṃ mahāvegaparākramaḥ
d tato 'bravīd vāsudevaḥ phalgunaṃ puruṣarṣabham
d divyāstreṇaiva nirbhidya pātayasva mahābala
a evam ukte tu rādheye vāsudevena pāṇḍavam
c manyur abhyāviśat tīvraḥ smṛtvā tat tad dhanaṃjayam
a tasya krodhena sarvebhyaḥ srotobhyas tejaso 'rciṣaḥ
c prādurāsan mahārāja tad adbhutam ivābhavat
a taṃ samīkṣya tataḥ karṇo brahmāstreṇa dhanaṃjayam
c abhyavarṣat punar yatnam akarod rathasarjane
d brahmāstreṇaiva taṃ pārtho vavarṣa śaravṛṣṭibhiḥ
d karṇaś cāpi tato rājan krodharaktāntalocanaḥ
e tad astram astreṇāvārya prajahārāsya pāṇḍavaḥ
a tato 'nyad astraṃ kaunteyo dayitaṃ jātavedasaḥ
c mumoca karṇam uddiśya tat prajajvāla vai bhṛśam
a vāruṇena tataḥ karṇaḥ śamayām āsa pāvakam
c jīmūtaiś ca diśaḥ sarvāś cakre timiradurdināḥ
a pāṇḍaveyas tv asaṃbhrānto vāyavyāstreṇa vīryavān
c apovāha tadābhrāṇi rādheyasya prapaśyataḥ
d tatrādbhutaṃ bhārata sūtaputraś
d cakre cakre bhūmim anupraviṣṭe
d yad yodhayat pāṇḍavam ugravegaṃ
d vivyādha cainaṃ daśabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ
d tato 'tividdho bharatapravīraḥ
d karṇena rājan samare 'rjunas tu
d babhūva kopena bhṛśaṃ pradīpto
d ghṛtāvasiktaḥ sadasīva vahniḥ
d tataḥ śaraṃ mahāghoraṃ jvalantam iva pāvakam
d ādade pāṇḍuputrasya sūtaputro jighāṃsayā
d yojyamāne tatas tasmin bāṇe dhanuṣi pūjite
d cacāla pṛthivī rājan saśailavanakānanā
d vavau saśarkaro vāyur diśaś ca rajasā vṛtāḥ
d hāhākāraś ca saṃjajñe surāṇāṃ divi bhārata
d tam iṣuṃ saṃdhitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sūtaputreṇa māriṣa
d viṣādaṃ paramaṃ jagmuḥ pāṇḍavā dīnacetasaḥ
d sa sāyakaḥ karṇabhujapramuktaḥ
d śakrāśaniprakhyaruciḥ śitāgraḥ
d bhujāntaraṃ prāpya dhanaṃjayasya
d viveśa valmīkam ivoragottamaḥ
d sa gāḍhaviddhaḥ samare mahātmā
d vighūrṇamānaḥ ślathahastagāṇḍivaḥ
d cacāla bībhatsur amitramardanaḥ
d kṣiteḥ prakampe ca yathācalottamaḥ
d tadantaraṃ prāpya vṛṣo mahāratho
d rathāṅgam urvīgatam ujjihīrṣuḥ
d rathād avaplutya nigṛhya dorbhyāṃ
d śaśāka daivān na mahābalo 'pi
d tataḥ kirīṭī pratilabhya saṃjñāṃ
d jagrāha bāṇaṃ yamadaṇḍakalpam
d dīpto 'rjunaḥ prāñjalikaṃ mahātmā
d tato 'bravīd vāsudevo 'pi pārtham
d chindhy asya mūrdhānam areḥ śareṇa
d na yāvad ārohati vai rathaṃ vṛṣaḥ
d tathaiva saṃpūjya sa tad vacaḥ prabhos
d tataḥ kṣuraṃ prajvalitaṃ pragṛhya
d jaghāna kakṣām amalārkavarṇāṃ
d mahārathe rathacakre vimagne
a taṃ hastikakṣyāpravaraṃ ca bāṇaiḥ
suvarṇamuktāmaṇivajramṛṣṭam
c kālaprayatnottamaśilpiyatnaiḥ
kṛtaṃ surūpaṃ vitamaskam uccaiḥ
a ūrjaskaraṃ tava sainyasya nityam
amitravitrāsanam īḍyarūpam
c vikhyātam ādityasamasya loke
tviṣā samaṃ pāvakabhānucandraiḥ
a tataḥ kṣureṇādhiratheḥ kirīṭī
suvarṇapuṅkhena śitena yattaḥ
c śriyā jvalantaṃ dhvajam unmamātha
mahārathasyādhirather mahātmā
a yaśaś ca dharmaś ca jayaś ca māriṣa
priyāṇi sarvāṇi ca tena ketunā
c tadā kurūṇāṃ hṛdayāni cāpatan
babhūva hāheti ca nisvano mahān
d dṛṣṭvā dhvajaṃ taṃ patitaṃ pṛthivyāṃ
d kurupravīreṇa nikṛttam āśu
d nāśaṃsire sūtaputrasya sarve
d jayaṃ janā bhārata ye tvadīyāḥ
a atha tvaran karṇavadhāya pāṇḍavo
mahendravajrānaladaṇḍasaṃnibham
c ādatta pārtho 'ñjalikaṃ niṣaṅgāt
sahasraraśmer iva raśmim uttamam
a marmacchidaṃ śoṇitamāṃsadigdhaṃ
vaiśvānarārkapratimaṃ mahārham
c narāśvanāgāsuharaṃ tryaratniṃ
ṣaḍvājam añjogatim ugravegam
a sahasranetrāśanitulyatejasaṃ
samānakravyādam ivātiduḥsaham
c pinākanārāyaṇacakrasaṃnibhaṃ
bhayaṃkaraṃ prāṇabhṛtāṃ vināśanam
d surendrasenāpatiśaktisaṃnibham
d jagrāha pārthas tam atiprahṛṣṭo
d yo devasaṃghair api durnivāryaḥ
d saṃpūjito yaḥ satataṃ mahātmā
d devāsurān yo vijayen maheṣuḥ
d yaṃ vai prakṛṣṭaṃ prasamīkṣya yuddhe
d cacāla sarvaṃ sacarācaraṃ jagat
d svasti jagat syād ṛṣayaḥ pracukruśus
d tam udyataṃ prekṣya mahāhaveṣum
d tatas tu taṃ vai śaram aprameyaṃ
d gāṇḍīvadhanvā dhanuṣi nyayojayat
a yuktvā mahāstreṇa pareṇa mantravid
vikṛṣya gāṇḍīvam uvāca sasvanam
c ayaṃ mahāstro 'pratimo dhṛtaḥ śaraḥ
śarīrabhic cāsuharaś ca durhṛdaḥ
a tapo 'sti taptaṃ guravaś ca toṣitā
mayā yad iṣṭaṃ suhṛdāṃ tathā śrutam
c anena satyena nihantv ayaṃ śaraḥ
sudaṃśitaḥ karṇam ariṃ mamājitaḥ
d dharmātmā satyasaṃdhaś ca dharmarājo dayāparaḥ
d jitendriyaḥ satyavādī tathainaṃ jahi sūtajam
a ity ūcivāṃs taṃ sa mumoca bāṇaṃ
dhanaṃjayaḥ karṇavadhāya ghoram
c kṛtyām atharvāṅgirasīm ivogrāṃ
dīptām asahyāṃ yudhi mṛtyunāpi
a bruvan kirīṭī tam atiprahṛṣṭo
ayaṃ śaro me vijayāvaho 'stu
c jighāṃsur arkendusamaprabhāvaḥ
karṇaṃ samāptiṃ nayatāṃ yamāya
d tato vimukto balinā maheṣuḥ
d prajvālayām āsa diśo nabhaś ca
a teneṣuvaryeṇa kirīṭamālī
prahṛṣṭarūpo vijayāvahena
c jighāṃsur arkendusamaprabheṇa
cakre viṣaktaṃ ripum ātatāyī
d sainyāny anekāni ca vipramohya
d gāṇḍīvamuktair vijayena bhallaiḥ
d tenārjunaḥ sannahanīyamadhyāc
d chiro 'harat sūtaputrasya rājan
d chinnaṃ papātāñjalikena tūrṇaṃ
d kāyo 'sya paścād dharaṇīṃ jagāma
d tato 'rjunas tasya śiro jahāra
d vṛtrasya vajreṇa yathā mahendraḥ
d śarottamenāñjalikena rājaṃs
d tadā mahāstrapratimantritena
d pārtho 'parāhṇe śira uccakarta
d vaikartanasyātha mahendrasūnuḥ
d tat prāpatac cāñjalikena chinnam
d athāsya kāyo nipapāta paścāt
a tad udyatādityasamānavarcasaṃ
śarannabhomadhyagabhāskaropamam
b śareṇa karṇasya śiro jahāra
c varāṅgam urvyām apatac camūpater
divākaro 'stād iva raktamaṇḍalaḥ
a tad asya dehī satataṃ sukhoditaṃ
svarūpam atyartham udārakarmaṇaḥ
c pareṇa kṛcchreṇa śarīram atyajad
gṛhaṃ maharddhīva sasaṅgam īśvaraḥ
a śarair vibhugnaṃ vyasu tad vivarmaṇaḥ
papāta karṇasya śarīram ucchritam
c sravadvraṇaṃ gairikatoyavisravaṃ
girer yathā vajrahataṃ śiras tathā
a dehāt tu karṇasya nipātitasya
tejo dīptaṃ khaṃ vigāhyācireṇa
c tad adbhutaṃ sarvamanuṣyayodhāḥ
paśyanti rājan nihate sma karṇe
d tataḥ śaṅkhān pāṇḍavā dadhmur uccair
d dṛṣṭvā karṇaṃ pātitaṃ phālgunena
d tathaiva kṛṣṇaś ca dhanaṃjayaś ca
d hṛṣṭau tadā dadhmatur āśu śaṅkhau
d athāntarikṣe 'pi vigāhya sūryaṃ
d viveśa tejo jvalitaṃ hi tasya
d hṛtottamāṅgaṃ ca śarīram ājau
d papāta karṇasya śarāvakīrṇam
a taṃ somakāḥ prekṣya hataṃ śayānaṃ
prītā nādaṃ saha sainyair akurvan
c tūryāṇi cājaghnur atīva hṛṣṭā
vāsāṃsi caivādudhuvur bhujāṃś ca
d saṃvardhayantaś ca narendrayodhāḥ
d pārthaṃ samājagmur atīva hṛṣṭāḥ
e balānvitāś cāpy apare hy anṛtyann
anyonyam āśliṣya nadanta ūcuḥ
a dṛṣṭvā tu karṇaṃ bhuvi niṣṭanantaṃ
hataṃ rathāt sāyakenāvabhinnam
c mahānilenāgnim ivāpaviddhaṃ
yajñāvasāne śayane niśānte
d rarāja karṇasya śiro nikṛttam
d astaṃ gataṃ bhāskarasyeva bimbam
d hatottamāṅgaś ca sa tasya dehaḥ
d pariplutaḥ śoṇitaughaprasekaiḥ
d rarāja karṇasya śarāvakīrṇaḥ
d svaraśmijātāvatato yathārkaḥ
d pratāpya senāṃ khalu pāṇḍavīṃ raṇe
d śarāṃśubhiḥ pāvakatulyadīptibhiḥ
d kirīṭikālena tu karṇabhāskaro
d vyanīyatāstaṃ divasāvasāne
d tad ānanaṃ sūtapurasya rājan
d vibhrājate padmam ivāpanālam
a śarair ācitasarvāṅgaḥ śoṇitaughapariplutaḥ
c vibhāti dehaḥ karṇasya svaraśmibhir ivāṃśumān
a pratāpya senām āmitrīṃ dīptaiḥ śaragabhastibhiḥ
c balinārjunakālena nīto 'staṃ karṇabhāskaraḥ
a astaṃ gacchan yathādityaḥ prabhām ādāya gacchati
c evaṃ jīvitam ādāya karṇasyeṣur jagāma ha
a aparāhṇe parāhṇasya sūtaputrasya māriṣa
c chinnam añjalikenājau sotsedham apatac chiraḥ
a upary upari sainyānāṃ tasya śatros tad añjasā
c śiraḥ karṇasya sotsedham iṣuḥ so 'pāharad drutam
d tac chiro bharataśreṣṭha śobhayām āsa medinīm
d yadṛcchayā mahārāja āditya iva gāṃ gataḥ
d taṃ dṛṣṭvā samaravimardalabdhanidraṃ
d daṣṭoṣṭhaṃ rudhiraparītakātarākṣam
d rādheyaṃ rathavarapṛṣṭhasaṃniṣaṇṇaṃ
d hīnāṃśur divasakaro muhūrtam āsīt
d niḥśabdatūryaṃ hatayaudhamukhyaṃ
d praśāntadarpaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasainyam
d na śobhate sūryasutena hīnaṃ
d vṛndaṃ grahāṇām iva candrahīnam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a karṇaṃ tu śūraṃ patitaṃ pṛthivyāṃ
śarācitaṃ śoṇitadigdhagātram
c dṛṣṭvā śayānaṃ bhuvi madrarājaś
chinnadhvajenāpayayau rathena
a karṇe hate kuravaḥ prādravanta
bhayārditā gāḍhaviddhāś ca saṃkhye
c avekṣamāṇā muhur arjunasya
dhvajaṃ mahāntaṃ vapuṣā jvalantam
d hate tu karṇe kuravaḥ prādravanta bhayārditāḥ
d gāḍhaviddhāś ca saṃkhye te bāṇair gāṇḍīvadhanvanā
d avekṣamāṇāḥ pārthasya dhvajaṃ bhīṣaṇavānaram
d pratīpasainyahantāraṃ prādravaṃs te diśo daśa
d karṇe hate pārthabhayāt pradudruvur
d vaikartane dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ saśalyāḥ
d avekṣamāṇā muhur arjunasya
d ketuṃ mahāntaṃ yaśasā jvalantam
a sahasranetrapratimānakarmaṇaḥ
sahasrapatrapratimānanaṃ śubham
c sahasraraśmir dinasaṃkṣaye yathā
tathāpatat tasya śiro vasuṃdharām
d vyūḍhoraskaṃ kamalanayanaṃ taptahemāvabhāsaṃ
d karṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhuvi nipatitaṃ pārthabāṇābhitaptam
d pāṃsugrastaṃ malinam asakṛt putram anvīkṣamāṇo
d mandaṃ mandaṃ vrajati savitā mandiraṃ mandaraśmiḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a śalyas tu karṇārjunayor vimarde
balāni dṛṣṭvā mṛditāni bāṇaiḥ
c duryodhanaṃ yāntam avekṣamāṇo
saṃdarśayad bhārata yuddhabhūmim
d nipātite cādhirathau mahārathe
d dhvaja ye somakapāṇḍavaiś ca
d yayau sa tenaiva rathena tūrṇaṃ
d helīkṛtaḥ sṛñjayasomakaiś ca
d śalyas tu karṇe nihate kirīṭinā
d trastaṃ balaṃ prasamīkṣyārtarūpam
d yayau hate cādhirathau padānuge
d rathena saṃcchinnaparicchadena
a nipātitasyandanavājināgaṃ
