c duryodhano 'śrupratipūrṇanetro
muhur muhur nyaśvasad ārtarūpaḥ
d dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
d kathaṃ nu karṇārjunayor vimarde
d dagdhasya raudre 'hani vidrutasya
d babhūva rūpaṃ kurusṛñjayānāṃ
d balasya bāṇonmathitasya saṃkhye
a karṇaṃ tu śūraṃ patitaṃ pṛthivyāṃ
śarācitaṃ śoṇitadigdhagātram
c yadṛcchayā sūryam ivāvanisthaṃ
didṛkṣavaḥ saṃparivārya tasthuḥ
a prahṛṣṭavitrastaviṣaṇṇavismṛtās
tathāpare śokagatā ivābhavan
c pare tvadīyāś ca paraspareṇa
yathā yathaiṣāṃ prakṛtis tathābhavan
a praviddhavarmābharaṇāmbarāyudhaṃ
dhanaṃjayenābhihataṃ hataujasam
c niśamya karṇaṃ kuravaḥ pradudruvur
hatarṣabhā gāva ivākulākulāḥ
d bhīmaś ca bhīmena mahāsvanena
d nādaṃ kṛtvā rodasī kampayānaḥ
d āsphoṭayan valgate nṛtyate ca
d hate karṇe trāsayan dhārtarāṣṭrān
d tathaiva rājan somakāḥ sṛñjayāś ca
d śaṅkhān dadhmuḥ sasvajuś cāpi sarve
d parasparaṃ kṣatriyā hṛṣṭarūpāḥ
d sūtātmaje nihate vai tadānīm
a kṛtvā vimardaṃ bhṛśam arjunena
karṇaṃ hataṃ kesariṇeva nāgam
b tīrṇā pratijñā puruṣarṣabheṇa
b vairasyāntaṃ gatavāṃś cāpi pārthaḥ
c dṛṣṭvā śayānaṃ bhuvi madrarājo
bhīto 'pasarpat sarathaḥ suśīghram
a madrādhipaś cāpi vimūḍhacetās
tūrṇaṃ rathenāpahṛtadhvajena
c duryodhanasyāntikam etya śīghraṃ
saṃbhāṣya duḥkhārtam uvāca vākyam
a viśīrṇanāgāśvarathapravīraṃ
balaṃ tvadiyaṃ yamarāṣṭrakalpam
c anyonyam āsādya hataṃ mahadbhir
narāśvanāgair girikūṭakalpaiḥ
a naitādṛśaṃ bhārata yuddham āsīd
yathādya karṇārjunayor babhūva
c grastau hi karṇena sametya kṛṣṇāv
anye ca sarve tava śatravo ye
a daivaṃ tu yat tat svavaśaṃ pravṛttaṃ
tat pāṇḍavān pāti hinasti cāsmān
c tavārthasiddhyarthakarā hi sarve
prasahya vīrā nihatā dviṣadbhiḥ
a kuberavaivasvatavāsavānāṃ
tulyaprabhāvāmbupateś ca vīrāḥ
c vīryeṇa śauryeṇa balena caiva
tais taiś ca yuktā vipulair guṇaughaiḥ
a avadhyakalpā nihatā narendrās
tavārthakāmā yudhi pāṇḍaveyaiḥ
c tan mā śuco bhārata diṣṭam etat
paryāyasiddhir na sadāsti siddhiḥ
a etad vaco madrapater niśamya
svaṃ cāpanītaṃ manasā nirīkṣya
c duryodhano dīnamanā visaṃjñaḥ
punaḥ punar nyaśvasad ārtarūpaḥ
d saṃjaya uvāca
d dṛṣṭvā tu sainyaṃ vinivartyamānaṃ
d putreṇa te madrapatis tadānīm
d saṃtrastarūpaḥ parimūḍhacetā
d duryodhanaṃ vākyam idaṃ babhāṣe
d dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
d tasmiṃs tu karṇārjunayor vimarde
d dagdhasya raudre 'hani vidrutasya
d babhūva rūpaṃ kurusṛñjayānāṃ
d saṃjaya uvāca
d balasya bāṇonmathitasya kīdṛk
d śṛṇu rājann avahito yathā vṛtto mahākṣayaḥ
d ghoro manuṣyadehānām ājau naravarakṣayaḥ
d yatra karṇe hate pārthaḥ siṃhanādam athākarot
d tadā tava sutān rājann āviveśa mahad bhayam
d na saṃdhātum anīkāni na caivātha parākrame
d āsīd buddhir hate karṇe tava yodhasya kasya cit
d vaṇijo nāvi bhinnāyām agādhe hy aplavā yathā
d apāre pāram icchanto hate dvīpe kirīṭinā
d sūtaputre hate rājan vitrastāḥ śaravikṣatāḥ
d anāthā nātham icchanto mṛgāḥ siṃhair ivārditāḥ
d bhagnaśṛṅgā iva vṛṣā bhagnadaṣṭrā ivoragāḥ
d pratyapāyāma sāyāhne nirjitāḥ savyasācinā
d hatapravīrā vidhvastā nikṛttā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
d sūtaputre hate rājan putrās te vyadravan bhayāt
d viśastrakavacāḥ sarve kāṃdiśīkā vicetasaḥ
d anyonyam avamṛdnanto vīkṣyamāṇā bhayārditāḥ
d mām eva tūrṇaṃ bībhatsur mām eva ca vṛkodaraḥ
d abhiyātīti manvānāḥ petur mamluś ca saṃbhramāt
d hayān anye rathān anye gajān anye mahārathāḥ
d āhatya javasaṃpannāḥ pādātāḥ prādravan bhayāt
d kuñjaraiḥ syandanāḥ kṣuṇṇāḥ sādinaś ca mahārathaiḥ
d padātisaṃghāś cāśvaughaiḥ palāyadbhir bhayārditāḥ
d vyālataskarasaṃkīrṇe sārthahīnā yathā vane
d tathā tvadīyā nihate sūtaputre tadābhavan
d hatārohās tathā nāgāś chinnahastās tathā narāḥ
d sarvaṃ pārthamayaṃ lokaṃ saṃpaśyanto bhayāturāḥ
d tān prekṣya dravataḥ sarvān bhīmasenabhayārditān
d duryodhano 'tha svaṃ sūtaṃ vāhety uktvedam abravīt
d nātikramiṣyate pārtho dhanuṣpāṇir vyavasthitaḥ
d jaghanya eva sainyānāṃ śanair aśvān acodayat
d jaghanye yudhyamānaṃ hi kaunteyo māṃ na saṃśayaḥ
d notsaheta vyatikrāntuṃ velām iva mahodadhiḥ
d adyārjunaṃ sagovindaṃ māninaṃ ca vṛkodaram
d nihatya śiṣṭāñ śatrūṃś ca karṇasyānṛṇyam āpnuyām
d tac chrutvā kururājasya śūrārthasadṛśaṃ vacaḥ
d sūto hemaparicchannāñ śanair aśvān acodayat
d rathāśvagajahīnās tu pādātās tava māriṣa
d pañcaviṃśatisāhasrā yuddhāyaiva vyavasthitāḥ
d tān bhīmasenaḥ saṃkruddho dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥ
d balena caturaṅgeṇa parikṣipya nijaghnatuḥ
d pratyayudhyanta te sarve bhīmasenaṃ sapārṣatam
d pārthapārṣatayoś cānye jagṛhus tatra nāmanī
d akrudhyata tadā bhīmas tai raṇe pratyupasthitaiḥ
d so 'vatīrya rathāt tūrṇaṃ gadāpāṇir ayudhyata
d na tān rathastho bhūmiṣṭhān dharmāpekṣī vṛkodaraḥ
d yodhayām āsa kaunteyo bhujavīryam upāśritaḥ
d jātarūpaparicchannāṃ pragṛhya mahatīṃ gadām
d avadhīt tāvakān sarvān daṇḍapāṇir ivāntakaḥ
d padātino 'pi saṃrabdhās tyaktvā jīvitam ātmanaḥ
d bhīmam abhyadravan saṃkhye pataṃgā iva pāvakam
d āsādya bhīmasenaṃ tu saṃrabdhā yuddhadurmadāḥ
d vineśuḥ sahasā dṛṣṭvā bhūtagrāmā ivāntakam
d śyenavad vyacarad bhīmo gadāhasto mahābalaḥ
d pañcaviṃśatisāhasrāṃs tāvakānām apothayat
d hatvā tat puruṣānīkaṃ bhīmaḥ satyaparākramaḥ
d dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ puraskṛtya punas tasthau mahābalaḥ
d dhṛṣṭadyumno 'pi ca mahān amitragaṇamardanaḥ
d putraḥ pāñcālarājasya dhanurdharavaro yudhi
d vipralīnān rathāśvena padātīyān samantataḥ
d pañcaviṃśatisāhasrān avadhīn niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
d śarair nikṛttāḥ samare dhṛṣṭadyumnena tāvakāḥ
d pañcaviṃśatisāhasrāḥ kālam ārchan padātayaḥ
d hatvā tat puruṣānīkaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumno mahābalaḥ
d bhīmasenaṃ puraskṛtya na cirāt pratyadṛśyata
d taṃ pārāvatavarṇāśvaṃ kruddhaṃ kruddhāntakopamam
d dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ raṇe dṛṣṭvā tvadīyāḥ prādravan bhayāt
d dhanaṃjayo rathānīkam abhyavartata vīryavān
d mādrīputrau tu śakuniṃ sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥ
d javenābhyapatan hṛṣṭā nighnantaḥ saubalaṃ balam
d tasyāśvavārān subahūn vinihatya śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
d tam abhyadhāvaṃs tvaritās tato yuddham abhūt tadā
d dhanaṃjayo 'pi cābhyetya rathānīkaṃ tava prabho
d viśrutaṃ triṣu lokeṣu vyākṣipad gāṇḍivaṃ dhanuḥ
d kṛṣṇasārathim āyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā śvetahayaṃ ratham
d arjunaṃ cāpi yoddhāraṃ tvadīyāḥ prādravan bhayāt
d viprahīnā rathāśvena gajaiś ca parivarjitāḥ
d pañcaviṃśatisāhasrāḥ kālam ārchan padātayaḥ
d hatvā tat puruṣānīkaṃ pāñcālānāṃ mahārathaḥ
d putraḥ pāñcālarājasya dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārathaḥ
d bhīmasenaṃ puraskṛtya na cirāt pratyadṛśyata
d mahādhanurdharaḥ śrīmān amitragaṇasūdanaḥ
d pārāvatasavarṇāśvaṃ kovidāramahādhvajam
d dhṛṣṭadyumnarathaṃ dṛṣṭvā prādravanta bhayād bhṛśam
d gāndhārarājaṃ śīghrāstram anusṛtya yaśasvinau
d na cirāt pratyadṛśyetāṃ mādrīputrau sasātyakī
d cekitānaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca draupadeyāś ca māriṣa
d hatvā tvadīyaṃ sumahat sainyaṃ śaṅkhān athādhaman
d te sarve tāvakān prekṣya dravamāṇān parāṅmukhān
d abhyadravañ jighāṃsanto vṛṣāñ jitvā yathā vṛṣāḥ
d senāvaśeṣaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā tava sainyaṃ parāṅmukham
d vyavasthitaṃ savyasācī cukrodha balavat tadā
d dhanaṃjayo rathānīkam abhyavartata vīryavān
d viśrutaṃ triṣu lokeṣu vyākṣipad gāṇḍivaṃ dhanuḥ
d tata etāñ śarai rājan sahasrān samavārayan
d rajasā coddhatenātha na sma kiṃ cid vyadṛśyata
d anyakārīkṛte loke śarabhūte mahītale
d diśaḥ sarvā mahārāja tāvakāḥ prādravan bhayāt
d bhajyamāneṣu sainyeṣu kururājo viśāṃ pate
d parān abhimukhāṃś caiva sutas te samupādravat
d tato duryodhanaḥ sarvān ājuhāvātha pāṇḍavān
d yuddhāya bharataśreṣṭha devān iva purā baliḥ
d ta enam abhivartanta sahitāḥ samupādravan
d nānāśastrasṛjaḥ sarve bhartsayanto muhur muhuḥ
d duryodhano 'py asaṃbhrāntas tān arīn niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
d vyadhamad yudhi rājendra ghorarūpo viśāṃ pate
d tatrādbhutam apaśyāma tava putrasya pauruṣam
d yad enaṃ pāṇḍavāḥ sarve na śekur ativartitum
d nātidūrāpayātaṃ tu kṛtabuddhiṃ palāyane
d duryodhanaḥ svakaṃ sainyam apaśyac charavikṣatam
d tato 'vasthāpya rājendra kṛtabuddhis tavātmajaḥ
d harṣayann iva tān yodhān idaṃ vacanam abravīt
d na taṃ deśaṃ prapaśyāmi pṛthivyāṃ parvateṣu ca
d yatra yātān na vo hanyuḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kiṃ sṛtena vaḥ
d alpaṃ ca balam eteṣāṃ kṛṣṇau ca bhṛśavikṣatau
d yadi sarve 'tra tiṣṭhāmo dhruvo no vijayo bhavet
d viprayātāṃś ca no bhinnān pāṇḍavāḥ kṛtakilbiṣāḥ
d anusṛtya vadhiṣyanti śreyān naḥ samare vadhaḥ
d sukhaṃ sāṃgrāmiko mṛtyuḥ kṣatradharmeṇa yudhyatām
d mṛto duḥkhaṃ na jānīte pretya cānantyam aśnute
d śṛṇudhvaṃ kṣatriyāḥ sarve yāvantaḥ stha samāgatāḥ
d yadā śūraṃ ca bhīruṃ ca mārayaty antako yamaḥ
d ko nu mūḍho na yudhyeta mādṛśaḥ kṣatriyavrataḥ
d dviṣato bhīmasenasya kruddhasya vaśam eṣyatha
d pitāmahair ācaritaṃ na dharmaṃ hātum arhatha
d na hi dharmo 'sti pāpīyān kṣatriyasya palāyanāt
d na yuddhadharmāc chreyo 'nyaḥ panthāḥ svargasya kauravāḥ
d acireṇa hatā lokaṃ sarve yodhāḥ samāpnuta
d evaṃ bruvati te putre sainikā bhṛśavikṣatāḥ
d anavekṣyaiva tad vākyaṃ prādravan sarvatomukham
a taṃ dhyānamūkaṃ kṛpaṇaṃ bhṛśārtam
ārtāyanir dīnam uvāca vākyam
c paśyedam ugraṃ naravājināgair
āyodhanaṃ vīrahataiḥ prapannam
a mahīdharābhaiḥ patitair mahāgajaiḥ
sakṛt praviddhaiḥ śaraviddhamarmabhiḥ
c tair vihvaladbhiś ca gatāsubhiś ca
pradhvastayantrāyudhavarmayodhaiḥ
a vajrāpaviddhair iva cācalendrair
vibhinnapāṣāṇamṛgadrumauṣadhaiḥ
c praviddhaghaṇṭāṅkuśatomaradhvajaiḥ
sahemamālai rudhiraughasaṃplutaiḥ
a śarāvabhinnaiḥ patitaiś ca vājibhiḥ
śvasadbhir anyaiḥ kṣatajaṃ vamadbhiḥ
c dīnaiḥ stanadbhiḥ parivṛttanetrair
mahīṃ daśadbhiḥ kṛpaṇaṃ nadadbhiḥ
a tathāpaviddhair gajavājiyodhair
mandāsubhiś caiva gatāsubhiś ca
a balāpaviddhai rathavīrasaṃghaiḥ
c narāśvanāgaiś ca rathaiś ca marditair
mahī mahāvaitaraṇīva durdṛśā
a gajair nikṛttāparahastagātrair
udvepamānaiḥ patitaiḥ pṛthivyām
b viśīrṇadantaiḥ kṣatajaṃ vamadbhiḥ
b sphuradbhir ārtaiḥ karuṇaṃ raṇājire
b suyodhavarmāyudhapādagoptṛbhiḥ
b prakīrṇatūṇīrapatākaketubhiḥ
b suvarṇajālāvatatair bhṛśāhatair
b mahī viyad dyaur jaladair ivāvṛtā
b saṃyaṃtṛyodhācaraṇair mahāgajaiḥ
c yaśasvibhir nāgarathāśvayodhibhiḥ
padātibhiś cābhimukhair hataiḥ paraiḥ
e viśīrṇavarmābharaṇāmbarāyudhair
vṛtā niśāntair iva pāvakair mahī
a śaraprahārābhihatair mahābalair
avekṣyamāṇaiḥ patitaiḥ sahasraśaḥ
c pranaṣṭasaṃjñaiḥ punar ucchvasadbhir
mahī babhūvānugatair ivāgnibhiḥ
d karṇārjunābhyāṃ śarabhinnagātrair
d hataiḥ pravīraḥ kurusṛñjayānām
e divaś cyutair bhūr atidīptimadbhir
naktaṃ grahair dyaur amaleva dīptaiḥ
a śarās tu karṇārjunabāhumuktā
vidārya nāgāśvamanuṣyadehān
c prāṇān nirasyāśu mahīm atīyur
mahoragā vāsam ivābhito 'straiḥ
a hatair manuṣyāśvagajaiś ca saṃkhye
śarāvabhinnaiś ca rathair babhūva
c dhanaṃjayasyādhiratheś ca mārge
gajair agamyā vasudhātidurgā
a rathair vareṣūn mathitaiś ca yodhaiḥ
saṃsyūtasūtāśvavarāyudhadhvajaiḥ
c viśīrṇaśastrair vinikṛttabandhurair
nikṛttacakrākṣayugatriveṇubhiḥ
a vimuktayantrair nihatair ayasmayair
hatānuṣaṅgair viniṣaṅgabandhuraiḥ
c prabhagnanīḍair maṇihemamaṇḍitaiḥ
stṛtā mahī dyaur iva śāradair ghanaiḥ
a vikṛṣyamaṇair javanair alaṃkṛtair
hateśvarair ājirathaiḥ sukalpitaiḥ
c manuṣyamātaṅgarathāśvarāśibhir
drutaṃ vrajanto bahudhā vicūrṇitāḥ
a sahemapaṭṭāḥ parighāḥ paraśvadhāḥ
kaḍaṅgarāyomusalāni paṭṭiśāḥ
c petuś ca khaḍgā vimalā vikośā
gadāś ca jāmbūnadapaṭṭabaddhāḥ
a cāpāni rukmāṅgadabhūṣaṇāni
śarāś ca kārtasvaracitrapuṅkhāḥ
c ṛṣṭyaś ca pītā vimalā vikośāḥ
prāsāḥ sakhaḍgāḥ kanakāvabhāsāḥ
a chatrāṇi vālavyajanāni śaṅkhāḥ
srajaś ca puṣpottamahemacitrāḥ
c kuthāḥ patākāmbaraveṣṭitāś ca
kirīṭamālā mukuṭāś ca śubhrāḥ
a prakīrṇakā viprakīrṇāḥ kuthāś ca
pradhānamuktātaralāś ca hārāḥ
c āpīḍakeyūravarāṅgadāni
graiveyaniṣkāḥ sasuvarṇasūtrāḥ
a maṇyuttamā vajrasuvarṇamuktā
ratnāni coccāvacamaṅgalāni
c gātrāṇi cātyantasukhocitāni
śirāṃsi cendupratimānanāni
a dehāṃś ca bhogāṃś ca paricchadāṃś ca
tyaktvā manojñāni sukhāni cāpi
c svadharmaniṣṭhāṃ mahatīm avāpya
vyāptāṃś ca lokān yaśasā samīyuḥ
c gatā itaḥ svargalokāya rājan
d nivarta duryodhana yāntu sainikā
d vrajasva rājañ śibirāya mānada
d divākaro hy eṣa vilambate prabho
d punas tvam evātra narendra kāraṇam
a ity evam uktvā virarāma śalyo
duryodhanaḥ śokaparītacetāḥ
c hā karṇa hā karṇa iti bruvāṇa
ārto visaṃjño bhṛśam aśrunetraḥ
d yuddhāya rājan viniviṣṭabuddhiṃ
d hā karṇa hā karṇa iti bruvāṇam
a taṃ droṇaputrapramukhā narendrāḥ
sarve samāśvāsya saha prayānti
c nirīkṣamāṇā muhur arjunasya
dhvajaṃ mahāntaṃ yaśasā jvalantam
a narāśvamātaṅgaśarīrajena
raktena siktā rudhireṇa bhūmiḥ
c raktāmbarasrak tapanīyayogān
nārī prakāśā iva sarvagamyā
a pracchannarūpā rudhireṇa rājan
raudre muhūrte 'tivirājamānāḥ
c naivāvatasthuḥ kuravaḥ samīkṣya
pravrājitā devalokāś ca sarve
a vadhena karṇasya suduḥkhitās te
hā karṇa hā karṇa iti bruvāṇāḥ
c drutaṃ prayātāḥ śibirāṇi rājan
divākaraṃ raktam avekṣamāṇāḥ
a gāṇḍīvamuktais tu suvarṇapuṅkhaiḥ
śitaiḥ śaraiḥ śoṇitadigdhavājaiḥ
c śaraiś citāṅgo bhuvi bhāti karṇo
hato 'pi san sūrya ivāṃśumālī
a karṇasya dehaṃ rudhirāvasiktaṃ
bhaktānukampī bhagavān vivasvān
c spṛṣṭvā karair lohitaraktarūpaḥ
siṣṇāsur abhyeti paraṃ samudram
a itīva saṃcintya surarṣisaṃghāḥ
saṃprasthitā yānti yathāniketam
c saṃcintayitvā ca janā visasrur
yathāsukhaṃ khaṃ ca mahītalaṃ ca
a tad adbhutaṃ prāṇabhṛtāṃ bhayaṃkaraṃ
niśamya yuddhaṃ kuruvīramukhyayoḥ
c dhanaṃjayasyādhiratheś ca vismitāḥ
praśaṃsamānāḥ prayayus tadā janāḥ
a śaraiḥ saṃkṛttavarmāṇaṃ vīraṃ viśasane hatam
c gatāsum api rādheyaṃ naiva lakṣmīr vyamuñcata
d niṣṭaptahemavapuṣaṃ jvalanārkasamatviṣam
d jīvantam iva taṃ śūraṃ sarvabhūtāni menire
d hatasyāpi mahārāja sūtaputrasya saṃyuge
d vitresuḥ sarvabhūtāni siṃhasyevetare mṛgāḥ
d hato 'pi puruṣavyāghro vyāharann iva lakṣyate
d nābhavad vikṛtaṃ kiṃ cin mṛtasyāpi mahātmanaḥ
d cāruveṣadharaṃ rājañ cārumauliśirodharam
d tan mukhaṃ sūtaputrasya pūrṇacandrasamadyuti
a nānābharaṇavān rājan mṛṣṭajāmbūnadāṅgadaḥ
b varṣitvā śaravarṣāṇi pratāpya ripuvāhinīm
b śrīmān iva sahasrāṃśur jvalan sarvān pratāpya ca
b hato vaikartanaḥ karṇaḥ saputraḥ sahavāhanaḥ
b arthināṃ pakṣisaṃghasya kalpavṛkṣo nipātitaḥ
c hato vaikartanaḥ śete pādapo 'ṅkuravān iva
a kanakottamasaṃkāśaḥ pradīpta iva pāvakaḥ
b sa śāntaḥ puruṣavyāghraḥ pārthasāyakavāriṇā
b yathā hi jvalano dīpto jalam āsādya śāmyati
b karṇāgniḥ samare tadvat pārthameghena śāmitaḥ
b pragṛhya ca yaśo dīptaṃ suyuddhenātmano bhuvi
b visṛjya śaravarṣāṇi pratāpya ca diśo daśa
c saputraḥ puruṣavyāghraḥ saṃśāntaḥ pārthatejasā
e pratāpya pāṇḍavān rājan pāñcālāṃś cāstratejasā
a dadānīty eva yo 'vocan na nāstīty arthito 'rthibhiḥ
c sadbhiḥ sadā satpuruṣaḥ sa hato dvairathe vṛṣaḥ
a yasya brāhmaṇasāt sarvam ātmārthaṃ na mahātmanaḥ
c nādeyaṃ brāhmaṇeṣv āsīd yasya svam api jīvitam
a sadā nṝṇāṃ priyo dātā priyadāno divaṃ gataḥ
b sa pārthāstravinirdagdho gataḥ paramikāṃ gatim
b yam āśrityākarod vairaṃ sutas te sa gato divam
c ādāya tava putrāṇāṃ jayāśāṃ śarma varma ca
a hate sma karṇe sarito na sravanti
jagāma cāstaṃ kaluṣo divākaraḥ
c grahaś ca tiryag jvalitārkavarṇo
yamasya putro 'bhyudiyāya rājan
a nabhaḥ paphālātha nanāda corvī
vavuś ca vātāḥ paruṣātivelam
c diśaḥ sadhūmāś ca bhṛśaṃ prajajvalur
mahārṇavāś cukṣubhire ca sasvanāḥ
a sakānanāḥ sādricayāś cakampuḥ
pravivyathur bhūtagaṇāś ca māriṣa
c bṛhaspatī rohiṇīṃ saṃprapīḍya
babhūva candrārkasamānavarṇaḥ
a hate karṇe na diśo viprajajñus
tamovṛtā dyaur vicacāla bhūmiḥ
c papāta colkā jvalanaprakāśā
niśācarāś cāpy abhavan prahṛṣṭāḥ
a śaśiprakāśānanam arjuno yadā
kṣureṇa karṇasya śiro nyapātayat
c athāntarikṣe divi ceha cāsakṛd
babhūva hāheti janasya nisvanaḥ
a sa devagandharvamanuṣyapūjitaṃ
nihatya karṇaṃ ripum āhave 'rjunaḥ
c rarāja pārthaḥ parameṇa tejasā
vṛtraṃ nihatyeva sahasralocanaḥ

śarannabhomadhyagabhāskaratviṣā
c patākinā bhīmaninādaketunā
himenduśaṅkhasphaṭikāvabhāsinā
d mahendravāhapratimena tāv ubhau
d mahendravīryapratimānapauruṣau
e suvarṇamuktāmaṇivajravidrumair
alaṃkṛtenāpratimānaraṃhasā
a narottamau pāṇḍavakeśimardanāv

c raṇājire vītabhayau virejatuḥ
samānayānāv iva viṣṇuvāsavau
a tato dhanurjyātalaneminisvanaiḥ
prasahya kṛtvā ca ripūn hataprabhān
c saṃsādhayitvaiva kurūñ śaraughaiḥ
kapidhvajaḥ pakṣivaradhvajaś ca
c ubhau tadā yādavapāṇḍunandanau
e prasahya śaṅkhau dhamatuḥ sughoṣau
manāṃsy arīṇām avasādayantau
a suvarṇajālāvatatau mahāsvanau
himāvadātau parigṛhya pāṇibhiḥ
c cucumbatuḥ śaṅkhavarau nṛṇāṃ varau
varānanābhyāṃ yugapac ca dadhmatuḥ
a pāñcajanyasya nirghoṣo devadattasya cobhayoḥ
c pṛthivīm antarikṣaṃ ca dyām apaś cāpy apūrayat
d vitrastāś cābhavan sarve kuravo rājasattama
d śaṅkhaśabdena śūrasya mādhavasyārjunasya ca
a tau śaṅkhaśabdena ninādayantau
vanāni śailān sarito diśaś ca
c vitrāsayantau tava putrasenāṃ
yudhiṣṭhiraṃ nandayataḥ sma vīrau
a tataḥ prayātāḥ kuravo javena
śrutvaiva śaṅkhasvanam īryamāṇam
c vihāya madrādhipatiṃ patiṃ ca
duryodhanaṃ bhārata bhāratānām
a mahāhave taṃ bahu śobhamānaṃ
dhanaṃjayaṃ bhūtagaṇāḥ sametāḥ
c tadānvamodanta janārdanaṃ ca
prabhākarāv abhyuditau yathaiva
a samācitau karṇaśaraiḥ paraṃtapāv
ubhau vyabhātāṃ samare 'cyutārjunau
c tamo nihatyābhyuditau yathāmalau
śaśāṅkasūryāv iva raśmimālinau
a vihāya tān bāṇagaṇān athāgatau
suhṛdvṛtāv apratimānavikramau
c sukhaṃ praviṣṭau śibiraṃ svam īśvarau
sadasyahūtāv iva vāsavācyutau
a sadevagandharvamanuṣyacāraṇair
maharṣibhir yakṣamahoragair api
c jayābhivṛddhyā parayābhipūjitau
nihatya karṇaṃ paramāhave tadā
d saṃjaya uvāca
d hate vaikartane karṇe kuravo bhayapīḍitāḥ
d vīkṣamāṇā diśaḥ sarvāḥ palāyante sma sarvataḥ
d vīraṃ tu nihataṃ śrutvā śatrubhiḥ paramāhave
d sarve diśo 'nvakīryanta tāvakā bhayamohitāḥ
d tato 'vahāraṃ cakrus te rājan yodhāḥ samantataḥ
d vāryamāṇā bhayodvignās tava putreṇa bhārata
d teṣāṃ tu matam ājñāya putras te bharatarṣabha
d avahāraṃ tataś cakre śalyasyānumate nṛpa
d yodhair mahārathaiḥ sārdhaṃ vṛto bhārata tāvakaiḥ
d hatāvaśeṣais tvaritaḥ śibirāyaiva dudruve
d gāndhārāṇāṃ sahasreṇa śakuniḥ parivāritaḥ
d hatam ādhirathiṃ dṛṣṭvā śibirāyaiva dudruve
d kṛpaḥ śāradvato rājan nāgānīkena saṃvṛtaḥ
d mahatā meghakalpena śibirāyaiva dudruve
d aśvatthāmā tataḥ śūro viniḥśvasya muhur muhuḥ
d pāṇḍavānāṃ jayaṃ dṛṣṭvā śibirāyaiva dudruve
d saṃśaptakāvaśeṣeṇa balena mahatā vṛtaḥ
d suśarmāpi yayau rājan vīkṣamāṇo bhayāturān
d duryodhano 'pi nṛpatir hatasarvasva āturaḥ
d yayau śokasamāviṣṭaś cintayan vimanā bahu
d chinnadhvajena śalyas tu rathena rathināṃ varaḥ
d prayayau śibirāyaiva vīkṣamāṇo diśo daśa
d tato 'pare subahavo bhāratānāṃ mahārathāḥ
d prādravanta raṇaṃ hitvā bhayāviṣṭā vicetasaḥ
d aśrukaṇṭhā bhayodvignā vepamānāḥ suvihvalāḥ
d kuravaḥ pradrutāḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā karṇaṃ nipātitam
d praśaṃsanto 'rjunaṃ ke cit ke cit karṇaṃ mahārathāḥ
d vyadravanta diśo bhītāḥ kuravaḥ kurusattama
d teṣāṃ yodhasahasrāṇāṃ tāvakānāṃ mahāmṛdhe
d nāsīt tatra pumān kaś cid yo yuddhāya mano dadhe
d hate karṇe mahārāja nirāśāḥ kuravo 'bhavan
d jīviteṣv atha rājyeṣu dāreṣu ca dhaneṣu ca
d tān samānīya putras te yatnena mahatā vibho
d niveśāya mano dadhre duḥkhaśokasamanvitaḥ
d tasyājñāṃ śirasā te 'pi pratigṛhya viśāṃ pate
d vivarṇavadanā dīnā nyaviśanta mahārathāḥ
d yathānurūpaṃ pratipūjya tān atha
d praśasyamānāv atulaiś ca karmabhiḥ
d nanandatus tau sasuhṛdgaṇau tadā
d baliṃ niyamyeva sureśakeśavau
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tathā nipātite karṇe tava sainye ca vidrute
c āśliṣya pārthaṃ dāśārho harṣād vacanam abravīt
a hato balabhidā vṛtras tvayā karṇo dhanaṃjaya
c vadhaṃ vai karṇavṛtrābhyāṃ kathayiṣyanti mānavāḥ
a vajriṇā nihato vṛtraḥ saṃyuge bhūritejasā
c tvayā tu nihataḥ karṇo dhanuṣā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a tam imaṃ vikramaṃ loke prathitaṃ te yaśovaham
c nivedayāvaḥ kaunteya dharmarājāya dhīmate
a vadhaṃ karṇasya saṃgrāme dīrghakālacikīrṣitam
c nivedya dharmarājasya tvam ānṛṇyaṃ gamiṣyasi
d vartamāne tu yuddhe vai tava karṇasya cobhayoḥ
d draṣṭum āyodhanaṃ pūrvam āgato dharmanandanaḥ
d subhṛśaṃ gāḍhaviddhatvān nāśakat sthātum āhave
d tataḥ svaśibiraṃ yātaḥ sa rājā puruṣarṣabha
a tathety ukte keśavas tu pārthena yadupuṅgavaḥ
c paryavartayad avyagro rathaṃ rathavarasya tam
d evam uktvārjunaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ sainikān idam abravīt
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ yudhāmanyuṃ mādrīputrau vṛkodaram
c yuyudhānaṃ ca govinda idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a parān abhimukhā yattās tiṣṭhadhvaṃ bhadram astu vaḥ
c yāvad āvedyate rājñe hataḥ karṇo 'rjunena vai
d tāvad bhavadbhir yat tais tu bhavitavyaṃ narādhipaiḥ
a sa taiḥ śūrair anujñāto yayau rājaniveśanam
c pārtham ādāya govindo dadarśa ca yudhiṣṭhiram

d utthāya sa mahābāhuḥ punaḥ punar ariṃdamaḥ
d vāsudevārjunau premṇā punaś ca pariṣasvaje
d vāsudevaṃ ca vārṣṇeyaṃ papraccha kurunandanaḥ
a tato 'smai tad yathāvṛttaṃ vāsudevaḥ priyaṃvadaḥ
c kathayām āsa karṇasya nidhanaṃ yadunandanaḥ
a īṣad utsmayamānas tu kṛṣṇo rājānam abravīt
c yudhiṣṭhiraṃ hatāmitraṃ kṛtāñjalir athācyutaḥ
a diṣṭyā gāṇḍīvadhanvā ca pāṇḍavaś ca vṛkodaraḥ
c tvaṃ cāpi kuśalī rājan mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavau
a muktā vīrakṣayād asmāt saṃgrāmāl lomaharṣaṇāt
c kṣipram uttarakālāni kuru kāryāṇi pārthiva
a hato vaikartanaḥ krūraḥ sūtaputro mahābalaḥ
c diṣṭyā jayasi rājendra diṣṭyā vardhasi pāṇḍava
a yaḥ sa dyūtajitāṃ kṛṣṇāṃ prāhasat puruṣādhamaḥ
c tasyādya sūtaputrasya bhūmiḥ pibati śoṇitam
a śete 'sau śaradīrṇāṅgaḥ śatrus te kurupuṃgava
c taṃ paśya puruṣavyāghra vibhinnaṃ bahudhā śaraiḥ
d hatāmitrām imām urvīm anuśādhi mahābhuja
d yatto bhūtvā sahāsmābhir bhuṅkṣva bhogāṃś ca puṣkalān
d saṃjaya uvāca
d iti śrutvā vacas tasya keśavasya mahātmanaḥ
a yudhiṣṭhiras tu dāśārhaṃ prahṛṣṭaḥ pratyapūjayat
c diṣṭyā diṣṭyeti rājendra prītyā cedam uvāca ha
a naitac citraṃ mahābāho tvayi devakinandana
c tvayā sārathinā pārtho yat kuryād adya pauruṣam
d na tac citraṃ mahābāho yuṣmad bāhuprasādajam
a pragṛhya ca kuruśreṣṭhaḥ sāṅgadaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ bhujam
c uvāca dharmabhṛt pārtha ubhau tau keśavārjunau
a naranārāyaṇau devau kathitau nāradena ha
c dharmasaṃsthāpane yuktau purāṇau puruṣottamau
a asakṛc cāpi medhāvī kṛṣṇadvaipāyano mama
c kathām etāṃ mahābāho divyām akathayat prabhuḥ
a tava kṛṣṇa prabhāveṇa gāṇḍīvena dhanaṃjayaḥ
c jayaty abhimukhāñ śatrūn na cāsīd vimukhaḥ kva cit
a jayaś caiva dhruvo 'smākaṃ na tv asmākaṃ parājayaḥ
c yadā tvaṃ yudhi pārthasya sārathyam upajagmivān
d bhīṣmo droṇaś ca karṇaś ca mahātmā gautamaḥ kṛpaḥ
d anye ca bahavaḥ śūrā ye ca teṣāṃ padānugāḥ
d tvadbuddhyā nihate karṇe hatā govinda sarvathā
a evam uktvā mahārāja taṃ rathaṃ hemabhūṣitam
c dantavarṇair hayair yuktaṃ kālavālair mahārathaḥ
a āsthāya puruṣavyāghraḥ svabalenābhisaṃvṛtaḥ
c kṛṣṇārjunābhyāṃ vīrābhyām anumanya tataḥ priyam
a āgato bahuvṛttāntaṃ draṣṭum āyodhanaṃ tadā
c ābhāṣamāṇas tau vīrāv ubhau mādhavaphalgunau
a sa dadarśa raṇe karṇaṃ śayānaṃ puruṣarṣabham
b yathā kadambakusumaṃ kesaraiḥ sarvato vṛtam
b citaṃ śaraśataiḥ karṇaṃ dharmarājo dadarśa ha
b gandhatailāvasiktābhiḥ kāñcanībhiḥ sahasraśaḥ
b dīpikābhiḥ kṛtoddyotaṃ paśyate vai vṛṣaṃ tadā
b saṃchinnabhinnakavacaṃ bāṇaiś ca vidalīkṛtam
c gāṇḍīvamuktair viśikhaiḥ sarvataḥ śakalīkṛtam
a saputraṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā karṇaṃ rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
b saṃjātapratyayo 'tīva vīkṣya caivaṃ punaḥ punaḥ
c praśaśaṃsa naravyāghrāv ubhau mādhavapāṇḍavau
a adya rājāsmi govinda pṛthivyāṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ saha
c tvayā nāthena vīreṇa viduṣā paripālitaḥ
a hataṃ dṛṣṭvā naravyāghraṃ rādheyam abhimāninam
c nirāśo 'dya durātmāsau dhārtarāṣṭro bhaviṣyati
e jīvitāc cāpi rājyāc ca hate karṇe mahārathe
a tvatprasādād vayaṃ caiva kṛtārthāḥ puruṣarṣabha
c tvaṃ ca gāṇḍīvadhanvā ca vijayī yadunandana
e diṣṭyā jayasi govinda diṣṭyā karṇo nipātitaḥ
f trayodaśa samāstīrṇā jāgareṇa suduḥkhitāḥ
f svapsyāmo 'dya sukhaṃ rātrau tvatprasādān mahābhuja
a evaṃ sa bahuśo hṛṣṭaḥ praśaśaṃsa janārdanam
c arjunaṃ cāpi rājendra dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d saṃjaya uvāca
d dṛṣṭvā ca karṇaṃ nihataṃ saputraṃ pārthasāyakaiḥ
d punar jātam ivātmānaṃ mene kurukulodvahaḥ
d sametya ca mahārāja kuntīputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
d praśaśaṃsus tataḥ sarve rājāno bhūritejasaḥ
a tato bhīmaprabhṛtibhiḥ sarvaiś ca bhrātṛbhir vṛtam
c vardhayanti sma rājānaṃ harṣayuktā mahārathāḥ
a nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca pāṇḍavaś ca vṛkodaraḥ
c sātyakiś ca mahārāja vṛṣṇīnāṃ pravaro rathaḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca pāṇḍupāñcālasṛñjayāḥ
c pūjayanti sma kaunteyaṃ nihate sūtanandane
a te vardhayitvā nṛpatiṃ pāṇḍuputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
c jitakāśino labdhalakṣā yuddhaśauṇḍāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
a stuvantaḥ stavayuktābhir vāgbhiḥ kṛṣṇau paraṃtapau

c tava durmantrite rājann atītaṃ kiṃ nu śocasi
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
 evam etan mahac cāsīd yuddhaṃ paramadāruṇam
a śrutvā tad apriyaṃ rājan dhṛtarāṣṭro mahīpatiḥ
c papāta bhūmau niśceṣṭaḥ kauravyaḥ paramārtivān
e tathā satyavratā devī gāndhārī dharmadarśinī
f śuśoca bahulālāpaiḥ karṇasya nidhanaṃ yudhi
a taṃ pratyagṛhṇād viduro nṛpatiṃ saṃjayas tathā
c paryāśvāsayataś caivaṃ tāv ubhāv eva bhūmipam
a tathaivotthāpayām āsur gāndhārīṃ rājayoṣitaḥ
b sa daivaṃ paramaṃ matvā bhavitavyaṃ ca pārthivaḥ
b parāṃ pīḍāṃ samāśritya naṣṭacitto mahātapāḥ
b cintāśokaparītātmā na jajñe mohapīḍitaḥ
c tābhyām āśvāsito rājā tūṣṇīm āsīd vicetanaḥ
d idaṃ mahāyuddhamakhaṃ mahātmanor
d dhanaṃjayasyādhiratheś ca yaḥ paṭhet
d sa samyag iṣṭasya makhasya yat phalaṃ
d tad āpnuyāt saṃśravaṇāc ca bhārata
d makho hi viṣṇur bhagavān sanātano
d vahanti taṃ cāgnyanilendubhānavaḥ
d ato 'nasūyuḥ śṛṇute paṭhec ca yaḥ
d sa sarvalokāṃś ca jayet sukhī bhavet
d sarvatīrtheṣu yat puṇyaṃ sarvadāneṣu yat phalam
d tat phalaṃ labhate martyaḥ karṇākhyānaṃ śṛṇoti hi
d hiraṇyavastradhānyāni gāṃ savatsām upānahau
d tena brahmā ca viṣṇuś ca rudrāś ca vasavas tathā
d pūjitā munayaḥ sarve pitaraś ca tathāśvinau
d yaḥ śṛṇoti sadā bhaktyā karṇākhyānam anuttamam
d dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ caturvidhaphalaṃ labhet

d paṭhanti puṇyāṃ varasaṃhitām imām
d dhanena dhānyena yaśasā ca mānuṣā
d nandanti te nātra vicāraṇāsti
d ato 'nasūyuḥ śṛṇuyāt sadā tu vai
d naraḥ sa sarvāṇi sukhāni cāpnuyāt
d viṣṇuḥ svayaṃbhūr bhagavān bhavaś ca
d tuṣyanti ye yasya narottamasya
d vedāvāptir brāhmaṇasyeha dṛṣṭā
d raṇe balaṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ jayo yudhi
d dhanajyeṣṭhāś cāpi bhavanti vaiśyāḥ
d śūdrārogyaṃ prāpnuvantīha sarve
d tathaiva viṣṇur bhagavān sanātanaḥ
d sa cātra devaḥ parikīrtyate yataḥ
d tataḥ sa kāmāṃl labhate sukhī naro
d mahāmunes tasya vaco 'rcitaṃ yathā
d kapilānāṃ savatsānāṃ varṣam ekaṃ nirantaram
d yo dadyāt sukṛtaṃ tad dhi śravaṇāt karṇaparvaṇaḥ
d cintayanto vadhaṃ ghoraṃ sūtaputrasya saṃyuge
d arjunasya jayaṃ yuddhe cintayānāḥ punaḥ punaḥ
d pāṇḍavānāṃ maheṣvāsā nyaviśanta paraṃtapāḥ
d prahṛṣṭamanasaḥ sarve jitvā śatrūn mahārathān
d tato yudhiṣṭhiraṃ tatra niviṣṭaṃ vai mudānvitam
d sametya sarve pañcālā vardhayanto yathāvidhi
d arjunas tu rathāt tūrṇam avaruhya mahāyaśāḥ
d dharmarājasya caraṇau pīḍayām āsa hṛṣṭavat
d tam utthāpya mahārāja dharmaputraḥ pratāpavān
d sasvaje bharataśreṣṭham upajighrann upaspṛśan
d nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca pāṇḍavaś ca vṛkodaraḥ
d abhivādya mahārājam asvajanta sma phalgunam
d dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca pāṇḍavānāṃ ca ye rathāḥ
d vardhayante sma rājānaṃ nihate sūtanandane
d tataḥ kṛṣṇo mahārāja sātyakiś cāpi sātvataḥ
d avardhayetāṃ rājānaṃ nihate sūtanandane
d vāsudevaś ca kaunteyaṃ praṇayād idam abravīt
d adya rājan hatāḥ sarve dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ sarājakāḥ
d hate vaikartane karṇe rathānāṃ pravare rathe
d yadi lokās trayaḥ sarve yodhayeyuḥ savāsavāḥ
d tathāpi durjayaḥ sūtas tava kopāt tu sūditaḥ
d evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca dharmarājo janārdanam
d tava prasādād govinda hataḥ karṇo mahāyaśāḥ
d pāṇḍavāś ca jayaṃ prāptā nāśitāś cāpi śatravaḥ
d tvaṃ hi śakto bhayāt trātuṃ yasya kasya cid āhave
d tvam asya jagato goptā pāṇḍavānāṃ ca sarvadā
d tvāṃ samāsādya śakro 'pi modate divi nityaśaḥ
d tvaṃ pātā pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ yathaiva jagatas tathā
d anāścaryo jayas teṣāṃ bhaktir yeṣāṃ tvayi prabho
d tvayā nāthena govinda nāthavanto vayaṃ yudhi
d yathendreṇa purā devās tvayā cāpi janārdana
d svapsyāmy adya sukhaṃ kṛṣṇa nidrāṃ lapsye vasan kṣapām
d vigataṃ hi bhayaṃ me 'dya tvatprasādān na saṃśayaḥ
d evam uktas tu pārthena keśavaḥ prāha pāṇḍavam
d nimittamātraṃ tu vayaṃ tava hy asmin mudāgame
d yasya te bhrātaraḥ śūrā bhīmasenādayo nṛpa
d saṃbandhinaś cendravīryāḥ pārṣatapramukhās tathā
d arhate ca bhavān vaktuṃ priyaṃ nityaṃ hi maddhitam
d priyo hi me tvam etena vacanena narottama
d ity ukto dharmarājas tu svarathaṃ hemabhūṣitam
d dantavarṇair hayair yuktaṃ kālavālair mahīpatiḥ
d āsthāya puruṣavyāghraḥ svabalenābhisaṃvṛtaḥ
d prayayau bahuvṛttāntaṃ draṣṭum āyodhanaṃ prati
d saṃbhāṣamāṇau tau vīrāv ubhau pāṇḍavamādhavau
d sa dadarśa raṇe karṇaṃ śayānaṃ puruṣarṣabha
d gāṇḍīvamuktair viśikhaiḥ sarvataḥ sunipīḍitam
d saputraṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā karṇaṃ rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d praśaśaṃsa naravyāghrāv ubhau pāṇḍavamādhavau
d adya rājāsmi sarvasyāṃ pṛthivyāṃ madhusūdana
d diṣṭyā jayasi govinda diṣṭyā śatrur nipātitaḥ
d evaṃ subahuśo rājan praśaśaṃsa janārdanam
d arjunaṃ ca kuruśreṣṭho dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d dṛṣṭvā ca nihataṃ karṇaṃ saputraṃ pārthasāyakaiḥ
d punar jātam ivātmānaṃ mene kurukulodvahaḥ
d sametya ca kuruśreṣṭhaṃ kuntīputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
d vardhayanti sma rājānaṃ harṣayuktā mahārathāḥ
d saṃjaya uvāca
d evam eṣa kṣayo vṛttaḥ sumahān romaharṣaṇaḥ
d tava durmantrite rājan diṣṭyā tvam anuśocasi
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d śrutvaitad vipriyaṃ rājā dhṛtarāṣṭro mahīpatiḥ
d papāta bhūmau niśceṣṭaḥ kauravyaḥ paramāsanāt
d tathā satyavratā devī gāndhārī divyadarśinī
d tatas tūrṇaṃ tu viduras taṃ nṛpaṃ saṃjayas tathā
d paryāśvāsayatāṃ caitāv ubhāv eva tu bhūmipam
d tathaivāśvāsayām āsa gāndhārī rājasattamam
d sa daivaṃ paramaṃ mene bhavitavyaṃ ca tat tathā
d tābhyām āśvāsito rājā tūṣṇīm āste viśāṃ pate
d evam ākhyāya rājñe ca saṃjayo rājasattama
d jagāma śibiraṃ bhūyo hate karṇe mahātmani
d sa dṛṣṭvā nihataṃ śalyaṃ rājānaṃ ca suyodhanam
d yodhāṃś ca subahūn rājan sainikāṃś ca sahasraśaḥ
d tathaiva pāṇḍavīṃ senāṃ nihatāṃ prekṣya saṃjayaḥ
d sauptike drauṇinā rājan hatavājinaradvipān
d sa hi dṛṣṭvā hatān sarvān samantād yudhi saṃjayaḥ
d prayāto hastinapuraṃ śokārto bhayavihvalaḥ
d hateṣu punar eteṣu prabhūtagajavājiṣu
d yodhaiś caiva mahārāja nānādeśasamudbhavaiḥ
d kurukṣetraṃ tu tat sarvaṃ śūnyam āsīj jagatpate
d nihataiḥ pāṇḍaveyaiś ca dhārtarāṣṭraiś ca saṃyuge
d yathāviṣayajaṃ vṛttaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya saṃjayaḥ
d nyavedayata tat sarvaṃ yathāvṛttaṃ yathāvidhi
d śaśaṃsur nihitaṃ karṇaṃ phalgunena mahātmanā
d yayatus tatra tau tūrṇaṃ yatrāsīd vīrasaṃkṣayaḥ
d pradīpahastāḥ śataśaḥ samantāt pratyayur narāḥ
d punaś ca śibiraṃ prāpto bhrātṛbhir bharatarṣabhaḥ
d yat kṛtvā tu ca kartavyaṃ sukhāsīnaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
